Ɔɣekparɛ Gɔ Ame I Yesu Ɔbɔrɛ.
Yesu Kristo gɔ nɖe Igara David ɔwa tɛtɛ, fiɛ David ɔ̃ wũ ɔɖe Abraham ɔwa ɔɣekparɛ i ngbe ne.
Abraham ɔɣe Isak, Isak ɔ̃ wũ ɔɣe Yakob gɔ loɣe Yuda ku ɔ̃ manyiibi.
Yuda gu ɔ̃ ɔre Tamai ɔɣe Perez gu Zera, fiɛ Perez ɔɣe Hezron, Hezron ɔɣe Aram, Aram ɔ̃ wũ ɔɣe Aminadab, Aminadab ɔɣe Naheson, Naheson ɔɣe Salmon.
Salmon gu ɔ̃ ɔre Rahab ɔɣe Boaz fiɛ Boaz gu ɔ̃ ɔre Rut ɔɣe Obed, Obed ɔɣe Isai, Isai ɔɣe Igara David.
Ita i Igara David iso isɛ iabo ɔwi gɔ mamɔɛ̃ Israel mabi makɛlɛgu sisande ame i Babilonia karɔ̃ iso ne, mawa ma nto maba i ngbe lowe ne, David gu ɔrɔ̃go gɔ ɔmɔɛ̃ ɔfɔ i Urea kɔrɛ ɔɣe Salomo.
Salomo ɔɣe Rehoboam, Rehoboam ɔ̃ wũ ɔɣe Abiya, Abiya ɔɣe Asa.
Asa ɔɣe Yosafat, Yosafat ɔɣe Yoram, fiɛ Yoram ɔɣe Uzia.
Uzia ɔɣe Yotam fiɛ Yotam ɔɣe Ahaz, Ahaz ɔɣe Hezekia, fiɛ Hezekia ɔɣe Manase gɔ loɣe Amon, Amon ɔɣe Yosia.
Yosia ɔɣe Yekoniya gu ɔ̃ manyiibi ku ɔwi gɔ makɛlɛ sisande ame i Babilonia.
Gɔ mabɔrɛ i sisande ame i Babilonia maba kama ne, Yekoniya ɔɣe Sealtiel fiɛ Sealtiel ɔɣe Zerubabel.
Zerubabel ɔɣe Abihud, Abihud ɔ̃ wũ ɔɣe Elyakim fiɛ Elyakim ɔɣe Azur, Azur ɔɣe Zadok, Zadok ɔɣe Akim, Akim ɔɣe Elihud, Elihud ɔɣe Eleazar, Eleazar ɔɣe Matan, fiɛ Matan ɔɣe Yakob, Yakob ɔɣe Yosef gɔ loyiri Maria, Maria gɔ loɣe Yesu gɔ marɔ sɔ Kristo.
Ne ɔso ita i Abraham iso isɛ iabo David iso ne, mawa iweo-ina maɣe masiaidzo.
Ita i David iso isɛ iabo ɔwi gɔ i Israel mabi ɔkɛlɛ sisande ame i Babilonia karɔ̃ iso ana ne, mawa iweo-ina maɣe masiaidzo.
Ana ne, ita i ɔwi gɔ mase i sisande ame maba isɛ iabo ɔwi gɔ maɣe Kristo ne, mawa iweo-ina maɣe masiaidzo.
Kumɛgɔ Maɣe Yesu Iso Itɔ̃me.
Kumɛgɔ isɛ karɔ̃ fiɛ maɣe Yesu i ngbe ne.
Makarɛ Maria matã Yosef, ɣɛɛ si ɔ̃akɔ wũ lɛ ɔ̃ ɔre ne, manya sɔ Maria ka ɔto kayiri iki i Siwarã Bielea ɔle ame.
Yosef ɖe ɔturi bɔlɔlɔa i Ɣaa anɔ, ɣɛɛ gɔ ɔ̃ito ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃apia Maria kunuarɛ ɔso ne, ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃anyua ɔrɔ̃go i iwɛrɛ ame.
Ɔwi gɔ ɔto ɔbara adzuni wagbe i ɔ̃ iti ame ne, Ɣaa kpabo ɔwɛ̃ ɔɖi so ɔte wũ i kurɛ ame ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Yosef, Igara David ɔwa tɛtɛ, daanigã sɔ aakɔ fɔ ɔre Maria abɔ so i kɔrɛ, ala kayiri ga ɔto ne, Siwarã Bielea kɔrɛ kabɔrɛ.
Ɔto ɔ̃aɣe ɔbirɛrɛĩ, tã wũ iyere sɔ Yesu, alasɔ ɔ̃ loaɖi ɔ̃ maturi ɔbɔrɛgu i ma akpi ame ne.” Nwagbe ɔɖuɖu ɔba sɔ si nnɛ i Ɣaa ɔɣɛ ɔkigu i ɔ̃ kanyaɖidze ɔwɛ̃ iso aaba i ne ame sɔ, “Ɔbitɛ gɔ loiɣe ɔrɛrɛ̃ to ɔ̃ala kayiri ɔɣe ɔbi birɛrɛĩ.
Maatã wũ iyere sɔ Imanuel,” gɔ karɔ̃ nɖe sɔ Ɣaa piagu bo.
Ne ɔso gɔ Yosef ɔta ne, ɔyiri Maria lɛ kumɛgɔ i Ɣaa kpabo ɔɣere wũ awe.
Ɣɛɛ ne, Yosef iirɛgu wũ gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ Maria ɔɣe ɔ̃ ɔbi ɖeakatɔ̃ gɔ nɖe ɔbi birɛrɛĩ, fiɛ Yosef ɔtã wũ iyere sɔ Yesu.
Manɔgbadze Ɔbɔrɛ I Kuɣɛ̃ Kabɔrɛkɔ̃ Maba.
Maɣe Yesu i Betlehem ɔmagɛ̃ ame i Yudea ku ɔwi gɔ ame i Herodes to ɔɖe sigara.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, manɔgbadze ma nɣe ara i awãmi iso ɔbɔrɛ i kuɣɛ̃kabɔrɛkɔ̃ maba Yerusalem Ɔmagɛ̃ ame.
Gɔ maba ne, makarɛ sɔ, “Lɛ maɣe ɔbi gɔ loaɖe ma Yudase igara?
Bonya ɔ̃ iwãmi i kuɣɛ̃kabɔrɛkɔ̃ ɔso boba sɔ si boba boasumu wũ.” Gɔ Igara Herodes ɔnɔ itɔ̃me nɛgbe ne, itidza ɔ̃ gu mma ɔɖuɖu mpia i Yerusalem gbaã.
Ne ɔso ɔkpere masɔrɛdze makpakpa ɔɖuɖu gu mmara matedze ɔsirakanya ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Lɛ maaɣe Kristo?” Ne maɣere wũ sɔ, “Maɣɛ sɔ maaɣe wũ i Betlehem ɔmagɛ̃ ame i Yudea ala Ɣaa kanyaɖidze ɔwɛ̃ ɔtsɛrɛ ɔsɛ sɔ, ‘Fɔ Betlehem ne, maturi sɛ maɣɛ sɔ ɔmagɛ̃ kosoi aɖe i Yudea karɔ̃ iso.
Ɣɛɛ iiɖe ngbɔ iɖe!
Alasɔ fɔ ame i tɔ̃ɖedze siare gɔ loakɔ wũ kaɖe Israel aabɔrɛ.’ ” Ne kama ne, Herodes ɔkpere mafɔ ma lobɔrɛ i kuɣɛ̃kabɔrɛkɔ̃ ɔnɔwɛ̃ ɔkɛlɛgu kawɛrɛkɔ̃ sɔ si ɔtsue ɔwi gɔ tutuutu manya iwãmi nɛmɔ.
Ɔɖi ma ɔri sɔ makɛlɛ Betlehem ku atɔ̃me wagbe sɔ, “Misɛ mianyɔnyɔ ɔbi gɔgbe kukaakɔ, si minya wũ ne, mikpese miba miaɣere me sɔ mme wũ loasɛ loasumu wũ.” -Ne ɔso mafɔ magbe ɔrui maɣo ɔri.
I ɔri ne, iwãmi nɛ manya i kuɣɛ̃kabɔrɛkɔ̃ mmɔ ɔledza ibɔrɛ.
Gɔ manya ne ne, mana isoɣɔ gbaã.
Iɖe ma katɔ̃ gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ isɛ iatui i ngbegɔ i ɔbi ɣɛtɛ rɛ.
Gɔ mabo i iyo ame fiɛ manya ɔbi gu ɔ̃ ɔnyi Maria ne, mapɛ agɛgɛ̃ masumu wũ.
Gɔ mabusi ma akpo ne, maɖi karatã sɛɛ ga nɖe sikãrɛtɛa, korobo gu ɔlufui matã wũ.
Ne kama gɔ makpese ne, Ɣaa ɔsɛ̃ ɔtã ma i kurɛ ame sɔ madaasɛ maaki i Herodes kɔrɛ.
Ne ɔso maki ɔri mama marui makɛlɛ ma aɖe.
Yosef Ɔteregu Maria Gu Yesu Ɔkɛlɛgu Egipte Karɔ̃ Iso.
Gɔ mafɔ mamɔ ɔɔrui kama ne, Ɣaa kpabo ɔwɛ̃ ɔɖi so ɔte Yosef i kurɛ ame ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Herodes to ɔ̃abie ɔri gɔ iso ɔ̃aki ɔ̃aɖoe ɔbi, ne ɔso ta si akɔ wũ gu ɔ̃ ɔnyi si ateregu ma akɛlɛgu Egipte.
Miwe i mmɔ gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ loaɣere mi sɔ mikpese miba.” Kasɛ̃ gamɔ ame ame ne, Yosef ɔta ɔkɔ ɔbi gu ɔnyi marui matere makɛlɛ Egipte.
Mawe i mmɔ gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ Herodes ɔkpi.
Iba ngbɔ sɔ si nnɛ i Ɣaa kanyaɖidze ɔwɛ̃ ɔtsɛrɛ ɔsɛ aaba i ne ame sɔ, “Ta Egipte lokpere wũ Ɔbi lobɔrɛgu.” Herodes Ɔtã Maɖoe Mabi Birɛrɛĩ Ɔɖuɖu I Betlehem.
Gɔ Herodes ɔnya sɔ manɔgbadze ma lobɔrɛ i kuɣɛ̃kabɔrɛkɔ̃ mmɔ ɔsɔsɔla wũ ne, sikpã ɔmɔɛ̃ wũ gbaã.
Ɔpia makpakpɛ̃dze sɔ maɖoe mabi birɛrɛĩ ɔɖuɖu ma i Betlehem gu simagɛ̃ dzɛ loki silɔ ame.
Mma ɔɖuɖu loɔfɔ ita i akɔ anyɔ iba karɔ̃ si ikategu ɔwi gɔ i mmamɔ ɔɣɛ sɔ manya iwãmi kanya.
Mabi iɖoe nɛgbe ɔba sɔ si nnɛ i Ɣaa kanyaɖidze Yeremia ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ aaba i ne ame sɔ, “Kulu kuwɛ̃ to i Rama.
Kaku gu isoma kulu kuɖe!
Rahel nto ɔbiɛ ɔ̃ mabi, fiɛ ɔ̃ito ɔbie sɔ malora wũ, ala sɔ ɔ̃ mabi ɔkpi.” Yosef Ɔkɔ Maria Gu Yesu Makpese Makɛlɛ Nasaret.
Gɔ Herodes ɔkpi ne, Ɣaa kpabo ɔwɛ̃ ɔɖi so ɔte Yosef i kurɛ ame i Egipte.
Ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ta si akɔ ɔbi gu ɔnyi si mikɛlɛ Israel karɔ̃ iso alasɔ mma lobie sɔ maaɖoe ɔbi ɔɔkpi.” Ne ɔso Yosef ɔta ɔkɔ ɔbi gu ɔnyi marui makɛlɛ Israel karɔ̃ iso.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ Yosef ɔnɔ sɔ Arkelao masɛra sigara i ɔ̃ ɔse kanya i Yudea ne, ɔnigã mmɔ ikɛlɛ, ne ɔso i kurɛ ame ne, Ɣaa ɔɣere wũ sɔ ɔkɛlɛ Galilea karɔ̃ iso.
Ɔsɛ ɔ̃awe i ɔmagɛ̃ gɔ marɔ sɔ Nasaret ame sɔ itɔ̃me nɛ i Ɣaa kanyaɖidze ɔwɛ̃ ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ aba i ne ame sɔ, “Maakpere wũ sɔ ɔ Nasaretse,” aaba i ne ame.
Ndupiedze Yohanes Ɔpɛ Imomo.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, Ndupiedze Yohanes ɔba Yudea fafuĩ ame ɔba ɔ̃atsɛ Ɣaa itɔ̃me iɣɛ sɔ, “Mifiniki i mi situ ame ala Ɣaa sigara ɔɖewi ɔɔɣo.” Yohanes gɔgbe nɖe ngɔ iso i Ɣaa Kanyaɖidze Yesaya ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ sɔ, “Ɔwɛ̃ to ɔla kulu teteree i fafuĩ ame sɔ, ‘Miledza ɔri mitã Bosate iba.
Mibara ɔ̃ ɔri gɔ iso ɔ̃asɛ tɔrɔrɔ.’ ” Awu wa i Yohanes ɔpia ne, kapuipɔngɔ siwɛrɛ̃ masu mawe ala, fiɛ ɔsu bɔi ɔko kafiami ɔtɔ so ɔsɔ.
Maɣendu gu kugbadzedzei loɖe ɔ̃ aɖera.
Maturi ɔbɔrɛ i Yerusalem gu Yudea ɔɖuɖu gu Yordan ɔwore kama abuiti ɔɖuɖu ame maba ɔ̃ kɔrɛ.
Gɔ maɖi ma akpi maɣɛ ne, Yohanes ɔpie ma Ɣaa ndu i Yordan ɔwore ame.
Gɔ Yohanes ɔnya ma Farisise gu ma Zadukise gbodzoo ma loba sɔ ɔpie ma Ɣaa ndu ne, ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mi ma lonyanyarĩ lɛ maɣɛ!
Midaasɔsɔla so iki i Ɣaa itupie ifɔ ame sɔ miawo ɔtere i Ɣaa sikpã dzɛ nto siba i kayiiso kanya!
Mite i mi nsɛgbai ame sɔ miɔfiniki mibɔrɛ i mi akpi ame.
Midaabu sɔ gɔ Abraham mawa miɖe ɔso ne, Ɣaa iibakpadzɛ̃ mi kutsue.
Nto loɣere mi sɔ Ɣaa to ɔ̃awo mawa ɔbara ɔɖi i ata wa nfere i ngbe ame ɔtã Abraham.
“Minyɔ!
Maɔkarã kaɣɛ i adziri iso koko sɔ maatu wã ta siɖu ame.
Kudziri biara gɔ loisɛ kuɣɔ̃ abi sɛɛ ne, maaɖaɛ kɔ̃ mapɛyu matsuedza.” “Mme ne, ndu losu nto lopie mi si ite sɔ miɔfiniki mibɔrɛ i mi akpi ame.
Ɣɛɛ ngɔ nsiai me i kama ɔto ɔba ne, Ɣaa Siwarã gu ɔtɔ ɔ̃asu ɔpie mi ndu.
Ɔmɔ ɔɖo me sɔ loikote sɔ loaɖe ɔ̃ ɔɖabo kɔra.
Ɔto ɔ̃ ifɛra nɛ ɔ̃afɛ ala simɔɣo ɔɖi i kamɔ ame.
Ɔ̃asu aɖera ɔfere i kawu ame, ɣɛɛ simɔɣo ne, ɔ̃atsuedza sɛ̃ ku ɔtɔ gɔ loisɛ ɔnyi!” Yohanes Ɔpie Yesu Ɣaa Ndu.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, Yesu ɔbɔrɛ i Galilea ɔba Yohanes kɔrɛ i Yordan ɔkpokpo sɔ Yohanes si ɔpie wũ Ɣaa ndu.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ Yohanes to ɔbie sɔ ɔfinikira ɔ̃ adzuni ɔso ne, ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Mme ikote sɔ loaba fɔ kɔrɛ apie me Ɣaa ndu ne iiɖe fɔ loaba wũ kɔrɛ!” Ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Tã ise ngbɔ si boawo ira biara nɛ i Ɣaa ɔbie sɔ bobara ɔbara.” Ne Yohanes ɔnɔ karɔ̃ ne.
Gɔ ɔpie Yesu ndu ɔro fiɛ ɔto ɔbɔrɛ i ɔwore ame ne, kuɖokpo ɔbusi kutã wũ.
Ɔnya Ɣaa Siwarã ɔso lɛ ilɔpɔ siba siasia wũ iso.
Ne manɔ silɔ ɔbɔrɛ i kato siɣɛ sɔ, “Wũ Ɔbi gɔ loisɛ lopia kuɣɛ i ngbe ne, ɔbo me anɔ gbaã.”
Tsirise Ɔla Yesu Ɔnyɔ.
Siwarã Bielea ɔkɔ Yesu sikɛlɛgu fafuĩ ame sɔ Tsirise si ɔsɛ ɔ̃ala wũ ɔnyɔ.
Gɔ ɔnyi kanya akpɛnɛ sina kasɛ̃ sina ne, kukã ɔkpɛ̃ wũ.
Mmɔ i Tsirise ɔba ɔ̃ kɔrɛ ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Si fɔ nɖe Ɣaa Ɔbi ne, ɣere ata wagbe sɔ akpese aɖera.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Matsɛrɛ mapia i Ɔko Sekelea ame sɔ, ‘Iiɖe aɖera ɔnɔwɛ̃ iso i ɔturi aasɛ ngbã, ɣɛɛ Ɣaa itɔ̃me atsue ikã ɔso bowũ.’ ” Tsirise ɔkɔ Yesu ɔkɛlɛgu Yerusalem, Ɔmagɛ̃ Sekelea ame, ma Yudase kasɔrɛkɔ̃ kakɔlɛkɔ̃ pelepele.
Ne ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Si Ɣaa Ɔbi aɖe ne, nyua so sɛ aawuĩ i karɔ̃.
Alasɔ Ɔko Sekelea ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Ɣaa ɔɣɛ sɔ ɔ̃apia ɔ̃ makpabo mamɔɛ̃-ɔ i nrɔɔ̃ ame sɔ aibasu fɔ kukpa awuĩ i ita kuiwɛ̃ iso.’ ” Yesu ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Ɔko Sekelea ɔɣɛ ana sɔ, ‘Daala Bosate Ɣaa anyɔ.’ ” Tsirise ɔledza Yesu ikɔ ikɛlɛgu kube kɔlɛa kuwɛ̃ itititɛ̃.
Ɔte wũ kayiiso sigarakuɖekɔ̃ ɔɖuɖu ku kɔ̃ sile.
Ne ɔɣere Yesu sɔ, “Si aapɛ agɛgɛ̃ atã me asɔrɛ me ne, loasu ara wagbe ɔɖuɖu lotã-ɔ.” Ne Yesu ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Satana, rui me i kɔrɛ!
Ɔko Sekelea ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Bosate Ɣaa ɔnɔwɛ̃ nɖe ngɔ lokote sɔ maapɛ agɛgɛ̃ matã masɔrɛ.’ ” Ne Tsirise ɔrui i Yesu kɔrɛ, fiɛ Ɣaa makpabo ɔba maabuai wũ ne.
Yesu Ɔsɛ Ɔ̃ Karabara Karɔ̃ I Galilea.
Gɔ Yesu ɔnɔ sɔ maɔmɔɛ̃ Yohanes mapia i iyo ne, ɔrui ɔkɛlɛ Galilea.
Ɔ̃iwe i Nasaret, ɣɛɛ ɔkɛlɛ Kapernaum, ɔmagɛ̃ gɔ nse i Galilea itubu kanya i Zebulon gu Naftali karɔ̃ iso.
Ɔsɛ ɔ̃awe i mmɔ, ne ɔso nnɛ i Ɣaa Kanyaɖidze Yesaya ɔɣɛ ɔba i ne ame sɔ, -“Zebulon gu Naftali maturi ma nsi i idududu ame i itubu ɔri iso i Yordan ɔkpokpo i Galilea ngbegɔ i maturi ma loiɖe ma Yudase si ne, maanya ikpawaĩ siare.
Fiɛ mma nsi i karɔ̃ ga iso i kukpi to kuɖe sigara ne, ikpawaĩ aafiɛ ifere ma.” Ita i ɔwi gɔgbe ame ne, Yesu ɔtsɛ imomo ipɛ iɣɛ sɔ, “Mifiniki i mi situ ame ala Ɣaa sigara ɔɖewi ɔɔbore ɔbo.” Yesu Ɔkpere Makpɛɖidze Ina Sɔ Masiai Wũ.
Gɔ Yesu to ɔkila i Galilea ibu kɔrɛ ne, ɔnya manyiibi inyɔ, Simon gɔ marɔ Petro gu ɔ̃ ɔnyiibi Andrea to mapia asabu ala makpɛɖidze maɖe.
Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Miba miasiai me si loakpesera mi maturi maɖidze mitã Ɣaa.” Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, manyua ma asabu masɛ marui masiai wũ.
Gɔ ɔrui i mmɔ ɔsɛ kɛkɛĩ ne, ɔnya manyiibi inyɔ mama, Yakobo gu Yohanes.
Ma gu ma ɔse Zebedeo si i ɔkolo ame mato maledza ma asabu fiɛ Yesu ɔkpere ma.
Ɔluwɛ̃ marui manyua ɔkolo gu ma ɔse masɛ masiai wũ.
Yesu Ɔte Ɣaa Itɔ̃me, Ɔsa Sinyɛ Ana.
Yesu ɔwe ɔki i Galilea abuiti ɔɖuɖu ame ɔto ɔte Ɣaa itɔ̃me i ma Yudase kusarɛkɔ̃, ɔɣɛ Sigarakaɖekɔ̃ iso Itɔ̃me Bielea, ɔsa mma ɔɖuɖu nto manyɛ sinyɛ agbãagbã.
Ɔ̃ iso itɔ̃me ɔki ikã i Siria karɔ̃ ɔɖuɖu iso, ne ɔso maturi ɔsore mma ɔɖuɖu nto manyɛ sinyɛ agbãagbã, mma i so to sibo, mma i siwarã lalaa to siɖaa, mma nto manyɛ kakpebubu gu mma lofɛfɛ̃ marɛ ɔɖuɖu ne, Yesu ɔsa ma ɔɖuɖu.
Maturi gbodzoo ɔsiai wũ.
Ma mawɛ̃ ɔbɔrɛ i Galilea gu Simagɛ̃ Iweo gu Yerusalem gu Yudea gu nrɔ̃ mɛ mpia i Yordan ɔwore kama isɛ ame.
Yesu Ɔte Ara I Kube Iso Gɔ Yesu ɔnya maturi gbodzoo ma nsiai wũ ne, ɔya ɔsɛ ɔ̃asɛ i kabemi iso fiɛ ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔba maasɛ wũ i kɔrɛ.
Ne ɔte ma ara ɔɣɛ sɔ, “So si siɣɔ mma nɣe sɔ mawɛrɛba maɖe i Ɣaa itsue ame.
Alasɔ ma ɔkpɛ nɖe Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃.
So si siɣɔ mma nto mamararã so ala ma i Ɣaa aatui kɔrɔ̃ i kagbegbe ne.
So si siɣɔ mma lobɔ so karɔ̃, alasɔ ma loaɖe kayiiso ara ne.
So si siɣɔ mma anɔ lorɛtɛ i Ɣaa kuɖɔɛ ibara iso, ala Ɣaa to ɔ̃abara ma kuɖɔɛ ɔtã ma.
So si siɣɔ mma nsɛ manyɔ maturi nnya, ala ma i Ɣaa aanyɔ nnya ne.
So si siɣɔ mma situ ame lokpa, ala ma loanya Ɣaa ne.
So si siɣɔ mma nsɛ maledza manyii ndɛ̃, ala ma i Ɣaa aakpere sɔ ɔ̃ mabi ne.
So si siɣɔ mma kama i maturi sɛ mati ala Ɣaa kuɖɔɛ ibara ɔso, ala ma ɔkpɛ nɖe Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ne.
“So si siɣɔ mi si maturi to matia mi, mati mi kama maɣɛ ara nyanyarĩa wa nɖe mila i mi iso alasɔ miɖe wũ masiaidze ɔso.
So si siɣɔ mi, mina isoɣɔ alasɔ Ɣaa to ɔ̃atã mi kuso siare i kato.
Ngbɔ makpɛ̃gu Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze ma loɖe mi katɔ̃ ne.
Yesu Masiaidze Se Lɛ Mma Gu Ikpawaĩ.
“Mi nse lɛ mma mitã maturi ɔɖuɖu, ɣɛɛ si mma ɔyu me ɔmɛrɛ̃ ne, maisibawo ɔri kuwɛ̃ iso ɔki ɔpia me ɔmɛrɛ̃.
Misiina kusia kukuwɛ̃ iɖo sɔ maasu me mawiri maturi ɔsɛ me iso.
“Mi nɖe ikpawaĩ mitã kayiiso ɔɖuɖu.
Ɔmagɛ̃ gɔ matsue masia i kube iso ne, ɔ̃ibawo ɔwɛrɛ.
Kuwɛ̃ iisɛ ɔtsue ɔkaniɛ ɔsu kapoi ɔfu iso, ɣɛɛ ɔ̃atara ɔsia i kakɔlɛkɔ̃ sɔ ɔ̃asa ɔtã ɔbiara.
Ngbɔ ame i mi sikaniɛ si sisa sitã maturi sɔ maanya mi kurabarara sɛɛ fiɛ maale mi Ɔse gɔ i kato ne.
Yesu Ara Ite I Mmara Iso.
“Loiba lotindza Mose mmara gu Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze ara ite ɖuɖuuɖu, ɣɛɛ loba sɔ si wã ibiara aba i ne ame.
Gbagbaã nto loɣere mi sɔ ayi kumɛgɔ i kato gu karɔ̃ se ne, mmara katotoi ɣee kakpoi kukawɛ̃ iibakpase kabɔrɛ gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ ibiara ɔba i ne ame.
Ne ɔso ɔbiara gɔ loatu mmara kosoi tsɔra fiɛ ɔ̃ate mamama sɔ mabara ngbɔ ne, maakpere wũ ɔtsɔra i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃.
Ngbɔ ame i ɔbiara gɔ loabara i mmara mɛgbe iso fiɛ ɔ̃ate maturi mama sɔ mabara i me iso ne, maakpere wũ sɔ ɔsiare i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃.
Ne ɔso nto loɣere mi sɔ miibawo Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ame ɔbo si mi Ɣaa kuɖɔɛ iso ibara iikɔlɛ iɖo mmara matedze gu ma Farisise ɔkpɛ.
Yesu Ɔte Ara I Sikpã Ina Iso.
“Ɔwiɔ ne, minɔ maɣɛ sɔ, ‘Daaɖoe ɔturi.’ Ngɔ loɖoe ɔturi ne, ɔkote ɔtã atɔ̃me iɣɛgu.
Ɣɛɛ nto loɣere mi sɔ ngɔ lonagu ɔ̃ ɔnyii sikpã ne, ɔkote ɔtã atɔ̃me iɣɛgu.
Ngɔ loaɣere ɔ̃ ɔnyiibi sɔ, ‘Ailɛ atã kuira’ ne, makpakpa aaɣɛgu wũ atɔ̃me.
Fiɛ ngɔ loakpere ɔ̃ ɔnyiibi sɔ, ‘Bɔi aɖe’ ne, ɔkote ɔtã Ɣaa kutsue ikpadzɛ̃ itɔkpe ame ikɛlɛ.
Ne ɔso si asu karatã ato abɔ Ɣaa isɔrɛkasege iso fiɛ anyigi i mmɔ sɔ irere pia i fɔ ɔnyii ɔtu ame i fɔ iso ne, nyua fɔ karatã sɛ i isɔrɛkasegetɔ̃ si akpese akɛlɛ mi gu fɔ ɔnyii si misɛ miafere kanya ndu fiɛ aaba aasu fɔ karatã atã Ɣaa.
“Si atsue sɔ fɔ ɔnyii to ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃abara-ɔ itɔ̃me ne, nyɔ sɔ miaɣɛ mirara so fiɛ miabo atɔ̃mekaɣɛkɔ̃.
Si iiɖe ngbɔ ne, fɔ gu ngɔ lona itɔ̃me to ɔ̃aɖi-ɔ ɔtã atɔ̃meɣɛdze fiɛ atɔ̃meɣɛdze ana aasu-ɔ ɔtã madzuɛ̃se mapia-ɔ i iyo.
Gbaã nto loɣere-ɔ sɔ ato aawe i iyo karɛkɔ̃ gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ ɔwi gɔ atã kuso gɔ ato kapɛrɛ tsɔra aro.
Ara Ite I Asɔrɔ̃ra Iso.
“Misɛ minɔ maɣɛ sɔ, ‘Marã gu mare si madaaɖe asɔrɔ̃.’ Ɣɛɛ nto loɣere mi sɔ si anyɔ ɔrɔ̃go fiɛ ɔkpɛ̃-ɔ ɔkã sɔ aasiai wũ ne, ɔɔsiai wũ koko i fɔ ɔtu ame.
Ne ɔso si fɔ kuɖearɔ̃ inɔmi sɛ itã abara ikpi ne, were ne ɖi pɛyu.
Alasɔ si fɔ sosina kakɔi kawɛ̃ ɔkpɛti ne, ilɛ iɖo sɔ Ɣaa asu fɔ kuturidziri ɔɖuɖu ɔpia i itɔkpe nɛ loisɛ inyi ame.
Fiɛ si fɔ kuɖearɔ̃ nsɛ kutã abara ikpi ne, tu kɔ̃ pɛyu.
Ilɛ iɖo sɔ fɔ iso kakɔi kawɛ̃ aakpɛti iɖo sɔ Ɣaa asu fɔ kuturidziri ɔɖuɖu ɔfuĩdza ɔpia i itɔkpe nɛ loisɛ inyi ame.
Yesu Ɔte Ara I Marã Gu Mare Isɛ̃so Iso.
“Masɛ maɣɛ sɔ, ‘Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ losɛ̃ ɔ̃ ɔre si ɔtã wũ ɔko gɔ loate sɔ ɔ̃ɔsɛ̃ ɔ̃ ɔre.’ Ɣɛɛ nto loɣere mi sɔ, ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔrere gɔ loasɛ̃ ɔ̃ ɔre fiɛ iiɖe kama i ɔrɔ̃go ɔfe wũ ne, ɔtã ɔrɔ̃go ɔbara asɔrɔ̃ iɖe ikpi si ɔyiri ɔrɛrɛ̃ mama, fiɛ ngɔ loayiri ɔrɔ̃go gɔ masɛ̃ mmɔ ana ɔbara asɔrɔ̃ iɖe ikpi.
Yesu Ɔte Ara I Ara Itarĩgu Iso “Ɔwiɔ ne minɔ masɛ maɣɛ ana sɔ, ‘Daatu ndamu, Ɣɛɛ bara i nnɛ aɣɛ sɔ aabara atã Ɣaa iso.’ Ɣɛɛ mme nto loɣere mi kiniɔ sɔ daatarĩgu kuira ɖuɖuuɖu si ato akã ndamu.
Daatarĩgu kato ala mmɔ nɖe Ɣaa sigaraiyara ne.
Daatarĩgu karɔ̃ ala mmɔ nɖe Ɣaa ngba kasiakɔ̃ ne.
Daatarĩgu Yerusalem ana ala Magara ɔɖuɖu Igara Ɔmagɛ̃ ɔɖe.
Daatarĩgu fɔ iti ala aibawo fɔ ɔwɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɔbara kpinakpina ɣee futututu.
Si nnɛ mato maɣɛ pia i ne ame ne, tɔrã kere sɔ aĩ, fiɛ si ina i ne ame ne, ɣɛ kere sɔ ooɣo.
Si irere ka ibua i nnɛgbe iso ne, Tsirise kɔrɛ ibɔrɛ.
Yesu Ɔte Ara Ikpi Ibara Itikuso Iso.
“Minɔ masɛ maɣɛ sɔ, ‘Si abiɛ fɔ ɔlaa inɔmi ne, maabiɛ fɔ ire, fiɛ si akpa fɔ ɔlaa inyɛ ne, maakpa fɔ ire fɔ wũ.’ Ɣɛɛ kiniɔ ne, nto loɣere mi sɔ, daabara fɔ ɔlaa ikpi nɛ ɔbara-ɔ atikuso.
Si ɔrere ɔpɛ-ɔ ɔrɔ̃ta i kuɖearɔ̃ kutsueti ne, finikira kunyɔare tã wũ si ɔpɛ.
Si ɔrere ɔbara-ɔ itɔ̃me sɔ si ɔfɔ fɔ awu wa apia asɛ karɔ̃ ne, ɖi nwa apia asia kato ana tã wũ.
Ngbɔ ame si kpakpɛ̃dze ɔmɔɛ̃-ɔ sikitii sɔ soregu wũ ɔ̃ ato si asɛ igu iwɛ̃ ne, sɛgu wũ agu anyɔ.
Si ɔturi ɔkarɛ-ɔ ira ne, tã wũ, fiɛ si ɔrere ɔba sɔ ɔba ɔnyɛ ira i fɔ kɔrɛ ne, nyɛ tã wũ.
Yesu Ɔte Ara I Matsirise Iɖɔɛ Iso.
“Misɛ minɔ maɣɛ sɔ, ‘Ɖɔɛ mma nto maɖɔɛ-ɔ si atsiri mma lotsiri-ɔ.’ Ɣɛɛ kiniɔ ne, nto loɣere mi sɔ miɖɔɛ mma lotsiri mi si mikparama kayi i mma nto mati mi kama iti si miakpese mi Ɔse gɔ i kato mabi.
Alasɔ ɔ̃ nsɛ ɔtã kuɣɛ̃ ɔbɔrɛ kutã maturi sɛɛ gu malalaa ɔɖuɖu fiɛ ɔsɛ ɔtã kado ɔpɛ ɔtã maturi bɔlɔlɔa gu maturi nyanyarĩa.
Si misɛ miɖɔɛ mma nsɛ maɖɔɛ mi ɔnɔwɛ̃ ne, be kuso miafɔ i Ɣaa kɔrɛ?
Ma lampofɔdze ma wũ masɛ mabara ngbɔ.
Fiɛ si fɔ malaa ɔnɔwɛ̃ asɛ aya ne, mme siba ipɛ aba gɔ mma loiɖe mafɔɖedze ma wũ masɛ mabara ngbɔ?
Ne ɔso milɛ miwiri lɛ kumɛgɔ i mi Ɔse gɔ i kato lɛ ɔwiri.
Yesu Ɔte Ara I Kayiribielea Ibara Iso.
“Minyɔ so kukaakɔ sɔ miibabara mi kasumu kubarara i ɔgbami sɔ maturi aanya.
Alasɔ si mibara ngbɔ ne, mi Ɔse Ɣaa gɔ i kato siina kukuso ɔ̃atã mi.
Ne ɔso si atã wɛrɛba ira ne, daapɛ ne imomo sɔ maturi aanɔ.
Ngbɔ i mma nsɛ mabara ara si mabo maturi anɔ sɛ mabara i kasɔrɛkɔ̃ gu kuɣa ame sɔ maturi aanya fiɛ maale ma ne.
Lobie sɔ lotã mi itsue sɔ maɔfɔ ma kuso koko!
Ne ɔso si abuai wɛrɛba ne, daatã nane fɔ ɔlaa gɔ lomatã-ɔ si ɔtsue nnɛ abara, iɖe iwɛrɛra, iyɔ mi Ɔse Ɣaa gɔ nsɛ ɔnya awɛrɛra ɔɖuɖu wa i maturi sɛ mabara to ɔ̃atã-ɔ kuso.
Yesu Ɔte Ara I Kayi Ikparama Iso.
“Fiɛ si mito mikparama kayi ne, midaase lɛ mma nsɛ mabara ara si mabo maturi anɔ.
Masɛ mabie sɔ maata maya makparama kayi i kasɔrɛkɔ̃ gu kuɣa ame sɔ maturi si manya ma.
Lobie sɔ lotã mi itsue sɔ ma kuso ame maɔfɔ mmɔ ne.
Ɣɛɛ fɔ si ato akparama kayi ne, kɛlɛ fɔ iyo kame si asɛ̃ iyo apia so fiɛ aakpere fɔ Ɔse gɔ maisɛ manya ala anɔmi, iyɔ gɔ ɔ̃ ɔsɛ ɔnya ta awɛrɛra ne, ɔto ɔ̃atã-ɔ kuso.
“Fiɛ si ato akparama kayi ne, daaɣɛ atɔ̃me gbodzoo wa nna karɔ̃ ala ngbɔ i maɣɔsɔrɛdze sɛ mabara ku adzuni sɔ mmɔ i ma aɣɔ aakã ma atsue ne.
Midaase lɛ ma, ala mi Ɔse ka ɔɣe ara wa lonya mi koko fiɛ miakarɛ wũ.
Ne ɔso si mito mikparama kayi ne, miɣɛ sɔ, ‘Bo Ɔse gɔ i kato, tã marɔ fɔ iyere sɛɛ.
Fɔ sigara iɖe si siba i bo ndɛ̃.
Maabara fɔ kuɖɔɛ i kayiiso lɛ kumɛgɔ masɛ mabara i kato.
Tã bo nɔme ikpɛnɛ aɖera.
Su bo akpi tsɛ bo lɛ kumɛgɔ bosɛ bosu botsɛ mma loɣɛrɛ bo.
Daatã sɔ boabo i kalakanyɔ ame, ɣɛɛ ɖi bo bɔrɛgu i ikpi ame.
Ala fɔ ɔkpɛ nɖe sigara iɖe gu ɔle gu ikpawaĩ ɔwi ɔɖuɖu ame.’ “Si misu maturi akpi mitsɛ ma ne, mi Ɔse gɔ i kato ana to ɔ̃asu mi are ɔtsɛ mi.
Ɣɛɛ si miisu maturi akpi mitsɛ ma ne, mi Ɔse ana iibasu mi are ɔtsɛ mi.” Yesu Ɔte Ara I Kanya Inyi Iso.
Yesu ɔledza iɣɛ sɔ, “Si mito minyi kanya ne, midaanyi katɔ̃ mila lɛ mma nsɛ mabara ara si mabo maturi anɔ awe.
Ala masɛ manyi katɔ̃ mala sɔ maturi si matsue sɔ mato manyi kanya, fiɛ gbaã loto loɣere mi sɔ maɔfɔ ma kuso koko.
Si mito minyi kanya ne, mifore anɔmi si mitara mi ati kukaakɔ miledza so.
Ne loatã sɔ maturi iibatsue sɔ ato anyi kanya, ɣɛɛ fɔ Ɔse gɔ maisɛ manya, fiɛ ɔsɛ ɔnya ara wɛrɛa aatã-ɔ kuso.
Kato Nɖe Ara Ka Kɔlakɔ̃ Sɛɛ.
“Midaakɔla karana mitã so i kayi gagbe ame ala ngbe ne, makorokpɛ to maanina kã ɣee kapɛ matɔ, fiɛ mayukukpe ana to maawo kukui ɔbiɛ mabo iyo mayu kã.
Ɣɛɛ ne, mikɔla karana misɛ so i kato.
Ala mmɔ ne, makorokpɛ iisɛ manina ara, kaisɛ kapɛ matɔ fiɛ mayukukpe ana iisɛ mabo i mmɔ mayu ara.
Alasɔ ngbegɔ i fɔ karana se ne, mmɔ i fɔ ɔtu ana aawe ne.
Yesu Ɔte Sɔ Anɔmi Nɖe Kuturidziri Ikpawaĩ.
“Anɔmi se lɛ ɔkaniɛ atã kuturidziri.
Si fɔ anɔmi ɔkpa ne, Fɔ kuturidziri ɔɖuɖu ame to kuakpa waĩ.
Ɣɛɛ si fɔ anɔmi iikpa ne, fɔ kuturidziri ɔɖuɖu to kuase guduu.
Ne ɔso si fɔ ikpawaĩ ɔgudu ne, fɔ idududu ɔwodoro gbaã!
Yesu Ɔte Ara I Ɣaa Gu Karana Isiai Iso.
“Kuwɛ̃ iibawo makɔse inyɔ ɔsumu.
Si iiɖe ngbɔ ne, ɔto ɔ̃aɖɔɛ ɔwɛ̃ ɔtsiri ɔwɛ̃.
Ɣee ɔ̃awarɛ ɔwɛ̃ ɔta ɔya ɔwɛ̃ iso.
Miibawo Ɣaa gu karana ɔsɔrɛ.
Ne ɔso nto loɣere mi sɔ midaamararã so i mi ngbã, nnɛ miaɖe gu nnɛ mianɛ, ɣee mi sosina gu nnɛ miapia iso.
Ɛɛbɛrɛ ngbã iifɔ kuɣa miɖo aɖera fiɛ kuturidziri iifɔ kuɣa kuɖo arapia?
Minyɔ kato kurodzai gɔ loisɛ kukpɛ̃ fiɛ kuisɛ kusɔrɛ̃ ɔraɖui, kuna siwu ɣɛɛ mi Ɔse gɔ i kato sɛ ɔkararã kɔ̃!
Miifɔ kuɣa miɖo kurodzai?
Mi nna loawo ikpɛnɛ iwɛ̃ ɔsu ɔbua i ɔ̃ agbanayi iso iki i imararãso ame?
“Be ɔso mito mimararã so i nnɛ miapia iso?
Minyɔ ipo ame adziri kumɛgɔ asɛ amɔ.
Aisɛ ata ɖɔti ɣee awe sikati.
Ɣɛɛ nto loɣere mi sɔ Igara Salomo kɔra si ɔkɛrɛ so ne, ɔ̃isɛ ɔlɛ ɔnyɔ lɛ kudziri gɔ lofere aɣɔ̃la.
Ɣaa nsɛ ɔkɛrɛ sikua ngbɔ.
Sikua dzɛ mpia nɔme kɔrãkaɖe maɔkpɛ̃ sɛ̃ mafere i ɔtɔ ame matsuedza.
Si Ɣaa to ɔnyɔ sikua iso ngbɔ ne, ɔ̃ibabara ɔtã mi ma loɖo sikua?
Be ɔso i mi kafɔkaɖe ɔfoforo ngbɔ?
“Ne ɔso midaasɛ mimararã so sɔ ‘Be boaɖe?
Be boanɛ?
Be boapia?’ Ara wagbe i maɣɔsɔrɛdze sɛ mabie ne, ɣɛɛ mi Ɔse gɔ i kato ɣe sɔ nwagbe ɔɖuɖu ɔnya mi.
Ɣɛɛ nnɛ iso i mi anɔ si arɛtɛ nɖe sɔ Ɣaa si ɔɖe sigara i mi iso gu si mibara sibɔlɔlɔ ara iyɔ ɔto ɔ̃asu ara wagbe ɔɖuɖu ɔtã mi.
Ne ɔso midaamararã so i kɔrãkaɖe ga loisɛ̃ iso.
Kɔrãkaɖe amɔrɛ̃ si ase ise ala nɔme are ɔɔfe isi.
Yesu Ɔte Ara I Atɔ̃me Iɣɛgu Maturi Iso.
“Midaaɣɛgu maturi atɔ̃me si Ɣaa iibaɣɛgu mi atɔ̃me.
Alasɔ ɔri gɔ iso aɣɛgu fɔ ɔlaa atɔ̃me akigu ne, ɔ̃ ame iso i Ɣaa aɣɛgu-ɔ ne.
Kaboũsuai ga igbã ako ala ara atã fɔ ɔlaa ne, kã ame igbã maasu mako matã-ɔ ne.
“Nda ato abara fiɛ ato anya iku nɛ mpia i fɔ ɔlaa inɔmi fiɛ aito abara kuira i idzirikpo nɛ mpia fɔ mɔmɔ inɔmi iso?
Nda aabara fiɛ aaɣere fɔ ɔlaa sɔ, ‘Tã loɖi-ɔ iku i inɔmi.’ ku ɔwi gɔ i idzirikpo pia-ɔ i inɔmi Ladze!
Ɖe katɔ̃ ɖi idzirikpo nɛ mpia i fɔ mɔmɔ inɔmi tɔtɔ fiɛ aanya kukaakɔ aɖi iku i fɔ ɔlaa inɔmi.
“Midaasu ara wa nse sekelee misa mifere maturi ma nse lɛ makpɛkpɛ alasɔ mato maafiniki mabo mi iso maɖoɖo mi.
Ngbɔ ame si midaasu anyi wa lofɔ kuɣa mifuĩdza misɛ makparako ne.
Si misu misɛ ma ne, ɔnene kere maanene mapia i iba ame.
“Mikarɛ ara si maatã mi ara, mibie ara si miana, mipɛ kukui kɔrɔ̃ si maasese mi iyo.
Alasɔ ɔbiara gɔ nsɛ ɔkarɛ ira sɛ ɔfɔ.
Ɔbiara gɔ nsɛ ɔbie ira sɛ ɔna ne, fiɛ ɔbiara gɔ nsɛ ɔkpura kukui kɔrɔ̃ ne, masɛ masese matã wũ.
“Ɣese ɔwɛ̃ aasu ita ɔtã ɔ̃ ɔbi gɔ lokarɛ wũ aɖera?
Ɣee ɔsu aɣɛ ɔtã ɔ̃ ɔbi si ɔkarɛ wũ ikpɛ?
Si mi ma nɖe makpibaradze kɔra ɣe kumɛgɔ miatã mi mabi ara sɛɛ ne, iyɔ mi Ɔse gɔ i kato to ɔ̃atã mma nto makarɛ wũ ara sɛɛ ɔɖo.
Ne ɔso ira biara nɛ miabie sɔ maturi si mabara matã mi ne, mi wũ mibara wã mitã ma.
Nnɛgbe ame kere i Mose mmara gu Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze ara wa matsɛrɛ masɛ to ate ne.
Miki I Kayogodɔ̃ Ga Lomɔmɔrĩ Ame.
“Miki i kayogodɔ̃ ga lomɔmɔrĩ ame, alasɔ kayogodɔ̃ ga nkpa Ɔbosam itɔkpe ame ne, kabɛ, kã ɔri ana iso isɛ se pɔkɔsɔɔ fiɛ maturi gbodzoo nsɛ i ɔri gɔmɔ iso.
Ɣɛɛ kayogodɔ̃ ga nkpa ngbã mɛ loisɛ miro ame ne, kase mɔmɔrĩ, kã ɔri ana iso isɛ ba ɔle fiɛ maturi kɛkɛĩ pɛ nsɛ i ɔ̃ iso.
Kudziri Biara Ba Kɔ̃ Abi.
“Minyɔ so i mila Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze ma nsɛ maba mi kɔrɛ iso.
I anɔmi ame ne, manyɔ lɛ masɛrɛrerɔ̃, ɣɛɛ aketeke maɖe.
Ma nsɛgbai miasu minya ma miɖi ite.
Kuwɛ̃ iisɛ ɔtɔtɔrɛ figi abi i miyu kudziri iso, fiɛ maisɛ matɔtɔrɛ adziribi ɖea i itongbã iso.
Ne ɔso ne, kudziri sɛɛ ne, abi sɛɛ kusɛ kuɣɔ̃ fiɛ kudziri lalaa ana ne, abi lalaa kusɛ kuɣɔ̃.
Kudziri sɛɛ iibawo abi lalaa ɔɣɔ̃, fiɛ ngbɔ ame i kudziri lalaa iibawo abi sɛɛ ɔɣɔ̃ ne.
Kudziri biara gɔ loisɛ kuɣɔ̃ abi sɛɛ ne, masɛ matu kɔ̃ mapɛyu matsuedza.
Ne ɔso mila kanyamaɖidze ne, ma nsɛgbai miasu minya ma miɖi ite.
Mma Igbã Loakɛlɛ Ɣaa Sigarakaɖekɔ̃.
“Iiɖe ɔbiara gɔ nsɛ ɔɣere me sɔ, ‘Bosate, Bosate,’ loakɛlɛ Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃.
Ɣɛɛ mma nto mabara wũ Ɔse gɔ i kato kuɖɔɛ loasɛ mmɔ.
Atɔ̃me iɣɛyi iso ne, maturi gbodzoo to maaɣere me sɔ, ‘Bosate!
Boɣɛ fɔ itɔ̃me fiɛ bosa siwarã lalaa i fɔ iyere ame.
Bobara awawãra i fɔ iyere ame.’ Mmɔ loaɣere ma sɔ, ‘Loiɣe mi kukakɔi!
Mi ara lalaa mabaradze, mirui me i kɔrɛ.’ Yesu Ɔte Ara I Ayo Matsuedze Agbã Anyɔ Iso.
“Ne ɔso ngɔ nsɛ ɔnɔ wũ itɔ̃me fiɛ ɔsɛ ɔbara i ne iso ne, ɔse lɛ nɔgbadze gɔ lotsue ɔ̃ iyo ɔsia i ita iso.
Kado ɔpɛ, siwore ɔyi, awɛ ɔkpɛ̃ teteree ɣɛɛ iyo iirɔ̃ ala mapia ne karɔ̃ ame kukaakɔ.
Ɣɛɛ ɔbiara gɔ nsɛ ɔnɔ wũ itɔ̃me fiɛ ɔ̃isɛ ɔbara i ne iso ne, ɔse lɛ dzimifɔ gɔ lotsue ɔ̃ iyo ɔsia i iwarĩ iso.
Kado ɔpɛ, siwore ɔyi, awɛ ɔkpɛ̃ amɔɛ̃ iyo fiɛ irɔ̃ teteree ibiɛbiɛ.” Yesu Ɔte Ara Gu Ɔle.
Gɔ Yesu ɔɣɛ ara wagbe ɔro ne, ɔ̃ ara ite ɔbara maturi gbodzoo mamɔ ɣii.
Alasɔ ɔte ara lɛ ngɔ mba ɔle fiɛ iiɖe lɛ ma mmara matedze awe.
Yesu Ɔsa Ɔrɛrɛ̃ Ɔwɛ̃ Gɔ Yesu ɔso i kabemi iso ɔba ne, maturi gbodzoo ɔsiai wũ.
Ne ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ nto ɔnyɛ ɔnyɛ rɛtɛa ɔba ɔ̃apɛ agɛgɛ̃ i ɔ̃ katɔ̃ ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Bosate!
Si aɖɔɛ ne, aawo me ɔsa lose sekelee.” Yesu ɔɖi kɔrɔ̃ ɔpɛgu wũ ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Loɖɔɛ, se sekelee.” Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, ɔsarɛ, ɔse sekelee.
Mmɔ i Yesu to ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Nyɔ kukaakɔ, daaɣere kuwɛ̃ kuira, ɣɛɛ kɛlɛ aasu so te Ɣaa sɔrɛdze si atã ara wa i Mose mmara ɔkarɛ si ite sɔ ka ase sekelee.” Yesu Ɔsa Roma Kpakpɛ̃dzekpakpa Ɔwɛ̃ Ɔɖabo.
Ne kama gɔ Yesu ɔbo i Kapernaum ɔmagɛ̃ ame ne, Roma kpakpɛ̃dzekpakpa ɔwɛ̃ ɔba ɔ̃atu wũ ɔtã wũ iti sɔ, “Bosate!
Wũ ɔɖabo rɛ ɔto ɔnyɛ, ɔ̃ito ɔwo ɔta gɔ so to sibo wũ kukaakɔ.” Yesu Ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Loaba loasa wũ.” Ɣɛɛ kpakpɛ̃dze gɔgbe ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Ooɣo!
Bosate, loikote sɔ aaba wũ iyo, fɔ ɣɛ itɔ̃me iwɛ̃ kere ne wũ ɔɖabo to ɔ̃asarɛ.
Alasɔ mme wũ ɔkpakpa loɖe i makpakpa mama kayirinɔ.
Loba makpakpɛ̃dze mama i wũ kayirinɔ.
Nsɛ loɣere ngɔ sɔ, ‘Kɛlɛ ngbe,’ ɔkɛlɛ fiɛ nsɛ loɣere ɔmama ana sɔ, ‘Ba ngbe’ ɔba.
Nsɛ loɣere wũ ɔɖabo sɔ, ‘Bara lɛ ngbe’ ɔbara.” Gɔ Yesu ɔnɔ atɔ̃me wagbe ne, ibara wũ ɣaa, ne ɔɣere mma nsiai wũ sɔ, “I ɔnukuare ame ne, loinya kafɔkaɖe siare gagbe igbã lonya i Israel karɔ̃ ɔɖuɖu iso.
Nto loɣere mi sɔ maturi gbodzoo to maabɔrɛ i kuɣɛ̃kabɔrɛkɔ̃ gu kɔ̃ iyo kabokɔ̃ maba maasɛ i ɔpɔrɔ̃ katɔ̃ maɖe ara ku Abraham gu Isak gu Yakob i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃.
Ɣɛɛ mma nɖe sigarakaɖekɔ̃ mabi ne, maafuĩdza ma mapia i idududu nɛ mpia i kayoma ame.
Mmɔ i kaku gu inyɛwe aawe ne.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere kpakpɛ̃dzekpakpa gɔmɔ sɔ, “Kɛlɛ!
Iaba itã-ɔ lɛ kumɛgɔ afɔ aɖe awe.” Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ame i iyo ne, ɔɖabo ɔna isosarɛ.
Yesu Ɔsa Maturi Gbodzoo.
Gɔ Yesu ɔsɛ Petro iyo ne, ɔnya sɔ Petro masɔrɔ̃go rɛ, ɔbe ɔtɔ ɔto ɔnyɛ.
Yesu ɔpɛgu wũ kɔrɔ̃, ɔluwɛ̃ ne, ɔsarɛ ɔta ɔwa aɖera ɔtã wũ.
Ne kutsuɛ ne, makɔ maturi gbodzoo ma i siwarã lalaa si i iso mabɔ Yesu.
Ɔsu itɔ̃me iwɛ̃ ɔsa siwarã lalaa ɔɖi i ma ame fiɛ ɔsa mma ɔɖuɖu nto manyɛ.
Nnɛ ɔbara ngbe ɔtã sɔ nnɛ i Ɣaa Kanyaɖidze Yesaya ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ ɔba i ne ame sɔ, “Ɔ̃ mɔmɔ ɔɖu iti i bo isobo kayirinɔ, fiɛ ɔsa bo sinyɛ ɔɖuɖu.” Maturi Inyɔ Mawɛ̃ Ɔbie Sɔ Maasiai Yesu.
Gɔ Yesu ɔnya maturi gbodzoo ma nɣɛ wũ i kɔrɛ mmɔ ne, ɔɣere ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ matã mawara ibu makɛlɛ ɔkpokpo gɔmɔ isɛ.
Mmaratedze ɔwɛ̃ ɔba ɔ̃atu wũ ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ratedze, loasiai-ɔ kakɔi biara ga aakɛlɛ.” Ne Yesu to ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Mabɔi lalaa ba awo wa ame masɛ mawɛrɛ fiɛ kurodzai ana ba ayo, ɣɛɛ mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, na iti kasiakɔ̃.” Rasuãdze ɔwɛ̃ ana ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Bosate, loasiai-ɔ, ɣɛɛ ɖi me ɔri si nsɛ loabiara tete tɔtɔ.” Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Siai me si atã mma nse lɛ makpise si mabiara ma makpise.” Yesu Ɔtindza Awɛ.
Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔbo i ɔkolo ɔwɛ̃ ame marui.
Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, awɛ siare awɛ̃ ɔtsɛ ikpɛ̃ i itubu iso gɔ itã ndu to mita mibo i ɔkolo ame, ɣɛɛ Yesu rɛ ɔto ɔrɛ sirɛ.
Marasuãdze ɔbore mabo wũ matara wũ sɔ, “Bosate, ɖi bo ne ɔkpi boto!” Ne Yesu ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Kafɔkaɖe tɛgɛlɛa maturi, midaanigã!” Ne ɔta ɔtɔ̃me ɔpia awɛ fiɛ anyua ɔkpɛ̃, ndu ana ɔlo kananana ne!
Ibara ma ɔɖuɖu ɣaa, ne mato makarɛ so sɔ, “Mme ɔturi igbã ɔɖe ngbe fiɛ ta awɛ gu ndu to makã wũ atsue?” Yesu Ɔsa Maturi Inyɔ Ma I Siwarã Lalaa Si I Iso.
Gɔ Yesu ɔwara itubu ɔbo i Gadara ibuiti ame ne, maturi inyɔ ma ame i siwarã lalaa si i iso ɔbɔrɛ i ɔkpolo gɔ ame masɛ mabiara maturi maba maasarɛgu wũ.
Maba silalaa sɔ kuwɛ̃ iisɛ ɔki i ndɛ̃ mmɔ ɔfe.
Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, mala kulu maɣɛ sɔ, “Fɔ Ɣaa Ɔbi, be mpia i bo gu-ɔ ndɛ̃?
Ɔba ɔɔba sɔ aba aakpadzɛ̃ bo kutsue aɖegu ɔwi gɔ masɛ katɔ̃?” Makparako ikuri iwɛ̃ ɣɛ i ndɛ̃ mɛmɔ isɛ mato maɖe ara.
Siwarã lalaa ɔtã Yesu iti sɔ, “Si aasa bo ne, tã bosɛ boabo i makparako ikuri nɛ nɣɛ i mmɔ ame.” Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mikɛlɛ ma ame.” Ne ɔso sibɔrɛ sisɛ siabo i ma ame.
Makparako ikuri ɔɖuɖu ɔtere kpitikpitikpiti maso kabemi mabo i itubu ame makpi.
Mma nto manyɔ makparako iso ɔtere makɛlɛ ɔmagɛ̃ ame masɛ maaɣere ma magɛ̃se nnɛ ɔɖuɖu loba gu nnɛ loba i mma iso i siwarã lalaa si iso.
Ne ɔso kaɖe ɔɖuɖu ɔba maasakanya sɔ si manyɔ Yesu.
Gɔ manya wũ ne, matã wũ iti sɔ ɔbɔrɛ i ma karɔ̃ iso.
Yesu Ɔsa Ɔrɛrɛ̃ Ɔwɛ̃ Gɔ Lofɛfɛ̃ Ɔrɛ.
Yesu ɔbo i ɔkolo ame ɔkpese ɔwara itubu ɔkɛlɛ ma aɖe.
Mawɛ̃ ɔsu ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ lofɛfɛ̃ ɔrɛ i ɔkala iso mabɔ wũ.
Gɔ Yesu ɔnya ma kafɔkaɖe ne, ɔɣere nyɛse sɔ, “Na ɔtu wũ ɔbi, losu fɔ akpi lotsɛ-ɔ.” Ne mmara matedze mawɛ̃ mmɔ to maɣere so sɔ, “Ngɔgbe to ɔɣɛ imusuora!” Yesu ɔtsue nnɛ mpia i ma adzuni ame ne ɔso ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Be ɔso mito misusu adzuni nyanyarĩa wagbe i mi situ ame?
Be iɣɛ nse pɔkɔsɔɔ iɖo sɔ ‘Losu fɔ akpi lotsɛ-ɔ,’ ɛɛbɛrɛ sɔ, ‘Ta ya si asɛ’?
Loate mi sɔ mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, ba ɔle i kayi gagbe ame sɔ loasu akpi lotsɛ.” Ne ɔso ɔɣere ngɔ lofɛfɛ̃ ɔrɛ sɔ, “Ta ya si asu fɔ ɔkala si akɛlɛ iyo.” Ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔta ɔya ɔrui ɔkɛlɛ iyo.
Gɔ maturi ɔnya nnɛ loba ne, manigã, matsɛ Ɣaa ile sɔ ɔsu ɔle gɔgbe igbã ɔtã maturi.
Yesu Ɔkpere Mateo Sɔ Ɔsiai Wũ.
Gɔ Yesu ɔrui i mmɔ ɔkɛlɛ katɔ̃ kɛkɛĩ ne, ɔnya lampofɔdze ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Mateo si i ɔ̃ karabara kabarakɔ̃.
Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ba siai me.” Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, Mateo ɔta ɔsiai wũ.
Gɔ Yesu si ɔto ɔɖe ara i Mateo iyo ne, ma lampofɔdze gbodzoo gu makpibaradze ɔba maasɛgu wũ i ɔpɔrɔ̃ iti gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze.
Gɔ ma Farisise ɔnya nnɛgbe ne, makarɛ ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Be ɔso i mi ratedze to ɔɖe ara ku mmagbe igbã?” Yesu ɔnɔ nnɛ mato maɣɛ, ne ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Manyɛse i kuabaradze ɔnya ne iiɖe mma nsarɛ.
Misɛ mianyɔnyɔ itɔ̃me nɛ mpia i Ɔko Sekelea ame sɔ, ‘Nnyainyɔ nto lobie ne iiɖe mabɔi isu ifɛ̃ ara itã’ karɔ̃.
Alasɔ loiba lokpere mma nsɛ mabu so maturi sɛɛ sɔ mafiniki, ɣɛɛ makpibaradze loba lokpere.” Makarɛ Yesu Ara I Kanya Inyi Iso.
Nwagbe kama ne, Ndupiedze Yohanes marasuãdze ɔba Yesu kɔrɛ maba maakarɛ wũ sɔ, “Be ɔso i bo gu ma Farisise sɛ bonyi kanya ɔwi biara, ɣɛɛ fɔ marasuãdze iisɛ manyi?” Yesu ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Mibu sɔ ɔrɔ̃go kɔdze malaa aamararã so ayi kumɛgɔ i ɔrɔ̃go kɔdze pia i ma kɔrɛ?
Ikpa sekelee sɔ maibabara ngbɔ!
Ɣɛɛ iyi to iba gɔ mato maakɔ ɔrɔ̃go kɔdze maruigu i ma kɔrɛ.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ mato maanyi kanya ne.
“Kuwɛ̃ iisɛ ɔta ɔkati kuere ala kakatisɛi ɣɛtɛ, alasɔ si abara ngbɔ ne, kakatisɛi ɣɛtɛ gamɔ to kaakarĩ karui iyoi nɛ loabɛ iɖo iɖeakatɔ̃.
“Ngbɔ ame i kuwɛ̃ iisɛ ɔsu ndã ɣɛtɛ ɔfere i bɔi ɔko akpo kuere ame ne.
Si abara ngbɔ fiɛ ndã ɣɛtɛ ɔtsɛ ifu ne, miatã sɔ akpo kuere aabiɛ gɔ ndã gu bɔi ɔko akpo ɔɖuɖu aanina.
Ne ɔso ndã ɣɛtɛ ne, bɔi ɔko akpo ɣɛtɛ ame masɛ mafere me sɔ wã anyɔ aase kukaakɔ.” Yesu Ɔbuai Ɔrɔ̃go Ɔwɛ̃ Gu Yairo Ɔbi.
Gɔ Yesu togu ma ika iɖe ne, ma Yudase tɔ̃ɖedze ɔwɛ̃ ɔba ɔ̃ kɔrɛ, ɔpɛ agɛgɛ̃ i ɔ̃ katɔ̃ ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Wũ ɔbi birɔ̃gomi ɔkpi kiniɔkiniɔ ɣɛɛ ba sia wũ kɔrɔ̃ iso si arɛgɛ̃ra wũ.” Ne ɔso Yesu ɔta ɔsiai wũ ku ɔ̃ marasuãdze.
Gɔ Yesu to ɔkɛlɛ ne, ɔrɔ̃go ɔwɛ̃ gɔ i ara to afere akɔ aweo-anyɔ ɔki i Yesu kama isɛ ɔpɛgu ɔ̃ awu kutsueti.
Ɔbara ngbɔ ala ɔɣere so sɔ, “Si lopɛgu ɔ̃ awu kutsueti ne, loto loana isosarɛ.” Yesu ɔfiniki ɔnyɔ, ne ɔnya ɔrɔ̃go ne.
Ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Na ɔtu, wũ ɔbi, fɔ kafɔkaɖe ɔɔsa-ɔ.” Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, ɔna isosarɛ.
Ne Yesu ɔkɛlɛ tɔ̃ɖedze gɔmɔ iyo ne.
Gɔ ɔnya kudadã mafɛ̃dze gu mma nto mabiɛ kaku gu kulu titiiti ne, Ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mibɔrɛ ne ɔbi iikpi, sirɛ kere ɔto ɔrɛ.” Gɔ ɔɣɛ ngbɔ ne, mama wũ.
Gɔ masa ɔbiara maɖi ne, Yesu ɔbo iyo ame i ɔbi kɔrɛ.
Ɔmɔɛ̃ wũ kɔrɔ̃ ɔtara wũ ɔɣedza gbanadze.
Itɔ̃me nɛgbe ɔki ikã i karɔ̃ ndɛ̃ mɛmɔ ɔɖuɖu iso.
Yesu Ɔsa Manɔbiɛdze Inyɔ Mawɛ̃.
Gɔ Yesu ɔbɔrɛ i mmɔ ɔto ɔfe ne, manɔbiɛdze inyɔ ɔsiai wũ mato mala kulu teteree sɔ, “Igara David Ɔbi, nyɔ bo nnya!” Gɔ Yesu ɔbo iyo ame ne, maba ɔ̃ kɔrɛ, ne ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Mifɔ miɖe sɔ loawo mi ɔsa?” Matã mmuai sɔ, “Aĩ, Bosate!” Ne Yesu ɔpɛgu ma anɔmi ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Iba itã mi lɛ kumɛgɔ mifɔ miɖe.” Ma anɔmi ɔbusi.
Ne Yesu ɔsɛ̃ ɔtã ma teteree sɔ, “Midaaɣere kuwɛ̃ itɔ̃me nɛgbe.” Ɣɛɛ gɔ mabɔrɛ i mmɔ ne, mapɛ ne imomo i Yesu iso i karɔ̃ gamɔ ɔɖuɖu iso.
Yesu Ɔsa Ɔmumu Ɔwɛ̃.
Gɔ mmagbe ɔrui mato makɛlɛ ne, mawɛ̃ ɔkɔ ɔmumu ɔwɛ̃ gɔ ame i siwarã lalaa pia mabɔ Yesu kɔrɛ.
Ne gɔ Yesu ɔsa siwarã lalaa ɔɖi i ɔ̃ ame ne, ɔtsɛ ika iɖe.
Ibara maturi gbodzoo mamɔ ɣii, ne mato maɣere so sɔ, “Boinya nnɛgbe igbã bonya i Israel karɔ̃ iso.” Ɣɛɛ ma Farisise ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Siwarã lalaa igara lotã wũ ɔle ɔto ɔsu ɔsa siwarã lalaa.” Maturi Ara Ɔɖo Yesu Kayiri.
Yesu ɔsɛ ɔ̃awe ɔki i simagɛ̃ gu nsɛkɔ̃ ame ɔte ara i ma kusarɛkɔ̃, ɔɣɛ sigarakaɖekɔ̃ iso Itɔ̃me Bielea, fiɛ ɔsa sinyɛ agbãagbã gu isobo igbã biara.
Gɔ ɔnya maturi gbodzoo magbe ne, ma ara ɔɖo wũ kayiri alasɔ so ɔɔtu ma fiɛ maɔre nrɔɔ̃ lɛ masɛrɛ ma nna kɔdze.
Ne Ɔso ɔɣere ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Ɔraɖui gɔ maasɔrɛ̃ ɔsi, ɣɛɛ marabaradze iisi.
Ne ɔso mitã kakpɛkɔ̃ Sate iti sɔ ɔsese marabaradze ɔ̃ kakpɛkɔ̃ ame.”
Yesu Ɔtã Ɔ̃ Katɔ̃memasɛdze Iweo-inyɔ Ɔle.
Yesu ɔrɔ ɔ̃ marasuãdze iweo-inyɔ ɔsirakanya ɔtã ma ɔle sɔ masa siwarã lalaa maɖi i maturi ame, masa sinyɛ agbãagbã gu isobo igbã biara.
Katɔ̃memasɛdze iweo-inyɔ mamɔ ayere ngbe ne.
Simon gɔ masɛ marɔ ana sɔ Petro gu ɔ̃ ɔnyiibi Andrea gu Yakobo gu ɔ̃ ɔnyiibi Yohanes ma nɖe Zebedeo mabi gu Filipo gu Bartolomeo gu Toma gu lampofɔdze Mateo gu Yakobo gɔ nɖe Alfeo ɔbi gu Tadeo gu Simon gɔ nsɛ ɔɖɔɛ ɔ̃ kaɖe gu Yuda Iskariot gɔ loaɖi Yesu ɔtã.
Mikɛlɛ Miaɣɛ Itɔ̃me.
Yesu ɔpia marɛrɛ̃ iweo-inyɔ magbe ɔtã ma mmara sɔ, “Midaasɛ mma loiɖe ma Yudase karɔ̃ iso gu ma Samariase simagɛ̃ ame.
Ɣɛɛ mikɛlɛ Israel mabi ma nse lɛ masɛrɛ ma loyu ɔri kɔrɛ.
Si misɛ ne, mipɛ imomo miɣɛ sɔ, ‘Ɣaa sigara ɔɖewi ɔɔɣo!’ Misa manyɛse si mitara makpise.
Mitã mma nto manyɛ ɔnyɛ rɛtɛa iso si ikpa, misa siwarã lalaa miɖi i maturi ame.
Miitã kuso kukuwɛ̃ i ɔle gɔ mifɔ iti, ne ɔso mi wũ midaafɔ kuwɛ̃ kuso.
Midaasu sikã kusiwɛ̃ mipia i mi sikoto ame.
Midaasu marawãnyidze akpo, awu pia aka anyɔ, ndokota ɣee ɔsɛdziri i mi irisɛ ame.
Ikote sɔ maatã rabaradze ɔ̃ aɖera.
“Si mibo ɔmagɛ̃ ɣee kasɛkɔ̃ biara ame ne, mibie ngɔ lonɔ karɔ̃ sɔ ɔ̃afɔ mi.
Mibo i ɔ̃ kɔrɛ si miwe i mmɔ gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ miarui.
Si mibo iyo irere ame ne, miya ma miɣɛ sɔ, ‘Isobuɛ itã mi.’ Si iyo ame maturi ɔfɔ mi ne, mi isobuɛ mibie mitã ma si iba itã ma, ɣɛɛ si maifɔ mi ne, mi isobuɛ mibie mitã ma si ikpese iba mi kɔrɛ.
Ɣɛɛ si iyo irere, ɣee kaɖe karere maturi iifɔ mi ɣee maikã mi atsue ne, mikpakpa mi ngba iso sise mifere si mito mirui.
Nto losia ita lotã mi sɔ iase pɔkɔsɔɔ itã Sodom gu Gomora maturi ku atɔ̃me iɣɛyi iɖo ɔmagɛ̃ gɔmɔ maturi.
Maturi To Maakpɛ̃gu Mi.
“Minyɔ!
Nto lopia mi lɛ masɛrɛrerɔ̃ i magidi ndɛ̃.
Ne ɔso mikpa anɔ lɛ maɣɛ, ɣɛɛ miɣɔ lɛ alɔpɔ.
Minyɔ so kukaakɔ i maturi iso alasɔ mato maaɖi mi matã mamɔɛ̃ makɛlɛgu atɔ̃mekaɣɛkɔ̃, mato maapɛ mi i ma kusarɛkɔ̃.
Wũ ɔso ne, mato maamɔɛ̃ mi makɛlɛgu matɔ̃ɖedze gu magara katɔ̃ sɔ maɣɛgu mi atɔ̃me, ɣɛɛ miɣɛ Itɔ̃me Bielea i mma loiɖe ma Yudase katɔ̃.
Si makɔ mi makɛlɛgu atɔ̃mekaɣɛkɔ̃ ne, midaamararã so sɔ be miasɛ miaɣɛ ɣee nda miaɣɛ mikigu.
Ɣɛɛ si ɔwi ɔɔɣo ne, Ɣaa to ɔ̃atã mi nnɛ miaɣɛ.
Alasɔ iiɖe mi loaɖe ika, ɣɛɛ mi Ɔse Siwarã loaɖe ika sikigu i mi iso.
“Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, maturi to maaɖi ma manyii matã sɔ maɖoe fiɛ mase ana to maaɖi ma mabi matã.
Mabi to maata maya ma maɣese iso maɖi ma matã maɖoe.
Ɔbiara to ɔ̃atsiri mi ala wũ ɔso, ɣɛɛ ngɔ loaya teteree i kafɔkaɖe ame isɛ iabo kawirikɔ̃ ne, Ɣaa to ɔ̃atã wũ ngbã.
Si makpɛ̃gu mi i ɔmagɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ame ne, mitere mikɛlɛ ɔmama ame.
Lobie sɔ lotã mi itsue sɔ miibaro karabara ɔbara i Israel simagɛ̃ ɔɖuɖu ame fiɛ Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi aakpese ɔba.
“Rasuãdze kuwɛ̃ iisɛ ɔɖo ɔ̃ ratedze, fiɛ ɔɖabo kuwɛ̃ ana iisɛ ɔɖo ɔ̃ ɔkɔse.
Ne ɔso ikote sɔ iawe rasuãdze ɔmɛrɛ̃ sɔ ɔ̃akotegu ɔ̃ ratedze, fiɛ ɔɖabo ɔ̃ wũ ne, iawe wũ ɔmɛrɛ̃ sɔ ɔ̃akotegu ɔ̃ ɔkɔse.
Si mato makpere iyo ɔse sɔ Siwarã lalaa igara ne, mme iyere igbã maibakpere iyo maturi?
Midaanigã Maturi.
“Ne ɔso midaanigã maturi alasɔ ira biara nɛ mafu ara ne, mato maabusi ne.
Fiɛ ira biara nɛ mabara i iwɛrɛ ame to iare kayi.
Ara wa ɔɖuɖu loɣere mi i idududu ame ne, miɣɛ wã ku anɔwã fiɛ nwa nto loɣere mi i siwɔwɔi ame ne, mipɛ wã imomo.
Midaanigã mma loaɖoe siturina, ɣɛɛ maibawo ɔkala ɔɖoe.
Ɣɛɛ minigã Ɣaa gɔ loawo siturina gu ɔkala ɔɖuɖu ɔwɔra i itɔkpe ame.
Kapɛrɛ kere masɛ marɔdɛ̃ kunagini kunyɔ, ɣɛɛ maisɛ maɖoe kukawɛ̃ si mi Ɔse gɔ i Kato iitɔrã.
Ɣɛɛ ta mi siwɛrɛ̃ dzɛ i mi ati iso ne, Ɣaa ɣe sɛ̃ kukame.
Ne ɔso midaanigã alasɔ mifɔ kuɣa miɖo kunagini.
Idaakpɛ̃-ɔ Kunuarɛ Sɔ Aɖe Yesu Ɔre.
“Ngɔ loibakpɛ̃ kunuarɛ i wũ iso fiɛ ɔ̃aɣɛ i maturi katɔ̃ sɔ wũ ɔre ɔɖe ne, mme wũ loaɣɛ i wũ Ɔse gɔ i Kato kɔrɛ sɔ wũ ɔre ɔɖe.
Ɣɛɛ ngɔ loasɛ̃ me i maturi katɔ̃ sɔ ɔ̃iɣe me ne, mme wũ loasɛ̃ wũ i wũ Ɔse gɔ i Kato kɔrɛ.
Maturi To Maaɣɛɣɛ So.
“Midaabu sɔ isobuɛ iɖe losu lobɔ kayiiso.
Ooɣo!
Iɣɛɣɛso iɖe lobɔ.
Mabirɛrɛĩ to maata maya ma mase iso, fiɛ mabirɔ̃gomi ana to maata maya ma manyi iso.
Mabi mare to maata maya i ma marã manyi iso.
Ɔturi mɔmɔ iyo maturi loaɖe ɔ̃ matsirise.
“Ɔbiara gɔ loaɖɔɛ ɔ̃ ɔse ɣee ɔ̃ ɔnyi ɔɖo me iibawo wũ rasuãdze ɔɖe.
Ngbɔ ame ngɔ nsɛ ɔɖɔɛ ɔ̃ ɔbi birɛrɛĩ ɣee ɔ̃ ɔbi birɔ̃gomi ɔɖo me iibawo wũ rasuãdze ɔɖe ne.
Ngɔ loisore ɔ̃ inyɛwe ɔnyigbã ɔsiai wũ nsɛgbai ne, ɔ̃ibawo wũ rasuãdze ɔɖe.
Ɔbiara gɔ loabie sɔ ɔ̃akɔkɔ ɔ̃ ngbã to ɔ̃ayura me, ɣɛɛ ɔbiara gɔ loasu ɔ̃ ngbã ɔtã ala wũ ɔso to ɔ̃ana ngbã.
Ɣaa To Ɔ̃atã Ɔbiara Gɔ Lofɔ Yesu Masiaidze Kuso.
“Ɔbiara gɔ loafɔ mi ne, mme iɖe ɔfɔ fiɛ ngɔ lofɔ me ne, ɔfɔ ngɔ lopia me katɔ̃me.
Ɔbiara gɔ loafɔ Ɣaa kanyaɖidze ne, ɔto ɔ̃ana kaɖekɔ̃ i kanyaɖidze kuso ame.
Ngɔ lofɔ ɔturi bɔlɔlɔa ala ɔ̃ sibɔlɔlɔ ɔso ne, ɔto ɔ̃afɔ sibɔlɔlɔ kuso.
Mitã ikpa mi sekelee sɔ ɔrere gɔ loatã wũ masiaidze koso magbe ndu yululua ikɔi ala wũ ɔso ne, ɔto ɔ̃afɔ ne kuso kokooko.”
Ndupiedze Yohanes Ɔpia Ɔ̃ Masiaidze Yesu Kɔrɛ.
Ɔwi gɔ i Yesu ɔɔro ɔ̃ marasuãdze katɔ̃me ɔpia ne, ɔrui i mmɔ ɔkɛlɛ sɔ ɔ̃ate ara ɔɣɛ Ɣaa Itɔ̃me i simagɛ̃ dzɛ mpia i mmɔ ame.
Gɔ ndupiedze Yohanes gɔ mamɔɛ̃ marara i iyo ɔnɔ ara wa i Kristo to ɔbara ne, ɔpia ɔ̃ marasuãdze mawɛ̃ Yesu kɔrɛ.
Masɛ maakarɛ wũ sɔ, “Fɔ nɖe ngɔ maɣɛ sɔ ɔ̃aba ɛɛbɛrɛ bonyɔ ɔmama ɔri?” Ne Yesu to ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Mikpese miaɣere Yohanes ara wa minya gu nwa minɔ.
Manɔbiɛdze to manya, mabafã to masɛ, mma nto manyɛ ɔnyɛ rɛtɛa iso to isekele, makpise to mata, fiɛ mato maɣere mawɛrɛba ana Itɔ̃me Bielea.
So aaɣɔ mma i wũ kurabarara iita kuya iso.” Ɔwi gɔ mma i Yohanes ɔpia katɔ̃me ɔɔkpese mato makɛlɛ ne, Yesu ɔtsɛ ika iɖe i ɔ̃ iso iɣere mma losakanya i mmɔ sɔ, “Ɔwi gɔ mibɔrɛ mikɛlɛ Yohanes kɔrɛ i fafuĩ ame ne, be iɖe minyɔ ɔri sɔ mianya?
Iyata nɛ i ɔwiri to ɔtidza?
Be mibɔrɛ misɛ mianyɔ?
Ngɔ mpia ɔgo awu?
Mma mpia ɔgo awu ne, magara ayo mapia.
Mibua miɣere me nnɛ misɛ mianyɔ.
Ɣaa kanyaɖidze?
Gbaã nto loɣere mi sɔ ɔɖo Ɣaa kanyaɖidze.
Alasɔ ɔ̃ iso i Ɔko Sekelea ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Loasese kpabo ɔɖe-ɔ katɔ̃, sɔ ɔ̃aledza maturi ɔtã fɔ iba.’ Gbaã nto loɣere mi sɔ Yohanes ɔɖo ɔturi igbã biara gɔ maɣe i kayi gagbe ame.
Ɣɛɛ ngɔ lokoso ɔɖo i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ɔɖo wũ.
Ita i ɔwi gɔ i Ndupiedze Yohanes ɔtsɛ ɔ̃ itɔ̃me iɣɛ ipɛ i nɔme ne, maturi to makpɛ̃gu Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃, ɣɛɛ mma i anɔ ɔrɛtɛ mato mabie Ɣaa sigara iɖe kotoo loabo i mmɔ.
Mose mmara gu Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze ɔɖuɖu ɔɖe ika i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ iso iba iabo Yohanes ɔwi iso.
Fiɛ si mibie sɔ miafɔ ma miɖe ne, minɔ sɔ Yohanes nɖe Eliya gɔ maɣɛ masɛ sɔ ɔ̃aba.
Ngɔ mba atsue si ɔnɔ nnɛ loto loɣɛ.
“Kiniɔ ne, be loasu nɔme maturi lokateragu?
Mase lɛ mabiɛtɛ ma nto maɣa kaɣa i kuɣa ame.
Ma malaa to maɣere ma sɔ, ‘Boka isoɣɔ aka botã mi, miitɔ, boɖi sikubiɛnɔ ana botã mi, mmɔ ana miibiɛ kaku.’ Gɔ Yohanes ɔba ɔ̃ito ɔɖe ara ɔnɛ ndã mɛ loamɔɛ̃ ne, maturi sɔ siwarã lalaa mpia i ɔ̃ ame.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, ɔba fiɛ loto loɖe ara lonɛ ndã ne, maturi to maɣɛ sɔ, ‘Minyɔ ɖeɖei gu tarɛ̃dze gɔgbe!
Ɔɖe ma lampofɔdze gu makpibaradze ɔlaa.’ Ɣɛɛ ne, Ɣaa iwola sɛ ite so i ɔturi nsɛgbai ame.” Simagɛ̃ Siwɛ̃ Maturi Iifɔ Yesu Maɖe.
Simagɛ̃ dzɛ ame i Yesu ɔbara awawãra gbodzoo maturi iifiniki, ne ɔso ɔbiɛ ma ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Ndzo miɖe mitã mi Korazin maturi!
Ndzo miɖe mitã mi Betsaida maturi!
Alasɔ si awawãra wa igbã lobara i mi ame iɖe lobara i Tiro gu Sidon simagɛ̃ ame ne, tee maakpase masɛ i ndɔ̃ ame mapia ara wa loate sɔ maɔfiniki mabɔrɛ i ma akpi ame.
Nto loɣere mi gbagbaã sɔ i atɔ̃me iɣɛyi ne, Ɣaa to ɔ̃anyɔ Tiro gu Sidon simagɛ̃ nnya ɔɖo mi.
Mi Kapernaum maturi ne, i mi adzuni ame ne, mito mibie sɔ miakɔlɛ so kato misɛ miabo kato, ɣɛɛ Ɣaa to ɔ̃abɔ mi karɔ̃ mikɛlɛ ta ikpibiɔ.
Alasɔ si awawãra wa lobara i fɔ ame mabara i Sodom ne, tee ɔmagɛ̃ gɔmɔ se ipɛ i nɔme.
Nto loɣere-ɔ sɔ Ɣaa to ɔ̃anyɔ Sodom nnya ɔɖo-ɔ ku atɔ̃me iɣɛyi ɔɖo mi.” Yesu Ɔɣere Maturi Sɔ Maana Iwarã I Ɔ̃ Kɔrɛ.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, Yesu ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Tete, Kato gu Karɔ̃ Sate, nto lole-ɔ sɔ ara wa lowɛrɛ manɔgbadze gu makotsuese ne, aɖi wã ate mabiɛtɛ.
Alasɔ gbaã ne Tete, ngbɔ ikote-ɔ ne.
“Tete ɔsu ara ɔɖuɖu ɔpia me i nrɔɔ̃ ame.
Kuwɛ̃kuwɛ̃ iiɣe Ɔbi iɖo Ɔse fiɛ kuwɛ̃ ana iiɣe Ɔse iɖo Ɔbi gu mma i Ɔbi ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃aɖi ɔ̃ Ɔse ɔte.
“Mibore miba wũ kɔrɛ mi ma ɔɖuɖu nsore ato fiɛ iɔɖa mi si loatã mi iwarã.
Misu wũ ɔnyigbã misia so iso si misuã ara mibɔrɛgu i wũ kɔrɛ si miana iwarã alasɔ wũ kayiri ɔɣɔ fiɛ lobɔ so karɔ̃.
Wũ ɔnyigbã se pɔkɔsɔɔ ku isore fiɛ wũ ato wa loasorera mi ana se foforoo.”
Ma Farisise Ɔkpadzɛ̃gu Yesu Atɔ̃me I Iwarãyi Iso.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ kama ne, gɔ Yesu sɛ ɔto ɔfe i kakpɛkɔ̃ kawɛ̃ ame ku Iwarãyi ne, kukã ɔkpɛ̃ ɔ̃ marasuãdze, ne ɔso mabɛse atita matsɛ iwe.
Gɔ ma Farisise ɔnya ne, maɣere Yesu sɔ, “Nyɔ, fɔ marasuãdze to mabara nnɛ i mmara iitã ɔri sɔ maabara ku Iwarãyi.” Mmɔ i Yesu to ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Miika i Ɔko Sekelea ame nnɛ i David ɔbara ɔwi gɔ i kukã ɔkpɛ̃ wũ gu ɔ̃ maturi?
Ɔbo i Ɣaa iyo ame ɔsɛ ɔ̃asu aɖera wa masu masɔrɛ Ɣaa maɖe gɔ iikote sɔ ɔ̃ gu ɔ̃ maturi aaɖe iɖo Ɣaa masɔrɛdze ɔnɔwɛ̃.
Ɛɛbɛrɛ miika i mmara ame sɔ masɔrɛdze ma nsɛ mabara karabara i isɔrɛyo sɛ matu Iwarãyi mmara ku Iwarãyi biara ɣɛɛ maiɖe ipɔ?
Nto loɣere mi sɔ nnɛ loɖo Ɣaa isɔrɛyo pia i mi ndɛ̃ ngbe.
Ɣaa ɔɣɛ i Ɔko Sekelea ame sɔ, ‘Nnyainyɔ nto lobie ne iiɖe mabɔi ma mafɛ̃ ala ara matã me.’ Si ɔnɔ minɔ itɔ̃me nɛgbe karɔ̃ kukaakɔ ne, tee mma loiɖe ipɔ ne, miibatã ma ipɔ.
Alasɔ Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi nɖe Iwarãyi Sate.” Yesu Ɔsa Ɔrɛrɛ̃ Gɔ Kɔrɔ̃ Lokarĩ.
Gɔ Yesu ɔrui i mmɔ ne, ɔkɛlɛ ma Yudase kasarɛkɔ̃ kawɛ̃.
Ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ kɔrɔ̃ lokarĩ ɔwe i mmɔ.
Mawɛ̃ ma nto mabie ɔri gɔ iso maaki fiɛ maaɖaɛ Yesu kanya ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Mmara ɔtã ɔri sɔ maasa ɔturi ku Iwarãyi?” Ne Yesu ana ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Mi ndɛ̃ nna sɛrɛrerɔ̃ loakpase ɔbo i iwo ame ku Iwarãyi fiɛ ɔ̃ibaso ɔbo ɔɖi wũ?
Ɣɛɛ ne, ɔturi ɔfɔ kuɣa ɔɖo sɛrɛrerɔ̃, ne ɔso mmara ɔtã ɔri sɔ ɔturi aabara isɛɛ ku Iwarãyi.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ngɔ kɔrɔ̃ lokarĩ sɔ, “Nabarã fɔ kɔrɔ̃.” Ɔnabarã kɔ̃, ɔluwɛ̃ ne, ilɛ wũ kɔrɔ̃ karĩa ɔse lɛ ngɔ nsarɛ.
Ma Farisise ɔrui i mmɔ masɛ maasɛ iti ame sɔ maaɖoe Yesu.
Yesu Nɖe Ɣaa Ɔɖabo Gɔ Ɔɖi Ɔtã So.
Gɔ Yesu ɔnɔ sɔ maɔbara adzuni sɔ maaɖoe wũ ne, ɔrui i mmɔ.
Maturi gbodzoo ɔsiai wũ fiɛ ɔsa manyɛse ɔɖuɖu.
Ɣɛɛ ɔsɛ̃ ɔtã ma sɔ madaaɖi wũ mate ngɔ ɔɖe.
Ɔbara ngbɔ, ne ɔso Ɣaa itɔ̃me nɛ maɣɛ i Kanyaɖidze Yesaya ɔko ame aaba i ne ame gbaã sɔ, “Wũ ɔɖabo gɔ loɖi lotã so i ngbe ne.
Ɔmɔɛ̃ me ɔtu fiɛ loipia wũ kuɣɛ.
Loafedza wũ Siwarã lofere wũ iso sɔ ɔ̃apɛ wũ atɔ̃me iɣɛgu imomo ɔtã abuiti ɔɖuɖu.
Ɔ̃ibakpadzɛ̃gu kuwɛ̃ atɔ̃me fiɛ ɔ̃ibafafã kuwɛ̃ ana.
Kuwɛ̃ iibanɔ wũ silɔ i ɔgbami.
Ɔto ɔ̃aɣara so ɔtã mma nna ɔle.
Ɔto ɔ̃awe kayiribielea ɔtã mma i kayi ɔɔtɔrɛ.
Ɔto ɔ̃akɛlɛgu i katɔ̃ ngbɔ gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ atɔ̃me iɣɛ tɔrɔrɔ aaɖe iso.
Abuiti ɔɖuɖu maturi to maasu ma ɔriinyɔ mapia i ɔ̃ ame.” Maɣɛ Sɔ Yesu Ɔle Ne, Siwarã Lalaa Igara Ame Ɔbɔrɛ.
Mawɛ̃ ɔkɔ ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ ame i siwarã lalaa pia fiɛ ɔɖe nɔbiɛdze gu ɔmumu mabɔ Yesu kɔrɛ.
Yesu Ɔsa wũ ne ɔso ɔtsɛ ika iɖe fiɛ ɔtsɛ ara inya ana.
Nnɛgbe ɔbara iturikuri nɛmɔ ɔɖuɖu ɣii, ne mato makarɛ so sɔ, “Iiɖe Igara David Ɔwa gɔ maɣɛ masɛ sɔ ɔ̃aba ɔɖe ngbe ɣɛɛ?” Gɔ ma Farisise ɔnɔ nnɛgbe ne, ma wũ maɣɛ sɔ, “Si iiɖe siwarã lalaa igara Beelzebul ɔɖe lotã wũ ɔle ne, tee ɔ̃ibawo siwarã lalaa ɔsa ɔɖi i maturi ame.” Yesu ɣe ma adzuni, ne ɔso ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Karɔ̃ biara ga maturi loɣɛɣɛ so fiɛ mata maɣɛ so iso aakpese ikpakpi.
Ngbɔ ame i ɔmagɛ̃ ɣee iyo biara nɛ maturi loɣɛɣɛ so fiɛ mata maɣɛ so iso iibawo ɔya ne.
Ne ɔso si Ɔbosam sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ɔta siɣɛ so iso ne, nda ɔ̃abara fiɛ ɔ̃ sigarakaɖekɔ̃ aaya?
Si mi sɔ Beelzebul lotã me ɔle fiɛ nto losa siwarã lalaa ne, iyɔ nna ɔle iso i mi masiaidze to maki mato masa sɛ̃?
Nnɛ i mi masiaidze to mabara loatã mi ipɔ.
Ɣɛɛ si Ɣaa Siwarã ɔle ame nto losa siwarã lalaa ne, mitsue kukaakɔ sɔ Ɣaa sigara ɔɖewi ɔɔba ɔ̃abo mi ndɛ̃.
“Kuwɛ̃ iibawo ɔturi gɔ mba ɔle iyo ɔbo ɔmala ɔ̃ ara iɖo sɔ ɔ̃aɖe katɔ̃ ɔmɔɛ̃ wũ, ɔnyi wũ tɔtɔ fiɛ ɔ̃abo i ɔ̃ iyo ɔmala ɔ̃ ara.
“Ngɔ loiɣɛ me i kama ne, ɔta ɔɣɛ me iso, fiɛ ngɔ loito ɔsagu me ara kanya ne, ara ɔto ɔsamarã.
Ne ɔso nto loɣere mi sɔ Ɣaa to ɔ̃asu ikpi igbã biara ku inyakpi igbã biara nɛ i maturi ɔɣɛ ɔtsɛ ma, ɣɛɛ ngɔ loaɣɛ inyakpi i Siwarã Bielea iso ne, Ɣaa iibasu ɔtsɛ wũ ɔnya.
Ɔbiara gɔ loaɣɛ inyakpi i mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, iso ne, Ɣaa to ɔ̃asu ɔtsɛ wũ, ɣɛɛ ngɔ loaɣɛ inyakpi i Siwarã Bielea iso ne, Ɣaa iibasu ɔtsɛ, kiniɔ ɣee ɔwi gɔ nto ɔba i katɔ̃ ame.
Kudziri Abi Maasu Manya Kɔ̃ Maɖi Ite.
“Si kudziri lɛ ne, kɔ̃ abi ana sɛ alɛ, ngbɔ ame si kudziri iilɛ ne, kɔ̃ abi ana iisɛ alɛ.
Abi wa i kudziri ɔɣɔ̃ nsɛ iɖi ite kudziri gɔ igbã kuɖe.
Mi ma lonyanyarĩ lɛ maɣɛ!
Nda miabara fiɛ miawo ara sɛɛ ɔɣɛ gɔ miɖe maturi lalaa?
Alasɔ nnɛ loyi ɔturi ɔtu ame i kanya sɛ kaɣɛ.
Ɔturi sɛɛ ne, ara sɛɛ ɔsɛ ɔɖi ɔbɔrɛgu i ɔ̃ ara sɛɛ kakɔlakɔ̃ i ɔ̃ ame fiɛ ɔturi lalaa ana ne, ara lalaa ɔsɛ ɔɖi ɔbɔrɛgu i ɔ̃ ara lalaa kakɔlakɔ̃ ga i ɔ̃ ame.
Nto lotã mi itsue sɔ ɔbiara to ɔ̃atã itsuɛpɛ̃ biara nɛ ɔtua ɔsɛ kere kuso ku atɔ̃me iɣɛyi iso.
Alasɔ fɔ mɔmɔ kanya ame atɔ̃me maasu matã-ɔ ibɛ ɣee ipɔ.” Yesu Ɔsɛ̃ Sɔ Ɔ̃ito Ɔbara Iwawãra Kuiwɛ̃ Ɔte.
Mmara matedze mawɛ̃ gu ma Farisise mawɛ̃ ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ratedze, boto bobie sɔ bara iwawãra irere si bofɔ-ɔ boɖe.” Ne Yesu ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Minyɔ kumɛgɔ i kiniɔgbe maturi ba ɔtile fiɛ maisɛ manigã Ɣaa.
Mato mabie iwawãra sɔ maanya, ɣɛɛ miibanya kuiwɛ̃ iɖo Ɣaa kanyaɖidze Yona ire igbã.
Kumɛgɔ ame i Yona ɔwe i ikpɛ iyiri ame akpɛnɛ atɛ kasɛ̃ aka atɛ ne, ngbɔ ame i Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi ana aawe i karɔ̃ ame akpɛnɛ atɛ kasɛ̃ aka atɛ ne.
I atɔ̃me iɣɛyi ne, Niniwe maturi to maatã mi ipɔ alasɔ mafiniki gɔ Yona ɔɣere ma Ɣaa itɔ̃me.
Ɣɛɛ lobie sɔ mitsue sɔ ngɔ loɖo Yona pia i mi ndɛ̃ ngbe.
Atɔ̃me iɣɛyi ne, Igararɔ̃go gɔ lobɔrɛ i bo karɔ̃ kala isɛ to ɔ̃ata ɔya ɔtã mi kiniɔgbe maturi ipɔ alasɔ ɔsɛ ɔri dzoroo ɔbɔrɛ i kayi iti tsɔra ɔba ɔ̃akã Salomo atɔ̃me wa ame i inɔgba pia atsue.
Ɣɛɛ nto loɣere mi sɔ ngɔ inɔgba loɖo Salomo ire pia i mi ndɛ̃ ngbe.
Siwarã Lalaa Aakpese Siba Siabie Kawekɔ̃.
“Si masa siwarã lalaa maɖi i ɔturi ame ne, sisɛ sikɛlɛ siawe siki sibie kawekɔ̃ i kakorekɔ̃.
Si siina kukakɔi ne, sisɛ siɣere so sɔ, ‘Loakpese lokɛlɛ iyo nɛ ame masa me maɖi.’ Siaba sianya sɔ mmɔ se ikunu, maɔfiɛ iyo ame, maledza ira biara isɛ kukaakɔ.
Iyɔ siakpese sikɛlɛ siakɔ siwarã lalaa aka akɔdzɛ mama dzɛ lonyanyarĩ siɖo sɛ̃ sibua so iso.
Maabo i ngɔmɔ ame mawe, ne ɔso ɔ̃ kawirikɔ̃ to kaanyanyarĩ kaɖo ɔ̃ karɔ̃kasɛkɔ̃.
Ngbɔ tutuutu iase itã nɔme maturi ma lonyanyarĩ ngbe ne.” Mabe Nɖe Yesu Manyii Mɔmɔ?
Ɔwi gɔ i Yesu to ɔɣɛ nwagbe ne, ɔ̃ ɔnyi gu manyiibi ɔba maɣɛ i inyamɔ mato mabie sɔ maɖegu wũ ika.
Ne ɔso mma nɣɛ i mmɔ ɔwɛ̃ ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Nyɔ, fɔ ɔnyi gu manyiibi ɣɛ i inyamɔ mato mabie sɔ manya-ɔ.” Yesu ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Nna nɖe wũ ɔnyi gu manyiibi?” Ne ɔsɔ̃ ɔ̃ marasuãdze kɔrɔ̃ ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Minyɔ wũ ɔnyi gu manyiibi!
Ɔbiara gɔ nsɛ ɔbara Tete gɔ i Kato kuɖɔɛ ne, ɔ̃ nɖe wũ ɔnyiibi rɛrɛ̃ gu ɔnyiiko gu wũ ɔnyi ne.”
Yesu Ɔpɛ Igbã I Ɔraɖuisadze Ɔwɛ̃ Iso.
Iyi nɛmɔ ame ne, Yesu ɔbɔrɛ i iyo ɔsɛ ɔ̃asɛ i ɔpo kanya ɔtsɛ ara ite.
Gɔ mma loki malɔ wũ ɔsi ɔso ne, ɔya ɔbo i ɔkolo ame i ndu iso fiɛ maturi ka maɣɛ i ɔkpokpo.
Ɔte ma ara gbodzoo i agbã ame.
Ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Kpɛ̃dze ɔwɛ̃ ɔsɛ ɔraɖui kasakɔ̃.
Gɔ ɔto ɔsa ne, ɔwɛ̃ ɔɣo i ɔri kuruɛ, ne kurodzai ɔrɛrɛ kuɖe ne.
Ɔwɛ̃ ɔɣo i ata iso ngbegɔ i sise iisi, ne ɔso ɔre mala.
Gɔ kuɣɛ̃ ɔsia kere ne, ɔ̃ ɔɖuɖu ɔkpi alasɔ ɔ̃ siɖu iibo karɔ̃.
Ɔraɖui ɔwɛ̃ ana ɔɣo i kuposɛ̃ ame, ne ɔso gɔ ɔre ne, kuɣa kufu wũ iso.
Ɣɛɛ ɔwɛ̃ ana ɔɣo i karɔ̃ sɛɛ iso, ne ɔso ɔbara kukaakɔ.
Ɔwɛ̃ ɔɣɔ̃ abi kulafa, ɔwɛ̃ abi sikuɔ, ɔwɛ̃ ana abi sitɛ.” Ne Yesu ɔwirigu ma sɔ, “Ngɔ mba atsue si ɔnɔ nnɛ nto loɣɛ.” Nnɛ Ɔso I Yesu Sɛ Ɔte Ara I Agbã Ame.
Ne marasuãdze ɔba maakarɛ Yesu sɔ, “Be ɔso fiɛ asɛ asu agbã ate maturi ara?” Ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Mi ne, Ɣaa ɔɖi ɔ̃ sigarakaɖekɔ̃ awɛrɛra karɔ̃ ɔte mi, ɔ̃iɖi ɔte matsɔra.
Alasɔ ngɔ mba ara ne, maatã wũ ara ɔ̃ ara ɔsi abua, ɣɛɛ ngɔ ina ne, kɛkɛĩ gɔ ame ɔba ne, maamɔɛ̃ mafɔ wũ iso.
Nnɛ ɔso nto lote ma ara i agbã ame nɖe sɔ, mato manya ara, ɣɛɛ maito manya maɖi ite, mato makã atsue, ɣɛɛ maito manɔ fiɛ maaba maanɔ karɔ̃.
Itã sɔ Kanyaɖidze Yesaya itɔ̃me nɛ ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ ɔba i ne ame sɔ, ‘Mmagbe to maanɔ ara, manɔ ara, ɣɛɛ maibanɔ karɔ̃!
Mato maanyɔ ara, manyɔ ara, ɣɛ maibanya maɖi ite.
Alasɔ ma adzuni ɔrɛ sirɛ fiɛ matɛ̃ra atsue sɔ maibanɔ mama anɔmi ana sɔ ma anɔmi iibanya.
Si iiɖe ngbɔ ne, tee maanya ala anɔmi fiɛ ma atsue aanɔ sɔ maanɔ karɔ̃ fiɛ maafiniki maba wũ kɔrɛ fiɛ loasa ma!’ Ɣɛɛ mi ne, iti ɔbua ilɛ mi sɔ mi anɔmi to anya ara fiɛ mi atsue ana to anɔ ara.
Nto loɣere mi sɔ ne, Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze gbodzoo gu maturi bɔlɔlɔa ɔbie teteree sɔ si manya ara wa mito minya, ɣɛɛ mainya, ɣee si manɔ ara wa mito minɔ, ɣɛɛ mainɔ.” Yesu Ɔɖi Ɔraɖuisadze Igbã Karɔ̃.
Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mikã atsue si loɖi ɔraɖuisadze igbã karɔ̃ lote mi.
Ngɔ nto lonɔ Sigarakaɖekɔ̃ iso itɔ̃me fiɛ ɔ̃ito ɔnɔ karɔ̃ se lɛ ɔraɖui gɔ loɣo i ɔri kuruɛ.
Tsirise sɛ ɔba ɔ̃amɔɛ̃ itɔ̃me nɛ ɔnɔ ɔɖi i ɔ̃ ɔtu ame.
Ɔraɖui gɔ loɣo i ata karɔ̃ iso se lɛ ngɔ lonɔ fiɛ ɔfɔ ne ku isoɣɔ ɔluwɛ̃.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ ɔ̃ siɖu iibo karɔ̃ kukaakɔ ɔso ne, si kutsuɛ iɖaa gu kama iti ɔba ala itɔ̃me iti ne, ɔsɛ ɔkpese kama.
Ɔraɖui gɔ loɣo i kuposɛ̃ ame nɖe ngɔ lonɔ itɔ̃me, ɣɛɛ imararãso gu karana itere isiai sɛ iɣa ifu itɔ̃me sɔ ɔ̃isɛ ɔwo abi ɔɣɔ̃.
Ɔraɖui gɔ loɣo i karɔ̃ sɛɛ iso nɖe ngɔ lonɔ itɔ̃me fiɛ ɔnɔ ne karɔ̃.
Ɔsɛ ɔɣɔ̃ abi, mawɛ̃ abi kulafa, mma sikuɔ fiɛ mawɛ̃ ana abi sitɛ.” Yesu Ɔpɛ Igbã I Sikua Iso.
Yesu ɔpɛ ma igbã mama ana ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ se lɛ ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ lopɛ ɔraɖui sɛɛ i ɔ̃ kakpɛkɔ̃ ame.
Kasɛ̃ gɔ maturi ka marɛ ne, ɔ̃ tsirise ɔsɛ ɔ̃asa sikua abi i ɔraɖui ame ɔledza ibɔrɛ malaa.
Ɔwi gɔ i kamɔ ɔmɔ fiɛ kaatsɛ iɣe ne, sikua dzɛ i tsirise ɔsa ana ɔre.
“Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔmɔ maɖabo ɔba maatu wũ maɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Bokɔse, iiɖe kamɔ sɛɛ kaɖe ako i kakpɛkɔ̃ ame?
Lɛ i sikua dzɛgbe ɔse i kamɔ ame?’ “Ne kakpɛkɔ̃ sate to ɔɣere ma sɔ, ‘Tsirise ɔɖe lobara karabara gagbe.’ “Ne maɖabo to makarɛ wũ sɔ, ‘Ato abie sɔ borurui sɛ̃ boɖi?’ “Ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, ‘Ooɣo.
Si misɛ miatsɛ sikua irurui ne, mito miarurui kamɔ ana mibua i sɛ̃ iso.
Mitã sikua gu kamɔ ɔɖuɖu si maya isɛ iabo kamɔ ɔruiwi si loatã marabaradze ɔɖe katɔ̃ maruɛ sikua matsuedza tɔtɔ fiɛ maarui kamɔ masɛ maafere i kawu ame.’ ” Yesu Ɔsu Ɣaa Sigarakaɖekɔ̃ Ɔkateragu Idziribi Kosoi Iwɛ̃.
Yesu Ɔledza ma igbã mama ipɛ iɣere ma sɔ, “Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ se lɛ idziribi kosoi iwɛ̃ nɛ i ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɔsu ɔsɛ ɔ̃apɛ i ɔ̃ ayo ame kakpɛkɔ̃ ame.
Idziribi nɛgbe ɔkoso iɖo atsɔra ɔɖuɖu, ɣɛɛ si imɔ ne, isɛ imɔ iɖo ayo ame kakpɛkɔ̃ ame siraɖui ɔɖuɖu ikpese kadzirimi ga akpa ame i kurodzai aabara ayo kuwe.” Yesu Ɔpɛ Igbã I Inyagɛ̃ Kua Iso.
Yesu ɔledza ma igbã ipɛ iɣɛ sɔ, “Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ se lɛ inyagɛ̃ kua gɔ i ɔrɔ̃go ɔwɛ̃ ɔsu ɔpia i mmɔre mɛ losi ame, ɔkpɔkɔtɔ ɔsakanya gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ mmɔre ɔɖuɖu ɔnyagɛ̃.” Nnɛ Ɔso I Yesu Ɔte Ara I Agbã Ame.
Yesu ɔki i agbã ame ɔte iturikuri nɛgbe ara wagbe ɔɖuɖu.
Ɔ̃isɛ ɔɖe ma ika si iiɖe igbã ɔto ɔpɛ ma.
Ɔbara ngbɔ gɔ itã sɔ nnɛ i Ɣaa kanyaɖidze ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ ɔba i ne ame sɔ, “Loaɖe ma ika i igbã ame.
Fiɛ loaɖi ara wɛrɛa wa mpia ita i kayi karɔ̃kasɛkɔ̃ lote ma.” Yesu Ɔɖi Igbã Nɛ Ɔpɛ I Sikua Iso Karɔ̃.
Gɔ Yesu ɔɔɖi iturikuri nɛmɔ ɔri fiɛ ɔba iyo ne, ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔba ɔ̃ kɔrɛ maba maaɣere wũ sɔ, “Ɖi igbã nɛ apɛ i sikua dzɛ mpia i ɔraɖui ame mmɔ karɔ̃ tã bo.” Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ngɔ nto ɔpɛ ɔraɖui nɖe mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi.
Kakpɛkɔ̃ nɖe kayiiso.
Mma nɖe Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ maturi nɖe ɔraɖui gɔ mapɛ i kakpɛkɔ̃ ame.
Tsirise masiaidze nɖe sikua.
Tsirise gɔ losa sikua nɖe Ɔbosam.
Ɔraɖui ɔsɔrɛ̃wi nɖe kayi kawirikɔ̃, fiɛ mma loasɔrɛ̃ ɔraɖui nɖe Ɣaa makpabo.
“Kumɛgɔ masa sikua kanya fiɛ matsuedza sɛ̃ ne, ngbɔ ame iase ku kayi kawirikɔ̃ ne.
Mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, to loapia wũ makpabo sɔ masa mma ɔɖuɖu lokɔ maturi mapia i ikpi ame gu mma lobara ara lalaa kanya.
Mato maasu ma mafuĩdza mapia i itɔkpe nɛ nto itsue ame ngbegɔ maabiɛ kaku maɖo arɔĩ makpa.
Ɣɛɛ Ɣaa maturi to maafiɛ lɛ kuɣɛ̃ i ma Ɔse sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ame.
Ngɔ mba atsue si ɔnɔ nnɛ nto loɣɛ!
Yesu Ɔpɛ Igbã I Karana Ga Makɔla Iso.
“Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ se lɛ karana ga makɔla i kakpɛkɔ̃ ame fiɛ ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɔnya ɔsu ɔledza isu ikɔla.
Ɔna isoɣɔ gbaã, ne ɔso ɔsɛ ɔ̃asu ɔ̃ ira biara ɔrɔdɛ̃ ɔsu sikã ɔsɛ ɔ̃aɣa kakpɛkɔ̃ gamɔ.” Yesu Ɔpɛ Igbã I Kunyi Gɔ Lofɔ Kuɣa Iso.
Yesu ɔɣere ma ana sɔ, “Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ se lɛ kuɣaɖese ɔwɛ̃ gɔ nto ɔbie anyi wa lofɔ kuɣa.
Gɔ ɔsɛ ɔ̃anya kuwɛ̃ gɔ lobua kufɔ kuɣa ne, ɔsɛ ɔ̃asu ɔ̃ ira biara nɛ ɔba ɔrɔdɛ̃ ɔsu sikã ɔsɛ ɔ̃aɣa kɔ̃.
Yesu Ɔpɛ Igbã I Asabu Wa Mapia Iso.
“Ana ne, Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ɔre asabu wa mapia i ɔpo ame fiɛ maɖi akpɛ agbãagbã.
Gɔ asabu ɔyi ne, makpadzɛ̃ wã mabɔ ɔkpokpo fiɛ marɛrɛ akpɛ ame, maɖi nwa masɛ maɖe mafere i kusɛsɛi ame.
Nwa maiɖe ana ne, mabodza wã mawiri.
Ngbɔ ame iase ku kayi kawirikɔ̃ ne.
Ɣaa makpabo to maabɔrɛ makɛlɛ maarɛrɛ maturi sɛɛ maɖi i malalaa ndɛ̃.
Mato maasu maturi lalaa mafuĩdza mapia i itɔkpe ame ngbegɔ maabiɛ kaku maɖo arɔĩ makpa.” Yesu Ɔte Ara I Ɔnukuare Atɔ̃me Kuere Gu Aɣɛtɛ Iso.
Yesu ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Minɔ ara wa loɣere mi i ngbe karɔ̃?” Matã mmuai sɔ, “Aĩ, bonɔ.” Ne ɔɣere ma ana sɔ, “Mmaratedze biara gɔ lokpese Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ rasuãdze ne, ɔse lɛ iyosate gɔ nsɛ ɔɖi ara kuere gu aɣɛtɛ ɔbɔrɛgu i ɔ̃ iyo ame ɔte.” Ma Nasaretse Ɔsɛ̃ Yesu.
Gɔ Yesu ɔpɛ agbã wagbe ɔro ne, ɔrui i mmɔ.
Ɔkpese ɔkɛlɛ ma aɖe fiɛ ɔsɛ ɔ̃ate ara i ma kasarɛkɔ̃ gɔ ibara mma lonɔ ɔ̃ atɔ̃me ɣaa mato makarɛ sɔ, “Lɛ i ngɔgbe ɔsuã inɔgba nɛgbe ɔbɔrɛgu?
Fiɛ lɛ ɔbɔrɛgu awawãra wagbe igbã?
Iiɖe rawedze ɔbi ɔɖe ngbe ɣɛɛ?
Iiɖe Maria ɔbi ɔɖe fiɛ ɔ̃ manyiibi nɖe Yakobo gu Yosef gu Simon gu Yuda ma mpia i bo ndɛ̃?
Ɔ̃ manyiiko ana pia i bo ndɛ̃ ni!
Lɛ kowũ ɔna ara wagbe ɔɖuɖu ɔbɔrɛgu?” Ɔ̃ ara ɔtsue ma anɔ, ne ɔso maifɔ wũ.
Ne ɔso ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ɣaa kanyaɖidze ba kuwarɛ i kakɔi biara iɖo ɔ̃ mɔmɔ ɔmagɛ̃ gu ɔ̃ maturi kɔrɛ.” Gɔ maifɔ wũ maɖe ɔso ne, ɔ̃iwo awawãra gbodzoo ɔbara i ma ndɛ̃.
Herodes Ɔtã Maɖoe Ndupiedze Yohanes.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ne, Herodes gɔ nto ɔɖe sigara i Galilea ɔnɔ Yesu iso itɔ̃me.
Ne ɔto ɔɣere ɔ̃ marabaradze sɔ, “Ndupiedze Yohanes loɔta ɔbɔrɛ i makpise ame ɔpia ngbã!
Ne ɔso ɔba ɔle ɔto ɔbara awawãra ɔbara ngbɔ ne.” Tɔtɔ ne, Herodes ɔtã mamɔɛ̃ Yohanes manyi wũ marara i iyo.
Ɔbara ngbɔ ala Herodia gɔ nɖe ɔ̃ ɔnyiibi Filipo ɔre ɔso.
Alasɔ Yohanes ɔɣere Herodes sɔ, “Mmara iitã ɔri sɔ aayiri fɔ ɔnyiibi ɔre Herodia.” Ne ɔso Herodes ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃aɖoe wũ, ɣɛɛ ɔnigã ma Yudase alasɔ masɛ mabu Yohanes lɛ Ɣaa kanyaɖidze.
Iyi nɛ i Herodes ɔɖe ɔ̃ iɣeyi ne, Herodia ɔbi bitɛ ɔba ɔ̃atɔ ɔte maturi ma loba mmɔ gɔ ibua ipia Herodes isoɣɔ.
Ne ɔkã ndamu ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Loatã-ɔ ira biara nɛ aakarɛ me.” Ɔbirɔ̃gomi ɔnyi ɔɣere wũ sɔ ɔkarɛ Ndupiedze Yohanes iti.
Ne ɔso ɔsɛ ɔ̃aɣere igara sɔ, “Tã me Ndupiedze Yohanes iti i kategelei iso ngbe kiniɔ.” Itɔ̃me nɛgbe ɔbo Herodes so, ɣɛɛ kumɛgɔ ɔkã ndamu i makpakpa ma nsigu wũ i ɔpɔrɔ̃ iti katɔ̃ ɔso ne, ɔpia sɔ masɛ maatu Yohanes iti mabɔ ɔbirɔ̃gomi.
Ne ɔso ɔpia masɛ maatu Yohanes iti i ngbegɔ ɔrɛ i iyo.
Masu ituriti masia i kategelei iso masu mabɔ ɔbirɔ̃gomi fiɛ ka ɔsu ɔkɛlɛgu ɔ̃ ɔnyi.
Gɔ Yohanes marasuãdze ɔnɔ ne, masɛ maasu wũ masɛ maabiara fiɛ ka masɛ maaɣere Yesu.
Yesu Ɔtã Maturi Gbodzoo Aɖera Maɖe.
Gɔ Yesu ɔnɔ nnɛ loba Yohanes iso ne, ɔbo i ɔkolo ame ɔwara ɔkɛlɛ ngbegɔ i maturi na.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ maturi gbodzoo ɔtsue ne, masɛ ngba mabɔrɛ i ma simagɛ̃ ame makɛlɛ ɔ̃ kɔrɛ.
Gɔ Yesu ɔso ɔbɔrɛ i ɔkolo ame fiɛ ɔnya maturi gbodzoo ma loba ne, ma ara ɔɖo wũ kayiri fiɛ ɔsa mma nto manyɛ.
Yesu Ɔtã Maturi Gbodzoo Aɖera Maɖe.
Kutsuɛ ɔwi ne ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔbore mabo wũ maɣere wũ sɔ, “Kaɖe ɔɔro, fiɛ ngbe ɔdzorogu ayo ame ne ɔso ɖi ma ɔri si makɛlɛ ngorowase maabie aɖera maɣa maɖe.” Yesu ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Iinya sɔ maakɛlɛ ne mi mɔmɔ mitã ma irere maɖe.” Ne marasuãdze ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Abolo abo aru gu akpɛ fɛ̃a anyɔ kere nɖe aɖera wa boba.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Misu mibɔ me i ngbe.” Ɔɣere maturi sɔ masɛ i karɔ̃ i sikua iso fiɛ ka ɔsu abolo abo aru gu akpɛ fɛ̃a anyɔ, ɔnyɔ kato ɔpɛ Ɣaa siba.
Ɔbɛbɛse ɔsu ɔtã ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ masu maɣɛɣɛ maturi.
Gɔ ma ɔɖuɖu ɔɖe ara mami fiɛ marasuãdze ɔsa nwa lobuburi kanya ne, ayi kusɛsɛi kuweo-kunyɔ.
Mma loɖe aɖera wamɔ aaɖe lɛ marɛrɛ̃ kukpi kuru gɔ maika marɔ̃go gu mabiɛtɛ.
Yesu Ɔsɛ I Galilea Itubu Iso.
Ɔluwɛ̃ Yesu ɔtã ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔya mabo i ɔkolo ame sɔ mawara makɛlɛ si ɔ̃ wũ ɔɖi maturi tsɔra ɔri.
Gɔ ɔ̃ɔɖi ma ɔri ɔro ne, ɔya ɔkɛlɛ kabemi iso ɔsɛ ɔ̃akparama kayi.
Si iabara kutsuɛ buɛɛ ne, Yesu ɔnɔwɛ̃ loɔkuti ɔɣɛ i mmɔ.
Ɔwi gɔgbe ame ne, ɔkolo ka ɔsia i itubu ndɛ̃, awɛ to akpɛ̃ fiɛ ndu to misɛgu ɔkolo mikpesegu.
Ɔɖesɛrã ne, Yesu ɔsɛ i ndu iso ɔba ɔ̃atu ɔ̃ marasuãdze.
Gɔ manya wũ ɔsɛ i ndu iso ne, ɔtu ɔkpa ma maɣɛ sɔ, “Kpise ɔɖe!” Mala kulu i ifɔ̃ ame.
Ɣɛɛ ɔluwɛ̃ ne, Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mina ɔtu!
Midaanigã.
Mme loɖe!” Ne Petro ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Bosate, si fɔ mɔmɔ aɖe ne, kpere me sɔ losɛ i ndu iso loba fɔ kɔrɛ.” Yesu ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Ba!” Ne ɔso Petro ɔso ɔbɔrɛ i ɔkolo ame ɔtsɛ isɛ i ndu iso ikɛlɛ Yesu kɔrɛ.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ ɔnya kumɛgɔ i ɔwiri to ɔkpɛ̃ teteree ne, ɔnigã ɔtsɛ ndu iwã.
Ne ɔla kulu teteree sɔ, “Bosate, ɖi me!” Ɔluwɛ̃ Yesu ɔɖi kɔrɔ̃ ɔmɔɛ̃ wũ ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Fɔ kafɔkaɖe ɔtɛgɛlɛ, be ɔso fiɛ ato awararã?” Ma inyɔɔ ɔya mabo i ɔkolo ame kere ne ɔwiri ɔnyua ɔkpɛ̃ ne.
Ne ɔso marasuãdze ma i ɔkolo ame ɔpɛ agɛgɛ̃ matã Yesu maɣɛ sɔ, “Gbaã ne, Ɣaa Ɔbi aɖe!” Yesu Ɔsa Manyɛse I Genezaret.
Gɔ mawara itubu ne, maba maabo ɔkpokpo gɔ i Genezaret karɔ̃ iso.
Maturi ɔnya Yesu maɖi ite, ne ɔso masɛ maakɔ manyɛse ma ɔɖuɖu mpia i abuiti wamɔ ame ɔɖuɖu mabɔ wũ.
Mapɛ wũ nrɔɔ̃ sɔ ɔtã manyɛse si mapɛgu bidɛ ɔ̃ awu kutsueti.
Mma ɔɖuɖu lopɛgu wũ ɔna isosarɛ.
Midaasɛ̃ Ɣaa Ala Mi Kubarara Ɔso.
Ma Farisise mawɛ̃ gu ma Yudase mmara matedze mawɛ̃ ɔbɔrɛ i Yerusalem maba Yesu kɔrɛ makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Be ɔso fiɛ fɔ marasuãdze iisɛ mabara i bo mawa kubarara iso?
Masɛ̃ maisɛ mafore nrɔɔ̃ i bo mmara kanya fiɛ masɛ maɖe aɖera.” Ne Yesu ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Mi wũ ne, be ɔso fiɛ miisɛ mibara i Ɣaa mmara iso fiɛ mi mawa mire iso misɛ mibara?
Ɣaa sɔ, ‘Warɛ fɔ ɔse gu fɔ ɔnyi.
Si ɔrere ɔɣɛ inyakpi i ɔ̃ ɣese iso ne, ɔkote ɔtã kukpi ipɔ.’ Ɣɛɛ mi wũ mito mite sɔ si ɔrere ba ira nɛ ikote sɔ ɔ̃asu ɔbuai ɔ̃ maɣese fiɛ ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Nnɛ loasu lotã-ɔ loɔsu lotã Ɣaa.’ ne, iisinya sɔ ɔturi aawarɛ ɔ̃ ɔse ɣee ɔ̃ ɔnyi.
Ne ɔso iki i mi kurabarara iso ne, miɔsɛ̃ Ɣaa mmara, mimɔɛ̃ mi mawa mire mito.
Mi ma nsɛ mibara ara sɔ si mibo maturi anɔ!
Ɣaa Kanyaɖidze Yesaya ɔkpɛ ɔya gɔ ɔɣɛ i mi iso sɔ, ‘Mmagbe ne, kanyakanya kere masu mato male me gɔ iibɔrɛ i ma situ ame.
Siefe kere mato mabara wũ karabara.
Mato mate maturi mmara i wũ mire kanya.’ ” Ara Wa Lobɔrɛ I Ɔtu Ame Nsɛ Aɣɛra Ɔturi.
Ne Yesu ɔkpere maturi gbodzoo ɔbɔ so i kɔrɛ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mikã atsue si minɔ ara karɔ̃.
Nnɛ i ɔturi ɔɖe iibawo wũ ɔpukutura, ɣɛɛ nnɛ nsɛ ibɔrɛ i ɔturi kanya ame nsɛ ipukutura wũ.” Ne ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔbore mabo wũ maɣere wũ sɔ, “Aɣe sɔ nnɛ aɣɛ mmɔ ɔta iya ma Farisise iso?” Yesu ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Kudziri biara gɔ iiɖe Tete gɔ i kato lopia ne, maarui kɔ̃ mapɛyu.
Ne ɔso minyua ma.
Manɔbiɛdze maɖe fiɛ mato makɔ manɔbiɛdze.
Si nɔbiɛdze to ɔkɔ nɔbiɛdze ne, iwo ame i ma inyɔɔ aakpase mabo.” Petro ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ɖi aɖera ɔturi iɣɛra igbã nɛmɔ karɔ̃ te bo.” Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Miinɔ itɔ̃me nɛ ana karɔ̃?
Minɔ karɔ̃ sɔ ira biara nɛ nsɛ ibo i ɔturi kanya ame ne, isɛ ikɛlɛ ɔ̃ iyiri ame, kama ne, ɔ̃anyi ne ɔpɛyu lɛ ɔdziriiso awe.
Ɣɛɛ atɔ̃me wa nsɛ abɔrɛ i ɔturi kanya ame ne, ɔ̃ ɔtu ame abɔrɛ fiɛ asɛ apukutura wũ.
Alasɔ ɔturi ɔtu ame i adzuni nyanyarĩa wa nsɛgu ituriɖoe, maturire isiai gu marã irɔ, asɔrɔ̃ iɖe, kayu, mila aɖansiɛ iɖe, anyakpi iɣɛ i maturi iso sɛ ibɔrɛ.
Nwagbe nsɛ aɣɛra ɔturi ne.
Iiɖe nrɔɔ̃ mɛ maifore fiɛ maɖe ara nsɛ iɣɛra ɔturi.” Yesu Ɔsa Ɔrɔ̃go Ɔwɛ̃ Ɔbi Birɔ̃gomi.
Yesu ɔbɔrɛ i mmɔ ɔkɛlɛ Tiro gu Sidon awo ame.
Mmɔ i ɔ Kananse rɔ̃go ɔwɛ̃ gɔ lobɔrɛ ndɛ̃ mɛmɔ ɔba Yesu kɔrɛ ku kulu teteree ɔba ɔ̃atã wũ iti sɔ, “Wũ Sate David ɔwa, nyɔ me nnya!
Wũ ɔbi birɔ̃gomi to ɔwe inyɛ gbaã i siwarã lalaa nrɔɔ̃ ame.” Ɣɛɛ Yesu iiɣɛ kuira.
Ne ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔba maaɣere wũ sɔ, “Sa wũ si ɔnyua kulu ɔla ɔtɛ̃ra bo atsue!” Mmɔ i Yesu ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Israel maturi ma nse lɛ masɛrɛ ma loyu kɔrɛ kere i Ɣaa ɔpia me.” Ɣɛɛ ne, ɔrɔ̃go gɔmɔ ɔba ɔ̃apɛ agɛgɛ̃ i ɔ̃ katɔ̃ ɔtã wũ iti sɔ, “Wũ Sate, buai me!” Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Iilɛ sɔ maasu mabiɛtɛ aɖera matã makpɛkpɛ.” Ɔrɔ̃go ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Wũ Sate gbaã iɖe, ɣɛɛ makpɛkpɛ sɛ marɛrɛ aɖera wa lokpakpase i makɔse ɔpɔrɔ̃ iso afere i karɔ̃ maɖe.” Gɔ Yesu ɔnɔ atɔ̃me wagbe ne, ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ɔrɔ̃go, fɔ kafɔkaɖe ɔmɔ gbaã!
Nnɛ ato akarɛ si iba itã-ɔ.” Ɔluwɛ̃ ɔbi birɔ̃gomi ko losarɛ.
Yesu Ɔsa Maturi Gbodzoo.
Yesu ɔrui i mmɔ ɔsɛ Galilea itubu kuruɛkuruɛ ɔsɛ ɔ̃aya kabemi kawɛ̃ ɔkpase ɔsɛ i karɔ̃.
Maturi gbodzoo ɔba ɔ̃ kɔrɛ.
Gɔ mato maba ne, masɛgu mma lofɛfɛ̃ mafu, manɔbiɛdze, mabafã, mamumu gu manyɛse agbãagbã.
Makɔ ma mabɔ Yesu katɔ̃.
Gɔ maturi ɔnya sɔ mamumu to maɖe aka, mabafã ɔta masɛ, mma lofɛfɛ̃ mafu ɔna ɔle fiɛ manɔbiɛdze to manya ara ne, male Israel Ɣaa.
Yesu Ɔtã Maturi Gbodzoo Aɖera Maɖe.
Yesu ɔkpere ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔbɔ so i kɔrɛ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mmagbe ara to akpɛ̃ me nnya, alasɔ maɔwe i wũ kɔrɛ akpɛnɛ atɛ fiɛ mana kuira nɛ maaɖe.
Loito lobie sɔ makɛlɛ ayo ku kukã, si iiɖe ngbɔ ne, mato maasɛ maafɛ̃ i ɔri.” Ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Fafuĩ gɔgbe ame ne, lɛ boana aɖera botã maturi gbodzoo magbe ɔɖuɖu fiɛ maaɖe mami?” Yesu ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Abolo kuboi kurɛ̃ mito?” Ne matã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Abolo kuboi kukɔdzɛ gu kufarai wiriwiria kurɛ̃saã.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere maturi ɔɖuɖu sɔ masɛ i karɔ̃ ne.
Ɔsu abolo kuboi kukɔdzɛ gu kufarai ne ɔpɛ Ɣaa siba i wã iti ne.
Ɔbɛbɛse ɔsu ɔtã ɔ̃ marasuãdze fiɛ masu maɣɛɣɛ maturi.
Ma ɔɖuɖu ɔɖe ara mami, ne gɔ marasuãdze ɔsa akutia kanya ne, mana kusɛsɛi kukɔdzɛ.
Marɛrɛ̃ kerekere kukpi kuna loɖe aɖera gɔ maika marɔ̃go gu mabiɛtɛ.
Yesu ɔɖi maturi ɔri fiɛ ɔ̃ wũ ka ɔya ɔbo i ɔkolo ame ɔwara ɔkɛlɛ Magadan karɔ̃ iso.
Ma Farisise Mawɛ̃ Gu Ma Zadukise Ɔkarɛ Yesu Sɔ Ɔbara Iwawãra Irere Ɔte Ma.
Ma Farisise gu ma Zadukise mawɛ̃ ɔba Yesu kɔrɛ maba maala wũ manyɔ sɔ ɔbara iwawãra ɔte sɔ Ɣaa kɔrɛ ɔbɔrɛ.
Ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Si kuɣɛ̃ to kusɛ kuabo iyo fiɛ kuɖokpo ɔrɛtɛ ne, misɛ miɣɛ sɔ, ‘Kayi to kaakpa kɔrãkaɖe.’ Ngbɔ ame si mita ku kaya fiɛ kuɖokpo ɔrɛtɛ, kayi ɔnyɔ guduu ne, misɛ miɣɛ sɔ, ‘Kado to ɔ̃apɛ nɔme.’ Misɛ miwo kuɖokpo ɔnyɔ ɔɣɛ kumɛgɔ i kayi aase ɣɛɛ miito miwo ɔwi gɔ ame mipia ɔnya ɔɖi ite!
Kiniɔgbe maturi ma mba ɔtile fiɛ maisɛ manigã Ɣaa, mato mabie awawãra sɔ maanya, ɣɛɛ maibanya kuiwɛ̃ iɖo Ɣaa kanyaɖidze Yona ire igbã.” Gɔ ɔɣere ma ngbɔ ne, ɔrui ɔnyua ma.
Yesu Ɔka Ɔ̃ Marasuãdze I Ma Farisise Gu Ma Zadukise Ara Ite Iso.
Gɔ marasuãdze ɔwara itubu makɛlɛ kama isɛ ne, maɣara maito abolo kuawɛ̃.
Ne Yesu to ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Midzuɛ̃ so i ma Farisise gu ma Zadukise inyagɛ̃ kua iso.” Ne matsɛ so ikarɛ sɔ, “Kumɛgɔ boito abolo ɔso fiɛ ɔto ɔɣere bo ngbɔ?” Ɣɛɛ Yesu ɣe nnɛ mato maɣɛ, ne ɔso ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Be ɔso fiɛ mito mikarɛ so atɔ̃me i aɖera wa miito iso?
Mi kafɔkaɖe ɔtɛgɛlɛ gbaã.
Miito minya ara miɖi ite?
Miito minyigi ɔwi gɔ losu abolo aru lotã marɛrɛ̃ kukpi kuru ɔɖe?
Kusɛsɛi kurɛ̃ i akutia ɔyi?
Fiɛ ɔwi gɔ i maturi kukpi kuna ɔɖe abolo kuboi kukɔdzɛ ne, kusɛsɛi kurɛ̃ i akutia ɔyi?
Nda ɔso fiɛ miito minɔ karɔ̃ sɔ iiɖe abolo iso loto loɖe ika?
Midzuɛ̃ so i ma Farisise gu ma Zadukise inyagɛ̃ kua iso!” Mmɔ ikpa marasuãdze sɔ iiɖe inyagɛ̃ kua gɔ masɛ masu mabara abolo iso ɔto ɔɖe ika ne, ma Farisise gu ma Zadukise ara ite ɔto.
Petro Ɔɖi Ɔte Sɔ Yesu Nɖe Kristo.
Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔkɛlɛ Kaisarea Filipi ɔmagɛ̃ kɔrɛ.
Mmɔ iɖe ɔkarɛ ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Nna i maturi sɛ maɣɛ sɔ mme Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi ɖe?” Matã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Mawɛ̃ sɔ Ndupiedze Yohanes, mawɛ̃ ana sɔ Eliya, fiɛ mawɛ̃ ana sɔ Yeremia ɣee Ɣaa kanyaɖidze ɔ aɖe.” Mmɔ i Yesu to ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Ne mi ɣɛɛ?
Nna mibu sɔ loɖe?” Simon Petro ɔtara kanya sɔ, “Fɔ nɖe Kristo gɔmɔ, Ɣaa gɔ mba ngbã Ɔbi.” Ne Yesu ɔɣɛ sɔ, “So si siɣɔ-ɔ Simon, Yona ɔbi, alasɔ iiɖe ɔturi awune loɖi ɔnukuare gɔgbe ɔte-ɔ, ɣɛɛ wũ Ɔse gɔ i kato ɔɖe.
Ne ɔso nto loɣere-ɔ sɔ fɔ nɖe Petro, gɔ karɔ̃ nɖe ita siare, fiɛ ita siare nɛgbe iso loatsue wũ mafɔɖedze ikuri losia gɔ kukpi kɔra iibawo ma iso ɔɖe.
Fiɛ nto loasu Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ sibɔi lotã-ɔ sɔ nnɛ asɛ̃ i karɔ̃ iso ne, maasɛ̃ ne i kato fiɛ nnɛ asese i karɔ̃ iso ne, maasese ne i kato.” Ne Yesu ka ɔsɛ̃ ɔtã ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ madaaɣere kuwɛ̃ sɔ ɔ̃ nɖe Kristo ne.
Yesu Ɔɖe Ika I Ɔ̃ Inyɛwe Gu Kukpi Iso.
Ita i ɔwi gɔmɔ ne, Yesu ɔtsɛ ɔ̃ marasuãdze iɣere iɖi sɔ, “Nto loakɛlɛ Yerusalem fiɛ loawe inyɛ gbaã i makpakpa, masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu mmara matedze nrɔɔ̃ ame.
Mato maaɖoe me, ɣɛɛ ikpɛnɛ tɛare ne, Ɣaa to ɔ̃atara me lowe ngbã.” Petro ɔkɔ wũ ɔɣedza i kuruɛ ɔtã wũ itai ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Kuiyikuiyi daasiɣɛ itɔ̃me nɛgbe!
Iibaba-ɔ iso ngbɔ!” Yesu ɔfiniki ɔɣere Petro sɔ, “Re me kama, Satana!
Ato abie sɔ akpesera so ɔri itɛ̃ra atã me alasɔ adzuni wagbe iibɔrɛ i Ɣaa kɔrɛ, ɣɛɛ ɔturi kɔrɛ abɔrɛ.” Ne Yesu to ɔɣere ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Si mi ɔrere ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃asiai me ne, ɔsɛ̃ so si ɔsu ɔ̃ inyɛwe ɔnyigbã si ɔ̃awo me ɔsiai.
Alasɔ ɔbiara gɔ loakpɛ̃ i ɔ̃ ngbã iti ne, ɔto ɔ̃ayura me, ɣɛɛ ngɔ loayura ɔ̃ ngbã ala wũ ɔso ne, ɔto ɔ̃ana ngbã.
Mme kusia i ɔturi aana si kayiiso ɔɖuɖu karana ɔkpese ɔ̃ kare fiɛ ɔ̃ayura ɔ̃ mɔmɔ ngbã?
Ɣee ira iwɛ̃ pia gɔ ɔturi aasu ɔnyuarã ala ɔ̃ ngbã?
Alasɔ Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi to ɔ̃aba i ɔ̃ Ɔse ikpawaĩ ame gu ɔ̃ makpabo fiɛ ɔ̃atã ɔbiara kuso i ɔ̃ karabara kanya.
Nto loɣere mi gbaã sɔ mi ndɛ̃ mawɛ̃ i ngbe iibakpi fiɛ maanya Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi to ɔba lɛ Igara awe.”
Ɣaa Ɔte Yesu Ikpawaĩ.
Ayi akuɔ kama ne, Yesu ɔkɔ Petro gu Yakobo gu Yohanes makɛlɛ kube kɔlɛa kuwɛ̃ iso ma ɔnɔwɛ̃.
Gɔ mato manyɔ kere ne, Yesu kumiamia ɔkpaki, ɔ̃ katɔ̃ to kafiɛ lɛ kuɣɛ̃, fiɛ ɔ̃ arapia ana to afiɛ atsue anɔmi.
Ne marasuãdze itɛ magbe ɔnya Mose gu Eliya to maɖegu Yesu ika ne.
Ne Petro ɔɣere Yesu sɔ, “Bosate, bo ngbe iba ɔbua ilɛ gbaã!
Si abie ne, tã bopɛ akpayo atɛ i ngbe.
Iwɛ̃ itã-ɔ, iwɛ̃ itã Mose fiɛ iwɛ̃ ana itã Eliya.” Gɔ ɔtogu ika iɖe ne, idɔdɔ fiɛa iwɛ̃ ɔso iba iafu ma iso fiɛ silɔ siwɛ̃ ɔɖe ika sibɔrɛgu i idɔdɔ ame siɣɛ sɔ, “Wũ Ɔbi mɔmɔ gɔ loipia kuɣɛ i ngbe ne, mikã wũ atsue.” Gɔ marasuãdze ɔnɔ silɔ dzɛgbe ne, ifɔ̃ ɔmɔɛ̃ ma sɔ makɔlɛ mafu i karɔ̃.
Yesu ɔba ma kɔrɛ, ɔpɛgu ma ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mita miya ne midaanigã.” Gɔ matara anɔ kato ne, mainya kuwɛ̃ i mmɔ, iɖo Yesu ɔnɔwɛ̃.
Gɔ maso i kube iso mato maba ne, Yesu ɔsi ma mmara sɔ, “Midaaɣere kuwɛ̃ kaɖikate ga maɖi mate mi i ngbe gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi ɔɔta ɔbɔrɛ i makpise ame.” Ne marasuãdze to makarɛ Yesu sɔ, “Be ɔso fiɛ mmara matedze sɛ maɣɛ sɔ Eliya aaɖe katɔ̃ ɔba tɔtɔ?” Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Gbaã iɖe sɔ Eliya aaɖe katɔ̃ ɔba ɔ̃aledza ira biara ɔsɛ.
Ɣɛɛ ne, nto loɣere mi sɔ Eliya ɔɔba koko, maturi iinya wũ maɖi ite.
Mabara wũ nnɛ mabie fiɛ ngbɔ ame mato maabara Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi ɔtile ana ne.” Mmɔ i marasuãdze ɔtsue sɔ Ndupiedze Yohanes ɔto ɔɣɛ ala ne.
Yesu Ɔsa Ɔbirɛrɛĩ Ɔwɛ̃ Gɔ I Siwarã Lalaa Si Iso.
Gɔ makpese maba iturikuri kɔrɛ ne, ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɔba ɔ̃apɛ agɛgɛ̃ i Yesu kɔrɛ.
Ne ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Bosate, nyɔ wũ ɔbi nnya!
Kakpebubu ɔnyɛ to ɔɖaa wũ gɔ isɛ inyɛdɛ̃ wũ teteree itã ɔpɛ ɔbo i ɔtɔ ɣee ndu ame.
Lokɔ wũ lobɔ fɔ marasuãdze sɔ masa wũ ɣɛɛ maiwo.” Ne Yesu ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Mi kiniɔgbe maturi ma loifɔ maɖe fiɛ manyanyarĩ, ayi sirɛ̃ loawe i mi kɔrɛ isɛ iabo?
Kɔ ɔbi bɔ me i ngbe!” Yesu ɔtɔ̃me ɔpia siwarã fiɛ sibɔrɛ i ɔbi ame.
Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, ɔbi ɔsarɛ.
Ne marasuãdze ɔbore mabo wũ makarɛ wũ pɔkɔsɔɔ sɔ, “Be ɔso fiɛ boiwo siwarã lalaa ɔsa ɔɖi?” Yesu ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Mi kafɔkaɖe ɔfe ikoso ɔso.
Gbaã nto loɣere mi sɔ si mi kafɔkaɖe ɔmɔ lɛ susuruba ibi ne, miaɣere kabemi gagbe sɔ, ‘Rui i ngbe kɛlɛ mmɔ,’ fiɛ iaba ngbɔ ana.
Kuira ibara iibaɖo mi!
Ɣɛɛ si iiɖe kanya inyi gu kayi ikparama ame ne, aibawo siwarã dzɛgbe igbã ɔsa.” Yesu Ɔɖe Ika I Ɔ̃ Kukpi Iso Ana.
Gɔ marasuãdze ɔɖuɖu ɔba maasakanya i Galilea ne, Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mato maba maaɖi mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, matã maturi, maɖoe, ɣɛɛ ikpɛnɛ tɛare ne, loto loaledza ita ibɔrɛ i makpise ame.” Itɔ̃me nɛgbe ɔɖaa marasuãdze gbaã.
Ɣaa Isɔrɛyo Toto Itã.
Gɔ Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔba Kapernaum ne, mma nsɛ mafɔ kasɔrɛkɔ̃ toto ɔba maakarɛ Petro sɔ, “Mi ratedze ne, ɔsɛ ɔtã kasɔrɛkɔ̃ toto?” Ne Petro ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Ɔsɛ ɔtã!” Gɔ Petro ɔsɛ ɔ̃abo iyo ne, Yesu loɖe katɔ̃ ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Simon, be nɖe fɔ adzuni i nnɛ nto loba lokarɛ-ɔ iso?
Kayiiso magara lampo ne, mabe nsɛ matã?
Karɔ̃ ga iso i igara to ɔɖe maturi ɛɛbɛrɛ mafɔ ma mpia i karɔ̃ gamɔ iso?” Ne Petro ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Mafɔ.” Yesu ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Ne karɔ̃ nɖe sɔ karɔ̃ gamɔ iso maturi iisɛ matã lampo gɔmɔ ne.
Ɣɛɛ si boibata boya i mmagbe iso ne, kɛlɛ itubu kanya si apia ɖaɖiwa.
Ikpɛ ɖeakatɔ̃ nɛ aaɖi ne, pia kɔrɔ̃ i ne kanya ame ne ato aanya sikã dzɛ loawo atã bo gu-ɔ isɔrɛyo lampo si asu atã ma.”
Yesu Ɔte Ɔturi Gɔ Loɖo Pelepele.
Ɔwi kama ne, marasuãdze ɔba Yesu kɔrɛ makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Nna ɔɖe loɖo i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃?” Ne Yesu ɔkpere ɔbiɛtɛ ɔba ɔ̃aɣedza ma i katɔ̃ ne.
Ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Gbaã nto loɣere mi sɔ si miifiniki miibara so lɛ mabiɛtɛ awe ne, miito miakɛlɛ Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ame minya.
Ngɔ lonya ɔɖo i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ame ne, ɔ̃ nɖe ngɔ lobɔ so karɔ̃ ɔkpesera so lɛ ɔbiɛtɛ gɔgbe awe.
“Ɔbiara gɔ loafɔ ɔbiɛtɛ gɔgbe i wũ iyere ame ne, mme iɖe ɔfɔ.
Daakpadzɛ̃ Kuwɛ̃ Apia I Kalakanyɔ Ame.
“Ɔrere gɔ loatã ɔbiɛtɛ gɔ mba kafɔkaɖe i wũ ame ɔfiniki i kafɔkaɖe kama ne, si masu ɔwɛ̃ manyi kukɔtɛ siare masarã wũ i ɔme mafuĩdza wũ mapia i ɔpo ame ne, ialɛgu wũ iɖo.
“Ndzo miɖe mitã kayiiso ala ara wa loatã maturi ɔbo i kalakanyɔ ame pia, fiɛ ato aaba kokooko, ɣɛɛ ndzo miɖe mitã ngɔ iso i ara wamɔ aaki fiɛ aaba maturi iso!
Ne ɔso si fɔ kɔrɔ̃ ɣee kukpa sɛ kukɔ-ɔ kupia i ikpi ame ne, tu kɔ̃ pɛyu!
Ilɛ iɖo sɔ aabo i ngbã ame sɔ ana kɔrɔ̃ ɣee kukpa iɖo sɔ aawe nrɔɔ̃ minyɔ ngba minyɔ mafuĩdza-ɔ mapia i itɔkpe nɛ loibanyi inya ame.
Si fɔ inɔmi ana nsɛ itã abo i ikpi ame ne, were ne ɖi pɛyu!
Ilɛ iɖo sɔ aawe inɔmi iwɛ̃ abo i ngbã ame iɖo sɔ aawe anɔmi anyɔ mafuĩdza-ɔ mapia i itɔkpe nɛ loisɛ inyi ame.
Yesu Ɔte Ara I Sɛrɛrerɔ̃ Gɔ Loyu Iso.
“Minyɔ kukaakɔ sɔ miibanyɔ makosoi magbe kuwɛ̃ pupurii.
Nto loɣere mi sɔ ma Ɣaa makpabo i kato ɣɛ i Ɣaa katɔ̃ ɔwi biara i ma kanya.
Alasɔ Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi ɔba sɔ ɔ̃afɔ mma loyu ɔtã ma ngbã.
“Si ɔturi ba masɛrɛ kulafa fiɛ ɔwɛ̃ ɔyu ne, be ɔ̃abara?
Ɔ̃ibanyua kasiwɛ̃-kaiwɛ̃ ɔɣedza i kube ɔkparuɛ ɔsɛ ɔ̃anyɔnyɔ ngɔ nto ɔyu?
Fiɛ si ɔnya wũ ne, nto loɣere mi sɔ ɔ̃ana isoɣɔ i ɔwɛ̃ gɔ loyu ngbe iso ɔɖo kasiwɛ̃-kaiwɛ̃ ma loiyu.
Ngbɔ ame i mi ɔse gɔ i kato iibabie sɔ makosoi magbe kuwɛ̃ si ɔyu ne.
Ɔri Gɔ Iso Aala Ɔnyii Fɔɖedze Gɔ Loɣɛrɛ-Ɔ.
“Si fɔ ɔnyii ɔɣɛrɛ-ɔ ne, kɛlɛ ɔ̃ kɔrɛ si asɛ aaɖi ate wũ i mi gu wũ inyɔ ndɛ̃ kere.
Si ɔkã-ɔ atsue ne, mi sinyii to siakɛlɛ i katɔ̃.
Ɣɛɛ si ɔ̃ikã-ɔ atsue ne, kɔ ɔturi ɔwɛ̃ ɣee inyɔ si misɛ ala Ɔko Sekelea ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Maɖansiɛ inyɔ ɣee itɛ kanya ame itɔ̃me iso maasia itɔ̃me biara ita.’ Si mmɔ ana ɔ̃ikã ma atsue ne, ɣere mafɔɖedze ikuri ɔɖuɖu, ɣɛɛ si ɔ̃ikã ma atsue ana ne, ɖi wũ atsue lɛ ngɔ loifɔ ɔɖe ɣee lampofɔdze.
“Ne ɔso nto loɣere mi ɔɖuɖu sɔ, nnɛ misɛ̃ i kayiiso ngbe ne, Ɣaa aasɛ̃ ne i kato, fiɛ nnɛ miɖi ɔri i karɔ̃ iso ngbe ne, Ɣaa aasia kɔrɔ̃ i ne iso i kato ana.
“Nto loledza mi iɣere sɔ ira biara nɛ i mi maturi inyɔ aatɔrã misia ita i kayi gagbe iso i kayi ikparama ame ne, wũ Ɔse gɔ i kato to ɔ̃abara ne ɔtã mi.
Alasɔ ngbegɔ i maturi inyɔ ɣee itɛ ɔsarɛ i wũ iɣere ame ne, lopia i ma ndɛ̃.” Igbã I Ɔɖabo Gɔ Loisu Ɔtsɛ Ɔ̃ Ɔlaa Iso.
Petro ɔbore ɔbo Yesu ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Bosate, ikpɛ irɛ̃ loasu lotsɛ wũ ɔnyii gɔ nto ɔɣɛrɛ me?
Ikpɛ ikɔdzɛ?” Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Iiɖe ikpɛ ikɔdzɛ kere!
Ɣɛɛ ikpɛ sikɔdzɛ aka akɔdzɛ si asu atsɛ wũ.
“Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ se lɛ ngbe.
Ɔwi ɔwɛ̃ ne, igara ɔwɛ̃ ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃aki i ɔ̃ maɖabo siko ame ɔnyɔ kumɛgɔ mato mabara ɔ̃ karabara.
Ku ɔ̃ isɛ karɔ̃ kere ne, makɔ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ nto wũ kuso titiiti mabɔ.
Gɔ ɔɖabo gɔmɔ na sikã ɔ̃atã kuso ɔso ne, igara ɔtã sɔ marɔdɛ̃ ɔ̃ gu ɔ̃ ɔre gu mabi lɛ masande gu ira biara nɛ ɔba si masu matã kuso.
“Ɔɖabo gɔgbe ɔpɛ agɛgɛ̃ i igara katɔ̃ ɔtã wũ iti sɔ, ‘Na ɔtu tã me ne nto loatã-ɔ kuso ɔɖuɖu gɔ loto-ɔ!’ Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ara ɔɖo igara kayiri ne ɔso ɔsu kuso ɔɖuɖu ɔtsɛ wũ ɔnyua wũ sɔ ɔkɛlɛ.
“Gɔ ɔrui ne, ɔsɛ ɔ̃atu ɔ̃ ɔɖabo laa gɔ nto wũ kuso kɛkɛĩ.
Ɔmɔɛ̃ ɔ̃ ɔlaa gɔgbe i ɔme gɔ ɔle ɔtsɛ wũ iro.
Ɔɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Tã me kuso gɔ ato me!’ “Ɔ̃ malaa ɔtã wũ iti sɔ ‘Na ɔtu tã wũ ne ɔto ɔ̃tã-ɔ kuso ɔɖuɖu gɔ ɔto-ɔ!’ “Ɣɛɛ ɔsɛ̃, ɔtã mamɔɛ̃ wũ mapia i iyo gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ ɔ̃atã wũ kuso gɔ ɔto.
Gɔ ɔ̃ maɖabo laa ɔnya nnɛ loba ne, ibua iɖaa ma, ne masɛ maaɣere igara ira biara nɛ loba ne.
“Ne ɔso igara ɔpia makpere ɔɖabo mabɔ ɔɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Ɔɖabo lalaa aɖe!
Losu fɔ kuso gɔ ato me ɔɖuɖu lotsɛ-ɔ alasɔ atã me iti.
Ikote sɔ fɔ wũ aanyɔ fɔ ɔlaa nnya lɛ kumɛgɔ lonyɔ-ɔ nnya.’ Sikpã ɔkpɛ̃ igara gbaã ne ɔsu ɔɖabo gɔgbe ɔsese mapia wũ i iyo sɔ ɔwe mmɔ makpadzɛ̃ wũ kutsue gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ ɔ̃atã kuso gɔ ɔto wũ ɔro.” Ne Yesu ɔwiri sɔ, “Ngbɔ i wũ Ɔse gɔ i kato aabara mi ɔbiara si miisu mi manyii akpi mitsɛ ma ta mi situ ame ɔɖuɖu ne.”
Yesu Ɔte Ara I Marã Gu Mare Kusɛ̃so Iso.
Gɔ Yesu ɔɣɛ ara wagbe ɔro ne, ɔrui i Galilea ɔkɛlɛ Yudea awo ame i Yordan Ɔwore kama isɛ.
Maturi gbodzoo ɔsiai wũ fiɛ ɔsa ma i mmɔ.
Ma Farisise mawɛ̃ ɔba ɔ̃ kɔrɛ mala wũ manyɔ makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Bo mmara ɔtã ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔri sɔ ɔ̃awo ɔ̃ ɔre ɔsɛ̃ i katɔ̃mei biara iso?” Yesu ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Miika i Ɔko Sekelea ame sɔ ta karɔ̃kasɛkɔ̃ ne, ɔrã gu ɔre i Ɣaa ɔbara?
Fiɛ Ɣaa ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Nnɛgbe ɔso i ɔrɛrɛ̃ aarui i ɔ̃ ɔse gu ɔnyi kɔrɛ ɔpɛ ɔmatã i ɔ̃ ɔre iso fiɛ ma inyɔɔ aakpese sosina siwɛ̃ ne.’ Ne ɔso maisiɖe maturi inyɔ ɣɛɛ ɔwɛ̃.
Ne ɔso kuwɛ̃ si ɔdaabɛse nnɛ i Ɣaa ɔsu ɔmatãra so iso.” Ne ma Farisise ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Iyɔ be ɔso i Mose ɔɖi ɔri sɔ ɔrɛrɛ̃ aatã ɔ̃ ɔre isɛ̃so ɔko iyɔ ɔ̃ɔɖi wũ ɔri?” Yesu ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Mose ɔtã mi ɔri sɔ misɛ̃ mi mare ala mi atsuele ɔso, ɣɛɛ ne, iiɖe ngbɔ ise ta karɔ̃kasɛkɔ̃.
Ne ɔso nto loɣere mi sɔ ɔrɛrɛ̃ biara gɔ loasɛ̃ ɔ̃ ɔre fiɛ iiɖe kama iɖe i ɔrɔ̃go ɔfe wũ ne, ɔɖe asɔrɔ̃ si ɔyiri ɔrɔ̃go mama.” Ne ɔ̃ marasuãdze to maɣere Yesu sɔ, “Si ngbɔ ise i ɔrã gu ɔre ndɛ̃ ne, iyɔ ilɛ iɖo si miiyiri so kɔra.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Iiɖe ɔturi biara loanɔ ara wagbe karɔ̃, mma i Ɣaa ɔtã kotoo loanɔ karɔ̃.
Alasɔ ara agbãagbã ɔso i marɛrɛ̃ iisɛ mayiri marɔ̃go.
Mawɛ̃ ne, ngbɔ maɣe ma ne, mawɛ̃ ana ne, maturi lobara ma ngbɔ, fiɛ mawɛ̃ ana iisɛ mayiri marɔ̃go ala Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ɔso.
Ngɔ loawo ara ite nɛgbe ɔfɔ si ɔfɔ ne.” Yesu Ɔtã Mabiɛtɛ Kusɛkusɛ.
Mawɛ̃ ɔkɔ mabiɛtɛ mabɔ Yesu sɔ ɔsia ma kɔrɔ̃ iso si ɔkparama kayi ɔtã ma, ɣɛɛ ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔnyagalagu mmamɔ.
Yesu ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Mitã mabiɛtɛ si maba wũ kɔrɛ ne midaatɛ̃ ma ɔri, alasɔ Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ se sitã ma igbã.” Yesu ɔsia ma nrɔɔ̃ iso, ɔtã ma kusɛkusɛ fiɛ ka ɔrui.
Ɔporoporoi Ranase Ɔwɛ̃ Iso Itɔ̃me.
Ɔwi ɔwɛ̃ ame ne, ɔporoporoi ɔwɛ̃ ɔba Yesu kɔrɛ ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ratedze, be nɖe ira sɛɛ nɛ loabara fiɛ loana ngbã mɛ loisɛ miro?” Ne Yesu ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Be ɔso ato akarɛ me itɔ̃me i ira sɛɛ iso?
Ɔturi ɔwɛ̃ saã pɛ nɖe ɔsɛɛ, fiɛ si ato abie ngbã mɛ loisɛ miro ne, mɔɛ̃ Ɣaa mmara ɔɖuɖu la.” Ne ɔkarɛ Yesu sɔ, “Mme mmara?” Yesu ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Daaɖoe ɔturi, daaɖe asɔrɔ̃, daayu kayu, daaɖaɛ fɔ ɔlaa kanya.
Warɛ fɔ ɔse gu fɔ ɔnyi si aɖɔɛ fɔ ɔnyii lɛ kumɛgɔ ato aɖɔɛ so.” Ne ɔporoporoi gɔmɔ ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Loɔbara ara wagbe ɔɖuɖu, be loɔkuti loabara?” Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Si ato abie sɔ aayi pɛpɛɛpɛ ne, kɛlɛ aasu fɔ ira biara rɔdɛ̃ si asu sikã atsɛ mawɛrɛba, si aana kusia siare i kato.
Si ɔɔro ne, kpese ba siai me.” Gɔ ɔporoporoi gɔgbe ɔnɔ nnɛgbe ne, ɔruigu isoma alasɔ ɔba karana gbaã.
Ne Yesu to ɔɣere ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Nto loɣere mi sɔ ito iabua iɖa fiɛ ranase aabo i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ame.
Nto loledza mi iɣere sɔ, ma mmɔ ibo ba ɔle iɖo kumɛgɔ i kapuipɔngɔ aaki kafe i ɔdzirikaãra iyoi ame.” Gɔ marasuãdze ɔnɔ ara wagbe ne, ibara ma ɣii ne mato makarɛ sɔ, “Iyɔ nna loabua ɔna iɖi?” Yesu ɔnyɔ ma i katɔ̃ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ɔturi kuwɛ̃ iibawo ɔbara, ɣɛɛ Ɣaa aawo ibiara ɔbara.” Ne Petro to ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Nyɔ, iyɔ bo ma lonyua bo ira biara bosɛ fiɛ bosiai-ɔ ne, mme kusia boana?” Yesu ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Nto loɣere mi i ɔnukuare ame sɔ, ɔwi gɔ i Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi aasɛ i ɔ̃ ifiɛ sigaraiyara iso i Kayi Ɣɛtɛ ga nto kaba ame ne, mi ma nɖe wũ marasuãdze iweo-inyɔ ne, mito miasɛ i sigara ayara iso miɖe sigara i Israel nlɛ aka aweo-anyɔ iso.
Ɔbiara gɔ lonyua ayo, manyiibi rɛrɛ̃ gu marɔ̃go, ɔ̃ ɔse gu ɔnyi, kukpɛkɔ̃ ɔsɛ ala wũ ɔso ne, ɔto ɔ̃afɔ ne ikpɛ kulafa fiɛ ɔ̃ana ngbã mɛ loisɛ miro ana.
Ɣɛɛ gbodzoo ma nɖe maɖeakatɔ̃ kiniɔ to maakpese matsɔra fiɛ mawɛ̃ ma nɖe matsɔra kiniɔ to maakpese maɖeakatɔ̃.
Marabaradze Mawɛ̃ Iso Itɔ̃me.
“Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ se lɛ ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ lota kaya tutuutu ɔsɛ ɔ̃abie marabaradze sɔ masɛ maabara karabara i ɔ̃ adziribi kakpɛkɔ̃ ame.
Ɔnɔ karɔ̃ sɔ ɔ̃atã ma ikpɛnɛ kuso lɛ kumɛgɔ masɛ matã fiɛ ɔsese ma sia.
“Lɛ iɖɔwũ kaiwɛ̃ ne, ɔledza kuɣa ame isɛ, ne ɔnya gɔ mawɛ̃ ɣɛ mmɔ maito mabara kuira.
Ne ɔɣere ma ma wũ sɔ, ‘Mikɛlɛ wũ kakpɛkɔ̃ miabara karabara ne nto loatã mi ikpɛnɛ kuso.’ Ne ɔso marui makɛlɛ.
“Iɖɔwũ iweo-inyɔ gu iɖɔwũ itɛ ame ne, ɔledza ibara ngbɔ ame.
Ito ikɛlɛ iɖɔwũ iru ame ana gɔ ɔsɛ kuɣa ame ne, ɔledza marɛrɛ̃ mawɛ̃ inya gɔ maɣɛ i mmɔ.
Ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, ‘Be ɔso mito miwɔra ikpɛnɛ siefe sɔ miito mibara kuira?’ “Ne matã mmuai sɔ, ‘Kuwɛ̃ iisu bo sɔ bosɛ boabara ɔ̃ karabara.’ “Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, ‘Mi wũ mikɛlɛ wũ kakpɛkɔ̃ ame miabara karabara.’ “Gɔ kutsuɛ ɔɣo ne, kakpɛkɔ̃sate ɔɣere ngɔ nto ɔnyɔ marabaradze iso sɔ, ‘Kpere marabaradze bɔ si atã ma ma kuso.
Sɛ karɔ̃ i mma lotsɔra sia ɔkɛlɛ iso si awirigu mma loɖe katɔ̃ makɛlɛ iso.’ “Marabaradze ma lokɛlɛ ku iɖɔwũ iru ame ne, matã ma ɔbiara ikpɛnɛ kuso.
Ne ɔso gɔ marabaradze ma loɖe katɔ̃ makɛlɛ ɔba mafɔ ma kuso ne, mabu sɔ maatã ma iɖo ngbɔ, ɣɛɛ ma wũ ikpɛnɛ kuso matã ma ɔɖuɖu.
Gɔ mafɔ sikã ne, matsɛ kakpɛkɔ̃ sate iɣɛtɛ sɔ, ‘Mma lotsɔra sia ɔba ne, ɔɖɔwũ ɔwɛ̃ pɛ mabara karabara atoa sɔ bo ne, bobara karabara ikpɛnɛ ɔɖuɖu i kuɣɛ̃ ame, ɣɛɛ kuso kuwɛ̃ ɔtã bo!’ “Ne kakpɛkɔ̃ sate ɔtã ma ɔwɛ̃ mmuai sɔ, ‘Ɔrɛrɛĩ, loiɖe mi amumu alasɔ kuso gɔ boɣɛ bosia ita kuɖe lotã mi.
Ne ɔso su fɔ sikã si akɛlɛ iyo.
Mme mɔmɔ me lobie sɔ loatã mma lotsɔra ɔba lɛ kumɛgɔ lotã mi.
Fiɛ loba ɔri sɔ lobara wũ sikã karabara kumɛgɔ loɖɔɛ, ne ɔso anɔ si adaarɛtɛ-ɔ i wũ ara itsɛ iso.’ ” Ne Yesu ɔwirigu ma sɔ, “Ne ɔso mma nɖe matsɔra to maakpese maɖeakatɔ̃ fiɛ mma nɖe maɖeakatɔ̃ to maakpese matsɔra.” Yesu Ɔɖe Ika I Ɔ̃ Kukpi Iso Ɔkpɛ Tɛare.
Gɔ Yesu to ɔkɛlɛ Yerusalem ne, ɔkpere ɔ̃ marasuãdze iweo-inyɔ ɔɣedza i kuruɛ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mikã atsue, boto bokɛlɛ Yerusalem ngbegɔ mato maaɖi mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, matã masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu mmara matedze matã me kukpi ipɔ.
Maaɖi me matã mma loiɖe ma Yudase mabara me aɣiãra, mapɛ me, fiɛ maapɛ me mamatãra i kudziri iso, ɣɛɛ ikpɛnɛ tɛare iso ne, nto loaledza ita iwe ngbã.” Yakobo Gu Yohanes Ɔnyi Ɔkarɛ Kasɛkɔ̃ Ɔtã Ɔ̃ Mabi.
Zebedeo ɔre ɔkɔ ɔ̃ mabi inyɔ maba Yesu kɔrɛ, mapɛ agɛgɛ̃ makarɛ wũ sɔ ɔbuai ma.
Ne Yesu ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Be mito mibie?” Ne ma ɔnyi ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Tã sɔ wũ mabi inyɔ magbe aasɛ i fɔ kuɖearɔ̃ gu fɔ kubena iso ku ɔwi gɔ aaɖe sigara.” Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Miiɣe nnɛ mito mikarɛ.
Miawo inyɛwe gu kukpi gɔ ame loaki ɔki?” Ne matã mmuai sɔ, “Aĩ, boto boawo.” Mmɔ i Yesu to ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Gbaã iɖe sɔ mito miawo.
Ɣɛɛ ne, lona ɔri sɔ loaɖi mma loasɛ i wũ kuɖearɔ̃ gu kubena iso.
Kusɛkɔ̃ gɔmɔ ne, mma i wũ Ɔse ɔledza ɔsɛ ɔkpɛ ɔɖe.” Gɔ marasuãdze iweo tsɔra ɔnɔ itɔ̃me nɛgbe ne, managu manyiibi inyɔ magbe sikpã.
Ne ɔso Yesu ɔkpere ma ɔɖuɖu ɔsirakanya ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Miɣe sɔ mma loiɖe ma Yudase magara sɛ mate so mapia mma mato maɖe iso, fiɛ ma matɔ̃ɖedze ana sɛ maɖe ma iso ku ɔle ɔɖuɖu.
Ɣɛɛ ne, idaawe i mi ame ngbɔ, si mi ndɛ̃ ɔrere to ɔbie sikpakpa ne, ɔbara so sumudze ɔtã matsɔra.
Fiɛ si mi ɔrere to ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃aɖe ɔɖeakatɔ̃ ne, ɔbara so ɔɖabo ɔtã matsɔra.
Mme Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi kɔra ne, loiba sɔ masumu me, ɣɛɛ sɔ loasumu losu wũ ngbã lotã ala maturi gbodzoo iɖi ɔso.” Yesu Ɔsa Manɔbiɛdze Inyɔ.
Ɔwi gɔ i Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze to mabɔrɛ i Yeriko ne, maturi gbodzoo ɔsiai ma.
Manɔbiɛdze inyɔ ma nsi i ɔri kuruɛ ɔnɔ sɔ Yesu to ɔfe, ne ɔso matsɛ kulu teteree sɔ, “Yesu, Igara David Ɔbi, nyɔ bo nnya!” Maturi ɔnyagalagu ma sɔ malo, ɣɛɛ makɔlɛ ma silɔ mabua sɔ, “Igara David Ɔbi nyɔ bo nnya soo!” Yesu ɔtui ɔya ne ɔkpere ma ɔkarɛ sɔ, “Be mito mibie sɔ lobara lotã mi?” Matã mmuai sɔ, “Tete, boto bobie sɔ boanya ara!” Ma ara ɔɖo Yesu kayiri, ne ɔpɛgu ma anɔmi matsɛ inya fiɛ marui masiai wũ ne.
Yesu Ɔbo I Yerusalem Lɛ Igara Awe.
Ɔwi gɔ i Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔɔbore mabo Yerusalem ne, maba maabo Betfage i kube gɔ marɔ sɔ Oliva adziri Kube iso.
Mmɔ ɔpia ɔ̃ marasuãdze inyɔ ɔɖegu katɔ̃ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mikɛlɛ akorowa wa mpia i katɔ̃, si mibo ne, mito mianya ɔfirimu gɔ makɔra maɣedza, ɔ̃ ibi ɣɛ wũ i kɔrɛ.
Mikurisi wũ mibɔ me.
