Si ɔrere ɔɣɛ ira irere ne, miɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Bosate nto ɔbie ma’ iyɔ ɔluwɛ̃ ne, ɔto ɔ̃aɖi ma arɔĩ.” Iba ngbɔ gɔ itã sɔ nnɛ i kanyaɖidze ɔɣɛ aaba i ne ame sɔ, “Miɣere Zion kaɖe sɔ, ‘Nyɔ, fɔ igara to ɔba fɔ kɔrɛ!
Ɔsi i ɔfirimu gu ɔ̃ ibi iso i karɔ̃ ibɔso ame ɔto ɔba.’ ” Ne ɔso marasuãdze ɔrui masɛ maabara lɛ kumɛgɔ i Yesu ɔpia ma.
Makɔ ɔfirimu gu ɔ̃ ibi mabɔ, maɖi ma sikati masia i mabɔi iso fiɛ Yesu ɔta ɔsɛ i ma iso.
Maturi gbodzoo ɔɖi ma awu masɛ i ɔri fiɛ mawɛ̃ ana ɔɖaɛ kudzirikpai mafere i ɔri iso.
Maturi gbodzoo ma nɖe Yesu katɔ̃ gu mma ngbikama to mafa kayiɖu teteree sɔ, “Boale David Ɔbi, fiɛ Ɣaa aafere ngɔ nto ɔba i Bosate iyere ame kusɛkusɛ.
Boale Ɣaa!” Gɔ Yesu ɔbo Yerusalem ɔmagɛ̃ ame ne, kulu ko nto ɣee, ne maturi to makarɛ sɔ, “Ne nna ɔɖe ngbe?” Ne mawɛ̃ to matã mmuai sɔ, “Ɔ̃ nɖe Kanyaɖidze Yesu gɔ lobɔrɛ i Nasaret i Galilea ne.” Yesu Ɔsa Kuɣamaɖese Ɔɖi I Ɣaa Kasɔrɛkɔ̃.
Yesu ɔkɛlɛ Ɣaa isɔrɛyo ɔsɛ ɔ̃asa mma ɔɖuɖu nto maɣa ara gu mma nto marɔdɛ̃ ara ɔɖi i mmɔ.
Ɔli mma nto manyuarã sikã sipɔrɔ̃ gu mma nto marɔdɛ̃ abɔrɔnuma ayara ɔpɛyu.
Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Matsɛrɛ i Ɔko Sekelea ame sɔ Ɣaa ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Maarɔ wũ iyo sɔ kayi kakparamakɔ̃,’ ɣɛɛ miɔsu ne mibara mayukukpe kawɛrɛkɔ̃!” Manɔbiɛdze gu mabafã ɔba ɔ̃ kɔrɛ i kasɔrɛkɔ̃ mmɔ fiɛ ɔsa ma.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu mmara matedze ɔnya awawãra wa ɔto ɔbara gu kumɛgɔ i mabiɛtɛ to mala kulu i isɔrɛyo ame sɔ, “Maale David Ɔbi!” ne, ikpɛ̃ ma sikpã.
Ne mato makarɛ Yesu sɔ, “Ato anɔ nnɛ mato maɣɛ i ngbe?” Yesu ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Nto lonɔ.
Miika itɔ̃me nɛgbe minya i Ɔko Sekelea ame sɔ, ‘Akararã mabiɛtɛ sɔ ma kanya ame i ile nɛ loyi sɛ ibɔrɛ.’ ” Ne kama ne, Yesu ɔrui ɔnyua ma ɔkɛlɛ Betania ɔmagɛ̃ ame ngbegɔ ɔsɛ ɔ̃arɛ.
Yesu Ɔgbarĩ Kuɖedziri Kuwɛ̃.
Kaɖesɛ̃a kaya tututu gɔ ɔ̃ɔkpese ɔto ɔba ɔmagɛ̃ ame ne, kukã ɔkpɛ̃ wũ.
I ɔri kuruɛ ne, ɔnya figi kudziri gɔ kuɣɛ ne ɔso ɔkɛlɛ kɔ̃ kɔrɛ, ɣɛɛ gɔ ɔsɛ ne, ɔ̃inya ibi kuiwɛ̃ iɖo aɣata.
Ne ɔɣere kudziri sɔ, “Ita i nɔme ne, aisibaɣɔ̃ abi anya.” Ɔluwɛ̃ kudziri ko loɣɔ.
Gɔ ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔnya nnɛ loba ne ibara ma ɣii, ne mato makarɛ sɔ, “Nda i kuɖedziri ɔɣɔ ɔluwɛ̃ ngbɔ?” Ne Yesu ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Nto loɣere mi gbaã sɔ si mifɔ miɖe fiɛ miiwararã ne, mito miawo nnɛ lobara kudziri gɔgbe ɔbara.
Fiɛ iiɖe ne kere, ɣɛɛ mito miaɣere kube gɔgbe sɔ, ‘Kɛlɛ aafuĩdza so apia i ɔpo ame,’ fiɛ iaba ngbɔ.
Si mifɔ Ɣaa miɖe ne, ira biara nɛ miakarɛ wũ i kayi ikparama ame ne, mito miafɔ ne.” Makarɛ Yesu Ngbegɔ Ɔna Ɔ̃ Ɔle Ɔbɔrɛgu.
Yesu ɔkpese ɔba isɔrɛyo ame ne gɔ ɔto ɔte ara ne, masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu makpakpa ɔba ɔ̃ kɔrɛ makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Lɛ ana ɔle gɔ ato abara ala ara wagbe fiɛ nna lotã-ɔ ɔle gɔmɔ?” Yesu ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Mitã lokarɛ mi itɔ̃me iwɛ̃ lonɔ, si mitã me mmuai ne, nto loaɣere mi ɔle gɔ loto lobara ala ara wagbe.
Yohanes ne, nna lotã wũ ɔle fiɛ ɔpie maturi Ɣaa ndu?
Ɣaa ɛɛbɛrɛ maturi lotã wũ?” Ne matsɛgu so iwararã sɔ, “Be boaɣɛ?
Si boɣɛ sɔ Ɣaa kɔrɛ ne, ɔto ɔ̃akarɛ bo sɔ ‘Be ɔso miifɔ Yohanes miɖe?’ Ɣɛɛ si boɣɛ ana sɔ ‘Maturi kɔrɛ’ ne, boto bonigã maturi alasɔ ma ɔɖuɖu ɔfɔ maɖe sɔ Ɣaa kanyaɖidze ɔɖe.” Ne ɔso maɣere Yesu sɔ, “Boiɣe ngbegɔ i ɔ̃ ɔle ɔbɔrɛ.” Ne Yesu ɔ̃ wũ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mme wũ loibaɣere mi ngbegɔ i wũ ɔle gɔ loto lobara ala karabara gagbe ɔbɔrɛ.” Yesu Ɔte Ara I Manyiibi Inyɔ Mawɛ̃ Iso.
“Nda minya itɔ̃me nɛgbe?
Ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɔwe gɔ ɔba mabirɛrɛĩ inyɔ.
Ɔɣere kpakpare sɔ, ‘Ɔbi, sɛ aabara karabara i kakpɛkɔ̃ ame nɔme.’ “Ɔbi ɔɣere ɔ̃ ɔse sɔ, ‘Loibasɛ,’ ɣɛɛ ne kama ne, ɔfinikira ɔ̃ adzuni ɔrui ɔkɛlɛ sia.
“Ɔse ɔkpere ɔbi nyɔare ɔpia wũ katɔ̃me gagbe ame.
Ɔtɔrã i ɔ̃ ɔse katɔ̃ sɔ ɔ̃asɛ, ɣɛɛ ɔ̃isɛ.
“Mabi inyɔ magbe ne, ma ɔmele lobara ɔ̃ ɔse kuɖɔɛ?” Matã mmuai sɔ, “Kpakpare.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Nto loɣere mi sɔ, ma lampofɔdze gu asɔrɔ̃ maɖedze ɔɔɖe mi katɔ̃ makpa Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃.
Alasɔ Ndupiedze Yohanes ɔba ɔ̃ate mi sibɔlɔlɔ ɔri, ɣɛɛ miifɔ wũ miɖe, ɣɛɛ ma lampofɔdze gu asɔrɔ̃maɖedze ɔfɔ wũ maɖe.
Atoa sɔ minya nwagbe ne, miifinikira mi adzuni mifɔ wũ miɖe.” Yesu Ɔpɛ Igbã I Marabaradze Lalaa Mawɛ̃ Iso.
Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Minɔ igbã mama ana.
Kpɛ̃dze ɔwɛ̃ ɔwe ku ɔwi gɔ lofe gɔ ɔkpɛ̃ adziribi wa masɛ masu mabara ala ndã kakpɛkɔ̃.
Ɔtɛ̃ ɔkpã ɔki ɔlɔ kakpɛkɔ̃, ɔɖi itawo nɛ ame maakã ndã, fiɛ ka ɔtsue iyo kɔlɛa ngbegɔ i ngɔ loadzuɛ̃ kakpɛkɔ̃ aaya.
Ɔsu kakpɛkɔ̃ ɔpia i marabaradze nrɔɔ̃ ame fiɛ ɔkɛlɛ ɔri.
Gɔ adziribi ɔsɔrɛ̃wi ɔɣo ne, ɔpia ɔ̃ maɖabo sɔ masɛ maafɔ ɔ̃ kaɖekɔ̃ mabɔ wũ i marabaradze kɔrɛ.
“Marabaradze ɔmɔɛ̃ maɖabo magbe, mapɛ ɔwɛ̃, maɖoe ɔwɛ̃, fiɛ mapɛ ɔwɛ̃ ata.
Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ɔledza maɖabo mama isese iɖo maɖeakatɔ̃.
Ma wũ ne, marabaradze ɔbara ma lɛ maɖeakatɔ̃.
Kawirikɔ̃ ne, ɔsese ɔ̃ ɔbi ala ɔɣere so sɔ, ‘Loɣe sɔ mato maawarɛ wũ ɔbi.’ “Ɣɛɛ gɔ marabaradze ɔnya ɔbi ne, maɣere so sɔ, ‘Kakpɛkɔ̃ sate ɔbi gɔ loaɖe ɔ̃ ara i ngbe ne.
Mitã boɖoe wũ si boaɖe ɔ̃ ara.’ Ne ɔso mamɔɛ̃ wũ mafuĩdza i ɔkpã kama fiɛ maɖoe wũ.” Ne Yesu ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Be mifɔ miɖe sɔ kakpɛkɔ̃ sate aabara marabaradze magbe si ɔba?” Matã mmuai sɔ, “Ɔto ɔ̃aɖoe marabaradze lalaa magbe ɔsu kakpɛkɔ̃ ɔtã marabaradze mama ma loasu ɔ̃ kaɖekɔ̃ mabɔ wũ i ɔwi iso si masɔrɛ̃ ɔraɖui.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Miika i Ɔko Sekelea ame sɔ, ‘Ita nɛ i mayotsuedze ɔsɛ̃ sɔ iilɛ ne, ne loba iakpese ita nɛ lofɔ kuɣa iɖo ata ɔɖuɖu pelepele ne.
Bosate lobara ira siare nɛgbe fiɛ ibo bo anɔ gbaã!’ ” Yesu ɔkɛlɛgu i katɔ̃ sɔ, “Ɣaa to ɔ̃amɔɛ̃ ɔ̃ sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ɔfɔ mi iso ɔsu ɔtã mma loaɣɔ̃ abi sɛɛ.
Ngɔ loakpase i itã nɛgbe iso ne, ɔto ɔ̃afɛfɛ̃ ɖukuɖuku, fiɛ ngɔ i ita nɛgbe aakpase iwuĩ ne, ito iakɔtɛ wũ ɖɛkpɛrɛɛ.” Gɔ masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu ma Farisise ɔnɔ agbã wa i Yesu ɔpɛ ne, matsue sɔ ma ɔto.
Ne ɔso mabie sɔ si mamɔɛ̃ wũ, ɣɛɛ manigã maturi gbodzoo ma mpia i mmɔ ala masɛ mabu Yesu lɛ Ɣaa kanyaɖidze awe.
Yesu Ɔpɛ Igbã I Ɔrɔ̃go Ikɔyi Iɖe Iso.
Yesu ɔledza agbã isu ite ma ara sɔ, “Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ se lɛ ngbe.
Ɔwi ɔwɛ̃ ame ne, igara ɔwɛ̃ ɔkɔ ɔrɔ̃go ɔtã ɔ̃ ɔbi.
Ɔpia ɔ̃ maɖabo sɔ masɛ maakpere mma matã itsue sɔ maba iyi kaɖekɔ̃ sɔ ka maba, ɣɛɛ masɛ̃ sɔ maito maba.
“Ne ɔso ɔpia maɖabo mama sɔ maɣere ma sɔ, ‘Lotã maɖoe mabɔi gu ma nantsuĩ ma mba iɖa, mawa aɖera masɛ, ira biara ɔɔkote, ne ɔso ka miba wũ ɔpɔrɔ̃ gɔ lotu lotã irɔ̃gokɔ katɔ̃!’ “Ɣɛɛ maturi ma makpere iipia wũ kanya.
Makɛlɛ ma kurabara iso, ɔwɛ̃ ɔkɛlɛ sia, ɔwɛ̃ ana ɔkɛlɛ kuɣa kaɖekɔ̃.
Mawɛ̃ ana ɔmɔɛ̃ maɖabo mamɔ mapɛ ma, maɖoe mma.
Sikpã ɔmɔɛ̃ igara gɔmɔ gbaã, ne ɔso ɔpia ɔ̃ makpakpɛ̃dze masɛ maaɖoe maturiɖoese mamɔ, matsuedza ma ɔmagɛ̃.
“Ne ɔkpere ɔ̃ maɖabo ɔɣere ma sɔ, ‘Wũ ɔrɔ̃go ikɔ aɖera wa mawa ka ase, ɣɛɛ mma lokpere sɔ maba maaɖe ara iikote.
Ne ɔso mikɛlɛ siri iso si mikpere ɔbiara gɔ mianya mibɔ.’ Ne maɖabo ɔrui makɛlɛ itiri gu siri iso masɛ maakpere maturi ɔɖuɖu ma manya, masɛɛ gu malalaa, itã sɔ iyo nɛ ame matu ɔpɔrɔ̃ ɔyi gu maturi.
“Gɔ igara ɔba ɔ̃anyɔ mma loba aɖera kaɖekɔ̃ ne, ɔnya ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ loipia awu wa masɛ mapia i ɔrɔ̃go kakɔkɔ̃.
Ne igara ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, ‘Wũ ɔlaa, nda abara fiɛ abo i ngbe gɔ aipia irɔ̃gokɔ awu?’ Ɣɛɛ ɔrɛrɛ̃ iinya kuira ɔɣɛ.
“Ne igara ɔɣere ɔ̃ maɖabo sɔ, ‘Minyi wũ nrɔɔ̃ gu ngba si mifuĩdza wũ i kayoma i idududu ame.
Mmɔ i kaku gu inyɛwe pia ne.’ ” Ne Yesu ka ɔwirigu ma sɔ, “Maturi gbodzoo i Ɣaa ɔkpere, ɣɛɛ kɛkɛĩ kere ɔ̃aɖi i ma ndɛ̃.” Yesu Ɔɖe Ika I Lampo Itã Iso.
Ma Farisise ɔsɛ maabara adzuni sɔ maamɔɛ̃ Yesu i ma atɔ̃me ikarɛ ame.
Ne ɔso mapia ma marasuãdze gu Herodes masiaidze mawɛ̃ ɔ̃ kɔrɛ makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ratedze, boɣe sɔ asɛ aɣɛ ɔnukuare, asɛ ate maturi nnɛ nɖe Ɣaa kuɖɔɛ gɔ aisɛ akã siruɛ atsue alasɔ aisɛ anyɔ ɔturi i katɔ̃.
Ne ɔso ɣere bo fɔ adzuni.
Lɛ sɔ boatã Roma Igarakpakpa lampo ɛɛbɛrɛ ita iya i bo mmara iso?” Yesu ɣe ma adzuni ne ɔso ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mi ma nsɛ mibie sɔ mibo maturi anɔ!
Be ɔso mito mibie sɔ miala me minyɔ?
Mitã me sikã dzɛ misɛ mitã ala lampo lonyɔ.” Ne masu mabɔ wũ ne.
Ne ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Nna katɔ̃ gu iyere iɖe nsia i sɛ̃ iso?” Matã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Roma Igarakpakpa ire iɖe.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Misu nnɛ nɖe Kaisaro ire mitã wũ si misu nnɛ nɖe Ɣaa ire ana mitã Ɣaa.” Gɔ manɔ nnɛgbe ne, ibara ma ɣii, ne marui maɣɛ wũ ne.
Yesu Ɔte Ara I Makpise Iledza Ita Iso.
Iyi nɛmɔ ame ne, ma Zadukise ma nsɛ maɣɛ sɔ makpise iisibata ɔba Yesu kɔrɛ maba maaɣere wũ sɔ, “Ratedze, Mose ɔɣɛ sɔ si ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔkpi ɔɣɛ ɔ̃ ɔre fiɛ maiɣe ɔbi ne, ɔ̃ ɔnyiibi si ɔsu ɔrɔ̃go ɔyiri si maɣe mabi.
Maanyɔ mabi ma maaɣe mmɔ lɛ ɔ̃ ɔnyiibi gɔ lokpi mabi.
Ɔwi ɔwɛ̃ ame ne, manyiibi rɛrɛ̃ ikɔdzɛ mawɛ̃ ɔwe i ngbe.
Kpakpare ɔyiri ɔrɔ̃go ɣɛɛ ɔ̃iɣe ɔbi fiɛ ɔkpi ɔnyua ɔ̃ ɔre ɔsɛ ɔ̃ ɔkpeama.
Ngbɔ ame ibara ɔbirɛrɛĩ nyɔare ɔtɛare gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ isɛ iabo ɔkɔdzɛva ne.
Kawirikɔ̃ ne, ɔrɔ̃go ɔ̃ wũ ɔba ɔ̃akpi.
Kiniɔ ne, ma nna ɔre i ɔrɔ̃go aaɖe ku iyi nɛ i makpise aaledza ita gɔ ma ɔɖuɖu ɔɔyiri wũ manya.” Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mmɔ miɣɛrɛ ne, alasɔ miiɣe Ɔko Sekelea ame atɔ̃me fiɛ miiɣe Ɣaa ɔle ana.
Alasɔ si makpise ɔta ne, maase lɛ Ɣaa makpabo ma i kato fiɛ maibayiri so.
Ɣɛɛ i makpise ita iso ne, miika nnɛ i Ɣaa ɔɣere mi?
Ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Mme nɖe Abraham Ɣaa gu Isak Ɣaa gu Yakob Ɣaa ne.’ Magbanadze Ɣaa ɔɖe ne iiɖe makpise ɔre ɔɖe.” Gɔ maturi gbodzoo ma mpia mmɔ ɔnɔ ara wagbe ne, ɔ̃ ara ite ɔbara ma ɣii.
Yesu Ɔte Mmara Mɛ Nɖe Misiare Miɖo.
Gɔ ma Farisise ɔnɔ kumɛgɔ i Yesu mmuai ɔpia ma Zadukise ibɔra i kanya ne, maba maasakanya.
Ne ma ndɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ nɖe mmaratedze ɔkarɛ Yesu itɔ̃me sɔ si ɔla wũ ɔnyɔ ne.
Ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ratedze, mme mmara lomɔ miɖo?” Yesu ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Ɖɔɛ Bosate Ɣaa ku fɔ ɔtu ɔɖuɖu gu fɔ ɔkala ɔɖuɖu gu fɔ adzuni ɔɖuɖu Mmɛgbe nɖe mmara ɖeakatɔ̃ gu mmɛ lonya miɖo pelepele ne.
Minyɔare mɛ ka lonya se lɛ miɖeakatɔ̃, ‘Ɖɔɛ fɔ ɔnyii lɛ kumɛgɔ ato aɖɔɛ so.’ Mmara aka anyɔ wagbe iso matsue Mose mmara ɔɖuɖu gu Kanyamaɖidze ara ite masia ne.” Nna Ɔbi Nɖe Kristo?
Gɔ ma Farisise mawɛ̃ ɔsakanya ne, Yesu ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Nna mibu sɔ Kristo ɖe?
Nna ɔbi ɔɖe?” Matã mmuai sɔ, “Igara David Ɔwa tɛtɛ ɔɖe.” Ne Yesu ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Si igara David ɔbi ɔɖe ne, lɛ ise ɔso i David ɔki i Ɣaa Siwarã ɔle ame ɔkpere wũ sɔ Bosate?
David ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Ɣaa ɔɣere Bosate sɔ, “Sɛ i wũ kuɖearɔ̃ iso gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ loatã asu ngba asia i fɔ matsirise iso.” ’ Si igara David ɔkpere wũ Bosate ne, nda i Kristo aaɖe ɔ̃ ɔbi ɔɣɛ?” Ma kuwɛ̃ iiwo Yesu mmuai ɔtã, ne ɔso ita iyi nɛmɔ iso ne, ma kuwɛ̃ iisikarɛ wũ kuira.
Yesu Ɔka Maturi Sɔ Madzuɛ̃ So I Mmara Matedze Gu Masɔrɛdze Iso.
Ne Yesu ɔɖegu maturi gbodzoo gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ika ne.
Ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mmara matedze gu ma Farisise nɖe mma maɖi ɔri sɔ mate Mose mmara.
Ne ɔso mikã ma atsue si mibara ibiara nɛ maɣere mi sɔ mibara, ɣɛɛ ne, midaasiai ma kurabarara, alasɔ maisɛ mabara i nnɛ masɛ mate iso.
Masɛ manyi ato wa mba ɔrɔrã fiɛ asɛ aɖa isore masorera maturi, ɣɛɛ maisɛ mabie sɔ maapiagu ma kɔrɔ̃ si mabuai ma masore.
“Masɛ mabara ira biara sɔ maturi aanyɔ ma.
Minyɔ Ɣaa atɔ̃me siare wa matsɛrɛ i ɔkati iso masu manyi so iti gu nrɔɔ̃ si minyɔ kumɛgɔ i ma awu atsueti amɔ fiɛ akarã!
Si makpere ma i ɔpɔrɔ̃ katukɔ̃ ne, masɛ maɖɔɛ kusɛkɔ̃ kɔlɛa.
Masɛ maɖɔɛ masɛ i kusɛkɔ̃ sɛɛ gu kusɛkɔ̃ kɔlɛa i ma kusarɛkɔ̃ ana.
Masɛ maɖɔɛ sɔ maturi si maya ma ku ibu i kuɣa ame si makpere ma ratedze.
“Madaakpere mi sɔ ratedze, alasɔ mi ɔɖuɖu ne, manyii miɖe fiɛ ratedze ɔwɛ̃ saã miba.
Midaakpere kuwɛ̃ i karɔ̃ iso ngbe sɔ Tete alasɔ ɔse ɔwɛ̃ saã miba gɔ mpia i kato.
Madaakpere mi sɔ Tɔ̃ɖedze alasɔ mi tɔ̃ɖedze ɔwɛ̃ saã gɔ miba nɖe Kristo.
Ngɔ nto ɔbie iyere i mi ndɛ̃ si ɔkpese mi ɔɖabo Ɔbiara gɔ lokɔlɛ so kato ne, maabɔ wũ karɔ̃ fiɛ ɔbiara gɔ lobɔ so karɔ̃ ne, makɔlɛ wũ kato.
Ndzo Miɖe Mitã Maladze.
“Ndzo miɖe mitã mi mmara matedze gu ma Farisise!
Miɖɔɛ Ɣaa i anɔmi anɔmi ame kere!
Misɛ misɛ̃ Ɣaa sigara kaɖekɔ̃ kayogodɔ̃ sɔ maturi si madaabo ku ɔwi gɔ i mi mɔmɔ ana ɔsɛ̃ sɔ miito mibo fiɛ misɛ̃ sɔ mma nto mabie sɔ maabo ana sɔ madaabo!
Ndzo miɖe mitã mi mmara matedze gu ma Farisise!
Miɖɔɛ Ɣaa i anɔmi anɔmi ame kere!
Alasɔ misɛ miɖe makpise mare amumu, fiɛ misɛ mikparama kayi dzoroo i iteso ame.
Nwagbe ɔso ne, mi kutsue ikpadzɛ̃ to iamɔ!
“Ndzo miɖe mitã mi mmara matedze gu ma Farisise!
Miɖɔɛ Ɣaa i anɔmi anɔmi ame kere!
Alasɔ misɛ miwara ɔpo misɛ nrɔ̃ agbãagbã iso misɛ miaɖi ɔturi ɔwɛ̃ mitã Ɣaa, ɣɛɛ si mibara ngbɔ miro ne, misɛ mibara wũ ngɔ lonyanyarĩ ɔɖo mi i itɔkpe ame ikɛlɛ ame!
“Ndzo miɖe mitã mi ma nto mikɔ maturi ɣɛɛ manɔbiɛdze miɖe!
Misɛ mite sɔ, ‘Si ɔturi ɔtarĩgu Ɣaa isɔrɛyo ne, mmara iinyi wũ, ɣɛɛ si ɔtarĩgu sikã dzɛ nse i isɔrɛyo ne, ɔ̃ i mmara ɔnyi ne.’ Manɔbiɛdze dzimifɔ!
Imele lonya iɖo?
Sikã ɛɛbɛrɛ isɔrɛyo nɛ losekelera sikã?
Misɛ mite ana sɔ, ‘Si ɔturi ɔtarĩgu isɔrɛkasege ga iso masɛ mafɛ̃ ara matã Ɣaa ne, mmara iinyi wũ, ɣɛɛ si ɔtarĩgu karatã ga nsia i isɔrɛkasege iso ɣɛɛ ne, mmara ɔnyi wũ.’ Anɔmi ɔbiɛ mi gbaã!
Imele lonya iɖo?
Karatã ɛɛbɛrɛ isɔrɛkasege ga losekelera karatã?
Ne ɔso si ɔturi ɔtarĩgu isɔrɛkasege ne, ta ara wa nsia i isɔrɛkasege iso ɔɖuɖu iɖe ɔtarĩgu.
Fiɛ si ɔturi ɔtarĩgu Ɣaa isɔrɛyo ne, ɔtarĩgu ta Ɣaa gɔ nsi i mmɔ.
Fiɛ si ɔrere ɔtarĩgu Kato ne, ɔtarĩgu Ɣaa sigaraiyara gu ngɔ nsi iso.
“Ndzo miɖe mitã mi mmara matedze gu ma Farisise!
Mi ma nsɛ mibara ara sɔ si mibo maturi anɔ!
Misɛ miɖi mi araɖea ika weova ta aposarɛbi, ibura sikɔma agbãagbã mitã Ɣaa.
Ɣɛɛ misɛ̃ sɔ miibabara ara wa lonya aɖo i mmara ame wa nɖe nnyainyɔ, atɔ̃me iɣɛ i ɔri iso gu ɔnukuare ame.
Ara wagbe ikote sɔ miasu mibua i nwa mimɔɛ̃ mito iso ne.
Ɣɛɛ miibanyua kuiwɛ̃ misɛ.
Matɔ̃ɖedze nɔbiɛdze!
Misɛ mitua ɔnidzɔ gɔ lobo i mi ndã ame ɣɛɛ misɛ mimɛ kapuipɔngɔ!
“Ndzo miɖe mitã mi mmara matedze gu ma Farisise!
Mi ma nsɛ mibara ara sɔ si mibo maturi anɔ!
Misɛ mifore mi akɔi gu arɔi kama, ɣɛɛ wã kame ɔyi ku ara wa miɖe maturi amumu mifɔ ku so ɔle.
Farisise nɔbiɛdze, fore ikɔi ame tɔtɔ, iyɔ kama ka ito iare sekelee!
“Ndzo miɖe mitã mi mmara matedze gu ma Farisise!
Mi ma nsɛ mibara ara sɔ si mibo maturi anɔ!
Mise lɛ maturi akpibiɔ wa matsue makua kukaakɔ, ɣɛɛ wã ame ɔyi ku makpise buria ku akui.
Ngbɔ ame i maturi ɔɖuɖu anɔmi ame ne, mire maturi sɛɛ, ɣɛɛ mi ame ɔyi ku mila gu akpi.
Yesu Ɔɣɛ Itɔ̃me I Mmara Matedze Gu Ma Farisise Kutsue Ikpadzɛ̃ Iso.
“Ndzo miɖe mitã mi mmara matedze gu ma Farisise!
Mi ma nsɛ mibara ara sɔ si mibo maturi anɔ!
Misɛ mitsue akpibiɔ mitã Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze fiɛ misɛ miledza mma losɛ ngbã sɛɛ akpibiɔ kukaakɔ.
Misɛ miɣɛ sɔ, ‘Si bo nsi ngbã ku bo mawa ɔwi ne, tee boiɖoe kanyamaɖidze mamɔ lɛ bo mawa awe.’ Ne ɔso mito misia ita sɔ mma loɖoe Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze mawa miɖe.
Mikɛlɛ i katɔ̃ si mibara ara wa i mi mawa ɔsɛ karɔ̃ miwiri.
“Maturi lalaa!
Mise lɛ maɣɛ gu ma mabi.
Mifɔ miɖe sɔ miawo ɔtere i itɔkpe kutsue ikpadzɛ̃ nɛ nto iba kanya?
Ne ɔso nto loɣere mi sɔ nto loasese mi kanyamaɖidze gu manɔgbadze gu mmara matedze.
Mito miaɖoe mawɛ̃, mipɛ mawɛ̃ mimatãra i kudziri iso, mipɛ mawɛ̃ i mi kusarɛkɔ̃, mitere misa ma ita i ɔmagɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ame ikpa ɔmama ame.
Ne ɔso ne, maturi sɛɛ ma ɔɖuɖu maɔɖoe ita i Abel bɔlɔlɔa iso isɛ iabo Zakaria gɔ nɖe Berakia ɔbi gɔ miɖoe i Ɣaa isɔrɛyo ku Isɔrɛkasege ndɛ̃ kutsue ikpadzɛ̃ to iaba mi iso.
Nto losia ita lotã mi sɔ ituriɖoe nɛgbe ɔɖuɖu ne, ne kutsue ikpadzɛ̃ to iaba kiniɔgbe maturi iso!
Yerusalem Ara Ɔɖo Yesu Kayiri.
“Yerusalem, Yerusalem, asɛ aɖoe kanyamaɖidze ma i Ɣaa sɛ ɔpia fɔ kɔrɛ, fiɛ asɛ apɛ Ɣaa maɖabo ma ɔsɛ ɔpia-ɔ ata.
Loɔkpɛ̃ sɔ si losu nrɔɔ̃ lofu-ɔ lɛ kumɛgɔ i kɔkɔ ɔnyi sɛ ɔwarɛ abue ɔfu akɔkɔibi, ɣɛɛ asɛ̃ me.
Ne ɔso fɔ Isɔrɛyo to iakpese iyoku.
Ita i kiniɔ ne, aisibanya me gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ miaɣɛ sɔ, ‘Ɣaa kusɛkusɛ si kuwegu ngɔ nto ɔba i Bosate iyere ame.’ ”
Yesu Ɔɣɛ Itɔ̃me Ɔsɛ I Ma Yudase Isɔrɛyo Ibiɛbiɛ Iso.
Gɔ Yesu ɔbɔrɛ i Ɣaa isɔrɛyo ɔto ɔkɛlɛ ne, ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔba maakarɛ wũ si ɔkarã inɔ i kumɛgɔ matsue ne ayo iso.
Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Minyɔ ara wagbe ɔɖuɖu kukaakɔ.
Alasɔ gbaã nto loɣere mi sɔ mato maabiɛbiɛ wã ɔɖuɖu gɔ ita kuiwɛ̃ iibakuti isia i ne ɔlaa iso sɔ maibasisi mapɛyu.” Yesu Ɔɣere Ɔ̃ Marasuãdze Ɔɣiã Gɔ Maaɖe.
Gɔ Yesu ɔsɛ ɔ̃asɛ i Nnɔĩ Adziri Kube iso ne, ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔba maakarɛ wũ pɔkɔsɔɔ sɔ, “Ɣere bo ɔwi gɔ i ara wagbe aaba, ɔwi gɔ aakpese aba gu nnɛ loate sɔ kawirikɔ̃ ɔɔɣo.” Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Midzuɛ̃ so sɔ kuwɛ̃ iibasɔsɔla mi.
Alasɔ maturi gbodzoo to maasu wũ iyere maba maaɣere mi sɔ, ‘Mme nɖe Kristo,’ fiɛ maasɔsɔla maturi gbodzoo.
Mito mianɔ kakpã gu kakpã iso atɔ̃me i mi kɔrɛ gu kadzorokɔ̃ ɣɛɛ midaamararã so, ara wagbe igbã to aaba ɣɛɛ iite sɔ kawirikɔ̃ ɔɔɣo.
Karɔ̃ kawɛ̃ iso maturi to maakpɛ̃gu karɔ̃ mama iso maturi, sigarakaɖekɔ̃ to siakpɛ̃gu sigarakaɖekɔ̃, kukã gu karɔ̃ iti to iaba i karɔ̃ agbãagbã iso.
Nwagbe ɔɖuɖu se lɛ kuɣe iɖoɖo ibo ɖeakatɔ̃.
“Mato maamɔɛ̃ mi matã makpadzɛ̃ kutsue fiɛ maaɖoe mi.
Nrɔ̃ ɔɖuɖu iso maturi to maatsiri mi ala wũ ɔso.
Maturi gbodzoo to maasɛ̃ ma kafɔkaɖe ku ɔwi gɔmɔ ame fiɛ maaɖi ma malaa matã, matsiri so.
Mila kanyamaɖidze gbodzoo to maabɔrɛ masɔsɔla maturi gbodzoo.
Ara lalaa ibara to iakɔlɛ kato sɔ maturi gbodzoo iisibaɖɔɛ so.
Ɣɛɛ mma loaya teteree isɛ iabo kawirikɔ̃ to maana iɖi.
Mato maaɣɛ Sigarakaɖekɔ̃ iso Itɔ̃me Bielea nɛgbe i kayiiso ɔɖuɖu sɔ iaɖe ikparĩ itã nrɔ̃ ɔɖuɖu iso maturi, ne kama ne, kawirikɔ̃ aaba.
Yesu Ɔka Marasuãdze I Inyɛwe Siare Nɛ Loaba Iso.
“Mito mianya Ɣaa itsirira ɔba iaya i kasekelekɔ̃, ngbegɔ iikote sɔ iaya lɛ kumɛgɔ i Ɣaa kanyaɖidze Daniel ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ.
Ngɔ nto ɔka ɔko gɔgbe si ɔpia kubɛ sɔ ɔ̃anɔ karɔ̃.
“Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, mma mpia i Yudea si matere makɛlɛ abe iso.
Ngɔ nsia i ɔ̃ iyo isã si ɔdaaso ɔba iyo ame sɔ ɔto ɔba ɔ̃asu ɔ̃ ara.
Ngɔ mpia i sia ana si ɔdaakɛlɛ ayo ame sɔ ɔ̃asu ɔ̃ awu.
Ndzo miɖe mitã mayirise gu matalɛpo ma nto mabi ɣɛtɛ ku ɔwi gɔmɔ ame!
Mitã Ɣaa iti sɔ ɔwi gɔ miatere iibaɖe ɔyu ɔwi ɣee iwarãyi iso.
Alasɔ inyɛwe siare nɛ loaba ku ɔwi gɔmɔ ne, ne igbã iiba inya ita i kayi karɔ̃kasɛkɔ̃ iba iabo nɔme, fiɛ ne igbã iisibaba inya ana.
Ɣɛɛ ne, Ɣaa ɔɔtu ayi wamɔ koko alasɔ si iiɖe ngbɔ ne, kuwɛ̃ iibana iɖi, ɣɛɛ Ɣaa maturi ma ɔɖi ɔsɛ so ɔso ne, ɔ̃abɛrɛkɛ i ayi wamɔ iso.
Ne ɔso si ɔrere ɔba ɔ̃aɣere mi sɔ, ‘Nyɔ, ɔɔnya Kristo i ngbe,’ ɣee ɔrere ɔɣere mi sɔ, ‘Ɔpia i mmɔ’ ne, midaafɔ miɖe.
Alasɔ mila ma Kristo gu kanyamaɖidze to maaba.
Mato maabara awawãra siare gu ara wa loabara maturi ɣii sɔ si masu masɔsɔla ta mma nɖe Ɣaa maturi si maawo.
Mikã me atsue!
Alasɔ loɔɣere mi loɖegu katɔ̃ fiɛ ɔwi gɔmɔ aaɣo.
“Si maɣere mi sɔ, ‘Ɔpia i fafuĩ ame’ ne, midaakɛlɛ sɔ mianyɔ.
Si maɣere mi sɔ, ‘Ɔwɛrɛ i iyo kame i ngbe’ ne, midaafɔ miɖe.
Alasɔ mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi ne, nto loaba lɛ kumɛgɔ i kado sɛ ɔma i kuɖokpo ɔbɔrɛ i kuɣɛ̃kabɔrɛkɔ̃ isɛ iabo kuɣɛ̃ iyo kabokɔ̃.
Ngbegɔ i ira kpia se ne, mmɔ i akolomo sɛ asakanya ne.
Ara Wa Loate Sɔ Kawirikɔ̃ Ɔɔɣo.
“Si inyɛwe ɔwi gɔmɔ ɔfe ɔro kere ne, kuɣɛ̃ to kuagudu, ɔgbaworeti iisibafiɛ, awãmi to aakpakpase abɔrɛ i kato fiɛ kato sile to siati sibɔrɛ i sɛ̃ kawekɔ̃.
“Iyɔ Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi ikparĩ to iabɔrɛ i kato fiɛ kayiiso maturi aapɛ kaku kumɛgɔ manya wũ to ɔba i ɔle gu ifiɛ siare ame.
Kadadã siare to kaare fiɛ ɔ̃apia ɔ̃ makpabo kayi akpakpai wã ana ɔɖuɖu sɔ masa ɔ̃ maturi ma ɔɖi ɔsɛ kanya ita i kayi iti nɛ isɛ iabo nnɛgbe.
Yesu Ɔsu Kuɖedziri Ɔte Ikparĩ.
“Mitã kuɖedziri si kute mi ara.
Si kuɔtsɛ akpa ɣɛtɛ itsue fiɛ ka kuto kuɖi aɣata ɣɛtɛ ne, mitsue sɔ kado ɔwi ɔɔbore ɔbo.
Ngbɔ ame si minya sɔ ara wagbe ɔɖuɖu ka ato aba ne, mitsue sɔ kawirikɔ̃ ka kaba kaasɛ karɔ̃.
Mitsue sɔ ara wagbe ɔɖuɖu to aaba fiɛ maturi ma nsi ku kiniɔ aakpi maro.
Kato gu karɔ̃ to kaafe, ɣɛɛ wũ atɔ̃me iibafe anya.
Kuwɛ̃ Iiɣe Ɔwi Gɔ I Yesu Aaledza Iba.
“Kuwɛ̃ iiɣe iyi ɣee ɔwi gɔ i nwagbe aaba.
Ɣaa makpabo ma i kato, ɣee Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi kɔra iiɣe iɖo wũ Ɔse ɔnɔwɛ̃ nɣe.
Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi iba to iase lɛ kumɛgɔ i Noa ɔwi ɔse awe.
Si kado aaba ɔ̃apɛ ndu ayi minina kayiiso ɔɖuɖu ne, maturi ɔla maɔɖe ara maɔnɛ ndã, marɛrɛ̃ gu marɔ̃go to mayiri so gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ iyi nɛ i Noa ɔya ɔbo i ɔkolo ame.
Ɣɛɛ maitsue nnɛ nto iba gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ ndu ɔyi miba miasore ma ɔɖuɖu miruigu.
Ngbɔ ame i Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi ɔbawi ana aase ne.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, marɛrɛ̃ inyɔ to maaya i kakpɛkɔ̃, Ɣaa aasu ɔwɛ̃ ɔruigu ɔnyua ɔwɛ̃ ɔɣedza.
Marɔ̃go inyɔ to maaya i kukɔtɛ katɔ̃ mala maɔkɔtɛ ara, Ɣaa to ɔ̃asu ɔwɛ̃ ɔruigu ɔnyua ɔwɛ̃ ɔsɛ.
“Ne ɔso midzuɛ̃ so alasɔ miiɣe iyi nɛ i Bosate aaba.
Si iyosate ɣe iyi nɛ i yukukpe aaba ɔ̃ayu wũ ne, tee ɔ̃ibarɛ sirɛ, ɔ̃asɛ ɔdzuɛ̃ sɔ ɔ̃ibatã yukukpe ɔbiɛ ɔ̃ iyo ɔbo ɔyu ara.
Ne ɔso mi wũ midzuɛ̃ so alasɔ Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi to ɔ̃aba ku ɔwi gɔ miito minyɔ wũ ɔri ame.
Mise Lɛ Ɔɖabo Gɔ Nɖe Ɔnukuarese.
“Kiniɔ ne, nna nɖe ɔɖabo nukuarese gu nɔgbadze?
Ɔ̃ nɖe ngɔ si makɔse ɔsu maɖabo tsɔra ɔpia i ɔ̃ kayirinɔ ne, ɔ̃atã ma aɖera i ɔwi sɛɛ iso.
So aaɣɔ ɔɖabo gɔmɔ si makɔse ɔkpese ɔba ɔ̃anya sɔ ɔto ɔbara ngbɔ.
Nto losia ita lotã mi sɔ makɔse to ɔ̃asu ɔ̃ karana ɔɖuɖu ɔpia wũ i nrɔɔ̃ ame sɔ ɔnyɔ iso.
Ɣɛɛ si ɔɖabo lalaa ɔɖe ne, ɔto ɔ̃aɣere so sɔ, ‘Bokɔse to ɔ̃ana ɔpã fiɛ ɔ̃aba!’ Ne ɔso ɔto ɔ̃atsɛ ɔ̃ maɖabo laa ipɛ, itsɛ aɖera iɖe, inɛ ndã ku matarɛ̃dze.
Ɔ̃ ɔkɔse to ɔ̃aba ku iyi nɛ ɔ̃ito ɔnyɔ wũ ɔri ku ɔwi gɔ ɔ̃iɣe.
Makɔse to ɔ̃akpadzɛ̃ wũ kutsue gbaã fiɛ ɔ̃ inyɛwe to iakotegu mma nsɛ mabie sɔ mabo maturi anɔ ɔkpɛ i ngbegɔ i kaku gu inyɛwe pia!
Yesu Ɔpɛ Igbã I Mabitɛ Iweo Iso.
“I ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ aase lɛ ngbe.
Ɔwi ɔwɛ̃ ame ne, mabitɛ iweo mawɛ̃ ɔsu ma sikaniɛ sɔ maasarɛgu ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ nto ɔkɔ ɔrɔ̃go.
Mabitɛ iweo magbe ame ne, iru ɖe madzimifɔ fiɛ iru ana ɖe manɔgbadze.
Madzimifɔ ɔsu ma sikaniɛ, ɣɛɛ maisu nnɔĩ mabua i sikaniɛ iso.
Manɔgbadze ɣɛɛ ne, mato nnɔĩ i abui ame mabua i mmɛ mpia i ɔkaniɛ ame iso.
Gɔ ɔrɔ̃go kɔdze ɔgbikama ku iba ɔso ne, mabitɛ ɔtsɛ sirɛ itua kere ne marɛ sirɛ ne.
“Lɛ kasɛ̃ ndɛ̃ ne, kulu ɔsia sɔ, ‘Ɔrɔ̃go kɔdze ɔɔba ɔ̃abo ne miba miasarɛgu wũ!’ “Mabitɛ iweo ɔɖuɖu ɔta, ne mayara ma sikaniɛ ne.
Ne madzimifɔ to maɣere manɔgbadze sɔ, ‘Mitã bo mi nnɔĩ kɛkɛĩ alasɔ bo sikaniɛ ka sinyi.’ “Ne manɔgbadze ɔɣere ma sɔ, ‘Ooɣo!
Bo nnɔĩ iibaɣo bo gu mi inyɔ ne mikɛlɛ mma nto marɔdɛ̃ kɔrɛ miaɣa.’ “Ku marui kere ne, ɔrɔ̃go kɔdze ɔba ɔ̃abo.
Mabitɛ iru ma nɣɛ masia wũ ɔsiai wũ makɛlɛ ɔrɔ̃go kakɔkɔ̃ kere ne masɛ̃ kayogodɔ̃ ne.
“Ne kama ne, mabitɛ dzimifɔ iru mamɔ ɔba maabo, ne makpere sɔ, ‘Tete!
Tete!
Sese bo!’ “Ne ɔrɔ̃go kɔdze ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, ‘Ooɣo!
Loiɣe mi!’ ” Ne Yesu ɔwirigu ma igbã sɔ, “Ne ɔso midzuɛ̃ so alasɔ miiɣe iyi ɣee ɔwi gɔ ame loaba.
Kumɛgɔ Boala Ara Wa I Ɣaa Ɔsu Ɔpia Bo I Nrɔɔ̃ Ame Kukaakɔ.
“Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ aase lɛ ngbe.
Ɔwi ɔwɛ̃ ame ne, ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ to ɔkɛlɛ ɔri dzoroa, ne ɔso ɔkpere ɔ̃ maɖabo ɔsu ɔ̃ karana ɔpia ma i nrɔɔ̃ ame.
Ɔtã ma ɔbiara i ma ɔle kanya.
Ɔwɛ̃ ne, ɔtã wũ sikã sikoto iru, ɔwɛ̃ ana ikoto inyɔ fiɛ ɔwɛ̃ ana ɔkoto ɔwɛ̃ fiɛ ɔrui ɔkɛlɛ ɔri.
Ɔɖabo gɔ lofɔ ikoto iru ɔkɛlɛ ɔsɛ ɔ̃afinikira nrɔɔ̃ i ɔ̃ sikã iso ɔna ikoto iru mama ɔsia i iso.
Ngbɔ ame ngɔ lofɔ ikoto inyɔ ana ɔsɛ ɔ̃ana ikoto inyɔ ɔbua ne.
Ɣɛɛ ɔɖabo gɔ lofɔ ɔkoto ɔwɛ̃ ne, ɔkɛlɛ ɔsɛ ɔ̃akuri iwo ɔsu makɔse sikã ɔkɔla.
“Ayi gbodzoo kama ne, makɔse ɔba sɔ si ɔba ɔ̃akigu ma i siko ame ɔnyɔ nnɛ maɔna masia.
Ɔɖabo gɔ lofɔ sikã ikoto iru ɔsu sikoto iru nɛ ɔna ɔsia i iso ɔbɔ.
Ɔɣere makɔse sɔ, ‘Tete, sikã ikoto iru atã me ɣɛɛ loɔna ikoto iru mama lobua iso.’ “Makɔse ɔɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Ɖafe, ɔɖabo sɛɛ gu nukuarese aɖe!
Gɔ aɖe ɔnukuare i ara kosoi ame ɔso ne, loasu ara siare lopia i fɔ nrɔɔ̃ ame.
Ba nagu me isoɣɔ!’ “Ɔɖabo gɔ matã sikã ikoto inyɔ ana ɔba ɔ̃abo, ne ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Tete, sikã ikoto inyɔ iɖe atã me, ɣɛɛ ne, nyɔ, loɔna ikoto inyɔ losia i iso.’ “Makɔse ɔɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Ɖafe, ɔɖabo sɛɛ gu nukuarese aɖe.
Kumɛgɔ aɖe ɔnukuare i ara kosoi ame ɔso ne, loasu ara siare lopia-ɔ i nrɔɔ̃ ame.
Ba nagu me isoɣɔ!’ “Ne ɔɖabo gɔ matã sikã ɔkoto ɔwɛ̃ ana ɔba ɔ̃abo ne.
Ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Tete, loɣe sɔ ɔturi gɔ itɔ̃me mba ɔle aɖe.
Asɛ asu aɖera i ngbegɔ aikpɛ̃, fiɛ asɛ asa ɔraɖui kanya i ngbegɔ aisa ɔraɖui.
Ne ɔso gɔ loto lonigã-ɔ ɔso ne, lokuri karɔ̃ losu fɔ sikã lobiara.
Nya fɔ sikã i ngbe!’ “Ne makɔse ɔfɔ kanya sɔ, ‘Ɔɖabo lalaa gu dãdze aɖe.
Aɣe sɔ nsɛ losu aɖera i ngbegɔ loikpɛ̃ fiɛ nsɛ losa ɔraɖui kanya i ngbegɔ loisa ɔraɖui?
Iyɔ be ɔso fiɛ aisu wũ sikã asɛ aasɛ i sikã kakɔlakɔ̃ sɔ si loba ne, loasɛ loafɔ sɛ̃ ku kusia?’ “Ne ɔ̃ ɔkɔse ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Mimɔɛ̃ sikã mifɔ i ɔ̃ kɔrɛ misu mitã ngɔ mba ikoto iweo.’ Alasɔ ɔbiara gɔ mba ira ne, maatã wũ mabua ɔna isi gbodzoo, ɣɛɛ ngɔ nna kuira ne, kɛkɛĩ gɔ ame ɔba ne, maamɔɛ̃ mafɔ wũ iso.
Ɔɖabo gɔ nna kusia kukuwɛ̃ i ngbe ɣɛɛ ne, mifuĩdza wũ mipia i idududu ame ngbegɔ i kaku gu arɔĩ iɖo ikpa pia.
Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi Loaɣɛgu Kayiiso Ɔɖuɖu Atɔ̃me.
“Ɔwi gɔ i Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi aaba lɛ igara gu ɔ̃ makpabo ne, ɔto ɔ̃asɛ i ɔ̃ sigaraiyara iso.
Fiɛ kayiiso maturi ɔɖuɖu aaya i ɔ̃ katɔ̃.
Mmɔ ɔ̃aɣɛ ma ame lɛ kumɛgɔ i ngɔ nto ɔɣedza masɛrɛ sɛ ɔɣɛ kutepuĩ gu masɛrɛrerɔ̃ ame ne.
Ɔto ɔ̃atã maturi bɔlɔlɔa ɔya i ɔ̃ kuɖearɔ̃ iso fiɛ malalaa ana aaya i ɔ̃ kubena iso.
“Ne igara aaɣere mma nɣɛ wũ i kuɖearɔ̃ iso sɔ, ‘Miba, mi ma i Tete ɔtã isobuɛ, miba miabo i sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ga maledza masɛ mi ta kayi karɔ̃kasɛkɔ̃ ame.
Alasɔ kukã ɔkpɛ̃ me, mitã me aɖera, ɔme ɔkore me, mitã me ndu lonɛ, loɖe ɔfɔ lobo mi, mifɔ me.
Minya me losɛ isɔ̃, mitã me arapia, gɔ lonyɛ ne, minyɔ me iso fiɛ gɔ mamɔɛ̃ me marara i iyo ne, miba minyɔ me.’ “Mmɔ i maturi bɔlɔlɔa aakarɛ wũ sɔ, ‘Bosate, ku mme ɔwi bonya-ɔ sɔ kukã to-ɔ botã-ɔ aɖera ɣee ɔme ɔkore-ɔ botã-ɔ ndu?
Ku mme ɔwi bonya-ɔ aɖe ɔfɔ aba bo kɔrɛ fiɛ bofɔ-ɔ ɣee asɛ isɔ̃ botã-ɔ arapia?
Ku mme ɔwi bonɔ sɔ ato anyɛ boba boaya-ɔ ɣee mamɔɛ̃-ɔ marara i iyo boba boaya-ɔ?’ “Mmɔ i igara aatã ma mmuai sɔ, ‘Ira biara nɛ miabara mitã manyii ma loire kuira i ngbe ne, mme mibara mitã.’ “Ne ka ɔ̃aɣere mma i ɔ̃ kubena iso sɔ, ‘Mirui me i kɔrɛ mi ma i Ɣaa ɔgbarĩ.
Mikɛlɛ itɔkpe nɛ mapia masɛ Ɔbosam gu ɔ̃ makpabo fiɛ iisɛ inyi ame!
Alasɔ kukã ɔkpɛ̃ me, miitã me aɖera, ɔme ɔkore me, miitã me ndu.
Loba loabo mi lɛ ɔfɔ, ɣɛɛ miifɔ me, losɛ isɔ̃ miitã me arapia.
Nto lonyɛ, miinyɔ me iso mamɔɛ̃ me marara i iyo miiba mianyɔ me.’ “Mmɔ maakarɛ wũ sɔ, ‘Bosate, ku mme ɔwi bonya sɔ kukã ɣee ɔme ɔkore-ɔ ɣee aɖe ɔfɔ ɣee asɛ isɔ̃ ɣee ato anyɛ ɣee arɛ i iyo fiɛ boibuai-ɔ?’ “Ne igara aatã ma mmuai sɔ, ‘Nto loɣere mi sɔ ira biara nɛ misɛ̃ sɔ miito mibara mitã manyii ma loire kuira i ngbe ne, mme miibara mitã!’ “Mmagbe ne, maakɛlɛ ngbegɔ inyɛwe iibaro inya fiɛ maturi sɛɛ ne, maakɛlɛ isoɣɔ nɛ loibaro inya ame.”
Ma Yudase Makpakpa Ɔsɛ Iti Ame Sɔ Maaɖoe Yesu.
Gɔ Yesu ɔɔɣɛ ara wagbe ɔɖuɖu ɔro ne, ɔɣere ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Miɣe sɔ iɔkuti ayi anyɔ gɔ maaɖe Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo Iyi fiɛ maaɖi mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, matã mapɛ me mamatãra i kudziri iso.” Masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu kaɖe makpakpa ɔsarɛ i Kayafa gɔ nɖe masɔrɛdze ɔkpakpa pelepele iyo.
Ne masɛ iti ame sɔ maamɔɛ̃ Yesu i iwɛrɛ ame maaɖoe.
Ɣɛɛ maɣɛ sɔ, “Boiba bara ne ku iyi ɔɖewi, si iiɖe ngbɔ kulu to kuaba.” Masɔla Yesu Nnɔĩ I Betania.
Gɔ Yesu ɔsɛ Betania ne, ɔsɛ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Simon, fiɛ ɔnyɛ ɔnyɛrɛtɛa ɔnya iyo.
Gɔ Yesu si ɔto ɔɖe ara ne, ɔrɔ̃go ɔwɛ̃ ɔbɔ nnɔĩ mɛ nsɛ mifɔrɛ̃ kɔrɔ̃kɔrɔ̃ fiɛ mipia i ita inɔĩbui ame ɔba ɔ̃afere wũ iti.
Gɔ marasuãdze ɔnya nnɛgbe ne, ikpɛ̃ ma sikpã.
Ne mato makarɛ sɔ, “Be nɖe karanina gagbe?
Tee maawo nnɔĩ mɛgbe ɔrɔdɛ̃ ku kuɣa siare masu sikã matã mawɛrɛba!” Yesu ɣe nnɛ mato maɣɛ, ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Be ɔso mito miɖaa wũ?
Ira sɛɛ iɖe ɔbara ɔtã me.
Mawɛrɛba to maawe i mi kɔrɛ ɔwi biara, ɣɛɛ mme ne, loito loawe i mi kɔrɛ ɖaa.
Ɔrɔ̃go gɔgbe nnɔĩ mɛ ɔsɔla me ngbe ne, ɔ̃ɔledza me ɔtã ibiara.
Ne ɔso nto losia ita lotã mi sɔ, kakɔi biara ga maaɣɛ Itɔ̃me Bielea nɛgbe ne, maasu nnɛ ɔbara ɔtã me ngbe manyigi wũ ala.” Yuda Iskariot Ɔfɔ Sikã Sɔ Ɔ̃aɖi Yesu Ɔtã.
Ne ɔ̃ marasuãdze iweo-inyɔ ndɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Yuda Iskariot ɔkɛlɛ masɔrɛdze makpakpa kɔrɛ, ɔsɛ ɔ̃akarɛ ma sɔ, “Be miatã me si loɖi Yesu lotã mi?” Ne ɔso maka sikãfudza abi sitɛ matã wũ.
Ita i ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, Yuda ɔtsɛ ɔri sɛɛ gɔ iso ɔ̃aki fiɛ ɔ̃aɖi Yesu ɔtã ma ibie.
Yesu Gu Ɔ̃ Marasuãdze Ɔɖe Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo Iyi Aɖera.
I iyi ɖeakatɔ̃ nɛ iso masɛ maɖe Boɖoboɖo Gɔ Loita Iyi ne, marasuãdze ɔba maakarɛ Yesu sɔ, “Lɛ ato abie sɔ bowa Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo iyi aɖera botã-ɔ?” Ne ɔpia ma ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ kɔrɛ i ɔmagɛ̃ ame ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Miɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Ratedze sɔ, “Wũ ɔwi ɔɔɣo, gu wũ marasuãdze aaɖe Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo aɖera i fɔ iyo.” ’ ” Marasuãdze ɔbara lɛ kumɛgɔ i Yesu ɔɣere ma, ne mawa Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo aɖera ne.
Gɔ kutsuɛ ɔɣo ne, Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze iweo-inyɔ ɔsɛ i karɔ̃ matsɛ aɖera iɖe.
Ɔwi gɔ mato maɖe ara ne, Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Nto loɣere mi sɔ mi ndɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ to ɔ̃aɖi me ɔtã.” Itɔ̃me nɛgbe ɔɖaa marasuãdze, ne mato makarɛ wũ isia isia sɔ, “Bosate, loɣe sɔ iiɖe mme ato.
Bɛrɛ mme ɔɖe?” Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ngɔ nto ɔpiagu me kɔrɔ̃ i irɔi ame ɔɖe loaɖi me ɔtã.
Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi to ɔ̃akpi lɛ kumɛgɔ i Ɔko Sekelea ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ, ɣɛɛ ndzo miɖe mitã ngɔ loaɖi wũ ɔtã.
Si maiɣe ɔnyiiɔ kɔra ne, ilɛ wũ iɖo!” Ne Yuda gɔ loɖi wũ ɔtã ɔtara kanya ɔkarɛ sɔ, “Ratedze, loɣe sɔ iiɖe mme ato lo?” Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Fɔ nto aɣɛ.” Maɖe Bosate Aɖera Tsɔra.
Ɔwi gɔ masi mato maɖe ara ne, Yesu ɔsu boɖoboɖo, ne gɔ ɔpɛ Ɣaa siba i ɔ̃ iti ne, ɔsu ɔtã ma ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Mifɔ miɖe, wũ sosina i ngbe ne.” Ne ɔsu ndã ikɔi ne, gɔ ɔpɛ Ɣaa siba i ne iti ne, ɔsu ɔtã ma, ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mifɔ minɛ.
Wũ ima nɛ nto isia ita i Ɣaa ndamu ɣɛtɛ iso ne, ima nɛ mafere i karɔ̃ itã maturi gbodzoo akpi isu itsɛ.
Nto loɣere mi gbaã sɔ loisibanɛ ndã gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ iyi nɛ loanɛgu mi miɣɛtɛ i wũ Ɔse sigarakaɖekɔ̃.” Ne gɔ maka kuka male Ɣaa ne, mabɔrɛ makɛlɛ Nnɔĩ Adziri Kube iso.
Yesu Ɔɣɛ Ɔsɛ Sɔ Petro To Ɔ̃asɛ̃ Wũ.
Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Kasɛ̃ gagbe ne, mi ɔɖuɖu to miatere minyua me, ikuti wũ ɔnɔwɛ̃, alasɔ Ɔko Sekelea ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Ɣaa to ɔ̃aɖoe masɛrɛkɔdze fiɛ ɔ̃ masɛrɛ aasame.’ Ɣɛɛ si loɔta lobɔrɛ i makpise ame ne, nto loaɖe mi katɔ̃ lokɛlɛ Galilea.” Petro ɔtara kanya sɔ, “Si matsɔra ɔɖuɖu aatere maɣɛ-ɔ kɔra ne, mme loibatere loɣɛ-ɔ lonya ɖa!” Ne Yesu ɔɣere Petro sɔ, “Si makɔkɔ aaɖi kanya nɔme ne, ato aasɛ̃ me ikpɛ itɛ sɔ aiɣe me.” Petro ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Si inya sɔ loakpigu-ɔ kɔra ne, loibasɛ̃-ɔ lonya ɖa.” Marasuãdze tsɔra ana ɔɣɛ ngbɔ ame.
Yesu Ɔkparama Kayi I Getsemane.
Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔrui makɛlɛ ngbegɔ marɔ sɔ Getsemane, ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Misɛ i ngbe si lokɛlɛ mmɔ loakparama kayi.” Ɔkɔ Petro gu Zebedeo mabi inyɔ, ne ɔtsɛ so imararã iti ikpakpa ne.
Ɔɣere ma sɔ, “So to sima me ta wũ ɔtu ame gɔ loɔro ɔfɛ̃, misɛ i ngbe si midzuɛ̃gu me.” Ne gɔ ɔkɛlɛ katɔ̃ kɛkɛĩ ne, ɔkɔlɛ ɔfu i karɔ̃ ɔkparama kayi ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Tete, si ialɛ ne, tã inyɛwe ɔwi gɔgbe si ɔta ɔwara me!
Ɣɛɛ ne, iiɖe wũ kuɖɔɛ, nnɛ i fɔ aɖɔɛ si abara.” Gɔ ɔkpese ɔba marasuãdze itɛ mamɔ kɔrɛ ne, ɔnya sɔ maɔrɛ sirɛ, ne ɔɣere Petro sɔ, “Ne ɔso miibawo me ɔsɛ ɔdzuɛ̃gu bidɛ ɔɖɔwũ ɔwɛ̃?
Misɛ mila miɔdzuɛ̃ si mikparama kayi si miibabo i ilainyɔ ame.
Siwarã ɣɛ teteree, ɣɛɛ siturina ɔɔfɛ̃.” Yesu ɔledza ikɛlɛ isɛ iakparama kayi iɣɛ sɔ, “Tete, si aibasɛnɛkɛ̃ra ikɔi nɛgbe aɖi me iso iɖo sɔ loanɛ ne, bara fɔ kuɖɔɛ, ne iiɖe wũ kure.” Gɔ ɔkpese ɔba ne, ɔnya sɔ marasuãdze ɔɔrɛ sirɛ, ala sirɛ to si mɔɛ̃ ma.
Yesu ɔrui i ma kɔrɛ ɔsɛ ɔ̃aledza kayi ikparama iɣɛ atɔ̃me wamɔ ame.
Ɔkpese ɔba marasuãdze kɔrɛ fiɛ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mikpese mirɛ mito miwarã?
Minyɔ ɔwi ɔɔɣo, maɔɖi Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi mapia makpibaradze i nrɔɔ̃ ame.
Mita si borui!
Minyɔ, miɔnya ngɔ nto ɔɖi me ɔtã.” Ma Yudase Ɔmɔɛ̃ Yesu.
Yesu ɣɛ ɔto ɔɣɛ ara wagbe fiɛ Yuda gɔ nɖe marasuãdze iweo-inyɔ ɔwɛ̃ ɔba ɔ̃abo.
Ɔsɛgu maturi gbodzoo ma i masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu kaɖe makpakpa ɔpia fiɛ mato atekpe gu kudziriku.
Ngɔ loɖi wũ ɔtã ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ngɔ minya sɔ loya fiɛ lofiɔ̃ irɛkpo ne, ɔ̃ ɔɖe ne, mimɔɛ̃ wũ!” Yuda ɔsɛ tiĩ ɔkɛlɛ Yesu kɔrɛ, ne ɔya wũ ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Isobuɛ itã-ɔ, ratedze.” Ne ɔfiɔ̃ wũ irɛkpo ne.
Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Wũ ɔlaa nnɛ ɔso aba ne, tã ipɛ-ɔ siwa si abara ne!” Ne mma i Yuda sɛgu ɔbore mabo Yesu fiɛ mamɔɛ̃ wũ teteree ne.
Mma nsiai Yesu mmɔ ɔwɛ̃ ɔɖi ɔ̃ itekpe ɔtu masɔrɛdze ɔkpakpa pelepele ɔɖabo kutsue.
Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Pia fɔ itekpe i ɔyuɛ ame ala mma ɔɖuɖu nsɛ masu atekpe i maturi iso ne, atekpe kanya maakpi.
Bɛrɛ miiɣe sɔ loawo wũ Ɔse ɔbiɛ ɔkpere ɔluwɛ̃ ɔsese me Ɣaa makpabo kpakpɛ̃dze akuri aweo-anyɔ ɔbɔrɛgu i kato?
Ɣɛɛ si iiba ngbɔ ne, nnɛ matsɛrɛ masɛ i Ɔko Sekelea ame iibaba i ne ame.” Ne Yesu ɔkarɛ maturi gbodzoo mamɔ sɔ, “Be ɔso fiɛ miaba miamɔɛ̃ me ku apɛmi gu kudziriku lɛ yukukpe loɖe?
Gɔ iyi biara lopia i isɔrɛyo nto lote ara ne, be ɔso miimɔɛ̃ me?
Ɣɛɛ nwagbe ɔɖuɖu ɔba i ne ame sɔ nnɛ i kanyamaɖidze ɔtsɛrɛ i Ɔko Sekelea ame aaba i ne ame.” Ne ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔɖuɖu ɔrui matere maɣɛ wũ ne.
Maɣɛgu Yesu Atɔ̃me.
Mma lomɔɛ̃ Yesu ɔkɔ wũ makɛlɛgu Kayafa iyo ngbegɔ i mmara matedze gu kaɖe makpakpa ɔsakanya.
Petro ɔsiai ma kamakama ɔsɛ ɔ̃abo sɔrɛdzekpakpa pelepele kakpataku ame.
Ɔsɛ ɔ̃asɛ i madzuɛ̃se kɔrɛ sɔ si ɔnyɔ kumɛgɔ i ira biara aakɛlɛ i katɔ̃.
Masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu matɔ̃meɣɛdze ɔɖuɖu ɔbie itɔ̃me nɛ maanyi masia Yesu iso fiɛ maaɖoe wũ.
Ɣɛɛ maina kuiwɛ̃ atoa sɔ maturi gbodzoo ɔba maala mila masia wũ iso.
Kama ne, marɛrɛ̃ inyɔ mawɛ̃ ɔba, ne maɣɛ sɔ, “Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Loabiɛ Ɣaa isɔrɛyo loledza ne itsue i ayi atɛ ame.’ ” Sɔrɛdzekpakpa pelepele ɔta ɔya ɔɣere Yesu sɔ, “Nwa ɔɖuɖu mato maɣɛ ne, ana kuira aaɣɛ i wã iso?” Ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔma kanya kpa.
Ne sɔrɛdzekpakpa pelepele ɔledza iɣɛ sɔ, “I Ɣaa iyere ame ne, nto lokã ndamu lotã-ɔ sɔ, ɣere bo si fɔ nɖe Kristo gɔ nɖe Ɣaa Ɔbi.” Ne Yesu ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Aĩ, ngbɔ iɖe ne.
Ɣɛɛ nto loɣere mi sɔ ita i kiniɔ ne, mito mianya Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi gɔ ɔsi i Ɔlesate kuɖearɔ̃ iso fiɛ ɔto ɔba i adɔdɔ ame!” Gɔ ɔɣɛ ngbɔ ne, sɔrɛdzekpakpa pelepele ɔkɛ ɔ̃ awu ne ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Mmusuo!
Maɖansiɛ kumawɛ̃ iisinya bo.
Mi ɔɖuɖu ɔnɔ mmusuo itɔ̃me nɛ ɔɣɛ!
Nda minya?” Ma ɔɖuɖu ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Ikote sɔ ɔ̃akpi!” Matua minyatu mafere wũ i katɔ̃, mapɛ wũ, fiɛ mma lopɛ wũ sirɔ̃ta to maɣere wũ sɔ, “Gɔ fɔ nɖe Kristo ne, ɣere bo ngɔ lopɛ-ɔ!” Petro Ɔsɛ̃ Sɔ Ɔ̃iɣe Yesu.
Gɔ Petro si i kakpataku ame mmɔ ne, sɔrɛdzekpakpa pelepele ɔɖaborɔ̃go ɔwɛ̃ ɔba ɔ̃aɣere wũ sɔ, “Fɔ wũ asiai Yesu gɔ lobɔrɛ i Galilea karɔ̃ iso.” Ɣɛɛ Petro ɔsɛ̃ i ma ɔɖuɖu katɔ̃ sɔ, “Loiɣe nnɛ ato aɣɛ i ngbe.” Ne ɔbɔrɛ ɔkɛlɛ ɔsɛ ɔ̃aya i kayogodɔ̃ ne.
Ɔɖaborɔ̃go mama ɔnya wũ gɔ ɔɣɛ, ne ɔɣere marɛrɛ̃ ma nɣɛ i mmɔ sɔ, “Ɔ̃ wũ ɔsiai Yesu Nasaretse.” Mmɔ ana Petro ɔsɛ̃ ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Lokã sɔ loiɣe ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔmɔ!” Iidzoro fiɛ marɛrɛ̃ ma nɣɛ i mmɔ ɔɣere Petro sɔ, “Fɔ wũ ma ndɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ aɖe ala fɔ ikaɖe ɔɖi-ɔ itã!” Ne Petro ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Lokã sɔ ɔnukuare nto loɣɛ!
Ɣaa si ɔkpadzɛ̃ me kutsue si iiɖe gbaã iɖe sɔ loiɣe ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔmɔ!” Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, kɔkɔ ɔɖi kanya.
Ne Petro ɔnyigi nnɛ i Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Si kɔkɔ aaɖi kanya ne, ato aasɛ̃ me ikpɛ itɛ sɔ aiɣe me.” Ne ɔso Petro ɔbɔrɛ ɔkɛlɛ inyamɔ ɔsɛ ɔ̃abiɛ kaku teteree.
Makɔ Yesu Makɛlɛgu Pilato Kɔrɛ.
Kaya tutuutu ne, masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu kaɖe makpakpa ɔbara adzuni sɔ maaɖoe Yesu.
Manyi wũ fiɛ masu wũ masɛ maapia i Roma Abã ɔkpakpa Pilato nrɔɔ̃ ame.
Yuda Iskariot Ɔɖoe So.
Gɔ Yuda gɔ loɖi Yesu ɔtã ɔnɔ sɔ maɔtã Yesu kukpi ipɔ ne, ibo wũ so, ne ɔso ɔkpesegu sikãfudza abi sitɛ wa ɔfɔ ɔkɛlɛgu masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu kaɖe makpakpa.
Ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Lobara ikpi, alasɔ loɖi ɔturi gɔ loibara ikpi lotã sɔ maɖoe.” Ne matã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Fɔ itɔ̃me iɖe ne iisu bo kuira i mmɔ.” Ne Yuda ɔsa sikã ɔfere i isɔrɛyo fiɛ ɔrui ɔsɛ ɔ̃asa so ɔɖoe ne.
Ne masɔrɛdze makpakpa ɔsu sikã fiɛ maɣɛ sɔ, “Ima sikã siɖe i ngbe fiɛ bo mmara iitã ɔri sɔ boasu sɛ̃ bopia i isɔrɛyo sikã ame.” Gɔ maɣɛ manɔgu so karɔ̃ ne, masu sɛ̃ masɛ maaɣa karɔ̃ ga masɛ marɔ sɔ, “Rapɔdze Karɔ̃” sɔ maala ma ɔbiara mafɔ i mmɔ.
Ne ɔso fiɛ ipɛ i nɔme ne, masɛ marɔ karɔ̃ gamɔ sɔ Ima Karɔ̃ ne.
Ne ɔso nnɛ i kanyaɖidze Yeremia ɔɣɛ ɔba i ne ame sɔ, “Masu sikãfudza abi sitɛ wa i Israel maturi ɔnɔ karɔ̃ sɔ maatã i ɔ̃ iti, masɛ maaɣa rapɔdze karɔ̃ lɛ kumɛgɔ i Bosate ɔɣere me.” Pilato Ɔkarɛ Yesu Atɔ̃me.
Yesu ɔya i Roma Abã Ɔkpakpa Pilato katɔ̃ fiɛ ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Fɔ nɖe ma Yudase Igara?” Yesu ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Aĩ.
Nnɛ ato aɣɛ pia i ne ame.” Ɣɛɛ nwa ɔɖuɖu i masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu kaɖe makpakpa ɔɣɛ ne, ɔ̃itã mmuai.
Ne Pilato to ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ato anɔ nwa ɔɖuɖu mato maɣɛ i fɔ iso?” Ibara abã ɔkpakpa ɣaa gbaã kumɛgɔ i Yesu ɔsɛ̃ sɔ ɔ̃ito ɔtã ku itɔ̃me mmuai.
Pilato Ɔtã Yesu Kukpi Ipɔ.
Ikɔ biara si ma Yudase to maɖe Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo Iyi ne, Roma abã ɔkpakpa sɛ ɔnyua yorɛdze ɔwɛ̃ gɔ i kaɖe ɔkarɛ ɔtã ma.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, yorɛdze ɔwɛ̃ gɔ iyere loɔre i ara lalaa ibara ame fiɛ marɔ wũ sɔ Baraba ɔwe.
Ne ɔso gɔ maturi gbodzoo ɔsakanya ne, Pilato ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Nna mito mibie sɔ lonyua lotã mi?
Baraba ɛɛbɛrɛ Yesu gɔ mato makpere sɔ Kristo?” Ɔbara ngbɔ alasɔ ɔnya sɔ ma Yudase makpakpa ne, sirerɛ ɔso kere maɖi wũ matã.
Gɔ Pilato si ɔ̃ atɔ̃mekaɣɛkɔ̃ iyo ame ne, ɔ̃ ɔre ɔpia wũ ɔturi ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Daapia kanya i ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔmɔ itɔ̃me ame alasɔ ɔ̃ibara kuira nɛ loatã maɖoe wũ.
Losɛ̃ arɛ nyanyarĩa i ɔ̃ iti i kasɛ̃ ame.” Masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu kaɖe makpakpa ɔɣɛ mapia maturi sɔ makarɛ Pilato sɔ ɔnyua Baraba ɔtã ma si ɔɖoe Yesu.
Ne ɔso gɔ Pilato ɔkarɛ iturikuri sɔ, “Nna mito mibie sɔ lonyua lotã mi?” ne, matã mmuai sɔ, “Baraba!” Ne Pilato to ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Be si lobara Yesu gɔ marɔ sɔ Kristo?” Matã mmuai sɔ, “Pɛ wũ matãra i kudziri iso!” Pilato ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Mme ikpi iɖe ɔbara.” Ne masiagu kulu teteree sɔ, “Pɛ wũ matãra i kudziri iso!” Gɔ Pilato ɔnya sɔ ɔ̃ibawo ma adzuni ɔfinikira ne kulu to kuaba ne, ɔsu ndu ɔfore nrɔɔ̃ i iturikuri katɔ̃ ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Wũ kɔrɔ̃ gu kukpa na i ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe kukpi ame.
Mi itɔ̃me iɖe.” Ne iturikuri to matã mmuai sɔ, “Ɔ̃ kukpi ato si aba i bo gu bo mabi iti iso!” Pilato ɔnyua Baraba ɔtã ma, ne gɔ ɔtã mapɛ Yesu ala iporoibi ne, ɔnyua wũ ɔtã ma sɔ masɛ maapɛ wũ mamatãra i kudziri iso.
Makpakpɛ̃dze Ɔbara Yesu Aɣiãra.
Ne Pilato makpakpɛ̃dze ɔkɔ Yesu mapia i Abã ɔkpakpa iyo ame fiɛ makpakpɛ̃dze ikuri ɔɖuɖu ɔki malɔ wũ ne.
Maɖi wũ ɔ̃ arapia fiɛ masu ɔgo rɛtɛa awu mapia wũ.
Masu miyu mabara ala igarakoto matɔ̃medza wũ fiɛ masu ɔdziri matã wũ.
Mapɛ agɛgɛ̃ i ɔ̃ katɔ̃, fiɛ ka mato mabara wũ aɣiãra sɔ, “Ii iɖuu!
Ma Yudase Igara si ɔsɛ ngbã dzoroo.” Matua minyatu mafere wũ fiɛ masu ɔdziri maɖeɖe wũ iti.
Gɔ maɔbara wũ aɣiãra maro ne, maɖi wũ ɔgo rɛtɛa awu wa mapia wũ fiɛ makpesegu ɔ̃ are mapia wũ fiɛ maɣo ɔri sɔ maapɛ wũ mamatãra i kudziri iso.
Mapɛ Yesu Mamatãra I Kudziri Iso.
Gɔ mato mabɔrɛ i ɔmagɛ̃ ame ne, manya ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ lobɔrɛ i Kirene fiɛ marɔ wũ sɔ Simon.
Makpakpɛ̃dze ɔya wũ iso sɔ ɔfɔgu Yesu ɔnyigbã gɔ ɔsore.
Masɛ maabo ngbegɔ masɛ marɔ sɔ Golgata gɔ karɔ̃ nɖe sɔ Ɔturi Itikui.
Matã Yesu ndã mɛ masakanya ku kua gɔ mba ɔɖo sɔ ɔnɛ, ɣɛɛ gɔ ɔti ɔnyɔ ne, ɔsɛ̃ sɔ ɔ̃ito ɔnɛ.
Makpakpɛ̃dze ɔpɛ wũ mamatara i kudziri iso fiɛ ka mapɛ sibɔ ala atalebi i ɔ̃ awu iti si matsue ɔbiara nwa loaɣo wũ.
Ne kama ne, masɛ i mmɔ mato madzuɛ̃ wũ.
I ɔ̃ sitikpe ne, matsɛrɛ masia i kakoloi kawɛ̃ iso nnɛ ɔso maɖoe wũ.
Matsɛrɛ sɔ, “Yesu, ma Yudase Igara ngbe ne.” Mapɛ mayukukpe inyɔ ana mamatãra ku wũ, ɔwɛ̃ i ɔ̃ kuɖearɔ̃ fiɛ ɔwɛ̃ ana i ɔ̃ kubena iso.
Mma nto mafe to matidza ma ati fiɛ mato matia Yesu.
Maɣere wũ sɔ, “Fɔ gɔ fɔ sɔ aabiɛ Ɣaa iyo aledza ne itsue i ayi atɛ ame!
Si Ɣaa Ɔbi aɖe ne, bɛse so i kudziri iso si aɖi so.” Ngbɔ ame i masɔrɛdze makpakpa, mmara matedze gu kaɖe makpakpa ana ɔma wũ maɣɛ sɔ, “Ɔbuai mamama, ɣɛɛ ɔ̃ mɔmɔ iito ɔwo so ɔɖi.
Iiɖe sɔ ɔ̃ nɖe Israel igara?
Si ɔbɛse so i kudziri iso kiniɔ ne, boto boafɔ wũ boɖe!
Ɔfɔ Ɣaa ɔɖe fiɛ ɔto ɔɣɛ sɔ ɔ̃ nɖe Ɣaa Ɔbi mɔmɔ, mitã bonyɔ si Ɣaa aaso ɔba ɔ̃aɖi wũ!” Ta mayukukpe ma mapɛ mamatãra ku wũ ana ɔtia wũ ngbɔ.
Yesu Ɔkpi.
Kakɔme iɖɔwũ iweo-inyɔ ame ne, kayi ɔsɛ̃ guduu ifɔ iɖɔwũ itɛ.
Lɛ kakɔme iɖɔwũ itɛ ame ne, Yesu ɔla kulu teteree sɔ, “Eli, Eli, lama sabaktani?” Gɔ karɔ̃ nɖe sɔ, “Wũ Ɣaa, wũ Ɣaa, be ɔso fiɛ anyua me asɛ ngbɔ?” Mma nɣɛ i mmɔ fiɛ manɔ wũ ne, maɣɛ sɔ, “Ɔto ɔkpere Eliya!” Ma ndɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɔtere ɔsu ɖɔti pukupukua ɔpia i ndã bea ame ɔsu ɔɖu i ɔdziri iso ɔtara ɔtã wũ sɔ ɔnɛ.
Ɣɛɛ matsɔra ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Miya!
Mitã bonyɔ si Eliya aaba ɔ̃aɖi wũ i kudziri iso.” Yesu ɔledza kulu ila teteree kere ne ka ɔsɔra ne.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame tutuutu ne ɔkati kpikpirikpi gɔ nsa i Kasɔrɛkɔ̃ ɔkɛ aka anyɔ ita i kato iba karɔ̃.
Karɔ̃ ɔti fiɛ ata ɔbiɛbiɛ, akpibiɔ ɔbusi, fiɛ maturi sekelea gbodzoo ma loɔkpi mafegu ɔta mabɔrɛ i makpise ame.
Mabɔrɛ i ma akpibiɔ ame fiɛ ɔwi gɔ i Yesu ɔta ɔbɔrɛ i makpise ame ne, makɛlɛ Ɔmagɛ̃ Sekelea ame fiɛ maturi gbodzoo ɔnya ma.
Gɔ kpakpɛ̃dze ɔkpakpa gu makpakpɛ̃dze ma nɣɛ mato madzuɛ̃ Yesu ɔnya karɔ̃ iti gu ira biara nɛ loba ne, maɣɛ i ifɔ̃ ame sɔ, “Gbaã ne, Ɣaa Ɔbi ɔɖe i ngbe!” Marɔ̃go gbodzoo ɔya dzoroo mala maɔnyɔ nnɛ nto ikɛlɛ i katɔ̃.
Marɔ̃go magbe losiai wũ mabɔrɛ i Galilea fiɛ mala maɔbuai wũ ne.
Ma nɖe Maria Magdalase gu Maria Yakobo gu Yosef mɛrɛ̃ ɔnyi gu Zebedeo ɔre.
Yosef Gɔ Lobɔrɛ I Arimatea Ɔbiara Yesu Kpise.
Gɔ kutsuɛ ɔɣo ne, ranase ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Yosef fiɛ ɔbɔrɛ i Arimatea ɔba.
Ɔ̃ wũ ne, Yesu rasuãdze ɔɖe.
Ɔsɛ Pilato kɔrɛ ɔsɛ ɔ̃akarɛ sɔ ɔsu Yesu kpise ɔtã wũ, ne Pilato ɔɖi ɔri sɔ masu matã wũ ne.
Ne ɔso Yosef ɔsu kpise ɔmini i ɔkati ɣɛtɛ ame, Ɔsu ɔrara i ɔ̃ ikpibiɔ nɛ ɔɖi ɔsɛ so i ita ame, ne ka ɔli ita siare ɔtɛ̃ i kanya fiɛ ɔrui ɔkɛlɛ iyo ne.
Maria Magdalase gu Maria nyɔare si mato manyɔ ikpibiɔ katɔ̃.
Madzuɛ̃ Yesu Ikpibiɔ.
Kaɖesɛ̃a ga nɖe Iwarãyi ne, masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu ma Farisise ɔsarɛgu Pilato.
Ne maɣere wũ sɔ, “Ɔbea, boto bonyigi sɔ gɔ ladze gɔmɔ si ngbã ne, ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Nto loaledza ita ibɔrɛ i makpise ame ku iyi tɛare si lokpi.’ Ne ɔso boto bobie sɔ tã ɔle si madzuɛ̃ ɔ̃ ikpibiɔ kukaakɔ sɔ ɔ̃ marasuãdze iibasɛ maayu ɔ̃ kpise mafiniki maɣere maturi sɔ ɔta ɔbɔrɛ i makpise ame.
Sila tsɔra dzɛgbe to sianyanyarĩ siɖo siɖeakatɔ̃.” Ne Pilato ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mikɔ makpakpɛ̃dze mikɛlɛgu si mitã madzuɛ̃ ikpibiɔ lɛ kumɛgɔ miɖɔɛ.” Ne ɔso marui masɛ maasɛ̃ ikpibiɔ kukaakɔ, masɛ ne ikparĩ fiɛ ka matã makpakpɛ̃dze ɣɛ mato madzuɛ̃.
Yesu Ɔta Ɔbɔrɛ I Makpise Ame.
Iwarãyi kama, ku Kɔsiɖa ɔɖesɛrã ne, Maria Magdalase gu Maria nyɔare ɔkɛlɛ sɔ maanyɔ Yesu ikpibiɔ.
Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, karɔ̃ ɔti teteree, Ɣaa kpabo ɔso ɔbɔrɛ i kato ɔli ita nɛ masɛ̃ i ikpibiɔ kanya ɔsɛ i kuruɛ fiɛ ɔkpase ɔsɛ ne iso.
Ɔnyɔ lɛ kumɛgɔ i kado sɛ ɔma fiɛ ɔ̃ arapia ɔfudza lɛ atumagɛrɛĩ.
Ifɔ̃ ɔmɔɛ̃ makpakpɛ̃dze mati makpakpa, makpese lɛ makpise.
Ne kpabo gɔmɔ ɔɣere marɔ̃go sɔ, “Midaanigã, loɣe sɔ Yesu gɔ mapɛ mamatãra i kudziri iso mito mibie.
Ɔna i ngbe.
Ɔ̃ɔta ɔpia ngbã lɛ kumɛgɔ ɔɣere mi ɔsɛ.
Miba mianyɔ ngbegɔ marara wũ.
Mikɛlɛ mala miaɣere ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, ‘Ɔ̃ɔta ɔpia ngbã ne ɔɖe mi katɔ̃ ɔkpa Galilea.
Mmɔ mianya wũ ne.’ Minyigi nnɛ loɣere mi.” Ne ɔso marui i ikpibiɔ kɔrɛ mmɔ ku ifɔ̃, ɣɛɛ ku isoɣɔ matere makɛlɛ masɛ maaɣere Yesu marasuãdze.
Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, Yesu ɔbɔrɛ ɔya i ma katɔ̃ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Isobuɛ itã mi.” Mabore mabo wũ mamɔɛ̃ ɔ̃ ngba masɔrɛ wũ.
Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Midaanigã, mikɛlɛ miaɣere wũ manyiibi sɔ makɛlɛ Galilea ne mmɔ maasarɛgu me ne.” Makpakpɛ̃dze Ɔɣɛ Ara Wa Manya.
Gɔ marɔ̃go ɔrui mato makɛlɛ ne, makpakpɛ̃dze ma wũ marui makɛlɛ ɔmagɛ̃ ame masɛ maaɣere masɔrɛdze makpakpa ara wa ɔɖuɖu manya.
Masɔrɛdze makpakpa ɔsarɛgu kaɖe makpakpa fiɛ mabara adzuni, matã makpakpɛ̃dze sikã titiiti.
Ne maɣere ma sɔ, “Miɣɛ sɔ, ‘Gɔ borɛ ku kasɛ̃ ne, ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔba maayu ɔ̃ kpise maruigu.’ Si Roma abã ɔkpakpa ɔnɔ fiɛ ikpese itɔ̃me ne, boto boaɖiɖi ara karɔ̃ bote wũ sɔ miibana itɔ̃me.” Makpakpɛ̃dze ɔfɔ sikã fiɛ mabara lɛ kumɛgɔ maɣere ma sɔ mabara, ne ɔso itɔ̃me nɛgbe ɔki ikã i ma Yudase ndɛ̃ iba iapɛ i nɔme.
Yesu Ɔɖi So Ɔte Ɔ̃ Marasuãdze.
Ne kama ne, marasuãdze iweo-ɔwɛ̃ ɔkɛlɛ kabemi kawɛ̃ ga i Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ makɛlɛ iso i Galilea.
Gɔ manya wũ ne, masɔrɛ wũ, atoa sɔ mawɛ̃ ɔwararã.
Yesu ɔbore ɔbo ma ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ɣaa ɔsu ɔle ɔɖuɖu gɔ i kato gu karɔ̃ ɔtã me.
Ne ɔso mikɛlɛ maturi ɔɖuɖu kɔrɛ i kayiiso ɔɖuɖu si mibara ma sɔ maakpese wũ marasuãdze.
Mipie ma Ɣaa ndu i Ɔse gu Ɔbi gu Siwarã Bielea iyere ame.
Si mite ma sɔ mabara ira biara nɛ loɣere mi.
Fiɛ minɔ!
Lopiagu mi ɔwi biara isɛ iabo kayi kawirikɔ̃.”
Ndupiedze Yohanes Ɔya Itɔ̃me Bielea Isã.
Itɔ̃me Bielea ise i Yesu Kristo, Ɣaa Ɔbi iso ngbe ne.
Koko ɔwi ne, Ɣaa Kanyaɖidze Yesaya ɔtsɛrɛ ɔsɛ sɔ Ɣaa ɔɣɛ i ɔ̃ Ɔbi iso sɔ, “Loasese kpabo ɔɖe-ɔ katɔ̃ sɔ ɔ̃aledza maturi ɔtã fɔ iba.
Mito mianɔ ɔ̃ isãya gɔ ɔto ɔki i fafuĩ karɔ̃ ame sɔ, ‘Miledza ɔri mitã Bosate iba.
Mikpɛ̃ ɔ̃ ɔri sekelee!’ ” Kpabo gɔgbe nɖe Yohanes gɔ lowe i fafuĩ ame ngbegɔ ɔpie maturi ndu i ɔwore ame lɛ ma Yudase sɛ mabara awe ne.
Ɔɣere ma sɔ mafiniki i ma situ ame manyua akpi ɔbara si mafɔ ndu ipie kubarara si Ɣaa aasu ma akpi ɔtsɛ ma.
Maturi gbodzoo ɔbɔrɛ i Yudea karɔ̃ iso gu ma ɔmagɛ̃ siare gɔ nɖe Yerusalem makɛlɛ fafuĩ ame sɔ maakã Yohanes itɔ̃me atsue.
Gɔ maɖi ma ara lalaa maɣɛ ne, Yohanes ɔpie ma ndu i Yordan ɔwore ame.
Ɔwi gɔgbe ame ne, Yohanes awu wa ɔpia ne, kapuipɔngɔ siwɛrɛ̃ masu mawe, fiɛ ɔsu bɔi ɔko kafiami ɔtɔ so ɔsɔ.
Aɖera wa ɔla ɔ̃ɔɖe nɖe maɣendu gu kugbadzedzei.
Ɔ̃ itɔ̃me nɛ ɔla iɣɛ nɖe sɔ, “Ɔturi gɔ loaba i wũ kama ne, ɔɖo me fafaafã, ngɔ ndokota iikote sɔ loabɔdzo loɖi.
Mme ne, ndu losu lopie mi.
Ɣɛɛ ɔ̃ ɔto ɔ̃asu Siwarã Bielea ɔpie mi.” Yohanes Ɔpie Yesu Ndu.
Ayi wamɔ ame ne, Yesu ɔbɔrɛ i Nasaret i Galilea karɔ̃ iso, ɔba ɔ̃ɔfɔ Yohanes itupie kubarara i Yordan ɔwere ame.
Gɔ Yesu to ɔbɔrɛ i ndu ame ne, ɔnya kato ɔbusi, Siwarã Bielea ɔso sisia wũ iso lɛ ilɔpɔ.
Manɔ silɔ ɔbɔrɛ i kato sɔ, “Fɔ nɖe wũ Ɔbi gɔ loipia kuɣɛ, fiɛ abo me anɔ ne.” Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, Siwarã Bielea ɔkɔ wũ sikɛlɛgu fafuĩ ame.
Ɔwe i mmɔ ɔ̃ ɔnɔwɛ̃ ayi sina, ne Ɔbosam ɔba ɔ̃ala wũ ɔnyɔ ne.
Ɔwe i mmɔ ku mabɔi lalaa.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, Ɣaa makpabo ɔso maba maabuai wũ mapia wũ ɔle.
Gɔ mamɔɛ̃ Yohanes mapia i iyo kama ne, Yesu ɔrui ɔkɛlɛ Galilea karɔ̃ iso ɔsɛ ɔ̃aɣɛ Ɣaa Itɔ̃me Bielea.
Mmɔ ɔto ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Ɔwi sɛɛ gɔmɔ ɔɔɣo.
Ɣaa sigara ɔɖewi ɔɔbore ɔbo.
Mifiniki si mifɔ Itɔ̃me Bielea nɛgbe miɖe.” Gɔ Yesu to ɔkila i Galilea ibu kɔrɛ ne, ɔnya asabu mapiadze inyɔ ma nɖe Simon gu ɔ̃ ɔnyiibi Andrea mato mapia asabu mamɔɛ̃ akpɛ.
Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Miba miasiai me si loakpesera mi maturi maɖidze mitã Ɣaa.” Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, manyua ma asabu masɛ marui masiai wũ.
Ɔsɛ kɛkɛĩ kere ne ɔnya manyiibi inyɔ ma nɖe Zebedeo mabi Yakobo gu Yohanes.
Masi i ɔkolo ame mato maledza ma asabu.
Gɔ Yesu ɔnya ma ne, ɔkpere ma sɔ masiai wũ.
Ma wũ mata ɔluwɛ̃, marui i ma ɔse Zebedeo gu ɔ̃ marabaradze kɔrɛ i ɔkolo ame masiai Yesu.
Yesu Ɔsa Siwarã Lalaa Ɔɖi I Ɔrɛrɛ̃ Ɔwɛ̃ Ame.
Yesu gu ɔ̃ masiaidze magbe ɔkɛlɛ ɔmagɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Kapernaum.
Ma Yudase Iwarãyi ne, Yesu ɔsɛ ma kasarɛkɔ̃ ɔsɛ ɔ̃ate Ɣaa Itɔ̃me.
Ibara mma lokã wũ atsue ɣii, alasɔ ɔte ara lɛ ngɔ mba ɔle, iiɖe lɛ ma Yudase mmara matedze awe.
Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ i siwarã lalaa si iso fiɛ ɔwe i kasarɛkɔ̃ mmɔ ɔsiagu kulu teteree sɔ, “Yesu Nasaretse, be mpia i bo gu-ɔ ndɛ̃?
Ɔba ɔɔba sɔ si aba aawɔra bo?
Nɣe ɔturi gɔ igbã aɖe.
Fɔ nɖe Ɣaa Ɔsesea Sekelea ne.” Yesu ɔtɔ̃me ɔpia siwarã sɔ, “Lo kutsuɛ si abɔrɛ i ɔ̃ ame.” Siwarã ɔtidza ɔrɛrɛ̃ ku ɔle, sitã ɔla kulu fiɛ sibɔrɛ i ɔ̃ ame sife.
Ibara mma lowe i mmɔ ɣaa, ne mato makarɛ so sɔ, “Be igbã iɖe ngbe ne?
Mme ara ite igbã ka iɖe ngbe?
Ngɔgbe ba ɔle ɔto ɔɖegu siwarã lalaa ika fiɛ sito sinɔ sibara i iso!” Ne ɔso Yesu iyere ɔre i Galilea karɔ̃ ɔɖuɖu iso.
Yesu Ɔsa Maturi Sinyɛ.
Gɔ Yesu ɔbɔrɛ i kasarɛkɔ̃ mmɔ ne, ɔ̃ gu Yakobo gu Yohanes ɔkɛlɛ Simon gu Andrea iyo.
Gɔ mabo ne, mawɛ̃ ɔɣere Yesu sɔ Simon masɔrɔ̃go rɛ ɔto ɔnyɛ ɔbe ɔtɔ.
Ne ɔso Yesu ɔbore ɔbo wũ, ɔmɔɛ̃ wũ kɔrɔ̃ ɔtara wũ ɔɣedza.
Ɔluwɛ̃ ɔsarɛ ɔta ɔwa aɖera ɔtã ma.
Gɔ kuɣɛ̃ ɔbo iyo ne, maturi ɔsore manyɛse gu mma i siwarã lalaa si iso gbodzoo mabɔ Yesu kɔrɛ.
Ne ɔso ɔmagɛ̃ ame maturi ɔɖuɖu ɔbɔrɛ maba maɣɛ i kayogodɔ̃ mato manyɔ.
Yesu ɔsa manyɛse ma nto manyɛ sinyɛ agbãagbã fiɛ ɔsa siwarã lalaa ɔɖi i mma ame sipia.
Ɔ̃itã siɖe ika alasɔ siɣe sɔ ɔ̃ nɖe Kristo.
Yesu Ɔɣɛ Ɣaa Itɔ̃me I Galilea Karɔ̃ Iso.
Ɔɖesɛrã si kaɖe aaɖaɛ ne, Yesu ɔkɛlɛ ngbegɔ i kuwɛ̃ na ɔsɛ ɔ̃akparama kayi.
Ɔwi kama ne, Simon gu ɔ̃ malaa ɔbie Yesu.
Gɔ manya wũ ne, maɣere wũ sɔ, “Maturi fu i mmɔ mato mabie-ɔ!” Ɣɛɛ ne, Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mitã bokɛlɛ simagɛ̃ dzɛ loki silɔ ame.
Ma wũ inya sɔ loaɣere ma Itɔ̃me Bielea, ala ne ɔso loba kayi ne.” Ne ɔso ɔki i Galilea karɔ̃ iso.
Ɔkiki ngbegɔ masɛ masarɛ ɔɣɛ Itɔ̃me Bielea fiɛ ɔsa siwarã lalaa ɔɖi i maturi ame.
Yesu Ɔsa Ɔrɛrɛ̃ Ɔwɛ̃ Gɔ Nto Ɔnyɛ Ɔnyɛ Rɛtɛa.
Ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ nto ɔnyɛ ɔnyɛ rɛtɛa ɔsɛ Yesu kɔrɛ.
Ɔpɛ agɛgɛ̃ ɔtã wũ iti ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Si aɖɔɛ ne, aawo me ɔsa lose sekelee.” Ɔ̃ itɔ̃me ɔɖo Yesu kayiri, ne ɔso ɔɖi kɔrɔ̃ ɔpɛgu wũ.
Ne ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Loɖɔɛ, se sekelee!” Ɔluwɛ̃ ɔsarɛ, ɔ̃ iso ɔse sekelee.
Mmɔ ame ne, Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ ɔrui ɔkɛlɛ.
Ɔsi wũ mmara sɔ, “Daaɣere kuwɛ̃ nnɛ loba.
Ɣɛɛ ne, kɛlɛ aasu so te Ɣaa sɔrɛdze si atã ara wa i Mose mmara ɔkarɛ si ite maturi sɔ ka ase sekelee.” Ɣɛɛ gɔ ɔrui ne, ɔtsɛ ɔtsɛ itɔ̃me ikararã kumɛgɔ i Yesu ɔsa wũ ɔnyɛ.
Ne ɔso Yesu iisiwo ɔmagɛ̃ ame ɔbo kpawee.
Ne ɔso ɔwe i fafuĩ ame fiɛ maturi ɔbɔrɛ i ngɔi gbodzoo maba ɔ̃ kɔrɛ.
Yesu Ɔsa Ɔrɛrɛ̃ Gɔ Lofɛfɛ̃ Ɔrɛ.
Ayi arɛ̃saã kama gɔ Yesu ɔkpese ɔkɛlɛ Kapernaum ne, iifɔ ɔwi fiɛ maturi ɔnɔ sɔ ɔ̃ɔba ɔ̃abo ɔmagɛ̃ ame.
Maturi gbodzoo ɔba mmɔ gɔ kukpa kanɛkɔ̃ iisiwe i iyo nɛ kame mapia gu kayogodɔ̃.
Ne ɔsɛ i mmɔ ɔɣɛ Itɔ̃me Bielea ne.
Marɛrɛ̃ ina mawɛ̃ ɔsore nyɛse gɔ lofɛfɛ̃ mato mabɔ wũ.
Maina ɔri mabo i iyo alasɔ maturi ɔɣede.
Ne ɔso ne, masɛ maabusi isã makigu nyɛse masora wũ i ɔkala ame masɛ i Yesu katɔ̃.
Gɔ Yesu ɔnya ma kafɔkaɖe ne, ɔɣere nyɛse sɔ, “Ɔbi, losu fɔ akpi lotsɛ-ɔ.” Ma Yudase mmara matedze ma losɛ i ndɛ̃ mmɔ ɔbu i ma situ ame sɔ, “Be ɔso ɔto ɔɖe aka ngbɔ?
Imusuora iɖe ɔɣɛ i Ɣaa iso ngbe.
Ɣaa kotoo loawo akpi ɔsu ɔtsɛ.” Yesu ɔtsue ma adzuni, ne ɔso ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Be ɔso mito misusu ara wagbe i mi situ ame?
Be iɣɛ nse pɔkɔsɔɔ iɖo?
Sɔ aaɣere nyɛse gɔ lofɛfɛ̃ sɔ, ‘Losu fɔ akpi lotsɛ-ɔ’ ɛɛbɛrɛ, ‘Ta, su fɔ ɔkala si asɛ’?
“Loaɖi lote mi sɔ mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, ba ɔle i kayi gagbe iso sɔ loasu akpi lotsɛ, ne ɔso minyɔ!” Yesu ɔfiniki ɔnyɔ nyɛse, ne ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ta si asu fɔ ɔkala si akɛlɛ iyo!” Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ɔta ɔluwɛ̃, ɔsu ɔ̃ ɔkala, ne ɔbɔrɛ i maturi ndɛ̃ ne.
Nnɛgbe ɔbara ma ɣii, ne ɔso matsɛ Ɣaa ile.
Maɣɛ sɔ mainya ara wagbe igbã manya.
Yesu Ɔkpere Levi Sɔ Ɔsiai Wũ.
Yesu ɔkpese ɔkɛlɛ Galilea ibu kɔrɛ.
Maturi gbodzoo ɔba ɔ̃ kɔrɛ fiɛ ɔtsɛ ma Itɔ̃me Bielea ite.
Gɔ ɔsɛ ne, ɔsɛ ɔ̃anya Levi gɔ nɖe Alfeo ɔbi gɔ ɔsi i ɔ̃ karabara kabarakɔ̃ ɔto ɔfɔ lampo.
Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ba siai me.” Ɔluwɛ̃ Levi ɔta ɔsiai wũ.
Kama ne, Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze gu iturikuri nɛ nsiai wũ ɔba Levi iyo ame sɔ maaɖegu wũ aɖera.
Ma lampofɔdze gu makpibaradze pia i mma nsiai wũ ndɛ̃.
Ne ɔso ɔwi gɔ mmara matedze ma nɖe ma Farisise ɔnya sɔ Yesu si ɔto ɔɖegu makpibaradze gu ma lampofɔdze aɖera ne, makarɛ ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Nda ɔso fiɛ mi ɔkɔse gu mmagbe igbã nsi maɖe ara?” Gɔ Yesu ɔnɔ nnɛ mato maɣɛ ne, ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Manyɛse i kuabaradze ɔnya ɔtã, iiɖe mma nsarɛ.
Loiba sɔ loaɣere mma nsɛ mabu sɔ ma sekele sɔ mafiniki, ɣɛɛ loba lotã maturi lalaa gu makpibaradze.” Makarɛ Yesu Itɔ̃me I Kanya Inyi Iso.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ gɔ Yohanes gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze gu ma Farisise sɛ manyi kanya ɔso ne, mawɛ̃ ɔba Yesu kɔrɛ sɔ, “Be ɔso fiɛ fɔ marasuãdze iisɛ manyi kanya lɛ kumɛgɔ i Yohanes gu ma Farisise mare sɛ mabara?” Yesu ɔtã mmuai i igbã ame sɔ, “Ɔrɔ̃go yiridze malaa sɛ manyi kanya i ɔrɔ̃go kakɔkɔ̃?
Ayi kumɛgɔ i ɔrɛrɛ̃ piagu ma ne, maibawo.
Ɣɛɛ ne, iyi iwɛ̃ mato maakɔ wũ maruigu i ma kɔrɛ, iyɔ ɔ̃ malaa ka maanyi kanya.
“Kuwɛ̃ iisɛ ɔta ɔkati kuere ala kakatisɛi ɣɛtɛ.
Si abara ngbɔ ne, kakatisɛi ɣɛtɛ gamɔ to kaakarĩ karui iyoi nɛ loabɛ iɖo iɖeakatɔ̃.
Ne ɔso ana ne, maisu ndã ɣɛtɛ mafere i bɔi ɔko akpo kuere ame.
Si ndã ɣɛtɛ ɔtsɛ ifu ne, miatã sɔ ɔko kuere aabiɛ gɔ ndã gu bɔi ɔko akpo ɔɖuɖu aanina.
Ne ɔso ndã ɣɛtɛ ne, akpo ɣɛtɛ ame masɛ mafere me.” Yesu Nɖe Iwarãyi Sate.
Iwarãyi iwɛ̃ gɔ Yesu sɛ ɔto ɔfe i kakpɛkɔ̃ kawɛ̃ ame gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ne, marasuãdze ɔtsɛ atita ibɛbɛse iwe.
Ne ma Farisise ɔkarɛ Yesu sɔ, “Be ɔso i fɔ marasuãdze to mabara nnɛ i bo mmara iitã ɔri sɔ maabara ku Iwarãyi.” Mmɔ i Yesu ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Miika i Ɔko Sekelea ame nnɛ i David ɔbara ɔwi gɔ i kukã ɔkpɛ̃ wũ gu ɔ̃ maturi?
David ɔkɛlɛ Ɣaa kasɔrɛkɔ̃ ɔwi gɔ i Abiata ɖe masɔrɛdze ɔkpakpa.
Ɔbo i Ɣaa iyo ɔsɛ ɔ̃asu aɖera wa masu masɔrɛ Ɣaa ɔɖe, ɔkuti ɔtã ɔ̃ masiaidze ɔɖe gɔ mmara iitã ɔri iɖo Ɣaa masɔrɛdze ɔnɔwɛ̃.” Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ɣaa ɔbara Iwarãyi ɔtã ɔturi isɛɛ, ɔ̃ibara ɔturi ɔtã Iwarãyi.
Ne ɔso Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi nɖe Iwarãyi Sate.”
Yesu Ɔsa Ɔturi Gɔ Kɔrɔ̃ Lokarĩ Ku Iwarãyi.
Ɔwi mama ne, Yesu ɔkɛlɛ ma Yudase kasarɛkɔ̃ ku Iwarãyi.
Ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ kɔrɔ̃ lokarĩ ɔwe i mmɔ.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ne, Yesu matsirise mawɛ̃ ma nto mabie ɔri gɔ iso maaki fiɛ maaɖaɛ wũ kanya sɔ ɔɣɛrɛ ma mmara ɔkarã anɔ sɔ maanya si ɔ̃asa sinyɛ ku Iwarãyi.
Yesu ɔɣere ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ kɔrɔ̃ lokarĩ sɔ ɔta ɔya i ma katɔ̃.
Ne ɔki ɔnyɔ ma fiɛ ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Be i mmara ɔte?
Sɔ ɔturi aabara isɛɛ, ɛɛbɛrɛ ilalaa ku Iwarãyi?
Ɣee ilɛ sɔ aabuai ɔturi ɛɛbɛrɛ aanina ngbã?” Ɣɛɛ ne, ma kuwɛ̃ iiɣɛ kuira.
Yesu ɔfiniki ɔnyɔ ma ku sikpã, ana ne, iɖo wũ kayiri ala ma situ gbogboroa iti.
Ne ɔɣere nyɛse sɔ, “Nabarã fɔ kɔrɔ̃.” Ɔnabarã kɔ̃.
Ɔluwɛ̃ kere, ilɛ wũ.
Ne ma Farisise ɔrui masɛ maatu Herodes masiaidze mawɛ̃ sɔ si mabie ɔri matã ɔ̃ iɖoe ne.
Yesu Ɔsa Maturi I Galilea Ibu Katɔ̃.
-Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔkɛlɛ Galilea ibu katɔ̃.
Maturi akuri wa lobɔrɛ i mmɔ abuiti gu Yudea gu Yerusalem gu Idumia gu mma lobɔrɛ i Yordan ɔwore kama gu mma lose i Tiro gu Sidon simagɛ̃ ame ana ɔsiai ma.
Ɔ̃ awawãra wa ɔto ɔbara ɔɔkɛlɛ dzoroo, fiɛ maturi ɔbie sɔ maanya wũ ku ma anɔmi.
Yesu ɔɣere ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ mabie ɔkolo masɛ i ibu kuruɛ si ɔ̃abo ɔsɛ i ɔ̃ ame alasɔ maturi ɔɣede.
Kumɛgɔ i maturi ɔsi ɔso ne, manyɛse to malili so sɔ maabore mabo wũ mapɛgu wũ fiɛ maasarɛ.
Mma i siwarã lalaa si iso ne, si manya Yesu ne, masɛ marɔ̃ marɛ i ɔ̃ ngbatɔ̃ ku kulu sɔ, “Fɔ nɖe Ɣaa Ɔbi ne!” Ɣɛɛ ne, Yesu ɔsɛ̃ ɔtã ma sɔ madaaɖi wũ mate ngɔ ɔɖe.
Yesu Ɔɖi Katɔ̃memasɛdze Iweo-inyɔ Ɔtã So.
Ara wagbe kama ne, Yesu ɔkɛlɛ kabemi iso.
Mmɔ ɔkpere mma ɔto ɔbie sɔ mawegu wũ ɔbɔ ɔ̃ kɔrɛ ne.
Ma ndɛ̃ ɔɖi iweo-inyɔ fiɛ ɔtã ma iyere sɔ katɔ̃memasɛdze ne.
Ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Loɖi mi sɔ si miawegu me, fiɛ loasese mi misɛ miaɣɛ Itɔ̃me Bielea.
Lotã mi ɔle sɔ misa siwarã lalaa miɖi i maturi ame.” Ma iweo-inyɔ ma ɔɖi mmɔ nɖe Simon gɔ i Yesu ɔtã iyere sɔ Petro gu Yakobo gu ɔ̃ kpeama Yohanes mma nɖe Zebedeo mabi ma i Yesu ɔtã iyere sɔ Boanerges gɔ karɔ̃ nɖe sɔ Kado Kaɣɛ Mabi.
Matsɔra nɖe Andrea gu Filipo gu Bartolomeo gu Mateo gu Toma gu Yakobo gɔ nɖe Alfeo ɔbi gu Tadeo gu Simon gɔ nsɛ ɔɖɔɛ ɔ̃ aɖe kaɖe gu Yuda Iskariot gɔ loɖi Yesu ɔtã.
Mmara Matedze Ɔsopara Yesu.
Gɔ Yesu ɔbɔrɛ i mmɔ ɔkɛlɛ iyo ne, maturi gbodzoo ɔba ma kɔrɛ ana.
Ne ɔso ne, iwe ɔle gbaã sɔ Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze aana ɔwi maɖe ara.
Gɔ ɔ̃ manyii ɔnɔ ngbɔ ne, makɛlɛ sɔ maakɔ wũ mabɔ iyo, alasɔ maturi to maɣɛ sɔ, “Iti ame ka inina wũ iso!” Mmara matedze ma lobɔrɛ i Yerusalem ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Siwarã lalaa igara lotã wũ ɔle ɔso ɔto ɔwo siwarã lalaa ɔsa ɔɖi i maturi ame.” Ne ɔso Yesu ɔkpere maturi ɔɖe ma ika i igbã ame sɔ, “Nda iawo ɔba fiɛ Ɔbosam aasa so ɔɖi i ɔturi ame?
Si iba sɔ sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ɔɣɛɣɛ so mato makpɛ̃gu so ne, sigarakaɖekɔ̃ gamɔ iibawo ɔya.
Si iyo maturi ɔɣɛ so, mata maɣɛ so iso ne, iyo nɛmɔ iibawo ɔya.
Ne ɔso si Ɔbosam sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ɔta siɣɛ so iso fiɛ siɣɛɣɛ so ne, ɔ̃ sigarakaɖekɔ̃ gamɔ iibawo ɔya, siɔba kawirikɔ̃.
“Kuwɛ̃ iibawo ɔturi gɔ mba ɔle iyo ɔbo ɔmala ɔ̃ ara iɖo sɔ ɔ̃aɖe katɔ̃ ɔmɔɛ̃ wũ ɔnyi wũ tɔtɔ fiɛ ɔ̃abo ɔ̃ iyo ɔmala ɔ̃ ara.
“Loto losia ita lotã mi sɔ Ɣaa to ɔ̃asu ara lalaa wa i ɔturi ɔbara gu anyakpi i Ɣaa iso ɔtsɛ.
Ɣɛɛ ne, imusuora biara nɛ i ɔturi aaɣɛ i Siwarã Bielea iso ne, Ɣaa iibasu ɔtsɛ wũ kuiyikuiyi.
Maibasu, aɣɛrɛ wagbe matsɛ manya.” Yesu ɔɣɛ ngbɔ alasɔ mato maɣɛ sɔ siwarã lalaa mpia i ɔ̃ ame.
Mabe Nɖe Yesu Manyii?
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ne, Yesu ɔnyi gu ɔ̃ manyiibi ɔba maaya i inyamɔ mapia wũ ɔturi sɔ mato mabie wũ.
Ne mma lomini wũ i mmɔ ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Nyɔ, fɔ ɔnyi gu manyiibi ɣɛ i inyamɔ mato makpere-ɔ!” Ne Yesu ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Loate mi ngɔ nɖe wũ ɔnyi mɔmɔ gu wũ manyiibi mɔmɔ.” Ne ɔki ɔnyɔ mma nsi maki malɔ wũ i mmɔ ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Minyɔ, mmagbe nɖe wũ ɔnyi gu wũ manyiibi ne!
Ɔbiara gɔ nsɛ ɔbara Ɣaa kuɖɔɛ ne, ɔ̃ nɖe wũ ɔnyiibi gu wũ ɔnyi ne.”
Yesu Ɔpɛ Igbã I Ɔraɖui Isa Iso.
Gɔ Yesu ɔkɛlɛ Galilea ibu kɔrɛ ana ne, ɔsɛ ɔ̃ate Itɔ̃me Bielea.
Gɔ mma loki malɔ wũ ɔsi ɔso ne, ɔya ɔbo ɔsɛ i ɔkolo ame i ndu iso.
Ne maturi ka maɣɛ i ɔkpokpo fiɛ Yesu to ɔɖegu ma ika ne.
Ɔte ma ara gbodzoo i agbã ame.
Ara wa ɔte ma i ngbe ne.
Ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Kpɛ̃dze ɔwɛ̃ ɔsɛ ɔraɖui kasakɔ̃.
Gɔ ɔto ɔsa ne, ɔwɛ̃ ɔɣo i ɔri kuruɛ, ne kurodzai ɔrɛrɛ kuɖe ne.
Ɔwɛ̃ ɔɣo i ata iso ngbegɔ i sise iisi, ne ɔso ɔre mala.
Gɔ kuɣɛ̃ ɔsia kere ne, ɔ̃ ɔɖuɖu ɔkpi, alasɔ ɔ̃ siɖu iibo karɔ̃.
Ɔraɖui ɔwɛ̃ ɔɣo i kuposɛ̃ ndɛ̃ ne ɔso gɔ ɔre ne, kuɣa kufu wũ sɔ ɔ̃iwo ɔmɔ fiɛ ɔ̃aɣɔ̃ abi.
Ɣɛɛ ne, ɔwɛ̃ ɔɣo i karɔ̃ sɛɛ iso.
Gɔ ɔre ne, ɔbara kukaakɔ fiɛ ɔɣɔ̃, ɔwɛ̃ abi sitɛ, ɔwɛ̃ abi sikuɔ, fiɛ ɔwɛ̃ ana kulafa.” Kawirikɔ̃ ne, Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ngɔ mba atsue si ɔnɔ nnɛ nto loɣɛ.” Yesu Ɔɖi Igbã Karɔ̃ Ɔte Ɔ̃ Masiaidze.
Ɔwi gɔ i Yesu ɔnɔwɛ̃ ka ɔsi ne, mma nsɛ masiai wũ ɔwi biara gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze iweo-inyɔ ɔba maakarɛ wũ sɔ ɔɖi igbã karɔ̃ ɔte ma.
Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ɣaa ɔɖi ɔ̃ sigarakaɖekɔ̃ awɛrɛra karɔ̃ ɔte mi.
Fiɛ mma i siruɛ ɣɛɛ ne, agbã lokote sɔ maanɔ.
Matsɛrɛ masɛ i Ɔko Sekelea ame sɔ, ‘Mato maanya, ɣɛɛ maibanya maɖi ite.
Mato maanɔ, ɣɛɛ maibanɔ karɔ̃, sɔ si maibafiniki fiɛ Ɣaa aasu ma akpi ɔtsɛ ma.’ ” Ne Yesu ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Ɔnɔ miinɔ igbã nɛ karɔ̃?
Nda miabara fiɛ mianɔ agbã tsɔra ɔɖuɖu karɔ̃?
Ɔraɖui sadze gɔgbe to ɔsa Ɣaa itɔ̃me.
Maturi mawɛ̃ se lɛ ɔraɖui gɔ loɣo i ɔri kuruɛ.
Gɔ manɔ ne Ɔbosam ɔmɔɛ̃ ɔɖi i ma iti ame ɔluwɛ̃.
Mamama ana se lɛ ɔraɖui gɔ losia i ata karɔ̃ iso.
Gɔ manɔ itɔ̃me ne, mafɔ ne ku isoɣɔ.
Ɣɛɛ ne, itɔ̃me siɖu iibo karɔ̃ kukaakɔ.
Mafɔ maɖe ɔwi kurukutu kere, ɣɛɛ si iɖaa gu kama iti ɔba ala Itɔ̃me Bielea iti ne, mato maafiniki makpese kama.
“Fiɛ maturi mawɛ̃ ana se lɛ ɔraɖui gɔ lobo i kuposɛ̃ ame.
Gɔ manɔ Itɔ̃me Bielea ne, kayi gagbe imararãso gu karana itere isiai gu sosina ɔmɛrɛ̃ ɔyi ma i situ ame.
Ara wagbe ɔnyi itɔ̃me ito sɔ iibaɣɔ̃ abi.
“Mawɛ̃ ana ɔnɔ Ɣaa itɔ̃me lɛ ɔraɖui gɔ losia i karɔ̃ sɛɛ iso.
Ma ne, mafɔ itɔ̃me ku ɔtu.
Ne maɣɔ̃ abi lɛ ɔraɖui, mawɛ̃ abi sitɛ, mawɛ̃ sikuɔ, mawɛ̃ kulafa.” Ɔkaniɛ Karabara Nɖe Sɔ Ɔ̃atã Ikpawaĩ.
Yesu ɔkarɛ ma ana sɔ, “Ɔturi sɛ ɔtsue ɔkaniɛ ɔsu ɔpia i kapoi ame ɣee karɛkɔ̃ kayirinɔ?
Iiɖe kasiakɔ̃ masɛ masia ɔkaniɛ fiɛ ɔ̃asa?
Ira biara nɛ lowɛrɛ to iabɔrɛ kayi fiɛ mato maabusi ibiara nɛ mafu ara.
Ne ɔso si miba atsue ne, si minɔ kukaakɔ!” Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mikã atsue kukaakɔ nwa mito minɔ lo!
Alasɔ ikerera nɛ misu mikere mitã maturi mama ne, ne ame maasu makere matã mi makuti mafa mi ne!
Alasɔ ngɔ mba ara ne, maatã wũ mabua, ɣɛɛ ngɔ mba ara kɛkɛĩ ne, kɛkɛĩ gɔ ame ɔba ne, maamɔɛ̃ mafɔ wũ iso.” Yesu Ɔɖe Ika Ɔsegu I Ɔraɖui Pɛdze Iso.
Yesu ɔɣere ma ana sɔ, “Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ se lɛ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ lopɛ ara i kakpɛkɔ̃ ame.
Ɔsɛ ɔrɛ ɔta, iyi biara, ɔraɖui ɔre, fiɛ amɔ, fiɛ ɔ̃iɣe kumɛgɔ ibara fiɛ ara se lɛ ngbe.
Karɔ̃ ga iso mapɛ ara mɔmɔ lonyɔ ɔraɖui iso ngbɔ.
Iɖeakatɔ̃ ne, ɔsɛ ɔre, ɔɖi aɣata, ɔfere aɣɔ̃la, ɔɣɔ̃ abi gbodzoo.
Si abi ɔrɛtɛ ne, kpɛ̃dze to ɔ̃asɔrɛ̃, alasɔ ɔraɖui ɔsɔrɛ̃wi ɔɔɣo.” Igbã Isegu Idziribi Kosoi Iso.
Yesu ɔkarɛ sɔ, “Be boasu bokateragu Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃?
Iɖe igbã nɛ loasu lokparara ne?
Ise lɛ idziribi kosoi iwɛ̃ nɛ i ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɔsu ɔsɛ ɔ̃apɛ.
Isɛ ire ibɔrɛ, imɔ ibara kadzirimi ga lomɔ kaɖo i ayo ame kakpɛkɔ̃ ga matɛ̃ ɔkpã mapia ame, kata akpa katã ɔyu sɔ kato kurodzai aabara ayo i kã ame.” Yesu ɔɣere ma Itɔ̃me Bielea i agbã wagbe ame sɔ si maawo karɔ̃ ɔnɔ.
Ɔ̃isɛ ɔɖe ma ika si iiɖe igbã ɔto ɔpɛ ma.
Ɣɛɛ si ɔ̃ gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ka masi ne, ɔsɛ ɔɖi wã karɔ̃ ɔte ma.
Yesu Ɔtindza Awɛ.
Iyi nɛmɔ kutsuɛ ame ne, Yesu ɔkpere marasuãdze ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mitã bowara ibu bokɛlɛ ɔkpokpo gɔmɔ isɛ.” Ne marui i iturikuri kɔrɛ mmɔ mabo i ɔkolo ame ku Yesu sɔ maakɛlɛ ibu kama isɛ.
Sikolo mama ana se i mmɔ.
Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, awɛ ɔtsɛ ikpɛ̃, gɔ ato apɛ ndu apia i ɔkolo ame sɔ miɔro ɔyi fiɛ ɔ̃awã.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, Yesu rɛ i ɔkolo kama, ɔsu iti ɔsia i isumuɛ iso ɔto ɔrɛ sirɛ.
Ne matara wũ sɔ, “Ratedze, bo kukpi iisu-ɔ kuira i mmɔ?” Yesu ɔta ɔya ɔtɔ̃me ɔpia awɛ ku silɔ teteree sɔ, “Awɛ, nyua ɔkpɛ̃!
Ndu, sɛ kpoo!” Ɔluwɛ̃ awɛ ɔɣɔ kananana, fiɛ ndu iso ana ɔlo kpoo.
Ne Yesu ɔkarɛ ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Be ɔso miba ifɔ̃ ngbɔ?
Miifɔ me miɖe?” Ifɔ̃ siare ɔmɔɛ̃ ma ne, mato makarɛ so sɔ, “Mme ɔturi igbã ɔɖe ngbe?
Ndu gu ɔwiri to makã wũ atsue!”
Yesu Ɔsa Siwarã Lalaa Ɔɖi I Ɔrɛrɛ̃ Ɔwɛ̃ Ame.
Nwagbe kama ne, Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔsɛ Gadara ibuiti ame i Galilea ibu kama.
Gɔ Yesu ɔnya ɔbɔrɛ i ɔkolo ame ne, ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ ame i siwarã lalaa pia ɔsarɛgu wũ.
Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe kawekɔ̃ nɖe maturi kabiarakɔ̃.
Kuwɛ̃ iisɛ ɔwo wũ ɔnyi ku ala nane ngɔsɔngɔsɔn.
Ɔwi gbodzoo si mawo wũ nrɔɔ̃ gu ngba ɔnyi ne, ɔsɛ ɔtu ngɔsɔngɔsɔn gu kugbagɔrɔĩ ɔɖi so.
Ɔwe ɔle gɔ kuwɛ̃ iisɛ ɔwo wũ ɔmɔɛ̃.
Kasɛ̃ ɔɖuɖu gu anɔwã ne, ɔsɛ ɔwe ɔki i kabiarakɔ̃ gu kubemi iso, ɔla kulu, ɔsu ata ɔtutu so.
Gɔ ɔnya Yesu dzoroo ne, ɔtere ɔba ɔ̃apɛ agɛgɛ̃ i ɔ̃ katɔ̃.
Ne ɔla kulu teteree ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Yesu, Ɣaa gɔ nɖe Ɔlesate Ɔbi!
Be mpia i bo gu-ɔ inyɔ ndɛ̃?
Loto-ɔ i kukpa i Ɣaa iyere ame sɔ daakpadzɛ̃ me kutsue!” Ɔɣɛ ngbɔ alasɔ ɔnɔ Yesu ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Siwarã lalaa, bɔrɛ i ɔ̃ ame!” Ne Yesu ɔkarɛ sɔ, “Nda marɔ-ɔ?” Ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Mme marɔ Isɛguri ne, alasɔ bo ma mpia i ɔ̃ ame ɔsi.” Ɔpɛ Yesu nrɔɔ̃ teteree sɔ ɔdaasa ma ɔɖi i karɔ̃ gamɔ ame.
Makparako gbodzoo ɣɛ mato maɖe ara i kabemi kawɛ̃ kuruɛ i mmɔ.
Siwarã lalaa ɔtã Yesu iti sɔ, “Sa bo pia i makparako ma nɣɛ i mmɔ ame.” Ne ɔtã ɔri fiɛ siwarã lalaa ɔbɔrɛ i ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ame sibo i makparako ame ne.
Makparako ma losi lɛ kukpi kunyɔ ɔtere kpitikpitikpiti maso kabemi mabo i itubu ame makpi.
Mma nto manyɔ makparako iso ɔtere makɛlɛ miya gu simagɛ̃ tsɔra ame, masɛ maaɣɛ nwa loba.
Ne ɔso maturi ɔtere masɛ sɔ maanyɔ.
Gɔ maba Yesu kɔrɛ ne, manya ngɔ ame i siwarã lalaa ɔwe sɔ ɔsi i karɔ̃, ɔpia awu, iti ame ɔɔkpa wũ waĩ.
Ifɔ̃ ɔmɔɛ̃ ma ɔɖuɖu gbaã.
Mma lonya nnɛ loba ɔɣere maturi nwa loba i ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔmɔ gu makparako iso.
Ne ɔso mapɛ Yesu nrɔɔ̃ sɔ ɔbɔrɛ i ma karɔ̃ iso.
Gɔ Yesu ɔbo i ɔkolo ame ne, ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ ame i siwarã lalaa ɔwe ɔpɛ wũ nrɔɔ̃ sɔ, “Tã me losiai-ɔ.” Yesu iitɔrãgu wũ.
Ɣɛɛ ne, ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Kpese kɛlɛ fɔ mɔmɔ maturi kɔrɛ sɛ aaɣere ma kumɛgɔ i Bosate ɔbuai-ɔ fiɛ ɔnyɔ-ɔ nnya.” Ne ɔso ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ɔrui ɔkila simagɛ̃ iweo dzɛmɔ ame, ɔɣere ma ibiara nɛ i Yesu ɔbara ɔtã wũ gɔ ibara mma lonɔ ɣii.
Yesu Ɔsa Yairo Ɔbi Birɔ̃gomi Gu Ɔrɔ̃go Nyɛse Ɔwɛ̃.
Yesu ɔkpese ɔbɔrɛ i mmɔ ɔkɛlɛ ibu ibesɛ nɛ i kama.
Gɔ ɔbo mmɔ ne, maturi gbodzoo ɔsarɛgu wũ.
Ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Yairo fiɛ ɔɖe ma Yudase kasarɛkɔ̃ ɔkpakpa ɔba mmɔ.
Gɔ ɔnya Yesu ne, ɔpɛ agɛgɛ̃ i ɔ̃ katɔ̃.
Ne ɔpɛ wũ nrɔɔ̃ teteree ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Wũ ɔbi birɔ̃gomi to ɔnyɛ gbaã, ne ɔso ba sia wũ fɔ kɔrɔ̃ iso si ɔna isosarɛ!” Yesu ɔta ɔsiai wũ.
Gɔ maturi ma nsiai wũ ɔsi ɔso ne, mamini wũ fiɛ masɛ.
Ɔrɔ̃go ɔwɛ̃ gɔ i ara to afere akɔ aweo-anyɔ buu ɔwe i maturi ndɛ̃.
Atoa sɔ sinyɛ masadze to matã wũ awa ne, ɔwe i ibo ame.
Ɔ̃ɔnina ɔ̃ sikã ɔɖuɖu ɔsa ɔnyɛ gɔgbe, ɣɛɛ ɔ̃ito ɔsarɛ.
Ɣɛɛ ɔnyagɛ̃ kere i ɔnyɛ togu.
Ɔnɔ Yesu iyere, ne ɔso ɔbo i maturi ndɛ̃, ɔki i Yesu kama isɛ ɔpɛgu ɔ̃ awu kutsueti.
Ala ɔɣere so sɔ, “Si loana ɔ̃ awu kere lopɛgu ne, loto loasarɛ.” Ne ɔso gɔ ɔpɛgu Yesu awu kere ne, ara wa nto afere wũ ko loɖaɛ!
Ne ɔtsue i ɔ̃ ame sɔ ɔ̃ɔna isosarɛ ne.
Ɔluwɛ̃ Yesu ɔtsue sɔ ɔle ɔwɛ̃ ɔbɔrɛ i ɔ̃ ame.
Ne ɔso ɔtui ɔfiniki ɔkarɛ mma nsiai wũ sɔ, “Nna ɔɖe lopɛgu me awu?” Ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Nyɔ kumɛgɔ i maturi ɔki malɔ bo.
Be ɔso fiɛ ato akarɛ sɔ nna lopɛgu-ɔ?” Yesu ɣɛ ɔto ɔpiapia anɔmi sɔ ɔ̃anya ngɔ lopɛgu wũ.
Ɔrɔ̃go ana ɔtsue kumɛgɔ ka ise wũ.
Ne ɔso i ifɔ̃ ame ne, ɔsɛ ɔba ɔ̃apɛ agɛgɛ̃ i Yesu ngbatɔ̃.
Ne ɔɖi ɔte wũ kumɛgɔ iba ne.
Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Wũ ɔbi birɔ̃gomi, fɔ kafɔkaɖe losa-ɔ.
Rui kɛlɛ i isoɣɔ ame.
Fɔ ɔnyɛ ɔɔlɛ-ɔ.” Gɔ Yesu togu ika iɖe ne, maturi ɔbɔrɛ i Yario iyo maba maaɣere wũ sɔ, “Fɔ ɔbi birɔ̃gomi ɔɔkpi.
Be ɔso akpese ato aɖaa Ratedze?” Yesu iifɔ itɔ̃me ne maɣɛ mmɔ.
Ne ɔɣere Yairo sɔ, “Daanigã, fɔɖe kere!” Yesu iibie sɔ kuwɛ̃ si ɔsiai wũ, ne ɔso ɔkɔ Petro gu Yakobo gu ɔ̃ ɔnyiibi Yohanes marui makɛlɛ Yairo iyo.
Gɔ mabo iyo fiɛ Yesu ɔnya sikpabo, kulu gu kaku ga mato mabiɛ ne, ɔbo i ma ndɛ̃, ne ɔkarɛ sɔ, “Be nsɛgu kulu gɔgbe?
Be fiɛ mito mibiɛ?
Ɔbi iikpi, sirɛ kere ɔto ɔrɛ!” Gɔ ɔɣɛ ngbɔ ne, mma nɣɛ i mmɔ ɔtsɛ wũ ima.
Ne Yesu ɔɖi ma ɔɖuɖu i iyo ne, ɔtã ɔbi ɔ̃ ɔse gu ɔbi ɔ̃ ɔnyi gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔbo iyo ngbegɔ i ɔbi kpise rɛ.
Yesu ɔmɔɛ̃ wũ i kɔrɔ̃, ne ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Talita Kumi.” Ne karɔ̃ i ma aɖe siɖe ame nɖe sɔ, “Ɔbirɔ̃gomi, ta!” Ɔluwɛ̃ kabirɔ̃gomi ga loɔfɔ akɔ aweo-anyɔ kere lota katsɛ isɛ iki.
Nnɛgbe ɔbara ma ɔɖuɖu ɣaa gbaã!
Yesu ɔsi ma mmara sɔ madaaɣere kuwɛ̃ ɖuɖuuɖu.
Ne ka ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mitã wũ aɖera ɔɖe.”
Ma Nasaretse Ɔsɛ̃ Yesu.
Yesu ɔbɔrɛ i mmɔ ɔkɛlɛ ma aɖe ku ɔ̃ marasuãdze.
Gɔ Iwarãyi ɔɣo ne, ɔsɛ ɔ̃ate ara ɔsegu i Itɔ̃me Bielea iso i ma Yudase kasarɛkɔ̃.
Ibara mma lonɔ ɔ̃ atɔ̃me ɣaa.
Makarɛ so sɔ, “Lɛ ɔsegu ara wagbe.
Mme inɔgba igbã matã wũ fiɛ ɔto ɔwo awawãra wagbe ɔbara?
Ɛɛbɛrɛ iɖe ɔ̃ nɖe Maria ɔbi gɔ nɖe rawedze?
Yakobo gu Yose gu Yuda gu Simon mɛrɛ̃ ɔnyiibi?
Fiɛ ɔ̃ manyiiko ana pia i bo ndɛ̃ ngbe.” Ne ɔso maifɔ wũ.
Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ɣaa kanyaɖidze ba kuwarɛ i kakɔi biara iɖo ɔ̃ mɔmɔ ɔmagɛ̃, ɔ̃ maturi gu ɔ̃ iyo maturi anɔmi ame.” Ɔ̃iwo awawãra gbodzoo ɔbara iɖo nrɔɔ̃ mɛ ɔsia manyɛse irɛ̃saã iti fiɛ masarɛ.
Ɔmagɛ̃ ame maturi idaafɔ iɖe ɔbara wũ ɣaa.
Yesu Ɔpia Ɔ̃ Marasuãdze Katɔ̃me.
Nwagbe kama ne, Yesu ɔkila simagɛ̃ kosoi tsɔra i mmɔ ɔte Itɔ̃me Bielea.
Ɔkpere ɔ̃ marasuãdze iweo-inyɔ ɔsirakanya, ne ɔsese ma inyɔ-inyɔ ne.
Ɔtã ma ɔle sɔ masa siwarã lalaa.
Ɔsɛ̃ ɔtã ma sɔ, “Midaasu kuira mila i mi irisɛ ame iɖo ɔsɛdziri.
Midaasu aɖera ɣee akpo.
Midaapia sikã i mi kukotoi ame.
Mipia ndokota, ɣɛɛ midaasu awu mama iɖo nwa mipia.” Ɔɣere ma ana sɔ, “Kakɔi biara ga maafɔ mi ne, miwe i mmɔ gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ miarui.
Ɣɛɛ kakɔi biara ga maturi loifɔ mi ɣee maikã mi atsue ne, mikpakpa mi ngba iso sise mifere lɛ Ɣaa kutsue ikpadzɛ̃ nɛ loaba ikparĩ.” Marasuãdze ɔsame mabo mato maɣɛ Itɔ̃me Bielea sɔ maturi si mafiniki i ma ara lalaa kama si mabara Ɣaa kuɖɔɛ.
Masa siwarã lalaa gbodzoo maɖi i maturi ame, masɔla manyɛse kasɛ siare nnɔĩ fiɛ mana iso ɔsarɛ.
Igara Herodes Ɔtã Ɔri Sɔ Matu Yohanes Ndupiedze Iti.
Ɔwi gɔgbe ame ne, Igara Herodes ka ɔto ɔnɔ ara wagbe, alasɔ Yesu iyere ɔɔpɛ ibiɛ.
Mawɛ̃ to maɣɛ sɔ, “Ndupiedze Yohanes loɔta ɔbɔrɛ i makpise ame ɔpia ngbã!
Ne ɔso ɔba ɔle ɔto ɔbara awawãra ne!” Mawɛ̃ ana sɔ, “Ɣaa Kanyaɖidze Eliya ɔɖe.” Mamama ana sɔ, “Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze ɔwɛ̃ ɔɖe lɛ makuere ɔwi.” Ɔwi gɔ i Herodes ɔnɔ atɔ̃me wagbe ne, ɔ̃ wũ ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Yohanes gɔ lotã matu iti ɔɖe loɔta ɔba ngbã ana!” Tɔtɔ ne, Herodes ɔtã mamɔɛ̃ Yohanes, manyi wũ marara i iyo ala Herodia gɔ nɖe ɔ̃ ɔnyiibi Filipo ɔre gɔ ɔfɔ ɔyiri iti.
Gɔ Yohanes ɔɣere Herodes sɔ, “Iilɛ sɔ aafɔ fɔ ɔnyiibi ɔ̃ ɔre” ɔso ne, ɔ̃ itɔ̃me to Herodia sikpã, ne ɔso ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃aɖoe wũ, ɣɛɛ ɔ̃iwo.
Herodes ɔla ɔ̃ɔnigã Yohanes, alasɔ ɔɣe sɔ ɔnukuarese gu ɔturi sekelea ɔɖe.
Ne ɔso ɔto ɔdzuɛ̃ wũ.
Ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃akã ɔ̃ itɔ̃me atsue ɔwi ku ɔwi ame atoa sɔ ɔ̃ atɔ̃me sɛ ɔtsue wũ ɔtu si ɔnɔ.
Katsɔrakɔ̃ ne, Herodia ɔna ɔri gɔ Herodes ɔɖe ɔ̃ iɣeyi.
Herodes ɔkpere magarakpakpa i ɔ̃ sigarakaɖekɔ̃ gu makpãrɛrɛĩ, katɔ̃maɖedze gu Galilea karɔ̃ katɔ̃maɖedze ɔsirakanya itã ɔpɔrɔ̃ itu.
Herodia ɔbi bitɛ ana ɔba ɔ̃atɔ ɔte Herodes gu ɔ̃ malaa ɔpia ma isoɣɔ i aɖera kaɖekɔ̃ mmɔ.
Ne ɔso Igara Herodes ɔkarɛ ɔbitɛ gɔgbe sɔ, “Be aɖɔɛ sɔ lotã-ɔ?” Ne ka ɔɣɛ ɔsia sɔ, “Lotarĩgu wũ sigaraiyara sɔ loatã-ɔ ira biara nɛ aakarɛ me, isɛ iatui i wũ sigarakaɖekɔ̃ kasɛ kawɛ̃!” Ne ɔso, ɔbitɛ gɔgbe ɔsɛ ɔ̃akarɛ ɔ̃ ɔnyi sɔ, “Be si lokarɛ?” Ne ɔ̃ ɔnyi ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Karɛ wũ Ndupiedze Yohanes iti.” Ɔbitɛ ɔpɛ siwa ɔkɛlɛ igara kɔrɛ ɔɣere Herodes sɔ, “Lobie sɔ loafɔ Ndupiedze Yohanes iti i kategelei iso ngbe kiniɔ!” Itɔ̃me nɛgbe ɔbo Herodes so kukaakɔ, ɣɛɛ kumɛgɔ ɔkã ndamu i makpakpa ma nsigu wũ i ɔpɔrɔ̃ iti katɔ̃ ɔso ne, ɔ̃isɛ̃ nnɛ i ɔbi ɔkarɛ.
Ɔluwɛ̃ ɔpia ɔ̃ kaɖaɛsime sɔ ɔsɛ ɔ̃atu Yohanes iti ɔbɔ.
Ne ɔkɛlɛ ngbegɔ i Yohanes rɛ i iyo ɔsɛ ɔ̃atu wũ iti ne.
Ɔsu ne ɔsia i kategelei iso, ɔsu ɔba ɔ̃atã ɔbitɛ gɔgbe.
Ne ɔfɔ, ɔsu ɔkɛlɛgu ɔ̃ ɔnyi ne.
Gɔ Yohanes marasuãdze ɔnɔ ne, masɛ maasu wũ masɛ maabiara.
Yesu Ɔtã Maturi Kukpi Kuru Aɖera.
Katɔ̃memasɛdze ma i Yesu ɔsese sɔ masɛ maaki maɣɛ Itɔ̃me Bielea ɔkpese maba maaɣere wũ nwa ɔɖuɖu mabara gu nwa masɛ maate i ma irisɛ ame.
Maturi ma nto maba ma kɔrɛ ɔfe iɣede sɔ Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze siina ɔwi sɔ maaɖe nane aɖera.
Ne ɔso Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mitã bo ɔnɔwɛ̃ saã si bokɛlɛ ngbegɔ i kuwɛ̃ na si bosɛ boawarã kɛkɛĩ.” Mata mabo i ɔkolo ame sɔ masɛ ngbegɔ i maturi na.
Ɔwi gɔ marui ne, maturi ɔnya maɖi ite, ne masɛ ngba mabɔrɛ i ma simagɛ̃ ame ɔɖuɖu maɖe ma katɔ̃ masɛ maabo fiɛ Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze kɔra ɔbo mmɔ.
Gɔ Yesu ɔso ɔbɔrɛ i ɔkolo ame fiɛ ɔnya maturi gbodzoo ma loba ne, ma ara ɔɖo wũ kayiri, alasɔ mase lɛ masɛrɛrerɔ̃ ma nna kɔdze.
Ne ɔso ɔtsɛ ma ara gbodzoo ite.
Gɔ kutsuɛ ɔɣo ne, marasuãdze ɔbore mabo wũ maɣere wũ sɔ, “Kaɖe ɔɔro fiɛ ngbe ɔdzorogu ayo ame.
Ɖi ma ɔri si makɛlɛ simagɛ̃ kosoi gu miya mɛ lobore mibo ngbe si masɛ maaɣa aɖera maɖe.” Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mi mɔmɔ mitã ma irere maɖe.” Ne maɣere wũ sɔ, “Nnɛmɔ to iafɔ lɛ ɔturi awa farafana kuso.
Ato abie sɔ bonina ngbɔ itã ma aɖera?” Ne Yesu ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Abolo arɛ̃ miba i mi ara ame?
Misɛ mianyɔ.” Gɔ masɛ maanyɔ ne, maɣere wũ sɔ, “Abolo abo aru gu kufarai kunyɔ lokuti.” Yesu ɔɣere ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ matã maturi si masɛ i karɔ̃ akuri ame i sikua iso.
Ne ɔso masɛ i karɔ̃ i akuri ame lɛ kulafa kulafa gu siru siru kusime.
Yesu ɔsu abolo gu afara anyɔ wamɔ, ɔnyɔ kato.
Gɔ ɔpɛ Ɣaa siba i wã iti ne, ɔbɛbɛse ɔtã ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ maɣɛɣɛ mmamɔ.
Ɔkpɛkpɛti kufarai kunyɔ ana ɔtã ma.
Gɔ ma ɔɖuɖu ɔɖe ara mami, fiɛ marasuãdze ɔsa nwa lobuburi kanya ne, mana kusɛsɛi kuweo-kunyɔ.
Mma loɖe aɖera wamɔ ne, marɛrɛ̃ kerekere ɔsi mabo kukpi kuru.
Yesu Ɔsɛ I Ndu Iso.
Ɔluwɛ̃ Yesu ɔtã ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔya mabo i ɔkolo ame sɔ mawara makɛlɛ Betsaida.
Ne ɔ̃ wũ ka ɔɖi iturikuri ɔri ne.
Gɔ ɔ̃ɔɖi ma ɔri ɔro ne, ɔrui ɔkɛlɛ kube iso sɔ ɔ̃akparama kayi.
Si kutsuɛ aaɣo ne, ɔkolo ka ɔsɛ i ibu ndɛ̃, Yesu ɔnɔwɛ̃ ana ɣɛ i ibu katɔ̃.
Ɔnya sɔ ɔ̃ maturi ba imɔrɛ̃ i ɔkolo iwa ame, alasɔ ɔwiri to ɔli ma.
Ne ɔso si iapɛ kaya iɖɔwũ iru ne, Yesu ɔtsɛ isɛ ikɛlɛ ma kɔrɛ i ibu iso, ɔbie sɔ si ɔfe ma, mala kulu i ifɔ̃ ame sɔ, “Iɣii!
Kpise ɔɖe!” Manigã gbaã sɔ manya wũ i ndu iso.
Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Midaanigã!
Mme loɖe.
Mina ɔtu.” Ne ɔya ɔbo i ɔkolo ame fiɛ ɔwiri ɔnyua ikpɛ̃ ne.
Ibara ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɣaa gbaã!
Alasɔ maitsue kumɛgɔ ibara fiɛ ɔtã maturi kukpi kuru aɖera maɖe mami.
Mainɔ karɔ̃, ne ɔso maifɔ maɖe.
Yesu Ɔsa Manyɛse I Genezaret.
Gɔ mawara itubu ne, maba maabo Genezaret karɔ̃ iso, ne ɔso mapɛ ma ɔkolo ikpo i ibu katɔ̃.
Gɔ maya mabɔrɛ ɔkolo ame kere ne, maturi ɔnya Yesu maɖi ite.
Ne ɔso matere maɣere matsɔra.
Kakɔi biara ga i Yesu ɔbo ne, masore manyɛse mabɔ wũ i ma sikala iso.
Ne ɔso ngɔi mɛ pelepele i Yesu ɔki, simagɛ̃ ame o-o, nsɛkɔ̃ o-o ne, maturi ɔsore manyɛse mabɔ kuɣakaɖekɔ̃ fiɛ mapɛ wũ nrɔɔ̃ sɔ ɔtã mapɛgu bidɛ ɔ̃ awu kutsueti kere.
Mma ɔɖuɖu lopɛgu wũ ne, mana isosare.
Midaasɛ̃ Ɣaa Ala Mi Kubarara Ɔso.
Ma Farisise mawɛ̃ gu ma Yudase mmara matedze mawɛ̃ ɔbɔrɛ i Yerusalem maba Yesu kɔrɛ.
Manya sɔ ɔ̃ marasuãdze mawɛ̃ si mato maɖe ara ku nrɔɔ̃ ɣɛa mɛ maifore i mmara kanya.
Ma Farisise gu ma Yudase tsɔra siai ma mawa kubarara gɔ manyua masɛ ma.
Ne ɔso ngbɛsi mafore nrɔɔ̃ lɛ kumɛgɔ mate ma fiɛ maaɖe ara.
Si mase i kuɣa ame fiɛ maipie ndu ne, maibaɖe ara.
Mamɔɛ̃ ma kubarara mama mato i akɔi gu awabui gu ndu abui ifore iso.
Ne ɔso ma Farisise gu mmara matedze magbe ɔkarɛ Yesu sɔ, “Be ɔso fiɛ fɔ marasuãdze iisɛ mabara i bo mawa kubarara iso?
Mato maɖe ara gɔ maifore nrɔɔ̃ i kubarara kanya.” Yesu ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Mi ne, maladze miɖe!
Ɣaa Kanyaɖidze Yesaya ɔkpɛ ɔya gɔ ɔɣɛ i mi iso sɔ, ‘Mmagbe ne, kanya kunu kere masu mato male me gɔ iibɔrɛ i ma situ ame.
Siefe kere mato mabara wũ karabara.
Mato mate maturi mmara i wũ mire kanya.’ Ite sɔ misu wũ mmara mibiara fiɛ misu ɔturi awune mire mito mite.” Yesu ɔɣere ma ana sɔ, “Misɛ̃ Ɣaa mmara sɔ si miawo mi mawa kubarara ɔla.
Mose ɔtsɛrɛ ɔsɛ sɔ, ‘Warɛ fɔ ɔse gu fɔ ɔnyi.
Si ɔrere ɔɣɛ inyakpi i ɔ̃ ɣese iso ne, ɔkote ɔtã kukpi ipɔ.’ Ɣɛɛ mi wũ mito mite sɔ si ɔrere ba ira nɛ ikote sɔ ɔ̃asu ɔbuai ɔ̃ maɣese fiɛ ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Nnɛ loasu lotã-ɔ loɔsu lotã Ɣaa’ ne.
Miitã ɔri sɔ ɔ̃asu karatã gagbe ɔbuai ɔ̃ maɣese.
Ɔri gɔgbe iso misu mi mawa kubarara mito minina Ɣaa mmara fiɛ mito mibara ara mama lɛ ngbe ana ne.” Ara Wa Nsɛ Abɔrɛ I Ɔturi Ame Nsɛ Aɣɛra Wũ.
Mmɔ kama ne, Yesu ɔkpere maturi gbodzoo ɔbɔ so i kɔrɛ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ngɔ mba atsue si ɔnɔ nnɛ nto loɣɛ.
Nnɛ i ɔturi ɔɖe iibawo wũ ɔpukutura, ɣɛɛ nnɛ nsɛ ibɔrɛ i ɔ̃ ame nsɛ ipukutura wũ.” Kama gɔ ɔrui i iturikuri kɔrɛ ɔkɛlɛ iyo ne, ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ ɔɖi ara wamɔ karɔ̃ ɔte ma.
Yesu ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Miinɔ itɔ̃me nɛ ana karɔ̃?
Iikpa sɔ ira nɛ ɔturi ɔɖe ne, iibatã sɔ ɔ̃ibase sekelee?
Alasɔ iibo i ɔ̃ ɔtu ame.
Ɣɛɛ ne, ɔ̃ iyiri ame ibo fiɛ ibɔrɛ ife ɔturi ame lɛ ɔdziriiso awe.” Ne ɔso Yesu to ɔɣɛ sɔ aɖera ɔɖuɖu lɛ atã iɖe.
Ne ɔkɛlɛgu i katɔ̃ sɔ, “Atɔ̃me wa nsɛ abɔrɛ i ɔturi kanya ame nsɛ ipukutura wũ.
Alasɔ ɔturi ɔtu ame i adzuni nyanyarĩa sɛ abɔrɛ lɛ fɔ ɔre ɣee ɔrã kama ife, kayu, ituriɖoe, asɔrɔ̃ra, amumu, ɔtile, mila gu sosina ɔmɛrɛ̃ gɔ nsɛgu kunuarɛ, anɔ ibɛbɛ i ɔturi ira iso, ɔturi iyere inina, iteso lalaa, ɔɖegbodzo, adzimira, gu ituridaawarɛ.
Nwagbe ɔɖuɖu ɔbɔrɛ i ɔturi ame gɔ atã wũ sɔ ɔ̃aɣɛ.” Ɔrɔ̃go Ɔwɛ̃ Gɔ Lobɔrɛ Foinike Karɔ̃ Iso Ɔfɔ Yesu Ɔɖe.
Yesu ɔbɔrɛ i mmɔ ɔkɛlɛ Tiro awo ame.
Ɔkɛlɛ iyo iwɛ̃ ame si madaatsue sɔ ɔbo mmɔ, ɣɛɛ ɔ̃iwɛrɛ.
Gɔ ɔrɔ̃go ɔwɛ̃ gɔ ɔbi birɔ̃gomi iso i siwarã lalaa si ɔnɔ sɔ Yesu pia i mmɔ ne, ɔba ɔ̃apɛ agɛgɛ̃ i ɔ̃ katɔ̃.
Ɔpɛ wũ nrɔɔ̃ sɔ ɔsa siwarã lalaa ɔɖi i ɔ̃ ɔbi ame.
Ɔrɔ̃go gɔgbe ne, ɔ Helase ɔɖe.
Maɣe wũ i ɔmagɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Foinike i Siria karɔ̃ iso.
Ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔɖi kanya sɔ, “Tã mabiɛtɛ si maɖe ara mami tɔtɔ.
Iilɛ sɔ maasu mabiɛtɛ aɖera matã makpɛkpɛ.” Ɔrɔ̃go gɔgbe ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Aĩ, Tete, makpɛkpɛ ma mpia i ɔpɔrɔ̃ kayirinɔ sɛ maɖe aɖera wa i mabiɛtɛ ɔɖe fiɛ akpakpase.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Fɔ mmuai mɛ atã ɔso ne, rui kɛlɛ iyo.
Ato aasɛ aanya sɔ siwarã dzɛmɔ ɔɔta i ɔbi iso.” Gɔ ɔrɔ̃go ɔkɛlɛ iyo ne, ɔsɛ ɔ̃anya sɔ ɔ̃ ɔbi rɛ ɔto ɔwarã fiɛ siwarã lalaa ɔɔta wũ iso.
Yesu Ɔsa Ɔrɛrɛ̃ Ɔwɛ̃ Gɔ Atsue Lotɛ̃ Fiɛ Ɔɖe Ɔmumu.
Gɔ Yesu ɔrui i Tiro awo ame mmɔ ne, ɔki i Sidon, ɔkɛlɛ Galilea Ibu kɔrɛ ngbegɔ i simagɛ̃ iweo siwɛ̃ pia.
Mabɔ wũ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ i atsue ɔtɛ̃ fiɛ ɔsɛ ɔtoto siɖe ana.
Ne mapɛ wũ nrɔɔ̃ sɔ ɔsia wũ kɔrɔ̃ iso si ɔsa wũ.
Yesu ɔkɔ wũ ɔsɛgu kuruɛ, ne ɔpia wũ arɔĩ i atsue ame ne.
Ɔti sinyatu ɔsu ɔpɛgu wũ ɔnyagɛmi.
Ne Yesu ɔnyɔ kato, ɔwarã ɔkuti, ne ɔɣere ɔrɛrɛ̃ sɔ, “Hefata!” gɔ karɔ̃ i ma siɖe ame nɖe sɔ, “Busi!” Ɔluwɛ̃ atsue ɔbusi wũ, ɔ̃ ɔnyagɛmi ɔkurisi, fiɛ ɔtsɛ aka iɖe kukaakɔ.
Yesu ɔsi ma mmara sɔ madaaɣere kuwɛ̃ ara wa manya.
Ɣɛɛ ne, ita iso kere ɔfere ndu, alasɔ ma kanya ɔla teteree.
Mma ɔɖuɖu lonɔ nwagbe ne, ibara ma ɣaa gbaã!
Ne mato maɣere so sɔ, “Ɔbara ibiara i ɔri iso.
Ɔtã ɔmumu ɔɖe aka, fiɛ matsuetɛ̃se ana ɔnɔ ara.”
Yesu Ɔtã Maturi Kukpi Kuna Aɖera.
Ayi wamɔ ame ne, maturi gbodzoo ɔba maasakanya.
Gɔ kuira iikuti gɔ maaɖe ɔso ne, Yesu ɔkpere ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔbɔ so i kɔrɛ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mmagbe ara to akpɛ̃ me nnya alasɔ maɔwe i wũ kɔrɛ akpɛnɛ atɛ i ngbe ne.
Kiniɔ ne, mana kuira nɛ maaɖe.
Si loɖi ma ɔri sɔ marui ne, mato maafɛ̃ i ɔri, alasɔ ma mawɛ̃ ɔbɔrɛ i ngɔi dzoroa.” Ne ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Fafuĩ gɔgbe ame ne, lɛ boana aɖera botã mmagbe ɔɖuɖu fiɛ maaɖe mami?” Mmɔ i Yesu ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Abolo kuboi kurɛ̃ mito?” Maɣere wũ sɔ, “Abolo kuboi kukɔdzɛ boba.” Yesu ɔɣere ma ɔɖuɖu sɔ masɛ i karɔ̃.
Ɔsu abolo akɔdzɛ, ɔpɛ Ɣaa siba fiɛ ɔbiɛbiɛ wã ɔsu ɔtã marasuãdze sɔ maɣɛ matã ɔbiara kɛkɛ.
Maba kufarai kurɛ̃ saã ana, ne Yesu ɔsu, ɔpɛ siba i kɔ̃ iti fiɛ ɔsu ɔtã marasuãdze maɣɛɣɛ ma ne.
Ma ɔɖuɖu ɔɖe mami pɔpɔɔpɔ ne gɔ marasuãdze ɔsa akutia kanya ne, mana kusɛsɛi kukɔdzɛ.
Marɛrɛ̃ kerekere kukpi kuna loɖe ara.
Ne gɔ Yesu ɔɔɖi ma ɔri ne, ɔ̃ gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔya mabo i ɔkolo ame mawara makɛlɛ Dalmanuta awo ame.
Ma Farisise Ɔkarɛ Sɔ Ɔɖi Iwawãra Ɔte Ma.
Ma Farisise ɔba Yesu kɔrɛ maakarɛ atɔ̃me sɔ si mala wũ manyɔ.
Ne maɣere wũ sɔ ɔbara iwawãra ɔte sɔ Ɣaa kɔrɛ ɔbɔrɛ.
Ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔwarã ɔkuti ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Nda ɔso fiɛ kiniɔgbe maturi to mabie awawãra sɔ maanya?
Ooɣo!
Loiba sɔ loabara awawãra lote mi lɛ kumɛgɔ mito mibie!” Ne ɔrui i ma kɔrɛ ɔbo i ɔkolo ame ɔkɛlɛ ibu kama isɛ ne.
Yesu Ɔpɛ Ma Igbã Ɔsegu I Inyagɛ̃ Kua Iso.
Gɔ mato mawara ibu ne, ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔɣara sɔ maabɔ abolo.
Kaboi kawɛ̃ kere mato i ɔkolo ame.
Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mikã me atsue si midzuɛ̃ so kukaakɔ i Igara Herodes gu ma Farisise inyagɛ̃ kua iso.” Ne ma wũ matsɛ so ikarɛ sɔ, “Kumɛgɔ boito abolo ɔso fiɛ ɔto ɔɣere bo ngbɔ?” Gɔ Yesu ɔtsue nnɛ mato maɣɛ ne, ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Be ɔso mito miɖe aka i abolo idaawe iso?
Ikã kiniɔ ne, miito minya fiɛ mianɔ karɔ̃?
Mi situ ba ɔle!
Miba anɔmi, ɣɛɛ miito minya!
Miba atsue, ɣɛɛ miito minɔ!
Miito minyigi, ɔwi gɔ loɣɛ abolo aru lotã maturi kukpi kuru ɔɖe?
Kusɛsɛi kurɛ̃ i aɖera kutia ɔyi?” Matã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Kɔ̃ kuweo-kunyɔ.” Yesu ɔkarɛ ma ana sɔ, “Ne ɔwi gɔ loɣɛ abolo akɔdzɛ lotã maturi kukpi kuna ne, asɛsɛ arɛ̃ i akutia ɔyi?” Matã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Wã akɔdzɛ.” Ne ka ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Ikã kiniɔ ne, miitsue ɔturi gɔ loɖe?” Yesu Ɔsa Nɔbiɛdze I Betsaida Ɔmagɛ̃ Ame.
Gɔ mabo Betsaida ɔmagɛ̃ ame ne, mawɛ̃ ɔkɔ nɔbiɛdze mabɔ, ne mapɛ wũ nrɔɔ̃ sɔ ɔpɛgu wũ.
Yesu ɔmɔɛ̃ wũ kɔrɔ̃ ɔbɔrɛgu i ɔmagɛ̃ ame.
Gɔ ɔfɛ̃ sinyatu ɔfere ɔrɛrɛ̃ anɔmi ne, ɔsia wũ kɔrɔ̃ iso, ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ato anya ira iwɛ̃?” Gɔ ɔtara anɔmi ne, ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Aĩ, nto lonya maturi mase kere lɛ adziri wa nsɛ.” Gɔ Yesu ɔledza wũ anɔmi ipɛgu ne, ɔkɛ anɔmi teteree, ne abusi waĩ, ɔnya ara kukaakɔ ne!
Gɔ Yesu ɔtã wũ ɔri sɔ ɔkɛlɛ iyo ne, ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Daakpese aki i ɔmagɛ̃ ame mmɔ!” Petro Ɔte Sɔ Yesu Nɖe Kristo Ne.
Ne kama ne, Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔkɛlɛ kusɛkɔ̃ gɔ i Kaisarea Filipi kɔrɛ.
Gɔ masɛ i ɔri ne, Yesu ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Nna i maturi sɛ maɣɛ sɔ loɖe?” Maɣere wũ sɔ, “Mawɛ̃ sɔ fɔ nɖe Ndupiedze Yohanes mawɛ̃ ana sɔ fɔ nɖe Eliya fiɛ mawɛ̃ ana sɔ Ɣaa kanyaɖidze ɔ aɖe.” Mmɔ i Yesu to ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Ne mi ɣɛɛ?
Nna mibu sɔ loɖe?” Petro ɔtara kanya sɔ, “Fɔ nɖe Kristo ne.” Yesu ɔsɛ̃ ɔtã ma sɔ madaaɣɛ ngɔ maɣe sɔ ɔɖe.
Yesu Ɔɖe Ika I Ɔ̃ Kukpi Gu Ita Iso.
Ne Yesu ɔtsɛ ara ite ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Ikote sɔ mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, aawe inyɛ gbodzoo i ma Yudase makpakpa gu masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu mmara matedze nrɔɔ̃ ame, mato maaɖoe me.
Ɣɛɛ ikpɛnɛ tɛare ne, Ɣaa to ɔ̃atara me lowe ngbã ana.” Ɔɣere ma nnɛgbe ɔɖi waĩ, fiɛ manɔ wũ karɔ̃ ana.
Ne Petro ɔkɔ wũ ɔɣedza i kuruɛ ɔtã wũ itai sɔ kuiyikuiyi ɔdaasiɣɛ ngbɔ.
Gɔ Yesu ɔfiniki ɔnyɔ ɔ̃ marasuãdze ne, ɔsɛ̃ Petro teteree sɔ, “Re me kama, Satana!” Ne ɔto ɔɣɛ ana sɔ, “Ato abie sɔ akpesera so ɔri itɛ̃ra atã me adzuni wagbe iibɔrɛ i Ɣaa kɔrɛ, ɣɛɛ ɔturi kɔrɛ abɔrɛ.” Yesu ɔkpere maturi gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔbɔ ɔ̃ kɔrɛ fiɛ ɔte ma ara sɔ, “Si ɔrere ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃asiai me ne, ɔsɛ̃ so, si ɔsu ɔ̃ inyɛwe ɔnyigbã si ɔ̃awo me ɔsiai.
Alasɔ ngɔ loakpɛ̃ i ɔ̃ ngbã iti ne, ɔto ɔ̃ayura me ɣɛɛ ngɔ loayura ɔ̃ ngbã ala mme gu wũ Itɔ̃me Bielea ɔso ne, ɔto ɔ̃ana ngbã mɛ loisɛ miro.
Mme kusia i ɔturi aana si kayiiso ɔɖuɖu karana ɔkpese ɔ̃ kare fiɛ ɔ̃ina ngbã mɛ loiɛ miro?
Ɣee be i ɔturi aasu ɔnyuarã fiɛ ɔ̃ana ngbã mɔmɔ?
Si mme gu wũ ara ite aakpɛ̃ ɔrere kunuarɛ i ɔkparɛ lalaa gɔgbe ame ne, mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, mme wũ ɔnyiiɔ akpɛ̃ me kunuarɛ i ɔwi gɔ ame loaba gu Ɣaa makpabo sekelea ku Ɣaa ikpawaĩ ɔɖuɖu.”
Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma ana sɔ, “Nto loɣere mi gbaã sɔ mi ndɛ̃ mawɛ̃ i ngbe iibakpi fiɛ Ɣaa sigara iɖe aaba ku ɔle.” Ɣaa Ɔte Yesu Ikpawaĩ.
Ayi akuɔ kama ne, Yesu ɔkɔ Petro gu Yakobo gu Yohanes masɛ kube kɔlɛa kuwɛ̃ iso ma ɔnɔwɛ̃.
Gɔ marasuãdze to manyɔ kere ne, Yesu kumiamia ɔkpaki!
Ɔ̃ awu ɔbara futututu atsɛ ifiɛ gelegelegele iɖo kumɛgɔ i ɔturi awune aawo ira ɔbara ifudza.
Ne manya sɔ Mose gu Eliya ɔte so mato maɖegu Yesu ika ne.
Ne Petro ɔɣere Yesu sɔ, “Ratedze, bo ngbe iba ɔbua ilɛ gbaã!
Tã bopɛ akpayo atɛ.
Iwɛ̃ itã-ɔ, iwɛ̃ itã Mose, fiɛ iwɛ̃ ana itã Eliya.” Ifɔ̃ ɔmɔɛ̃ Petro gu matsɔra gbaã sɔ ɔ̃isiɣe nwa ɔto ɔɣɛ.
Idɔdɔ ɔso ifu ma iso, ne silɔ ɔbɔrɛ i idɔdɔ ame sɔ, “Wũ Ɔbi gɔ loipia kuɣɛ i ngbe ne, mikã wũ atsue!” Ɔluwɛ̃ mabusi anɔmi, ɣɛɛ maisinya kuwɛ̃ iɖo Yesu ɔnɔwɛ̃ kere nɣɛ i ma kɔrɛ.
Gɔ maso i kube iso mato maba ne, Yesu ɔsi ma mmara sɔ, “Midaaɣere kuwɛ̃ nwa minya ngbe gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ ɔwi ɔɣo sɔ mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, loata lobɔrɛ i makpise ame.” Mabara masia i atɔ̃me wagbe iso, ɣɛɛ si ma ɔnɔwɛ̃ si ne, masɛ makarɛ so sɔ, “Be i ita i makpise ame ɔbua iɖe?” Ne mato makarɛ Yesu sɔ, “Be ɔso fiɛ mmara matedze sɛ maɣɛ sɔ Eliya aaɖe katɔ̃ ɔba tɔtɔ?” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Gbaã iɖe sɔ Eliya aaɖe katɔ̃ ɔba ɔ̃aledza ira biara ɔsɛ.
Fiɛ be ɔso matsɛrɛ i Ɔko Sekelea ana ame sɔ Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi aawe anyɛ fiɛ maasopara wũ?
Nto loɣere mi sɔ Eliya ɔɔba koko.
Ɣɛɛ ne, maturi iinya wũ maɖi ite.
Mabara wũ kumɛgɔ maɖɔɛ fiɛ matsɛrɛ masɛ i ɔ̃ iso.” Yesu Ɔsa Ɔbirɛrɛĩ Gɔ I Siwarã Lalaa Si I Iso.
Gɔ makpese maba marasuãdze tsɔra kɔrɛ ne, manya sɔ maturi gbodzoo ɔki malɔ ma fiɛ ma gu mmara matedze to makpadzɛ̃ itɔ̃me.
Gɔ maturi ɔnya sɔ Yesu ka ɔba ne, ibara ma ɣii, ne matere masarɛgu wũ fiɛ matofora wũ ne.
Yesu ɔkarɛ ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Be kakpadzɛ̃ i mi gu ma to?” Ne ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ i ma ndɛ̃ ɔɣere Yesu sɔ, “Ratedze, lokɔ wũ ɔbi lobɔ-ɔ, alasɔ siwarã lalaa si wũ iso fiɛ sikpesera wũ ɔmumu.
Ɔwi biara si sito sikpɛ̃gu wũ ne, sisɛ sitara wũ siwuĩ i karɔ̃, minyatu sɛ mibɔrɛ wũ i kanya kpɔɔ, fiɛ ɔsɛ ɔwewe kanya, ɔmɔɛ̃ ɔtɔ gogori.
Ne ɔso lokɔ wũ lobɔ fɔ marasuãdze sɔ masa wũ, fiɛ maiwo ne.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mi kiniɔgbe maturi ma loifɔ maɖe fiɛ manyanyarĩ, ayi sirɛ̃ loawe i mi kɔrɛ isɛ iabo?
Kɔ ɔbi bɔ me i ngbe!” Makɔ wũ mabɔ Yesu kɔrɛ.
