Ɔluwɛ̃ gɔ siwarã lalaa dzɛgbe ɔnya Yesu ne, sikpɛ̃gu ɔbi sitara wũ siwuĩ i karɔ̃, ɔto ɔmɛrɛ̃ fiɛ minyatu kpɔɔ sɛ wũ i kanya.
Ne Yesu ɔkarɛ ɔ̃ ɔse sɔ, “Gɔ isɛ wũ karɔ̃ ne, iɔfɔ ɔwi?” Ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Itsɛ ta ɔ̃ sibiɛtɛ ame.
Ɔwi gbodzoo ne, siwarã dzɛgbe sɛ sibie sɔ siaɖoe wũ.
Si iba ngbɔ ne, ɔsɛ ɔta sɔ si ɔbo i ɔtɔ ɣee ndu ame.
Loto-ɔ i kukpa, nyɔ bo nnya si abuai bo, si iɖe ira ne aawo ɔbara!” Yesu ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Be ɔso fiɛ ato aɣere me sɔ si loawo?
Kuira na ngɔ lofɔ ɔɖe ɔle.” Ɔbi ɔse ɔsiagu kulu ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Mba kafɔkaɖe, ɔmɔ kere kaimɔ.
Buai me si lona kafɔkaɖe lobua!” Gɔ Yesu ɔnya sɔ maturi to malili so sɔ maabore mabo ma ne, ɔtɔ̃me ɔpia siwarã dzɛgbe sɔ, “Siwarã lalaa dzɛ lotɛ̃ra ɔbi atsue fiɛ atã sɔ ɔ̃ito ɔwo ika ɔɖe, nto loɣere-ɔ sɔ bɔrɛ i ɔ̃ ame, fiɛ daasikpese abo i ɔ̃ ame kuiyikuiyi ana!” Siwarã ɔsia kulu titiiti, si tidza ɔbi i karɔ̃ fiɛ sibɔrɛ i ɔ̃ ame.
Ɔbi rɛ i mmɔ lɛ ɔkpi ɔkpi.
Ne mma nɣɛ i mmɔ to maɣɛ sɔ, “Ɔ̃ɔkpi!” Ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔmɔɛ̃ wũ kɔrɔ̃ ɔtara ɔɣedza.
Kama gɔ Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔbo iyo iwɛ̃ ame ne, makarɛ wũ pɔkɔsɔɔ sɔ, “Be ɔso fiɛ boiwo siwarã dzɛgbe ɔsa ɔɖi i ɔbi ame?” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ngbɛsi ɔturi ɔsu kayi ikparama gu kanya inyi fiɛ ɔ̃awo siwarã dzɛgbe igbã ɔsa.” Yesu Ɔɖe Ika I Ɔ̃ Kukpi Iso Ana.
Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔrui i mmɔ masɛ maaki i Galilea awo ame.
Yesu iibie sɔ kuwɛ̃ si ɔtsue ngbegɔ ɔpia, alasɔ ɔto ɔte ma ara sɔ, “Mato maaɖi mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, matã maturi maɖoe, ikpɛnɛ tɛare ne, loata lowe ngbã.” Ɣɛɛ mainɔ nnɛ ɔɣere ma karɔ̃, fiɛ manigã sɔ maakarɛ wũ ana.
Yesu Ɔte Ara I Ɔturi Gɔ Loɖo Pelepele Iso.
Gɔ masɛ maabo Kapernaum ɔmagɛ̃ ame ne, makɛlɛ iyo iwɛ̃, mmɔ i Yesu ɔkarɛ ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Be itɔ̃me mito mikpadzɛ̃ gɔ bosɛ i ɔri boto boba?” Maiwo wũ ɔɣere alasɔ gɔ masɛ i ɔri mato maba ne, mato makpadzɛ̃ so sɔ nna loɖo i ma ndɛ̃ pelepele.
Ne Yesu ɔsɛ i karɔ̃ fiɛ ɔkpere ɔ̃ marasuãdze iweo-inyɔ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mi ndɛ̃ ɔrere gɔ lobie sɔ mawarɛ wũ ne, ɔbara so ɔtsɔra i mi ndɛ̃ si ɔsumu mamama.” Ɔkpere ɔbiɛtɛ ɔba ɔ̃aɣedza ma i katɔ̃.
Ne ɔmɔɛ̃ wũ ɔsia so i ngba fiɛ ka ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ɔbiara gɔ loafɔ ɔbiɛtɛ gɔgbe i wũ iyere ame ne, mme iɖe ɔfɔ.
Fiɛ ɔbiara gɔ lofɔ me ne, iiɖe mme kere ɔfɔ.
Ɔfɔ Tete gɔ losese me ana.” Ɔbiara Gɔ Loitsiri-ɔ Ne, Mi Ndɛ̃ Ɔwɛ̃ Ɔɖe.
Rasuãdze gɔ marɔ sɔ Yohanes ɔɣere Yesu sɔ, “Ratedze, bonya ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɔto ɔsa siwarã lalaa ɔɖi i maturi ame i fɔ iyere ame.
Ne boɣere wũ sɔ ɔnyua, alasɔ ɔ̃iɖe bo ndɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃.” Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Midaatɛ̃ wũ ɔri, alasɔ ngɔ loabara awawãra i wũ iyere ame ne, ɔ̃ibawo pɛ ɔfiniki mala ɔɣɛ wũ ilalaa.
Ngɔ loita ɔɣɛ bo iso ne, mawɛ̃ boɖe.
“Lotã mi itsue gbaã sɔ ɔbiara gɔ loatã mi ndu minɛ alasɔ miɖe wũ mare ɔso ne, ɔto ɔ̃afɔ ne kuso kokooko.
Midaatã Kuira Si Ifinikira Mi Kafɔkaɖe.
“Ngɔ loatã ɔbiɛtɛ gɔ mba kafɔkaɖe i wũ ame afiniki i kafɔkaɖe kama ne, si masu ɔwɛ̃ manyi kukɔtɛ siare masarã wũ i ɔme mafuĩdza wũ mapia i ɔpo ame ne, ialɛgu wũ iɖo.
-“Ne ɔso si fɔ kɔrɔ̃ kuwɛ̃ to kukpɔkpɔtɔra fɔ kafɔkaɖe ne, tu kɔ̃ ɖi.
Ilɛ sɔ aawe kɔrɔ̃ kuwɛ̃ asɛ ngbã mɛ loibaro iɖo sɔ aba nrɔɔ̃ minyɔ ne, aakɛlɛ itɔkpe nɛ loisɛ inyi ame.
-Si fɔ kukpa nto kukpɔkpɔtɔra fɔ kafɔkaɖe ne, tu kɔ̃ ɖi.
Ilɛ iɖo sɔ aawe kukpa kuwɛ̃ ana ngbã iɖo sɔ aawe ngba minyɔ maapɛ-ɔ mapia i ɔtɔ ame.
Si fɔ inɔmi ana nsɛ itã abo i ikpi ame ne, were ne ɖi.
Ilɛ sɔ aasu inɔmi iwɛ̃ abo i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ame iɖo sɔ aba anɔmi anyɔ ne, mapɛ-ɔ mapia i itɔkpe ame lɛ kumɛgɔ maɣɛ sɔ, ‘Arɔrɛ̃ wa nsɛ anina ara i mmɔ ne, aibakpi!
Fiɛ ɔtɔ gɔ nto ɔtsue mmɔ ne, ɔ̃ibanyi.’ Alasɔ lɛ kumɛgɔ masɛ mapia mma i aɖera ame masekelera wã matã Ɣaa ne, ngbɔ ame i Ɣaa aatã sɔ ɔbiara aaki i inyɛwe ɔtɔ gɔmɔ ame ne.
“Mma lɛ, ɣɛɛ si miyura me ɔmɛrɛ̃ ne, maibawo me ɔmɛrɛ̃ ɔpia.
Ne ɔso mitã mma karabara sɛɛ si kawe i mi ame si misɛgu mi malaa i isobuɛ ame.”
Yesu Ɔte Ara Ɔsegu Ɔrã Gu Ɔre Isɛ̃so Iso.
Yesu ka ɔrui i mmɔ ɔkɛlɛ Yudea karɔ̃ iso gu Yordan ɔwore kama.
Maturi gbodzoo ɔba maasakanya i mmɔ ana, ne ɔte ma Itɔ̃me Bielea lɛ kumɛgɔ ame ɔsɛ ɔbara awe ne.
Ma Farisise mawɛ̃ ɔba ɔ̃ kɔrɛ si mala wũ manyɔ.
Makarɛ Yesu sɔ, “Ɣaa mmara ɔtã ɔri sɔ ɔrɛrɛ̃ aasɛ̃ ɔ̃ ɔre?” Ne Yesu ɔtã mmuai ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Nda i Mose mmara ɔte mi?” Matã mmuai sɔ, “Mose ɔtã ɔri sɔ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ nto ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃asɛ̃ ɔ̃ ɔre ne, ɔ̃atã wũ kusɛ̃so ɔko iyɔ ɔ̃ɔɖi wũ ɔri.” Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mose ɔtsɛrɛ ngbɔ ala mi atsuele ɔso.
Ta kayiiso karɔ̃kasɛkɔ̃ ne, ɔrã gu ɔre i Ɣaa ɔbara.
‘Nnɛgbe ɔso i ɔrɛrɛ̃ aarui i ɔ̃ ɔse gu ɔ̃ ɔnyi kɔrɛ ɔpɛ ɔmatã ɔ̃ ɔre iso, fiɛ ma inyɔɔ aakpese sosina siwɛ̃ ne.’ Ne ɔso maisiɖe maturi inyɔ, ɣɛɛ ɔwɛ̃!
Ne ɔso kuwɛ̃ si ɔdaabɛse nnɛ i Ɣaa ɔsu ɔmatãra so iso.” Kama gɔ makɛlɛ iyo ne, ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔkarɛ wũ itɔ̃me nɛmɔ iso ara.
Yesu ɔɖi karɔ̃ sɔ, “Ɔrɛrɛ̃ biara gɔ losɛ̃ ɔ̃ ɔre fiɛ ɔyiri ɔmama ne, ɔfe ɔ̃ ɔre kama fiɛ ɔɣɛrɛ wũ.
Ngbɔ ame i ɔrɔ̃go gɔ losɛ̃ ɔ̃ ɔrã fiɛ ɔsɛ ɔ̃ayiri kurã ɣɛtɛ ne, ɔfe ɔ̃ ɔrã kama fiɛ ɔɣɛrɛ wũ.” Yesu Ɔtã Mabiɛtɛ Kusɛkusɛ.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, mawɛ̃ ɔkɔ mabiɛtɛ mabɔ Yesu sɔ ɔsia ma kɔrɔ̃ iso.
Ɣɛɛ ne, ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔnyagalagu ma.
Gɔ Yesu ɔnya ne, ɔnagu ma sikpã, ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mitã mabiɛtɛ si maba wũ kɔrɛ ne midaatɛ̃ ma ɔri, alasɔ Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ se sitã ma igbã.
Gbagbaã nto loɣere mi sɔ ɔbiara gɔ loifɔ Ɣaa sigara iɖe lɛ ɔbiɛtɛ awe ne, ɔ̃ibawo sɛ̃ ame ɔkɛlɛ ɖa.” Ɔsira mabiɛtɛ ma nɣɛ i mmɔ kanya ɔsia ma nrɔɔ̃ iso fiɛ ka ɔtã ma kusɛkusɛ.
Ranase Ɔkarɛ Yesu Ɔri Gɔ Ɔ̃aki Ɔ̃ana Ngbã Mɛ Nna Katui.
Gɔ Yesu ɔta ɔɣo ɔri ne, ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɔtere ɔba ɔ̃apɛ agɛgɛ̃ i ɔ̃ katɔ̃ ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ratedze bielea, be loabara fiɛ loana ngbã mɛ nna katui?” Yesu ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Be ɔso fiɛ ato akpere me Ɔbielea?
Ɔturi kuwɛ̃ iiɖe ɔbielea iɖo Ɣaa ɔnɔwɛ̃.
Aɣe Ɣaa mmara.
Daaɖoe ɔturi, daaɖe asɔrɔ̃, daayu kayu, daaɖaɛ fɔ ɔlaa kanya, daasɔsɔla fɔ ɔnyii afɔ ɔ̃ ara, warɛ fɔ ɔse gu fɔ ɔnyi.” Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ratedze, ita i wũ sibiɛtɛ ame ne, loɔɖe mmara mɛ ɔɖuɖu iso.” Yesu ɔnyɔ wũ ku kuɖɔɛ ne ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ikuti-ɔ ira ka iwɛ̃ aabara.
Kɛlɛ aasu fɔ ira biara rɔdɛ̃ si asu sikã atsɛ mawɛrɛba, si aana kusia siare i kato.
Si ɔɔro ne, kpese ba siai me!” Gɔ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ɔnɔ nwagbe ne, ɔtu ɔbiɛ wũ, ne ɔruigu isoma alasɔ ɔba karana gbaã.
Yesu ɔki ɔnyɔ ɔ̃ marasuãdze, ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ito iabua iɖa fiɛ ranase aabo i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃.” Itɔ̃me nɛ ɔbara ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɣaa.
Ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔɣere ma ana sɔ, “Wũ mabi, ito iabua iɖa fiɛ ranase aabo i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃!
Ma mmɔ ibo ba ɔle iɖo kumɛgɔ i kapuipɔngɔ aaki kafe i ɔdzirikaãra iyoi ame!” Gɔ ɔɣere ma ngbɔ ne, ikpɔkpɔtɔra ma ibua!
Ne mato makarɛ so sɔ, “Iyɔ nna loabua ɔna iɖi?” Ne Yesu ɔnyɔ ma totoroo fiɛ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ɔturi kuwɛ̃ iibawo ɔbara, ɣɛɛ Ɣaa aawo ibiara ɔbara.” Ne Petro ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Nyɔ, iyɔ bo ma lonyua bo ira biara bosɛ fiɛ bosiai-ɔ ɣɛɛ?” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Nto loɣere mi gbagbaã sɔ ɔbiara gɔ lonyua ɔ̃ iyo, ɣee manyiirɛrɛĩ gu manyiiko, ɣee ɔnyi, ɣee ɔse, ɣee ɔ̃ mabi, ɣee aputu ɔsɛ, fiɛ ɔsiai me sɔ si Itɔ̃me Bielea si isɛ katɔ̃ ne, ɔ̃ wũ ɔ̃ana ara ikpɛ kulafa ɔsia i ngbã mɛ ngbe ame.
Ɔ̃ana ayo gu manyiirɛrɛĩ gu manyiiko gu manyi gu mabi gu aputu gu kama iti.
Fiɛ kama ne, ɔ̃ wũ ɔ̃ana ngbã mɛ nna katui i kayi ɣɛtɛ ga loaba ame.
Ɣɛɛ ne, gbodzoo ma nɖe maɖeakatɔ̃ aakpese matsɔra, fiɛ matsɔra aakpese maɖeakatɔ̃.” Yesu Ɔɖe Ika I Ɔ̃ Kukpi Iso.
Ɔwi gɔ masɛ i ɔri mato makɛlɛ Yerusalem ɔmagɛ̃ ame ne, Yesu ɖe katɔ̃ fiɛ ɔ̃ marasuãdze siai wũ.
Ifɔ̃ ɔyu ɔtidza marasuãdze, fiɛ ifɔ̃ ɔmɔɛ̃ maturi ma nsiai ma ana.
Yesu ɔkpere marasuãdze iweo-inyɔ ɔpia so fiɛ ɔɣere ma ara wa loabɔrɛ wũ iso.
Ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Minɔ!
Bosɛ Yerusalem, kakɔi ga mato maasu Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi mapia ma Yudase masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu mmara matedze nrɔɔ̃ ame.
Mato maatã me kukpi ipɔ fiɛ maatara me matã mma loiɖe ma Yudase.
Mato maasopara me, matua minyatu mafere me, mapɛ me fiɛ maaɖoe me, ɣɛɛ iyi tɛare ne, nto loata ana.” Yesu Ɔte Ara Ɔsegu I Maturi Isumu Iso.
Ne kama ne, Zebedeo mabi ma nɖe Yakobo gu Yohanes ɔba Yesu kɔrɛ, ne maɣere wũ sɔ, “Ratedze, ira ika iwɛ̃ pia aabara atã bo.” Yesu ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Be iɖe?” Maɣere wũ sɔ, “Si akɛlɛ fɔ isekele sigaraiyara iso ne, tã sɔ bo ɔwɛ̃ aasɛ i fɔ kuɖearɔ̃ iso fiɛ ɔwɛ̃ ana aasɛ i fɔ kubena iso.” Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Miiɣe nnɛ mito mikarɛ!
Miawo inyɛwe gu kukpi gɔ ame loaki ɔki?
Fiɛ miawo Ɣaa itupie kubarara gɔ loafɔ i kayi ame ɔfɔ?” Ne matã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Boawo.” Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Aĩ, mito mianɛ ndu i ikɔi nɛ loanɛ ame, fiɛ miafɔ Ɣaa itupie kubarara gɔ loafɔ.
Ɣɛɛ ne, lona ɔri sɔ loaɖi mma loasɛ i wũ kuɖearɔ̃ gu wũ kubena iso.
Maturi ma i Ɣaa ɔledza mmɔ ɔsɛ mba mmɔ.” Gɔ marasuãdze iweo tsɔra ɔnɔ itɔ̃me nɛ ne, mana sikpã i Yakobo gu Yohanes iso.
Ne ɔso Yesu ɔkpere ma ɔɖuɖu ɔsirakanya ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mi ɔɖuɖu ɣe sɔ kayiiso magara ma loiɖe ma Yudase sɛ mate so mapia mma mato maɖe iso fiɛ maba ɔle ɔɖuɖu i ma iso.
Ɣɛɛ ne, idaawe i mi ame.
Si mi ɔrere to ɔbie sikpakpa ne, ɔbara so sumudze ɔtã matsɔra.
Fiɛ si mi ɔrere to ɔbie iyere ne, ɔbara so ɔturi gɔ nna kayakpa i mi ndɛ̃.
Alasɔ mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, kɔra iiba kayi gagbe ame sɔ masumu me.
Ɣɛɛ ne, loba sɔ si loasumu maturi gu si loasu so losɔrɛ lotã maturi gbodzoo akpi iti sɔ si loafɔ ma.” Yesu Ɔsa Nɔbiɛdze Bartimeo.
Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔba Yeriko ɔmagɛ̃ ame.
Ne gɔ mato marui ne, maturi gbodzoo ɔsiai ma.
Nɔbiɛdze ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ sɔ Bartimeo gɔ nɖe Timeo ɔbi si ɔto ɔwanyi ara i ɔri kuruɛ.
Gɔ ɔnɔ sɔ Yesu Nasaretse nto ɔfe ne, ɔsiagu kulu sɔ, “Yesu!
Igara David Ɔbi!
Nyɔ me nnya!” Maturi gbodzoo ɔsi wũ kanya iso sɔ ɔlo kulu.
Ɣɛɛ ɔkɔlɛ ɔ̃ silɔ ɔbua ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Igara David Ɔbi!
Nyɔ me nnya soo!” Gɔ Yesu ɔnɔ ne, ɔtui ɔya ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mikpere wũ mitã me.” Ne makpere nɔbiɛdze sɔ, “Na ɔtu!
Ta mala, alasɔ ɔto ɔkpere-ɔ.” Ɔpɛyu ɔ̃ kato awu siare wa ɔpia, ɔkɔlɛ ɔɣo ne ɔba Yesu kɔrɛ ne.
Yesu ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Be ato abie sɔ lobara lotã-ɔ?” Nɔbiɛdze ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Wũ Sate, tã wũ anɔmi si abusi si loledza ara inya.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Rui kɛlɛ.
Fɔ kafɔkaɖe ɔsa-ɔ.” Ɔluwɛ̃ ɔ̃ anɔmi ɔbusi ɔtsɛ ara inya.
Ne ka ɔsiai Yesu gu matsɔra makɛlɛ ɔri ne.
Mafɔ Yesu Lɛ Igara I Yerusalem.
Ɔwi gɔ ame mabore mabo Yerusalem fiɛ mabo Betfage gu Betania simagɛ̃ kɔrɛ gu kube gɔ marɔ sɔ Nnɔĩ Adziri Kube iso ne, Yesu ɔsese ɔ̃ marasuãdze inyɔ sɔ maɖe katɔ̃.
Ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Si mibo ɔmagɛ̃ gɔ i mi katɔ̃ ame ne, mito mianya sɔ makɔra ɔfirimu ibi maɣedza i mmɔ gɔ kuwɛ̃ iisɛ ne iso ɔnya.
Miɖi ne i ɔwɛ̃ ame mibɔ me.
Si ɔrere ɔkarɛ mi sɔ, ‘Be ɔso mito miɖi ne ne?’ ne miɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Sate nto ɔbie, ɔto ɔ̃akpesera wũ ɔbɔ i ɔwi kurukutu ame.’ ” Ne ɔso makɛlɛ masɛ maanya sɔ makɔra ɔfirimu ibi maɣedza i ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ kayogodɔ̃ i ɔri kuruɛ.
Ne ɔwi gɔ maɖi wũ i ɔwɛ̃ ame ne, mma nɣɛ i mmɔ ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Be mito mikurisi wũ mibaragu?” Maɣɛ lɛ kumɛgɔ i Yesu ɔɣere ma kere ne matã ɔri ne.
Gɔ makɔ bɔi gɔgbe mabɔ Yesu ne, maɖi ma sikati masia wũ i imatɛ̃, ne Yesu ɔta ɔsɛ wũ iso ne.
Maturi gbodzoo ana ɔwarɛ ma sikati masɛ i ɔri iso fiɛ mawɛ̃ ana ɔfɛfɛ̃ kudzirikpai mafere i ɔri iso sɔ Yesu ɔfirimu si ɔsɛ iso ɔfe.
Mma nɖe katɔ̃ gu mma ngbikama to mafa kayiɖu sɔ, “Hosiana!
Boto bole ngɔ nto ɔba i Bosate iyere ame!
Mile bo ɔwa David sigarakaɖekɔ̃ dzɛ nto siba!
Hosiana itã Ɣaa i kato dzoroo!” Gɔ ɔbo Yerusalem ne, Yesu ɔkɛlɛ ma Yudase isɔrɛyo.
Ɔnyɔ ara wa ɔɖuɖu mpia i mmɔ ɔkidza.
Gɔ kaɖe ɔɔro ɔso ne, ɔrui ɔkɛlɛ Betania gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze iweo-inyɔ.
Yesu Ɔgbarĩ Kuɖedziri Kuwɛ̃.
Gɔ kaɖe ɔsɛ̃ fiɛ maarui i Betania ɔmagɛ̃ ame ne, kukã ɔkpɛ̃ Yesu.
Ɔnya ɔsese sɔ kuɖedziri kuwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ figi ɣɛgu aɣata wiawia.
Ne ɔso ne, ɔsɛ sɔ ɔ̃anyɔ si ɔ̃anya abi.
Gɔ ɔbore ɔbo kɔ̃ ne, ɔnya sɔ lɛ ibi na iso.
Aɣata aɣata kere aɖe.
Kɔ̃ ɔwi gɔ kuaɣɔ̃ ana iiɣo.
Ne Yesu ɔɣere kudziri sɔ, “Kuwɛ̃ iisibasu fɔ ibi ɔpia i kanya ɔnya!” Ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔnɔ sɔ ɔɣɛ ngbɔ.
Yesu Ɔsa Kuɣamaɖese Ɔɖi I Ɣaa Kasɔrɛkɔ̃.
Gɔ mabo Yerusalem ne, Yesu ɔkɛlɛ isɔrɛyo ame, ne ɔtsɛ mma nto maɖe kuɣa isa iɖi ne.
Ɔli sikã manyuarãdze sipɔrɔ̃ ɔwiri gu maturi ma nto marɔdɛ̃ abɔrɔnuma ana ayara ɔpɛyu.
Ɔ̃itã ma ɔri sɔ maasu kuira makigu isɔrɛyo sɔ maarɔdɛ̃.
Ne ka ɔte ma ara sɔ, “Maitsɛrɛ masɛ i Ɔko Sekelea ame sɔ, ‘Maakpere wũ iyo sɔ iyo nɛ ame i kayi iso maturi ɔɖuɖu aakpere Ɣaa?’ Ɣɛɛ ne, miɔsu ne mikpesera mayukukpe kawɛrɛkɔ̃!” Ma Yudase masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu ma Yudase mmara matedze ma lowe i mmɔ ɔnɔ ara wa i Yesu ɔɣɛ.
Ne ɔso ne, mabie ɔri gɔ iso maaki fiɛ mana wũ maɖoe.
Ɣɛɛ mato manigã wũ alasɔ maturi ɔɖuɖu to maɖɔɛ ɔ̃ ara ite gbaã.
Gɔ kutsuɛ ɔɣo ne, Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔbɔrɛ i ɔmagɛ̃ ame.
Yesu Ɔɖe Ika Ɔsegu I Kayi Ikparama Gu Kafɔkaɖe Iso.
Kaɖesɛ̃a kaya tutuutu gɔ masɛ mato maba ne, manya sɔ kuɖedziri gɔmɔ ɔɔkpi kuta i kɔ̃ siɖu ame.
Petro ɔnyigi nnɛ loba ne ɔto ɔɣere Yesu sɔ, “Ratedze, nyɔ!
Kudziri gɔ agbarĩ ɔɔkpi!” Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mifɔ Ɣaa miɖe.
Gbaã nto loɣere mi sɔ ɔrere gɔ loaɣere kube gɔgbe sɔ kuta si kukɛlɛ ɔpo ame, fiɛ ɔ̃iwararã i ɔ̃ ɔtu ame fiɛ ɔba kafɔkaɖe ne, ito iaba itã wũ.
Ne ɔso ne, nto loɣere mi sɔ ibiara nɛ miakarɛ Ɣaa i kayi ikparama ame ne, mifɔ miɖe sɔ mina ne, iyɔ iaba itã mi ngbɔ.
Si mito mitɔ̃me mitã Ɣaa, fiɛ minya sɔ ɔrere ɔɣɛrɛ-mi ne, misu mitsɛ wũ si mi Ɔse i kato ana aasu mi akpi ɔtsɛ mi.
Ɣɛɛ si miisu mitsɛ ne, mi ɔse gɔ mpia i kato iibasu mi akpi ɔtsɛ mi.” Maturi Ɔkarɛ Yesu Ngbegɔ Ɔna Ɔ̃ Ɔle Ɔbɔrɛgu.
Gɔ Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔbo Yerusalem fiɛ ɔsɛ i isɔrɛyo ame ne, ma Yudase kasɔrɛkɔ̃ makpakpa gu mmara matedze gu mabea mawɛ̃ ɔba ɔ̃ kɔrɛ.
Ne makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Nna ɔle ame ato abara ara wagbe.
Fiɛ nna tutuutu lobua ɔtã-ɔ ɔri?” Yesu ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Tɔtɔ ne, loakarɛ mi itɔ̃me iwɛ̃ pɛ.
Si mitã me mmuai ne, loaɣere mi ngɔ ɔle ame nto lobara nwagbe.
Miɣere me ngbegɔ i Yohanes ɔna ɔle ɔbɔrɛ gu fiɛ ɔpie maturi ndu i katu ame?
Ɔle gɔmɔ ne, Ɣaa ame ɔse ɛɛbɛrɛ ɔturi lotã wũ?
Mitã me mmuai!” Matsɛ kakpadzɛ̃ i ma kerekere ndɛ̃ mato makarɛ so sɔ, “Be boaɣɛ?
Si boɣɛ sɔ Ɣaa ɔle ɔɖe ne, ɔto ɔ̃akarɛ sɔ, ‘Si ngbɔ iɖe ne, be ɔso fiɛ miifɔ Yohanes miɖe?’ Si boɣɛ sɔ ɔturi lotã wũ ana ne, ne iilɛ!” Alasɔ ɔbiara ɔfɔ ɔɖe sɔ Ɣaa kanyaɖidze ɔɖe.
Ne ɔso ne, maɣere Yesu sɔ, “Boiɣe.” Ne Yesu ɔ̃ wũ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mme wũ loibaɣere mi ɔle gɔ nto lobara ala ara wagbe!”
Yesu Ɔpɛ Igbã Ɔsegu I Kakpɛkɔ̃ Sate Gu Ɔ̃ Marabaradze Iso.
Ne Yesu ɔpɛ igbã sɔ, “Ɔwi ɔwɛ̃ ne, ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɔkpɛ̃ adziribi awɛ̃ kakpɛkɔ̃.
Ɔtɛ̃ ɔkpã ɔki ɔlɔ.
Ne ɔɖi itawo i kakpɛkɔ̃ ndɛ̃ kumɛgɔ ɔ̃afɔ adziribi ndu ɔfere maakã masirakanya.
Ɔtsue kakɔi kɔlɛa ɔɣedza sɔ maaya iso madzuɛ̃ kakpɛkɔ̃.
Ɔsu kakpɛkɔ̃ ɔtã marabaradze mawɛ̃ sɔ madzuɛ̃.
Ne ɔrui ɔkɛlɛ ɔri ne.
Gɔ ɔwi ɔɣo sɔ maasɔrɛ̃ ɔraɖui ne, ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ɔsese ma ɔ̃ ɔɖabo sɔ masu ɔ̃ ɔkpɛ matã mabɔ wũ.
Ɣɛɛ marabaradze mamɔ ɔmɔɛ̃ wũ mapɛ, masa wũ, ne ɔruigu nrɔɔ̃ kunu ne.
Kakpɛkɔ̃ sate ɔsese ɔɖabo mama.
Gɔ ɔsɛ ne, marabaradze ɔpɛ wũ, maɖi wũ igbɛ i iti, masopara wũ gbaã.
Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ ɔsese ɔɖabo mama, ɔ̃ ne, maɖoe wũ.
Ɔpia mamama ana, mapɛ mawɛ̃ fiɛ maɖoe matsɔra.
“Ɔturi gɔ kotoo loɔkuti sɔ ɔ̃apia katɔ̃me nɖe ɔ̃ ɔbi gɔ ɔ̃ipia kuɣɛ.
Katsɔrakɔ̃ ne, ɔpia ɔ̃ ɔbi gɔgbe.
Ne ɔɣere so sɔ, ‘Lofɔ loɖe sɔ mato maawarɛ wũ ɔbi.’ “Ɣɛɛ ne, marabaradze mamɔ ɔɣere so sɔ, ‘Bo ɔkɔse ɔbi ngbe ne, ɔ̃ nɖe biarase ne.
Mitã boɖoe wũ si kaɖekɔ̃ aaɣo bo!’ Ne ɔso mamɔɛ̃ ɔbi.
Ne gɔ maɖoe wũ ne, masu wũ mafuĩdza masɛ i ɔkpã kama.” Ne Yesu ɔkarɛ mma i mmɔ sɔ, “Be mifɔ miɖe sɔ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe aabara?
Loɣere mi!
Ɔto ɔ̃akɛlɛ ɔ̃aɖoe marabaradze ɔɖuɖu fiɛ ɔ̃asu kakpɛkɔ̃ ɔpia maturi mama i nrɔɔ̃ ame.
Miika i Ɔko Sekelea ame ngbegɔ maɣɛ sɔ, ‘Ita nɛ i mayotsuedze ɔsɛ̃ sɔ iilɛ ne, ikpese ita nyaa gu nnɛ lofɔ ma kuɣa iɖo atsɔra?
Ɣaa lobara ira siare nɛ.
Ibo bo anɔ, fiɛ ibara bo ɣaa ana.’ ” Gɔ manɔ nwagbe ne, ma Yudase matɔ̃ɖedze ɔbie sɔ si maamɔɛ̃ Yesu.
Alasɔ matsue sɔ ma iso ɔpɛ igbã.
Ɣɛɛ ne, manigã maturi ma loya i mmɔ.
Ne ɔso marui maɣɛ wũ.
Makarɛ Yesu Ira I Lampo Itɔ̃me Iso.
Ɔwi kama ne, masese ma Farisise gu Herodes masiaidze sɔ masɛ Yesu kɔrɛ mabie ɔ̃ kanya ame itɔ̃me fiɛ maana ɔ̃ kamɔɛ̃kɔ̃ ɔri.
Gɔ mabore mabo wũ ne, maɣere wũ sɔ, “Ratedze, boɣe sɔ asɛ aɖe ika sɛɛ ɔwi gbodzoo.
Aisɛ afinikira fɔ itɔ̃me, fiɛ aisɛ anyɔ maturi i katɔ̃.
Asɛ ate ɔbiara Ɣaa ɔri sɛɛ.
Ne ɔso ne, ɣere bo si ɔri pia sɔ boatã Kaisaro lampo.
Botã wũ, ɛɛbɛrɛ bodaatã?” Yesu ɔtsue sɔ ɔnyɔnyɔ kere maba manyɔnyɔ wũ, ne ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Be fiɛ mito migbere me ibuɛ?
Mitã me kapɛrɛ si lonyɔ.” Masu mabɔ wũ.
Ne ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Nna iti gu iyere nsia iso?” Matã mmuai sɔ, “Kaisaro ire iɖe.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ne ɔso ne, misu Kaisaro ira mitã wũ.
Si misu Ɣaa ire ana mitã Ɣaa.” Kumɛgɔ ɔtã mmuai ɔso ne, mawa nnya mato, alasɔ ibara ma ɣaa.
Makarɛ Yesu Atɔ̃me I Makpise Iso.
Ma Zadukise ma nsɛ mate sɔ si ɔturi ɔkpi ne, ɔ̃isibata mawɛ̃ ɔba Yesu kɔrɛ, ne makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ratedze, Mose ɔtsɛrɛ ɔsɛ bo sɔ si ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔkpi ɔnyua ɔrɔ̃go maiɣe mabi ne, ɔ̃ ɔnyiibi aasu wũ ɔyiri sɔ si maɣe ɔbi ne, maabu wũ lɛ ɔrã ɖeakatɔ̃ ɔbi awe.
Ɔwi ɔwɛ̃ ne, manyiibirɛrɛ̃ ikɔdzɛ ɔwe.
Ɔɖeakatɔ̃ ɔyiri ɔrɔ̃go maiɣe ɔbi fiɛ ɔkpi.
Ne ɔnyɔare ɔsu ɔrɔ̃go ne, maiɣe ɔbi kuwɛ̃ fiɛ ɔ̃ wũ ɔkpi.
Ɔtɛare ɔsu ɔrɔ̃go ngbɔ ame ne, ɔ̃ wũ ɔkpi ɔnyua ɔrɔ̃go ɔbi idaaɣe ku wũ.
Manyi mabi ikɔdzɛ magbe ɔyiri ɔrɔ̃go gɔgbe makã ku ɔbi idaaɣe fiɛ ɔrɔ̃go ana ɔba ɔ̃akpi i katsɔrakɔ̃.
Ɔwi gɔ i makpise ɔɖuɖu aata masɛ ngbã ne, ma nna loayiri ɔrɔ̃go gɔgbe gɔ ma ikɔdzɛ ɔɖuɖu ɔyiri wũ makã?” Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mmɔ miɣɛrɛ ne.
Lonya sɔ miinɔ itɔ̃me karɔ̃, alasɔ miiɣe Ɔko Sekelea ame itɔ̃me gu Ɣaa ɔle.
Ɔwi gɔ i makpise aata ne, maase lɛ Ɣaa makpabo ma i kato, gɔ maibayiri so.
Fiɛ makpise ita itɔ̃me ne, Mose ɔtsɛrɛ ira ɔpia i Ɔko Sekelea ame ɔwi gɔ ɔnya kudzirimi to kutsue.
Mmɔ ɔtsɛrɛ sɔ Ɣaa ɔɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Mme nɖe Abraham Ɣaa gu Isak Ɣaa gu Yakob Ɣaa.’ Ne ɔso gɔ Ɣaa to ɔnyɔ makpise lɛ manyɔdze ɔso ne, magbanadze Ɣaa ɔɖe, ɔ̃iɖe makpise Ɣaa.
Mi ne, miyu ɔri gbaã!” Nɖe Mmara Mɛ Nɖe Misiare Miɖo?
Ne mmaratedze gɔ nɣɛ i mmɔ fiɛ ɔnɔ nwagbe ɔɖuɖu fiɛ ɔnɔ sɔ Yesu ɔtã mmuai kukaakɔ ɔbore ɔbo Yesu ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Iɖe Ɣaa mmara mɛ nɖe misiare miɖo?” Mmɔ i Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Mmara mɛ loɖo me ɔɖuɖu nɖe sɔ, ‘Israel mabi, minɔ kukaakɔ!
Bosate Ɣaa ne, ɔwɛ̃ saã ɔɖe fiɛ ɔ̃ ɔnɔwɛ̃ saã mpia.
Ne ɔso ne, ikote sɔ aaɖɔɛ Bosate gɔ nɖe Ɣaa gu fɔ ɔtu gu fɔ siwarã gu fɔ kasusu gu fɔ ɔle ɔɖuɖu.’ Fiɛ mmɛ nsiai mmɛgbe kama nɖe sɔ, ‘Ɖɔɛ fɔ ɔnyii lɛ kumɛgɔ ato aɖɔɛ so.’ Mmara kumiwɛ̃ siina miɖo mmɛgbe.” Mmaratedze gɔmɔ ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Ratedze, aɖe ika gbaã!
Titiriu kumɛgɔ aɣɛ sɔ Bosate pɛ nɖe Ɣaa, fiɛ ɔmama kuwɛ̃ siina iɖo wũ.
Ne ɔso ne, ɔturi aaɖɔɛ Ɣaa gu ɔ̃ ɔtu ɔɖuɖu, gu ɔ̃ kasusu ɔɖuɖu gu ɔ̃ so ɔle ɔɖuɖu, sɔ ɔ̃aɖɔɛ ɔ̃ ɔnyii lɛ kumɛgɔ ɔto ɔɖɔɛ so.
Fiɛ ilɛ iɖo sɔ ɔturi aasiai mmara mɛgbe ɔɖo sɔ ɔ̃asu mabɔi gu ara mama ɔfɛ̃ ɔtã Ɣaa.” Gɔ Yesu ɔnya kumɛgɔ ɔtã mmuai gu inɔgba ne, ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Fɔ ne, aidzorogu Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃.” Nnɛgbe kama ne, kuwɛ̃ iisibara kagbegbe sɔ ɔ̃akarɛ Yesu kuira kuira.
Nna Nɖe Kristo?
Gɔ Yesu to ɔte ara i Ɣaa iyo ame ne, ɔkarɛ sɔ, “Nda ɔso fiɛ mmara matedze sɛ maɣɛ sɔ Kristo ne, Igara David ɔbi ɔɖe?
Alasɔ Siwarã Bielea ɔki i David mɔmɔ iso ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Ɣaa ɔɣere wũ Sate sɔ, “Sɛ i wũ kuɖearɔ̃ iso gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ loabɔ fɔ matsirise karɔ̃ lopia i fɔ ngbatata kayirinɔ.” ’ Ngbe ne, si David mɔmɔ to ɔkpere wũ sɔ ɔ̃ Sate ne, nda iba sɔ Kristo aaɖe David ɔwa?” Maturi gbodzoo ɔya ku isoɣɔ manɔ ara wa i Yesu to ɔɣɛ ku ɔmɛrɛ̃.
Yesu Ɔka Ma Sɔ Madzuɛ̃ So I Mmara Matedze Iso.
Gɔ Yesu togu ara ite ne, ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Midzuɛ̃ so i mmara matedze iso.
Masɛ mapia ara siare fiɛ masɛ mawe maki sɔ maturi si maya ma ku ibu i kuɣa ame.
Masɛ mabie sɔ maasɛ i kakɔlɛkɔ̃ i kusarɛkɔ̃ gu sipɔrɔ̃ katukɔ̃.
Masɛ maɖe makpise mare amumu mafɔ ma ara maɖe.
Ɣɛɛ masɛ matɛ̃ra maturi atsue i kayi ikparama ame, alasɔ masɛ maɖe aka tagbaraa i iteso ame.
Ma kutsue ikpadzɛ̃ ɔmɔ iɖo maturi tsɔra ɔɖuɖu.” Kuɛdze Wɛrɛba Ɔwɛ̃ Karatã.
Yesu ɔsɛ ɔ̃asɛ i karɔ̃ i kasɔrɛkɔ̃ ngbegɔ mato matã sikã, ɔsi ɔto ɔnyɔ kumɛgɔ i maturi to matã ara.
Maranase ɔtã sikã siare.
Ɣɛɛ kuɛdze wɛrɛba ɔwɛ̃ ɔba ɔ̃ɔpia kupɛrɛ kunyɔ.
Ne Yesu ɔkpere ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔsirakanya fiɛ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Nto loɣere mi sɔ i Ɣaa anɔmi ame ne, kuɛdze wɛrɛba gɔgbe ɔtã ɔɖo maturi tsɔra.
Gbaã ne, mmagbe ara wa maɖe makuti masu maba maatã sɔ si mate so.
Ɣɛɛ ɔrɔ̃go gɔgbe ne, bidɛ sɔ wɛrɛba ɔɖe ne, ɔ̃ iyo gu kayi ɔsu ɔtã.
Ira nɛ ɔ̃asu ɔɣa aɖera ɔɖe ɔsu ɔba ɔ̃atã ngbe ne.”
Yesu Ɔɖe Ika Ɔsegu I Yerusalem Isɔrɛyo Ibiɛbiɛ Iso.
Gɔ Yesu ɔbɔrɛ i ma Yudase isɔrɛyo mmɔ ne, ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔwɛ̃ ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ratedze, nyɔ ata gu kulɛ wa masu matsue iyo siare nɛ gu kumɛgɔ matsue ne ana makigu.
Ito ilɛ ɔnyɔ lo!” Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Nyɔ iyo siare nɛgbe kukaakɔ, alasɔ ita kuiwɛ̃ iibakuti isia i ne ɔlaa iso, nɛ maibali mapɛyu!” Yesu Ɔɣere Ɔ̃ Masiaidze Sɔ Mato Maana Inyɛwe Gu Kama Iti.
Yesu ɔkɛlɛ ɔsɛ ɔ̃asɛ i Nnɔĩ Adziri Kube iso ɔto ɔnyɔ isɔrɛyo isɛ.
Petro gu Yakobo gu Yohanes gu Andrea mɛrɛ̃ ɔba maakarɛ wũ pɔkɔsɔɔ sɔ, “Bosate, iɖe ɔwi gɔ i ara wagbe aaba?
Ɣere bo ara wa loaba fiɛ boatsue sɔ ɔwi ɔɔkote sɔ ara wagbe aaba.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Midzuɛ̃ so sɔ miibatã kuwɛ̃ aasɔsɔla mi.
Maturi gbodzoo to maaba i wũ iyere ame, maɣere mi sɔ, ‘Mme nɖe Kristo!’ Fiɛ maasu wũ iyere masɔsɔla maturi gbodzoo.
Sitsue si sidaabɔrɛ mi si minɔ sɔ kakpã to i mi kɔrɛ ɣee kadzorokɔ̃.
Ito iaba sɔ ara wagbe igbã aaba, ɣɛɛ iite sɔ kayi karokɔ̃ ɔɔwo.
Abuiti aakpɛ̃ gu abuiti.
Fiɛ sigarakaɖekɔ̃ to siata siya sigarakaɖekɔ̃ iso.
Karɔ̃ to kaati i ngɔi, fiɛ kukã to kuabo.
Nwagbe ɔɖuɖu nɖe lɛ kumɛgɔ i kuɣe sɛ kusɛ karɔ̃ ku iɖoɖo ne.
“Mi ne, midzuɛ̃ so kukaakɔ.
Mato maamɔɛ̃ mi masɛgu atɔ̃mekaɣɛkɔ̃.
Mato maapɛ mi i ma Yudase kasarɛkɔ̃ ala wũ ɔso, mito miaya i matɔ̃ɖedze gu magara anɔ miɣere ma wũ iso itɔ̃me, si iɖe ikparĩ itã ma.
Si kawirikɔ̃ aaba ne, ito iaba sɔ maɣere nɖebi ɔɖuɖu Ɣaa Itɔ̃me Bielea.
Si maamɔɛ̃ mi fiɛ makɛlɛgu mi atɔ̃mekaɣɛkɔ̃ ne, midaamararã so sɔ be miaɣɛ.
Si ɔwi ɔɣo ne, miɣɛ nnɛ i Siwarã Bielea aatã mi.
Alasɔ iiɖe mi mɔmɔ ati ame atɔ̃me miaɣɛ, ɣɛɛ ne, Ɣaa Siwarã loatã sɔ miaɣɛ ɔ̃ adzuni.
“Maturi to maaɖi ma manyii matã sɔ maɖoe.
Fiɛ mase to maaɖi ma mabi matã.
Mabi to maata maya maɣese iso maɖi ma matã sɔ maɖoe.
Ɔbiara to ɔ̃atsiri mi, ala wũ ɔso.
Ɣɛɛ ne, ɔbiara gɔ loaya teteree ɔbo kawirikɔ̃ to ɔ̃ana iɖi.
Yesu Ɔka Ma I Inyɛwe Nɛ Loaba Iso.
“Kiniɔ ne, mikã atsue kukaakɔ si minɔ karɔ̃.
Si minya imusuora nɛ nsɛ iwɔra maturi fiɛ Ɣaa ɔtsiri sɔ iba iaya i ngbegɔ loikote ne, mma mpia i Yudea si matere teteree makɛlɛ abe iso maawɛrɛ.
Ngɔ loya ɔsia i isã si ɔdaanina ɔwi sɔ ɔso ɔba iyo sɔ ɔ̃asu kuira i iyo kame.
Ngɔ mpia i sia si ɔdaaɣɛ sɔ ɔsɛ kaa sɔ ɔ̃asu awu.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ to ɔ̃awe ɔle gbaã ɔtã mayirise gu matalɛpo ɣɛtɛ.
Mitã Ɣaa iti sɔ ɔwi gɔmɔ si ɔdaaba ku kulele ɔwi.
Alasɔ ibo gu ibɛbɛrɛ nɛ loaba ne, ito iaɖo ibiara nɛ i kayi gagbe ɔnya kanya ita i kayi karɔ̃kasɛkɔ̃ iba iabo nɔme.
Fiɛ inyɛwe nɛgbe igbã iisibaba kuiyikuiyi.
Ɣɛɛ ne, si Bo Ɔse Ɣaa iitu ayi wagbe ne, ɔturi kuwɛ̃ iibakuti.
Ɣɛɛ mma ɔ̃ɔɖi ɔtã so ɔso ne, ɔ̃abɛrɛkɛ ayi wagbe.
“Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame si ɔrere ɔɣere-ɔ sɔ, ‘Nyɔ!
Nya Kristo ngbe!’ ɣee, ‘Nya wũ mmɔ ne!’ daafɔ wũ aɖe!
Alasɔ mila ma Kristo gu mila kanyamaɖidze gbodzoo to maabara akparĩ gu awawãra gbodzoo, sɔ si maawo kɔra ne, maasɔsɔla kuta Ɣaa maturi ma ɔɖi ɔsɛ kokooko.
Ne ɔso midzuɛ̃ so!
Loɔɣere mi losɛ fiɛ ɔwi aaɣo.
Yesu Ɔledza Iɣɛ Kumɛgɔ I Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi Aba Ana.
“Ayi wa ka loasiai inyɛwe ɔwi ne, ‘kuɣɛ̃ to kuanyi, fiɛ ɔgbaworeti ana iibare.
Awãmi to aakpase abɔrɛ i kato, fiɛ kato sile ɔɖuɖu to siati kpukpukpu sibɔrɛ i sɛ̃ kawekɔ̃.’ “Ne maturi aanya Ɔturi awune Ɔbi gɔ ɔto ɔso i adɔdɔ ame ɔba i ɔle siare gu ifiɛ ame.
Fiɛ ɔ̃asese ɔ̃ kato makpabo kayi abesɛ ana ɔɖuɖu sɔ ɔ̃ maturi ma ɔɖi ɔsɛ ita i kayi iti nɛ, ikɛlɛ iti nɛmɔ ne, masira ma kanya.
Yesu Ɔɣere Ɔ̃ Marasuãdze Sɔ Maledza So Matã Kawirikɔ̃.
“Misuã ara i kuɖedziri iso.
Si minya sɔ kudziri gɔmɔ to kuɖi ayata ɣɛtɛ ne, mitsue sɔ kado ɔpɛwi ka ɔba.
Ne ɔso si miɔtsɛ ara wa loɣere mi ngbe inya ne, mitsue sɔ, wũ iba ɔɔbore ibo iɣɛ i fɔ kayogodɔ̃!
Nto loɣere mi sɔ ara wagbe aaba fiɛ mi kiniɔgbe maturi aakpi maro.
Kato gu karɔ̃ ɔɖuɖu to kaafe, ɣɛɛ ne, wũ itɔ̃me iibafe kuiyikuiyi.
“Fiɛ ɣɛɛ ne, kuwɛ̃ iiɣe iyi ɣee ɔɖɔwũ gɔ ame iaba, nane Ɣaa makpabo gu mme Ɣaa Ɔbi kɔra iiɣe, isu iɖo wũ Ɔse ɔnɔwɛ̃.
Midzuɛ̃ so si mila so, alasɔ miiɣe iyi nɛ i ɔwi gɔmɔ aaba.
Wũ iba to iase lɛ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ lota sɔ ɔsɛ ɔri, fiɛ ɔrui ɔnyua ɔ̃ marabaradze ɔpia iyo.
Ɔtã ɔbiara ɔ̃ karabara sɔ ɔbara.
Ne kama ne, ɔɣere iyodzuɛ̃se sɔ ɔnyɔ ɔ̃ iba ɔri kukaakɔ.
“Ne ɔso mi wũ midzuɛ̃ so.
Alasɔ miiɣe ɔwi gɔ tutuutu i Bosate aaba ɔ̃abo.
Ito iawo ɔba ku kutsuɛ ɣee kasɛ̃ ndɛ̃ ɣee ɔɖesɛrã siare, marodza silɔ ɔɖi ɔwi, ɣee kaya tutuutu.
Si ɔba ɔ̃ɔbɔrɛ mi iso ngbɔ ne, idaaba sɔ ɔ̃aba ɔ̃anya mi sɔ mito mirɛ sirɛ.
Ira nɛ loɣere mi ngbe ne, ne ame nto loɣere matsɔra ne.
Ne ɔso minyɔ ɔ̃ iba ɔri.”
Ma Yudase Masɔrɛdze Makpakpa Ɔsɛ Iti Ame Sɔ Maaɖoe Yesu.
Ikuti ayi anyɔ fiɛ ma Yudase aaɖe ma iyi sekelea nɛ masɛ masu manyigi ma sisande ame ibɔrɛ i Egipte, iyi nɛ mato marɔ sɔ Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo gu Abolo Ɣɛtɛ Wa Loita Iɖe Iyi.
Kasɔrɛkɔ̃ matɔ̃ɖedze gu mmara matedze mawɛ̃ ɔnyɔnyɔ ɔri gɔ maaki fiɛ maamɔɛ̃ Yesu maɖoe.
Maɣere so sɔ, “Iito ialɛ sɔ boabara ngbɔ ku iyi iɖe ayi wagbe ame.
Alasɔ si iiɖe ngbɔ ne, kulu to kuapɛ.” Ɔrɔ̃go Ɔwɛ̃ Ɔfere Yesu Nnɔĩ Kɔrɔ̃kɔrɔ̃a Iti.
Yesu ɔwe i Betania ɔmagɛ̃ ame i Simon gɔ lonyɛ ɔnyɛ rɛtɛa iyo.
Gɔ Yesu si i aɖera kaɖekɔ̃ ne, ɔrɔ̃go ɔwɛ̃ ɔba mmɔ ku ita inɔĩbui sɔlɔsɔlɔa nɛ ame i nnɔĩ kɔrɔ̃kɔrɔ̃a ɔyi pɔpɔɔpɔ fiɛ mifɔ kuya gbaã.
Ɔrɔ̃go gɔgbe ɔfɛ̃ inɔĩbui kanya, ne ɔfedza me ɔfere Yesu iti ne.
Nnɛgbe ɔɖaa mma nɣɛ mmɔ mawɛ̃ fiɛ ibo ma so sɔ, “Be ɔso fiɛ ɔnina nnɔĩ mɛgbe?
Tee ɔsu ɔrɔdɛ̃ ɔfɔ ɔturi ikɔ buu kuwakuso gɔ ɔ̃asu ɔtã mawɛrɛba.” Ne ɔso ne, manyagalagu wũ, managu wũ sikpã.
Ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Minyua wũ!
Be ɔso fiɛ miibatã wũ ɔwarã?
Ɔbara me ira sɛɛ.
Mawɛrɛba pia i mi kɔrɛ ɔwi biara.
Fiɛ ɔwi biara miɖɔɛ ne, miawo ma ɔbuai.
Mme ɣɛɛ ne, iiɖe ɔwi biara nto loawe i mi kɔrɛ.
Ɔrɔ̃go gɔgbe ne, ɔbara nnɛ ɔ̃awo ɔbara.
Ɔsu nnɔĩ mɛ ɔfere me iso ɔledza me ɔtã wũ ibiara.
Fiɛ nto losia ita sɔ kakɔi biara ga maaɣɛ Ɣaa Itɔ̃me i kayi gagbe ame ne, maaɣɛ nnɛ i ɔrɔ̃go gɔgbe ɔbara.” Yuda Ɔtɔrã Sɔ Ɔ̃aɖi Yesu Ɔtã.
Yuda Iskariot gɔ nɖe Yesu katɔ̃memasɛdze iweo-inyɔ ɔwɛ̃ ɔsɛ kasɔrɛkɔ̃ makpakpa kɔrɛ sɔ ɔ̃aɖi Yesu ɔtã ma sɔ maɖoe.
Mana isoɣɔ gbaã, ne ɔso maɣɛ sɔ maatã wũ sikã.
Ne ɔso ɔtsɛ ɔri gɔ iso ɔ̃aki fiɛ ɔ̃aɖi wũ ɔtã ma mamɔɛ̃ inyɔnyɔ.
Yesu Gu Ɔ̃ Marasuãdze Ɔtu Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo Ɔpɔrɔ̃.
I Abolo Ɣɛtɛ Wa Loita Iɖe Iyi ikpɛnɛ ɖeakatɔ̃ nɛ iso masɛ maɖoe Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo sɛrɛ lɛ kumɛgɔ i ma Yudase kubarara se ne, Yesu marasuãdze ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Lɛ abie sɔ boledza bosɛ botã bo iyi aɖera kaɖekɔ̃?” Ne Yesu ɔɖi ma inyɔ mawɛ̃ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mikɛlɛ ɔmagɛ̃ ame, mito mianya ɔwɛ̃ sore ndu kabui.
Misiai wũ si minyɔ iyo nɛ ame ɔ̃abo.
Miɣere iyosate sɔ, ‘Ratedze sɔ te bo iyo nɛ ame i ɔ̃ gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze aaba maatu Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo Iyi ɔpɔrɔ̃.’ Ɔto ɔ̃ate mi iyo siare iwɛ̃ nɛ matsue masia ame ngbegɔ maledza masɛ.
Miwa ikpɛnɛ bielea nɛgbe aɖera misɛ i mmɔ.” Marasuãdze magbe ɔkɛlɛ ɔmagɛ̃ ame, ne manya sɔ ibiara nɛ i Yesu ɔɣɛ ɔba ngbɔ.
Ne mawa Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo Iyi aɖera masɛ ne.
Gɔ kutsuɛ ɔɣo ne, Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze iweo-inyɔ ɔsɛ maabo mmɔ.
Ne gɔ masɛ i ɔpɔrɔ̃ katɔ̃ mato maɖe ara ne, Yesu ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Nto loɣere mi sɔ ɔwɛ̃ i mi ndɛ̃ gɔ bo gu wũ nsi ngbe boto boɖe ara to ɔ̃aɖi me ɔtã.” Itɔ̃me nɛgbe ɔɖaa ma, ne matsɛ wũ ikarɛ isia isia sɔ, “Loɣe sɔ iiɖe mme ato, ɛɛbɛrɛ mme loɖe?” Yesu ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Mi iweo-inyɔ ndɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ i bo gu wũ inyɔ to bopia kɔrɔ̃ i irɔi iwɛ̃ ame ngbe ɔɖe.
Mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, to ɔsɛ ɔ̃akpi lɛ kumɛgɔ ame i Ɔko Sekelea ɔte.
Ɣɛɛ iito iase ngɔ loaɖi wũ ɔtã pɔkɔsɔɔ.
Si maiɣe wũ kɔra ne, ialɛgu wũ iɖo!” Maɖe Bosate Aɖera Tsɔra.
Gɔ mato maɖe ara ne, Yesu ɔsu abolo.
Ne gɔ ɔpɛ Ɣaa siba i wã iti ne, ɔkpɛkpɛti ɔtã ɔ̃ marasuãdze.
Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mifɔ si miɖe.
Wũ siturina i ngbe ne.” Ne ɔsu ndã ikɔi ne, gɔ ɔpɛ Ɣaa siba i ne iti ne, ɔsu ɔtã ma, ne manɛ ne.
Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Wũ ima nɛ loasu lofere i karɔ̃ i maturi gbodzoo iti fiɛ iɖe ndamu ɣɛtɛ i maturi awune gu Ɣaa ndɛ̃ i ngbe ne.
Gbaã ne, loisibanɛ ndã kumiwɛ̃, gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ loanɛ miɣɛtɛ i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃.” Gɔ maɖe ara maro ne, maka kuka male Ɣaa fiɛ makɛlɛ Nnɔĩ Adziri Kube iso.
Yesu Ɔɣɛ Ɔsɛ Sɔ Petro To Ɔ̃asɛ̃ Wũ.
Mmɔ i Yesu ɔɣere marasuãdze sɔ, “Mi ɔɖuɖu to miatere miɣɛ me.
Alasɔ Ɣaa ɔɣɛ i Ɔko Sekelea ame sɔ, ‘Loaɖoe masɛrɛkɔdze, fiɛ ɔ̃ masɛrɛ aasame.’ Ɔwi gɔ loata lobɔrɛ i makpise ndɛ̃ ne, loaɖe mi katɔ̃ lokɛlɛ Galilea karɔ̃ iso.” Ne Petro ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Mme loibatere loɣɛ-ɔ, si ɔbiara ɔnyua-ɔ ɔsɛ.” Yesu ɔɣere Petro sɔ, “Nto loɣere-ɔ gbagbaã sɔ, kasɛ̃ gagbe si rodza aaɖi kanya ɔkpɛ nyɔa ne, ato aasɛ̃ me ikpɛ itɛ sɔ aiɣe me.” Petro ɔledza ita isia ɔɖo iɖeakatɔ̃ sɔ, “Si loakpigu-ɔ kɔra ne, loibaɣɛ sɔ loiɣe-ɔ.” Ne ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔɖuɖu ana ɔɣɛ ngbɔ ne.
Yesu Ɔkparama Kayi Ku Isomararã I Getsemane.
Gɔ masɛ maabo ngbegɔ marɔ Getsemane ne, Yesu ɔɣere ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Misɛ i ngbe si nsɛ loakparama kayi.” Ne ɔkɔ Petro gu Yakobo gu Yohanes ɔruigu, ɔtsɛ so imararã iti ikpakpa ne.
Ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Nto lona ibo ta wũ ame gbaã, lɛ kukpi lomɔɛ̃ me kuto.
Miya i ngbe si midzuɛ̃gu me.” Gɔ ɔkɛlɛ katɔ̃ kɛkɛĩ ne, ɔkɔlɛ ɔfu i karɔ̃ ɔpɛ ɔ̃ ɔse nrɔɔ̃ sɔ, “Si ialɛ ne, tã inyɛwe ɔwi gɔgbe si ɔta ɔwara me.” Ne ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Tete!
Aawo ibiara ɔbara.
Si atɔrã ne, aawo inyɛwe ikɔi nɛgbe sɛnɛkɛ̃ra ɔrera me kama, ɣɛɛ daabara wũ kuɖɔɛ, bara fɔ kuɖɔɛ.” Gɔ ɔkpese ɔba marasuãdze itɛ kɔrɛ ne, ɔnya sɔ mato marɛ sirɛ.
Ne ɔɣere Simon Petro sɔ, “Simon, sirɛ ato arɛ?
Aibawo ɔsɛ ɔdzuɛ̃ iɣo ɔɖɔwũ ɔwɛ̃ pɛ kere?” Ne ka ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Misɛ midzuɛ̃, si mikparama kayi si miibabo i ilainyɔ ame.
Siwarã to sibie, ɣɛɛ siturina ɔɔfɛ̃.” Ne ɔrui ɔkɛlɛ ɔsɛ ɔ̃akparama kayi ɔɣɛ atɔ̃me wamɔ ame ana ne.
Gɔ ɔkpese ɔba ne, ɔ̃ marasuãdze to marɛ sirɛ ana.
Makpi sirɛ, ne ɔso maiɣe kumɛgɔ maaɖi so kanya.
Gɔ ɔkpese ɔba ɔkpɛ tɛare ne, ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Mitogu sirɛ?
Mitogu iwarã?
Ka ilɛ!
Ɔwi ɔɔɣo!
Maɔɖi mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, matã maturi lalaa!
Minyɔ ka masɛ i ɔri.
Mita si borui.
Minyɔ, ngɔ loɖi me ɔtã nɖegu ma katɔ̃.” Mamɔɛ̃ Yesu.
Gɔ Yesu togu ma ika iɖe ne, Yuda gɔ nɖe marasuãdze iweo-inyɔ ɔwɛ̃ ɔba ɔ̃abo.
Maturi ikuri nɛ i ma Yudase kasɔrɛkɔ̃ makpakpa gu mmara matedze gu ɔmagɛ̃ makpakpa ɔpia siai wũ maba.
Mato apɛ gu kudziriku.
Ngɔ loɖi wũ ɔtã ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ngɔ minya sɔ loya fiɛ lofiɔ̃ irɛkpo ne, ɔ̃ ɔɖe ne, mimɔɛ̃ wũ teteree mikɛlɛgu!” Ne ɔso gɔ Yuda ɔbore ɔbo Yesu ne, ɔkpere wũ sɔ, “Ratedze!” Ɔmini wũ ɔpia wũ kɔrɔ̃.
Mamɔɛ̃ Yesu mapɔrɛ wũ teteree.
Mma nɣɛgu Yesu mmɔ ɔwɛ̃ ɔɖi itekpe, ɔtu kasɔrɛkɔ̃ ɔkpakpa pelepele ɔɖabo kutsue.
Ne Yesu ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Be ɔso fiɛ miala akpo gu apɛ sɔ miba miamɔɛ̃ me lɛ yukukpe?
Ikpɛnɛ biara bo gu mi mpia i Ɣaa isɔrɛyo, fiɛ lowe i mmɔ lote Itɔ̃me Bielea, miimɔɛ̃ me.
Ɣɛɛ ne, iba ngbɔ sɔ nnɛ maɣɛ masɛ i Ɔko Sekelea ame aayi.” Ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔɖuɖu ɔtere maɣɛ wũ.
Ɔwi gɔgbe ne, ɔporoporoi ɔwɛ̃ gɔ nfu so ɔkati fudza siai Yesu i kama fiɛ ɔnya nwagbe ɔɖuɖu.
Makpakpɛ̃dze ɔbie sɔ si mamɔɛ̃ wũ, ɣɛɛ ɔkpɛ̃ ɔbɔrɛ ma iso.
Ɔ̃ ɔkati kere mana.
Ɔbɔrɛ ma i nrɔɔ̃ ame ɔrui ɔtere isɔ̃isɔ̃.
Yesu Ɔya I Yuda Makpakpa Pelepele Anɔmi.
Makɔ Yesu makɛlɛgu ma Yudase sɔrɛdzekpakpa pelepele iyo.
Mmɔ i Ɣaa iyo masɔrɛdze gu ɔmagɛ̃ makpakpa gu mmara matedze ɔsarɛ ne.
Petro ɔsiai ma kama dzoroo ɔba ɔ̃abo mmɔ, ne ɔsɛ i ikpata ame i madzuɛ̃se kɔrɛ ɔto ɔwa ɔtɔ ne.
Ɣaa masɔrɛdze gu atɔ̃memaɣɛdze ma ɔɖuɖu nsi ne, mato manyɔnyɔ itɔ̃me nɛ maasu matã Yesu ipɔ fiɛ mana wũ maɖoe.
Ɣɛɛ mainya kuira lalaa kuiwɛ̃.
Maturi gbodzoo ɔɖe aka maɖaɛ wũ kanya, ɣɛɛ ne, ma atɔ̃me ɔta aya so iso.
Ne mawɛ̃ ɔta maya maɖaɛ wũ kanya sɔ, “Bonɔ ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Loabiɛ Ɣaa Isɔrɛyo nɛ masu nrɔɔ̃ matsue i ngbe.
Fiɛ ayi atɛ kama ne, loatsue imama nɛ iiɖe maturi lotsue.’ ” Ɣɛɛ ma wũ ma atɔ̃me ana iikategu ma malaa are.
Ɣaa sɔrɛdzekpakpa pelepele ɔta ɔya i ma ɔɖuɖu katɔ̃ ɔkarɛ Yesu sɔ, “Anɔ itɔ̃me nɛ mato maɣɛ?
Be aba aaɣɛ?” Ɣɛɛ ne, Yesu ɔma kanya kpa, ɔ̃iɣɛ kuira.
Sɔrɛdzekpakpa pelepele ɔkarɛ wũ ana sɔ, “Fɔ nɖe Kristo gɔ nɖe Bosate Sekelea mɔmɔ Ɔbi?” Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Mme mmɔ ne.
Mi ɔɖuɖu to mianya Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi sɔ ɔsi i Ɣaa Ɔlesate kuɖearɔ̃ iso.
Fiɛ mianya sɔ ɔ̃abɔrɛ i kato i adɔdɔ ame ɔto ɔba!” Ɔluwɛ̃ sɔrɛdzekpakpa pelepele ɔkɛ so awu i sikpã ame sɔ, “Boisito bobie ku itɔ̃me kuiwɛ̃ i ɔmama kɔrɛ!
Ɔɣɛ imusuora ɔsegu i Ɣaa iso!
Nda minya?” Ne ma ɔɖuɖu ɔtɔrã masia ita sɔ matã wũ ipɔ sɔ ɔ̃akpi.
Ma mawɛ̃ ɔtsɛ minyatu itua ifere Yesu.
Manyi wũ anɔmi fiɛ matsɛ wũ ipɛ, mato maɣere wũ sɔ, “Ɣɛ ngɔ lopɛ-ɔ!” Ɔ̃ madzuɛ̃se mawɛ̃ to mapɛ wũ sirɔ̃ta.
Petro Ɔsɛ̃ Sɔ Ɔ̃iɣe Yesu.
Gɔ Petro si i ikpata ame mmɔ ne, iyo ame ɔsande birɔ̃gomi ɔwɛ̃ ɔbɔrɛ i sɔrɛdzekpakpa pelepele iyo ɔba.
Gɔ ɔnya Petro to ɔwa ɔtɔ ne, ɔnyɔ wũ totoroo ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Fɔ wũ asiai Yesu Nasaretse!” Ne Petro ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Be?
Loiɣe itɔ̃me nɛ ato aɣere me ngbe kiniɔ!” Ne ɔta ɔya ɔkɛlɛ kayogodɔ̃ kɔrɛ, kere ne rodza ɔɖi kanya ne.
Ɔbirɔ̃gomi gɔmɔ ɔledza wũ inya, ne ka ɔto ɔɣere mma nɣɛ i mmɔ sɔ, “Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ɔ̃ wũ ma ɔwɛ̃ ɔɖe!” Ɣɛɛ Petro ɔledza isɛ̃ ana.
Iifɔ ɔwi kɔra fiɛ mma nɣɛ i mmɔ ɔtsɛ Petro iɣere sɔ, “Gbagbaã ma ɔwɛ̃ aɖe, alasɔ fɔ wũ abɔrɛ i Galilea karɔ̃ iso!” Ne Petro ɔtsɛ ndamu ikã itarĩgu ara iɣɛ sɔ, “Lotarĩgu Ɣaa sɔ ɔkpadzɛ̃ me kutsue si lola sila!
Loiɣe ngɔ itɔ̃me mito miɣɛ i ngbe!” Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, rodza ɔɖi kanya ɔkpɛ nyɔare, ne ɔnyigi nnɛ i Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Si rodza aaɖi kanya ɔkpɛ nyɔare ne, ato aasɛ̃ me ikpɛ itɛ sɔ aiɣe me.” Ɔtu ɔbiɛ Petro, ne ɔpɛ kaku ne.
Makɔ Yesu Makɛlɛgu Abã Ɔkpakpa Pilato Iyo.
Gɔ kaɖe ɔsɛ̃ kaya tutuutu ne, ma Yudase masɔrɛdze ɔsarɛgu ma ɔmagɛ̃ makpakpa gu mmara matedze gu matɔ̃meɣɛdze ɔɖuɖu.
Gɔ masɛ iti ame i itɔ̃me iso ne, manyi Yesu fiɛ makɔ wũ makɛlɛgu Roma abã ɔkpakpa Pilato.
Mmɔ i Pilato ɔkarɛ Yesu sɔ, “Fɔ nɖe ma Yudase Igara ne?” Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Aĩ, ise lɛ kumɛgɔ ato aɣɛ.” Ɣaa masɔrɛdze ɔnyi atɔ̃me gbodzoo masia Yesu iso.
Ne ɔso Pilato ana ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Fɔ aito aɣɛ kuiwɛ̃?
Kã atsue si anɔ atɔ̃me wa mato maɣɛ i fɔ iso!” Ɣɛɛ Yesu iibusi kanya, ne ɔso ibara Pilato ɣaa.
Iyi siare nɛgbe ɔɖewi ne, Pilato sɛ ɔtɔrã maɖi yorɛdze ɔwɛ̃ gɔ makarɛ ɔtã ma.
Ɔwi gɔgbe ame ne, mamɔɛ̃ ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ sɔ Baraba mapia iyo gu mma lota maya ma Romase Igara iso, Gɔ mabara ngbɔ ɔso ne, mamɔɛ̃ ma fiɛ matã ma kukpi ipɔ alasɔ maɖoe maturi.
Ne iturikuri ɔkarɛ Pilato sɔ ɔnyigi ɔ̃ nnyainyɔ ɔtã ayo marɛdze lɛ kumɛgɔ ame ɔbua ɔsɛ ɔbara ɔwi biara.
Ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Mitɔrã sɔ lonyua ma Yudase Igara lotã mi?” Pilato ɔkarɛ ma ngbɔ alasɔ ɔɣe sɔ sirerɛ ɔso fiɛ makpakpa ɔmɔɛ̃ Yesu mabɔ wũ.
Ɣɛɛ Ɣaa masɔrɛdze ɔɣɛ mapia maturi sɔ Pilato si ɔnyua Baraba ɔtã ma.
Pilato ɔɖe iturikuri ika, ne ɔto ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Be mibie sɔ lobaragu ngɔ mito mirɔ sɔ ma Yudase Igara?” Ne masia kulu sɔ, “Tã mapɛ wũ mamatãra i kudziri iso!” Pilato ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Be iɖe ɔso?
Iɖe iɣɛrɛ nɛ ɔɣɛrɛ?” Ma ɔɖuɖu ɔsia kulu titiiti mabua mato maɣɛ sɔ, “Tã mapɛ wũ mamatãra i kudziri iso.” Gɔ Pilato to ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃abara ma kuɖɔɛ ɔso ne, ɔnyua Baraba ɔtã ma.
Ne ka ɔtã mapɛ Yesu kukaakɔ fiɛ ɔsu wũ ɔtã sɔ makɛlɛgu wũ maapɛ mamatãra i kudziri iso ne.
Makpakpɛ̃dze Ɔsopara Yesu.
Makɔ Yesu makɛlɛgu Roma abã ɔkpakpa iyo siare ame fiɛ makpere makpakpɛ̃dze tsɔra mabɔ.
Masu ɔgo rɛtɛa awu mapia wũ fiɛ masu igba miyu mabara igara ikoto masu matɔ̃medza wũ.
Ne mato mabara wũ, aɣiãra sɔ, “Ɣii-ɣiiɖuu!
Ma Yudase Igara, sɛ ngbã dzoroo!” Masu sidziri maɖeɖe wũ iti, fiɛ matua minyatu mafere wũ.
Ne mato mapɛ agɛgɛ̃ i ɔ̃ katɔ̃ sɔ mato masɔrɛ wũ ne.
Ɔwi gɔ maɔbara wũ aɣiãra maro ne, manyuarã ɔgo rɛtɛa awu, fiɛ masu ɔ̃ are mapia wũ.
Ne makɔ wũ maruigu sɔ maapɛ wũ mamatãra i kudziri iso ne.
Mapɛ Yesu Ma Matãra I Kudziri Iso.
Gɔ masɛ ne, masarɛgu ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Simon gɔ ɔse i ɔ̃ kasɛkɔ̃ ɔto ɔba Yerusalem.
Makpakpɛ̃dze ɔya wũ iso sɔ ɔfɔgu Yesu ɔnyigbã ɔsore.
Simon ɔse i Sireni, fiɛ ɔ̃ mabi nɖe Aleksandra gu Rufo ne.
Makɔ Yesu makɛlɛgu kabemi kawɛ̃ ga marɔ sɔ Golgata, gɔ karɔ̃ nɖe sɔ ɔturi iti ikui.
Gɔ mabo mmɔ ne, mabie sɔ si matã wũ ndã bea mɛ malupu kua gɔ mba ɔɖo sɔ ɔnɛ si ɔ̃ibana ibo, ɣɛɛ Yesu iinɛ.
Ne makpakpɛ̃dze ka mapɛ wũ mamatãra i kudziri iso ne.
Mapɛ sibɔ ala atalebi i ɔ̃ arapia iti si matsue ɔbiara nwa loaɣo wũ, masu maɣɛɣɛ so.
Mapɛ wũ mamatãra ku kaya iɖɔwũ kaiwɛ̃ tutuutu.
Matsɛrɛ nnɛ ɔbara masia i kakolo iso, masu mapɛ mamatãra i ɔ̃ sitikpe sɔ, “Ɔ̃ Nɖe Ma Yudase Igara Ne.” Mapɛ mayukukpe inyɔ ana mamatãra i Yesu kɔrɛ mmɔ, ɔwɛ̃ i ɔ̃ kuɖearɔ̃ iso, fiɛ ɔwɛ̃ ana sa i ɔ̃ kubena iso.
Iba lɛ kumɛgɔ matsɛrɛ masɛ i Ɔko Sekelea ame sɔ, “Maɖoe wũ ku makpibaradze.” Mma ɔɖuɖu loki i mmɔ mafe ɔtidza ati fiɛ matiatia Yesu sɔ, “Yuɛ!
Fɔ tutuutu fɔ loɣɛ sɔ aabiɛ bo isɔrɛyo siare nɛgbe aledza ne itsue i akpɛnɛ atɛ kama ne!
So ba si aɖi so i kukpi nrɔɔ̃ ame si bonya.” Ngbɔ ame i masɔrɛdze gu mmara matedze ana ɔma wũ maɣere so sɔ, “Ɔɖi mawɛ̃, ɣɛɛ ɔ̃ito ɔwo so ɔɖi!
Si fɔ nɖe Israel Igara gu Kristo gɔ i Ɣaa ɔɖi ɔsɛ mɔmɔ ne, ɖi so i kudziri iso si boafɔ-ɔ boɖe.” Maturi inyɔ ma mapɛ mamatãra mabua wũ iso ana ɔtiatia wũ.
Yesu Ɔkpi.
Kakɔme iɖɔwũ iweo-inyɔ ame ne, kayi ɔsɛ̃ guduu, ifɔ iɖɔwũ itɛ.
Iɖɔwũ itɛ̃ nɛgbe kama ne, Yesu ɔla kulu teteree sɔ, “Eli, Eli, lama sabaktani?” Gɔ karɔ̃ nɖe sɔ, “Wũ Ɣaa, wũ Ɣaa, be ɔso anyua me asɛ ngbɔ?” Mawɛ̃ ma loya i mmɔ manɔ ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Minɔ!
Ɔto ɔkpere Eliya.” Ma ɔwɛ̃ ɔtere ɔsu ɖɔti pukupukua ɔpia i ndã bea ame, ne ɔɖu ɔdziri ɔsu ɔtã Yesu ne.
Ne ɔɣere matsɔra sɔ, “Mitã bonyɔ si Eliya aaba ɔ̃aɖi wũ i kudziri iso!” Yesu ɔla kulu teteree ana kere ne ɔma kanya ne.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ tutuutu ne, ma Yudase isɔrɛyo ame ɔkati kpikpirikpi gɔ loɣɛ kasɔrɛkɔ̃ gu kasekelekɔ̃ ɔkɛ i ndɛ̃ndɛ̃ ita i kato iba iafere i karɔ̃.
Gɔ kpakpɛ̃dzekpakpa gɔ nɣɛ i Yesu katɔ̃ ɔnya kumɛgɔ ɔsu ɔkpi ne, ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Gbaã iɖe sɔ Ɣaa Ɔbi ɔɖe i ngbe.” Marɔ̃go mawɛ̃ ana ɔya dzoroo mato manyɔ.
Ma mawɛ̃ nɖe Maria Magdalase gu Salome gu Maria gɔ mabi nɖe Yakobo koso gu Yose ne.
Ɔwi gɔ i Yesu ɔwe i Galilea karɔ̃ iso ne, ma losiai wũ mala maɔbuai wũ ne.
Marɔ̃go gbodzoo mama ma losiai wũ maba Yerusalem ana ɔya i mmɔ.
Mabiara Yesu.
Nwagbe ɔɖuɖu ɔba ku iyi nɛ nɖe iledzaso itã ma Yudase Iwarãyi katɔ̃.
Ne gɔ kutsuɛ to kuɣo ne, ma Yudase atɔ̃meɣɛdze ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ sɔ Yosef, Arimatease, ɔpia so ɔle, ɔkɛlɛ Roma abã ɔkpakpa Pilato kɔrɛ.
Yosef ɖe ɔturi ɔwɛ̃ gɔ masɛ mawarɛ fiɛ ɔ̃ anɔ sia i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ iba iso.
Gɔ ɔbo Pilato kɔrɛ ne, ɔpɛ wũ nrɔɔ̃ sɔ ɔtã wũ ɔri si ɔsɛ ɔ̃abɛse Yesu kpise ɔsɛ ɔ̃abiara fiɛ Iwarãyi aaɣo.
Ibara Pilato ɣii gɔ ɔnɔ sɔ Yesu ɔkpi mala ngbɔ.
Ne ka ɔkpere kpakpɛ̃dzekpakpa gɔ loya i mmɔ ɔnya nwa loba pelepele, ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ iɔna ɔpã gɔ Yesu ɔkpi?
Ne gɔ ɔkpakpa ɔɣere wũ sɔ ɔ̃ɔkpi koko ne, Pilato ɔtã Yosef ɔri sɔ ɔsɛ ɔ̃aɖi wũ ɔbiara.
Ne Yosef ɔsɛ ɔ̃abɛse Yesu ɔbɔ karɔ̃, ɔmini wũ i ɔkati fudza gɔ ɔɣa ame.
Ne ka ɔsu wũ ɔbiara i itawo nɛ makuri masɛ i kube kukpa ame ne.
Ɔmɛrɛdza ita siare ɔtɛ̃ iwo kanya.
Maria Magdalase gu Maria gɔ nɖe Yose ɔnyi ɣɛ i mmɔ manya ngbegɔ ɔbiara wũ.
Yesu Ɔta Ɔbɔrɛ I Makpise Ndɛ̃.
Ikpɛnɛ nyɔare kutsuɛ gɔ Iwarãyi ɔɔro ne, Maria Magdalase gu Maria gɔ nɖe Yakobo ɔnyi gu Salome ɔsɛ maaɣa korobo sɔ maasɛ maasɔla Yesu.
Ne ɔso gɔ kaɖe ɔɖaɛ ku Kɔsiɖa kaya ne, mata sɔ masɛ kabiarakɔ̃.
-Gɔ masɛ i ɔri ne, mato makarɛ so sɔ, “Nna loamɛrɛdza ita ɔɖi i iwo kanya ɔtã bo?” Makarɛ so ngbɔ alasɔ ita siare iɖe.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ mabo mmɔ ne, manya sɔ ɔnyiiɔ ɔli ita sɛnɛkɛ̃ra ɔsɛ i kuruɛ.
Ne ɔso maso mabo i iwo ame, ne manya ɔporoporoi ɔwɛ̃ si i kuɖearɔ̃ iso, ɔpia awu fudza futututu ne.
Makpɛ̃ so.
Ɔporoporoi gɔmɔ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Midaanigã.
Loɣe sɔ Yesu Nasaretse gɔ mapɛ mamatãra i kudziri iso mito mibie.
Ɔna i ngbe!
Ɔ̃ɔta, ɔpia ngbã!
Minyɔ ngbegɔ marara wũ!
Ne ɔso misɛ miaɣere ɔ̃ marasuãdze gu Petro ana sɔ, ‘Yesu ɔɔɖe mi katɔ̃ ɔkpa Galilea karɔ̃ iso.
Mmɔ mianya wũ lɛ kumɛgɔ ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ ne.’ ” Ibara marɔ̃go magbe ɣii, ne marui i kabiarakɔ̃ mmɔ ku ifɔ̃ gu iti ikpakpa gu ise ne.
Gɔ marui ne, maiwo kuwɛ̃ ɔɣere i ɔri iso, alasɔ ifɔ̃ ɔmɔɛ̃ ma.
Yesu Ɔɖi So Ɔte Maria Magdalase.
Gɔ Yesu ɔta ɔbɔrɛ i makpise ame ku Kɔsiɖa kaya tutuutu ame ne, ɔɖe katɔ̃ ɔɖi so ɔte Maria Magdalase gɔ ame ɔsa siwarã lalaa ikɔdzɛ ɔɖi ɔnya.
Ɔsɛ ɔ̃aɣere Yesu malaa sɔ, Yesu ɔɔta ɔwi gɔ ame mato mabiɛ mamararã so ala ɔ̃ kukpi ɔso.
Gɔ Maria ɔɣere ma sɔ Yesu ɔɔta ɔpia ngbã ne ɔnya wũ ne, maifɔ wũ maɖe.
Yesu Ɔɖiso Ɔte Marasuãdze Inyɔ I Ɔri Iso.
Ɔwi gɔgbe kama ne, Yesu ɔɖi so ɔte marasuãdze inyɔ ma nsɛ i Yerusalem ɔri.
Mainya wũ maɖi ite i karɔ̃kasɛkɔ̃.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ matsue ne, makpese masɛ maaɣere matsɔra.
Ɣɛɛ ne, maifɔ ma maɖe.
Yesu Ɔɖi So Ɔte Marasuãdze Iweo-Ɔwɛ̃.
Katsɔrakɔ̃ ne, Yesu ɔɖi so ɔte marasuãdze iweo-ɔwɛ̃ i aɖera kaɖekɔ̃.
Ɔnyagalagu ma alasɔ mana kafɔkaɖe fiɛ ma atsue ba ɔle aɣede, fiɛ maifɔ mma lonya wũ maɖegu katɔ̃ maɖe sɔ ɔpia ngbã.
Ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mikɛlɛ kayi ɔɖuɖu ame si miɣɛ Ɣaa Itɔ̃me Bielea i maturi ɔɖuɖu ndɛ̃.
Ɔbiara gɔ loafɔ Itɔ̃me Bielea nɛ ɔɖe, fiɛ ɔ̃afɔ Ɣaa itupie kubarara ne, ɔ̃ana iɖi.
Ɣɛɛ ngɔ loifɔ ɔɖe ne, Ɣaa to ɔ̃atã wũ kukpi ipɔ.
Akparĩ wagbe loasiai mma lofɔ maɖe ne.
Maabara awawãra, maasa siwarã lalaa maɖi i wũ iyere ame.
Maaɣɛ siɖe ɣɛtɛ agbãagbã dzɛ maiɣe fiɛ maisuã.
Si mamɔɛ̃ aɣɛ ɣee si manɛ ndu lalaa ne, iibabara ma kuira.
Si masia manyɛse nrɔɔ̃ i ati ne, maana isosarɛ.” Ɣaa Ɔsu Yesu Ɔkɛlɛgu Kato.
Gɔ Bosate Yesu ɔɖe ma aka wamɔ kama ne, Ɣaa ɔsu wũ ɔkɛlɛgu kato ɔsɛra i ɔ̃ kuɖearɔ̃ iso.
Ɔ̃ masiaidze ana ɔki nrɔ̃ ɔɖuɖu iso maɣɛ ɔ̃ Itɔ̃me Bielea.
Ne Bosate ɔwe i ma ame, ɔsɛgu ma sɔ maɖi ɔ̃ Itɔ̃me Bielea mate iki awawãra agbãagbã wa mabara i ɔ̃ ɔle ame ne.
Wũ ɔnyii Tiofilo, maturi gbodzoo ɔɔpia so kubɛ kumɛgɔ maawo sɔ si matsɛrɛ ira masegu i ara wa loba i bo ndɛ̃ iso masɛ.
Matsɛrɛ lɛ kumɛgɔ i mma lonya Itɔ̃me Bielea karɔ̃kasɛkɔ̃ ɔɣere bo awe, fiɛ mato maya ne isã ana.
Ne ɔso ne, Bokɔse Tiofilo, gɔ mme wũ losu losia so iso lotsue ara wagbe ta karɔ̃kasɛkɔ̃ ɔso ne, lobara adzuni sɔ ilɛ sɔ loatsɛrɛ wã kukaakɔ losese-ɔ kumɛgɔ aba.
Nto lobara ngbɔ ala lobie sɔ aatsue ira biara nɛ mate-ɔ wodoroo.
Maɣɛ Yohanes Iɣe Masɛ.
Ɔwi gɔ ame i Herodes ɔɖe sigara i Yudea karɔ̃ iso ne, Ɣaa sɔrɛdze ɔwɛ̃ ɔwe gɔ marɔ Zakaria.
Ɔbɔrɛ i sɔrɛdze Abia ikuri ame.
Zakaria gɔgbe ɔre marɔ Elisabet ne.
Ɔ̃ wũ ɔbɔrɛ i masɔrɛdze ɔɣekparɛ ame.
Ɔrã gu ɔre gɔgbe ɔsɛ ngbã lɛ Ɣaa masɔrɛdze awe i Ɣaa anɔ.
Maɖe ɔ̃ mmara ɔɖuɖu iso kukaakɔ.
Ɣɛɛ ne, maiɣe ɔbi ala Elisabet ɖe ɔlɛma fiɛ ma inyɔɔ ana ɔɔsɛ katɔ̃ i akɔ ame.
Iyi iwɛ̃ ne, Zakaria ɔkɛlɛ ma Yudase isɔrɛyo sɔ ɔ̃abara ɔ̃ masɔrɛdze karabara ala ma ikuri iɔɣo sɔ maabara.
I masɔrɛdze kubarara kanya ne, gɔ mabara kareremi ne, Zakaria iso isia, ne ɔso ɔkɛlɛ Ɣaa isɔrɛyo ame sɔ ɔ̃atsuedza kua kɔrɔ̃kɔrɔ̃a ɔtã Ɣaa i isɔrɛkasege iso.
Ɔwi gɔ ɔto ɔtsuedza kua kɔrɔ̃kɔrɔ̃a mmɔ ne, masumudze tsɔra ɣɛ i inyamɔ mato makparama kayi.
Ɣaa kpabo ɔwɛ̃ ɔɖi so ɔte wũ.
Ɔɣɛ i isɔrɛkasege ga iso ɔto ɔtsuedza kua kɔrɔ̃kɔrɔ̃a kuɖearɔ̃ iso.
Gɔ Zakaria ɔnya wũ ne, ɔkpɛ̃ so, ifɔ̃ ɔmɔɛ̃ wũ gbaã.
Ɣɛɛ Ɣaa kpabo gɔmɔ ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Zakaria, daanigã!
Ɣaa ɔɔnɔ fɔ kayi ikparama, ne ɔso fɔ ɔre Elisabet to ɔ̃aɣe ɔbirɛrɛĩ ɔtã-ɔ.
Tã wũ iyere sɔ Yohanes.
Si maɣe wũ ne, ato aana isoɣɔ, alɛlɛ gbaã lɛ kumɛgɔ iaɖe maturi gbodzoo ana isoɣɔ.
Ɔto ɔ̃aɖe ɔturi siare i Ɣaa anɔ.
Ɔdaanɛ̃ ndã kpokporoa kumiwɛ̃ mɛ loamɔɛ̃ wũ ɖuɖuuɖu.
Siwarã Bielea to siayi ɔ̃ ame fiɛ maaɣe wũ.
Ɔ̃ loakpesera Israel maturi gbodzoo ɔbɔ ma Sate Ɣaa kɔrɛ ne.
Ɔ̃ ɔɖe loaɖe Bosate iba katɔ̃ fiɛ siwarã gu ɔle gɔ lowe i Ɣaa kanyaɖidze Eliya ame to iawe i ɔ̃ ame.
Ɔto ɔ̃afere mabi gu mase kanya ndu.
Ɔto ɔ̃afinikira matsuelese ɔkpesera mma nsɛ mabu iti ame i ibɔlɔlɔ iso.
Nnɛgbe loatã Bosate maturi ɔnyɔ tuee matã ɔ̃ iba ne.” Mmɔ i Zakaria to ɔkarɛ kpabo gɔgbe sɔ, “Be loatã lofɔ nnɛgbe loɖe?
Bo gu wũ iyo ɔnyi ɔɖuɖu somina ɔɔsɛ katɔ̃ i akɔ ame.” Ne kpabo to ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Mme nɖe Gabriel gɔ nsɛ ɔya i Ɣaa katɔ̃ ne.
Ɔ̃ ɔɖe lopia me sɔ loɣere-ɔ kanya gagbe ne.
Atoa sɔ aifɔ nnɛ loɣere-ɔ aɖe ne, ito iaba lɛ kumɛgɔ loɣɛ ku ɔwi gɔ i Ɣaa ɔsia ita.
Ɣɛɛ kumɛgɔ aifɔ aɖe ɔso ne, fɔ ɔnyagɛmi iisibata ɔnya gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ nnɛ loɣɛ ɔba i ne ame.” Ɔwi gɔ i nnɛgbe ɔɖuɖu to ikɛlɛ i katɔ̃ ne, mma nɣɛ masia Zakaria i isɔrɛyo inyamɔ ɔkpɔkpɔtɔ alasɔ maiɣe nnɛ ɔso fiɛ ɔ̃ɔna ɔpã ngbɔ.
Gɔ ɔba ɔ̃abɔrɛ i iyo ne, ɔ̃isito ɔwo ika ɔɖegu ma.
Ne ɔso matsue sɔ ɔnya iɖi ite i isɔrɛyo mmɔ.
Gɔ ɔ̃ito ɔwo ika ɔɖe ɔso ne, nrɔɔ̃ ka ɔto ɔɖiɖi si ɔ̃aɣere ma ira.
Ɔwi gɔ i Zakaria ɔɔro ɔ̃ karabara i isɔrɛyo ne, ɔkpese ɔkɛlɛ ɔ̃ iyo.
Ɔwi kurukutu kama ne, Elisabet ɔba ɔ̃ala kayiri, ne ɔso ɔkɔla so i iyo awa aru i kuɖokpo.
Ne Elisabet ɔɖe ika ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Kiniɔ ne, Ɣaa ɔɔnyɔ me nnya.
Ɔ̃ɔɖi me kunuarɛ i anɔ ɔkɔlɛ me anɔ kato i maturi ndɛ̃.” Maɣɛ Yesu Iɣe Masɛ.
Ɔwi gɔ i Elisabet kayiri ɔɔfɔ awa akuɔ ne, Ɣaa ɔpia ɔ̃ kpabo Gabriel sɔ ɔkɛlɛ ɔmagɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Nasaret i Galilea karɔ̃ iso.
Ɔsia wũ kanya i ɔbitɛ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ sɔ Maria kɔrɛ.
Ɔbitɛ gɔgbe makarɛ matã Yosef gɔ lobɔrɛ i igara David ɔɣekparɛ ame ne.
Gɔ kpabo ɔba ɔ̃abo Maria kɔrɛ ne, ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Isobuɛ itã-ɔ!
Bosate piagu-ɔ fiɛ ɔ̃ kusɛkusɛ ana sia-ɔ iso.” Kpabo gɔgbe atɔ̃me ɔkpɔkpɔtɔra Maria adzuni ala ɔ̃inɔ kaya gagbe karɔ̃.
Mmɔ i kpabo to ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Maria, daanigã ala Ɣaa nnyainyɔ piagu-ɔ.
Ato aba aala kayiri aɣe ɔbirɛrɛĩ, tã wũ iyere sɔ Yesu.
Ɔto ɔ̃afɔ iyere gbaã fiɛ maarɔ wũ sɔ Ɣaa Ɔlesate mɔmɔ ɔbi.
Bokɔse Ɣaa to ɔ̃asɛra wũ sigara lɛ ɔ̃ ɔwa tɛtɛ David awe.
Ɔto ɔ̃aɖe sigara i Yakob mawa iso ɔwi ɔɖuɖu ame.
Fiɛ ɔ̃ sigara iɖe iibafe inya ɖa.” Mmɔ i Maria to ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Nda nwagbe aawo ɔba gɔ loiɣe ɔrɛrɛ̃ kuwɛ̃?” Mmɔ i kpabo gɔmɔ to ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Siwarã Bielea to siayi fɔ ame fiɛ Kato gu Karɔ̃ Baradze ɔle to ɔ̃aba-ɔ iso.
Ne ɔso ɔbirɛrɛĩ gɔ aaɣe ne, maarɔ wũ sɔ, Ɔsekelea, Ɣaa Ɔbi Birɛrɛĩ.
Lobie sɔ loatã-ɔ itsue sɔ ne, fɔ ɔnyiibi gɔ nɖe Elisabet fiɛ ɔɖe ɔlɛma ne, ka ɔto kayiri awa akuɔ atoa sɔ ɔ̃ akɔ ɔɔsɛ katɔ̃.
Alasɔ kuira iiɖo Ɣaa ibara.” Ne Maria ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Nyɔ!
Mme ne, Ɣaa ɔɖabo loɖe.
Ɔbara ɔtã me lɛ kumɛgɔ aɣɛ.” Ne Ɣaa kpabo ɔrui ne.
Maria Ɔkɛlɛ Elisabet Kɔrɛ.
-Ayi wamɔ ame ne, Maria ɔledza so ɔpɛ siwa ɔkɛlɛ Yudea karɔ̃ iso i abe ndɛ̃.
Ɔkɛlɛ Zakaria iyo ɔsɛ ɔ̃aya Elisabet.
Gɔ Elisabet ɔnɔ Maria kaya ne, ɔ̃ ɔbi gɔ i kayiri ame ko lotsue ngba, ɔluwɛ̃ Siwarã Bielea ɔyi Elisabet ame ɔɖuɖu.
Ne ɔto ɔkpagɛ silɔ kato ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Maafere-ɔ kusɛkusɛ i marɔ̃go ndɛ̃ fiɛ fɔ ɔbi gɔ aaɣe ne, mafere wũ kusɛkusɛ!
Mme nɖe nna fiɛ Bosate ɔnyi aaba ɔ̃aya me?
Alasɔ ɔluwɛ̃ gɔ lonɔ fɔ kaya ne, ɔbi gɔ mpia me i kayiri ame ko lokpɛ̃ so i isoɣɔ ame.
Na isoɣɔ gbaã alasɔ afɔ kanya ga i Ɣaa kpabo ɔba ɔ̃aɣere-ɔ aɖe sɔ iaba ɔso.” Maria Ɔka Siba Ipɛ Ɔnɔ.
Ne Maria ɔpia ɔnɔ kanya sɔ, “Wũ ɔtu to ɔle Bosate.
Fiɛ so ɔɣɔ me i Ɣaa gɔ nɖe wũ Ɖidze iso, alasɔ ɔnyigi me ɔ̃ ɔɖabo gɔ loire kuira.
Ita i kiniɔ ito ikɛlɛ ne, mawa gu mawa tɛtɛ ɔɖuɖu to maakpere me sɔ ɔturi gɔ ilɛgu.
Alasɔ Ɔlesate ɔbara ara siare ɔtã me, fiɛ ɔ̃ iyere se sekelee.
Ɔ̃ nnyainyɔ se itã mawa gu mawa ma ɔɖuɖu nsɛ manigã wũ.
Ɔɖi ɔ̃ ɔle ɔte fiɛ ɔsamarã mma nsɛ makɔlɛ so kato i ma situ ame.
Ɔkpasera magarakpakpa fiɛ ɔkɔlɛ mma lobɔ so karɔ̃ kato.
Ɔsu ara sɛɛ ɔmidza mma i kukã to, ɔkpesera maranase mawɛrɛba.
Ɔ̃ anɔ sia i itɔ̃me nɛ ɔɣere bo mawa ɔsɛ iso, fiɛ ɔ̃ɔba sɔ ɔ̃abuai Israel kaɖe.
Ɔnyigi ɔ̃ nnyainyɔ nɛ ɔsu ɔtã Abraham gu ɔ̃ mawa ikpa ta kayi karokɔ̃.” Ne ɔso Maria ka ɔwegu Elisabet awa atɛ ɔɖui fiɛ ɔkpese ɔkɛlɛ ɔ̃ aɖe.
Ndupiedze Yohanes Iɣe.
Gɔ ɔwi ɔɣo sɔ Elisabet aaɣe ɔbi ne, ɔɣe ɔbirɛrɛĩ.
Ɔ̃ magbamikui gu ɔ̃ manyii ɔɖuɖu ɔnɔ iwawãra siare nɛ i Ɣaa ɔbara ɔtã wũ.
Ne ɔso managu wũ isoɣɔ gbaã.
Iyi nɛ maɖi ɔbi i iyo ne, masɛ maatu wũ sirɛrɛ̃ fiɛ mabie sɔ si masu ɔ̃ ɔse iyere Zakaria masia wũ.
Ɣɛɛ ɔ̃ ɔnyi iinɔgu ma karɔ̃.
Ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Misia wũ Yohanes.” Mawararã ku wũ sɔ, “Mi ɔlɛdze ɔmele masɛ marɔ ngbɔ?” Mmɔ maɖiɖi nrɔɔ̃ makarɛ ɔbi ɔse sɔ mme iyere ɔto ɔbie sɔ masia ɔbi.
Zakaria ɔkarɛ ita nɛ iso masɛ matsɛrɛ ara.
Gɔ ɔfɔ ne ne, ɔtsɛrɛ sɔ, “Ɔ̃ iyere nɖe Yohanes.” Ne ɔso ibara ma ɔɖuɖu ɣii.
Ɔluwɛ̃ Zakaria ɔnyagɛmi ɔkurisi ɔtsɛ ika iɖe ile Ɣaa.
Ifɔ̃ siare ɔmɔɛ̃ ɔ̃ magbamikui itã sɔ itɔ̃me nɛgbe ɔki ikã Yudea simagɛ̃ dzɛ i abe iso abuiti ɔɖuɖu ame.
Mma ɔɖuɖu lonɔ ara wagbe ɔla maɔkarɛ so sɔ, “Mme ɔturi igbã i ɔbi gɔgbe to ɔba ɔ̃aɖe?” Makarɛ so ngbɔ ala ite sekelee sɔ Ɣaa kɔrɔ̃ sia wũ iso.
Zakaria Ɔɣɛ Itɔ̃me Ɔsɛ.
Mmɔ i Siwarã Bielea ɔbo i ɔbi ɔse Zakaria ame ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ sɔ, “Mitã bole Bosate gɔ nɖe Israel Ɣaa alasɔ ɔbuai kaɖe, ɔɖi bo sɔ boana isobuɛ.
Ɔsu Ɖidze gɔ mba ɔle ɔtã bo gɔ lobɔrɛ i ɔ̃ ɔɖabo igara David ɔkparɛ ame.
Ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ kokooko ɔkigu i ɔ̃ kanyamaɖidze sekelea iso sɔ ɔ̃aɖi bo ɔbɔrɛgu i mma nto mabie bo ikpi gu bo matsirise ɔɖuɖu nrɔɔ̃ ame.
Ɔɣɛ sɔ ɔ̃anyɔ bo nnya lɛ kumɛgɔ ɔɣere bo mawa ɔsɛ fiɛ ɔ̃anyigi kanya ga ɔnyi ku bo mawa.
Ɔkã ndamu ɔtã bo ɔwa Abraham teteree sɔ, ɔ̃aɖi bo ɔbɔrɛgu i bo matsirise nrɔɔ̃ ame ɔtã bo bobara ɔ̃ karabara sɔ ifɔ̃ iisibakpɛ̃ bo.
Ɔto ɔ̃asekelera bo fiɛ ɔ̃abara bo bɔlɔlɔ i ɔ̃ anɔ i bo agbanayi ɔɖuɖu ame.
Fiɛ fɔ, wũ ɔbi ne, maakpere-ɔ sɔ, Ɣaa Ɔlesate kanyaɖidze.
Fɔ loaɖe Bosate katɔ̃ aledza ɔri atã ɔ̃ iba ne.
Ato aaɖi ate maturi sɔ maana iɖi ala mato maana akpi isu itsɛ.
Bo Ɣaa sɛ ɔɣara so pɔkɔsɔɔ fiɛ ɔba nnyainyɔ.
Ɔto ɔ̃asese bo Ɖidze gɔ loafiɛ ɔfere bo lɛ kuɣɛ̃.
Ɔto ɔ̃atã ikpawaĩ nɛgbe ɔba itã maturi ma nsi i idududu ame fiɛ kukpi ifɔ̃ to ma sɔ ɔ̃akɔ bo ɔkigu i isobuɛ ɔri iso.” Gɔ ɔbi ɔba ɔ̃are iti ne, ɔwe ɔle i Siwarã Bielea ame.
Ɔwe i fafuĩ ame ngbegɔ i maturi na gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ ɔwi gɔ ɔ̃ɔledza so ɔtã sɔ ɔ̃abara ɔ̃ karabara i Israel.
Maɣe Yesu.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, Roma Igarakpakpa Kaisaro Augusto ɔtã ɔle sɔ matsɛrɛ maturi ma ɔɖuɖu mpia i Roma Sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ame ayere.
Maturi ayere itsɛrɛ ɖeakatɔ̃ nɛgbe ame ne, abã ɔkpakpa gɔ marɔ sɔ Kirenio nto ɔɖe Siria karɔ̃ iso.
Ne ɔso ɔbiara ɔkɛlɛ ɔ̃ aɖe sɔ ɔ̃atsɛrɛ iyere.
Yosef ana ɔbɔrɛ i Nasaret ɔmagɛ̃ ame i Galilea karɔ̃ iso ɔkɛlɛ Betlehem ɔmagɛ̃ ame i Yudea karɔ̃ iso ngbegɔ maɣe igara David.
Yosef ɔkɛlɛ mmɔ alasɔ David ɔkparɛ ame ɔbɔrɛ.
Ɔkɔ Maria gɔ makarɛ mata wũ fiɛ ka ɔto kayiri ana ɔsɛgu.
Ɔwi gɔ mapia i Betlehem mmɔ ne, Maria ɔwi ɔɣo sɔ ka ɔ̃aɣe ɔbi.
Ɔɣe ɔ̃ ɔbi ɖeakatɔ̃ gɔ nɖe ɔbirɛrɛĩ.
Ɔmini wũ i ɔkati ame ɔsu wũ ɔrara i ira nɛ ame masɛ mafere mabɔi aɖera, alasɔ maina kabokɔ̃ i mafɔ kawekɔ̃.
Ɣaa Makpabo Ɔsu Itɔ̃me Bielea Mabɔ Masɛrɛkɔdze.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame i karɔ̃ gamɔ iso ne, masɛrɛkɔdze mawɛ̃ pia mmɔ mato manyɔ masɛrɛ iso ku kasɛ̃.
Ɣaa kpabo ɔwɛ̃ ɔɖi so ɔte ma fiɛ Bosate ifiɛ ɔfere ma ibɔrɛ i kato.
Itã sɔ ifɔ̃ ɔmɔɛ̃ ma gbaã, Ɣɛɛ Ɣaa kpabo ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Midaanigã.
Itɔ̃me sɛɛ nɛ loatã maturi ɔɖuɖu isoɣɔ losu lobɔ mi.
Nɔme ikpɛnɛ nɛgbe iso ne, maɣe Ɖidze gɔ nɖe Bosate Kristo matã mi i igara David ɔmagɛ̃ ame.
Nnɛ miasu minya wũ miɖi ite nɖe sɔ ne, mito mianya ɔbi ɣɛtɛ gɔ mamini i ɔkati ame fiɛ ɔrɛ i mabɔi ara kaɖekɔ̃.” Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, Ɣaa makpabo ikuri siare ɔbɔrɛ i kato maba mabuai kpabo gɔmɔ iso matsɛ Ɣaa ile sɔ, “Ikpawaĩ nɖe Ɣaa ɔkpɛ i kato dzoroo, isobuɛ itã karɔ̃ iso maturi ɔɖuɖu ma i Ɣaa sɛ ɔɖɔɛ!” Gɔ Ɣaa makpabo ɔrui makɛlɛ kato ne, masɛrɛkɔdze ɔɣere so sɔ, “Mitã bokɛlɛ Betlehem boanyɔ nnɛ loba fiɛ Bosate to ɔɖi ɔte bo ngbe.” Ne ɔso mapɛ siwa masɛ maanya Maria gu Yosef gu ɔbi ɣɛtɛ gɔ nrɛ i mabɔi aɖera kaɖekɔ̃.
Gɔ manya wũ ngbɔ ne, maɣɛ ara wa i Ɣaa kpabo gɔmɔ ɔɣere ma i ɔbi iso.
Mma ɔɖuɖu lonɔ ara wa i masɛrɛkɔdze ɔɣɛ ne, ibara ma ɣii.
Ɣɛɛ Maria ɔmɔɛ̃ ara wagbe ɔɖuɖu ɔpia i ɔ̃ adzuni ame ɔla ɔ̃ɔbu wã iti ame.
Masɛrɛkɔdze ɔkpese makɛlɛ mato male Ɣaa makɔlɛ ɔ̃ iyere kato i ira nɛ manya gu nwa manɔ ɔso alasɔ iba ngbɔ tutuutu lɛ kumɛgɔ i Ɣaa kpabo ɔɣere ma.
Masia Ɔbi Ɣɛtɛ Iyere.
Iyi farafanava gɔ maɖi ɔbi i iyo fiɛ matu wũ sirɛrɛ̃ ne, masia wũ iyere sɔ Yesu lɛ kumɛgɔ i Ɣaa kpabo gɔmɔ ɔɣɛ fiɛ mala ɔ̃ kayiri.
Masu Yesu Makɛlɛgu Ma Yudase Isɔrɛyo.
Gɔ ɔwi ɔɣo sɔ Yosef gu Maria aabara so sekelee i kubarara kanya lɛ kumɛgɔ i Mose mmara ɔte ne, makɔ ɔbi ɣɛtɛ ana makɛlɛgu Yerusalem sɔ maasu wũ mapia i Bosate nrɔɔ̃ ame.
Lɛ kumɛgɔ matsɛrɛ mapia i Ɣaa mmara ɔko ame sɔ, “Ɔbirɛrɛĩ ɖeakatɔ̃ biara gu bɔi rɛrɛ̃ ɖeakatɔ̃ biara ne, ikote sɔ maatɛ wũ masɛ i kuruɛ matã Bosate.” Masɛ maafɛ̃ ara matã Ɣaa alasɔ mmara ɔkarɛ sɔ maasu abɔrɔnuma ɣee kukpaboi kunyɔ mafɛ̃ ara mata wũ.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Simeon ɔwe i Yerusalem.
Ɔɖe ɔturi sɛɛ gɔ nsɛ ɔnigã Ɣaa fiɛ ɔto ɔnyɔ ɔri ɔtã Israel iɖi.
Siwarã Bielea sɛgu wũ fiɛ sisia ita sitã wũ sɔ ɔ̃ibakpi gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ ɔnya maɣe Ɣaa Kristo gɔ maɣɛ masɛ kokooko.
Ne ɔso Siwarã Bielea ɔkɔ Simeon sikɛlɛgu ma Yudase isɔrɛyo.
Gɔ maɣese ɔsu Yesu biɛtɛ mabɔ sɔ maba maabara kubarara gɔ i Mose mmara ɔkarɛ sɔ mabara ne, Simeon ɔfɔ ɔbi ɔla i nrɔɔ̃ ame ɔle Ɣaa sɔ, “Kiniɔ ne Bosate, gɔ ɔɔbara nnɛ aɣɛ asɛ atã me ne, ka aawo fɔ ɔɖabo ɔri ɔɖi i isobuɛ ame.
Mme mɔmɔ ku wũ anɔ ne, loɔnya Ɖidze gɔ asese sɔ ɔba ɔ̃aɖi maturi ɔɖuɖu katɔ̃.
Ɔ̃ nɖe ikpawaĩ nɛ loaɖi fɔ kuɖɔɛ ite maturi ma loiɖe ma Yudase ne.
Fiɛ ɔ̃aɖi fɔ ibu ɔte fɔ kaɖe Israel maturi.” Ara wa i Simeon ɔɣɛ i ɔbi iso ɔbara Yosef gu Maria ɣii.
Ne Simeon ɔtã ma kusɛkusɛ ɔɣere ɔbi ɔnyi sɔ, “Ɣaa ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ i ɔbi gɔgbe iso sɔ, iaki i ɔ̃ iso ne, maturi gbodzoo aarɔ̃, fiɛ iaki i ɔ̃ iso ana ne, gbodzoo ana to maata maya i Israel.
Maledza wũ iɖi sɔ ɔ̃aɖe ikparĩ nɛ iso i maturi aaɖe ika mata maya.
Ɔto ɔ̃aɖi maturi adzuni wɛrɛa ɔbɔ i ɔgbami.
Nnɛgbe ɔso ne, ibo gu ibɛbɛrɛ to iabo-ɔ i ɔtu ame lɛ ipɛmi matsue-ɔ awe.” Ɔrɔ̃go ɔwɛ̃ gɔ nɖe Ɣaa kanyaɖidze marɔ wũ sɔ Hana ɔwe i mmɔ.
Ɔ̃ ɔse Fanuel ɔbɔrɛ i Aser kalɛ ame.
Akɔ akɔdzɛ pɛ ɔsɛ i kurã iyo fiɛ ɔ̃ ɔrã ɔkpi.
Ɔ̃ɔsɛ sikuɛdze ɔfɔ akɔ fasinafasina-ina.
Kasɛ̃ i kakɔme ne, ɔsɛ ɔwe i ma Yudase isɔrɛyo ɔle Ɣaa ɔnyi kanya ɔkparama kayi ana.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, ɔ̃ wũ ɔba isɔrɛyo ɔba ɔ̃apɛ Ɣaa siba.
Ɔɖe ika i ɔbi gɔgbe iso ɔɣere maturi ma ɔɖuɖu nto manyɔ ɔri sɔ Ɣaa aaɖi Yerusalem.
Makpese Makɛlɛ Nasaret.
Gɔ Yosef gu Maria ɔɔro kubarara lɛ kumɛgɔ i Ɣaa mmara ɔte ne, makpese makɛlɛ ma aɖe Nasaret i Galilea karɔ̃ iso.
Ɔbi ɔmɔ ɔre iti fiɛ ɔwe isosarɛ gu iwola ana gbaã gɔ itã sɔ ɔbo Ɣaa anɔ.
Yesu Ɔkɛlɛ Ma Yudase Kasɔrɛkɔ̃ Ikɔ biara ne, Yesu maɣese sɛ masɛ Yerusalem maaɖe iyi nɛ masɛ marɔ sɔ Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo Iyi.
Ne ɔso gɔ Yesu ɔfɔ akɔ aweo-anyɔ ne, masɛ Yerusalem lɛ kumɛgɔ masɛ mabara kokooko awe.
Gɔ maɖe iyi maro fiɛ makpese mato makɛlɛ ma aɖe ne, Yesu ɔkpese ɔwe i Yerusalem gɔ ɔ̃ maɣese iitsue.
Mabu sɔ ɔpia i maturi ma nsɛ i ɔri ndɛ̃, ne ɔso masɛ ɔri ikpɛnɛ iwɛ̃ buu fiɛ matsɛ wũ ibie i ma malɛdze gu malaa ndɛ̃.
Gɔ mainya wũ ɔso ne, makpese makɛlɛ Yerusalem masɛ mapia manyɔnyɔ wũ.
Ikpɛnɛ tɛare iso ne, masɛ maanya wũ i ma Yudase isɔrɛyo gɔ ɔ̃ gu ma Yudase maratedze mawɛ̃ si.
Ɔto ɔkã ma atsue ɔkarɛ ma atɔ̃me ɔnɔ.
Mma ɔɖuɖu lonɔ ɔ̃ ara karɔ̃ iɖiɖi ne, ibara ma ɣii i ɔ̃ iwola wodoroa nɛ ɔto ɔtã ala atɔ̃me mmuai ɔso.
Ibara ɔ̃ maɣese lɛ kurɛ gɔ manya wũ ngbɔ.
Ne ɔ̃ ɔnyi ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ɔbi, be ɔso fiɛ abara bo ngbɔ?
Bo gu fɔ ɔse ɔɔmararã so bowe bobie-ɔ.” Ne Yesu to ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Be ɔso fiɛ mipia mibie me?
Miiɣe sɔ ikote sɔ loawe i wũ ɔse iyo?” Ɣɛɛ mainɔ nnɛ ɔɣere ma karɔ̃.
Ne Yesu ka ɔta ɔsiai ma marui makɛlɛ Nasaret, ɔbɔ so karɔ̃ ɔtã ma.
Ɣɛɛ ɔ̃ ɔnyi ne, ɔkɔla ara wagbe i ɔ̃ iti ame.
Yesu ɔre iti i sosina gu iwola ame, ɔbo maturi gu Ɣaa ɔɖuɖu anɔ.
Ndupiedze Yohanes Ɔya Itɔ̃me Bielea Isã.
Igarakpakpa Kaisaro Tiberio ikɔ weoruva i iyara iso ne, Pontio Pilato loɖe abã ɔkpakpa i Yudea karɔ̃ iso.
Galilea karɔ̃ iso ana ne, Herodes loɖe ɔkpakpa fiɛ ɔ̃ kpeama gɔ marɔ Filipo ɔɖe Iturea gu Trakoniti abuiti iso ɔkpakpa.
Lisania ana ɔɖe Abilene ibuiti iso.
Hana gu Kayafa loɖe Ɣaa masɔrɛdze makpakpa pelepele.
Ikɔ nɛmɔ ame ne, Yohanes gɔ nɖe Zakaria ɔbi ɔfɔ silɔ ɔbɔrɛgu i Ɣaa kɔrɛ i fafuĩ ame.
Ne ɔso Yohanes ɔwe ɔki i Yordan sikpokpo gu abuiti ame ɔɖuɖu ɔto ɔɣɛ Ɣaa itɔ̃me sɔ, “Mifiniki mibɔrɛ i mi akpi ame si mifɔ Ɣaa itupie kubarara si Ɣaa aasu mi akpi ɔtsɛ mi.” Lɛ matsɛrɛ mapia i Ɣaa Kanyaɖidze Yesaya ɔko ame sɔ, “Ɔwɛ̃ to ɔla kulu i fafuĩ ame sɔ, ‘Miledza Bosate ɔri misɛ.
Mibara ɔ̃ siri tɔrɔrɔ.
Miyira kugbolomi ɔɖuɖu si mibiɛ abe gu kubemi ɔɖuɖu mibɔ karɔ̃.
Mibara siri gɔgɔlɔa ɔɖuɖu tɔrɔrɔ.
Si mitã sɔ siri woworea ɔɖuɖu iso aase sɔlɔsɔlɔ.
Mmɔ i maturi ɔɖuɖu aanya Ɖidze gɔ i Ɣaa ɔsese ne!’ ” Maturi gbodzoo ɔba sɔ Yohanes si ɔpie ma ndu ɣɛɛ Yohanes ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mi ma lo nyanyarĩ lɛ maɣɛ!
Nna loɣere mi sɔ miawo ɔtere ɔbɔrɛ i Ɣaa kutsue ikpadzɛ̃ nɛ ɔ̃abɔ i maturi lalaa iso ame?
Mite i mi nsɛgbai ame sɔ miɔfiniki mibɔrɛ i mi akpi ame.
Midaabu sɔ gɔ Abraham mawa miɖe ɔso ne, Ɣaa iibakpadzɛ̃ mi kutsue.
Nto loɣere mi sɔ Ɣaa to ɔ̃awo mawa ɔbara ɔɖi i ata wa nfere i ngbe ame ɔtã Abraham.
Minyɔ!
Maɔkarã kaɣɛ i adziri iso koko sɔ maatu wã ta siɖu ame.
Kudziri biara gɔ loisɛ kuɣɔ̃ abi sɛɛ ne, maaɖaɛ kɔ̃ mapɛyu matsuedza.” Mmɔ mato makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Be si bobara kiniɔ?” Ne Yohanes to ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ngɔ mba awu aka anyɔ ne, ɔsu awɛ̃ ɔtã ngɔ nna kuawɛ̃.
Ngɔ mba araɖea si ɔɣɛ wã ɔtã mma nna.” Ma lampofɔdze mawɛ̃ ana ɔba sɔ ɔpie ma ndu.
Makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ratedze, be si bobara?” Ne ɔto ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Midaafɔ sikã i maturi kɔrɛ miɖo kumɛgɔ i mmara ɔkarɛ.” Makpakpɛ̃dze mawɛ̃ ana ɔba maakarɛ wũ sɔ, “Bo ne, be si bobara?” Ma wũ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mitã mi kuso si kusi mi.
Midaasu ɔle mifɔ kuwɛ̃ sikã i ɔri gɔ loikote iso.
Midaaɖaɛ kuwɛ̃ ana kanya.” Maturi ɔriinyɔ ɔtsɛ kato ikɔlɛ.
Matsɛ ibu sɔ bɛrɛ Yohanes nɖe Kristo gɔ mato manyɔ ɔri.
Ne ɔso Yohanes ɔɣere ma ɔɖuɖu sɔ, “Ndu losu loto lopie mi, Ɣɛɛ ngɔ nsiai me i kama ne, ɔmɔ ɔɖo me fafaafã.
Loikote sɔ loabɔdzo lokurisi ɔ̃ ndokota kɔra.
Ngɔgbe nto ɔ̃asu Siwarã Bielea gu ɔtɔ ɔpie mi ndu.
Ɔto ɔ̃ ifɛra nɛ ɔ̃asu ɔfɛ simɔɣo ɔɖi i araɖea ame fiɛ ɔ̃asu kamɔ ɔfere i kawu ame.
Ɔto ɔ̃atsuedza simɔɣo gu ɔtɔ gɔ loibanyi ɔnya!” I siri agbãagbã iso ne, Yohanes ɔɖiɖi Ɣaa itɔ̃me karɔ̃ ɔte maturi ku ɔle sɔ mafinikira ma nsɛgbai.
Ɣɛɛ Yohanes ɔkidza abã ɔkpakpa Herodes ala Herodia gɔ nɖe ɔ̃ ɔnyiibi ɔre fiɛ ɔfɔ ɔyiri iti.
Ɔkidza wũ ala ara nyanyarĩa mama wa ana ɔto ɔbara ɔso.
Nnɛ i Herodes ɔbara i ne kama gɔ inyanyarĩ iɖo nɖe sɔ ɔtã mamɔɛ̃ Yohanes mapia i iyo.
Yohanes Ɔpie Yesu Ndu.
Gɔ Yohanes ɔɔpie maturi ɔɖuɖu ndu ɔro ne, Yesu ɔ̃ wũ mapie wũ ndu.
Gɔ ɔto ɔkparama kayi ne, kato ɔbusi.
Ne Siwarã Bielea ɔso siba siasɛ wũ iso lɛ ilɔpɔ ne.
Manɔ silɔ ɔbɔrɛ i kato sito siɣɛ sɔ, “Fɔ nɖe wũ ɔbi gɔ loipia kuɣɛ ne, abo me anɔ gbaã.” Ɔɣekparɛ Gɔ Ame I Yesu Ɔbɔrɛ Ngbe Ne.
Yesu ɔfɔ lɛ akɔ sitɛ fiɛ ɔtsɛ ɔ̃ karabara.
Maturi ne, ɔbu masɛ mabu sɔ ɔ̃ ɔse nɖe Yosef gɔ ɔse nɖe Eli gɔ ɔse nɖe Mattat gɔ ɔse nɖe Levi gɔ ɔse nɖe Melki gɔ ɔse nɖe Yona gɔ ɔse nɖe Yosef gɔ ɔse nɖe Matatia gɔ ɔse nɖe Amos gɔ ɔse nɖe Nahum gɔ ɔse nɖe Esli gɔ ɔse nɖe Nagae gɔ ɔse nɖe Mahat gɔ ɔse nɖe Matatia gɔ ɔse nɖe Semein gɔ ɔse nɖe Yosef gɔ ɔse nɖe Yuda gɔ ɔse nɖe Yohanan gɔ ɔse nɖe Resa gɔ ɔse nɖe Zerubabel gɔ ɔse nɖe Sealtiel gɔ ɔse nɖe Neri gɔ ɔse nɖe Melki gɔ ɔse nɖe Adi gɔ ɔse nɖe Kosam gɔ ɔse nɖe Elmadam gɔ ɔse nɖe Er gɔ ɔse nɖe Yosua gɔ ɔse nɖe Eliezer gɔ ɔse nɖe Yorim gɔ ɔse nɖe Matat gɔ ɔse nɖe Levi gɔ ɔse nɖe Simeon gɔ ɔse nɖe Yuda gɔ ɔse nɖe Yosef gɔ ɔse nɖe Yonam gɔ ɔse nɖe Eliakim gɔ ɔse nɖe Melea gɔ ɔse nɖe Mena gɔ ɔse nɖe Matata gɔ ɔse nɖe Natan gɔ ɔse nɖe David gɔ ɔse nɖe Isai gɔ ɔse nɖe Obed gɔ ɔse nɖe Boaz gɔ ɔse nɖe Salmon gɔ ɔse nɖe Naheson gɔ ɔse nɖe Aminadab gɔ ɔse nɖe Admin gɔ ɔse nɖe Arni gɔ ɔse nɖe Ezron gɔ ɔse nɖe Perez gɔ ɔse nɖe Yuda gɔ ɔse nɖe Yakob gɔ ɔse nɖe Isak gɔ ɔse nɖe Abraham gɔ ɔse nɖe Tara gɔ ɔse nɖe Nahor gɔ ɔse nɖe Seruk gɔ ɔse nɖe Regu gɔ ɔse nɖe Peleg gɔ ɔse nɖe Eber gɔ ɔse nɖe Sala gɔ ɔse nɖe Kainan gɔ ɔse nɖe Arfaksad gɔ ɔse nɖe Sem gɔ ɔse nɖe Noa gɔ ɔse nɖe Lamek gɔ ɔse nɖe Metusala gɔ ɔse nɖe Henok gɔ ɔse nɖe Yared gɔ ɔse nɖe Mahalaleel gɔ ɔse nɖe Kainan gɔ ɔse nɖe Enok gɔ ɔse nɖe Set gɔ ɔse nɖe Adam gɔ ɔse nɖe Ɣaa.
Ɔbosam Ɔla Yesu Ɔnyɔ.
Gɔ Yesu ɔbɔrɛ i Yordan ɔwore ame ne, Siwarã Bielea ɔyi i ɔ̃ ame, ne si kɔ wũ sikɛlɛgu fafuĩ ame ne.
Mmɔ i Ɔbosam ɔla wũ ɔnyɔ akpɛnɛ sina buu ne.
Ɔwi gɔgbe ame ɔɖuɖu ne, Yesu iiɖe kuira ne ɔso kukã ɔkpɛ̃ wũ i kawirikɔ̃.
Ɔbosam ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Si fɔ nɖe Ɣaa Ɔbi ne, ɣere ita nɛgbe sɔ ikpese aɖera.” Ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Matsɛrɛ mapia i Ɔko Sekelea ame sɔ, ‘Iiɖe aɖera ɔnɔwɛ̃ iso i ɔturi aasɛ ngbã.’ ” Ne kama ne, Ɔbosam ɔledza wũ ikɔ ikɛlɛgu kakɔi kɔlɛa kawɛ̃.
Ɔte wũ kayiiso Sigarakuɖekɔ̃ ɔɖuɖu i ɔwi kurukutu ame.
Ne ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Loasu kayiiso ɔle gɔgbe ɔɖuɖu gu kã karana lotã-ɔ alasɔ mme masu matã fiɛ loawo ɔsu ɔtã ngɔ loɖɔɛ.
Nwagbe ɔɖuɖu to aakpese fɔ are si abɔ iti karɔ̃ atã me.” Mmɔ i Yesu to ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Matsɛrɛ i Ɔko Sekelea ame sɔ ne, ‘Bosate Ɣaa ɔnɔwɛ̃ nɖe ngɔ lokote sɔ maapɛ agɛgɛ̃ matã, masɔrɛ.’ ” Ne kama ne, Ɔbosam ɔledza Yesu ikɔ ikɛlɛgu Yerusalem ma Yudase isɔrɛyo itititɛ̃ pelepele.
Ne ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Si Ɣaa ɔbi aɖe ne, nyua so sɛ aawuĩ i karɔ̃.
Alasɔ matsɛrɛ i Ɔko Sekelea ame sɔ, ‘Ɣaa to ɔ̃atã sɔ ɔ̃ makpabo aaya madzuɛ̃-ɔ kukaakɔ.’ ‘Mamɔɛ̃-ɔ i nrɔɔ̃ ame sɔ aibasu fɔ kukpa awuĩ i ita kuiwɛ̃ iso.’ ” Ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ɔko Sekelea ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Daala Bosate Ɣaa anyɔ.’ ” Gɔ Ɔbosam ɔro Yesu ɔla ɔnyɔ ne, ɔrui ɔnyua wũ ɔwi kɛkɛĩ.
Yesu Ɔtsɛ Ɔ̃ Karabara I Galilea Karɔ̃ Iso.
Yesu ɔyi ku Siwarã Bielea ɔle fiɛ ɔkpese ɔba Galilea.
Ɔ̃ iyere ɔre i abuiti wamɔ ɔɖuɖu ame.
Ɔte ara i ma Yudase kasarɛkɔ̃ fiɛ ɔbiara ɔle ɔ̃ ara ite.
Masɛ̃ Yesu I Nasaret.
Nnɛgbe kama ne, Yesu ɔkɛlɛ Nasaret ngbegɔ makararã wũ ita i ɔ̃ sibiɛtɛ ame.
Ma Yudase Iwarãyi iso ne, ɔkɛlɛ ma Kasarɛkɔ̃ lɛ kumɛgɔ ɔsɛ ɔɖɔɛ ɔbara.
Ne ɔta ɔya sɔ ɔ̃aka Ɔko Sekelea ne.
Masu Ɣaa Kanyaɖidze Yesaya ɔko matã wũ.
Gɔ ɔbusi ɔko ne, ɔtsɛ ika i ngbegɔ matsɛrɛ sɔ, “Siwarã Bielea si me iso alasɔ Ɣaa ɔsɔla me nnɔĩ sɔ loasu ɔ̃ Itɔ̃me Bielea lokɛlɛgu mawɛrɛba.
Ɔpia me sɔ losɛ loaɣere mayorɛdze sɔ maana iwarã.
Mma anɔ lobiɛ ma wũ mato maanya ara.
Mma mpia i inyɛwe ame ne, ma wũ maana isobuɛ.
Si lotã matsue sɔ Ɣaa ɔwi gɔ ɔ̃aɖi ɔ̃ mare ɔɔɣo.” Ne Yesu ɔkarĩ ɔko ɔsu ɔtã ngɔ nto ɔnyɔ kasarɛkɔ̃ iso fiɛ ɔrui ɔsɛ i karɔ̃ ne.
Maturi ɔɖuɖu ma i kasarɛkɔ̃ mmɔ ɔɖi anɔ mafere wũ iso tuee.
Ne Yesu to ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ɔko Sekelea ame ara wa minɔ loka ngbe ne, nɔme kaɖe gagbe iba i ne ame.” Ɔ̃ atɔ̃me wa ɔɣɛ gu kumɛgɔ i ɔ̃ ɔnyagɛmi to ɔta ɔbara mma nto makã wũ atsue ɣii.
Makarɛ sɔ, “Iiɖe Yosef ɔbi ɔɖe ngbe?” Mmɔ i Yesu to ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Loɣe sɔ mito miapɛ me igbã nɛgbe sa sɔ, ‘Wase, sa so fɔ mɔmɔ.’ Fiɛ loɣe sɔ mito miaɣere me ana sɔ, ‘Ara wa bonɔ sɔ ato abara i Kapernaum ne, bara wã i fɔ aɖe ngbe ana.’ ” Ne Yesu to ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Lobie sɔ loɣere mi gbaã sɔ ne, Ɣaa kanyaɖidze kuwɛ̃ na kuwarɛ i ɔ̃ mɔmɔ aɖe.
Gbaã iɖe sɔ makuɛdze gbodzoo ɔwe i Israel karɔ̃ iso ku ɔwi gɔ i Ɣaa kanyaɖidze Eliya ɔwe fiɛ kado iipɛ akɔ atɛ gu awa akuɔ.
Kukã ɔbo i karɔ̃ ɔɖuɖu iso.
Ɣɛɛ ne, Ɣaa iipia Eliya sɔ ɔsɛ ɔ̃abuai Israel kuɛdze kuwɛ̃ iɖo kuɛdze gɔ i Zerepta ɔmagɛ̃ ame i Sidon karɔ̃ iso.
Ana ne, ɔnyɛ rɛtɛa manyɛse gbodzoo ɔwe i Israel ku ɔwi gɔ i Ɣaa kanyaɖidze Elisa ɔwe.
Ɣɛɛ ma kuwɛ̃ iina isosarɛ iɖo Naeman gɔ lobɔrɛ i Siria karɔ̃ iso ɔnɔwɛ̃.” Gɔ mma mpia i kasarɛkɔ̃ mmɔ ɔnɔ ara wagbe ne, sikpã ɔmɔɛ̃ ma gbaã.
Mata mali Yesu maɖi i ɔmagɛ̃ ame makɛlɛgu kuwaruɛ i kabemi ga iso matsue ɔmagɛ̃ masia kutsueti ku adzuni sɔ maali wũ makpasera si ɔkpi.
Ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔki i ma ndɛ̃ ɔfe ɔrui ɔɣɛ ma.
Yesu Ɔsa Siwarã Lalaa Ɔɖi I Ɔturi Ɔwɛ̃ Ame.
Nnɛmɔ kama ne, Yesu ɔrui ɔkɛlɛ Kapernaum ɔmagɛ̃ ame i Galilea karɔ̃ iso.
Mmɔ ɔte maturi ara ku Iwarãyi iso ne.
Ɔ̃ ara ite ɔbara ma ɔɖuɖu ɣii ala ɔte wã ku ɔle.
I ma Yudase kasarɛkɔ̃ mmɔ ne, ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɔwe gɔ siwarã lalaa si wũ iso.
Ɔsiagu kulu titiiti sɔ, “Ao!
Be aba abara i bo kɔrɛ ngbe Yesu Nasaretse?
Ɔba ɔɔba sɔ aba aawɔra bo?
Nɣe ɔturi gɔ aɖe!
Fɔ nɖe Ɣaa Ɔturi Sekelea ne!” Mmɔ i Yesu ɔsa siwarã dzɛmɔ sɔ, “Lo kutsuɛ!
Bɔrɛ i ɔ̃ ame fe!” Siwarã ɔnyɛdɛ̃ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe, sipuri wũ siwuĩ i karɔ̃ i ma katɔ̃ fiɛ sibɔrɛ i ɔ̃ ame.
Ɣɛɛ ɔ̃ire igbɛ kuiwɛ̃.
Ibara maturi ɔɖuɖu ɣii ne mato makarɛ so sɔ, “Mme itɔ̃me igbã iɖe i ngbe?
Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ba ɔle ɔto ɔtɔ̃me ɔpia siwarã lalaa i maturi ame fiɛ sito sibɔrɛ ana.” Ne ɔso Yesu iso itɔ̃me ɔkã mmɔ abuiti ɔɖuɖu ame.
Yesu Ɔsa Maturi Gbodzoo.
Gɔ Yesu ɔbɔrɛ i ma Yudase kasarɛkɔ̃ mmɔ ne, ɔkɛlɛ Simon iyo.
Ɔ̃ masɔrɔ̃go rɛ ɔto ɔnyɛ, ɔbe ɔtɔ ne ɔso matã Yesu itsue.
Gɔ ɔsɛ ɔ̃aya i ɔ̃ kɔrɛ i ngbegɔ ɔrɛ ne, ɔsa ɔnyɛ siwarã ɔɖi i ɔ̃ ame.
Ɔluwɛ̃ ɔsarɛ ɔta ɔwa aɖera ɔtã ma.
Ito ikɛlɛ iɣɛ̃kɛlɛ ne, maturi ɔkɔ ma manyii ma nto manyɛ sinyɛ agbãagbã mabɔ Yesu.
Ɔsu nrɔɔ̃ ɔɔsia ma iso ɔwɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɔsa ma ɔɖuɖu.
Siwarã lalaa agbãagbã ana ɔbɔrɛ i maturi ame sito kulu sɔ, “Fɔ nɖe Ɣaa ɔbi ne!” Ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔsɛ̃ ɔtã sɛ̃ ɔ̃itã siɖe ika, alasɔ siɣe sɔ ɔ̃ nɖe Kristo.
Yesu Ɔwe Ɔte Ara I Ma Yudase Kusarɛkɔ̃.
Gɔ kaɖe ɔsɛ̃ ne, Yesu ɔbɔrɛ i ɔmagɛ̃ ame ɔkɛlɛ kawɛrɛkɔ̃, ne ɔso maturi ɔtsɛ wũ inyɔnyɔ.
Gɔ manya wũ ne, maibie sɔ ɔkpese ɔrui i ma kɔrɛ.
Ɣɛɛ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ikote sɔ loaɣɛ Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ itɔ̃me nɛgbe i simagɛ̃ tsɔra ame alasɔ ngbɔ i Ɣaa ɔpia me sɔ lobara ne.” Ne ɔso ɔɣɛ Itɔ̃me Bielea i ma Yudase kusarɛkɔ̃ i karɔ̃ ɔɖuɖu iso.
Yesu Ɔkpere Ɔ̃ Marasuãdze Ɖeakatɔ̃.
Iyi iwɛ̃ ne, Yesu ɣɛ i Genezaret ɔpo kanya ɔto ɔɣɛ Ɣaa itɔ̃me.
Maturi to malili so sɔ maabore mabo wũ manɔ itɔ̃me nɛ ɔto ɔɣɛ.
Ɔnya sɔ sikolo inyɔ ɣɛ i ɔpo kanya mmɔ gɔ akpɛ maɖidze ɔɔso mabɔrɛ mato mafore ma asabu.
Ne Yesu ɔya ɔbo i ɔkolo ɔwɛ̃ gɔ nɖe Simon ɔre ame ɔɣere wũ sɔ ɔli ɔ̃asia i ndu iso kɛkɛĩ.
Ne ka ɔsɛ i ɔkolo ame ɔte ara ne.
Gɔ ɔte ma ara ɔro ne, Yesu ɔɣere Simon sɔ, “Miwa ɔkolo mikɛlɛgu ngbegɔ ndu ɔwodoro kɛkɛĩ si minabarã mi asabu miɖi akpɛ.” Ne Simon ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Bokɔse, kasɛ̃ ɔɖuɖu bobara karabara ku anɔ rɛtɛa boiɖi kuira.
Ɣɛɛ ne, lɛ kumɛgɔ aɣɛ ɔso ne, loatã boapia asabu.” Gɔ mapia asabu ne, mamɔɛ̃ akpɛ asi gɔ ma asabu ɔtsɛ ikɛkɛ.
Ne ɔso ne, makpere ma malaa i ɔkolo nyɔare ame sɔ maba maabuai ma.
Maɖi akpɛ mafere i sikolo sɛ̃ inyɔ ame ayi gbegbeegbe gɔ ikuti kɛkɛĩ fiɛ sikolo aatsɛ ndu iwã.
Gɔ Simon Petro ɔnya nnɛ loba ne, ɔpɛ agɛgɛ̃ i Yesu katɔ̃ ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Bosate, re me kama alasɔ kpibaradze loɖe.” Akpɛ gbodzoo wa maɖi ngbe ɔtã sɔ ibara ma ɣii.
Ngbɔ ame ibara Simon malaa Yakobo gu Yohanes ma nɖe Zebedeo mabi ana ɣii ne.
Mmɔ i Yesu ɔɣere Simon sɔ, “Daanigã.
Ita i kiniɔ ne, maturi ka aaɖi atã Ɣaa.” Ne kama ne, gɔ makpadzɛ̃ sikolo mabɔ i ɔkpokpo ne, manyua ira biara masɛ marui masiai Yesu.
Yesu Ɔsa Ɔrɛrɛ̃ Ɔwɛ̃ Gɔ Nto Ɔnyɛ Ɔnyɛ Rɛtɛa.
Ɔwi ɔwɛ̃ ne, Yesu ɔsɛ ɔmagɛ̃ gɔ ame i ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ nto ɔnyɛ ɔnyɛrɛtɛa pia.
Gɔ ɔnya Yesu ne, ɔpɛ agɛgɛ̃ i ɔ̃ katɔ̃ ɔtã wũ iti sɔ, “Bosate, si aɖɔɛ ne, aawo me ɔsa lose sekelee.” Yesu ɔɖi kɔrɔ̃ ɔpɛgu wũ, ne ɔɣere ɔrɛrɛ̃ sɔ, “Loɖɔɛ, se sekelee.” Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, ɔna isosarɛ.
Yesu ɔsɛ̃ ɔtã wũ sɔ, “Daaɣere kuwɛ̃ nnɛ loba.
Ɣɛɛ kɛlɛ aasu so te Ɣaa sɔrɛdze si atã ara wa i Mose mmara ɔkarɛ si ite ɔbiara sɔ ɔɔsarɛ.” Ɣɛɛ Yesu iso itɔ̃me ɔki ikã i kakɔi biara ibua.
Maturi gbodzoo ɔba maakã ɔ̃ ara ite atsue fiɛ ɔsa ma.
Ɣɛɛ ɔsɛ ɔrui ɔkɛlɛ kawɛrɛkɔ̃ ngbegɔ i kuwɛ̃ na ɔsɛ ɔ̃akparama kayi.
Yesu Ɔsa Ɔrɛrɛ̃ Gɔ Lokpi Kasɛkasɛ.
Iyi iwɛ̃ gɔ Yesu to ɔte ara ne, ma Yudase ikuri nɛ marɔ sɔ ma Farisise gu Mose mmara matedze mawɛ̃ ɔbɔrɛ i Galilea simagɛ̃ ɔɖuɖu gu Yudea karɔ̃ iso gu Yerusalem maba masi i mmɔ.
Ɣaa ɔle gɔ i Yesu to ɔsa ala sinyɛ ana pia i ɔ̃ ame.
Marɛrɛ̃ mawɛ̃ ɔsore ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ lofɛfɛ̃ ɔrɛ i ɔkala iso mabɔ wũ.
Mabie ɔri gɔ iso maaki fiɛ maabogu wũ i iyo ame i Yesu katɔ̃.
Ɣɛɛ kumɛgɔ i maturi ɔsi ɔso ne, maiɣe ɔri gɔ iso maaki.
Ne ɔso masore wũ maya isã.
Gɔ makpa isã ne, masora wũ ku ɔkala gɔ iso ɔrɛ masɛ i Yesu katɔ̃ i iyo nɛ ame mapia.
Gɔ Yesu ɔnya ma kafɔkaɖe ne, ɔɣere ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔmɔ sɔ, “Wũ ɔnyii, losu fɔ akpi lotsɛ-ɔ!” Ne ma Farisise gu mmara matedze ɔbu i ma situ ame sɔ, “Be ɔso i ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe to ɔɣɛ amusuora ngbɔ?
Ɣaa ɔnɔwɛ̃ pɛ loawo ɔturi akpi ɔsu ɔtsɛ wũ!” Gɔ Yesu ɔtsue ma adzuni ne, ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Be ɔso fiɛ mito misusu ara wagbe igbã i mi situ ame?
Be iɣɛ nse pɔkɔsɔɔ iɖo, ‘Losu fɔ akpi lotsɛ-ɔ’ ɛɛbɛrɛ ‘Ta ya si asɛ’?
Loaɖi lote mi sɔ mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, ba ɔle i kayi gagbe iso sɔ loasu akpi lotsɛ.” Ne ɔso ɔfiniki ɔɣere ngɔ lokpi kasɛkasɛ sɔ, “Nto loɣere-ɔ sɔ ta ya si asu fɔ ɔkala si akɛlɛ iyo!” Ɔluwɛ̃ i ma ɔɖuɖu anɔmi ame ne, ɔta ɔya ɔsu ɔ̃ ɔkala gɔ iso ɔrɛ ɔrui ɔɣo iyo ɔri ɔto ɔle Ɣaa.
Ibara maturi ɔɖuɖu ɣii.
Kumɛgɔ ifɔ̃ ɔmɔɛ̃ ma ɔso ne, matsɛ Ɣaa ile ikarɛ so sɔ, “Mme awawãra boto bonya i ngbe nɔme?” Yesu Ɔkpere Levi.
Nnɛmɔ kama gɔ Yesu ɔbɔrɛ i mmɔ ne, ɔnya lampofɔdze ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Levi gɔ ɔsi i ɔ̃ karabara ame.
Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ta siai me.” Levi ɔta ɔsiai wũ ɔnyua ira biara ɔsɛ.
Levi ɔtã mawa aɖera ɔtu ɔpɔrɔ̃ siare i ɔ̃ iyo ɔtã Yesu.
Maturi gbodzoo gu ma lampofɔdze ana pia i mma ɔkpere ɔbɔ mmɔ ame.
Ma Farisise gu mmara matedze ma mpia i mmɔ ɔtsɛ kawararã ku Yesu masiaidze sɔ, “Be ɔso mito miɖe minɛ ku lampo mafɔdze gu makpibaradze?” Ne Yesu to ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Mma nsarɛ iisɛ mabie kuwabaradze, manyɛse nsɛ mabie.
Iiɖe maturi ma nse bɔlɔlɔ loba lokpere sɔ mafiniki ɣɛɛ makpibaradze.” Yesu Ɔɖe Ika I Ɣaa Ɔri Ɣɛtɛ Iso.
Maturi mawɛ̃ ɔkarɛ Yesu sɔ, “Be ɔso fiɛ Yohanes masiaidze sɛ manyi kanya makparama kayi, ma Farisise masiaidze ma wũ ngbɔ ame ne, ɣɛɛ fɔ mare ma ne, ɔɖe gu ɔnɛ ko mato?” Ne Yesu ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Mifɔ miɖe sɔ ɔrɔ̃go kɔdze malaa aasɛ kukã gɔ ɔrɔ̃go kɔdze pia i ma kɔrɛ?
Ooɣo!
Iibakote ngbɔ!
Ɣɛɛ ne, iyi iwɛ̃ to iba gɔ maakɔ ɔrɔ̃go kɔdze maruigu i ma kɔrɛ.
Mmɔ ne, iisiɖe kuwɛ̃ loaɣere ma sɔ manyi kanya.” Nnɛgbe kama ne, Yesu ɔledza ma igbã ipɛ sɔ, “Kuwɛ̃ iisɛ ɔkɛ ɔkati ɣɛtɛ kasɛi ɔta ɔkuere iyoi.
Si ɔbara ngbɔ ne, iibakote, ɔ̃ɔkɛ ɔkati ɣɛtɛ siefe.
Ngbɔ ame maisɛ masu ndã ɣɛtɛ mafere i bɔi ɔko akpo kuere ame ne.
Si iba ngbɔ ne, ndã ɣɛtɛ to miafu mitã sɔ akpo kuere aabiɛ itã ndã ɔwiri.
Ɣɛɛ ndã ɣɛtɛ ne, sikomi akpo ɣɛtɛ ame masɛ mafere me.
Ngbɔ ame ana si ɔturi ɔɔnɛ ndã kuere ka ɔto ɔrɛ̃ ne, ɔ̃isisɛ ɔbie miɣɛtɛ.
Ɔsɛ ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Mikuere lɛ miɖo miɣɛtɛ!’ ”
Yesu Gu Ma Farisise Ɔkpadzɛ̃ So I Iwarãyi Iso.
Iwarãyi iwɛ̃ gɔ Yesu sɛ ɔto ɔfe i kakpɛkɔ̃ kawɛ̃ ame gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ne, marasuãdze ɔtsɛ atita ibɛbɛse iɣɛrɛ iwe.
Mmɔ i ma Farisise mawɛ̃ to makarɛ ma sɔ, “Be ɔso mito mibara nnɛ i mmara iitã ɔri sɔ maabara ku Iwarãyi?” Ne Yesu ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Miika i Ɔko Sekelea ame nnɛ i David ɔbara ɔwi gɔ i kukã ɔkpɛ̃ wũ gu ɔ̃ maturi?
Ɔbo i Ɣaa iyo ame ɔsɛ ɔ̃asu aɖera wa masu masɔrɛ Ɣaa ɔɖe ɔkuti ɔtã ɔ̃ masiaidze ɔɖe gɔ mmara iitã ɔri iɖo Ɣaa masɔrɛdze ɔnɔwɛ̃.” Kawirikɔ̃ ne, Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi nɖe Iwarãyi Sate.” Yesu Ɔsa Ɔrɛrɛ̃ Gɔ Kɔrɔ̃ Lokarĩ Iwarãyi mama ne, Yesu ɔsɛ ma Yudase kasarɛkɔ̃ ɔsɛ ɔ̃ate ara.
Ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ kuɖearɔ̃ lokarĩ ɔwe i mmɔ.
Ne gɔ mmara matedze gu ma Farisise mawɛ̃ to mabie ɔri gɔ iso maaki fiɛ maaɖaɛ Yesu kanya sɔ ɔɣɛrɛ ma mmara ɔso ne, makarã anɔ sɔ maanya si ɔ̃asa sinyɛ i Iwarãyi iso.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ Yesu ɣe ma adzuni ɔso ne, ɔɣere ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ kɔrɔ̃ lokarĩ sɔ ɔta ɔya i ma katɔ̃.
Ne ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔmɔ ɔta ɔba ɔ̃aya i katɔ̃ ne.
Ne Yesu to ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Be i mmara ɔte?
Sɔ ɔturi aabara isɛɛ ɛɛbɛrɛ ilalaa ku Iwarãyi?
Ilɛ sɔ aabuai ɔturi ɛɛbɛrɛ aanina ɔ̃ ngbã?” Yesu ɔla anɔ i ma ɔɖuɖu iso ɔɣere ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔmɔ sɔ, “Nabarã fɔ kɔrɔ̃.” Ɔnabarã kɔ̃, ɔluwɛ̃ ne, kɔrɔ̃ ko lolɛ wũ.
Sikpã ɔmɔɛ̃ ma ɔɖuɖu ne ɔso matsɛ adzuni imɔɛ̃ i nnɛ maabara Yesu iso.
Yesu Ɔɖi Katɔ̃memasɛdze Iweo-inyɔ.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, Yesu ɔkɛlɛ kabemi kawɛ̃ iso ɔsɛ ɔ̃akparama kayi kasɛ̃ ɔɖuɖu.
Gɔ kaɖe ɔsɛ̃ ne, ɔkpere ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔsirakanya i ɔ̃ kɔrɛ, ne ɔɖi ma iweo-inyɔ ɔtã ma iyere sɔ ɔ̃ katɔ̃memasɛdze ne.
Ma nɖe Simon gɔ ɔtã iyere sɔ Petro gu ɔ̃ ɔnyiibi Andrea gu Yakobo gu Yohanes gu Filipo gu Bartolomeo gu Mateo gu Toma gu Alfeo ɔbi Yakobo gu Simon gɔ masɛ marɔ sɔ, “Ɔturi gɔ lokpɛ̃ i ɔ̃ kaɖe iti,” gu Yakobo ɔbi Yuda gu Yuda Iskariot gɔ lokpese ngɔ loaɖi wũ ɔtã.
Yesu Ɔsa Maturi Gbodzoo.
Ɔwi gɔ i Yesu gu ɔ̃ katɔ̃memasɛdze ɔso i kabemi gamɔ iso maba ne, maba maya i katɛfɛkɔ̃ kawɛ̃.
Ɔ̃ masiaidze gbodzoo gu maturi ikuri titiiti nɛ lobɔrɛ i Yudea karɔ̃ ɔɖuɖu iso gu Yerusalem gu simagɛ̃ dzɛ mpia i ɔpo kuruɛ Tiro gu Sidon ɔba maasakanya.
Maba sɔ maanɔ ara wa i Yesu to ɔte fiɛ ɔ̃asa ma sinyɛ agbãagbã dzɛ mato manyɛ.
Mma ana i siwarã lalaa to siɖaa ɔba fiɛ ɔsa ma.
Ɔbiara to ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃apɛgu wũ alasɔ ɔle to ɔbɔrɛ i ɔ̃ ame ɔsa ma ɔɖuɖu.
So To Siaɣɔ Mawɛ̃ Fiɛ Inyɛwe Ana To Iatu Mawɛ̃.
Yesu ɔnyɔ ɔ̃ masiaidze i katɔ̃ ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “So si siɣɔ mi mawɛrɛba alasɔ mi ɔkpɛ nɖe Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃!
So si siɣɔ mi ma i kukã to kiniɔ, alasɔ mito miami!
So si siɣɔ mi ma nto mibiɛ kiniɔ, alasɔ mito miama!
So si siɣɔ mi si maturi ɔtsiri mi fiɛ masɛ̃ mi fiɛ mato matia mi, maɣɛ mi iso ara lalaa ala mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, iti!
“Mina isoɣɔ si nwagbe ɔɖuɖu ɔba ngbɔ, mitɔ i isoɣɔ ame alasɔ Ɣaa to ɔ̃atã mi kuso siare i kato.
Alasɔ ara wagbe igbã i ma mawa ɔbara Ɣaa Kanyamaɖidze ne.
Ɣɛɛ ndzo miɖe mitã mi maranase alasɔ miɔna mi ɔkpɛ i ngbã mɛgbe ame!
Ndzo miɖe mitã mi ma lomi kiniɔ, alasɔ Kukã to kuakpɛ̃ mi Ndzo miɖe mitã mi ma nto mima kiniɔ, alasɔ mito miamararã so mibiɛ nnɔmɛ!
“Ndzo miɖe mitã mi ma i maturi ɔɖuɖu sɛ male kiniɔ.
alasɔ ngbɔ ame i ma mawa ɔla maɔle maladze ma nsɛ maɣɛ sɔ Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze maɖe ne.
Ɖɔɛ Fɔ Matsirise “Ɣɛɛ mi ma nto minɔ me ne, nto loɣere mi sɔ miɖɔɛ mi matsirise si mibara isɛɛ mitã ma.
Mma nsɛ magbarĩ mi ne, mitã ma kusɛkusɛ.
Mma ana nto mabara mi ɔtile ne, mikparama kayi i ma iti.
Si ɔrere ɔpɛ-ɔ ɔrɔ̃ta i kutsueti kuwɛ̃ ne, finikira kunyɔare tã wũ.
Si ɔrere ɔmɔɛ̃ fɔ kato awu wa apia ɔbɛ-ɔ iso ne, ɖi nwa apia asɛ karɔ̃ ana tã wũ.
Ɔturi biara gɔ loakarɛ mi ira ne, mitã wũ.
Si ɔrere ɔmɔɛ̃ nnɛ nɖe fɔ ire ɔsu ne, daati wũ kama sɔ aakpese afɔ.
Kumɛgɔ abie sɔ mabara matã-ɔ ne, fɔ wũ bara ngbɔ tã maturi mama.
“Si maturi ma nsɛ maɖɔɛ-ɔ ɔnɔwɛ̃ asɛ aɖɔɛ ne, be ɔso fiɛ maale-ɔ?
Akpi mabaradze ma wũ masɛ maɖɔɛ mma nsɛ maɖɔɛ ma.
Si maturi ma nsɛ mabara-ɔ isɛɛ ɔnɔwɛ̃ asɛ abara isɛ atã ne, be ɔso maale-ɔ?
Akpi mabaradze ma wũ masɛ mabara ngbɔ.
Si ngɔ loana nnɛ ɔnyɛ i fɔ kɔrɛ ɔtã-ɔ kotoo aanyɛ ira atã ne, be ɔso fiɛ maale-ɔ?
Akpi mabaradze ma wũ masɛ manyɛ ara matã mma loawo ma ɔkpesegu ɔtã.
Ɣɛɛ ne, miɖɔɛ mi matsirise si mibara isɛɛ mitã ma.
Minyɛ ara mitã ma ɣɛɛ midaanyɔ ɔri sɔ maakpesegu mabɔ mi kokooko.
Si mibara ngbɔ ne, mi kuso to kuasi fiɛ maakpere mi sɔ Ɣaa Kato gu Karɔ̃ baradze mabi.
Alasɔ Ɣaa ba kayiribielea ɔtã ta mma nsɛ masu karɔ̃ma mapɛ ala maturi siba gu maturi lalaa.
Minyɔ maturi nnya lɛ kumɛgɔ i mi ɔse Ɣaa sɛ ɔnyɔ nnya.
Yesu Ɔte Ara Ɔsegu I Atɔ̃me Iɣɛgu Fɔ Ɔlaa Iso.
“Midaaɣɛgu maturi atɔ̃me si Ɣaa iibaɣɛgu mi atɔ̃me.
Daatã maturi ipɔ si Ɣaa iibatã-ɔ ipɔ.
Su tsɛ maturi si Ɣaa aasu ɔtsɛ-ɔ.
Mitã maturi ara si Ɣaa ana atã mi ara.
Gbaã ne, kaboũsuai sɛɛ ga loyi pɔpɔɔpɔ, matitidza masɛra kabiɛ kawiri maako ala matã mi.
Kaboũsuai ga igbã ako ala ara atã fɔ ɔlaa ne, kã ame igbã maasu mako matã-ɔ ne.” Mmɔ i Yesu to ɔpɛ ma igbã nɛgbe sɔ, “Si nɔbiɛdze to ɔkɔ nɔbiɛdze ne, iwo ame i ma inyɔɔ aakpase mabo.
Rasuãdze kuwɛ̃ iisɛ ɔɖo ɔ̃ ratedze.
Ɣɛɛ si ɔro ara ɔsuã ne, ɔ̃ase lɛ ɔ̃ ratedze awe.
“Nda ato abara fiɛ ato anya iku nɛ mpia i fɔ ɔlaa inɔmi fiɛ aito abara kuira i idzirikpo nɛ mpia fɔ mɔmɔ inɔmi iso?
Nda aabara fiɛ aaɣere fɔ ɔlaa sɔ, ‘Wũ ɔnyii, tã loɖi-ɔ iku i inɔmi’ ku ɔwi gɔ nnɛ lomɔ iɖo pia i fɔ inɔmi ame?
Ladze!
Ɖi idzirikpo nɛ mpia-ɔ inɔmi tɔtɔ fiɛ aanya kukaakɔ aɖi fɔ ɔnyii iku i inɔmi.” Kudziri Biara Ku Kɔ̃ Abi.
“Kudziri sɛɛ iisɛ kuɣɔ̃ abi nyanyarĩa fiɛ kudziri lalaa ana iibawo abi sɛɛ ɔɣɔ̃.
Kudziri biara ne, kɔ̃ abi aasu anya kɔ̃ aɖi ite.
Kuwɛ̃ iisɛ ɔtɔtɔrɛ figi abi i miyu kudziri iso fiɛ maisɛ matɔtɔrɛ adziribi ɖea i itongbã iso.
Ɔturi sɛɛ ne, ara sɛɛ ɔsɛ ɔɖi ɔbɔrɛgu i ɔ̃ ara kakɔlakɔ̃ ga nɖe ɔ̃ ɔtu ame.
Ɔturi lalaa ɔ̃ wũ ne, ara lalaa ɔsɛ ɔɖi ɔbɔrɛgu i ɔ̃ ɔtu ame.
Alasɔ nnɛ loyi ɔturi ɔtu ame ɔsɛ ɔɖi ɔbɔrɛgu i ɔ̃ kanya ame.
Nɔ Yesu Itɔ̃me Si Abara I Ne Iso.
“Be ɔso fiɛ mito mikpere me sɔ Bosate, Bosate, ɣɛɛ miito mibara ara wa loto loɣere mi iso?
Ɔturi biara gɔ nsɛ ɔba wũ kɔrɛ fiɛ ɔto ɔnɔ ara wa nto lote fiɛ ɔsɛ ɔbara iso ne, loate mi nnɛ i ngɔmɔ ɔre.
Ɔse lɛ ɔturi gɔ si ɔ̃atsue iyo ne, ɔpia ne i karɔ̃ ame ku ata siare kukaakɔ fiɛ ɔtsue kubereku ɔsia iso.
Si ɔwore ɔyi fiɛ ndu ɔbo kabereku gamɔ iso ne, iyo nɛmɔ iibabiɛ alasɔ mapia ne i karɔ̃ ame kukaakɔ.
Ɣɛɛ ɔbiara gɔ nsɛ ɔnɔ wũ itɔ̃me fiɛ ɔ̃isɛ ɔbara i ne iso ne, ɔse lɛ ngɔ lotsue ɔ̃ iyo ɔsia i karɔ̃ kunu iso ɔ̃ipia ne i karɔ̃ ame.
Si ɔwore ɔyi fiɛ ndu ɔbo iyo nɛmɔ iso ne, iabiɛ ifu i karɔ̃ pelepele!”
Yesu Ɔsa Ɔ Romase Kpakpɛ̃dzekpakpa Ɔwɛ̃ Ɔɖabo.
Gɔ Yesu ɔɔro ma nwagbe ɔɖuɖu ɔɣere ne, ɔrui ɔkɛlɛ Kapernaum.
Roma kpakpɛ̃dzekpakpa ɔwɛ̃ i mmɔ ba ɔɖabo gɔ ɔbua ɔsɛ ɔɖɔɛ gbaã.
Ɔɖabo gɔgbe ɔmɔɛ̃ ɔnyɛ gɔ ɔ̃ɔro ɔkpi.
Gɔ ɔkpakpa gɔgbe ɔnɔ Yesu iyere ne, ɔpia ma Yudase makpakpa mawɛ̃ sɔ makpere Yesu matã wũ si ɔba ɔ̃asa ɔ̃ ɔɖabo ɔtã wũ.
Maba maatã wũ iti teteree sɔ, “Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ɔkote ɔtã sɔ aabuai, alasɔ ɔsɛ ɔɖɔɛ bo aɖe kaɖe.
Ɔ̃ mɔmɔ lotsue bo kasarɛkɔ̃ ɔtã bo.” Ne ɔso Yesu ɔta ɔsiai ma.
Gɔ iɔkuti kɛkɛĩ fiɛ ɔ̃abo iyo mmɔ ne, ɔkpakpa gɔgbe ɔpia ɔ̃ malaa sɔ masɛ maaɣere wũ sɔ, “Tete, loito lobie sɔ loaɖa-ɔ.
Loikote sɔ aaba wũ iyo.
Loikote ana sɔ loaba fɔ katɔ̃.
Ne ɔso ɣɛ itɔ̃me sese kere si wũ ɔɖabo si ɔna isosarɛ.
Mme wũ ɔkpakpa loɖe i makpakpa mama kayirinɔ.
Loba makpakpɛ̃dze mama i wũ kayirinɔ.
Nsɛ loɣere ngɔ sɔ, ‘Kɛlɛ ngbe’ ɔkɛlɛ, fiɛ nsɛ loɣere ɔmama ana sɔ, ‘Ba ngbe’ ɔba.
Nsɛ loɣere wũ ɔɖabo sɔ, ‘Bara lɛ ngbe’ ɔbara.” Gɔ Yesu ɔnɔ atɔ̃me wagbe ne, ibara wũ ɣaa.
Mmɔ ɔto ɔfiniki ɔɣere mma nsiai wũ sɔ, “Nto loɣere mi sɔ loinya kafɔkaɖe siare gagbe igbã lonya i Israel karɔ̃ ɔɖuɖu iso!” Maturi ma lokpese makɛlɛ kpakpɛ̃dze ɔkpakpa gɔgbe iyo mmɔ ɔnya sɔ ɔ̃ ɔɖabo ɔɔsarɛ.
Yesu Ɔtara Kuɛdze Ɔwɛ̃ Ɔbi Gɔ Lokpi.
Nnɛmɔ kama ne, Yesu ɔkɛlɛ ɔmagɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Nain ame gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze gu maturi gbodzoo ma nsiai wũ.
Gɔ mabo kabenya ne, masarɛgu maturi ma nsore kpise maabiara.
Ngɔ lokpi ne, kuɛdze ɔwɛ̃ ɔbi ɔwɛ̃ saã gɔ ɔɣe ɔɖe.
Ne ɔso maturi gbodzoo ɔbɔrɛ i kaɖe ame maki malɔ kuɛdze gɔgbe.
Gɔ Bosate ɔnya ɔrɔ̃go ne, ɔ̃ ara ɔɖo wũ kayiri.
Ne ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Lo kaku.” Yesu ɔbo i maturi ndɛ̃ ɔsɛ ɔ̃apɛgu nnɛ iso masore kpise.
Gɔ mma nsore ɔtui ne, ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Ɔporoporoi!
Mme sɔ ta!” Ɔluwɛ̃ kpise ɔkpɛ̃ ɔta ɔsɛ ɔtsɛ ika iɖe.
Ne Yesu ɔtara wũ ɔtã ɔ̃ ɔnyi ne.
Ifɔ̃ ɔmɔɛ̃ maturi ɔɖuɖu gbaã ne matsɛ Ɣaa ile iɣɛ sɔ, “Ɣaa kanyaɖidze siare ɔɔba i bo ndɛ̃.
Ɣaa ɔɔba sɔ ɔ̃aba ɔ̃aɖi ɔ̃ mare!” Yesu ira nɛ ɔbara ngbe ɔki ikã Yudea karɔ̃ gu abuiti ɔɖuɖu iso.
Ndupiedze Yohanes Ɔpia Ɔ̃ Marasuãdze Yesu Kɔrɛ.
Gɔ Yohanes marasuãdze ɔɣere wũ ara wagbe ɔɖuɖu ne, ɔkpere ma inyɔ.
Ɔpia ma Bosate kɔrɛ sɔ masɛ maakarɛ wũ sɔ, “Fɔ nɖe ngɔ maɣɛ sɔ ɔ̃aba ɛɛbɛrɛ bonyɔ ɔmama ɔri?” Gɔ maba Yesu kɔrɛ ne, maɣere wũ sɔ, “Ndupiedze Yohanes lopia bo sɔ bo karɛ-ɔ sɔ, ‘Fɔ nɖe ngɔ maɣɛ sɔ ɔ̃aba ɛɛbɛrɛ bonyɔ ɔmama ɔri?’ ” Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, Bosate ɔɔsa maturi gbodzoo sinyɛ, ɔsa siwarã lalaa, ɔtã sɔ manɔbiɛdze gbodzoo ana to manya ara.
Ne ɔɣere mma mapia katɔ̃me sɔ, “Mikpese miaɣere Yohanes ara wa minya gu nwa minɔ.
Manɔbiɛdze to manya, mabafã to masɛ, mma nto manyɛ ɔnyɛ rɛtɛa iso to isekele, matsuetɛ̃se to manɔ, makpise to mata fiɛ mato maɣere mawɛrɛba ana Itɔ̃me Bielea.
So aaɣɔ mma i wũ kurabarara iita kuya iso.” Gɔ Yohanes marasuãdze ɔɔrui kama ne, Yesu ɔtsɛ ika iɖe i ɔ̃ iso iɣere mma losakanya mmɔ sɔ, “Ɔwi gɔ mibɔrɛ mikɛlɛ Yohanes kɔrɛ i fafuĩ ame ne, be iɖe minyɔ ɔri sɔ mianya?
Iyata nɛ i ɔwiri to ɔtidza?
Be mibɔrɛ misɛ mianyɔ?
Ngɔ mpia ɔgo awu?
Mma mpia ɔgo awu fiɛ mato maɖe isoɣɔ ne, magara ayo masɛ mawe.
Mibua miɣere me nnɛ misɛ mianyɔ!
Ɣaa kanyaɖidze?
Gbaã nto loɣere mi sɔ ɔɖo Ɣaa kanyaɖidze.
Alasɔ ɔ̃ iso i Ɔko Sekelea ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Loasese kpabo ɔɖe-ɔ katɔ̃, sɔ ɔ̃aledza maturi ɔtã fɔ iba.’ ” Yesu ɔledza ma iɣere ana sɔ, “Yohanes ɔɖo ɔturi igbã biara gɔ maɣe i kayi gagbe ame.
Ɣɛɛ ngɔ lokoso ɔɖo i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ɔɖo wũ.” Tɔtɔ ne, maturi ɔɖuɖu ɔɔnɔ itɔ̃me nɛ i Yohanes ɔɣɛ titirio ma lampofɔdze ma lobara Ɣaa kuɖɔɛ fiɛ mafɔ Ɣaa itupie kubarara i ɔ̃ kɔrɛ.
Ɣɛɛ ma Farisise gu Mose mmara matedze ɔsɛ̃ ara wa nɖe Ɣaa kuɖɔɛ kutã ma fiɛ maibie sɔ ɔpie ma ndu.
“Kiniɔ ne, mabe loasu nɔme maturi lokateragu?
Nda mase?
Mase lɛ mabiɛtɛ ma nto maɣa kaɣa i kuɣa ame.
Mawɛ̃ to maɣere ma malaa sɔ, ‘Boka isoɣɔ aka botã mi, miitɔ!
Boɖi sikubiɛnɔ ana botã mi, miibiɛ kaku.’ Gɔ Ndupiedze Yohanes ɔba ɔ̃ito ɔɖe ara ɔnɛ ndã mɛ loamɔɛ̃ ne, miɣɛ sɔ, ‘Siwarã lalaa mpia i ɔ̃ ame!’ Mme Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi gɔ loba fiɛ loto loɖe ara lonɛ ndã ne, mi sɔ, ‘Minyɔ ɖeɖei gu tarɛ̃dze gɔgbe!
Ma lampofɔdze gu makpibaradze ɔlaa ɔɖe!’ Ɣɛɛ Ɣaa iwola sɛ ite so i ɔturi nsɛgbai ame.” Yesu Ɔsɛ Farisise Simon Iyo.
Ɔ Farisise ɔwɛ̃ ɔkpere Yesu sɔ ɔba ɔ̃aɖe aɖera i ɔ̃ iyo, ne ɔsɛ ɔ̃asɛ ɔtsɛ araɖea iɖe ne.
Ɔrɔ̃go ɔwɛ̃ pia i ɔmagɛ̃ gɔmɔ ame gɔ nsi ngbã nyanyarĩa.
Gɔ ɔnɔ sɔ Yesu to ɔɖe ara i ɔ Farisise gɔmɔ iyo ne, ɔsu nnɔĩ miwɛ̃ mɛ nsɛ mifɔrɛ̃ kɔrɔ̃kɔrɔ̃ fiɛ me ibui ɔnyɔ sɔlɔsɔlɔ ɔbɔ mmɔ.
Ɔba ɔ̃aya i Yesu kama ɔto ɔbiɛ nnɔmɛ ɔfere i ɔ̃ ngba iso.
Ɔrɔ̃go gɔgbe ɔsu ɔ̃ iti siwɛrɛ̃ ɔnyɛnyɛdɛ̃ Yesu ngba, ɔfiɔfiɔ̃ me fiɛ ka ɔsu nnɔĩ kɔrɔ̃kɔrɔ̃a mɛmɔ ɔfere wũ i ngba ana.
Gɔ Farisise gɔ lokpere Yesu ɔnya ira nɛgbe ne, ɔɣɛ i ɔ̃ iti ame sɔ, “Si ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ne Ɣaa kanyaɖidze ɔɖe ne, tee ɔ̃atsue ɔturi gɔ igbã i ɔrɔ̃go gɔ nto ɔpɛpɛgu wũ ngbe ɖe gu ngbã nyanyarĩa mɛ igbã ɔsi!” Ne Yesu ɔfɔ kanya ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Simon, lobie sɔ loaɣere-ɔ ira iwɛ̃.” Ne Simon ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ratedze, ɣɛ nnɛ aba.” Ne Yesu ɔsɛ karɔ̃ ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Maturi inyɔ mawɛ̃ ɔla ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ kuso.
Ɔwɛ̃ to wũ lɛ kuwa kuwɛ̃ kuso.
Ɔnyɔare to wũ lɛ awa aweo kuso.
Ma inyɔ magbe kuwɛ̃ iiwo wũ kuso ɔtã.
Ne ɔso ɔsu kuso gɔ mato wũ ɔɖuɖu ɔtsɛ ma.
Maturi inyɔ magbe ndɛ̃ ne, nna loaɖɔɛ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ɔɖo?” Ne Simon ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Lofɔ loɖe sɔ ngɔ masu kuso siare matsɛ.” Mmɔ i Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Aɣɛ kukaakɔ.” Yesu ɔfiniki ɔnyɔ ɔrɔ̃go gɔgbe, ne ɔɣere Simon sɔ, “Ato anya ɔrɔ̃go gɔgbe?
Gɔ loba fɔ iyo ne, aitã me ndu sɔ lofore ngba.
Ɣɛɛ ɔrɔ̃go gɔgbe ɔsu ɔ̃ nnɔmɛ ɔfore me ngba fiɛ ɔsu ɔ̃ iti siwɛrɛ̃ ɔnukutu me.
Gɔ loba fɔ iyo ne, aipɔrɛ me apia me isoɣɔ.
Ɣɛɛ ita i ɔwi gɔ lobo i fɔ iyo ne, ɔrɔ̃go gɔgbe iinyua wũ ngba ɔsɔla.
Aitã me nnɔĩ sɔ lopia i iti.
Ɣɛɛ ɔ̃ ɔsu nnɔĩ kɔrɔ̃kɔrɔ̃a ɔfere me ngba ɔɖuɖu.
Ne ɔso nto loɣere-ɔ sɔ ne, ɔ̃ kuɖɔɛ gɔ ɔɖi ɔte me ɔso ne, ɔna ɔ̃ akpi gbodzoo wa ɔbara isu itsɛ.
