Ɔturi gɔ masu akpi kɛkɛĩ matsɛ ne, ɔ̃ kuɖɔɛ ana ne, kɛkɛĩ kere kuse.” Mmɔ i Yesu to ɔɣere ɔrɔ̃go gɔmɔ sɔ, “Ɔɔna fɔ akpi isu itsɛ.” Gɔ mma nsi i ɔpɔrɔ̃ katɔ̃ gu Yesu ɔnɔ ara wa ɔɣɛ ne, makarɛ so sɔ, “Nna ɔɖe ngbe fiɛ ɔto ɔwo maturi akpi ɔsu ɔtsɛ ma?” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ɔrɔ̃go gɔmɔ sɔ, “Fɔ kafɔkaɖe ɔɖi-ɔ ne ɔso kɛlɛ i isobuɛ ame.”
Marɔ̃go Mawɛ̃ Ma Losiai Yesu Kama.
Ɔwi kama ne, Yesu ɔki i simagɛ̃ gu ngorowase wiriwiria ame ɔɣɛ Itɔ̃me Bielea i sigarakaɖekɔ̃ iso.
Ɔ̃ marasuãdze iweo-inyɔ ana siai wũ.
Marɔ̃go mawɛ̃ ma i Yesu ɔsa sinyɛ agbãagbã gu mma ame ɔsa siwarã lalaa ɔɖi ana ɔsiai wũ.
Ma ndɛ̃ mawɛ̃ nɖe Maria gɔ masɛ marɔ Magdalase, ngɔ ame i Yesu ɔsa siwarã lalaa aka akɔdzɛ ɔɖi.
Ɔwɛ̃ ana nɖe Yohana gɔ ɔrã marɔ Kusa gɔ nsɛ ɔbara karabara i Igara Herodes atɔ̃mekaɣɛkɔ̃ lɛ ɔkpakpa awe.
Ɔmama ana nɖe Susana gu mamama gbodzoo ma losiai Yesu masu ma karana mabuai wũ gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze.
Yesu Ɔpɛ Igbã I Ɔraɖuisadze Ɔwɛ̃ Iso.
Maturi gbodzoo to mabɔrɛ i simagɛ̃ agbãagbã ame maba Yesu kɔrɛ.
Gɔ maba maasakanya ne, Yesu ɔpɛ ma igbã nɛgbe sɔ, “Kpɛ̃dze ɔwɛ̃ ɔsɛ ɔraɖui kasakɔ̃.
Gɔ ɔto ɔsa ne, ɔwɛ̃ ɔfere i ɔri iso maturi ɔsɛ iso ne kurodzai ɔrɛrɛ kuɖe ne.
Ɔwɛ̃ ana ɔɣo i ata iso ɣɛɛ gɔ ɔre kere ne, ɔ̃ ɔɖuɖu ɔkpi alasɔ ɔ̃ siɖu iibo karɔ̃.
Ɔraɖui ɔwɛ̃ ana ɔbo i kuposɛ̃ ndɛ̃, ne ɔso gɔ ɔre ne, kuɣa kufu wũ iso, ne ɔso ɔkpi pelepele.
Ɣɛɛ ɔwɛ̃ ana ɔɣo i karɔ̃ sɛɛ iso.
Gɔ ɔre ne, ɔɣɔ̃ abi, ɔwɛ̃ abi kulafa kulafa.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ngɔ mba atsue si ɔnɔ nnɛ nto loɣɛ!” Nnɛ Ɔso I Yesu Ɔte Ara I Agbã Ame.
Yesu marasuãdze ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ ɔɖi igbã nɛgbe karɔ̃ ɔtã ma.
Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ɣaa ɔɖi ɔ̃ sigarakaɖekɔ̃ awɛrɛra karɔ̃ ɔte mi.
Ɣɛɛ maturi mama ne, agbã ame maanɔ sɔ, ‘si mato manya ne, maibatsue.
fiɛ si mato manɔ ne, maibanɔ karɔ̃.’ Yesu Ɔɖi Ɔraɖuisadze Igbã Karɔ̃.
“Igbã nɛ lopɛ karɔ̃ ngbe ne.
Ɔraɖui gɔ mato masa nɖe Ɣaa itɔ̃me.
Ɔraɖui gɔ loɣo i ɔri kuruɛ se lɛ maturi ma nsɛ manɔ itɔ̃me fiɛ Ɔbosam sɛ ɔba ɔ̃amɔɛ̃ ne ɔɖi i ma situ ame.
Isɛ itã sɔ maibawo ɔfɔ ɔɖe fiɛ maana iɖi.
Ngɔ ana loɣo i ita iso ne, ɔse lɛ maturi ma lonɔ itɔ̃me fiɛ mafɔ ne ku isoɣɔ ɔluwɛ̃, ɣɛɛ iibo i ma ame wodoroo.
Ne ɔso ma kafɔkaɖe ɔwi se kurukutu gɔ si ita iya iso ɔba ma iso ne, masɛ mafɛ̃.
Ngɔ ana loɣo i kuposɛ̃ ame ne, ɔse lɛ maturi ma lonɔ itɔ̃me ɣɛɛ kayiiso imararã gu karana gu ngbã iɖe sɛ iɣa ifu ma sɔ maisɛ mawo iti ɔre fiɛ maaɣɔ̃ abi abe.
Ɔraɖui gɔ loɣo i karɔ̃ sɛɛ iso ɔ̃ wũ ne, ɔse lɛ maturi ma lonɔ itɔ̃me fiɛ imɔɛ̃ ma ɔtu gbaã gu karɔ̃ ibɔso.
Maya teteree gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ isɛ iabo kawirikɔ̃ maɣɔ̃ abi gbodzoo.
Tã Sɔ Ɔkaniɛ Si Ɔfiɛ Ɔtã Maturi.
“Kuwɛ̃ iisɛ ɔtsue ɔkaniɛ ɔsu ɔkɔla i kabui ame ɣee ɔsu ɔɣedza i karɛkɔ̃ kayirinɔ.
Ɣɛɛ ɔ̃atara wũ ɔsia i ira kɔlɛa iso sɔ si ɔ̃asa ɔfere i kakɔi biara sɔ si ɔturi biara ɔbo iyo ne, ɔ̃anya kame sekelee.
Ira biara nɛ makɔla i kakɔi biara ne, mato maaɖi ne mabɔ i ɔgbami.
Ira biara nɛ mafu ara ne, mato maaɖi ne mabɔ ikpawaĩ ame.
“Midzuɛ̃ so i kumɛgɔ miakã atsue alasɔ ngɔ mba ara ne, maatã wũ mabua, ɣɛɛ ngɔ mba ara kɛkɛĩ ne, kɛkɛĩ gɔ ame ɔbu sɔ ɔba ne, maamɔɛ̃ mafɔ wũ iso.” Nna Nɖe Yesu Ɔnyi Gu Ɔ̃ Manyiibi?
Yesu ɔnyi gu ɔ̃ manyiibi ɔba ɔ̃ kɔrɛ, ɣɛɛ maiwo Yesu ɔnya ala kumɛgɔ i maturi ɔmini wũ ɔso.
Ɔwɛ̃ ɔba ɔ̃aɣere Yesu sɔ, “Fɔ ɔnyi gu manyiibi ɣɛ i inyamɔ mato mabie-ɔ.” Ne Yesu to ɔɣere ma ɔɖuɖu sɔ, “Wũ ɔnyi gu wũ manyiibi nɖe mma nsɛ manɔ Ɣaa itɔ̃me fiɛ masɛ mabara i ne iso.” Yesu Ɔtindza Awɛ.
Iyi iwɛ̃ ne, Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔbo i ɔkolo ame.
Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mitã bowara ibu bokɛlɛ ɔkpokpo gɔmɔ isɛ.” Ne ɔso mabo i ɔkolo ame marui.
Gɔ masia ndu iso kɛkɛĩ kere ne, sirɛ ɔsu Yesu.
Ɔluwɛ̃ awɛ ɔtsɛ ikpɛ̃ teteree gɔ mma ɔɖuɖu mpia i ɔkolo ame ngbã ɔwe i imɔrɛ̃ ame ala ndu ɔtsɛ ɔkolo ame ibo.
Marasuãdze ɔbore mabo wũ maatara wũ sɔ, “Tete!
Ɔkpi boto lo!” Mmɔ i Yesu ɔta ɔya ɔtɔ̃me ɔpia ɔwiri gu ndu mɛ nto miɖa so.
Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, ira biara ko lolo kananana.
Ne ɔto ɔkarɛ marasuãdze sɔ, “Be iɖe ɔso fiɛ mina kafɔkaɖe?” Ɣɛɛ ifɔ̃ ɔmɔɛ̃ ma ibara ma ɣii ne mato makarɛ so sɔ, “Mme ɔturi igbã ɔɖe ngbe?
Ɔto ɔɖegu ɔwiri gu ndu ika makã wũ atsue!” Yesu Ɔsa Siwarã Lalaa Ɔɖi I Ɔrɛrɛ̃ Ɔwɛ̃ Ame.
Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔwara ɔpo makɛlɛ Gadara ibuiti ame si abɔrɛ i Galilea isɛ.
Ɔluwɛ̃ gɔ Yesu ɔso ɔbɔrɛ i ɔkolo ame ne, ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ ame i siwarã lalaa pia ɔsarɛgu wũ.
Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ɔbɔrɛ i ɔmagɛ̃ gɔmɔ ame fiɛ ɔwi gbodzoo ne, ɔsɛ ɔwe ɔki isɔ̃isɔ̃.
Ɔ̃isɛ ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃asɛ i ayo ame, ɣɛɛ ɔwi biara ne, ɔsɛ ɔwe i maturi kabiarakɔ̃.
Gɔ ɔnya Yesu ne, ɔla kulu teteree ɔpɛ agɛgɛ̃ i Yesu ngbatɔ̃.
Ɔɣere wũ teteree sɔ, “Yesu, Ɣaa gɔ nɖe Ɔlesate Ɔbi!
Be ato abie abɔrɛgu i wũ kɔrɛ?
Loto-ɔ i kukpa daakpadzɛ̃ me kutsue!” Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ɔɣɛ ngbɔ ala Yesu ɔtɔ̃me ɔpia siwarã dzɛ mpia i ɔ̃ ame sɔ, “Bɔrɛ i ɔ̃ ame fe!” Ɔwi gbodzoo si siwarã dzɛgbe si ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe iso ne, si manyi wũ nrɔɔ̃ gu ngba ala ngɔsɔngɔsɔn kɔra ne, ɔsɛ ɔmɔɛ̃ ɔfɛfɛ̃ fiɛ sisɛ siɖi wũ ɔbɔrɛ ɔkɛlɛ fafuĩ ame.
Yesu ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Nda marɔ-ɔ?” Ne ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Mme marɔ Isɛguri ne.” Ɔɣɛ ngbɔ alasɔ siwarã lalaa dzɛ mpia i ɔ̃ ame ɔsi.
Mmɔ i Siwarã to sitã Yesu iti sɔ ɔdaafuĩdza ma ɔpia i iwo gudua nɛ ame maawe inyɛ.
Makparako gbodzoo mawɛ̃ ɣɛ i kabemi iso mato maɖe ara.
Ne siwarã lalaa to sitã Yesu iti sɔ ɔtã ma mabo i makparako ma mmɔ ame.
Ne Yesu ɔtã ma ɔri ne.
Siwarã dzɛgbe ɔbɔrɛ i ɔrɛrɛ̃ ame sibo i makparako ame, ma ɔɖuɖu ɔtere kpitikpitikpiti maso kabemi mabo i itubu ame makpi.
Gɔ mma nto manyɔ makparako iso ɔnya nnɛ loba ne, matere makɛlɛ ɔmagɛ̃ ame masɛ maaɣere maturi ɔɖuɖu gu ngorowase ɔɖuɖu.
Maturi ɔbɔrɛ maba sɔ si maba maanyɔ nnɛ loba.
Gɔ mabo Yesu kɔrɛ ne, manya sɔ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ ame i Yesu ɔsa siwarã lalaa ɔɖi ka ɔsi i Yesu ngbatɔ̃, ɔpia awu, iti ame ɔɔkpa waĩ.
Ne ɔso ifɔ̃ ɔmɔɛ̃ ma ɔɖuɖu.
Mma lonya nnɛ loba ne, maɣere matsɔra kumɛgɔ ibara fiɛ siawarã lalaa ɔbɔrɛ i ɔ̃ ame fiɛ ɔsarɛ.
Nnɛgbe ɔso ne, Gadara karɔ̃ gu kã abuiti maturi ɔɣere Yesu sɔ ɔbɔrɛ i ma karɔ̃ iso alasɔ manigã.
Ne ɔso Yesu ɔbo i ɔkolo ame ɔledza irui.
Mmɔ i ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ i Yesu ɔsa ɔpɛ wũ nrɔɔ̃ sɔ, “Tã me losiai-ɔ.” Ɣɛɛ Yesu iinɔgu wũ karɔ̃, ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Kpese kɛlɛ fɔ iyo si asɛ aaɣɛ nnɛ i Ɣaa ɔbara ɔtã-ɔ.” Ne ɔso ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ɔkpese ɔkɛlɛ ma ɔmagɛ̃ ame ɔsɛ ɔ̃awe ɔɣɛ ara wa ɔɖuɖu i Yesu ɔbara ɔtã wũ.
Yesu Ɔsa Yairo Ɔbi Birɔ̃gomi Gu Ɔrɔ̃go Ɔwɛ̃.
Ɔwi gɔ i Yesu ɔwara ɔpo ɔkpese ɔba kama isɛ ne, maturi gbodzoo ɔsarɛgu wũ kukaakɔ alasɔ mato manyɔ wũ ɔri.
Ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Yairo fiɛ ɔɖe ma Yudase kasarɛkɔ̃ makpakpa ndɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɔba ɔ̃apɛ agɛgɛ̃ i Yesu katɔ̃ ɔtã wũ iti sɔ ɔsiai wũ ɔba ɔ̃ iyo, alasɔ ɔ̃ ɔbi birɔ̃gomi ɔwɛ̃ saã gɔ loɔfɔ lɛ akɔ aweo-anyɔ ne, ɔrɛ ɔto ɔnyɛ ɔ̃ɔro ɔkpi.
Gɔ Yesu ɔrui ɔsiai wũ ne, maturi ɔmini wũ mato malili so.
Maturi magbe ndɛ̃ ne, ɔrɔ̃go ɔwɛ̃ gɔ i ara to afere akɔ aweo-anyɔ buu ana pia.
Ɔrɔ̃go gɔgbe ɔɔnina ɔ̃ sikã ɔɖuɖu ɔsu ɔbie so kua ɣɛɛ ɔ̃ina isosarɛ.
Ɔbo i maturi ndɛ̃ ɔbara pɔkɔsɔɔ ɔpɛgu Yesu awu kutsueti i kama isɛ.
Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, ara ko lonyua wũ ɔfere.
Mmɔ i Yesu to ɔkarɛ sɔ, “Nna ɔɖe lopɛgu me?” Ɣɛɛ ɔbiara ɔsɛ̃.
Ne Petro ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Bokɔse, nyɔ kumɛgɔ i maturi ɔki malɔ-ɔ!” Ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Loɣe sɔ ɔnyiiɔ ɔpɛgu me alasɔ ɔle ɔwɛ̃ ɔbɔrɛ i wũ ame.” Gɔ ɔrɔ̃go ɔnya sɔ ɔ̃ibawo ɔwɛrɛ ɔso ne, ɔbɔrɛgu ifɔ̃ ɔto ɔti ɔkpakpa ɔba ɔ̃apɛ agɛgɛ̃ i Yesu katɔ̃ i maturi ɔɖuɖu anɔ.
Ɔɣere Yesu nnɛ ɔso ɔpɛgu wũ gu kumɛgɔ ɔna isosarɛ ɔluwɛ̃.
Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Wũ ɔbi birɔ̃gomi, fɔ kafɔkaɖe losa-ɔ.
Kɛlɛ i isobuɛ ame.” Gɔ Yesu ɣɛ i mmɔ ɔtogu itɔ̃me nɛgbe iɣɛ ne, mapia ɔturi mabɔrɛgu i ma Yudase kasarɛkɔ̃ ɔkpakpa gɔ marɔ Yairo iyo sɔ ɔba ɔ̃aɣere wũ sɔ, “Fɔ ɔbi birɔ̃gomi ɔɔkpi ne ɔso kanyua ratedze kutsuɛ ɔɖaa.” Ɣɛɛ gɔ Yesu ɔnɔ ne, ɔɣere Yairo sɔ, “Daanigã, fɔɖe kere sɔ fɔ ɔbi to ɔ̃asarɛ.” Gɔ masɛ maabo Yairo iyo ne, Yesu iitã kuwɛ̃ ɔri sɔ ɔbo iyo kame iɖo Petro gu Yohanes gu Yakobo gu ɔbirɔ̃gomi maɣese.
Maturi ɔɖuɖu ɣɛ i mmɔ mato mabiɛgu kulu, ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Minyua ɔbiɛ, alasɔ ɔbi iikpi, sirɛ kere ɔto ɔrɛ.” Gɔ ɔɣɛ ngbɔ ne, mama wũ alasɔ maɣe sɔ ɔ̃ɔkpi.
Ne Yesu ɔmɔɛ̃ ɔbirɔ̃gomi kɔrɔ̃, ɔkpere wũ sɔ, “Ɔbi, ta ya!” Ɔbirɔ̃gomi ko lorɛgɛ̃ ɔta ɔsɛ.
Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ mabie irere matã ɔbi si ɔɖe.
Ira nɛgbe ɔbara ɔ̃ maɣese ɣii, ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ madaaɣere kuwɛ̃ nnɛ loba i mmɔ.
Yesu Ɔpia Ɔ̃ Marasuãdze Iweo-inyɔ Itɔ̃me Bielea Kaɣɛkɔ̃.
Yesu ɔkpere ɔ̃ marasuãdze iweo-inyɔ ɔsirakanya ne ɔtã ma ɔri gu ɔle sɔ masa siwarã lalaa ɔɖuɖu si masa sinyɛ agbãagbã ana.
Ɔsese ma sɔ makɛlɛ maaɣɛ Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ iso itɔ̃me si masa manyɛse.
Si maarui ne, Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Midaasu kuira mila i irisɛ ame lɛ ɔsɛdziri ɣee akpo ɣee aɖera ɣee sikã.
Midaasu awu nyɔare sɔ mianyuarã i ɔri.
Iyo biara nɛ ame mafɔ mi ne, miwe i mmɔ gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ miarui i ɔmagɛ̃ gɔmɔ ame.
Ngbegɔ masɛ̃ maifɔ mi ne, si miarui i mmɔ ne, mikpakpa mi ngba sise mifere lɛ Ɣaa kutsue ikpadzɛ̃ nɛ loaba ikparĩ.” Marasuãdze ɔrui mabo i nsɛkɔ̃ mɛmɔ ame mato maɣɛ Itɔ̃me Bielea masa maturi sinyɛ i kakɔi biara.
Herodes Ikpɔkpɔtɔ I Yesu Iso.
Gɔ Herodes gɔ nto ɔɖe Galilea karɔ̃ iso ɔnɔ ara wa nto aba ngbe ne, ɔkpɔkpɔtɔ alasɔ maturi mawɛ̃ to maɣɛ sɔ Ndupiedze Yohanes loɔta ɔbɔrɛ i makpise ame ɔpia ngbã.
Mawɛ̃ ana to maɣɛ sɔ Eliya ɔɖe loɔledza iba.
Fiɛ mawɛ̃ ana sɔ Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze kuere ɔwɛ̃ ɔɖe loɔkpese ɔba maɣe wũ.
Ne Herodes to ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Lotã matu Yohanes iti, ne ɔso nna ɔɖe nto ɔbara ara wa nto lonɔ ngbe?” Ne ɔso Herodes ɔbie ɔri gɔ iso ɔ̃aki fiɛ ɔ̃anya Yesu.
Yesu Ɔtã Maturi Gbodzoo Aɖera Maɖe Mami.
Katɔ̃memasɛdze ɔba maaɣere Yesu nwa ɔɖuɖu mabara.
Ne ka ɔkɔ ma kerekere marui makɛlɛ ɔmagɛ̃ gɔ marɔ sɔ Betsaida ame ne.
Gɔ maturi ɔnɔ ngbɔ ne, masiai ma kama makɛlɛ mmɔ.
Yesu ɔ̃ wũ ɔfɔ ma ɔɣere ma Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ itɔ̃me fiɛ ɔsa mma nto manyɛ.
Iɣɛ̃kɛlɛ ame ne, katɔ̃memasɛdze iweo-inyɔ ɔba maaɣere Yesu sɔ, “Ɖi ma ɔri si makɛlɛ ngorowase mɛ lobore mimatã ngbe si masɛ maabie aɖera gu ngbegɔ maarɛ ala ngbe ɔfe idzoro gu ayo ame.” Mmɔ i Yesu to ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mi mɔmɔ mitã ma irere maɖe.” Ne mato maɣere wũ sɔ, “Araɖea wa ɔɖuɖu boba ngbe nɖe abolo abo aru gu afara anyɔ.
Ato abie sɔ bosɛ boaɣa araɖea botã maturi gbodzoo magbe?” Marɛrɛ̃ kerekere i ma ndɛ̃ aaɖe lɛ maturi kukpi kuru mmɔ.
Ne Yesu to ɔɣere ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Mitã ma masɛ i akuri ame lɛ siru siru awe.” Ne gɔ marasuãdze ɔbara ngbɔ ne, Yesu ɔsu abolo abo aru gu afara anyɔ wamɔ, ɔkɔlɛ anɔ kato.
Gɔ ɔpɛ Ɣaa siba i wã iti ne, ɔbɛbɛse ɔtã ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ masu maɣɛɣɛ mmamɔ.
Gɔ ma ɔɖuɖu ɔɖe ara mami fiɛ marasuãdze ɔsa nwa lobuburi kanya ne, mana kusɛsɛi kuweo-kunyɔ.
Petro Ɔɖi Yesu Ɔte Sɔ Ɔ̃ Nɖe Kristo.
Gɔ Yesu ɔnɔwɛ̃ to ɔkparama kayi iyi iwɛ̃ ne, ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔwe i ɔ̃ kɔrɛ.
Ne ɔto ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Nna i maturi sɛ maɣɛ sɔ loɖe?” Ne matã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Mawɛ̃ sɛ maɣɛ sɔ fɔ nɖe Ndupiedze Yohanes, mawɛ̃ ana sɔ fɔ nɖe Eliya, fiɛ mawɛ̃ ana sɛ maɣɛ sɔ Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze kuere ɔwɛ̃ loɔkpese ɔba ngbã.” Mmɔ ɔto ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Ne mi ɣɛɛ?
Nna miɣe sɔ loɖe?” Petro ɔfɔ kanya sɔ, “Fɔ nɖe Ɣaa Kristo ne.” Yesu Ɔɖe Ika I Ɔ̃ Kukpi Gu Ita Iso.
Mmɔ i Yesu ɔsɛ̃ ɔtã ma teteree sɔ madaaɣere kuwɛ̃ itɔ̃me nɛgbe.
Yesu ɔledza ma iɣere sɔ, “Ikote sɔ mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, awe inyɛ gbodzoo i ma Yudase makpakpa gu masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu mmara matedze nrɔɔ̃ ame maasɛ̃ me, maɖoe me.
Ɣɛɛ ikpɛnɛ tɛare ne, Ɣaa to ɔ̃atara me lowe ngbã.” Mmɔ ɔto ɔɣere ma ɔɖuɖu sɔ, “Si ɔrere ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃asiai me ne, ɔsɛ̃ so si ɔsu ɔ̃ inyɛwe ɔnyigbã si ɔ̃awo me ɔsiai.
Alasɔ ɔbiara gɔ loakpɛ̃ i ɔ̃ ngbã iti ne, ɔto ɔ̃ayura me, ɣɛɛ ngɔ loanyua ɔ̃ ngba ala wũ ɔso ne, ɔto ɔ̃ana ngbã mɛ loisɛ miro.
Mme kusia i ɔturi ana si kayi iso ɔɖuɖu karana ɔkpese ɔ̃ kare fiɛ ɔ̃ina ngbã mɛ loisɛ miro?
Si mme gu wũ ara ite to ikpɛ̃ ɔrere kunuarɛ ne, mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, mme wũ ɔto ɔ̃akpɛ̃ me kunuarɛ ku ɔwi gɔ ame loaba i wũ ikpawaĩ gu wũ ɔse Ɣaa ɔle gu ɔ̃ makpabo sekelea ɔɖuɖu ikpawaĩ ame.
Nto loɣere mi gbaã sɔ mi ndɛ̃ mawɛ̃ i ngbe iibakpi fiɛ Ɣaa aaɖi ɔ̃ Sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ɔle ɔte.” Yesu Ɔfinikirã Ɔ̃ Kumiamia I Kube Iso.
Lɛ ɖapɛ ɔwɛ̃ kama gɔ Yesu ɔɣere ma ara wagbe ne, ɔkɔ Petro gu Yohanes gu Yakobo maya kube kuwɛ̃ makɛlɛ itititɛ̃ sɔ maakparama kayi.
Gɔ ɔto ɔkparama kayi ne, ɔ̃ katɔ̃ ko lokpaki kato kafiɛ futututu gɔ ta ɔ̃ ara wa ɔpia to atsue anɔmi.
Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, marɛrɛ̃ inyɔ ma nɖe Mose gu Eliya ɔba maaya i ɔ̃ kɔrɛ mato maɖegu wũ ika.
Maba i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ikpawaĩ ame fiɛ maɖe ku Yesu ika i ɔri gɔ iso ɔ̃aki fiɛ ɔ̃abara Ɣaa kuɖɔɛ i ɔ̃ kukpi i Yerusalem iso.
Petro gu ɔ̃ malaa ɔrɛ sirɛ dzoroo, ɣɛɛ gɔ mata ne, manya Yesu i ɔ̃ ikpawaĩ ame gu maturi inyɔ ma nɣɛ wũ i kɔrɛ.
Gɔ maturi inyɔ mamɔ to marui ne, Petro ɔɣere Yesu sɔ, “Tete, bo ngbe iba ɔbua ilɛ gbaã!
Tã bopɛ akpayo atɛ i ngbe.
Iwɛ̃ itã-ɔ, iwɛ̃ itã Mose fiɛ iwɛ̃ ana itã Eliya.” Ɔ̃ mɔmɔ kɔra iiɣe ara wa ɔɣɛ i ngbe.
Gɔ ɔɣɛ i mmɔ ɔto ika iɖe ne, idɔdɔ ɔso ifu ma iso ne ɔso ifɔ̃ ɔmɔɛ̃ marasuãdze gbaã.
Ne manɔ silɔ i idɔdɔ ame gɔ sito siɣɛ sɔ, “Wũ ibiete gɔ losia ikparĩ ngbe ne, mikã wũ Atsue!” Gɔ silɔ dzɛmɔ ɔlo ikaɖe ne, manya sɔ Yesu ɔnɔwɛ̃ lokuti ɔɣɛ i mmɔ.
Marasuãdze ɔma kanya i ara wagbe iso.
Maiɣere kuwɛ̃ nnɛ manya ku ɔwi gɔmɔ ame.
Yesu Ɔsa Siwarã Lalaa Ɔɖi I Ɔbirɛrɛĩ Ɔwɛ̃ Ame.
Gɔ kaɖe ɔsɛ̃ ne, Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze itɛ mammɔ ɔso mabɔrɛ i kube iso maba.
Maturi gbodzoo ɔba maasarɛgu wũ.
Ne ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ i mmɔ to ɔla kulu ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Ratedze!
Loto-ɔ i kukpa, nyɔ wũ ɔbi!
Wũ ɔbi ɔwɛ̃ saã!
Siwarã lalaa ɔ to siɖaa wũ gɔ sito sitã sɔ ɔ̃ala kulu teteree, ɔluwɛ̃ sipuri wũ siwuĩ i karɔ̃ iyɔ minyatu ka misɛ wũ i kanya.
Si iba ngbɔ ne, isɛ ibua iwe ɔle, ina ɔpã fiɛ isɛ ikpa wũ.
Lotã fɔ marasuãdze iti sɔ masa siwarã dzɛgbe matã me ɣɛɛ maiwo.” Mmɔ i Yesu to ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mi kiniɔgbe maturi ma kafɔkaɖe lotɛgɛlɛ fiɛ miba atsuele!
Ku mme ɔwi loawe i mi kɔrɛ fiɛ loaɣara so lotã mi lotui?” Ne ɔɣere ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔmɔ sɔ, “Kɔ fɔ ɔbi bɔ me ngbe.” Gɔ ɔbi to ɔba ne, ɔluwɛ̃ siwarã ɔpuri wũ siwuĩ i karɔ̃ ɔleso ɔto.
Ne Yesu ɔtɔ̃me ɔpia siwarã lalaa dzɛmɔ ɔsa ɔbi ɔtara wũ ɔta ɔ̃ ɔse ne.
Ɣaa ɔle siare gɔgbe ɔbara maturi ɔɖuɖu ɣii.
Yesu Ɔledza Ika Iɖe I Ɔ̃ Kukpi Iso.
Gɔ Yesu Kurabarara togu maturi ibara ɣii ne, ɔɣere ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Midaaɣara nnɛ nto loba loaɣere mi!
Mato maaɖi mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, matã maturi.” Ɣɛɛ mainɔ nnɛ ɔɣere ma karɔ̃.
Ɣaa ɔsu ira nɛgbe ɔkɔla ma sɔ mainɔ karɔ̃ fiɛ mato manigã sɔ maakarɛ wũ ana.
Yesu Ɔɖi Ɔturi Gɔ Loɖo Ɔte.
Kakpadzɛ̃ ɔba i marasuãdze ndɛ̃ sɔ ma nna nɖe ngɔ loɖo pelepele.
Gɔ Yesu ɔtsue ma adzuni ɔso ne, ɔkɔ ɔbiɛtɛ ɔwɛ̃ ɔba ɔ̃aɣedza ma i katɔ̃.
Ne ɔto ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ɔbiara gɔ loafɔ ɔbiɛtɛ gɔgbe i wũ iyere ame ne, mme iɖe ɔfɔ.
Fiɛ ɔbiara gɔ lofɔ me ne, ɔfɔ ngɔ lopia me katɔ̃me.
Alasɔ ɔturi gɔ nsɛ ɔbɔ so karɔ̃ i mi ɔɖuɖu ndɛ̃ ne, ɔ̃ nɖe ngɔ lokɔlɛ ɔɖo pelepele ne.” Ɔturi Gɔ Loitsiri-Ɔ Ne, Ɔɣɛ-Ɔ I Kama.
Mmɔ i Yohanes to ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Bokɔse, bonya ɔwɛ̃ gɔ ɔto ɔsa siwarã lalaa i fɔ iyere ame ɣɛɛ ne, botindza wũ sɔ ɔnyua ala ɔ̃iɖe bo ndɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃.” Ne Yesu to ɔɣere ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Midaatɛ̃ wũ ɔri, alasɔ si ɔturi iita ɔɣɛ mi iso ne, mitsue sɔ ɔɣɛ mi i kama.” Samaria Maturi Mawɛ̃ Ɔsɛ̃ Yesu.
Gɔ ɔwi gɔ i Ɣaa aasu Yesu ɔkɛlɛgu kato ɔɔpɛtɛpɛtɛ ne, ɔbara ɔ̃ adzuni sɔ ɔ̃akɛlɛ Yerusalem.
Ɔpia mawɛ̃ ɔɖegu katɔ̃ sɔ masɛ maaledza ara masɛ i Samaria akorowa awɛ̃ matã ɔ̃ iba.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ mmɔ maturi ɔtsue sɔ Yerusalem ɔto ɔfe ɔkɛlɛ ɔso ne, maifɔ wũ.
Gɔ ɔ̃ marasuãdze inyɔ ma nɖe Yohanes gu Yakobo ɔnya ne, makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Bokɔse, ato abie sɔ bokpere ɔtɔ si ɔbɔrɛ i kato ɔba ɔ̃atsuedza ma?” Ne Yesu ɔfiniki ɔsɛ̃ ma sɔ, “Miiɣe siwarã dzɛ nto siɖe mi iso!
Alasɔ mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, iiba sɔ loawɔra maturi ngbã ɣɛɛ ɔba loba sɔ loaɖi me bowũ.” Ne ɔ̃ gu marasuãdze ɔrui makɛlɛ ɔmagɛ̃ mama ame ne.
Mawɛ̃ Ɔbie Sɔ Maasiai Yesu.
Gɔ mato makɛlɛ ne, ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɔba ɔ̃aɣere Yesu sɔ, “Loasiai-ɔ kakɔi biara ga aakɛlɛ.” Ne Yesu ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Mabɔi lalaa ba awo wa ame masɛ mawɛrɛ fiɛ kurodzai ana ba ayo, ɣɛɛ mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, na iti kasiakɔ̃.” Ne Yesu to ɔɣere ɔmama ana sɔ, “Siai me.” Ɣɛɛ ngɔmɔ ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Bosate, loasiai-ɔ, ɣɛɛ ɖi me ɔri si nsɛ loabiara tete tɔtɔ.” Ne Yesu to ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Tã mma nse lɛ makpise si mabiara ma makpise, ɣɛɛ fɔ ne kɛlɛ aaɣɛ Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ itɔ̃me.” Ɔwɛ̃ ana ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Bosate lobie sɔ loasiai-ɔ, ɣɛɛ ne, tã me losɛ loamala wũ maturi so tɔtɔ.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ngɔ loisɛ ɔbara ɔ̃ karabara ku ɔ̃ ɔtu ɔɖuɖu iikote ɔtã Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃.”
Yesu Ɔpia Ɔ̃ Masiaidze Sikɔdzɛ-inyɔ Katɔ̃me.
Nnɛgbe kama ne, Bosate ɔɖi marɛrɛ̃ sikɔdzɛ-inyɔ mama gɔ ɔpia ma inyɔ inyɔ, ɔɣere ma sɔ maɖe wũ katɔ̃ makɛlɛ simagɛ̃ gu ngorowase mɛ ame ɔto ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃asɛ.
Ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ɔraɖui gɔ maasɔrɛ̃ ɔsi ɣɛɛ marabaradze iisi.
Ne ɔso mitã kakpɛkɔ̃ sate iti sɔ ɔsese marabaradze ɔ̃ kakpɛkɔ̃ ame.
Mikɛlɛ!
Nto lopia mi lɛ masɛrɛrerɔ̃ abi i magidi ndɛ̃.
Midaasu sikã kawumi ɣee ndokota ɣee akpo mila.
Midaatui i ɔri sɔ mito miya kuwɛ̃.
“Iyo biara nɛ ame miabo ne, miɖe katɔ̃ miɣere ma sɔ, ‘Isobuɛ itã iyo nɛgbe maturi.’ Si ngɔ nsɛ ɔɖɔɛ isobuɛ pia i iyo nɛmɔ ame ne, mitã sɔ mi isobuɛ si isiai wũ.
Ɣɛɛ si kuwɛ̃ na ngbɔ ne, misu mi isobuɛ kaya miruigu.
Miwe i iyo biara nɛ ame maafɔ mi.
Araɖea igbã biara nɛ maatã mi ne, miɖe si minɛ.
Ikote sɔ maatã rabaradze ɔ̃ aɖera.
Midaawe mikiki, mibɔrɛ i iyo nɛ ame mikɛlɛ imama ame.
“Ɔmagɛ̃ biara gɔ ame maafɔ mi ne, miɖe nnɛ masu matã mi.
Misa manyɛse i ɔmagɛ̃ gɔmɔ ame si miɣere ma sɔ, ‘Ɣaa sigara ɔɖewi ɔɔbore ɔbo mi.’ Ɣɛɛ si misɛ ɔmagɛ̃ ɔrere ame fiɛ maifɔ mi ne, mirui mikɛlɛ ma itiri si miɣere ma sɔ, ‘Mi ɔmagɛ̃ ame ɔsebu gɔ lota ɔfere bo i ngba kɔra ne, boɔkpakpa bofere mi.
Ɣɛɛ minyigi sɔ Ɣaa sigara ɔɖewi ɔɔbore ɔbo mi!’ Nto losia ita lotã mi sɔ iase pɔkɔsɔɔ itã Sodom ɔmagɛ̃ iɖo ɔmagɛ̃ gɔmɔ maturi!
Simagɛ̃ Siwɛ̃ Maturi Ɔsɛ̃ Yesu Itɔ̃me.
“Ndzo miɖe mitã mi Korazin maturi!
Fiɛ ndzo miɖe mitã mi Betsaida maturi!
Alasɔ si awawãra wa igbã lobara i mi ame iɖe lobara i Tiro gu Sidon simagɛ̃ ame ne, tee maakpase masɛ i ndɔ̃ ame mapia ara wa loate sɔ maɔfiniki mabɔrɛ i ma akpi ame!
Ɣaa to ɔ̃anyɔ Tiro gu Sidon simagɛ̃ nnya ɔɖo mi ku atɔ̃me iɣɛyi.
Mi Kapernaum maturi ne, i mi adzuni ame ne, mito mibie sɔ miakɔlɛ so misɛ miabo kato, ɣɛɛ Ɣaa to ɔ̃abɔ mi karɔ̃ mikɛlɛ ta ikpibiɔ!” Mmɔ i Yesu to ɔɣere ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Ɔbiara gɔ loakã mi atsue ne, mme iɖe ɔkã atsue fiɛ ɔbiara gɔ loasɛ̃ mi ne, mme iɖe ɔsɛ̃.
Ɔbiara gɔ loasɛ̃ me ne, ngɔ lopia me katɔ̃me ɔsɛ̃.” Marasuãdze Sikɔdzɛ-Inyɔ Ɔkpese Maba Yesu Kɔrɛ Maturi sikɔdzɛ-inyɔ mamɔ ɔkpese maba ku isoɣɔ maba maaɣere wũ sɔ, “Bosate, ta siwarã lalaa to sikã bo atsue i fɔ iyere ame.” Ne Yesu to ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Lonya Ɔbosam ɔkpase ɔbɔrɛ i kato lɛ kumɛgɔ i kado sɛ ɔma awe.
Mikã atsue!
Lotã mi ɔle sɔ miawo maɣɛ gu siboitɛtɛ iso ɔnene ɣɛɛ kuira iibabara mi.
Miaɖe Tsirise ɔle ɔɖuɖu iso fiɛ kuira iibabara mi.
So si sidaaɣɔ mi sɔ siwarã lalaa to sikã mi atsue.
Ɣɛɛ so si siɣɔ mi sɔ Ɣaa ɔtsɛrɛ mi aɣere ɔpia i ɔ̃ sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ɔko ame.” Yesu Ɔle Ɣaa.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, Siwarã Bielea isoɣɔ ɔbo i Yesu ame ɔɖuɖu ne ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Tete, Kato gu Karɔ̃ Sate, nto lole-ɔ sɔ asu ara wa lowɛrɛ manɔgbadze gu makotsuese ne, aɖi wã ate mabiɛtɛ.
Fiɛ gbaã ne, Tete, ngbɔ ikote-ɔ ne.” Mmɔ ɔtsɛ ma iɣere sɔ, “Tete ɔsu ara ɔɖuɖu ɔpia me i nrɔɔ̃ ame.
Kuwɛ̃kuwɛ̃ iiɣe Ɔbi iɖo Ɔse ɔnɔwɛ̃, fiɛ kuwɛ̃ ana iiɣe Ɔse iɖo Ɔbi gu mma i Ɔbi ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃aɖi ɔ̃ Ɔse ɔte.” Ne Yesu ɔfiniki ɔnyɔ ɔ̃ marasuãdze i iwɛrɛ ame ɔɣere ma sɔ, “So si siɣɔ mi gbaã sɔ mito minya ara wa mito minya i ngbe!
Nto loɣere mi sɔ ne, Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze gbodzoo gu magara ana ɔbie teteree sɔ manya ara wa mito minya, ɣɛɛ mainya, ɣee si manɔ ara wa mito minɔ, ɣɛɛ mainɔ.” Yesu Ɔpɛ Ma Igbã I Ɔ Samariase Ɔwɛ̃ Kayiribielea Ibara Iso.
Mmaratedze ɔwɛ̃ ɔba Yesu kɔrɛ sɔ si ɔba ɔ̃ala Yesu ɔnyɔ.
Ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ratedze, be loabara fiɛ loana ngbã mɛ loisɛ miro?” Ne Yesu ɔta wũ mmuai ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Be i Ɔko Sekelea Ɔɣɛ?
Fiɛ nda anɔ itɔ̃me nɛmɔ karɔ̃?” Ne ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔmɔ to ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ɖɔɛ Bosate Ɣaa ku fɔ ɔtu ɔɖuɖu ku fɔ siwarã ɔɖuɖu ku fɔ ɔle ɔɖuɖu ku fɔ adzuni ɔɖuɖu ana si aɖɔɛ fɔ ɔnyii lɛ kumɛgɔ ato aɖɔɛ so.” Ne Yesu to ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Gbaã iɖe.
Bara ngbɔ ne ato aasɛ ngbã.” Ɣɛɛ gɔ mmaratedze gɔgbe to ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃atã so ibɛ ɔso ne, ɔledza Yesu i karɛ sɔ, “Nna nɖe wũ ɔnyii?” Ne Yesu to ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ɔwi ɔwɛ̃ ame ne, ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɔbɔrɛ i Yerusalem isɛ ɔto ɔkɛlɛ Yeriko ɔmagɛ̃ ame.
Mayukukpe ɔsɛ maamɔɛ̃ wũ i ɔri iso, mapɛ wũ maɖi wũ igbɛ maɖi ta ɔ̃ iso ara fiɛ manyua wũ masɛ sɔ ka ɔtsɔra ɔkpi.
Iba sɔ Ɣaa sɔrɛdze ɔwɛ̃ to ɔfe i ɔri gɔmɔ iso.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ ɔnya ngɔ maɖi igbɛ i ɔri kuruɛ ne, ɔki isɛ isɛ ɔfe.
Iifɔ ɔwi, ɔ Levise ɔwɛ̃ ɔ̃ wũ ɔba ɔ̃aki i mmɔ ɔfe.
Gɔ ɔnya ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ne, ɔki i kuruɛ ɔfe.
Ɣɛɛ ɔ Samariase ɔwɛ̃ gɔ nto ɔfe i ɔri gɔmɔ iso ne, gɔ ɔba ɔ̃anya ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ne, ɔ̃ ara ɔɖo wũ kayiri.
Ɔbore ɔbo wũ, ɔsu nnɔĩ gu ndã ɔnukutu wũ aɣɛi ame ɔnyi wã kukaakɔ.
Ɔputa ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ɔsia i ɔ̃ mɔmɔ bɔi iso.
Ɔkɔ wũ ɔkɛlɛgu mafɔ kafɔkɔ̃ fiɛ ka ɔnyɔ wũ iso.
Gɔ kaɖe ɔsɛ̃ ne, ɔɖi sikã ɔtã mafɔ kafɔkɔ̃ nyɔisose ɔɣere wũ sɔ, ‘La ɔɔnyɔ wũ iso.
Si loɔkpese loba ne, loatã-ɔ ira biara nɛ aledza inina i ɔ̃ iso.’ ” Ne Yesu to ɔkarɛ mmaratedze gɔgbe sɔ, “I fɔ adzuni kanya ne, maturi itɛ magbe ndɛ̃ ne, nna afɔ aɖe sɔ ɔɖe ɔnyii ɔtã ngɔ lobo i mayukukpe nrɔɔ̃ ame?” Ne mmaratedze to ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Ngɔ lonyɔ wũ nnya.” Ne Yesu to ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Fɔ wũ kɛlɛ si asɛ aabara ngbɔ.” Yesu Ɔkɛlɛ Marta Gu Maria Kɔrɛ.
Gɔ Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔrui maɣo ɔri ne, masɛ maabo ɔmagɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ame.
Mmɔ masɛ maatu ɔrɔ̃go ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Marta fiɛ ɔfɔ ma i ɔ̃ iyo ne.
Marta ba ɔnyiibi gɔ marɔ sɔ Maria.
Ɔ̃ ne, ɔkpase ɔsɛ i Yesu katɔ̃ ɔto ɔnɔ ɔ̃ ara wa ɔto ɔte.
Iyo karabara ɔɖuɖu ɔba kaasia i Marta ɔnɔwɛ̃ iso gɔ iɖaa wũ ɔtu.
Ne ɔso ɔba ɔ̃aɣere Yesu sɔ, “Bosate, gɔ wũ ɔnyiibi ɔnyua iyo karabara ɔɖuɖu ɔsia me i iso ne, aibaɣere wũ kuira?
Ɣere wũ sɔ ɔba ɔ̃abuai me!” Mmɔ i Yesu to ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “O Marta, ato aɖaa so i ara gbodzoo iso lo!
Ɣɛɛ ne, ira ka iwɛ̃ pɛ lonya sɔ aabie, fiɛ isɛɛ nɛmɔ i Maria ɔɖi gɔ kuwɛ̃ iisibafɔ wũ ne iso.”
Yesu Ɔte Ɔ̃ Marasuãdze Kumɛgɔ Maakparama Kayi.
Iyi iwɛ̃ ne, Yesu ɔwe i kakɔi kawɛ̃ ɔto ɔkparama kayi.
Gɔ ɔro ne, ɔ̃ marasuãdze mawɛ̃ ɔba ɔ̃ kɔrɛ maɣere wũ sɔ, “Bosate, te bo kumɛgɔ boakparama kayi lɛ Yohanes ɔte ɔ̃ marasuãdze awe.” Ne Yesu to ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Si mito mikparama kayi ne, miɣɛ sɔ, ‘Bo ɔse, tã sɔ boarɔ fɔ iyere i kuwarɛ ame.
Fɔ sigara iɖe si iba i bo ndɛ̃.
Tã bobara fɔ kuɖɔɛ i karɔ̃ iso lɛ masɛ mabara i kato.
Tã bo ikpɛnɛ ame araɖea iyi biara.
Si asu bo akpi atsɛ bo, alasɔ bo wũ bosɛ bosu botsɛ ɔturi biara gɔ loɣɛrɛ bo.
Daatã sɔ boabo i kalakanyɔ ame.
Ɣɛɛ ɖi bo borɛgu i akpi ame.’ ” Ne Yesu to ɔɣere ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Si mi ndɛ̃ ɔrere ɔsɛ ɔ̃ ɔlaa iyo ku kasɛ̃ ndɛ̃ ɔsɛ ɔ̃atara wũ sɔ, ‘Wũ ɔlaa, nyɛ abolo abo atɛ tã me, alasɔ wũ ɔlaa ɔwɛ̃ ɔse i ɔri ɔba ɔ̃abo me kiniɔ, ɣɛɛ lona ku araɖea wa loatã wũ!’ “Si fɔ ɔlaa gɔmɔ ɔɣere-ɔ sɔ, ‘Daaba aaɖa me!
Bo gu wũ mabi ka borɛ fiɛ boɔsɛ̃ akui ana.
Loisibawo ɔledza ita iba iatã-ɔ kuira.’ Si iba ngbɔ ne, be iɖe aabara?
Nto loɣere mi sɔ si kulaa kerekere ɔso ne, ɔ̃ibata.
Ɣɛɛ kumɛgɔ aɣɛ atogu wũ iti itã ɔso ne, ɔto ɔ̃ata ɔtã-ɔ ira biara nɛ ato abie.
“Ne ɔso nto loɣere mi sɔ, mikarɛ ara si maatã mi ara, mibie ara si miana, mipɛ kukui kɔrɔ̃ si maasese mi iyo.
Alasɔ ɔbiara gɔ nsɛ ɔkarɛ ira ne, ɔsɛ ɔfɔ.
Ɔbiara gɔ nsɛ ɔbie ira ne, ɔsɛ ɔna ne, fiɛ ɔbiara gɔ nsɛ ɔkpura kukui kɔrɔ̃ ne, masɛ masese matã wũ.
“Fiɛ mi ma nɖe maɣese ne, mi ɔwɛ̃ aasu aɣɛ ɔtã ɔ̃ ɔbi si ɔkarɛ wũ ikpɛ?
Ɣee ɔsu ɔboitɛtɛ ɔtã wũ si ɔkarɛ wũ ikɔkɔɣɔ?
Si mi ma nɖe makpibaradze kɔra ɣe kumɛgɔ miasu ara sɛɛ mitã mi mabi ne, iyɔ mi ɔse gɔ mpia i kato ɣɛɛ?
Be ɔso ɔ̃ibasu ɔ̃ Siwarã Bielea ɔtã mma nto makarɛ wũ?” Mawɛ̃ Ɔkpadzɛ̃gu Yesu Atɔ̃me I Ɔ̃ Ɔle Iso.
Ɔwi ɔwɛ̃ ne, Yesu to ɔsa siwarã lalaa dzɛ lotã sɔ ɔturi iito ɔwo ika ɔɖe.
Ne gɔ siwarã dzɛmɔ ɔbɔrɛ i ɔmumu gɔmɔ ame ne, ɔtsɛ ika iɖe ne ɔso ibara mma nɣɛ i mmɔ ɣii.
Ɣɛɛ ma ndɛ̃ mawɛ̃ ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Siwarã lalaa igara Beelzebul ɔɖe lotã wũ ɔle gɔ ɔsu ɔto ɔsa siwarã lalaa ɔɖi.” Mawɛ̃ ana ɔla Yesu manyɔ ne ɔso maɣere wũ sɔ ɔbara iwawãra ɔte sɔ Ɣaa kɔrɛ ɔbɔrɛ.
Ɣɛɛ Yesu ɣe nnɛ mpia i ma adzuni ame.
Ne ɔso ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Karɔ̃ biara ga maturi loɣɛɣɛ so mato makpɛ̃gu so ne, karɔ̃ gamɔ to kaakpese ikpakpi.
Ngbɔ ame si iyo irere maturi ɔta maɣɛ so iso mato makpɛ̃gu so ne, iyo nɛmɔ to iasasame.
Ne ɔso si Ɔbosam sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ɔta siɣɛ so iso ne, nda i sigarakaɖekɔ̃ dzɛmɔ aawo ɔya?
Nto loɣɛ ngbɔ ala mito miɣɛ sɔ nto losa siwarã lalaa i Beelzebul iyere ame.
Si Beelzebul ɔle iso nto losa sɛ̃ ne, nna ɔle iso i mi masiaidze to masa siwarã lalaa maɖi i maturi ame?
Mi mɔmɔ masiaidze to maatã mi ipɔ.
Ɣɛɛ si Ɣaa Siwarã ɔle ame nto losa siwarã lalaa ne, mitsue kukaakɔ sɔ Ɣaa sigara ɔɖewi ɔɔba ɔ̃abo mi ndɛ̃.
“Si ɔturi gɔ mba ɔle ɔnyɔme akpadza ɔto ɔdzuɛ̃ ɔ̃ iyo ne, ɔ̃ kuira iibayu.
Ɣɛɛ si ngɔ mba ɔle ɔɖo wũ ɔba ɔ̃akpɛ̃gu wũ fiɛ ɔɖe wũ iso ne, ɔto ɔ̃afɔ ɔ̃ akpakpɛ̃ra wa ɔɖuɖu ɔsu ɔto ɔdzuɛ̃ so ala ɔsu ɔ̃ karana ɔ̃aɣɛɣɛ ɔ̃ malaa.
“Ngɔ loiɣɛgu me ne, mitsue sɔ ɔta ɔɣɛ me iso gbaã.
Ngɔ loito ɔsagu me ara kanya ne, ɔto ɔsamarã ara.
Siwarã Lalaa Ikpese Iba.
“Si masa siwarã lalaa maɖi i ɔturi ame ne, sisɛ sikɛlɛ siawe siki sibie kawekɔ̃ i kakorekɔ̃.
Si siina kukakɔi ne, sisɛ siɣere so sɔ, ‘Loakpese lokɛlɛ iyo nɛ ame masa me maɖi.’ Ne ɔso siaba sianya sɔ maɔfiɛ iyo nɛmɔ ame maledza ira biara se kukaakɔ.
Iyɔ siakpese sikɛlɛ siakɔ siwarã lalaa aka akɔdzɛ mama dzɛ lonyanyarĩ siɖo sɛ̃ sibua so iso.
Maabo i ngɔmɔ ame mawe, ne ɔso ɔ̃ kawirikɔ̃ to kaanyanyarĩ kaɖo ɔ̃ karɔ̃kasɛkɔ̃.” Yesu Ɔte Ara I Ɔturi Gɔ Mba Isoɣɔ Mɔmɔ Iso.
Gɔ Yesu ɔɣɛ ara wagbe ɔro ne, ɔrɔ̃go ɔwɛ̃ i maturi ndɛ̃ mmɔ ɔla kulu ɔɣɛ sɔ, “So aaɣɔ ɔrɔ̃go gɔ loɣe-ɔ gu ngɔ lotã-ɔ inyɛ ameme!” Ne Yesu to ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Mma nto manɔ Ɣaa itɔ̃me fiɛ mato mabara i ne iso i so aaɣɔ!” Yesu Ɔsɛ̃ Sɔ Ɔ̃ibabara Iwawãra Ɔte.
Gɔ maturi ma loki malɔ Yesu ɔɔsi mabua ne, ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Minyɔ kumɛgɔ kiniɔgbe maturi ba ɔtile!
Mato mabie awawãra sɔ maanya ɣɛɛ maibanya kuiwɛ̃ iɖo Ɣaa kanyaɖidze Yona ire igbã.
Kumɛgɔ ame i Ɣaa kanyaɖidze Yona ɔɖe ikparĩ ɔtã Niniwe maturi ne, ngbɔ ame i Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi ana aaɖe ikparĩ ɔta kiniɔgbe maturi ne.
Atɔ̃me iɣɛyi ne, Igararɔ̃go gɔ lobɔrɛ i bo karɔ̃ kala isɛ to ɔ̃ata ɔya ɔtã mi kiniɔgbe maturi ipɔ, alasɔ ɔsɛ ɔri dzoroo ɔbɔrɛ i kayi iti tsɔra ɔba ɔ̃akã Salomo atɔ̃me wa ame i inɔgba pia atsue.
Ɣɛɛ nto loɣere mi sɔ ngɔ inɔgba loɖo Salomo ire pia i mi ndɛ̃ ngbe.
Niniwe maturi to maata maya masɔ̃ mi arɔĩ i katɔ̃ ku atɔ̃me iɣɛyi.
Alasɔ ɔwi gɔ i Yona ɔɣere ma Ɣaa itɔ̃me ne, mafiniki i ma ara lalaa wa mato mabara ame.
Ɣɛɛ nto loɣere mi sɔ ne, ngɔ loɖo Yona pia i mi ndɛ̃ ngbe!
Yesu Ɔte Ara Wa Loatã Ɔturi Ikpawaĩ.
“Kuwɛ̃ iisɛ ɔtsue ɔkãniɛ ɔsu ɔwɛrɛra ɣee ɔfu ara.
Ɣɛɛ ɔsɛ ɔtara ɔsia i ngbegɔ i maturi ma loabo iyo aanya kukaakɔ.
Ɔturi anɔmi nɖe ɔkaniɛ atã wũ.
Si fɔ anɔmi to anya kukaakɔ ne, iyɔ fɔ ame ɔɖuɖu ɔkpa.
Ɣɛɛ si fɔ anɔmi iito anya kukaakɔ ne, idududu sɔɔ̃ iɖe i fɔ ame.
Ne ɔso nyɔ sɔ aibatã ikpawaĩ nɛ mpia i fɔ ame ɔkpese idududu.
Si ikpawaĩ ɔyi i fɔ ame ɔɖuɖu fiɛ fɔ kukakɔi na i idududu ame ne, tsue sɔ fɔ iso ɔɖuɖu ɔɔkpa lɛ kumɛgɔ matsue ɔkaniɛ masia i ira iso fiɛ iyo ɔɖuɖu ame ɔkpa awe.” Yesu Ɔtã Ma Farisise Gu Mmara Matedze Ipɔ.
Gɔ Yesu ɔɖe ika ɔro ne, ɔ Farisise ɔwɛ̃ ɔkpere wũ sɔ ɔba ɔ̃aɖe ara i ɔ̃ iyo.
Ɔkɛlɛ ɔsɛ ɔ̃asɛ i iyo ame sɔ maaɖe ara.
Ibara ɔ Farisise gɔmɔ ɣii gɔ ɔnya sɔ Yesu iifore nrɔɔ̃ lɛ kumɛgɔ i kubarara ɔte kanya fiɛ ɔtsɛ aɖera iɖe.
Ne ɔso Bosate ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Mi ma Farisise ne, misɛ mifore mi aɖerɔi gu akɔi kama ɣɛɛ ne, mi ame ɔyigu ɔtile gu anyanyara ɔɖuɖu ibara.
Madzimifɔ!
Ɣaa gɔ lobara ira kama ne, iiɖe ɔ̃ ame lobara kame ne?
Misu ira biara nɛ mpia i mi arɔi gu akɔi ame mitã mawɛrɛba si mi ira biara aakpa sekelee i Ɣaa katɔ̃.
“Ndzo miɖe mitã mi ma Farisise!
Misɛ miɖi mi araɖea ika weova ta aposarɛbi, ibura, sikɔma agbãagbã mitã Ɣaa.
Ɣɛɛ misɛ̃ sɔ miibaɣɛ atɔ̃me i ɔri iso fiɛ miiɖɔɛ Ɣaa ana.
Ara wagbe ikote sɔ miasu mibua i nwa mimɔɛ̃ mito iso ne.
Ɣɛɛ miibanyua kuiwɛ̃ misɛ.
“Ndzo miɖe mitã mi ma Farisise!
Alasɔ misɛ mibie nsɛkɔ̃ kɔlɛa i mi kusarɛkɔ̃.
Misɛ mibie sɔ maturi si maya mi ku karɔ̃ ibɔso i kuɣa ame.
“Ndzo miɖe mitã mi, alasɔ mise lɛ akpibiɔ wa maisɛ ikpo fiɛ maturi sɛ maki i wã iso i idaatsue ame.” Mmɔ i mmaratedze ɔwɛ̃ i ma ndɛ̃ to ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ratedze, Si aɣɛ ngbɔ ne, ato atia bo bo wũ.” Ne Yesu ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Ndzo miɖe mitã mi mmara matedze ana.
Ato wa i maturi iibawo ɔsore ne, wã aɖe misu misorera ma fiɛ miito mibara adzuni sɔ miabuai ma masore wã.
“Ndzo miɖe mitã mi alasɔ mitsue Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze ma loɔkpi akpibiɔ, ɣɛɛ ne, mi mawa loɖoe ma.
Fiɛ mi mɔmɔ to mitɔrã misia sɔ ara wa i mi mawa ɔbara ne, apia mi isoɣɔ.
Maɖoe Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze, ne mi wũ miɔtsue ma akpibiɔ ne.
Nnɛgbe ɔso i Ɣaa iwola ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Loasese wũ kanyamaɖidze gu makpabo i ma ndɛ̃, maaɖoe mawɛ̃, makpɛ̃gu mawɛ̃.’ Ne ɔso kiniɔgbe maturi ɔɖuɖu ne, mato maakpadzɛ̃ ma kutsue i Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze ma ɔɖuɖu maɔɖoe, ita i karɔ̃kasɛkɔ̃ iba iabo kiniɔ.
Ita i ɔwi gɔ maɖoe Abel isɛ iabo Zakaria gɔ maɖoe i isɔrɛkasege gu ngbegɔ marɔ sɔ kasekelekɔ̃ ndɛ̃.
Gbaã nto loɣere mi sɔ Ɣaa to ɔ̃akpadzɛ̃ kiniɔgbe maturi kutsue i ma ɔɖuɖu iti!
“Ndzo miɖe mitã mi mmara matedze!
Alasɔ iyo nɛ ame i iwola pia ne, misɛ̃ ne akui misɛ.
Mi mɔmɔ ne, misɛ̃ sɔ miito mibo i ne ame.
Mma ana nto mabie sɔ maabo ne, mitɛ̃ ma ɔri sɔ madaabo.” Gɔ Yesu ɔrui i mmɔ ne, ma Farisise gu mmara matedze ɔnagu wũ sikpã gbaã matsɛ wũ atɔ̃me ikpadzɛ̃ gu i ara agbãagbã iso.
Mabie ɔri gɔ iso maaki fiɛ ɔ̃aɣɛ inyakpi irere fiɛ maaya i ne iso matã wũ ipɔ.
Yesu Ɔte Ara I Mila Ara Ibara Iso.
Gɔ maturi kukpi kukpi ɔba maasakanya fiɛ mato malili so manene so ne, Yesu ɔtsɛ ɔ̃ marasuãdze iɣere sɔ, “Midzuɛ̃ so i ma Farisise mila ara wa loakpɔkpɔtɔra maturi iso.
Ira biara nɛ mafu ara ne, mato maabusi ne.
Fiɛ ira biara nɛ mabara i iwɛrɛ ame to iare kayi.
Ne ɔso ibiara nɛ maɣɛ i idududu ame ne, ito iaba i inyamɔ.
Awɛrɛra gu ara wa maɣɛ i iyo kame ɔɖuɖu ne, mato maapɛ wã imomo.
Minigã Ɣaa Ne Iiɖe Maturi.
“Wũ malaa, nto loɣere mi sɔ midaanigã mma loaɖoe siturina fiɛ ne kama ne, maisibawo kuira ɔbara.
Ɔturi gɔ ikote sɔ mianigã ne, loaɖi wũ lote mi.
Minigã Ɣaa gɔ si ɔ̃ɔɖoe ɔturi ɔro ne, ɔba ɔle ana sɔ ɔ̃asu wũ ɔpia i itɔkpe nɛ loisɛ inyi ame.
Loaɣere mi sɔ ɔ̃ lokote sɔ mianigã ne.
Iiɖe kupɛrɛ kunyɔ masɛ marɔdɛ̃ kunagini kuru?
Ɣɛɛ Ɣaa anɔ iisɛ ata i kukawɛ̃ iso.
Mi ati siwɛrɛ̃ kɔra ne, Ɣaa ɣe sɛ̃ kusime.
Ne ɔso ne, midaanigã alasɔ mifɔ kuɣa miɖo kunagini gbodzoo.
Miya I Yesu Kama Teteree.
“Loto loɣere mi kukaakɔ sɔ ngɔ loaya i maturi katɔ̃ ɔɣɛ sɔ wũ ɔre ɔɖe ne, Mme Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi mme wũ nto loaɣɛ ngbɔ ame i Ɣaa makpabo ɔɖuɖu katɔ̃ i ɔ̃ iso.
Ɣɛɛ ɔbiara gɔ loasɛ̃ me i maturi katɔ̃ ne, Mme Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi mme wũ nto loasɛ̃ wũ i Ɣaa makpabo anɔ.
Ɔturi biara gɔ loaɣɛ inyakpi i mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, iso ne, Ɣaa to ɔ̃asu ɔtsɛ wũ.
Ɣɛɛ ngɔ loaɣɛ imusuora i Siwarã Bielea iso ne, Ɣaa iibasu ɔtsɛ wũ.
“Si makpadzɛ̃ mi makɛlɛgu ma Yudase kasarɛkɔ̃ ɣee makpakpa ɣee magara katɔ̃ sɔ maaɣɛgu mi atɔ̃me ne, midaamararã so sɔ be miasɛ miaɣɛ ɣee nda miaɖi so kanya.
Alasɔ Siwarã Bielea to siate mi nnɛ miaɣɛ si ɔwi gɔmɔ ɔɔɣo.” Ranase Dzimifɔ Ɔwɛ̃ Iso Itɔ̃me.
Ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ i maturi ndɛ̃ i mmɔ ɔɣere Yesu sɔ, “Ratedze, ɣere wũ ɔnyiibi sɔ ɔtã boɣɛ so bo ɔse ara wa ɔnyua ɔsɛ bo.” Mmɔ i Yesu to ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Wũ ɔturi, nna lobara me atɔ̃meɣɛdze gu ngɔ loaɣɛ mi ara?” Ne Yesu to ɔɣere ma ɔɖuɖu sɔ, “Minyɔ tuee si minyɔ so i kanɔbɛbɛ biara iso, alasɔ ɔturi ngbã mɔmɔ na i ɔ̃ karana ga ɔba ame.” Ne Yesu to ɔpɛ ma igbã nɛgbe sɔ, “Ranase ɔwɛ̃ ɔwe gɔ karɔ̃ lolɛ kukaakɔ ɔso ɔ̃ ɔraɖui ɔbua ɔlɛ gbaã.
Ne ɔso ɔɣere so sɔ, ‘Gɔ nna ngbegɔ loafere wũ ɔraɖui kiniɔ ne, be loabara?
“ ‘Nnɛ loabara nɖe sɔ, loabiɛbiɛ wũ siwu lotsue siɣɛtɛ dzɛ lomɔ siɖo ndzɛgbe.
Iyɔ loana ngbegɔ loafere wũ ɔraɖui ɔɖuɖu.
Loaɣere so sɔ, “Iti ɔbua ilɛ me.
Ɔraɖui gɔ lona to ɔ̃ase akɔ akɔ.
Loawarã, loɖe ara, lonɛ ara, lona isoɣɔ.” ’ “Ɣɛɛ Ɣaa ɔɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Fɔ dzimifɔ!
Kasɛ̃ gagbe ame nto loafɔ fɔ ngbã ne.
Nna loaɖe ara wa ɔɖuɖu asakanya asɛ so ngbe?’ ” Ne Yesu ɔwirigu ma sɔ, “Ngbɔ iase itã ngɔ lotã karana ɔfu so ɣɛɛ ɔna kuira i Ɣaa anɔ ne.” Ɣaa Sɛ Ɔnyɔ Ɔ̃ Mabi Iso.
Ne Yesu to ɔɣere ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Ne ɔso nto loɣere mi sɔ midaamarã so i mi ngbã, nnɛ miaɖe gu nnɛ miapia iso.
Ngbã ɔfɔ kuɣa miɖo aɖera fiɛ sosina ɔfɔ kuɣa siɖo arapia.
Minyɔ kukparodza gɔ i ɔwiri ame, kuisɛ kupɛ ɔraɖui, ngbɔ ame kuisɛ kusɔrɛ̃ ɔraɖui ana ne.
Kuna siwu gu awumi.
Ɣɛɛ Ɣaa sɛ ɔtã kɔ̃ aɖera.
Mi ne, mifɔ kuɣa miɖo kukparodza kokooko.
Mi nna loawo ikpɛnɛ iwɛ̃ ɔsu ɔbua i ɔ̃ agbanayi iso iki i imararãso ame?
Si miibawo kuira ɔbara i ara wiriwiria wagbe iso ne, iyɔ midaamararã so i ara mama iso.
“Minyɔ kumɛgɔ adziri sɛ alɛ ɔnyɔ si afere aɣɔ̃la.
Aisɛ ata ɖɔti ɣee awe ɔkati atã so.
Ɣɛɛ loɣere mi sɔ, Igara Salomo kɔra si ɔkɛrɛ so ne, ɔ̃isɛ ɔlɛ ɔnyɔ lɛ kudziri gɔ lofere aɣɔ̃la.
Ɣaa nsɛ ɔkɛrɛ sikua ngbɔ.
Sikua dzɛ mpia nɔme kɔrãkaɖe maɔkpɛ̃ sɛ̃ mafere i ɔtɔ ame matsuedza.
Si Ɣaa to ɔnyɔ sikua iso ngbɔ ne, ɔ̃ibabara ɔtã mi ma loɖo Sikua?
Be ɔso i mi kafɔkaɖe ɔfoforo ngbɔ?
Ne ɔso midaasu mi ɔtu misia i nnɛ miaɖe ɣee mianɛ iso, midaamararã so i ne iso.
Alasɔ mma loifɔ Ɣaa maɖe ne, ara wagbe iso masu ma ati masia ne.
Mi ɔse ɣe ara wa ɔɖuɖu lonya mi.
Ɣɛɛ ne, mila miɔbu iti ame i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ iso si ɔ̃asu ara wagbe ɔɖuɖu ɔbua mi.
Misu Anɔ Misia I Ɣaa Sigarakaɖekɔ̃ Iso.
“Wũ masiaidze ma loisi, midaanigã.
Alasɔ Ɣaa isoɣɔ iɖe sɔ ɔ̃atã mi ɔ̃ sigarakaɖekɔ̃.
Misu mi iso ara mirɔdɛ̃ si mibara mi karana karabara i mawɛrɛba iso.
Mibie sikã akpo wa loisɛ anina misɛ so i kato.
Mmɔ ne, kaase kpoo, kuwɛ̃ iibapɛgu fiɛ kaibaro ana.
Alasɔ yukukpe iibawo mmɔ ɔbo fiɛ makorokpɛ ma nsɛ manina ara ana iibawo mmɔ ɔbo.
Alasɔ ngbegɔ i fɔ karana se ne, mmɔ i fɔ ɔtu ana aawe ne.
Yesu Ɔɣere Ɔ̃ Marasuãdze Sɔ Manyɔ Tuee.
“Miledza so mitã ira biara nɛ loaba si mi sikaniɛ ana si sidaanyi lɛ maɖabo ma nto manyɔ ma ɔkɔse gɔ ngba ɔrɔ̃go kakɔkɔ̃ ɔri sɔ ɔ̃aba.
Fiɛ si ɔba ɔ̃akpura kukui kɔrɔ̃ ne, maasese wũ ɔluwɛ̃.
Maɖabo mamɔ aana isoɣɔ si ma ɔkɔse aaba ɔ̃anya ma sɔ manyɔ tuee mato manyɔ ɔ̃ iba ɔri.
Nto loɣere mi sɔ, ɔ̃akpasa ɔkati ɔtã masɛ i karɔ̃, ɔ̃ mɔmɔ ɔtã ma araɖea sɔ maɖe.
So abua siɣɔ ma si ɔ̃aba ku kasɛ̃ ndɛ̃ ɣee ɔɖesɛrã ɔba ɔ̃anya sɔ manyɔ ne, sirɛ iisu ma.
Kiniɔ ne, mitsue sɔ si iyosate ɣe ɔwi gɔ ame i yukukpe aaba ɔ̃ayu wũ ne, ɔ̃ibatã wũ ɔri sɔ ɔbiɛ ɔ̃ iyo ɔbo i kame.
Ne ɔso mi wũ ne, minyɔ tuee alasɔ mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, to loaba loabɔrɛ mi iso ku ɔwi gɔ miito minyɔ ɔri.” Ikote Sɔ Ɔɖabo Aakã Atsue.
Mmɔ iɖe i Petro to ɔkarɛ Yesu sɔ, “Bosate, bo kere ato apɛ igbã nɛgbe ɛɛbɛrɛ maturi ɔɖɔɖu ato?” Mmɔ i Yesu to ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Ɔɖabo gɔ mba iwola fiɛ ɔsɛ ɔbara ara i ɔri iso ne, ɔ̃ i ɔ̃ ɔkɔse sɛ ɔsu ɔbara maɖabo tsɔra nyɔisose sɔ ɔ̃atã ma araɖea i ɔwi sɛɛ iso ne.
Nyɔ, so to siaɣɔ ɔɖabo gɔmɔ gbaã, si ɔ̃ ɔkɔse ɔba ɔ̃anya sɔ ɔto ɔbara ngbɔ!
Gbaã ne, nto loɣere mi sɔ ɔkɔse gɔmɔ to ɔ̃asu ɔɖabo gɔgbe ɔsɛra i ɔ̃ ara ɔɖuɖu kanya.
Ɣɛɛ si ɔɖabo gɔmɔ ɔɣere so sɔ, ‘Wũ ɔkɔse to ɔ̃awe ina ɔpã i ɔri gɔ ɔkpa ame,’ Ne ɔso ɔtsɛ ɔɖe gu ɔnɛ, ɔrɛ̃ ndã, ɔpɛ maɖabo tsɔra, marɛrɛ̃ gu marɔ̃go ɔɖuɖu ne, ɔ̃ ɔkɔse to ɔ̃aba ɔ̃abo ku ɔwi gɔ i ɔɖabo iito ɔnyɔ wũ ɔri.
Mmɔ ne, ɔ̃ ɔkɔse to ɔ̃akpadzɛ̃ wũ kutsue i matsuelese ndɛ̃.
“Ɔɖabo gɔ nɣe ira nɛ i ɔ̃ ɔkɔse sɛ ɔbie sɔ ɔbara ɔtã wũ ɣɛɛ ɔsɛ̃ sɔ ɔ̃ito ɔbara ne, ipɛ to iabo wũ gbaã.
Ɣɛɛ ɔɖabo gɔ loiɣe nnɛ i ɔ̃ ɔkɔse to ɔbie sɔ ɔbara fiɛ ɔbara nnɛ lokote itã ipɛ ne, ɔ̃ ipɛ iibafe isi.
Ngɔ matã ara gbodzoo ne, mato maakarɛ ara gbodzoo mabɔrɛgu i ɔ̃ kɔrɛ.
Ngɔ ana matã ara abua afe isi ne, ngbɔ ame maakarɛ mabɔrɛgu i ɔ̃ kɔrɛ ne.
Maturi To Maɣɛɣɛ So Ala Yesu Ɔso.
“Ɣaa kutsue ikpadzɛ̃ nɛ nse lɛ ɔtɔ losu lobɔ kayiiso.
Fiɛ wũ kayiri tee ɔtɔ gɔmɔ ɔɔwara.
Ɣaa itupie iwɛ̃ to iaba me iso fiɛ lona iwarã kuiwɛ̃ gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ inyɛwe nɛgbe ɔwi ɔfe ɔro.
Mibu sɔ isobuɛ iɖe losu lobɔ kayiiso?
Ooɣo!
Iiɖe isobuɛ losu lobɔ ɣɛɛ iɣɛɣɛ so iɖe.
Ita i kiniɔ ne, iyo nɛ ame i maturi iru pia ne, mato maata maya so iso.
Ma inyɔ to maata maya itɛ iso fiɛ itɛ ana to maata maya i inyɔ iso.
Ɔse to ɔ̃ata ɔya i ɔ̃ ɔbi birɛrɛĩ iso fiɛ ɔbirɛrɛĩ to ɔ̃ata ɔya ɔ̃ ɔse iso.
Mabi manyi to maata maya ma mabi birɔ̃gomi iso fiɛ mabirɔ̃gomi ana to maata maya ma manyi iso.
Marã manyi to maata maya ma mabire iso fiɛ mabire ana to maata maya ma marã manyi iso.” Yesu Ɔka Maturi Ma Ɔto Ɔɖegu Ika.
Yesu ɔɣere ma ana sɔ, “Si minya sɔ adɔdɔ to abɔrɛ i kuɣɛ̃ iyo kabokɔ̃ ne, misɛ miɣɛ sɔ kado to ɔ̃apɛ, fiɛ isɛ iba ngbɔ ana.
Si minya sɔ ɔwiri to ɔkpɛ̃ ɔbɔrɛ i kala isɛ ne, misɛ miɣɛ sɔ awururu ka aba fiɛ isɛ iba ngbɔ.
Maladze!
Misɛ miwo kuɖokpo ɔnyɔ ɔɣɛ kumɛgɔ i kayi aase, ɣɛɛ miito miwo ɔwi gɔ ame mipia ɔnya ɔɖi ite!
Yesu Ɔte Kumɛgɔ Maaledza Maturi Inyɔ Ndɛ̃.
“Be ɔso miibabo i ara ame minyɔ sɔ imele nlɛ gɔ miabara?
Si fɔ gu ɔturi ɔna atɔ̃me fiɛ ɔkɔ-ɔ ɔto ɔkɛlɛgu atɔ̃mekaɣɛkɔ̃ ne, ki i ɔri biara iso si aledza mi gu wũ inyɔ ndɛ̃ fiɛ miabo atɔ̃mekaɣɛkɔ̃.
Si iiɖe ngbɔ ne, ɔto ɔ̃asu-ɔ ɔtã matɔ̃meɣɛdze, ma wũ masu-ɔ matã mma nsɛ mamɔɛ̃ maturi mamɔɛ̃-ɔ mapia i iyo.
Fiɛ lobie sɔ mitsue sɔ ato aawe i iyo karɛkɔ̃ gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ ɔwi gɔ atã kuso gɔ ato kapɛrɛ tsɔra aro.”
Si Miifiniki I Situ Ame Ne, Mito Miakpi Miwɔ.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, mawɛ̃ ma mpia i mmɔ ɔɣere Yesu kumɛgɔ i Pilato ɔɖoe Galilea maturi mawɛ̃ ku ɔwi gɔ mato mafɛ̃ ara matã Ɣaa.
Mmɔ i Yesu ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Mifɔ miɖe sɔ Galilea maturi mamɔ nɖe makpibaradze maɖo ɔso fiɛ maɖoe ma ngbɔ?
Ooɣo, iiɖe ngbɔ iɖe!
Ɣɛɛ nto loɣere mi sɔ si miinyua ara lalaa ibara ne, mi wũ ngbɔ ame miakpi ne.
Maturi iweo-farafana ma i Siloa iyo kɔlɛa nɛmɔ ɔbiɛ ifu ɣɛɛ?
Mifɔ miɖe sɔ ma nɖe makpibaradze maɖo mma ɔɖuɖu mpia i Yerusalem?
Ooɣo, iiɖe ngbɔ iɖe!
Nto loɣere mi sɔ si miifiniki minyua mi akpi ibara ne, ngbɔ ame i mi ɔɖuɖu aakpi ne.” Yesu Ɔpɛ Igbã I Kuɖedziri Gɔ Loito Kuɣɔ̃ Abi Iso.
Yesu ɔpɛ igbã nɛgbe sɔ, “Ɔwi ɔwɛ̃ ame ne, ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɔwe gɔ lopia kuɖedziri i ɔ̃ kakpɛkɔ̃ ame.
Ɔsɛ kuɖedziri gɔgbe katɔ̃ sɔ ɔ̃abie kɔ̃ abi, ɣɛɛ ɔ̃ina kuiwɛ̃.
Mmɔ ɔɣere ngɔ nto ɔnyɔ kakpɛkɔ̃ iso sɔ, ‘Akɔ atɛ sɔɔ̃ loɔba loabie adziribi i kudziri gɔgbe iso fiɛ loina kuiwɛ̃ ne.
Ɖaɛ kɔ̃ alasɔ kuto kunina karɔ̃ ga iso kuɣɛ.’ “Ɣɛɛ ngɔ nto ɔnyɔ kakpɛkɔ̃ iso ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, ‘Bokɔse, tã botã kɔ̃ ikɔ iwɛ̃ saã bobua bonyɔ.
Loakuri kɔ̃ kayirinɔ lofere ara wa loatã karɔ̃ iɖa lonyɔ.
Si kuɣɔ̃ abi ne, iyɔ ilɛ.
Ɣɛɛ si kuiɣɔ̃ abi ne, boawo kɔ̃ ɔɖaɛ ɔpɛyu.’ ” Kakpadzɛ̃ Mama I Iwarãyi Iso.
Iwarãyi iwɛ̃ iso ne, Yesu ɔsɛ ɔ̃ate ara i ma Yudase kasarɛkɔ̃.
Ɔrɔ̃go ɔwɛ̃ ana ɔwe i mmɔ gɔ siwarã lalaa ɔɔnyɛra wũ akɔ aweo-farafana sɔɔ̃.
Siwarã dzɛgbe ɔtã sɔ ɔrɔ̃go gɔgbe ɔkɔ, ɔ̃isɛ ɔwo ɔta ɔya tɔrɔrɔ.
Gɔ Yesu ɔnya wũ ne, ɔkpere wũ ɔɣere sɔ, “Ɔrɔ̃go, ɔɔna isosarɛ!” Yesu ɔsu ɔ̃ nrɔɔ̃ ɔsia wũ iso.
Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, ɔrɔ̃go gɔgbe ko lota ɔya tɔrɔrɔ ɔtsɛ Ɣaa ile.
Sikpã ɔmɔɛ̃ ɔkpakpa gɔ nto ɔnyɔ kasarɛkɔ̃ mmɔ iso gbaã sɔ Yesu ɔsa nyɛse ku Iwarãyi iso.
Ne ɔso ɔɣere maturi ɔɖuɖu sɔ, “Boba ayi akuɔ wa boasu bobara bo karabara ne ɔso si irere to mi ndɛ̃ ɔrere fiɛ ɔto ɔbie sɔ masa wũ ne, ɔba i ayi wamɔ ame ne iiɖe Iwarãyi iso!” Mmɔ i Bosate to ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Mi maladze, manantsuĩ gu mafirimu ma nsɛ mabara mi karabara ne, mi nna loikurisi ma i siwɛ̃ ame sɔ makɛlɛ ndu kanɛkɔ̃?
Ɣɛɛ ne, Abraham ɔ̃ ɔwa tɛtɛ gɔ i Ɔbosam ɔpia ɔnyɛ akɔ aweo farafana ngbe ne, iikote sɔ maasa wũ ku Iwarãyi?” Itɔ̃me nɛ i Yesu ɔɣɛ ngbe ɔtã sɔ kunuarɛ ɔkpɛ̃ ɔ̃ matsirise ɣɛɛ maturi tsɔra ɔna isoɣɔ i awawãra wa ɔto ɔbara ɔɖuɖu iso.
Yesu Ɔsu Ɣaa Sigarakaɖekɔ̃ Ɔkoteragu Kadzirimi Kawɛ̃.
Ne Yesu to ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Miɣe nnɛ maasu Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ makateragu?
Be iɖe boasu bokateragu iakote?
Ise lɛ idziribi kosoi iwɛ̃ nɛ i ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔsu ɔsɛ ɔ̃apɛ i ɔ̃ kakpɛkɔ̃ ame.
Gɔ ɔraɖui gɔgbe ɔre ne, ɔmɔ ɔkpese kudziri siare gɔ kurodzai aabara ayo i kɔ̃ akpa ame.” Yesu Ɔsu Ɣaa Sigarakaɖekɔ̃ Ɔkoteragu Inyagɛ̃ Kua.
Yesu ɔledza ma igbã mama ipɛ iɣɛ sɔ, “Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ sɛ siɣa lɛ ngbe.
Ɔrɔ̃go ɔwɛ̃ ɔsu inyagɛ̃ kua ɔpia i mmɔre mɛ losi ame, ɔkpɔkɔtɔ ɔsakanya gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ mmɔre ɔɖuɖu ɔnyagɛ̃.” Yesu Ɔɣɛ Sɔ Ngbã Kayogodɔ̃ Se Mɔmɔrĩ Yesu ɔwe ɔki i simagɛ̃ gu ngorowase ame ɔto ɔte maturi ara ku ɔwi gɔ ɔto ɔkɛlɛ Yerusalem.
Mmɔ i ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ to ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Tete, maturi kɛkɛĩ kere loana iɖi?” Ne Yesu to ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Pia kubɛ si aki i kayogodɔ̃ mɔmɔrĩa ame.
Alasɔ maturi gbodzoo to maabie sɔ maaki i mmɔ mabo ɣɛɛ maibawo ɔbo.
Ɔwi to ɔba gɔ iyosate to ɔ̃ata ɔmɔɛ̃ kukui ɔsɛ̃.
Iyɔ mi ma lokuti miɣɛ i kayoma to miatsɛ kukui ikpukpura iɣɛ sɔ, ‘Tete, sese bo iyo!’ “Ɣɛɛ iyosate gɔmɔ to ɔ̃aɣɛ sɔ, ‘Loiɣe mi!’ “Iyɔ mito miaɣɛ sɔ, ‘Bo gu-ɔ ɔɖe ara bonɛ ara fiɛ ate ara i bo ɔmagɛ̃ ame!’ ” “Ɣɛɛ ɔto ɔ̃aledza mi iɣere sɔ, ‘Loiɣe ngbegɔ mibɔrɛ!
Mirui me i kɔrɛ, mi ara lalaa mabaradze ɔɖuɖu.’ “Kaku gu inyɛwe aaba si minya Abraham gu Isak gu Yakob gu Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze ɔɖuɖu i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ame ɣɛɛ Ɣaa aasa mi sɔ midaabo.
Maturi to maabɔrɛ i kuɣɛ̃kabɔrɛkɔ̃ gu kɔ̃ iyo kabokɔ̃ maba.
Maabɔrɛ i kato gu kala isɛ maba maasakanya i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ maɖe ara manɛ ara.
Maturi mawɛ̃ ma nɖe matsɔra to maakpese maɖeakatɔ̃.
Fiɛ maɖeakatɔ̃ mawɛ̃ to maakpese matsɔra.” Yesu Ba Kuɖɔɛ Ɔtã Yerusalem.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, ma Farisise mawɛ̃ ɔba Yesu kɔrɛ maba maɣere wũ sɔ, “Bara mala si abɔrɛ ngbe akɛlɛ kakɔi mama ala Igara Herodes to ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃aɖoe-ɔ.” Ne Yesu to ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mikɛlɛ miaɣere raninadze gɔmɔ sɔ, ‘Nɔme ne, loasa siwarã lalaa loɖi i maturi ame, losa manyɛse isɛ iabo kɔrãkaɖe.
Ikpɛnɛ tɛare iso ne, loaro wũ karabara.’ Ne ɔso kiniɔ ne, ita i nɔme isɛ iabo kɔranɔwɛ̃ ne, loaɣo ɔri.
Alasɔ iikote sɔ maaɖoe Ɣaa kanyaɖidze i kakɔi mama iɖo Yerusalem ɔmagɛ̃ ame.
“Yerusalem, Yerusalem!
Fɔ gɔ maturi nto maɖoe Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze, fiɛ masɛ mabara mma i Ɣaa ɔpia katɔ̃me i fɔ kɔrɛ ɔtile mapɛ ma ata.
Ɔwi gbodzoo ame loɔwarɛ nrɔɔ̃ losɔ̃-ɔ sɔ loafu fɔ maturi lɛ kɔkɔ ɔnyi sɛ ɔwarɛ ɔ̃ abue ɔfu ɔ̃ mabi ɣɛɛ masɛ̃ sɔ lodaabara.
Nnɛgbe ɔso ne, Ɣaa to ɔ̃aɖi ɔmagɛ̃ gɔgbe atsue.
Nto loɣere-ɔ gbaã sɔ ne, aisibanya me gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ ɔwi gɔ miala kulu miɣɛ sɔ, ‘Maale ngɔ nto ɔba i Bosate iyere ame!’ ”
Yesu Ɔledza Ɔrɛrɛ̃ Ɔwɛ̃ Isa Ku Iwarãyi Iso.
Iwarãyi iwɛ̃ ne, Yesu ɔsɛ ma Farisise ɔkpakpa ɔwɛ̃ iyo gɔ makpere wũ sɔ ɔba ɔ̃aɖe ara.
Mma lowe mmɔ ɔkarã anɔ i ɔ̃ iso totoroo.
Ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ nrɔɔ̃ gu ngba loɣe ɔba ɔ̃ kɔrɛ.
Ne Yesu to ɔkarɛ mmara matedze gu ma Farisise mamɔ sɔ, “Bo mmara ne, mitã bo ɔri sɔ bosa ɔnyɛ ku Iwarãyi ɛɛbɛrɛ miitã bo ɔri?” Ɣɛɛ maiwo kuira ɔɣɛ.
Ne Yesu ɔmɔɛ̃ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe kɔrɔ̃ ɔsa wũ fiɛ ɔɖi wũ ɔri ne.
Mmɔ ɔto ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mi ndɛ̃ nna ɔbi ɣee nantsuĩ loakpase ɔbo i ibu ɣee iwo ame ku Iwarãyi fiɛ ɔ̃ibaɖi wũ i Iwarãyi nɛmɔ iso?” Ɣɛɛ maiwo wũ itɔ̃me mmuai ɔtã.
Yesu Ɔɣɛ Kumɛgɔ Maabɔ So Karɔ̃ Gu Mafɔ Ifɔ Iso.
Gɔ Yesu ɔnya kumɛgɔ i mma makpere mabɔ aɖera kaɖekɔ̃ i mmɔ to makpɛ̃ mabie nsɛkɔ̃ kɔlɛa ne, ɔpɛ ma igbã nɛgbe sɔ, “Si ɔturi ɔkpere-ɔ sɔ ba ɔ̃ ɔrɔ̃go kakɔkɔ̃ ne, daasɛ aasɛ i kasɛkɔ̃ kɔlɛa pelepele.
Alasɔ iawo ɔba sɔ ɔkpere ɔmama gɔ lokɔlɛ ɔɖo-ɔ ana ɔbɔ i mmɔ.
Daatã sɔ ngɔ lokpere mi inyɔ ɔɖuɖu aaba ɔ̃aɣere-ɔ sɔ, ‘Tã ngɔgbe si ɔba ɔ̃asɛ i mmɔ.’ Iyɔ ka aba aata aasɛ i katsɔrakɔ̃ gɔ kunuarɛ amɔɛ̃-ɔ.
Ɣɛɛ si makpere-ɔ makɛlɛgu kakɔi ne, sɛ aasɛ i iyara kosoi iso.
Si ngɔ lokpere-ɔ ɔbɔ ɔba ɔ̃anya-ɔ ne, ɔ̃aɣere-ɔ sɔ, ‘Wũ ɔlaa, ta ba sɛ i iyara siare nɛgbe iso.’ Nnɛgbe to iakɔlɛ-ɔ kato i maturi mama ma makpere mabɔ ɔɖuɖu anɔ.
Alasɔ ɔbiara gɔ nsɛ ɔkɔlɛ so kato ne, Ɣaa to ɔ̃abɔ wũ karɔ̃ fiɛ ɔturi biara gɔ lobɔ so karɔ̃ ne, Ɣaa to ɔ̃akɔlɛ wũ kato.” Ne Yesu to ɔfiniki ɔɣere ngɔ lokpere wũ ɔbɔ araɖea kaɖekɔ̃ sɔ, “Si ato akpere maturi sɔ maba maaɖe aɖera i fɔ iyo ne, daakpere fɔ malaa ɣee fɔ manyiibi ɣee fɔ malɛdze ma mba karana.
Alasɔ ma wũ mato maakpere-ɔ lɛ kumɛgɔ akpere ma sɔ maba maaɖe ara.
Si iba ngbɔ ne, tsue sɔ maɔbara mati-ɔ kuso.
Ɣɛɛ si ato ana isoɣɔ nɛgbe igbã ne, kpere mawɛrɛba gu mma lofɛfɛ̃ mafu maisɛ mawo ɔsɛ, mma lokpi kasɛkasɛ gu manɔbiɛdze.
Nnɛgbe loatã Ɣaa ɔfere-ɔ kusɛkusɛ ne.
Alasɔ mmamɔ iibawo-ɔ kuso kukuwɛ̃ ɔtã.
Ɣaa to ɔ̃atã-ɔ kuso ku iyi nɛ i maturi sekelea aata mabɔrɛ i makpise ame.” Makpere Maturi Sɔ Maba Maaɖe Ara I Ɣaa Sigarakaɖekɔ̃.
Gɔ mma nsi mato maɖe ara ɔwɛ̃ ɔnɔ itɔ̃me nɛgbe ne, ɔɣere Yesu sɔ, “So to siaɣɔ mma loaɖe ara i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ gbaã!” Ne Yesu to ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ɔwi ɔwɛ̃ ame ne, ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɔkpere maturi gbodzoo sɔ maba ɔ̃ ɔpɔrɔ̃ katukɔ̃ maba maaɖe ara.
Ɔwi gɔ maɔwa aɖera maro fiɛ ira biara ɔɔkote ne, ɔpia ɔ̃ maɖabo sɔ masɛ maaɣere mma ɔɖuɖu ɔkpere sɔ ka maba alasɔ ira biara ɔɔkote!
“Ɣɛɛ ma ɔɖuɖu ɔtsɛ kafara itu.
Ɔɖeakatɔ̃ ɔɣere ɔɖabo sɔ, ‘Loɣa karɔ̃ kawɛ̃, ne ɔso losɛ loanyɔ kã gɔ itã sɔ loibawo ɔba.’ ” “Ɔmama ana sɔ, ‘Loɣa manantsuĩ iweo ma loakpɛ̃ matã me i wũ kakpɛkɔ̃ ame.
Ɔri ka nto loɣo sɔ loanyɔ kumɛgɔ maawo karabara ɔbara ne ɔso loibawo ɔba.’ ” “Ɔmama ana sɔ, ‘Kiniɔ ame loyiri ɔrɔ̃go ne, ne ɔso loibawo ɔba.’ “Ɔɖabo ɔkpese ɔsɛ ɔ̃aɣere ɔ̃ ɔkɔse ara wagbe ɔɖuɖu.
Sikpã ɔmɔɛ̃ ɔkɔse gbaã ne ɔɣere ɔɖabo sɔ, ‘Pɛ siwa kɛlɛ siri iso gu amamai ɔɖuɖu ame i simagɛ̃ ame si akpere mawɛrɛba gu maturi ma lofɛfɛ̃ mafu gu manɔbiɛdze gu mma lokpi kasɛkasɛ ɔɖuɖu abɔ.’ “Ɔɖabo ɔsɛ ɔ̃abara ngbɔ, ne ɔkpese ɔba ɔ̃aɣere ɔ̃ ɔkɔse sɔ ɔɔkpere ma ɔbɔ ɣɛɛ ne, kasɛkɔ̃ ɔkuti kase gbodzoo ana.
Mmɔ i ɔ̃ ɔkɔse to ɔledza wũ iɣere sɔ, ‘Kɛlɛ aaki i sivurã iso gu nsɛkɔ̃ si akpere maturi abɔ sɔ wũ iyo ɔɖuɖu ayi ku maturi.
Nto loɣere-ɔ sɔ mma ɔɖuɖu lokpere sɔ tee maba wũ ɔpɔrɔ̃ katukɔ̃ ne, ma kuwɛ̃ iibati wũ aɖera ɔnyɔ!’ ” Ato Aawe Anyɛ Si Aɖe Rasuãdze.
Ɔwi ɔwɛ̃ ame gɔ maturi gbodzoo siai Yesu ne, ɔfiniki ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ɔbiara gɔ loasiai me ne, ɔ̃ibawo wũ siaidze ɔɖe si ɔ̃iɖɔɛ me ɔɖo ta ɔ̃ ɔse gu ɔ̃ ɔnyi gu ɔ̃ ɔre gu mabi gu ɔ̃ manyiibi gu ɔ̃ mɔmɔ.
Ngɔ loisore inyɛwe ɔnyigbã ɔsiai wũ nsɛgbai ne, ɔ̃ibawo wũ rasuãdze ɔɖe.
“Si ɔrere to ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃atsue iyo siare ne, ɔ̃aɖe katɔ̃ ɔsɛ i karɔ̃ ɔbu ara wa ɔɖuɖu lonya gu wã kuɣa ɔnyɔ si ɔba sikã ɔ̃awo ɔtsue ɔro tɔtɔ fiɛ ɔ̃asɛ karɔ̃.
Si ɔ̃ibara ngbɔ ne, si ɔ̃ɔpia ne i karɔ̃ ame ɔro ne, ɔ̃anyua iyoku ɔɣedza.
Mma ɔɖuɖu lonya iyoku nɛgbe to maatsɛ wũ ima iɣɛ sɔ, ‘Ngɔgbe ɔtsɛ iyo itsue ɣɛɛ ɔ̃iwiri.’ “Si igara ɔrere to ɔkɛlɛ ɔ̃akpɛ̃ kakpã ku makpakpɛ̃dze kukpi kuweo fiɛ ma gu igara gɔ loakpɛ̃ ba makpakpɛ̃dze kukpi sinyɔ ne, ikote sɔ ɔ̃abu iti ame ɔnyɔ tɔtɔ si sɔ ɔ̃ ɔle gɔ ɔba aawo ɔ̃ tsirise gɔmɔ ɔkpɛ̃gu.
Si ɔnya sɔ ɔna ɔle ngbɔ ne, ɔ̃apia ɔ̃ maturi masɛ maasarɛgu igara nyɔare gɔmɔ matã wũ iti sɔ ɔ̃ibawo wũ ɔkpɛ̃gu ne ɔtã mafere kanya ndu tɔtɔ kɔra fiɛ igara gɔmɔ aaba kakpãtɔ̃.” Kawirikɔ̃ ne, Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ngbɔ ame i mi ndɛ̃ kuwɛ̃ iibawo wũ rasuãdze ɔɖe si ɔ̃isɛ̃ so pelepele ne.
Ara Wa Nna Kusia Ne, Maaɖi Wã Mawiri.
“Mma ba ɔmɛrɛ̃.
Ɣɛɛ si me ɔmɛrɛ̃ ɔɔro ne, aisibawo ɔri kuwɛ iso ɔki ɔpia me ɔmɛrɛ̃.
Miiɖe ira nɛ maasu mapia karɔ̃ iɖa ɣee mafere me i aku kawirikɔ̃.
Maasu me masa mawiri.
“Ne ɔso mi ma mba atsue si minɔ nnɛ nto loɣɛ!”
Yesu Ɔpɛ Igbã I Masɛrɛ Ma Loyu Iso.
Iyi iwɛ̃ ne, ma lampofɔdze gu akpi mama mabaradze ɔba Yesu kɔrɛ sɔ si maba maanɔ ɔ̃ itɔ̃me.
Ma Farisise gu mmara matedze mawɛ̃ ɔtsɛ wũ iɣɛtɛ iɣereso sɔ, “Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe sɛ ɔfɔ makpibaradze ɔɖegu ma ta aɖera!” Ne ɔso Yesu ɔpɛ ma igbã nɛgbe sɔ, “Si mi ndɛ̃ ɔrere ba masɛrɛ kulafa fiɛ ma ndɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɔyu ne, be ɔ̃abara?
Ɔ̃ibanyua kasiwɛ̃-kaiwɛ̃ ɔɣɛdza i aɖera kaɖekɔ̃ ɔ̃anyɔnyɔ ngɔ loyu gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ ɔ̃anya wũ?
Fiɛ si ɔnya wũ ne, ɔ̃ana isoɣɔ gbaã ɔputa wũ ɔsia i iloi.
Ɔsore wũ ɔbɔ iyo ɔba ɔ̃akpere ɔ̃ mala gu magbamikui ɔɣere ma sɔ, ‘So ɔɣɔ me gbaã alasɔ lonya wũ sɛrɛ gɔ loyu ne ɔso minagu me isoɣɔ!’ Nto loɣere mi sɔ ngbɔ ame i isoɣɔ siare aawe i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ɔɖuɖu i kpibaradze ɔwɛ̃ saã gɔ lofiniki i ɔ̃ ɔtu ame ɔso iɖo maturi kasiwɛ̃-kaiwɛ̃ ma loinya ifiniki ne.
Yesu Ɔpɛ Igbã I Sikãfudza Ibi Nɛ Loyu Iso.
“Si ɔrɔ̃go ba sikãfudza abi aweo fiɛ ɔyura iwɛ̃ ne, be mifɔ miɖe sɔ ɔ̃abara?
Ɔ̃atsue ɔkaniɛ ɔfiɛ ɔ̃ iyo ɔɖuɖu ame ɔnyɔnyɔ siyokã ɔɖuɖu ame gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ ɔ̃anya ne.
Fiɛ si ɔnya ne ne, ɔto ɔ̃akpere ɔ̃ mala gu magbamikui ɔsirakanya ɔɣere ma sɔ, ‘So ɔɣɔ me gbaã alasɔ lonya wũ sikã ibi nɛ loyu ne ɔso minagu me isoɣɔ.’ Nto loɣere mi sɔ gbaã ne, ngbɔ ame i Ɣaa makpabo ana aana isoɣɔ i kpibaradze ɔwɛ̃ saã gɔ lofiniki ɔso ne.” Ɔbirɛrɛĩ Gɔ Loyu Fiɛ Ɔledza Ikpese Iba Ɔ̃ Ɔse Kɔrɛ.
Yesu ɔkɛlɛgu i katɔ̃ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɔwe mabirɛrɛĩ inyɔ.
Kosore ɔba ɔ̃atu ɔ̃ ɔse ɔɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Tete, su wũ kaɖekɔ̃ ga loaɣo me si akpi tã me kiniɔ.’ Ne ɔso ɔ̃ ɔse ɔɣɛ ɔ̃ ara ɔtã mabi ma inyɔɔ.
“Ayi arɛ̃saã kama ne, kosore ɔsu ɔ̃ ara wa loɣo wũ ɔɖuɖu ɔrɔdɛ̃ ɔfɔ sikã ɔpia i ɔkoto ame ɔrui ɔkɛlɛ karɔ̃ dzoroa kawɛ̃ iso ngbegɔ ɔsɛ ɔ̃asɛ ngbã nyanyarĩa ɔnina ɔ̃ sikã ɔɖuɖu.
Ɔwi gɔ ɔ̃ɔnina ira biara nɛ ɔba ɔro kama ne, kukã siare kuwɛ̃ ɔbo i karɔ̃ gamɔ ɔɖuɖu iso gɔ itã sɔ kukã ɔkpɛ̃ wũ gbaã.
Ne ɔso ɔsu so ɔsɛ ɔ̃atã karɔ̃ gamɔ iso ɔturi ɔwɛ̃ sɔ ɔ̃abara karabara igbã biara ga ɔ̃atã wũ.
Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔmɔ ɔsese wũ sɔ ɔsɛ ɔ̃anyɔ ɔ̃ makparako iso i akorowa awɛ̃.
Kukã ɔso ne, ɔbie sɔ si ɔna makparako aɖera wa ɔto ɔtã ma ne, tee ɔ̃aɖe fiɛ ɣɛɛ kuwɛ̃ iitã wũ.
“Kawirikɔ̃ ne, ɔledza ikpese ibo so ame ɔɣere so sɔ, ‘Wũ ɔse maɖabo ma nsɛ mabara ɔ̃ karabara kɔra ne, masɛ mana aɖera maɖe mami akuti.
Ne mme losi ngbe kukã to kuɖoe me ne!
Loata lokɛlɛ tete kɔrɛ losɛ loaɣere wũ sɔ, “Tete, lobara ikpi, loɣɛrɛ ɔ gu Ɣaa.
Loisikote sɔ aakpere me sɔ fɔ ɔbi.
Ɣɛɛ su me bara lɛ fɔ maɖabo ma nsɛ mabara fɔ karabara ndɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃.” ’ Ne ɔta ɔmala ɔ̃ ara ɔɣo ɔ̃ ɔse kɔrɛ ɔri ne.
“Gɔ ɔsɛ dzoroo ne, ɔ̃ ɔse ɔnya wũ ɔɖi ite sɔ ɔ̃ ɔbi ɔɖe nto ɔba.
Ɔ̃ ara ɔɖo wũ kayiri ne ɔtere ɔsɛ ɔ̃ɔmini wũ ku isoɣɔ ne.
“Mmɔ i ɔbi gɔgbe ɔɣere ɔ̃ ɔse sɔ, ‘Tete, lobara ikpi i Ɣaa gu fɔ iso.
Loisikote sɔ aakpere me sɔ fɔ ɔbi.’ “Ɣɛɛ ne, ɔ̃ ɔse ɔkpere ɔ̃ maɖabo ɔɣere ma sɔ, ‘Mipɛ siwa si miɖi ara sɛɛ mipia wũ.
Mipia wũ inyi si misu ndokota sɛɛ ana miba miapia wũ.
Ne kama ne, misɛ mianyɔ nantsuĩ gɔ loɔbo iɖa miɖoe si boba boaɖe iyi.
Alasɔ wũ ɔbi gɔgbe ne, bosu wũ sɔ ɔ̃ɔkpi ɣɛɛ ɔkpese ɔba ngbã.
Ɔyu fiɛ boledza wũ inya ana.’ Ne ɔso matsɛ iyi iɖe.
“Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, ɔbi kpakpare ɔ̃ wũ ɔkpa iputu ame.
Gɔ ɔsɛ ɔto ɔba fiɛ ɔ̃ɔbore ɔbo iyo ne, ɔtsɛ aka gu katɔ kulu inɔ iyo ame.
Ne ɔkpere ɔɖabo ɔwɛ̃ ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, ‘Be nto ikɛlɛ i katɔ̃ i iyo ame?’ “Ɔɖabo ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, ‘Fɔ ɔnyiibi loɔkpese ɔba kaa.
Ne ɔso i fɔ ɔse ɔtã maɖoe nantsuĩ gɔ mba iɖa alasɔ ɔ̃iɣe sɔ ɔ̃akpese ɔnya wũ ɔnyɔa.’ “Nnɛgbe ɔtã sɔ sikpã ɔmɔɛ̃ ɔbirɛrɛĩ kpakpare gbaã ne ɔso ɔsɛ̃ sɔ ɔ̃ito ɔkɛlɛ iyo.
Ne ɔ̃ ɔse ɔbɔrɛ ɔkɛlɛ ɔ̃ kɔrɛ i inyamɔ ɔsɛ ɔ̃atã wũ iti sɔ ɔrui ɔba iyo.
Ɣɛɛ ɔbi ɔfiniki ɔkarɛ ɔ̃ ɔse sɔ, ‘Be ɔso i mme gɔ mme nto lobara-ɔ karabara akɔ gbodzoo nɖe nwagbe lɛ fɔ ɔɖabo fiɛ loibara kuira lota loya-ɔ iso ne, aitã me nane katepuĩ sɔ bo gu wũ malaa si bosu bopia so isoɣɔ?
Ɣɛɛ gɔ fɔ ɔbi gɔ lonina fɔ karana ɔsɛ̃ ɔ̃asu ɔsiai marɔ̃go ɔbara ara nyanyarĩa ɔkpese ɔba ɔmagɛ̃ ame ne, aɖoe bɔi gɔ mba iɖa atã wũ.’ “Mmɔ i ɔ̃ ɔse to ɔɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Wũ ɔbi, fɔ ne, bo gu-ɔ mpia ngbe ɔwi biara fiɛ wũ ira biara ne, fɔ ire iɖe.
Ɣɛɛ ne, ikote sɔ boaɖe iyi, bona isoɣɔ alasɔ fɔ ɔnyibi gɔgbe ne, bosu sɔ ɔkpi ɣɛɛ ɔkpese ɔba ngbã.
Ɔyu fiɛ boledza wũ inya.’ ”
Ara Nyɔisose Ɔwɛ̃ Gɔ Loibara Ara I Ɔri Iso.
Yesu ɔɣere ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Ɔwi ɔwɛ̃ ame ne, ranase ɔwɛ̃ ɔwe gɔ ɔba ɔɖabo gɔ nsɛ ɔnyɔ ɔ̃ ara iso.
Maba maaɣere ranase gɔgbe sɔ ɔɖabo gɔ nto ɔnyɔ ɔ̃ ara iso to ɔnina wũ sikã.
Ne ɔso ranase ɔkpere ɔ̃ ɔɖabo gɔgbe ɔɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Be iɖe nto lonɔ i fɔ iso ngbe?
Wũ ara wa ɔɖuɖu ato anyɔ iso ne, su siko bɔ si boki i ara ame alasɔ aisibawo wũ ara ɔnyɔ iso ita i kiniɔ.’ “Mmɔ i ɔɖabo gɔgbe to ɔɣere so sɔ, ‘Wũ ɔkɔse ka ɔfɔ me karabara iso.
Be loala loɔbara?
Lona ɔle gɔ loakpɛ̃.
Ara iwanyi ana to iakpɛ̃ me kunuarɛ.
Ɛɣɛɛ̃!
Loɣe nnɛ loabara fiɛ si wũ karabara ɔbɔrɛ me i nrɔɔ̃ ame ne, wũ malaa aafɔ me manyɔ me iso i ma ayo.’ “Ne ɔso ɔkpere mma ɔɖuɖu nto ɔ̃ ɔkɔse kuso ɔwɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃.
Ɔkarɛ ɔɖeakatɔ̃ sɔ ‘Nda ato wũ ɔkɔse?’ “Ne ngɔmɔ ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, ‘Nnɔĩ akuku siare kulafa.’ “Ne ɔɖabo gɔgbe ɔɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Su fɔ kuso gɔ ato ɔko bɔ.
Sɛ i karɔ̃ si atsɛrɛ sɔ akuku siru kere loɔkuti aatã.’ “Ngbɔ ame ɔkpere ɔmama ana gɔ nto ma kuso sɔ, ‘Fɔ ɣɛɛ?
Nda kuso ato?’ “Sose gɔmɔ ɔ̃ wũ ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Loto atita sikoto kulafa kuso.’ “Ne ɔɖabo gɔgbe ɔɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Su fɔ ɔko gɔ ame botsɛrɛ fɔ kuso bopia bɔ si atsɛrɛ fasinafasina apia.’ “Nnɛgbe ɔso ne, ɔkɔse gɔgbe ɔle ɔ̃ ɔɖabo gɔ nna ɔnukuare ngbe ala ɔ̃ inɔgba i kayu siri dzɛ iso ɔkigu wũ ɔso.
Gbaã ne, mma nsi ngbã matã kayi gagbe ara ne, masu ma anɔ masia nnɛ mato mabara iso kɔra maɖo mma nto mabara Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ karabara.” Ne Yesu ɔkɛlɛgu i katɔ̃ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Misu mi kayiiso karana mibuai maturi.
Iyɔ si kaba kaaro ne, Ɣaa aafɔ mi ɔpia i ɔ̃ kasɛkɔ̃.
“Ɔbiara gɔ nsɛ ɔmɔɛ̃ ara wiriwiria ɔla i ɔnukuare ame ne, maatã wũ ɔri i ara siare ana iso.
Ɔbiara gɔ loisɛ ɔɖe ɔnukuare i ara wiriwiria ame ne, ɔ̃ibaɖe ɔnukuare i ara siare ana iso.
Ne ɔso si miimɔɛ̃ kayiiso karana mila i ɔnukuare ame ne, nda maabara fiɛ mafɔ mi maɖe i siwarã ara wa i Ɣaa sɛ ɔtã iso?
Fiɛ si aiɖe ɔnukuare i ara wa nɖe ɔturi mama are iso ne, nda iabara fiɛ maasu fɔ mɔmɔ are matã-ɔ?
“Ɔɖabo kuwɛ̃ iibawo makɔse inyɔ ɔsumu.
Si iiɖe ngbɔ ne, ɔto ɔ̃aɖɔɛ ɔwɛ̃ ɔtsiri ɔwɛ̃.
Ɣee ɔ̃awarɛ ɔwɛ̃ ɔta ɔya ɔwɛ̃ iso.
Miibawo Ɣaa gu karana ɔsɔrɛ.” Yesu Ɔte Ara Mama Ana.
Gɔ ma Farisise ɔnɔ ara wa i Yesu ɔɣɛ ne, mabara wũ aɣiãra alasɔ masɛ maɖɔɛ sikã gbaã.
Mmɔ i Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Miɖe maturi ma nsɛ mate so lɛ masɛɛ i maturi anɔ.
Ɣɛɛ Ɣaa ɣe mi situ ɔɖuɖu ame.
Alasɔ ara wa lofɔ kuɣa i maturi anɔ ne, anyanyara aɖe i Ɣaa anɔ.
“Mose mmara ɔko gu Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze ara wa matsɛrɛ masɛ ne, abara wã karabara isɛ iabo Ndupiedze Yohanes ɔwi.
Ita i ɔwi gɔmɔ ne, minɔ sɔ mato maɣɛ Itɔ̃me Bielea i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ iso.
Fiɛ ɔbiara to ɔkpɛ̃ sɔ ɔ̃ana ɔri ɔbo i mmɔ.
Ɣɛɛ ne, ise pɔkɔsɔɔ sɔ kato gu karɔ̃ aawã iɖo sɔ maakpasera mmara kakpoi kosoi tsɔra maɖi.
“Ɔrɛrɛ̃ biara gɔ losɛ̃ ɔ̃ ɔre fiɛ ɔyiri ɔmama ne, marɔ̃go rɔdze ɔɖe.
Fiɛ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ loyiri ɔrɔ̃go gɔ masɛ̃ ne, ɔsiai ɔturire.
Yesu Ɔɣɛ Ranase Ɔwɛ̃ Gu Lazaro Iso Itɔ̃me.
“Ɔrɛrɛ̃ ranase ɔwɛ̃ gɔ nsɛ ɔpia ara wa lofɔ kuɣa fiɛ ɔwe i isoɣɔ ame i ɔ̃ ngba ayi ɔɖuɖu ame ɔwe.
Wɛrɛba ɔwɛ̃ ana gɔ marɔ sɔ Lazaro ɔwe.
Aɣɛi ɔkã ɔ̃ iso ɔɖuɖu fiɛ masɛ masu wũ maasɛ i ranase gɔmɔ kayogodɔ̃.
Ɔsɛ ɔnyɔ ɔri sɔ si ranase gɔmɔ to ɔɖe ara ne, kupupui gɔ nsɛ kukpakpase i mmɔ aaɣo wũ ɔɖe.
Ta makpɛkpɛ sɛ maba maaɣaɣa ɔ̃ aɣɛi ame.
“Wɛrɛba gɔgbe ɔba ɔ̃akpi, ne Ɣaa makpabo ɔba maasore wũ makɛlɛgu Abraham kɔrɛ i kato ne.
Ranase gɔmɔ ana ɔba ɔ̃akpi ne mabiara wũ ne.
I makpise aɖe ne, ranase ɔwe i inyɛwe ame.
Ne gɔ ɔkɔlɛ anɔ kato ne, ɔnya Abraham i kato gɔ Lazaro si wũ i kɔrɛ.
Mmɔ ɔto ɔkpere sɔ, ‘Tete Abraham!
Nyɔ me nnya si atã Lazaro si ɔsu ɔ̃ irɔi ɔpia i ndu ame ɔba ɔ̃asora ɔɣora me i ɔnyagɛmi iso si ibara me pɔkɔsɔɔ alasɔ nto lona ibo i ɔtɔ gɔgbe ame!’ “Ɣɛɛ Abraham ɔɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Wũ ɔbi, nyigi sɔ i fɔ ngbã ame ne, afɔ fɔ ara sɛɛ ɔɖuɖu.
Fiɛ Lazaro ɔ̃ wũ ne, ara nyanyarĩa kerekere ɔfɔ.
Ɣɛɛ kiniɔ ne, ka ɔto ɔna isoɣɔ fiɛ fɔ wũ ato awe inyɛ.
Ne kama ana ne, kuwɛ titiiti kuwɛ̃ pia i bo gu-ɔ inyɔ ndɛ̃.
Si ɔturi ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃awara ɔba mmɔ ne, ɔ̃ibawo.
Ngbɔ ame i kuwɛ̃ iibawo mi kɔrɛ mmɔ ana ɔbɔrɛ ɔba ngbe ne.’ “Mmɔ i ranase gɔmɔ to ɔɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Tete Abraham, loto-ɔ i kukpa sɔ pia Lazaro si ɔsɛ wũ ɔse iyo.
Loba manyiibi rɛrɛ̃ iru ma mpia ngbã.
Tã ɔsɛ ɔ̃aka ma teteree sɔ madaaba ngbe ne inyɛwe ɔɣede.’ “Ne Abraham to ɔɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Fɔ manyiibi ba ara wa i Mose gu Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze ɔtsɛrɛ masɛ.
Ikote sɔ maakã ara wamɔ atsue mabara i wã iso!’ “Mmɔ i ranase to ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Tete Abraham, maibakã itɔ̃me nɛmɔ atsue.
Ɣɛɛ si ɔturi ɔbɔrɛ i makpise ame ɔsɛ ɔ̃aɣere ma ne, mato maakã wũ atsue mafiniki i ma akpi ibara ame.’ “Ɣɛɛ Abraham ɔɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Si maibakã Mose gu Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze itɔ̃me atsue ne, si ɔturi ɔta ɔbɔrɛ i makpise ame ngbe ɔkɛlɛ ma kɔrɛ kɔra ne, maibakã wũ atsue!’ ”
Daatã Sɔ Ɔturi Abara Ikpi Ala Fɔ Ɔso.
Yesu ɔɣere ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Ara wa loatã ɔturi ɔbara ikpi to aaba, ɣɛɛ ne, ndzo miɖe mitã ngɔ iso aaki fiɛ aaba.
Si masu kukɔtɛ siare manyi masarã wũ i ɔme fiɛ mafuĩdza wũ mapia i ɔpo ame kɔra ne, ialɛ wũ iɖo kutsue gɔ i Ɣaa aakpadzɛ̃ ngɔ loatã mabiɛtɛ magbe ɔbo i ikpi ame.
Ne ɔso minyɔ so kukaakɔ nnɛ mito mibara.
“Si fɔ ɔnyii ɔbara-ɔ ikpi ne, sɛ̃ tã wũ.
Si ɔfiniki ne, su tsɛ wũ.
Si ɔɣɛrɛ-ɔ ikpɛ ikɔdzɛ i ikpɛnɛ iwɛ̃ ame fiɛ ɔkpese ɔba ɔ̃atã-ɔ iti ikpɛ ikɔdzɛ ɔɖuɖu ne, su tsɛ wũ.” Matã Yesu Iti Sɔ Ɔtã Ma Kafɔkaɖe Si Kamɔ Kabua.
Yesu katɔ̃memasɛdze ɔtã wũ iti sɔ, “Bokɔse, tã sɔ bo kafɔkaɖe aamɔ kabua.” Ne Bokɔse ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Si mi kafɔkaɖe ɔmɔ lɛ susuruba ibi ne, miaɣere kudziri gɔgbe sɔ, ‘Rui ngbe kɛlɛ ɔpo ame.’ Fiɛ iaba ngbɔ ana.
Yesu Ɔɣɛ Kumɛgɔ I Ɔɖabo Sɛɛ Sɛ Ɔbara Karabara.
“Mibu nnɛgbe minyɔ.
Si mi ndɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ba ɔɖabo gɔ nto ɔkpɛ̃ ɔtã-ɔ ɣee ɔto ɔnyɔ fɔ mabɔi iso fiɛ ɔse i sia ɔba ɔ̃abo ne, aaɣere wũ sɔ ɔba ɔ̃asɛ i karɔ̃ mala si ɔɖe ɔ̃ araɖea?
Ooɣo!
Ɣɛɛ ɔɣere aaɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Ledza so si asɛ̃ ɔkati ndɛ̃ si awa aɖera atã me.
Si loɔɖe lonɛ loro ne, fɔ wũ aaɖe anɛ fɔ are.’ Iinya sɔ aapɛ ɔɖabo siba i ɔ̃ Karabara iti.
Ngbɔ ame ise itã mi ana ne.
Si mibara ira biara nɛ loɣere mi sɔ mibara ne, miɣɛ sɔ, ‘Maɖabo kere boɖe fiɛ nnɛ lokote sɔ boabara kere iɖe bobara.’ ” Yesu Ɔsa Marɛrɛ̃ Iweo Mawɛ̃ Ma Nto Manyɛ Ɔnyɛ Rɛtɛa.
Gɔ Yesu ɔɣo Yerusalem ɔri ne, ɔki i Samaria gu Galilea kumɛ iso.
Ne gɔ ɔto ɔba ɔ̃abo akorowa awɛ̃ ame ne, marɛrɛ̃ iweo mawɛ̃ ma nto manyɛ ɔnyɛ rɛtɛa ɔba matu wũ.
Manyɛse magbe ɔya dzoroo, ne mala kulu teteree sɔ, “Tete Yesu, nyɔ bo nnya!” Gɔ Yesu ɔnya ma ne, ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mikɛlɛ maisu so mite Ɣaa Masɔrɛdze si manyɔ mi kukaakɔ.” Gɔ marui mato makɛlɛ ne, manya sɔ maɔna isosarɛ.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ ma ndɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɔnya sɔ ɔ̃ɔna isosarɛ ne, ɔpɛ ɔfiniki ɔto ɔle Ɣaa ku silɔ teteree.
Ɔba ɔ̃apɛ agɛgɛ̃ i Yesu katɔ̃ ɔpɛ wũ siba.
Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ne, ɔ Samariase ɔɖe.
Mmɔ i Yesu to ɔkarɛ sɔ, “Iiɖe mi maturi iweo miɖe losa ɣɛɛ?
Kaiwɛ̃ tsɔra ne lɛ maki?
Nda ibara fiɛ ɔfɔ gɔ loiɖe ɔ Yudase ɔnɔwɛ̃ loakpese ɔba ɔ̃apɛ Ɣaa siba?” Mmɔ i Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ta ya si akɛlɛ.
Fɔ kafɔkaɖe ɔtã-ɔ isosarɛ.” Yesu Ɔte Kumɛgɔ I Ɣaa Sigara Iɖe Aaba.
Ma Farisise mawɛ̃ ɔkarɛ Yesu sɔ mabie sɔ maatsue ɔwi gɔ tutuutu i Ɣaa sigara ɔɖewi aaba.
Ne Yesu to ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Ɣaa sigara iɖe iibaba i ɔri gɔ iso i maturi aanya.
Kuwɛ̃ iibaɣɛ sɔ, ‘Minyɔ!
Iɔba ngbe!’ ɣee ‘Nyɔ mmɔ.’ Alasɔ Ɣaa sigara iɖe ka ipia i mi ndɛ̃.” Ne Yesu to ɔɣere ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Ɔwi to ɔba gɔ miabie sɔ mianya mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, iyi iwɛ̃, ɣɛɛ miibanya!
Maturi to maaba maaɣere mi sɔ ‘Minyɔ wũ i mmɔ!’ ɣee ‘Minyɔ wũ i ngbe!’ Ɣɛɛ midaasɛ mianyɔnyɔ me i mmɔ!
Alasɔ lɛ kumɛgɔ i kado sɛ ɔma i kato kasɛ kawɛ̃ isɛ iabo kasɛ nyɔa ne, ngbɔ i Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi iyi nɛmɔ to iase ne.
Ɣɛɛ tɔtɔ ne, ikote sɔ loaki i inyɛwe gbodzoo ame kiniɔgbe maturi ɔsɛ̃ me.
“Ara wa loba ku Noa ɔwi ne, wã ame loaba ku ɔwi gɔ ame i Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi aaledza iba ne.
Maturi to maɖe manɛ, marɛrɛ̃ to mayiri marɔ̃go fiɛ mato masu marɔ̃go matã sɔ mayiri gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ iyi nɛ i Noa ɔbo i ɔkolo siare gɔmɔ ame.
Kado ɔpɛ, siwore ɔyi si fɔ karɔ̃, ndu ɔɖoe maturi ɔɖuɖu.
“Ito iase lɛ kumɛgɔ i Lot ɔwi ɔse awe.
Maturi to ɔɖe gu ɔnɛ mato maɖe kuɣa ana.
Mawɛ̃ to mapia ɔraɖui mma to matsue ayo.
Iyi nɛ i Lot ɔbɔrɛ i Sodom ne, ɔtɔ gu akaĩ wa nsɛ afɔrɛ̃ nyanyarĩ ɔpɛ abɔrɛ i kato afere ɔmagɛ̃ iso, ma ɔɖuɖu ɔtsue.
“Ngbɔ ame iase ku iyi nɛ mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, aaba ne.
Iyi nɛmɔ ne, ngɔ nsia i ɔ̃ isã si ɔdaaso ɔba karɔ̃ sɔ ɔto ɔba ɔ̃abo iyo kame ɔsu ɔ̃ kuira.
Ngbɔ ame ngɔ nɣɛ i sia si ɔdaaɣɛ sɔ ɔ̃akpese ɔsɛ kaa ɔ̃asu kuira ne.
Minyigi nnɛ lobara Lot ɔre!
Ɔbiara gɔ loakpɛ̃ sɔ si ɔ̃aɖi ɔ̃ ngbã ne, ɔto ɔ̃ayura me.
Ɣɛɛ ɔbiara gɔ loayura ɔ̃ ngbã to ɔ̃aledza me ina.
Kasɛ̃ gamɔ ne, maturi inyɔ to maarɛ i ara iso.
Ɣaa to ɔ̃akɔ ɔwɛ̃ ɔnyua ɔwɛ̃ ɔrara.
Marɔ̃go inyɔ to maala maɔkɔtɛ ɔraũ i kukɔtɛ iso Ɣaa to ɔ̃akɔ ɔwɛ̃, ɔnyua ɔwɛ̃ ɔsɛ.
Marɛrɛ̃ inyɔ to maaya mala maɔbara karabara, Ɣaa to ɔ̃akɔ ɔwɛ̃ ɔnyua ɔwɛ̃ ɔɣedza.” Ne marasuãdze to makarɛ Yesu sɔ, “Bokɔse, lɛ isɛ?” Ne Yesu to ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ngbegɔ i ira kpia se ne, mmɔ i akolomo sɛ asakanya ne.”
Yesu Ɔpɛ Igbã I Atɔ̃meɣɛdze Lalaa Gu Kuɛdze Ɔwɛ̃ Iso.
Yesu ɔpɛ ɔ̃ marasuãdze igbã si ɔte ma sɔ inya sɔ maakparama kayi ɔwi biara fiɛ nrɔɔ̃ iibafɛ̃ ma.
Ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Atɔ̃meɣɛdze ɔwɛ̃ ɔwe i ɔmagɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ame gɔ loisɛ ɔnigã Ɣaa fiɛ ɔ̃isɛ ɔwarɛ ɔturi ana.
Ɔmagɛ̃ gɔmɔ ame ame ne, kuɛdze ɔwɛ̃ pia gɔ ɔsɛ ɔba atɔ̃meɣɛdze kɔrɛ ɔba ɔ̃atã wũ iti sɔ, ‘Buai me ala wũ matsirise ɔso.’ “Ifɔ ɔwi gbodzoo gɔ atɔ̃meɣɛdze gɔgbe ɔsɛ̃ sɔ ɔ̃ito ɔbara kuira i itɔ̃me nɛmɔ iso.
Ɣɛɛ kawirikɔ̃ ne, ɔɣere so sɔ, ‘Atoa sɔ loito lonigã Ɣaa fiɛ loisɛ lowarɛ ɔturi ne, Kumɛgɔ i kuɛdze gɔgbe to ɔɖaa me ɔso ne, loanyɔ sɔ lokpɛ̃ lofɔ wũ i ɔ̃ tsirise nrɔɔ̃ ame.
Si iiɖe ngbɔ ne, ɔto ɔ̃amararã me ɔɖoe.’ ” Ne Bosate ɔkɛlɛ i katɔ̃ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Minɔ nnɛ i atɔ̃meɣɛdze lalaa gɔgbe to ɔɣɛ.
Kiniɔ ne, Ɣaa gɔ nɖe atɔ̃meɣɛdze i ɔri bɔlɔlɔa iso ne, ɔ̃ibaɖi ɔ̃ maturi ma nsɛ mabiɛ makpere wũ kasɛ̃ i kakɔme?
Ɣaa iibaɣɛ itɔ̃me ɔtã ɔ̃ maturi ma nto mabiɛ makpere wũ kasɛ̃ i kakɔme?
Nto loɣere mi gbaã sɔ Ɣaa to ɔ̃aɣɛ ma itɔ̃me ɔtã ma ibɛ i ɔwi iso.
Ɣɛɛ ne, si Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi ɔba ne, ɔ̃anya maturi ma mba kafɔkaɖe?” Yesu Ɔpɛ Igbã I Ɔ Farisise Ɔwɛ̃ Gu Lampofɔdze Ɔwɛ̃ Iso.
Yesu ɔpɛ igbã nɛgbe i maturi ma nsɛ mabu so sɔ ma ɔnɔwɛ̃ nlɛ fiɛ masɛ manyɔ maturi tsɔra pupurii iso.
Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ɔwi ɔwɛ̃ ame ne, maturi inyɔ mawɛ̃ ɔsɛ Ɣaa isɔrɛyo sɔ maakparama kayi.
Ɔwɛ̃ ɖe ɔ Farisise fiɛ ɔwɛ̃ ana ɖe lampofɔdze.
Farisise ɔkpɛ so ɔɣedza i kuruɛ ne ɔkparama kayi ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Ɣaa nto lopɛ-ɔ siba sɔ lona kanɔbɛbɛ, loisɛ lobara maturi akpi fiɛ loisɛ losiai maturire lɛ maturi mama awe.
Nto lopɛ-ɔ siba ana alasɔ loise lɛ lampofɔdze gɔgbe awe.
Nsɛ lonyi kanya akpɛnɛ anyɔ i ɖapɛ ame fiɛ nsɛ lotã-ɔ wũ ira ɔɖuɖu ika weova.’ “Ɣɛɛ lampofɔdze ɔ̃ wũ ɔya dzoroo gɔ ɔ̃ibie sɔ ɔ̃akɔlɛ ɔ̃ iti kato kɔra.
Ɣɛɛ ɔsu nrɔɔ̃ ɔfu so igbegbe, ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Ɣaa nyɔ me gɔ nɖe kpibaradze nnya!’ ” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Nto loɣere mi sɔ gɔ ma inyɔɔ ɔkpese makɛlɛ ma ayo ne, lampofɔdze ɔbo Ɣaa anɔ ɔɖo ɔ Farisise.
Alasɔ ɔturi biara gɔ nsɛ ɔkɔlɛ so kato ne, Ɣaa to ɔ̃abɔ wũ karɔ̃.
Fiɛ ɔturi biara gɔ nsɛ ɔbɔ so karɔ̃ ne, Ɣaa to ɔ̃akɔlɛ wũ kato.” Yesu Sɛ Ɔɖɔɛ Mabiɛtɛ Gbaã.
Mawɛ̃ ɔkɔ ma mabi mabɔ Yesu sɔ ɔsia ma kɔrɔ̃ iso.
Gɔ Yesu katɔ̃memasɛdze ɔnya nnɛgbe ne, manyagalagu maturi mamɔ.
Ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔkpere mabiɛtɛ ɔbɔ so i kɔrɛ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mitã mabiɛtɛ si maba wũ kɔrɛ ne midaatɛ̃ ma ɔri, alasɔ Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ se sitã ma igbã.
Gbagbaã nto loɣere mi sɔ, ɔbiara gɔ loifɔ Ɣaa sigara iɖe lɛ ɔbiɛtɛ awe ne, ɔ̃ibawo sɛ̃ ame ɔkɛlɛ ɖa.” Yesu Ɔɣɛ Ara I Maranase Gu Ɣaa Sigarakaɖekɔ̃ Iso.
Ma Yudase tɔ̃ɖedze ɔwɛ̃ ɔkarɛ Yesu sɔ, “Ratedze bielea, be loabara fiɛ loana ngbã mɛ loisɛ miro minya?” Ne Yesu ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Be ɔso fiɛ ato akpere me Ɔbielea?
Ɔturi kuwɛ̃ iiɖe ɔbielea iɖo Ɣaa ɔnɔwɛ̃.
Aɣe Ɣaa mmara mɛ loɣɛ sɔ, ‘Daaɖoe ɔturi, daaɖe asɔrɔ̃, daayu kayu daaɖaɛ fɔ ɔlaa kanya, warɛ fɔ ɔse gu fɔ ɔnyi.’ ” Mmɔ i ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔmɔ to ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Ita i wũ sibiɛtɛ ame ne, loɔbara i mmara mɛgbe ɔɖuɖu iso.” Gɔ Yesu ɔnɔ nnɛ ɔɣɛ ne, ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ikuti-ɔ ira ka iwɛ̃ aabara.
Kɛlɛ aasu fɔ ira biara rɔdɛ̃ si asu sikã atsɛ mawɛrɛba, si aana kusia siare i kato.
Si ɔɔro ne, kpese ba siai me.” Ɣɛɛ gɔ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ɔnɔ nnɛgbe ne, ɔruigu isoma alasɔ ɔba karana gbaã.
Gɔ Yesu ɔnya kumɛgɔ i so ɔma wũ ne, ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Ito iabua iɖa fiɛ ranase aabo i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃!
Gbaã ne, ma mmɔ ibo ba ɔle iɖo kumɛgɔ i kapuipɔngɔ aaki kafe i ɔdzirikaãra iyoi ame.” Mma lonɔ itɔ̃me nɛgbe ɔkarɛ Yesu sɔ, “Iyɔ nna loabua ɔna iɖi?” Ne ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Ira nɛ i ɔturi iibawo ɔbara ne, Ɣaa aawo ɔbara.” Ne Petro ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Nyɔ, iyɔ bo ma lonyua bo ara ɔɖuɖu bosɛ bosiai-ɔ ɣɛɛ?” Ne Yesu to ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Gbagbaã iɖe.
Fiɛ lobie sɔ mitsue sɔ ɔturi biara gɔ lonyua ɔ̃ iyo gu ɔ̃ ɔre, ɔ̃ ɔnyiibi rɛrɛ̃ gu ɔ̃ ɔnyiibi rɔ̃go gu ɔ̃ maɣese, ɣee mabi ɔsɛ ala Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ɔso ne, ɔto ɔ̃ana ara wagbe gbodzoo i ngbã mɛgbe ame gu ngbã mɛ loisɛ miro minya i ɔwi gɔ nto ɔba i katɔ̃ ame ana.” Yesu Ɔledza Ika Iɖe Ɔkpɛ Tɛare I Ɔ̃ Kukpi Iso.
Yesu ɔkɔ ɔ̃ marasuãdze iweo-inyɔ ɔkɛlɛgu kuruɛ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mikã atsue.
Boto bokɛlɛ Yerusalem ngbegɔ i ara wa i Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze ɔtsɛrɛ masɛ i mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, iso ɔɖuɖu aaba i ne ame.
Mato maaɖi me matã mma loiɖe ma Yudase sɔ mabara me aɣiãra.
Mato maatia me, matua minyatu mafere me iso.
Mato maapɛ me fiɛ maaɖoe me.
Ɣɛɛ akpɛnɛ atɛ kama ne, loata lobɔrɛ i makpise ame.” Ɣɛɛ ara wagbe ɔɖuɖu ne, marasuãdze iinɔ wã karɔ̃.
Atɔ̃me wagbe karɔ̃ inɔ ana ɔwɛrɛ ma.
Maiɣe nnɛ i Yesu ɔɣere ma ngbe karɔ̃.
Yesu Ɔsa Nɔbiɛdze Ɔwɛ̃ Gɔ Nsɛ Ɔwanyi Ara.
Ɔwi gɔ i Yesu ka ɔto ɔbore ɔbo Yeriko ne, nɔbiɛdze ɔwɛ̃ si i ɔri kuruɛ ɔto ɔwanyi ara.
Gɔ ɔnɔ maturi gbodzoo to mafe ne, ɔkarɛ sɔ, “Be nto iba?” Ne mato maɣere wũ sɔ, “Yesu Nasaretse nto ɔfe.” Mmɔ ɔsia kulu teteree sɔ, “Yesu!
Igara David Ɔbi!
Nyɔ me nnya!” Maturi ma nɖe katɔ̃ ɔnyagalagu wũ sɔ ɔlo kulu.
Ɣɛɛ ɔkɔlɛ ɔ̃ silɔ ɔbua ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Igara David Ɔbi!
Nyɔ me nnya soo!” Ne ɔso Yesu ɔtui ɔya ne ɔɣɛ sɔ makɔ nɔbiɛdze mabɔ ɔ̃ kɔrɛ.
Gɔ ɔba ɔ̃abo ɔ̃ kɔrɛ ne, Bosate ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Be ato abiɛ sɔ lobara lotã-ɔ.” Nɔbiɛdze ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Tete, lobie sɔ loanya ara.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Nya ara!
Fɔ kafɔkaɖe losa-ɔ.” Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, ɔtsɛ ara inya, ɔsiai Yesu ɔto ɔle Ɣaa.
Maturi gbodzoo ma lonya nnɛgbe ne, ma ɔɖuɖu ɔle Ɣaa.
Yesu Ɔɖe Zakeo Ika.
Yesu ɔsɛ ɔ̃aki i Yeriko ɔmagɛ̃ ame ɔfe.
Ma lampofɔdze ɔkpakpa ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ sɔ Zakeo fiɛ ɔba karana gbaã ɔwe mmɔ.
Ɔto ɔbie ɔri gɔ iso ɔ̃aki fiɛ ɔ̃atsue ɔturi gɔ igbã i Yesu ɖe.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ ɔkurukutu fiɛ maturi ana ɔsi i ɔri ɔso ne, ɔ̃inya wũ.
Ne ɔso ɔtere ɔɖe ma katɔ̃ ɔsɛ ɔ̃aya ɔsia i kudziri ame sɔ ɔ̃anya Yesu ala ɔɣe sɔ ɔto ɔ̃aki i mmɔ.
Gɔ Yesu ɔbo kudziri kayirinɔ ne, ɔtui ɔya, ɔkɔlɛ anɔ kato ne ɔɣere Zakeo sɔ, “Zakeo, so ba mala, alasɔ fɔ iyo loabo nɔme.” Zakeo ɔso mala ɔba karɔ̃ ɔfɔ Yesu ku isoɣɔ.
Mma ɔɖuɖu lonya nnɛgbe ɔtsɛ Yesu iɣɛtɛ iɣɛ sɔ, “Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe to ɔkɛlɛ ɔ̃abo i kpibaradze iyo.” Mmɔ i Zakeo ɔta ɔya ne ɔɣere Bosate sɔ, “Tete!
Nyɔ, loasu wũ karana kasɛ kawɛ̃ lotã mawɛrɛba.
Mma ɔɖuɖu loɖe amumu lofɔ nnɛ loikote sɔ loafɔ ne, loakpesera ma ara lotã ma ikpɛ ina.” Ne Yesu ana to ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Nɔme ne, iɖi ɔba i iyo nɛgbe ame.
Alasɔ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ɔ̃ wũ ne, Abraham ɔwa tɛtɛ ɔɖe.
Fiɛ mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, ne, loba lonyɔnyɔ mma ɔɖuɖu loyu, loɖi ma.” Yesu Ɔpɛ Igbã I Sikãrɛtɛa Ibi Iso.
Maturi to makã ara wa i Yesu to ɔɣɛ atsue.
Ne ɔpɛ ma igbã nɛgbe alasɔ ka ɔbore ɔbo Yerusalem fiɛ mabu sɔ Ɣaa sigara ɔɖewi to ɔ̃aba kiniɔ.
Ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ɔwi ɔwɛ̃ ne, ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ nɖe ɔturi nyaa ɔkɛlɛ karɔ̃ dzoroa kawɛ̃ iso sɔ maamɔɛ̃ wũ sigara.
Si maɔro ne, ɔbara ɔ̃ adzuni sɔ ɔ̃akpese ɔba.
Si ɔ̃arui ne, ɔkpere ɔ̃ marabaradze iweo ɔsirakanya.
Ɔtã ma ɔbiara sikãrɛtɛa ibi iwɛ̃, ɔɣere ma sɔ, ‘Misu sikã dzɛgbe miɖe ala kuɣa si bonyɔ kusia gɔ miana si lona.’ “Ɣɛɛ ɔ̃ mɔmɔ aɖe maturi ɔtsiri wũ.
Ne ɔso mapia ma kpabo sɔ masiai wũ i kama si masɛ maaɣere igarakpakpa sɔ, ‘Boito bobie sɔ ngɔgbe aaɖe bo igara.’ “Ɣɛɛ gɔ masɛra wũ sigara maro ne, ɔkpese ɔba ɔ̃ aɖe.
Ɔpia sɔ marɔ ɔ̃ maɖabo ma ɔtã sikã mabɔ si maba maaɣɛ kusia gɔ maɔna.
“Ɔɖabo ɖeakatɔ̃ ɔba ɔ̃aya ne ɔɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Tete, sikã dzɛ atã me ne, loɔna sɛ̃ ikpɛ iweo losia iso.’ “Ne ɔ̃ ɔkɔse ɔɣere wũ sɔ ‘Ɖafe!
Ɔɖabo sɛɛ aɖe.
Gɔ awo ara kɛkɛĩ wagbe ɔsu ɔbara karabara ɔso ne, loasu-ɔ losɛra i simagɛ̃ iweo kanya.’ “Ɔɖabo nyɔare ɔ̃ wũ ɔba ɔ̃aɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Tete, lona sikã dzɛ atã me ikpɛ iru losia iso!’ “Ne ɔ̃ ɔkɔse ɔɣere ɔɖabo gɔgbe ɔ̃ wũ sɔ, ‘Fɔ ne, loasu-ɔ losɛra i simagɛ̃ iru kanya!’ “Ɔɖabo mama ɔ̃ wũ ɔba ɔ̃aɣɛ sɔ, ‘Tete, ɔɔnya fɔ sikã dzɛ atã me i ngbe.
Losu sɛ̃ lopɛ ikpo i wũ ɔkati ikpakpai ame.
Nto lonigã-ɔ alasɔ aba ɔle, asɛ asu ara wa loiɖe fɔ are sɔ fɔ are.
Ngbegɔ aikpɛ̃ ana ne, mmɔ asɛ asu fɔ araɖea ne.’ “Ne ɔ̃ ɔkɔse to ɔɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Ɔɖabo lalaa aɖe!
Fɔ mɔmɔ kanya ame atɔ̃me loasu lotã-ɔ ipɔ!
Aɣe sɔ ɔturi gɔ mba ɔle loɖe, fiɛ nsɛ losu nnɛ loiɖe wũ ire lokpesera wũ ire.
Nsɛ losu araɖea i ngbegɔ loipɛ ɔraɖui.
Gɔ aɣe ngbɔ ne, be ɔso fiɛ aisu wũ sikã asɛ aapia i sikã kakolakɔ̃?
Mmɔ ne, kumɛkumɛ iɖe ne, loɣe sɔ nto loana sɛ̃ gu kusia lofɔ.’ “Ne ɔɣere mma nɣɛ i mmɔ sɔ, ‘Mimɔɛ̃ ɔ̃ sikã mifɔ mitã ɔɖabo gɔ lona kusia ikpɛ iweo.’ “Ɣɛɛ maturi ma nɣɛ i mmɔ ɔɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Tete, ɔɖabo gɔmɔ ka ɔba sikã abi aweo koko!’ “Ne igara gɔmɔ ɔɣere ma sɔ, ‘Gbaã nto loɣere mi sɔ ngɔ mba ara ne, maatã wũ mabua.
Ɔbiara gɔ nna kuira ne, kɛkɛĩ gɔ ame ɔba ne, maamɔɛ̃ mafɔ wũ iso.
Kiniɔ ne, wũ matsirise ma loito mabie sɔ loɖe sigara ne, mibɔ ma i wũ katɔ̃ miba miaɖoe.’ ” Yesu Ɔbo Yerusalem.
Gɔ Yesu ɔɣere ma ara wagbe ɔro ne, ɔɖe ma katɔ̃ ɔɣo Yerusalem ɔri.
Ɔwi gɔ ɔ̃ɔbore ɔbo Betfage gu Betania i Nnɔĩ Adziri Kube kuruɛ ne, ɔpia ɔ̃ marasuãdze inyɔ sɔ maɖe katɔ̃.
Ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Misɛ kamagɛĩ ga i bo katɔ̃ ngbe ame.
Si mibo ne, mito mianya ɔfirimu ibi iwɛ̃ nɛ makɔra maɣedza fiɛ kuwɛ̃ iisɛ ne iso ɔnya.
Mikurisi ne mibɔ me ngbe.
Si ɔrere ɔkarɛ mi sɔ be ɔso mito mikurisi ne ne, miɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Bokɔse nto ɔbie ne.’ ” Gɔ marasuãdze magbe ɔrui maɣo ɔri ne, manya ira biara lɛ kumɛgɔ i Yesu ɔɣere ma awe.
Ɔwi gɔ mato makurisi bɔi ne, ɔ̃ masate ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Be ɔso mito mikurisi wũ?” Ne marasuãdze ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Bokɔse nto ɔbie wũ.” Makɔ ɔfirimu ibi mabɔ Yesu.
Mawarɛ ma sikati masia bɔi kama ne ka mabuai Yesu ɔta ɔsɛ iso ne.
Gɔ marui ne, mawɛ̃ ɔwarɛ ma sikati masɛ i ɔri sɔ ɔsɛ iso.
Ɔwi gɔ i Yesu ɔɔbore ɔbo Yerusalem ngbegɔ i ɔri ɔtsɛ iso i Nnɔĩ Adziri Kube iso ne, ɔ̃ marasuãdze gbodzoo ɔtsɛ Ɣaa siba ipɛ mato mafa kayiɖu teteree iki ɔ̃ ara siare wa manya ɔso.
Mato maɣɛ sɔ, “Ɣaa kusɛkusɛ itã igara gɔ nto ɔba i Bosate iyere ame!
Isobuɛ si iwe i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ɔɖuɖu!
Ɣaa ɔkpɛ nɖe ikpawaĩ!” Ne ma Farisise mawɛ̃ i maturi ndɛ̃ to maɣere Yesu sɔ, “Ratedze, sɛ̃ fɔ marasuãdze sɔ malo kulu!” Ne Yesu ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Gbaã nto loɣere mi sɔ si malo kulu ne, ata to aatsɛ kulu ila.” Yesu Ɔbiɛ I Yerusalem Iti.
Gɔ Yesu ɔbore ɔbo ɔmagɛ̃ fiɛ ɔnya wũ ɔsese ne, ɔbiɛ nnɔmɛ i ɔ̃ iti.
Ne ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Lobie sɔ tee gbaã ne, aatsue nɔme nnɛ lokotegu-ɔ fiɛ iatã-ɔ isobuɛ.
Ɣɛɛ ipɛ i kiniɔ ne, aito anya aɖi ite!
Ɔwi to ɔba gɔ fɔ matsirise to maaki malɔ-ɔ i kakɔi biara.
Mato maatɛ̃-ɔ mapia masɛ̃ kuyogodɔ̃ gɔ ɔɖuɖu ame aawo ɔki ɔbɔrɛ.
Mato maabiɛ ɔmagɛ̃ gɔgbe maɖoe maturi ma ɔɖuɖu mpia i ɔ̃ ame.
Maibanyua ita kuiwɛ̃ masɛ i ne kasɛkɔ̃.
Alasɔ asɛ̃ sɔ aibatsue ɔwi gɔ i Ɣaa ɔba sɔ ɔba ɔɖi-ɔ!” Yesu Ɔsa Kuɣamaɖese Ɔɖi I Ɣaa Kasɔrɛkɔ̃.
Yesu ɔsɛ ɔ̃abo Ɣaa isɔrɛyo ɔtsɛ kuɣa maɖese ma mpia i mmɔ isa iɖi.
Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Matsɛrɛ mapia i Ɔko Sekelea ame sɔ Ɣaa ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Wũ iyo ne, maakpere ne sɔ iyo nɛ ame masɛ makparama kayi.’ Ɣɛɛ miɔsu ne mibara mayukukpe kawɛrɛkɔ̃!” Iyi biara ne, Yesu ɔte ara i Ɣaa kasɔrɛkɔ̃ mmɔ.
Ɣaa masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu kaɖe matɔ̃ɖedze gu mmara matedze ɔbie sɔ maaɖoe wũ.
Ɣɛɛ maiɣe ɔri gɔ iso maaki alasɔ maturi gbodzoo pia mmɔ fiɛ mato makã wũ atsue totoroo.
Ma Yudase Ɔkpadzɛ̃gu Yesu Atɔ̃me I Ɔ̃ Ɔle Iso.
Iyi iwɛ̃ gɔ Yesu pia ɔto ɔte maturi ara i Ɣaa isɔrɛyo ɔɣere ma Itɔ̃me Bielea ne, masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu mmara matedze gu kaɖe matɔ̃ɖedze ɔba mmɔ.
Ne maɣere wũ sɔ, “Ɣere bo ngbegɔ ana ɔle gɔ ato abara ala karabara abɔrɛgu.
Nna lotã-ɔ ɔle gɔ?” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mitã lokarɛ mi ira iwɛ̃ si mitã me mmuai.
Yohanes gɔ lopie maturi ndu ne, lɛ ɔna ɔ̃ ɔle ɔbɔrɛgu.
Ɣaa kɔrɛ ɛɛbɛrɛ maturi kɔrɛ ɔbɔrɛ?” Ne matsɛ so iwararãgu sɔ, “Be iɖe boaɣɛ?
Si boɣɛ sɔ Ɣaa kɔrɛ ɔna ɔle ɔbɔrɛgu ne, ɔto ɔ̃akarɛ bo sɔ, ‘Be ɔso fiɛ miifɔ wũ miɖe?’ Fiɛ si boɣɛ sɔ maturi kɔrɛ ɔfɔ ɔbɔrɛ gu ne, mma loba maasakanya ngbe to maapɛ bo ata alasɔ ma ɔɖuɖu ɔfɔ maɖe sɔ Ɣaa kanyaɖidze i Yohanes ɖe.” Ne ɔso ne, matã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Boiɣe ngbegɔ ɔna ɔ̃ ɔle ɔbɔrɛgu.” Ne Yesu ɔ̃ wũ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mme wũ loibaɣere mi ngbegɔ lona wũ ɔle lobɔrɛgu fiɛ nto lobara karabara gagbe.” Yesu Ɔpɛ Igbã I Mafɔ Ma Nto Manyɔ Kakpɛkɔ̃ Iso.
Ne Yesu ɔpɛ ma igbã nɛgbe sɔ, “Ɔwi ɔwɛ̃ ne, ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɔkpɛ̃ adziribi kakpɛkɔ̃.
Gɔ ɔto ɔkɛlɛ ɔri dzoroa ɔwɛ̃ ɔso ne, ɔsu kakpɛkɔ̃ ɔpia i mapaase nrɔɔ̃ ame sɔ manyɔ kã iso matã wũ.
Gɔ ɔwi ɔɣo sɔ maasɔrɛ̃ adziribi wamɔ ne, ɔpia ɔ̃ ɔɖabo ɔwɛ̃ sɔ ɔsɛ ɔ̃afɔ ɔ̃ kaɖekɔ̃ ga loaɣo wũ ɔbɔ i mapaase ma mpia i sia kɔrɛ.
Ɣɛɛ mapaase mamɔ ɔmɔɛ̃ ɔɖabo gɔgbe mapɛ wũ, masa wũ masese nrɔɔ̃ kunu.
Ne ɔso ɔpia ɔɖabo mama.
Ɣɛɛ ɔ̃ wũ mapaase mamɔ ɔpɛ wũ, masopara wũ, makpesera wũ masese nrɔɔ̃ kunu.
Ɔledza ɔɖabo tɛare ipia.
Ɔ̃ ne, mapɛ wũ maɖi wũ igbɛ masa wũ maɖi i sia mmɔ.
“Ne kakpɛkɔ̃ Sate gɔmɔ ɔkarɛ so sɔ, ‘Be loabara?
Loasese wũ ɔbi ɖɔɛse.
Lofɔ loɖe sɔ mato maawarɛ wũ.’ “Ɣɛɛ gɔ mapaase ɔnya ɔbi gɔmɔ ne, maɣere so sɔ, ‘Nya kakpɛkɔ̃ Sate mɔmɔ ɔbi nto ɔba ngbe.
Mitã boɖoe wũ si ara wagbe ɔɖuɖu aakpese bo are!’ Ne ɔso mafuĩdza wũ maɖi i ɔkpã ame ne maɖoe wũ ne.” Ne Yesu ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Be i kakpɛkɔ̃ sate aabara mafɔ magbe?
Ɔto ɔ̃aba ɔ̃aɖoe mapaase magbe ɔɖi i kakpɛkɔ̃ ame ɔbie maturi mama ɔpia i kã ame.” Gɔ maturi ɔnɔ ngbɔ ne, maɣɛ sɔ, “Ooɣo, iibaba ngbɔ!” Yesu ɔkarã ma anɔ iso ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Ɣaa itɔ̃me nɛ matsɛrɛ masɛ ngbe karɔ̃ ɣɛɛ?
‘Ita nɛ i mayotsuedze ɔsɛ̃ sɔ iilɛ ne, ne loba iakpese ita nɛ lonya iɖo pelepele ne.’ Ɔbiara gɔ loatura i ita nɛmɔ iso ne, ɔto ɔ̃afɛfɛ̃ ɖukuɖuku.
Fiɛ si ita nɛmɔ ɔkpase iwuĩ ɔrere ne, ito iakɔtɛ wũ ɖɛkpɛrɛɛ.” Yesu Ɔte Ara I Lampo Itã Iso.
Mmara matedze gu masɔrɛdze makpakpa ɔbie sɔ si mamɔɛ̃ Yesu mmɔ alasɔ maɣe sɔ ma iso ɔpɛ igbã nɛmɔ.
Ɣɛɛ manigã maturi mamɔ.
Ne ɔso ne, matsɛ ɔri mama gɔ iso maaki fiɛ maamɔɛ̃ wũ ibie.
Mapia maturi i iwɛrɛ ame sɔ mabara so lɛ mma nto manyɔnyɔ ɔnukuare si masɛ maakarɛ Yesu atɔ̃me wa loapia wũ i kulu ame si maawo wũ ɔɖi ɔtã ma Romase abã.
Ne ɔso kanyamaɖaɛse magbe ɔkɛlɛ Yesu kɔrɛ masɛ maakarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ratedze boɣe sɔ fɔ ne, ɔnukuare ara asɛ ate ɔwi biara.
Boɣe sɔ fɔ ara ite ame ne, aisɛ anyɔ ɔturi i katɔ̃ ɣɛɛ asɛ aɣɛ nnɛ loabo Ɣaa anɔ iiɖe nnɛ i maturi sɛ maɖɔɛ.
Bobie sɔ ɣere bo si ilɛ sɔ boatã ma Romase Igarakpakpa lampo.” Ɣɛɛ gɔ Yesu ka ɔɣe ma adzuni nyanyarĩa ɔso ne, ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Misu sikãfudza ibi iwɛ̃ mibɔ me.
Nna iti gu iyere nsia iso ngbe?” Ne matã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Igarakpakpa Kaisaro ire iɖe.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Misu nnɛ nɖe Kaisaro ire mitã wũ si misu nnɛ nɖe Ɣaa ire ana mitã Ɣaa.” I maturi katɔ̃ mmɔ ne, maiwo wũ ɔmɔɛ̃ i itɔ̃me kuiwɛ̃ iso.
Ati ɔmɔ ma i mmuai mɛ i Yesu ɔtã ma iso fiɛ ibara ma ɣii ana.
Yesu Ɔɖe Ika I Makpise Ita Gu Kuyiriso Iso.
Ma Zadukise ma nsɛ maɣɛ sɔ makpise iisibata ɔba Yesu kɔrɛ maba maakarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ratedze, Mose ɔtsɛrɛ ɔpia i mmara ame ɔtã bo sɔ, ‘Si ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔkpi ɔnyua ɔ̃ ɔre fiɛ maiɣe ɔbi ne, ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔmɔ ɔnyiibi si ɔsu kpise ɔre ɔyiri.
Mabi ma i ɔ̃ gu kpise ɔre gɔmɔ aaɣe ne, maanyɔ ma lɛ ɔ̃ ɔnyiibi gɔ loɔkpi mabi.’ Ɔwi ɔwɛ̃ ame ne, manyiibi rɛrɛ̃ ikɔdzɛ mawɛ̃ ɔwe.
Kpakpare ɔyiri ɔrɔ̃go, iina ɔpã kere ɔba ɔ̃akpi ɔɣɛ wũ gɔ maiɣe ɔbi.
Ɔ̃ ɔkpeama gɔ nsiai wũ ɔyiri kuɛdze gɔmɔ.
Ɔtɛare ɔ̃ wũ ngbɔ ame gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ isɛ iabo ɔkɔdzɛva.
Ma ɔɖuɖu ɔyiri ɔrɔ̃go gɔmɔ makã maiɣe ɔbi.
Kawirikɔ̃ ne, ɔrɔ̃go ɔ̃ wũ ɔba ɔ̃akpi.
Kiniɔ ne, si makpise ɔba maatã ne, ma ndɛ̃ ɔmele loayiri ɔrɔ̃go gɔgbe gɔ ma ikɔdzɛ ɔɖuɖu ɔyiri wũ manya?” Yesu Ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Marɛrɛ̃ gu marɔ̃go sɛ mayiri so i ngbã mɛgbe ame.
Ɣɛɛ marɛrɛ̃ gu marɔ̃go ma ɔɖuɖu ma lokote sɔ maata masɛ ngbã mɛ loisɛ miro ne, maisibayiri so i ngbã mɛmɔ ame.
Maase lɛ Ɣaa makpabo awe gɔ maisibakpi manya.
Ka maɖe Ɣaa mabi ala maɔta mabɔrɛ i makpise ame.
Mose ɔtsɛrɛ ɔpia i Ɔko Sekelea ame sɔ makpise to maaledza ita iwe ngbã.
Alasɔ ɔwi gɔ ame ɔɣɛ i miyu kadzirimi ga nto katsue kɔrɛ ne, ɔkpere Ɣaa sɔ Abraham Ɣaa gu Isak Ɣaa gu Yakob Ɣaa.
Magbanadze Ɣaa ɔɖe, iiɖe makpise ɔre ɔɖe.
Ne ɔso i ɔ̃ kɔrɛ ne, makpise ana ba ngbã.” Mmara matedze mawɛ̃ ma nɣɛ i mmɔ ɔɖi kanya sɔ, “Ratedze, abua atã mmuai gbaã!” Ne kama ne, kuwɛ̃ iisiwe ɔtu ɔkarɛ wũ kuira.
Nna Ɔbi Nɖe Kristo?
Yesu ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Be ɔso fiɛ maturi sɛ maɣɛ sɔ Kristo ne, David ɔwa tɛtɛ ɔɖe?
Alasɔ David mɔmɔ ɔɣɛ i ɔ̃ Sinɔ ɔko ame sɔ, ‘Bosate ɔɣere Wũ Sate sɔ, “Sɛ i wũ kuɖearɔ̃ iso gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ loasu fɔ matsirise lopia i fɔ ngba kayirinɔ?” ’ Si David to ɔkpere wũ sɔ ɔ̃ Sate ne, nda iabara fiɛ Kristo aaɖe David ɔ̃ ɔwa tɛtɛ?” Yesu Ɔka Ɔ̃ Marasuãdze Sɔ Madzuɛ̃ So I Mmara Matedze Iso.
Ɔwi gɔ i ma ɔɖuɖu ɣɛ mato makã nnɛ i Yesu to ɔɣɛ atsue ne, ɔɣere ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Midzuɛ̃ so i mmara matedze iso.
Masɛ maɖɔɛ mawe maki ku ma awu siare.
Masɛ mabie sɔ maturi si mabɔ so karɔ̃ maya ma i kuɣa ame.
Masɛ mabie nsɛkɔ̃ kɔlɛa i ma Yudase kasarɛkɔ̃ gu sipɔrɔ̃ katukɔ̃.
Masɛ mate so lɛ makuɛdze mabuaidze ɣɛɛ masɔsɔla ma mafɔ ma ara.
Masɛ mate so iki i ma kayi ikparama tagbaraa ame.
Ne ɔso ma kutsue ikpadzɛ̃ to iasi gbaã!”
Kuɛdze Ɔwɛ̃ Karatã.
I Isɔrɛyo mmɔ ne, Yesu ɔtara anɔ kato ɔnya kumɛgɔ i maranase to masu ma karatã mapia i ira nɛ ame mato mato ara mapia.
Ɔnya wɛrɛba kuɛdze ɔwɛ̃ gɔ ɔ̃ wũ ɔsu kupɛrɛ kunyɔ ɔba ɔ̃apia i kame.
Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Nto loɣere mi sɔ kuɛdze gɔgbe ne, ɔtã ara ɔɖo ma ɔɖuɖu.
Alasɔ matsɔra ne, ma karana ame kere maɖi kɛkɛĩ maba maatã.
Ɣɛɛ kuɛdze gɔgbe ne, i ɔ̃ kusa ame nnɛ ɔɖuɖu ɔba ɔ̃aɖe iɖe ɔsu ɔba ɔ̃ato ngbe.” Yesu Ɔɣɛ Kumɛgɔ Maabiɛ Ɣaa Kasɔrɛkɔ̃.
Marasuãdze mawɛ̃ to maɖe ika i Ɣaa kasɔrɛkɔ̃ iso kumɛgɔ ibua ito ilɛ ɔnyɔ, ata wa masu matsue ala gu karatã ga i maturi sɛ matã i mmɔ.
Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ira biara nɛ mito minya ngbe ne, ɔwi to ɔba gɔ ku ita iibasia i nɛ ɔlaa iso.
Mato maasasamara ira biara mafere i karɔ̃.” Inyɛwe Gu Maturi Ikpɛ̃gu To Iaba.
Mmɔ mato makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ratedze, ku mme ɔwi iaba ngbɔ?
Fiɛ be loate sɔ ɔwi ɔɔɣo gɔ ara wagbe aaba?” Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Midzuɛ̃ so sɔ kuwɛ̃ iibasɔsɔla mi.
Maturi gbodzoo to maaba i wũ iyere ame sɔ wũ itɔ̃me mato maɣɛ.
Mato maaɣɛ sɔ, ‘Mme nɖe wũ’ fiɛ ‘Ɔwi ɔɔɣo.’ Ɣɛɛ midaasiai ma.
Midaanigã si minɔ kakpã kulu gu maturi ita iya so iso.
Ara wagbe igbã to aaba, ɣɛɛ iite sɔ kawirikɔ̃ ɔɔɣo.” Yesu ɔkɛlɛgu i katɔ̃ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Karɔ̃ to kaakpɛ̃ gu karɔ̃ fiɛ sigarakaɖekɔ̃ aka anyɔ to aakpɛ̃gu so.
Karɔ̃ to kaati i ngɔi.
Kukã siare to kuabo fiɛ sinyɛ agbãagbã ana to siaba.
Afɔ̃ra ana to aabɔrɛ i kuɖokpo.
“Si ara wagbe aaba ne, mato maamɔɛ̃ mi, makpɛ̃gu mi.
Mato maakɔ mi makɛlɛgu ma Yudase kasarɛkɔ̃, maapia mi iyo.
Mato maakɔ mi makɛlɛgu magara gu matɔ̃ɖedze katɔ̃ sɔ maaɣɛgu mi atɔ̃me ala wũ ɔso.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame loaɖe ɔwi sɛɛ gɔ ame miaɣɛ Ɣaa Itɔ̃me Bielea ne.
Mibara mi adzuni sɔ miibamararã so kumɛgɔ miaɖi so kanya iso.
Alasɔ nto loatã mi atɔ̃me gu iwola nɛ kanya i mi matsirise kuwɛ̃ iibawo ɔya manya.
Mi maɣese gu manyiibi gu mi mɔmɔ malɛdze gu mi malaa to maaɖi mi matã.
Mato maaɖoe mi mawɛ̃.
Ɔbiara to ɔ̃atsiri mi ala wũ ɔso.
Ɣɛɛ nane ɔnidzɔ iibasɛ mi i iso.
Miya teteree fiɛ miana ngbã mɛ loisɛ miro.
Yesu Ɔɣɛ Kumɛgɔ Maabiɛ Yerusalem.
“Ɔwi gɔ mianya sɔ makpakpɛ̃dze ɔba maaki malɔ Yerusalem ne, mitsue sɔ ɔmagɛ̃ ɔbiɛwi ɔɔɣo.
Mma mpia i Yudea si matere makɛlɛ abe iso, mma mpia i ɔmagɛ̃ ame si matere mabɔrɛ.
Mma mpia i miya si madaakpese maba ɔmagɛ̃ ame.
Alasɔ ɔwi gɔmɔ to ɔ̃aɖe kutsue ikpadzɛ̃ ɔwi lɛ kumɛgɔ i Ɔko Sekelea Ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ awe.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ to ɔ̃awe ɔle ɔtã marɔ̃go ma nto nyiri gu matalɛpo ma nto mabi ɣɛtɛ.
Inyɛwe siare to iaba i karɔ̃ gagbe iso.
Ɣaa kutsue ikpadzɛ̃ to iaba maturi magbe iso.
Mato maaɖoe mawɛ̃ ala ipɛmi fiɛ maamɔɛ̃ mawɛ̃ ana makɛlɛgu nrɔ̃ mama iso.
Mma loiɖe ma Yudase to maaɖe sigara ku ɔtile i Yerusalem iso isɛ iabo ɔwi gɔ i Ɣaa ɔtɔrã ɔtã ma.
Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi To Ɔ̃aledza Iba.
“Awawãra agbãagbã to aaba i kuɣɛ̃ gu ɔgbaworeti gu awami iso.
Kayiiso ɔɖuɖu to kaayu ɔriinyɔ.
Ifɔ̃ siare to iamɔɛ̃ maturi ala kumɛgɔ i ɔpo to ɔ̃asia so ara ɔso.
Maturi to maasɛ̃ kulele ala ifɔ̃ nɛ nto ma gɔ maiɣe nnɛ nto iaba i kayi ɔɖuɖu iso ɔso.
Sile dzɛ i kuɖokpo ame ɔɖuɖu to siati teteree i sɛ̃ kusɛkɔ̃.
Ne kama ne, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi to ɔ̃abɔrɛ i adɔdɔ ame gu ɔ̃ ɔle gu ifiɛ teteree ame.
Si ara wagbe ɔnya asɔ̃ katɔ̃ ne, miledza so si mitsɛ ɔri inyɔ alasɔ mi iɖi ɔwi ɔɔbore ɔbo.” Misuã Ara I Kuɖedziri Iso.
Ne Yesu to ɔpɛ ma igbã iwɛ̃ sɔ, “Mikarã inɔ i kuɖedziri gu adziri agbã mama iso.
Si minya sɔ ato aɖi aɣata ɣɛtɛ ne, misɛ miɣɛ sɔ kusɛ ɔɔɣo.
Ngbɔ ame si minya ara wagbe to aba ne, mitsue sɔ Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ɔɔbore sibo.
“Nto loɣere mi sɔ ara wagbe ɔɖuɖu to aaba fiɛ mi mawɛ̃ ma nɣɛ ngbe aakpi miro.
Kato gu karɔ̃ to kaafe, ɣɛɛ wũ atɔ̃me iibafe anya ɖa.
Ikote Sɔ Mianyɔ Tuee Midzuɛ̃.
“Minyɔ so kukaakɔ sɔ miibanina ɔwi i ɔɖegbodzo gu itarɛ̃ iso.
Midaasɛ mimararã so i kayiiso ara iti.
Si iiɖe ngbɔ ne, iyi nɛmɔ to iapatu imɔɛ̃ mi lɛ iyebi.
Ito iapatura kayiiso maturi ɔɖuɖu.
“Ne ɔso midzuɛ̃ so si mila miɔkparama kayi ɔwi biara sɔ miana ɔle miya teteree mibɔrɛ i inyɛwe nɛmɔ ame sɔ miaya bɔlɔlɔ i Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi anɔ.” Ayi wamɔ ɔɖuɖu ne, Yesu ɔsu ɔte maturi ara i Ɣaa kasɔrɛkɔ̃.
Kutsuɛ biara ne, ɔsɛ ɔkɛlɛ Nnɔĩ Adziri Kube iso ɔ̃awe i kasɛ̃ ame.
Kaya tutuutu biara ne, maturi ɔɖuɖu sɛ mata maba isɔrɛyo maba maakã ɔ̃ ara ite atsue.
Masɔrɛdze Makpakpa Ɔsɛ Iti Ame Sɔ Maaɖoe Yesu.
Ɔwi ɔɔɣo gɔ ma Yudase aaɖe Boɖoboɖo Gɔ Loita Iyi nɛ masɛ marɔ ana sɔ Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo Iyi.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ Ɣaa masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu mmara matedze to manigã maturi ɔso ne, matsɛ ɔri gɔ iso maaki fiɛ maaɖoe Yesu i iwɛrɛ ame ibie.
Yuda Ɔnɔ Karɔ̃ Sɔ Ɔ̃aɖi Yesu Ɔtã.
Ɔbosam ɔbo i Yuda gɔ marɔ Iskariot fiɛ ɔ̃ wũ ɔɖe Yesu marasuãdze iweo-inyɔ ndɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ame.
Ne ɔso Yuda ɔkɛlɛ Ɣaa masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu mma nsɛ madzuɛ̃ Ɣaa isɔrɛyo makpakpa kɔrɛ masɛ maasɛ iti ame i ɔri gɔ iso ɔ̃aki fiɛ ɔ̃aɖi Yesu ɔtã ma.
Mana isoɣɔ gbaã, ne ɔso maɣɛ sɔ maatã wũ kuso.
Yuda ɔ̃ wũ ɔnɔ karɔ̃, ne ɔso ɔtsɛ ɔri sɛɛ gɔ iso ɔ̃aki fiɛ ɔ̃aɖi Yesu ɔtã ma ibie.
Yesu Ɔledza So Ɔtã Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo Iyi Iɖe.
Iyi ɔba iaɣo nɛ masɛ maɖe Boɖoboɖo Gɔ Loita Iyi fiɛ ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ame masɛ maɖoe Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo Sɛrɛ maɖe ana ne.
Yesu Ɔpia Petro gu Yohanes ɔɖegu katɔ̃ sɔ, “Misɛ mialedza Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo aɖera wa boaɖe misɛ.” Ne mato makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Lɛ ato abie sɔ boledza bosɛ?” Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Si mibo Yerusalem ɔmagɛ̃ ame ne, Ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ nsore ndu ku ibui to ɔ̃asarɛgu mi.
Misiai wũ misɛ miabo i iyo nɛ ame ɔ̃abo.
Miɣere iyo nɛmɔ sate sɔ, ‘Ratedze sɔ bokarɛ-ɔ sɔ, “Mme iyo nse gɔ mme gu wũ marasuãdze aaɖe Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo aɖera?” ’ Ɔto ɔ̃ate mi iwɛ̃ i iyo siare nɛ matsue masia i kato fiɛ maledza ne, masɛ kuta ayara.
