Miledza ibiara misɛ i mmɔ.” Gɔ maɣo ɔri ne, masɛ maanya ira biara lɛ kumɛgɔ i Yesu ɔɣere ma.
Ne mawa Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo aɖera ne.
Maɖe Bosate Araɖea.
Gɔ ɔwi ɔɣo ne, Yesu gu ɔ̃ katɔ̃memasɛdze ɔsɛ i karɔ̃ sɔ maaɖe ara.
Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Iɖe wũ kuɖɔɛ kokooko sɔ loaɖegu mi Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo aɖera wagbe fiɛ inyɛwe aatu me.
Nto loɣere mi sekelee sɔ loisibaɖe aɖera wagbe lonya gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ ɔwi gɔ boanɔ wã karɔ̃ i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃.” Ne kama ne, Yesu ɔsu itãkɔi, ɔpɛ Ɣaa Siba.
Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mifɔ si minɛ mitã so.
Nto loɣere mi sɔ ita i kiniɔ ito ikɛlɛ ne, loisibanɛ ndã mɛgbe gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ ɔwi gɔ i Ɣaa sigara iɖe aaba.” Ne ka ɔsu boɖoboɖo ɔpɛ Ɣaa siba i ɔ̃ iti ne.
Ɔbɛse wũ kusɛkusɛ ɔsu ɔtã ma.
Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Wũ sosina dzɛ losu lotã i mi iti ngbe ne.
Mibara ne si misu minyigi me.” Ngbɔ ame ɔsu itãkɔi nɛ ame i ndã pia ɔtã ma gɔ maɖe ara maro.
Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ikɔi nɛgbe nɖe Ɣaa kanya ɣɛtɛ ga ɔto ɔnyigu mi ikparĩ ala wũ ima nɛ loafere i karɔ̃ ala mi ɔso ne.
Ɣɛɛ ne, mitsue sɔ ngɔ loaɖi me ɔtã wũ matsirise si ɔto ɔɖegu me aɖera i ngbe.
Mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi ne, nto loakpi lɛ kumɛgɔ i Ɣaa ɔsia ita.
Ɣɛɛ ne, ndzo mitã ngɔ loaɖi me ɔtã.” Ne matsɛ so ikakarɛ sɔ, ma ndɛ̃ nna loabara ira nɛgbe igbã.
Nna Nɖe Ngɔ Loɖo I Marasuãdze Ndɛ̃?
Kakpadzɛ̃ kawɛ̃ ɔbo i marasuãdze ndɛ̃ mabie sɔ matsue ma ndɛ̃ ngɔ nɖe ɔsiare pelepele.
Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Kayiiso magara ma loiɖe ma Yudase sɛ mate so mapia mma mato maɖe iso fiɛ maba ɔle i ma iso.
Magara magbe sɛ mafera so sɔ ma nɖe Maturi Malaa.
Ɣɛɛ iikote sɔ iase ngbɔ i mi ndɛ̃.
Ngɔ nɖe ɔsiare i mi ɔɖuɖu ndɛ̃ ne, ɔ̃ ikote sɔ ɔ̃abara so ɔbiɛtɛ si mi tɔ̃ɖedze si ɔsu so ɔbara ɔɖabo.
Nna nɖe ɔkpakpa?
Ngɔ nsi i karɔ̃ ɔto ɔɖe ara ɛɛbɛrɛ ngɔ nto ɔtu wũ ɔpɔrɔ̃?
Ikpa sekelee sɔ ngɔ nsi i karɔ̃ ɔto ɔɖe ara loɖo.
Ɣɛɛ lopia i mi ndɛ̃ lɛ ngɔ nto ɔsumu mi awe.
Miɔpia kubɛ misiai me i wũ amɔrɛ̃ ɔwi ɔɖuɖu ame.
Kumɛgɔ ame i Tete ɔtã me ɔle sɔ loɖe maturi iso ne, ngbɔ ame loatã mi ɔle mi wũ ne.
Mito miaɖe minɛgu me ara i wũ sigarakaɖekɔ̃ fiɛ miasɛ i sigara ayara iso miɖe sigara i Israel nlɛ aka aweo-anyɔ iso.” Yesu Ɔɣɛ Ɔsɛ Sɔ Petro To Ɔ̃asɛ̃ Wũ.
Ne Yesu to ɔɣere Simon Petro sɔ, “Simon Simon!
Kã atsue!
Ɣaa ɔtã Ɔbosam ɔri sɔ ɔla mi ɔnyɔ si ɔnyɔ mma nɖe masɛɛ gu mma loilɛ lɛ kumɛgɔ i kpɛ̃dze sɛ ɔfuri simɔɣo ɔɖi i kamɔ ame.
Ɣɛɛ ne, Simon, loɔkparama kayi i fɔ iti sɔ fɔ kafɔkaɖe iibakpase.
Si ɔɔkpese aya parataa ne, pia fɔ manyiibi tsɔra ɔle.” Ne Petro to ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Bokɔse, loɣɛ teteree sɔ si inya ne, maapia bo gu-ɔ i iyo ɣee lokpigu-ɔ.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere Petro sɔ, “Petro, nto loɣere-ɔ sɔ kasɛ̃ gagbe si kɔkɔ aaɖi kanya ne, ato aasɛ̃ me ikpɛ itɛ sɔ aiɣe me.” Sikã Kakotoi Gu Akpo Gu Ipɛmi.
Ne Yesu to ɔkarɛ ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Ɔwi gɔ lofe ame gɔ lopia mi katɔ̃me fiɛ mme sɔ midaasu sikã kakotoi ɣee akpo ɣee ndokota ne, ira iwɛ̃ ɔnya mi?” Ne matã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Ooɣo kuira iinya bo kuwɛ̃.” Mmɔ i Yesu to ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ɣɛɛ kiniɔ ne, ɔbiara gɔ mba sikã kawumi ɣee akpo ne, ɔsu ɔla.
Ngɔ nna ipɛmi ne, ɔsu ɔ̃ arapia ɔrɔdɛ̃ si ɔsɛ ɔ̃aɣa ipɛmi.
Fiɛ nto loɣere mi sɔ, Ɔko Sekelea ame itɔ̃me nɛ loɣɛ sɔ, ‘Maaka wũ mapia i maturi lalaa ndɛ̃’ ne, ka iba ngbɔ.
Alasɔ ira nɛ matsɛrɛ i wũ iso ne, ikote sɔ iaba i ne ame.” Ne marasuãdze to maɣere wũ sɔ, “Bokɔse, Nyɔ!
Nya apɛmi anyɔ ngbe!” Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ka ilɛ.” Yesu Ɔkparama Kayi I Nnɔĩ Adziri Kube Iso.
Yesu ɔbɔrɛ i ɔmagɛ̃ ame ɔkɛlɛ Nnɔĩ Adziri Kube iso lɛ kumɛgɔ ɔsɛ ɔɖɔɛ ɔbara.
Ɔ̃ marasuãdze ana siai wũ.
Gɔ ɔbo mmɔ ne, Yesu ɔɣere ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Mikparama kayi si miibabo i ilainyɔ ame.” Ɔrui ɔnyua ma ɔkɛlɛ katɔ̃ kɛkɛĩ ne ɔpɛ agɛgɛ̃ ɔkparama kayi ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Tete, si aatɔrã ne, ɖi inyɛwe ikɔi nɛgbe bɔrɛgu me iso iiɖe wũ kuɖɔɛ sɔ bara ne fɔ kure.” Ne Ɣaa Kpabo ɔwɛ̃ ɔbɔrɛ i kato ɔba ɔ̃apia wũ ɔle ne.
I isomararã siare ame ne, ɔledza kayi ikparama ku anɔ rɛtɛa.
Awururu wa nto abɔrɛ wũ iso se lɛ ima nto ifere i karɔ̃.
Gɔ Yesu ɔta i ngbegɔ ɔto ɔkparama kayi ne, ɔkpese ɔkɛlɛ ɔ̃ marasuãdze kɔrɛ.
Ɔba ɔ̃anya sɔ mato marɛ sirɛ alasɔ isoma ɔmɔɛ̃ ma.
Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Be ɔso mito mirɛ sirɛ?
Mita si mikparama kayi si miibabo i ilainyɔ ame.” Masɔrɛdze Makpakpa Ɔmɔɛ̃ Yesu.
Gɔ Yesu ɣɛ ɔtogu ma ika iɖe ne, maturi gbodzoo ɔba maabo ma iso.
Yuda gɔ nɖe marasuãdze iweo-inyɔ ndɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ nɖe ma katɔ̃.
Ɔkɛlɛ Yesu kɔrɛ ɔsɛ ɔ̃amini wũ.
Ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔkarɛ Yuda sɔ, “Yuda, iminigu asu ato aɖi me, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi atã?” Ɔwi gɔ i marasuãdze ma mpia i mmɔ gu Yesu ɔnya nnɛ nto iba ne, makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Bokɔse, bokpɛ̃gu ma ala bo apɛmi?” Ne marasuãdze ndɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɔɖi ipɛmi ɔtu masɔrɛdze ɔkpakpa pelepele ɔɖabo kuɖearɔ̃ kutsue ɔɖi ne.
Ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔsɛ̃ ɔtã ma sɔ, “Midaabara!” Ɔpɛgu ɔɖabo gɔmɔ kutsue kere ne ɔsa wũ ne.
Ne Yesu to ɔkarɛ masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu kasɔrɛkɔ̃ madzuɛ̃se makpakpa gu kaɖe makpakpa ma loba mamɔɛ̃ wũ sɔ, “Be ɔso fiɛ mito kudziriku gu apɛmi lɛ turiɖoese loɖe?
Lowe i mi kɔrɛ i ma Yudase isɔrɛyo iyi biara ɣɛɛ miimɔɛ̃ me.
Ɣaa lotã mi ɔri gɔgbe fiɛ idududu ame ɔle nto ɔɖe mi iso kiniɔ.” Petro Ɔsɛ̃ Yesu.
Mamɔɛ̃ Yesu makɔ wũ makɛlɛgu masɔrɛdze ɔkpakpa pelepele iyo.
Petro ana siai ma i kama kama.
Mapia ɔtɔ i inyamɔ, ne ɔso Petro ɔ̃ wũ ɔsɛ ɔ̃asɛ i ma kɔrɛ.
Gɔ ɔɖabo rɔ̃go ɔwɛ̃ ɔnya Petro si i ɔtɔ katɔ̃ mmɔ ne, ɔnyɔ wũ totoroo ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Ngɔgbe ɔ̃ wũ Yesu siaidze ɔwɛ̃ ɔɖe.” Ɣɛɛ Petro ɔsɛ̃ ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Ɔrɔ̃go, loiɣe wũ kɔra!” Ɔwi kurukutu kama ne, ɔwɛ̃ ana ɔnya Petro ɔɖi ite ne ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Fɔ wũ ma ndɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ aɖe.” Ɣɛɛ Petro ɔledza iɣɛ sɔ, “Ɔrɛrɛĩ, iiɖe mme loɖe!” Si iabara lɛ ɔɖɔwũ kama ne, ɔrɛrɛ̃ mama ana gɔ nɣɛ i mmɔ ɔledza irɔĩ ikarã teteree sɔ, “Kakpadzɛ̃ kukawɛ̃ na i ne ame sɔ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ana ɔsiai Yesu alasɔ Galilea ɔturi ɔɖe.” Ɣɛɛ Petro ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Nyɔ me ɔrɛrɛ̃, nnɛ ato aɣɛ ngbe ne, loiɣe kuira i ne iso.” Gɔ ɔɣɛ ɔto ɔɣɛ nnɛgbe ne, makɔkɔ ɔɖi kanya.
Ne Bosate ɔfiniki ɔnyɔ Petro ne.
Ɔnyigi nnɛ i Bosate ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Si makɔkɔ aaɖi kanya nɔme kasɛ̃ gagbe ne, ato aasɛ̃ me ikpɛ itɛ sɔ aiɣe me.” Petro ɔbɔrɛ ɔkɛlɛ inyamɔ ɔsɛ ɔ̃abiɛ teteree.
Mma Lodzuɛ̃ Yesu Ɔbara Wũ Aɣiãra, Mapɛ Wũ Mma nto madzuɛ̃ Yesu ɔtsɛ wũ aɣiãra ibara ipɛ wũ.
Masu ira manyi wũ katɔ̃ mapɛ wũ iyɔ maɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ɣere bo ngɔ lopɛ-ɔ!” Matia wũ i siri agbãagbã ana iso.
Yesu Ɔya I Matɔ̃meɣɛdze Katɔ̃.
Gɔ kaɖe ɔsɛ̃ ne, kaɖe makpakpa gu Ɣaa masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu mmara matedze ɔsakanya ne makɔ Yesu mabɔ ma katɔ̃ ne.
Mma losakanya i mmɔ ɔkarɛ Yesu sɔ, “Ɣere bo si fɔ nɖe Kristo.” Ne ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Si loɣere mi ira irere kɔra ne, miibafɔ miɖe.
Fiɛ si lokarɛ mi itɔ̃me irere ne, miibatã me mmuai.
Ɣɛɛ ita i kiniɔ ito ikɛlɛ ne, Ɣaa, Ɔlesate to ɔ̃atara me, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, ɔsɛra i ɔ̃ kuɖearɔ̃ iso.” Ne ma ɔɖuɖu to makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Iyɔ ite sɔ fɔ nɖe Ɣaa ɔbi?” Ne ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Ise lɛ kumɛgɔ miɣɛ.” Ne maɣɛ sɔ, “Iisinya sɔ kuwɛ̃ aaba ɔ̃aɣere bo kuira i ɔ̃ iso.
Bo mɔmɔ ɔɔnɔ ara wa ɔto ɔɣɛ!”
Pilato Ɔkarɛ Yesu Atɔ̃me.
Ne ma ɔɖuɖu ɔta makɔ Yesu makɛlɛgu Pilato ne.
Matsɛ wũ kanya iɖaɛ sɔ, “Bomɔɛ̃ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe gɔ ɔto ɔkã bo aɖe kaɖe ɔyura.
Ɔto ɔɣere ma sɔ madaatã lampo gɔ i ma Romase igarakpakpa ɔsia.
Ɔɣɛ sɔ ɔ̃ nɖe Kristo fiɛ ɔmɔɛ̃ so sigara ana.” Ne Pilato ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Fɔ nɖe ma Yudase igara?” Ne Yesu ɔta wũ mmuai sɔ, “Ise lɛ kumɛgɔ aɣɛ.” Ne Pilato ɔɣere masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu mmamɔ sɔ, “Loinya sɔ ɔɣɛrɛ mmara kumiwɛ̃.” Ɣɛɛ ma kanya ɔwe ɔle teteree sɔ, “Ɔ̃ ara wa ɔto ɔte to abɔ ikpɔkpɔtɔ i ma Yudase ɔɖuɖu ndɛ̃.
Ɔsɛ ne karɔ̃ i Galilea, ne ɔ̃ɔbɔ ne i ngbe ana ne.” Herodes Ɔkarɛ Yesu Atɔ̃me.
Ɔwi gɔ i Pilato ɔnɔ itɔ̃me nɛgbe ne, ɔkarɛ sɔ, “Galilea ɔturi ɔɖe ngbe?” Gɔ ɔtsue sɔ Yesu ɔbɔrɛ i Galilea ibuiti nɛ iso i Herodes to ɔɖe ne, ɔsu wũ ɔsese Herodes ala ɔba ɔpia i Yerusalem ku ɔwi gɔmɔ ame.
So ɔɣɔ Herodes gbaã gɔ ɔnya Yesu alasɔ ɔ̃ɔnɔ wũ iyere fiɛ ɔto ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃anya wũ kokooko.
Ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃anya Yesu ɔbara iwawãra iwɛ̃.
Ne ɔso Herodes ɔkarɛ Yesu atɔ̃me gbodzoo ɣɛɛ Yesu iipia wũ kanya.
Masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu mmara matedze ɔbɔrɛ maba maɖaɛ nnya masia Yesu iso.
Herodes gu ɔ̃ makpakpɛ̃dze ɔbara Yesu aɣiãra, matia wũ.
Ne masu awu sɛɛ awɛ̃ mapia wũ lɛ igara awe fiɛ makpesera wũ masese Pilato ne.
Iyi nɛmɔ iso ne, Herodes gu Pilato ɔkpese malaa, ɣɛɛ sasaasa ne, maisɛ mafe.
Pilato Ɔtã Yesu Kukpi Ipɔ.
Pilato ɔkpere masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu matɔ̃ɖedze gu maturi tsɔra ɔsakanya.
Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mikɔ ngɔgbe mibɔ me sɔ ɔto ɔkɔ maturi ɔyura i ɔri lalaa iso.
I mi mɔmɔ anɔmi ame ne, loɔkarɛ wũ atɔ̃me ɣɛɛ loinya kuira nyanyarĩa nɛ iso miɣɛ mito miɖaɛ wũ kanya.
Herodes ana ɔkpesera wũ ɔsese alasɔ ɔ̃inya kuira lalaa i ɔ̃ iso.
Ngɔgbe iibara kuira nɛ loatã sɔ maaɖoe wũ.
Ne ɔso loatã mapɛ wũ kere lonyua wũ ɔkɛlɛ.” Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo Iyi iɖe biara ame ne, Pilato sɛ ɔnyua yorɛdze ɔwɛ̃ ɔtã ma.
Ne ma ɔɖuɖu ɔtsɛ kulu teteree sɔ, “Ɖoe wũ!
Si anyua Baraba atã bo!” Baraba gɔgbe ne, mapia wũ i iyo ala kulu gɔ ɔbara i Yerusalem ɔmagɛ̃ ame gu ituriɖoe.
Gɔ Pilato to ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃anyua Yesu ɔso ne, ɔledza ma ika iɖegu.
Ɣɛɛ mala kulu teteree mabua sɔ, “Pɛ wũ matãra i kudziri iso!
Pɛ wũ matãra i kudziri iso!” Ne Pilato ɔledza ma ikarɛ ɔkpɛ̃ tɛare sɔ, “Mme ikpi ɔbua ɔbara?
Loinya nnɛ ɔbara fiɛ ikote sɔ loatã wũ kukpi ipɔ.
Loatã mapɛ wũ iyɔ loɔnyua wũ.” Ɣɛɛ matogu kulu teteree sɔ, “Ikote sɔ aatã mapɛ Yesu mamatãra i kudziri iso.” Kawirikɔ̃ ne, maɖe iso iki i ma kulu ila ame.
Ne ɔso Pilato ɔɖaɛ itɔ̃me lɛ kumɛgɔ mato mabie.
Ɔnyua ngɔ mato mabie ɔtã ma, ngɔ mapia iyo ala ɔ̃ kulu ibara gu ituriɖoe ɔso.
Ɔnyua Yesu ana ɔtã ma sɔ masɛ maabara wũ kumɛgɔ maɖɔɛ.
Makpakpɛ̃dze Ɔpɛ Yesu Mamatãra I Kudziri Iso.
Makpakpɛ̃dze ɔkɔ Yesu maruigu.
Gɔ masɛ i ɔri mato makɛlɛ ne, manya ɔ Kirenese ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Simon gɔ ɔbɔrɛ i akorowa awɛ̃ ɔto ɔba Yerusalem.
Matindza wũ maya wũ iso sɔ ɔfɔ ɔnyigbã gɔ i Yesu sore si ɔsiai wũ i kama.
Maturi gbodzoo siai Yesu i kama.
Marɔ̃go mawɛ̃ pia i ma ndɛ̃ gɔ mato mabiɛ masiai wũ.
Mmɔ i Yesu ɔfiniki ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Yerusalem marɔ̃go, midaabiɛ me.
Ɣɛɛ mibiɛ mitã so gu mi mabi.
Alasɔ ɔwi to ɔba gɔ maturi aaɣɛ sɔ, ‘Iti lɛ malɛma gu ayiri wa ame i mabi iisɛ gu mma loitã mabi inyɛ mameme!’ Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame i maturi aaɣere abe sɔ, ‘Biɛ fu bo iso!’ Fiɛ maaɣere kubemi sɔ, ‘Kɔla bo!’ Alasɔ si kudziri yuɛ to kutsue kumɛgɔgbe ne, nda i kukorea aabara?” Makpakpɛ̃dze ɔmɔɛ̃ marɛrɛ̃ inyɔ ma nɖe maturi lalaa masɛgu sɔ maaɖoe gu Yesu.
Gɔ masɛ maabo ngbegɔ masɛ marɔ sɔ, itikui ne, mapɛ Yesu mamatãra i kudziri iso.
Marɛrɛ̃ lalaa mamɔ ana ne, mapɛ ma mamatãra i kudziri iso, ɔwɛ̃ i kuɖearɔ̃ iso ɔnyɔare i kubena iso, Ne Yesu ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Tete, su tsɛ ma alasɔ maiɣe nnɛ mato mabara.” Ne kama ne, makpakpɛ̃dze ɔɣɛ so Yesu arapia gɔ mabara kareremi maro.
Maturi ɣɛ i mmɔ mato manyɔ fiɛ ma Yudase matɔ̃ɖedze ana to mabara Yesu aɣiãra sɔ, “Ɔɖi maturi mama, ne ɔso si ɔ̃ nɖe Kristo gɔ i Ɣaa ɔsia ikparĩ ne, ɔɖi so si bonyɔ!” Makpakpɛ̃dze ma wũ ngbɔ ame mabara Yesu aɣiãra ne.
Masu ndã bea mabɔ wũ sɔ ɔnɛ.
Ne maɣere wũ sɔ, “Si fɔ nɖe ma Yudase igara ne, kpɛ̃ ɖi so!” I ɔ̃ sitikpe ne, matsɛrɛ mamatãra sɔ, “Ma Yudase Igara i ngbe ne.” Maturi lalaa ma mapɛ mamatãra i kudziri iso mmɔ ɔwɛ̃ ana ɔtia Yesu ɔɣere sɔ, “Iiɖe fɔ nɖe Kristo?
Ɖi so si aɖi bo bo wũ!” Ne ɔ̃ ɔnyɔare to ɔnyagalagu wũ sɔ, “Aisɛ anigã Ɣaa?
Kutsue ikpadzɛ̃ iwɛ̃ saã i makpakpɛ̃dze ɔtã bo gu wũ.
Bo kutsue ikpadzɛ̃ ne, ikotegu bo.
Alasɔ nnɛ bobara ne, ne kuso boto bofɔ ne.
Ɣɛɛ ɔ̃ ne, ɔ̃ibara ikpi kuiwɛ̃.” Ne ɔɣere Yesu sɔ, “Yesu, nyigi me si abo fɔ sigarakaɖekɔ̃.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Gbaã nto loɣere-ɔ sɔ nɔme ne, bo gu-ɔ aasarɛ i Paradiso ame.” Yesu Kukpi Ɔwi gɔ ipɛ lɛ iɖɔwũ iweo-inyɔ ne, kayi ɔbara guduu gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ isɛ iabo lɛ iɖɔwũ itɛ ame.
Kuɣɛ̃ ɔnyi, Ɣaa isɔrɛyo ɔkati gɔ nsa i mmɔ ɔkɛ aka anyɔ.
Ne Yesu ɔla kulu teteree sɔ, “Tete, fɔ nrɔɔ̃ ame losu wũ siwarã lopia.” Gɔ ɔɣɛ ngbɔ ne, ɔsɔra.
Makpakpɛ̃dze ɔkpakpa gɔ nɣɛ i mmɔ fiɛ ɔnya nnɛ loba ɔle Ɣaa ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Gbaã iɖe sɔ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ne, ɔturi sɛɛ ɔɖe.” Gɔ maturi gbodzoo ma loba maɣɛ mato manyɔ ara ɔnya nnɛ loba ne, masore nrɔɔ̃ i ati makpese makɛlɛ ayo ku isomararã.
Mma ɔɖuɖu nɣe Yesu gu marɔ̃go ma losiai wũ mabɔrɛ i Galilea ɔya dzoroo manyɔ ara wa lokɛlɛ i katɔ̃.
Yosef Arimatease Ɔbiara Yesu.
-Ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ sɔ Yosef fiɛ ɔbɔrɛ i ɔmagɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Arimatea i Yudea karɔ̃ iso ɔwe i mmɔ.
Ɔturi sɛɛ gɔ masɛ mawarɛ gbaã ɔɖe.
Ɔ̃ wũ ɔto ɔnyɔ Ɣaa sigara iɖe iba ɔri.
Atoa sɔ ɔpia i ma Yudase matɔ̃meɣɛdze ndɛ̃ ne, ɔ̃inɔgu ma karɔ̃ i nɛ mabara i ngbe iso.
Ɔkɛlɛ Pilato kɔrɛ ɔsɛ ɔ̃akarɛ ɔri sɔ ɔtã wũ ɔbɛse Yesu kpise.
Gɔ mabɛse wũ i kudziri iso ne, ɔsu ɔkati fudza ɔmini wũ.
Ne ɔsu wũ ɔsɛ ɔ̃apia i itawo nɛ ame maibiara kuwɛ̃ manya ne.
Iyi nɛmɔ ne, Fiɖa iɖe ne ɔso Iwarãyi ka iba iasɛ karɔ̃.
Marɔ̃go ma losiai Yesu mabɔrɛ i Galilea ne, masiai Yosef masɛ maanya ngbegɔ ɔbiara Yesu gu kumɛgɔ ɔrara ɔ̃ kpise.
Makpese makɛlɛ iyo masɛ maakɔtɛ awa wa nsɛ afɔrɛ̃ kɔrɔ̃kɔrɔ̃ fiɛ masɛ masu maledza ala makpise masɛ.
Iwarãyi iso ne, mawarã lɛ kumɛgɔ i mmara ɔte awe.
Yesu Ɔta Ɔbɔrɛ I Makpise Ame.
Kɔsiɖa kaya tutuutu ne, marɔ̃go magbe ɔta makɛlɛ maturi kabiarakɔ̃ ku ara wa maaledza wũ ala. Gɔ masɔ̃ ne, manya sɔ ita nɛ mali matɛ̃ ikpibiɔ kanya ne, maɔli ne masɛ i kuruɛ.
Ne ɔso mabo i ikpibiɔ ame, ɣɛɛ mainya Bosate Yesu kpise.
Nnɛgbe ɔbara ma ɣii.
Ne gɔ maɣɛ mato mabu ne iso ne, maturi inyɔ ma awu nto afiɛ atsue anɔmi ɔbɔrɛ maya ma i katɔ̃.
Ifɔ̃ ɔmɔɛ̃ marɔ̃go gbaã ne ɔso mabɔ ma ati karɔ̃ matã ma.
Ne mmamɔ ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Be ɔso mito minyɔnyɔ gbanadze i makpise ndɛ̃?
Ɔna i ngbe.
Ɔ̃ɔta!
Minyigi nnɛ ɔɣere mi gɔ ɔpiagu mi i Galilea sɔ, ‘Mato maaɖi Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi matã maturi lalaa.
Mato maapɛ wũ mamatãra i kudziri iso.
Fiɛ ayi atɛ kama ne, ɔto ɔ̃aledza ita ibɔrɛ i makpise ndɛ̃.’ ” Ne marɔ̃go ɔnyigi atɔ̃me wamɔ ne.
Gɔ mabɔrɛ i maturi kabiarakɔ̃ mmɔ ne, masɛ maaɣere katɔ̃memasɛdze iweo-ɔwɛ̃ gu matsɔra ara wagbe.
Marɔ̃go magbe nɖe Maria Magdalene gu Yohana gu Maria gɔ nɖe Yakobo ɔnyi.
Ma gu marɔ̃go mama ɔsɛ maaɣere katɔ̃memasɛdze ara wagbe.
Ɣɛɛ katɔ̃memasɛdze ɔbu sɔ ara wa i marɔ̃go to maɣɛ ne, adzimira aɖe.
Ne ɔso maifɔ maɖe.
Ɣɛɛ Petro ɔta ɔtere ɔkɛlɛ mmɔ.
Gɔ ɔbɔdzo ɔnyɔ ikpibiɔ ame ne, ɔnya ɔkati gɔ mamini kpise.
Ɔ̃isinya kuira, ne ɔso ɔkpese ɔkɛlɛ iyo ɔto ɔbu nnɛ loba ngbe iti ame.
Maturi Inyɔ Mawɛ̃ Ɔnya Yesu I Emaus Ɔri Iso.
Iyi nɛmɔ ame iso ne, Yesu masiaidze inyɔ mawɛ̃ sɛ i ɔri mato makɛlɛ ɔmagɛ̃ kosoi ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Emaus.
Ita i mmɔ iba Yerusalem aaɖe lɛ agu akɔdzɛ ɔɖui.
Masɛ mato maɖe ika i ara wa loba iso.
Gɔ masɛ mato maɖe ika maɣɛ ara wagbe ne, Yesu mɔmɔ ɔba ɔ̃atu ma ɔsiai ma.
Gɔ manya wũ ne, maiɣe sɔ ɔ̃ ɔɖe.
Mmɔ i Yesu ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Be misɛ miɣɛ i ɔri iso?” Matui maya mabara so nnya nnya.
Ne ma ndɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Kleopa ɔkarɛ Yesu sɔ, “Fɔ ɔnɔwɛ̃ fɔ nɖe ɔfɔ i Yerusalem fiɛ aiɣe ara wa loba i ɔwi kurukutu gɔgbe ame?” Ne Yesu ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Be ara?” Ne mapia kanya sɔ, “Ara wa lobɔrɛ i Yesu Nasaretse iso gɔ nɖe Ɣaa kanyaɖidze iso.
Ɔbara awawãra fiɛ ɔte ara ana ku ɔle i Ɣaa gu maturi ɔɖuɖu anɔ.
Ma Yudase Ɣaa masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu bo matɔ̃ɖedze ɔsu wũ mapia i Roma abã makpakpa nrɔɔ̃ ame sɔ matã wũ kukpi ipɔ fiɛ mapɛ wũ mamatãra i kudziri iso.
Ɣɛɛ bonyɔ ɔri sɔ ɔ̃ nɖe ngɔ loaɖi Israel kaɖe ɔɖuɖu fiɛ.
Ne kama ne, nɔme nɖe ikpɛnɛ tɛare gɔ ara wagbe ɔba.
Bo ikuri ame marɔ̃go mawɛ̃ ɔba maatara bo situ maɣedza gɔ masɛ maturi kabiarakɔ̃ maba ku kaya gagbe.
Mainya ɔ̃ kpise, ne makpese maba maaɣere bo sɔ Ɣaa makpabo mawɛ̃ ɔɖi so mate ma.
Maɣere ma sɔ Yesu pia ngbã.
Bo ndɛ̃ mawɛ̃ ɔsɛ maturi kabiarakɔ̃ masɛ maanya lɛ kumɛgɔ i marɔ̃go ɔɣere bo pɛpɛɛpɛ, ɣɛɛ mainya wũ.” Ne mmɔ i Yesu to ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Miikpa anɔ ɖuɖuuɖu.
Mi kafɔkaɖe i Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze ara wa maɣɛ iso se tɛgɛlɛ.
Miiɣe sɔ ikote sɔ Kristo aaki i inyɛwe nɛgbe igbã ame fiɛ ɔ̃akɛlɛ ɔ̃ sigarakaɖekɔ̃ i ikpawaĩ ame?” Ne Yesu ɔɖiɖi ara wa matsɛrɛ i ɔ̃ iso mapia i Ɔko Sekelea ame ita i Mose gu ara wa i Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze ɔɖuɖu ɔtsɛrɛ masɛ karɔ̃ ɔte ma ne.
Gɔ mabore mabo ɔmagɛ̃ kosoi gɔmɔ ne, Yesu ɔbara lɛ ɔfe ɔto ɔfe awe.
Ɣɛɛ matɛ̃ wũ ɔri maɣere wũ sɔ, “Kaɖe ɔɔro ɔso ne, tui we i bo kɔrɛ ngbe.” Ne ɔso ɔsɛ ɔ̃abo i ma kɔrɛ.
Ɔsɛ ɔ̃asɛ i karɔ̃ sɔ si ɔɖegu ma ara.
Gɔ ɔsu boɖoboɖo ne, ɔpɛ Ɣaa siba, ne ɔbɛbɛse ɔsu ɔtã ma ne.
Ɔluwɛ̃ ma anɔ ɔbusi manya wũ maɖi ite, ɣɛɛ ɔyu ma iso.
Ne maɣere so sɔ, “Ɔwi gɔ ɔto ɔɖegu bo ika fiɛ ɔɖiɖi Ɣaa itɔ̃me karɔ̃ ɔte bo i ɔri iso ne, isoɣɔ siare ɔwe i bo situ ame.” Mata ɔluwɛ̃ makpese maɣo Yerusalem ɔri.
Masɛ maanya katɔ̃memasɛdze iweo-ɔwɛ̃ gɔ masi fiɛ maturi mama ana si i ma kɔrɛ mato maɣɛ sɔ, “Bokɔse ɔta gbaã ɔbɔrɛ i makpise ame fiɛ ɔɖi so ɔte Simon.” Ne maturi inyɔ mamɔ ana ɔɣɛ ara wa manya i ɔri gu kumɛgɔ ɔɖi so ɔte ma gɔ ɔkpɛti boɖoboɖo ɔtã ma ne.
Yesu Ɔɖi So Ɔte Ɔ̃ Marasuãdze.
Gɔ maɣɛ mato maɣɛ nnɛgbe ne, ɔluwɛ̃ Yesu ɔba ɔ̃aya i ma ndɛ̃.
Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Isobuɛ itã mi.” Ifɔ̃ ɔmɔɛ̃ ma gbaã ne maɣɛ sɔ kpise ɔɖe manya.
Ɣɛɛ ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Be ɔso fiɛ mikpɔkpɔtɔ mito miwararã so?
Minyɔ wũ nrɔɔ̃ gu ngba si mipɛgu me minyɔ sɔ mme loɖe.
Alasɔ kpise na sosina gu akui lɛ mito minya sɔ loba.” Gɔ ɔɣere ma ngbɔ ne, ɔsu ɔ̃ nrɔɔ̃ gu ngba ɔte ma.
Isoɣɔ siare ɔso ne, iɖa ma ifɔ iɖe, ibara ma ɣii.
Ne Yesu ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Araɖea awɛ̃ se i ngbe?” Ne masu ikpɛ fɛ̃a matã wũ ne.
Ɔfɔ ɔwe i ma katɔ̃.
Mmɔ ɔto ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ara wagbe iso lola loɔɖe mi ika gɔ lopia i mi kɔrɛ ne.
Ira biara nɛ matsɛrɛ i Mose mmara ɔko ame gu Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze siko ame gu David Sinɔ ɔko ame i wũ iso ne, ikote sɔ iaba ngbɔ.” Ne ka ɔbusi ma adzuni ame sɔ maanɔ Ɔko Sekelea ame atɔ̃me karɔ̃ ne.
Ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ngbɔ matsɛrɛ sɔ Kristo aawe inyɛ ɔta ɔbɔrɛ i makpise ame ku ikpɛnɛ tɛare iso ne.
I ɔ̃ iyere ame ne, maaɣɛ ifiniki gu kasukatsɛ itɔ̃me i kayi ɔɖuɖu iso ita i Yerusalem.
Mi loaɖi atɔ̃me wa ɔɖuɖu minɔ gu nwa minya kanya.
Mme mɔmɔ to loasese mi nnɛ i Ɣaa ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ sɔ ɔ̃asese mi.
Ɣɛɛ miya misia Ɣaa ɔle i Yerusalem gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ ɔwi gɔ ame ɔ̃aba mi iso ɔbɔrɛ i kato.” Ɣaa Ɔsu Yesu Ɔkɛlɛgu Kato.
Ne ka ɔkɔ ma ɔbɔrɛgu i Yerusalem masɛ maabo Betania kɔrɛ.
Ɔkɔlɛ ɔ̃ nrɔɔ̃ ɔfere ma kusɛkusɛ iso.
Ne gɔ ɔto ɔtã ma kusɛkusɛ ne, Ɣaa ɔsu wũ ɔkɛlɛgu kato.
Mapɛ agɛgɛ̃ masɔrɛ wũ, ne makpese makɛlɛ Yerusalem ku isoɣɔ siare ne.
Mala maɔsɛ maɔle Ɣaa i kasɔrɛkɔ̃ ɔwi biara.
Ɣaa Itɔ̃me Nɛ Nsɛ Itã Ngbã.
Ta kayi karɔ̃kasɛkɔ̃ ne, Itɔ̃me pia.
Itɔ̃me gu Ɣaa mpia, fiɛ Ne nɖe Ɣaa.
Itɔ̃me gu Ɣaa pia fiɛ ira biara ɔsɛ karɔ̃.
Ɔ̃ iso i Ɣaa ɔki ɔbara ira biara, fiɛ kuira na nɛ iiɖe ɔ̃ iso iki fiɛ mabara ne.
Itɔ̃me nɛgbe ame i ngbã mɔmɔ pia ne.
Fiɛ ngbã mɛgbe nsɛ mitã maturi ikpawaĩ ne.
Ikpawaĩ nɛgbe sɛ ifiɛ ibo i idududu ame, fiɛ idududu iisɛ iwo ikpawaĩ ɔɖe iso.
Ɣaa ɔpia ɔ̃ ɔɖabo ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Yohanes.
Ɔba ɔ̃aɖe maturi ika i ikpawaĩ iso, sɔ ma ɔɖuɖu aaki i ɔ̃ iso mafɔ maɖe.
Iiɖe Yohanes nɖe ikpawaĩ, ɣɛɛ ne, aɖansiɛ kere ɔba ɔ̃aɖe i ikpawaĩ iso.
Ikpawaĩ mɔmɔ nɛ nsɛ ifiɛ itã ɔbiara to iba kayiiso.
Itɔ̃me nɛgbe ka ipia i kayi ame, fiɛ ɔ̃ iso maki fiɛ mabara kayi, ɣɛɛ kayiiso iiɣe wũ.
Ɔba ɔ̃ mɔmɔ aɖe maturi kɔrɛ, ɣɛɛ ɔ̃ aɖe maturi iifɔ wũ.
Ɣɛɛ mma ɔɖuɖu lofɔ wũ fiɛ mafɔ wũ maɖe ne, ɔtã ma ɔle sɔ maakpese Ɣaa mabi.
Maikpese Ɣaa mabi iki i iɣe ame, ana ne iiɖe ɔrã gu ɔre kere ikpɛ̃ ɔkã fiɛ maɣe ma, ɣɛɛ Ɣaa mɔmɔ lobara ma ɔ̃ mabi.
Itɔ̃me nɛgbe ɔkpese ɔturi awune gɔ loyi ku abualɛra gu ɔnukuare, ɔba ɔ̃awe i bo ndɛ̃.
Bonya ɔ̃ ikpawaĩ nɛ ɔfɔ i Ɣaa kɔrɛ lɛ ɔ̃ Ɔbi ɔwɛ̃ saã.
Yohanes ɔɖe ika i ɔ̃ iso.
Ɔla kulu ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Ngɔgbe nɖe ɔturi gɔ itɔ̃me lola loɔɣere mi sɔ ɔto ɔ̃aba i wũ kama ne ɔɖo me fafaafã ne.
Ka ɔpia kokooko fiɛ maɣe me.” Kumɛgɔ ɔyi ku abualɛra i ɔ̃ ame ɔso ne, ɔ̃ɔfedza kusɛkusɛ ɔfere i bo ɔbiara iso gɔ kufere bo iso ɔwi biara.
Ɣaa ɔtã bo mmara ɔkigu i Mose iso, ɣɛɛ ɔtã bo abualɛra gu ɔnukuare iki i Yesu Kristo iso.
Kuwɛ̃ iinya Ɣaa ɔnya.
Ɣaa Ɔbi ɔwɛ̃ saã gɔ lokategu Ɣaa fiɛ ɔpia i ɔ̃ Ɔse kɔrɛ ne, ɔ̃ loɖi wũ ɔte maturi ne.
Yohanes Ɔɣɛ Sɔ Iiɖe Ɔ̃ Nɖe Kristo.
Ma Yudase makpakpa ma i Yerusalem ɔpia masɔrɛdze gu ma Levise sɔ masɛ maakarɛ Yohanes sɔ, “Nna kowũ abua aɖe?” Yohanes iikɔla ma kuira, ɣɛɛ ɔɣere ma ɔɖi sekelee sɔ, “Iiɖe mme nɖe Kristo gɔmɔ.” Ne makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Iyɔ fɔ nɖe nna?
Fɔ nɖe Kanyaɖidze Eliya?” Ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Iiɖe mme nɖe wũ.” Maledza wũ ikarɛ sɔ, “Fɔ nɖe Kanyaɖidze gɔ maɣɛ masɛ sɔ ɔ̃aba?” Ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Ooɣo.” Ne maɣere wũ sɔ, “Ɣere bo ngɔ kowũ abua aɖe alasɔ ikote sɔ boasɛ boatã mma lopia bo katɔ̃me mmuai.
Fɔ nɖe nna?” Yohanes ɔtã ma mmuai lɛ kumɛgɔ i Kanyaɖidze Yesaya ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Mme nɖe ngɔ nto ɔla kulu i fafuĩ ame ɔɣɛ sɔ, miledza Bosate ɔri misɛ itã ɔ̃ iba.” Ne mma i ma Farisise ɔpia katɔ̃me, makarɛ Yohanes sɔ, “Si iiɖe fɔ nɖe Kristo, ɣee Eliya, ɣee Ɣaa Kanyaɖidze gɔ boto bonyɔ ɔri ne, be ɔso fiɛ ato apie maturi Ɣaa ndu?” Yohanes ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mme ne, losu ndu nto lobara mi ala kubarara gɔgbe, ɣɛɛ ɔwɛ̃ ɣɛ i mi ndɛ̃ gɔ miiɣe.
Ɔ̃ nɖe ngɔ loaba i wũ kama ne, ɣɛɛ mme ne, loikote sɔ loabɔdzo loɖi ɔ̃ ndokota.” Nwagbe ɔɖuɖu ɔkɛlɛ i katɔ̃ i Betania ɔmagɛ̃ i Yordan ɔwore ɔkpokpo gɔmɔ ngbegɔ i Yohanes to ɔpie maturi Ɣaa ndu.
Yesu Nɖe Ɣaa Sɛrɛrerɔ̃ Ibi.
Gɔ kaɖe ɔsɛ̃ fiɛ Yohanes ɔnya Yesu sɛ ɔto ɔba ɔ̃ kɔrɛ ne, ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Minyɔ, Ɣaa Sɛrɛrerɔ̃ Ibi nɛ loafore kayiiso maturi akpi ɔɖi ma iso ne!
Ɔ̃ nɖe ngɔ iso loɣere mi sɔ, ‘Ɔwɛ̃ to ɔba i wũ kama gɔ loɖo me, alasɔ ka ɔpia kokooko fiɛ maɣe me.’ Mme wũ loiɣe wũ loɖegu katɔ̃, ɣɛɛ loba nto lopie maturi Ɣaa ndu si Ɣaa aaɖi wũ ɔte Israel kaɖe.” Yohanes ɔɣɛ i ɔ̃ iso ana sɔ, “Lonya Ɣaa Siwarã ɔso lɛ ilɔpɔ sibɔrɛ i Kato siba siasɛ wũ iso.
Loiɣe wũ loɖegu katɔ̃, ɣɛɛ Ɣaa gɔ lopia me sɔ lopie maturi ndu ɔɣere me sɔ, ‘Ngɔ iso aanya wũ Siwarã ɔso siba siasia ne, ɔ̃ nɖe ngɔ loapie maturi Siwarã Bielea ne.’ Lonya iba ngbɔ, ne ɔso loto loɣere mi sɔ ɔ̃ nɖe Ɣaa Ɔbi ne.” Yesu Ɔkpere Marasuãdze Ɖeakatɔ̃.
Kaɖesɛ̃a gɔ Yohanes gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze inyɔ ɣɛ fiɛ ɔnya Yesu to ɔfe ne, ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Minyɔ, Ɣaa Sɛrɛrerɔ̃ Ibi mmɔ!” Marasuãdze inyɔ magbe ɔnɔ nnɛ i Yohanes ɔɣɛ, ne ɔso marui masiai Yesu.
Gɔ Yesu ɔpɛ ɔfiniki fiɛ ɔnya sɔ masiai wũ ne, ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Be mito mibie?” Matã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Rabi,” gɔ karɔ̃ nɖe, Ratedze, “Botã-ɔ iti i lɛ isɛ asi?” Ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Miba mianyɔ.” Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, ka ito isɛ kutsuɛ iɖɔwũ ina ame, ne ɔso masiai wũ masɛ maawe i ɔ̃ kɔrɛ kutsuɛ gɔmɔ ɔɖuɖu.
Marasuãdze inyɔ ma lonɔ nnɛ i Yohanes ɔɣɛ fiɛ masiai Yesu mmɔ ɔwɛ̃ nɖe Andrea, Simon Petro ɔnyiibi.
Ira ɖeakatɔ̃ nɛ ɔbara nɖe sɔ ɔnyɔnyɔ ɔ̃ ɔnyiibi Simon.
Gɔ ɔnya wũ ne, ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Boɔnya Mesia,” gɔ karɔ̃ nɖe Kristo ngɔ masɔla nnɔĩ.
Andrea ɔkɔ Simon ɔkɛlɛgu Yesu kɔrɛ.
Gɔ Yesu ɔnya wũ ne, ɔnyɔ wũ totoroo ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Fɔ nɖe Yohanes ɔbi Simon ne, ɣɛɛ ita i kiniɔ ne, maarɔ-ɔ sɔ Kefas,” ɣee Petro, gɔ karɔ̃ nɖe ita siare.
Yesu Ɔkpere Filipo Gu Nataniel.
Kaɖesɛ̃a ne, Yesu ɔbara adzuni sɔ ɔ̃akɛlɛ Galilea karɔ̃ iso.
Gɔ ɔsɛ i ɔri ne, ɔnya ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Filipo, ne ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Siai me.” Filipo ana ne, Betsaida gɔ nɖe Andrea gu Petro mɛrɛ̃ ɔmagɛ̃ ame iɖe ɔbɔrɛ.
Ne kama ne, Filipo ɔsɛ ɔ̃ɔnya Nataniel, ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Boɔnya ngɔ iso i Mose gu Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze ɔtsɛrɛ ara masegu i Ɔko Sekelea ame.
Ɔ̃ nɖe Yosef ɔbi Yesu gɔ lobɔrɛ i Nasaret ne.” Nataniel ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Akuã!
Ira sɛɛ iwɛ̃ aawo ɔbɔrɛ i Nasaret?” Filipo ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Fɔ ba nyɔ kere!” Gɔ Yesu ɔnya Nataniel sɛ ɔto ɔba ɔ̃ kɔrɛ ne, ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Israelse mɔmɔ gɔ iso i sila kusiwɛ̃ na i ngbe ne!” Nataniel ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Nda abara fiɛ atsue ɔturi gɔ igbã loɖe?” Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Lonya-ɔ i kubo kayirinɔ fiɛ Filipo aakpere-ɔ.” Nataniel ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Rabi, Ɣaa Ɔbi aɖe.
Fɔ nɖe Israel Igara ne.” Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Be!
Ɔɔfɔ aɖe alasɔ loɣere-ɔ sɔ lonya-ɔ i kubo kayirinɔ?
Ato aanya ara wa lomɔ aɖo nwagbe!” Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Gbagbaã ne, mito mianya kato ɔbusi minya Ɣaa makpabo to maya maso i mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, iso.”
Makɔ Ɔrɔ̃go I Kana.
Ikpɛnɛ tɛare i nnɛmɔ kama ne, makɔ ɔrɔ̃go i ɔmagɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Kana i Galilea.
Yesu ɔnyi ana ɔwe i mmɔ.
Makpere Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ana makɛlɛgu ɔrɔ̃go kakɔkɔ̃.
Gɔ ndã mɛ karabara mato mabara ɔro ne, Yesu ɔnyi ɔbore ɔbo wũ ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ma ndã ɔɔro ma iso.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ɔ̃ ɔnyi sɔ, “Mmã, iiɖe fɔ itɔ̃me iɖe mmɔ.
Wũ ɔwi iiɣo.” Ne Yesu ɔnyi ɔɣere maɖabo ma i iyo mmɔ sɔ, “Ibiara nɛ ɔɣere mi sɔ mibara ne, mibara.” Gɔ iɖe ma Yudase kurabara sɔ maafofore so ɔso ne, maɣedza ndu ita abuiku akuɔ i inyamɔ i mmɔ.
Ibuiku biara sɛ ifɔ kusorebui kuna ɣee kuru.
Yesu ɔɣere maɖabo sɔ maɖu ndu mafere i abuiku wamɔ ame si miyi, ne mabara ngbɔ ne.
Ne ka ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mika ndu mikɛlɛgu ɔkpakpa gɔ nto ɔnyɔ araɖea iso.” Ne maka makɛlɛgu wũ ne.
Gɔ ɔtu ndu mɛ loɔkpese ndã ɔnyɔ, fiɛ ɔ̃iɣe ngbegɔ mise, ɣɛɛ maɖabo ma maɣe ne, ɔtã makpere ɔrɔ̃go kɔdze matã wũ.
Ne ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ɔbiara ne, ndã sɛɛ miɖe ɔsɛ ɔɖe katɔ̃ ɔɖi ɔtã maturi manɛ, si ka mato marɛ̃ ne, ne ɔsɛ ɔɖi mibea ɔbɔ ne.
Ɣɛɛ fɔ ne, kini ato aɖi ndã sɛɛ abɔ ne!” Yesu ɔbara iwawãra ɖeakatɔ̃ nɛgbe i Kana i Galilea karɔ̃ iso.
Mmɔ ɔɖi ɔ̃ ɔle ɔte fiɛ ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔfɔ wũ maɖe ne.
Ne kama ne, Yesu gu ɔ̃ ɔnyi gu ɔ̃ manyiibi gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔkɛlɛ Kapernaum masɛ maawe i mmɔ ayi kɛkɛĩ.
Yesu Ɔsa Kuɣa Maɖedze Ɔɖi I Kasɔrɛkɔ̃ Gɔ ma Yudase Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo Iyi ɔɔro ɔɣo ne, Yesu ɔkɛlɛ Yerusalem.
I Ɣaa Isɔrɛyo ame ne, ɔnya maturi to marɔdɛ̃ manantsuĩ, masɛrɛ gu ayo ame alɔpɔ gu mma nto manyuarã sikã si i karɔ̃ mmɔ.
Ne ɔso Yesu ɔfɛ̃ iporoibi ala awɛĩ ɔsu ɔsa manantsuĩ gu masɛrɛ ɔɖuɖu ɔɖi i Isɔrɛyo ame, ɔturi sikã manyuarãdze sipɔrɔ̃ gu ma sikã ɔfere i karɔ̃.
Ne ɔɣere mma nto marɔdɛ̃ ayo ame alɔpɔ sɔ, “Mimala mi ara miɖi i ngbe si minyua Tete iyo ɔsu ɔbara kuɣa ame.” Ne ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔnyigi itɔ̃me nɛ matsɛrɛ masɛ sɔ, “Wũ kuɖɔɛ gɔ loba lotã fɔ iyo ɔtã wũ anɔmi ɔrɛtɛ.” Ne ma Yudase makpakpa ɔba Yesu kɔrɛ makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Mme iwawãra aawo ɔbara asu asia ita sɔ aba ɔle aabara nnɛ abara i ngbe?” Yesu ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Mibiɛ Isɔrɛyo nɛgbe, ɣɛɛ akpɛnɛ atɛ kama ne, loaledza ne itsue!” Ne ma Yudase ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Be ato aɣɛ?
Aawo akpɛnɛ atɛ ɔsu ɔledza iyo nɛ masu akɔ sina akuɔ matsue ɔtsue?” Ɣɛɛ mainɔ karɔ̃ sɔ ɔ̃ sosina ɔsu ɔto ɔkateragu Isɔrɛyo.
Ne ɔso ɔwi gɔ i Ɣaa ɔɔtara wũ ɔbɔrɛgu i makpise ame ne, ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔnyigi sɔ ɔɣɛ itɔ̃me nɛgbe.
Itã mafɔ Ɣaa Itɔ̃me nɛ matsɛrɛ masɛ maɖe gu ara wa i Yesu ɔɣere ma.
Yesu Ɣe Ɔturi Awune Nsɛgbai.
Gɔ Yesu ɔwe i Yerusalem ku Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo Iyi iɖe ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, maturi gbodzoo ɔfɔ wũ maɖe ala awawãra wa manya ɔbara ɔso.
Ɣɛɛ Yesu iibaragu ma mawɛ̃, alasɔ ɔɣe maturi ɔɖuɖu.
Iinya sɔ kuwɛ̃ aaɣere wũ kumɛgɔ i maturi awune se alasɔ ɔ̃ mɔmɔ ɣe ma situ ame.
Yesu Ɔte Nikodemo Ara.
Ma Yudase tɔ̃ɖedze ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ sɔ Nikodemo fiɛ ɔpia i ikuri nɛ masɛ marɔ sɔ ma Farisise ɔwe.
Kasɛ̃ kawɛ̃ ne, ɔba Yesu kɔrɛ ɔba ɔ̃aɣere wũ sɔ, “Rabi, boɣe sɔ Ratedze aɖe abɔrɛ i Ɣaa kɔrɛ ala ara wa ato abara ne, kuwɛ̃ iibawo wã ɔbara si Ɣaa kɔrɔ̃ iisia wũ iso.” Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Gbagbaã nto loɣere-ɔ sɔ si mailedza ɔturi iɣe ne, ɔ̃ibanya Ɣaa sigara iɖe ɔnya.” Ne Nikodemo ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Nda maabara maaledza ɔkpakpa iɣe gɔ ɔ̃isibawo ɔ̃ ɔnyi kayiri ame ɔkpese ɔbo?” Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Gbagbaã nto loɣere-ɔ sɔ, si maiɣe ɔturi makigu i ndu gu Ɣaa Siwarã ame ne, ɔ̃ibawo Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ame ɔbo.
Maɣese nsɛ maɣe ɔturi i siturina ame, ɣɛɛ Ɣaa Siwarã nsɛ siɣe ɔturi i siwarã ame.
Ne ɔso daatã ibara-ɔ ɣaa sɔ nto loɣere-ɔ sɔ ikote sɔ maaledza mi ɔɖuɖu iɣe.
Ɔwiri sɛ ɔkpɛ̃ ɔkɛlɛ ngbegɔ iɖe ɔɖɔɛ, ɣɛɛ ɔ̃ kulu kere iɖe aanɔ, aibatsue ngbegɔ iɖe ɔbɔrɛ, ɣee ngbegɔ iɖe ɔsɛ.
Ngbɔ ame nɖe ɔbiara gɔ maɣe makigu i Siwarã ame ne.” Ne Nikodemo ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Nda i nnɛgbe aabara iaba?” Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Fɔ lɛ ratedzekpakpa i Israel ne, aiɣe nnɛgbe?
Gbagbaã nto loɣere-ɔ sɔ, ara wa boɣe boto boɣere mi, fiɛ nwa bonya iso boto boɖe mi ika, ɣɛɛ miito mibie sɔ miafɔ nnɛ boto boɣere mi.
Si aito afɔ me aɖe si loɣere-ɔ kayiiso ngbe ara ne, nda aabara fiɛ aafɔ me aɖe si loɣere-ɔ ara wa mpia i kato?
Kuwɛ̃ iisɛ kato ɔnya iɖo mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, gɔ lose i kato ɔba karɔ̃.
“Lɛ kumɛgɔ i Mose ɔsu aɣɛ wa mabara ala ibɔra ɔsa i ɔdziri iso i fafuĩ ame ne, ngbɔ ame iɖe maakɔlɛ mme, Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi, kato ne, sɔ mma ɔɖuɖu lofɔ me maɖe ne, maana ngbã mɛ loisɛ miro.
“Alasɔ Ɣaa ɔbua ɔto ɔɖɔɛ kayiiso maturi sɔ ɔsu ɔ̃ Ɔbi ɔwɛ̃ saã ɔtã sɔ ɔbiara gɔ lofɔ wũ ɔɖe ne, ɔ̃ibawɔ, ɣɛɛ ɔ̃ana ngbã mɛ loisɛ miro.
Alasɔ Ɣaa iipia ɔ̃ Ɔbi sɔ ɔba ɔ̃atã kayiiso maturi ipɔ, ɣɛɛ sɔ si ɔba ɔ̃aɖe ma Ɖidze.
“Mma lofɔ Ɔbi maɖe ne, Ɣaa iitã ma ipɔ, ɣɛɛ mma loifɔ wũ maɖe ne, maɔɖe ipɔ koko alasɔ maifɔ Ɣaa Ɔbi ɔwɛ̃ saã maɖe.
Nnɛ ɔso i Ɣaa sɛ ɔtã maturi ipɔ nɖe sɔ, ikpawaĩ ɔba kayiiso, ɣɛɛ mato maɖɔɛ idududu maɖo ikpawaĩ alasɔ ma kurabarara ɔnyanyarĩ.
Mma ɔɖuɖu nsɛ mabara ara lalaa ɔtsiri ikpawaĩ, fiɛ maisɛ mabie sɔ maabore mabo ne alasɔ maito mabie sɔ ma ara lalaa si are kayi.
Ɣɛɛ mma nsɛ mabara ara i ɔnukuare ɔri iso, masɛ mabore maba ikpawaĩ kɔrɛ sɔ si iate sɔ mato makã Ɣaa atsue.” Ndupiedze Yohanes Ɔɖe Ika I Yesu Iso.
Nnɛgbe kama ne, Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔkɛlɛ Yudea ibuiti ame.
Ɔwegu ma i mmɔ kɛkɛĩ fiɛ ɔpie maturi Ɣaa ndu i ɔwore ame.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, Yohanes ɔ̃ wũ ɔto ɔpie maturi Ɣaa ndu i Aenon gɔ lobore ɔbo Salim alasɔ ndu ɔsi i mmɔ.
Maturi to maba ɔ̃ kɔrɛ fiɛ ɔto ɔpie ma Ɣaa ndu.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, maimɔɛ̃ Yohanes mapia i iyo.
Iyi iwɛ̃ ne, karawararã ɔbo i Yohanes marasuãdze gu ɔ Yudase ɔwɛ̃ ndɛ̃ i ma Yudase ifoforeso kubarara iso.
Ne ɔso maba maaɣere Yohanes sɔ, “Ratedze, ato anyigi ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ lowegu-ɔ i Yordan kama isɛ fiɛ aɖe ɔ̃ iso aɖansiɛ mmɔ?
Kiniɔ ne, ɔ̃ ka nto ɔpie maturi Ɣaa ndu fiɛ ma ɔɖuɖu ɔɔsore so makpa ɔ̃ kɔrɛ ne.” Yohanes ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Ɔturi iibawe kuira si iiɖe Ɣaa lotã wũ.
Mi mɔmɔ ɖe me aɖansiɛ sɔ loɣere mi sɔ, iiɖe me nɖe Kristo gɔmɔ, ne Ɣaa lopia me sɔ loɖe wũ katɔ̃.
Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ nto ɔkɔ ɔrɔ̃go ne, ɔ̃ mba ɔrɔ̃go ne.
Ɔ̃ ɔlaa gɔ nɖe ɔ̃ masaa fiɛ ɔɣɛ i ɔ̃ kɔrɛ ɔto ɔkã wũ atsue sɛ ɔna isoɣɔ si ɔto ɔnɔ ɔ̃ silɔ.
Ngbɔ ame i isoɣɔ ɔɔyi i wũ ame ne.
Ne ɔso ɔ̃ iyere aakɔlɛ kato, ɣɛɛ wũ ire aaba karɔ̃.
Ngɔ Lose I Kato Lokɔlɛ Ɔɖo.
“Ngɔ lose i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ɔmɔ ɔɖo ɔbiara.
Ngɔ lose i karɔ̃ iso ne, karɔ̃ iso ɔre ɔɖe fiɛ karɔ̃ iso ara iso ɔsɛ ɔɖe ika.
Ɣɛɛ ngɔ lose i kato ne, ɔɖo ma ɔɖuɖu.
Ɔsɛ ɔɣɛ ara wa ɔnya gu nwa ɔnɔ, ɣɛɛ kuwɛ̃ iisɛ ɔfɔ ɔ̃ itɔ̃me.
Ɣɛɛ ngɔ lofɔ ɔ̃ itɔ̃me ɔɖe ɔsia ita sɔ Ɣaa ne, ɔnukuarese ɔɖe.
Ngɔ i Ɣaa ɔpia katɔ̃me ne, ɔsɛ ɔɣɛ Ɣaa itɔ̃me, alasɔ Ɣaa sɛ ɔtã ɔ̃ Siwarã ɔyi i ɔ̃ ame.
Ɣaa sɛ ɔɖɔɛ ɔ̃ Ɔbi, fiɛ ɔsu ira biara ɔpia i ɔ̃ ɔle kayirinɔ.
“Ɔbiara gɔ lofɔ Ɔbi ɔɖe ba ngbã mɛ loibaro, ɣɛɛ ɔbiara gɔ losɛ̃ Ɣaa Ɔbi atsue ikã ne, ɔ̃ibana ngbã, ɣɛɛ Ɣaa kutsue ikpadzɛ̃ sia wũ iso.”
Yesu Ɔɖegu Samaria Ɔrɔ̃go Ɔwɛ̃ Ika.
Ma Farisise ɔnɔ sɔ Yesu to ɔpie maturi Ɣaa ndu, fiɛ ɔto ɔna marasuãdze ɔɖo Yohanes.
Atoa sɔ Yesu mɔmɔ iipie kuwɛ̃ Ɣaa ndu, ɣɛɛ ɔ̃ marasuãdze nto mabara.
Ne ɔso Yesu ɔrui i Yudea ɔkpese ɔkɛlɛ Galilea.
Ɣɛɛ ne, ipia sɔ ɔ̃aki i Samaria karɔ̃ iso fiɛ ɔ̃akɛlɛ.
Yesu ɔba ɔ̃abo Samaria ɔmagɛ̃ gɔ marɔ sɔ Sikar kabenya.
Ɔmagɛ̃ gɔgbe ɔbore ɔbo iputu nɛ i ma ɔwa Yakob ɔtã ɔ̃ ɔbi Yosef.
Yakob itubiɔ nɛ ɔɖi pia i mmɔ.
Gɔ Yesu ɔba ɔ̃abo mmɔ lɛ kakɔme iɖɔwũ iweo-inyɔ ame ne, iɖa wũ ala ɔsɛ ɔso, ne ɔso ɔkpase ɔsɛ i itubiɔ nɛgbe kɔrɛ.
Samaria ɔrɔ̃go ɔwɛ̃ ɔba sɔ ɔba ɔ̃aɖu ndu, ne ɔso Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Tã me ndu lonɛ.” Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, Yesu marasuãdze ɔrui makpa ɔmagɛ̃ ame maaɣa araɖea.
Ɔrɔ̃go gɔgbe ɔkarɛ Yesu sɔ, “Nda ibara fiɛ fɔ ɔ Yudase to akarɛ me Samaria ɔrɔ̃go ndu nɛa?” Ɔkarɛ wũ ngbɔ alasɔ ma Yudase gu ma Samariase iisɛ mafe.
Yesu ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Si ɔɣe aɣe Ɣaa karatã gu ngɔ nto ɔkarɛ-ɔ ndu ne, tee fɔ bowũ fɔ loakarɛ wũ sɔ ɔtã-ɔ ndu mɛ nsɛ mitã ngbã.” Ɔrɔ̃go ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Tete, gɔ ana nnɛ aaɖu ala ndu, fiɛ itubiɔ ana ɔwodoro ne, lɛ aaka ndu mɛ nsɛ mitã ngbã ngbe abɔrɛgu?
Ɛɛbɛrɛ fɔ loɖo bo Ɔwa Yakob gɔ loɖi itubiɔ nɛgbe ɔtã bo fiɛ ɔ̃ gu ɔ̃ mabi gu ma mabɔi ɔnɛ ndu mɛgbe?” Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ɔbiara gɔ nsɛ ɔnɛ ndu mɛgbe ne, ɔme to ɔ̃aledza wũ ikore.
Ɣɛɛ ngɔ loanɛ ndu mɛ loatã wũ ne, ɔme iisibakore wũ ɔnya.
Alasɔ ndu mɛ loatã wũ ɔnɛ to miakpese ndu gɔdɛ̃a mɛ nto mibore mife ɔwi biara i ɔ̃ ame mitã wũ ngbã mɛ loisɛ miro.” Ɔrɔ̃go ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Bosate, tã me ndu mɛgbe lonɛ si ɔme iisibakore me ɔnya sɔ loibakpese loba ngbe sɔ loba loaɖu ndu.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Kɛlɛ aakpere fɔ ɔrã si miba.” Ɔrɔ̃go ɔɣere Yesu sɔ, “Lona kurã.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Aɣɛ ɔnukuare sɔ ana kurã.
Gbaã iɖe aɣɛ.
Alasɔ ɔɔyiri marɛrɛ̃ iru anya, fiɛ ngɔ iyo asi kiniɔ ana ne, iiɖe fɔ ɔrã ɔɖe.” Ɔrɔ̃go ɔɣere Yesu sɔ, “Tete, lonya sɔ Ɣaa kanyaɖidze aɖe!
Bo ma Samariase mawa ɔsɔrɛ Ɣaa i kube gɔgbe iso, ɣɛɛ mi ma Yudase sɔ Yerusalem nɖe ngbegɔ boasɔrɛ Ɣaa.” Ne Yesu ɔɖi kanya sɔ, “Ɔrɔ̃go, fɔ me ɖe sɔ ɔwi to ɔba gɔ maturi iisibasɔrɛ bo Ɔse Ɣaa i kube gɔgbe iso, ɣee Yerusalem.
Mi ma Samariase ne, miiɣe ngɔ mito misɔrɛ.
Ɣɛɛ bo ma Yudase ne, boɣe ngɔ boto bosɔrɛ, alasɔ bo kɔrɛ i Ɣaa iɖi ɔbɔrɛ.
Ɣɛɛ ɔwi to ɔba fiɛ ɔwi gɔmɔ ɔɔɣo sɔ Ɣaa masɔrɛdze gbaã aasɔrɛ wũ i Ɔ̃ Siwarã gu ɔnukuare ame, alasɔ masɔrɛdze magbe igbã i Ɣaa to ɔbie ne.
Gɔ Ɣaa ne Siwarã ɔɖe ɔso ne, ɔ̃ Siwarã ɔle gu ɔnukuare ame pɛ i maturi aawo ɔki fiɛ maasɔrɛ wũ lɛ kumɛgɔ ikote.” Ne ɔrɔ̃go ɔɣere Yesu sɔ, “Loɣe sɔ Mesia gɔ marɔ sɔ Kristo to ɔ̃aba, fiɛ si ɔba ne, ɔto ɔ̃aɖi ira biara ɔɣere bo.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Mme gɔ mme nto loɖegu-ɔ ika ne, mme nɖe wũ ne.” Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, Yesu marasuãdze ɔba maabo fiɛ ibara ma ɣaa sɔ ɔto ɔɖegu ɔrɔ̃go ika, ɣɛɛ ma kuwɛ̃ iiwo ɔrɔ̃go ɔkarɛ sɔ, “Be ato abie?” ɣee makarɛ Bosate sɔ, “Be ɔso ato aɖegu wũ ika?” Ɔrɔ̃go ɔnyua ɔ̃ ituɖura ɔsɛ ɔrui ɔkɛlɛ ɔmagɛ̃ ame ɔsɛ ɔ̃aɣere maturi sɔ, “Miba mianyɔ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ loɣere me ira biara nɛ loɔbara lonya i wũ ngbã ame!
Bɛrɛ ɔ̃ nɖe Kristo gɔmɔ?” Ne ɔso maturi ɔbɔrɛ i ɔmagɛ̃ ame makɛlɛ sɔ maanyɔ Yesu.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, marasuãdze to mapɛ Yesu nrɔɔ̃ sɔ, “Ratedze, boto-ɔ i kukpa sɔ ba ɖe ara!” Ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Loba aɖera wa loaɖe ɣɛɛ miiɣe wã.” Ne ɔso marasuãdze ɔtsɛ so ikarɛ sɔ, “Bɛrɛ ɔwɛ̃ ɔbɔ wũ aɖera fiɛ boiɣe?” Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Wũ aɖera nɖe sɔ loabara ngɔ lopia me katɔ̃me kuɖɔɛ, lobara karabara ga ɔpia me lowiri.
Mi nsɛ miɣɛ sɔ, ‘Awa ana loɔkuti fiɛ ɔraɖui aabo kaa,’ ɣɛɛ mme nto loɣere mi sɔ, si minyɔ nkpɛkɔ̃ iso kukaakɔ ne, mianya sɔ kamɔ ɔɔbe kanya irui!
Ngɔ nto ɔsɔrɛ̃ ɔraɖui fiɛ ɔto ɔsa ɔraɖui kanya ɔtã ngbã mɛ loisɛ miro i Ɣaa sɛ ɔtã kuso.
Ne ɔso ngɔ losa ɔraɖui gu ngɔ losɔrɛ̃ ɔraɖui isoɣɔ aaɖe iwɛ̃.
Ne ɔso itɔ̃me nɛgbe pia i ne ame sɔ, ‘Ɔturi ɔwɛ̃ sɛ ɔsa ɔraɖui fiɛ ɔmama ana sɛ ɔsɔrɛ̃ ɔraɖui.’ Lopia mi sɔ misɛ miasɔrɛ̃ ɔraɖui i kakpɛkɔ̃ ga iiɖe mi lokpɛ̃ ame, maturi mama lobara karabara i mmɔ, ɣɛɛ mi loana kã kusia.” Ma Samariase Gbodzoo Ɔfɔ Yesu Maɖe.
Ma Samariase gbodzoo i ɔmagɛ̃ gɔmɔ ame ɔfɔ Yesu maɖe, alasɔ ɔrɔ̃go gɔmɔ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ɔɣere me ira biara nɛ loɔbara lonya i wũ ngbã ame.” Gɔ mabɔrɛ maba ɔ̃ kɔrɛ ne, mapɛ wũ nrɔɔ̃ sɔ ɔwe i ma kɔrɛ kɛkɛĩ, ne ɔso Yesu ɔwe i ma kɔrɛ ayi anyɔ.
Maturi gbodzoo mama ana ɔfɔ wũ maɖe gɔ manɔ ɔ̃ itɔ̃me.
Ne maɣere ɔrɔ̃go sɔ, “Kiniɔ ne, bofɔ wũ boɖe, iiɖe nnɛ aɣere bo ɔso, ɣɛɛ bo mɔmɔ ɔɔnɔ ɔ̃ itɔ̃me fiɛ boɣe sɔ ɔ̃ nɖe kayiiso Ɖidze gbaã.” Yesu Ɔsa Ɔkpakpa Ɔwɛ̃ Ɔbi.
Ayi anyɔ kama ne, Yesu ɔbɔrɛ i mmɔ ɔkɛlɛ Galilea karɔ̃ iso.
Atoa sɔ Yesu mɔmɔ ɔɣɛ ku ɔwi gɔ lofe ame sɔ, “Ɣaa kanyaɖidze na kuwarɛ i ɔ̃ mɔmɔ aɖe ne,” gɔ ɔba ɔ̃abo Galilea ne, mafɔ wũ kukaakɔ, alasɔ gɔ masɛ Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo Iyi iɖe i Yerusalem ne, manya ira biara nɛ ɔbara i iyi kaɖekɔ̃.
Yesu ɔkpese ɔkɛlɛ Kana i Galilea ngbegɔ ɔfinikira ndu ɔbara ndã ɔnya.
Abã ɔkpakpa ɔwɛ̃ pia i mmɔ gɔ ɔbi birɛrɛĩ nto ɔnyɛ i Kapernaum.
Gɔ ɔnɔ sɔ Yesu ɔbɔrɛ i Yudea ɔba Galilea ne, ɔba ɔ̃apɛ wũ nrɔɔ̃ ɔɣere wũ sɔ ɔba makɛlɛ Kapernaum si ɔba ɔ̃asa ɔ̃ ɔbi gɔ nto ɔnyɛ fiɛ ɔ̃ɔro ɔkpi.
Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Si miinya awawãra gu akparĩ ne, miisɛ mifɔ miɖe.” Ɣɛɛ ɔkpakpa gɔmɔ ɔtã Yesu iti sɔ, “Bosate, loto-ɔ i kukpa sɔ ba bokɛlɛ si wũ ɔbi iibakpi.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Kɛlɛ ne fɔ ɔbi to ɔ̃awe ngbã.” Ɔkpakpa gɔgbe ɔfɔ nnɛ i Yesu ɔɣere wũ ɔɖe, ne ɔso ɔrui ɔɣo ma aɖe ɔri.
Ɔwi gɔ ɔsɛ ɔto ɔkɛlɛ ne, ɔ̃ maɖabo ɔba maaɣere wũ sɔ, “Fɔ ɔbi ɔɔsarɛ!” Ɔkarɛ ma sɔ mme ɔwi ame iɖe ɔsarɛ.
Ne matã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Lɛ kakɔme ɔɖɔwũ ɔwɛ̃ ame ku kɔmakaɖe i kubetɔ ɔta wũ iso.” Ne ɔ̃ ɔse ɔnyigi sɔ ɔwi gɔmɔ ame tutuutu iɖe i Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Fɔ ɔbi to ɔ̃awe ngbã,” ne.
Ne ɔso ɔ̃ gu ɔ̃ iyo maturi ɔɖuɖu ɔfɔ Yesu maɖe.
Nnɛgbe nɖe iwawãra nyɔare nɛ i Yesu ɔbara i Galilea karɔ̃ iso gɔ ɔse i Yudea ɔba.
Yesu Ɔsa Ɔrɛrɛ̃ Ɔwɛ̃ I Itubu Kɔrɛ.
Nnɛgbe kama ne, gɔ ma Yudase to maɖe ma iyi iwɛ̃ ne, Yesu ɔsɛ Yerusalem.
I ɔmagɛ̃ ame ne, kayogodɔ̃ kawɛ̃ pia ga masɛ marɔ sɔ Masɛrɛ Kayogodɔ̃.
I kã kɔrɛ ne, ibu iwɛ̃ nɛ i kukpakɛ kuru ɔki kulɔ se fiɛ masɛ marɔ ibu nɛgbe sɔ Betesda i ma Yudase siɖe ame.
Manyɛse gbodzoo rɛ i kukpakɛ gɔgbe kayirinɔ.
Ma mawɛ̃ ɖe manɔbiɛdze, mawɛ̃ ɖe mabafã gu mma lokpi kasɛkasɛ.
(Marɛ i mmɔ alasɔ ipɔlɛipɔlɛ ne, Ɣaa kpabo sɛ ɔba ɔ̃atidza ndu.
Nyɛse gɔ loaɖe katɔ̃ ɔbo me ame si matidza ndu sɛ ɔna isosarɛ ɔluwɛ̃.)
Ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ rɛ i mmɔ gɔ ɔto ɔnyɛ akɔ sitɛ farafana.
Gɔ Yesu ɔnya wũ fiɛ ɔtsue sɔ ɔ̃ɔrɛ i mmɔ ɔwi ɔdzoro ne, ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ato abie sɔ aasarɛ?” Ne nyɛse to ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Tete, lona kuwɛ̃ gɔ loaputa me ɔpia i ndu ame si matidza me, fiɛ si loto lokpɛ̃ sɔ loabo i ibu ame ne, ɔturi mama sɛ ɔɖe me katɔ̃.” Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ta si akarĩ fɔ ɔkala si asɛ.” Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, ɔsarɛ, ɔsu ɔ̃ ɔkala ɔtsɛ isɛ.
Iyi nɛ ira nɛgbe ɔba ne, ma Yudase Iwarãyi iɖe.
Ne ɔso gɔ ma Yudase makpakpa ɔnya ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe gɔ ɔto ɔ̃ ɔkala ne, maɣere wũ sɔ, “Iwarãyi iɖe nɔme, ne ɔso ita iya i bo mmara iso sɔ aala fɔ ɔkala asɛ.” Ɣɛɛ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ losa me loɣere me sɔ, ‘Su fɔ ɔkala si asɛ.’ ” Ne makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Nna ɔɖe loɣere-ɔ sɔ bara ngbɔ?” Ɣɛɛ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe iiɣe ngɔ i Yesu ɖe, fiɛ maturi ana ɔsi i mmɔ, ne ɔso Yesu ɔma ɔbo i ma ndɛ̃ ɔrui i mmɔ.
Ne kama ne, Yesu ɔnya wũ i Isɔrɛyo, ne ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Nyɔ, kiniɔ gɔ ɔɔsarɛ ne, daasibara ikpi sɔ nnɛ loɖo ngbe aaba iabara-ɔ.” Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔmɔ ɔrui ɔsɛ ɔ̃aɣere ma Yudase makpakpa sɔ Yesu ɔɖe losa wũ.
Ne ɔso matsɛ Yesu kama iti, alasɔ ɔsa ɔturi ku Iwarãyi.
Ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Wũ Ɔse to ɔbara karabara ɔwi biara ame, ne ɔso me wũ loto lobara karabara.” Nnɛ i Yesu ɔɣɛ ngbe ɔtã ma Yudase makpakpa ɔsia ita sɔ ngbɛsi maɖoe wũ.
Manya sɔ iiɖe ma mmara kere miɖe ɔtu, ɣɛɛ ana ne, ɔsu so ɔbara Ɣaa Ɔbi gɔ ite sɔ ɔkategu Ɣaa.
Ɣaa Ɔbi Ɔle Gɔ Ɔba.
Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Gbagbaã nto loɣere mi sɔ, Ɣaa Ɔbi iibawo kuira ɔbara i ɔ̃ mɔmɔ ɔle ame iɖo nnɛ ɔnya ɔ̃ Ɔse to ɔbara, fiɛ nnɛ i Ɔse to ɔbara ne, ne i Ɔbi sɛ ɔbara ne.
Alasɔ Ɔse to ɔɖɔɛ Ɔbi ne ɔso ɔsɛ ɔte wũ ira biara nɛ ɔto ɔbara.
Ɔse to ɔ̃ate ara wa lomɔ aɖo ngbe gɔ ito iabara mi ɣii.
Kumɛgɔ ame i Ɔse sɛ ɔtara makpise ɔtã ma ngbã ne, ngbɔ ame i Ɔbi ana sɛ ɔtã mma ɔto ɔɖɔɛ ngbã ne.
Ɔse mɔmɔ iisɛ ɔɣɛgu kuwɛ̃ atɔ̃me, ɣɛɛ ɔsu atɔ̃me iɣɛ ɔle ɔɖuɖu ɔpia i Ɔbi nrɔɔ̃ ame.
Ɔse ɔbara ngbɔ sɔ si maturi ɔɖuɖu aawarɛ Ɔbi lɛ kumɛgɔ masɛ mawarɛ Ɔse.
Ɔbiara gɔ loisɛ ɔwarɛ Ɔbi iisɛ ɔwarɛ Ɔse gɔ lopia wũ katɔ̃me.
“Gbaã nto loɣere mi sɔ ngɔ nsɛ ɔnɔ wũ itɔ̃me fiɛ ɔfɔ ngɔ lopia me katɔ̃me ɔɖe ba ngbã mɛ loisɛ miro.
Ɣaa iibaɣɛgu wũ atɔ̃me, ɣɛɛ ɔ̃ɔbɔrɛ i kukpi ame ɔbo i ngbã ame.
Gbaã nto loɣere mi sɔ ɔwi to ɔba fiɛ ɔwi ɔɔɣo gɔ makpise aanɔ Ɣaa Ɔbi silɔ fiɛ mma lonɔ to maata masɛ ngbã.
Kumɛgɔ ame i Ɔse ɖe ngbã Sate ne, ngbɔ ame iɖe ɔbara Ɔbi ana sɔ ɔɖe ngbã Sate ne.
Fiɛ ɔtã wũ ɔle sɔ ɔɣɛgu maturi atɔ̃me alasɔ ɔ̃ nɖe Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi.
“Nnɛgbe si idaabara mi ɣaa alasɔ ɔwi to ɔba gɔ makpise ɔɖuɖu to maanɔ ɔ̃ silɔ, fiɛ maata mabɔrɛ i ma akpibiɔ ame.
Mma lobara ara sɛɛ to maata masɛ ngbã, ɣɛɛ mma lobara ikpi ana to maata matã kutsue ikpadzɛ̃.
“Loibawo kuira ɔbara i wũ ɔle ame, nsɛ loɣɛgu maturi atɔ̃me lɛ kumɛgɔ i Ɣaa ɔɣere me.
Ne ɔso wũ atɔ̃me iɣɛ se tɔrɔrɔ, alasɔ loisɛ lobara nnɛ loɖɔɛ, ɣɛɛ nnɛ i ngɔ lopia me katɔ̃me ɔɖɔɛ nsɛ lobara.
Mma Nɖe Yesu Maɖansiɛ.
“Si loɖe so aɖansiɛ ne, iyɔ wũ aɖansiɛ iibaɖe ɔnukuare.
Ɣɛɛ ɔmama pia gɔ nsɛ ɔɖe me aɖansiɛ fiɛ loɣe sɔ nnɛ ɔsɛ ɔɣɛ i wũ iso ne, gbaã iɖe.
“Mipia mi makpabo Yohanes kɔrɛ i wũ iso, fiɛ ɔɖe aɖansiɛ i ɔnukuare iso.
Iiɖe sɔ ɔnya ko inya sɔ loana ɔturi awune ɔɖe me aɖansiɛ, ɣɛɛ loto loɣɛ ngbɔ sɔ si miana iɖi.
Yohanes se lɛ ɔkaniɛ gɔ losa, fiɛ miɖɔɛ ɔwi kurukutu sɔ miawe i ɔ̃ ikpawaĩ ame ku isoɣɔ.
“Ɣɛɛ loba aɖansiɛ wa mba ɔrɔrã aɖo Yohanes ɔkpɛ.
Wã nɖe wũ kurabarara gɔ losɛ lobara ne.
Karabara ga i Tete ɔtã me sɔ lobara loro ne, kã nsɛ kaɖe me aɖansiɛ sɔ ɔ̃ lopia me katɔ̃me ne.
Fiɛ Tete gɔ lopia me katɔ̃me ana sɛ ɔɖe me aɖansiɛ.
Miinɔ ɔ̃ silɔ minɔ fiɛ miinya wũ ana minya.
Miisɛ mimɔɛ̃ ɔ̃ itɔ̃me mipia i mi situ ame, alasɔ miifɔ ngɔ ɔpia katɔ̃me miɖe.
Misɛ mifafarɛ Ɔko Sekelea ame, alasɔ minyɔ sɔ ne ame miana ngbã mɛ loisɛ miro, ɣɛɛ wũ iso matsɛrɛ ara wagbe ɔɖuɖu masegu.
Ɣɛɛ miito mibie sɔ miaba wũ kɔrɛ fiɛ miana ngbã mɛmɔ.
“Loito lobie ɔturi awune ile, alasɔ loɣe maturi ma igbã miɖe fiɛ loɣe sɔ miisɛ miɖɔɛ Ɣaa i mi situ ame.
Loba i wũ Ɔse ɔle ame, ɣɛɛ miifɔ me, si ɔrere ɔba i ɔ̃ mɔmɔ ɔle ame ne, mito miafɔ wũ.
Misɛ miɖɔɛ sɔ mi malaa si male mi, ɣɛɛ miisɛ mibie sɔ ngɔ ɔnɔwɛ̃ nɖe Ɣaa si ɔle mi.
Ne ɔso nda miabara fiɛ miafɔ me miɖe?
“Midaanyɔ ɔri sɔ me loatã mi ipɔ i Tete kɔrɛ.
Mose gɔ ame i mi ɔɖuɖu ɔriinyɔ pia ne, ɔ̃ mɔmɔ loatã mi ipɔ ne.
Si gbaã iɖe sɔ mifɔ Mose miɖe ne, tee miafɔ me miɖe, alasɔ wũ iso ɔtsɛrɛ ara ɔsegu.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ miifɔ nnɛ ɔtsɛrɛ miɖe ne, nda miabara fiɛ miafɔ nnɛ loɣere mi miɖe?”
Yesu Ɔtã Maturi Kukpi Kuru Aɖera Maɖe.
Nnɛgbe kama ne, Yesu ɔwara Galilea itubu nɛ masɛ marɔ ana sɔ Tiberia itubu.
Maturi gbodzoo siai wũ alasɔ kumɛgɔ ɔto ɔsa sinyɛ ɔbara ma ɣii.
Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔya kabemi kawɛ̃ masɛ maasɛ i kã iso.
Ma Yudase Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo Iyi iɖe ana ɔɔbore ibo.
Gɔ Yesu ɔnyɔ ne, ɔnya maturi gbodzoo to maba ɔ̃ kɔrɛ, ne ɔso ɔkarɛ Filipo sɔ, “Lɛ boaɣa aɖera wa losi aaɣo mmagbe ɔɖuɖu maɖe?” Ɔɣɛ ngbɔ si ɔkere Filipo ɔnyɔ atoa sɔ ka ɔɣe koko nnɛ ɔto ɔba ɔ̃abara.
Ne Filipo to ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Maturi alafa anyɔ ikpɛnɛ kuso kɔra iibawo aɖera ɔɣa aɣo mmagbe ɔɖe nane kɛkɛĩ kɛkɛĩ!” Mmɔ ne rasuãdze mama gɔ nɖe Andrea gɔ nɖe Simon Petro ɔnyiibi ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Ɔbirɛrɛĩ ɔwɛ̃ pia i ngbe gɔ mba abolo kuboi kuru gu kufarai kunyɔ, ɣɛɛ ne, be i nnɛmɔ aabara maturi gbodzoo magbe?” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mitã maturi si masɛ i karɔ̃.” Mmɔ ɔkpa ne ɔso masɛ i sikua iso.
Marɛrɛ̃ kerekere aaɖe lɛ kukpi kuru ɔɖui.
Ne Yesu ɔfɔ aɖera ne, ɔpɛ ɣaa siba i wã iti fiɛ ka ɔsu ɔɣɛɣɛ mma nsi karɔ̃.
Ɔfɔ kufarai kuna fiɛ ɔbara ngbɔ ame, ɔbiara ɔɖe ara ɔmi.
Gɔ ma ɔɖuɖu ɔɔɖe mami ne, ɔɣere ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Mimala kupupui ɔɖuɖu ne midaatã kukawɛ̃ si kanina.” Ne ɔso masa kupupui gɔ lokpɛkpɛti i abolo kuboi kuru gɔ i maturi ɔɖe ɔɖuɖu kanya ne, kuyi kusɛsɛi kuweo-kunyɔ.
Gɔ mma mpia i mmɔ ɔnya iwawãra nɛ i Yesu ɔbara ne, maɣɛ sɔ, “Gbaã ne, Kanyaɖidze gɔ sɔ ɔto ɔ̃aba i ngbe ne!” Ne gɔ Yesu ɔnya sɔ mato mabie sɔ maaba maamɔɛ̃ wũ sigara i so ɔle ame ne, ɔrui i ma kɔrɛ ɔkɛlɛ kube iso ɔ̃ ɔnɔwɛ̃.
Yesu Ɔsɛ I Ndu Iso.
Kutsuɛ gɔmɔ ne, ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔrui makɛlɛ itubu kɔrɛ.
Gɔ maya mabo i ɔkolo ame ne, matsɛ iwa ikɛlɛ Kapernaum isɛ, atoa sɔ kaɖe ɔɔro ne, Yesu iiba ɔ̃abo ma kɔrɛ.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ne, ndu to miɖa so ala ɔwiri to ɔkpɛ̃ teteree.
Gɔ marasuãdze ɔɔwa ɔkolo masɛ i ndu iso lɛ agu atɛ ito ikɛlɛ ana kere ne, manya Yesu sɛ i ndu iso ɔto ɔba ɔkolo kɔrɛ, ne ɔso ifɔ̃ ɔmɔɛ̃ ma!
Ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Midaanigã ne mme loɖe!” Ma situ ɔkpase sisɛ, mafɔ wũ mapia i ɔkolo ame kere fiɛ mabo ɔkpokpo ngbegɔ masɛ ne.
Maturi Ɔnyɔnyɔ Yesu.
Gɔ kaɖe ɔsɛ̃ ne, maturi gbodzoo ma lowe i itubu ɔkpokpo gɔmɔ isɛ ɔnya sɔ ɔkolo ɔwɛ̃ pɛ lose i mmɔ.
Maɣe sɔ Yesu iibo i ɔkolo gɔmɔ ame gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze ne ma ɔnɔwɛ̃ lorui.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ne, sikolo mama dzɛ lose i Tiberia ɔba siabo i ngbegɔ i Bosate ɔpɛ Ɣaa siba i aɖera iti ɔsu ɔtã maturi ɔɖe kɔrɛ.
Ne ɔso gɔ maturi gbodzoo mamɔ ɔnya sɔ Yesu ɣee ɔ̃ marasuãdze na i mmɔ ne, mata mabo i sikolo ame makɛlɛ Kapernaum sɔ maanyɔnyɔ wũ.
Yesu Nɖe Ngbã Aɖera.
Gɔ manya Yesu i itubu ɔkpokpo gɔmɔ isɛ ne, makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ratedze, ku mme ɔwi abo ngbe?” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Gbaã loto loɣere mi sɔ, miito mibie me alasɔ minɔ wũ awawãra karɔ̃, ɣɛɛ sɔ mina aɖera miɖe mimi ɔso.
Midaamararã so i aɖera wa loanina iso, ɣɛɛ i nwa loase atã ngbã mɛ loisɛ miro.
Aɖera wagbe i Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi aatã mi ne, alasɔ Ɣaa gɔ nɖe Ɔse ɔɔpɛ wũ kufe.” Ne makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Nda boabara fiɛ boawo nnɛ i Ɣaa to ɔɖɔɛ ɔbara?” Yesu ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Nnɛ i Ɣaa to ɔbie sɔ mibara nɖe sɔ miafɔ ngɔ ɔpia katɔ̃me miɖe.” Makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Mme iwawãra aabara ate bo bonya fiɛ boafɔ-ɔ boɖe?
Be aawo ɔbara?
Bo mawa ɔɖe aɖera wa marɔ sɔ mana i fafuĩ ame lɛ kumɛgɔ i Ɣaa itɔ̃me ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Ɣaa ɔtã ma aɖera wa lobɔrɛ i kato maɖe.’ ” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Gbaã loto loɣere mi sɔ, iiɖe Mose ɔɖe lotã mi aɖera wa lobɔrɛ i kato, ɣɛɛ wũ Ɔse nsɛ ɔtã aɖera gbaã wa lobɔrɛ i kato.
Alasɔ aɖera wa i Ɣaa sɛ ɔtã nɖe ngɔ lose i kato ɔba fiɛ ɔsɛ ɔtã kayiiso maturi ngbã.” Ne maɣere wũ sɔ, “Bosate, la ɔɔtã bo aɖera wagbe ɔwi biara.” Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mme nɖe ngbã aɖera wamɔ ne.
Ngɔ loba wũ kɔrɛ ne, kukã iibakpɛ̃ wũ kunya, fiɛ ngɔ lofɔ me ɔɖe ne, ɔme iibakore wũ ɔnya.
Ɣɛɛ, nto loɣere mi sɔ atoa sɔ miɔnya me ne, miifɔ me miɖe.
Ɔbiara gɔ i wũ Ɔse ɔsu ɔtã me ne, ɔto ɔ̃aba wũ kɔrɛ, fiɛ loibasɛ̃ kuwɛ̃ gɔ loba wũ kɔrɛ lonya.
Alasɔ loise i kato loba sɔ loaba loabara wũ kuɖɔɛ, ɣɛɛ ngɔ lopia me katɔ̃me kuɖɔɛ loabara.
Fiɛ ngɔ lopia me katɔ̃me kuɖɔɛ nɖe sɔ loibayura kuwɛ̃ i mma ɔɖuɖu ɔsu ɔtã me ndɛ̃, ɣɛɛ sɔ loatara ma ɔɖuɖu lobɔ ngbã ku iyi tsɔra.
Alasɔ nnɛ i wũ Ɔse to ɔbie nɖe sɔ, ɔbiara gɔ lonya Ɔbi fiɛ ɔfɔ wũ ɔɖe ne, ɔ̃ana ngbã mɛ loisɛ miro, fiɛ iyi tsɔra ne, loatara wũ ɔsɛ ngbã.” Ma Yudase ɔtsɛ siwũti alasɔ ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Mme nɖe aɖera wa lose i kato.” Ne maɣɛ sɔ, “Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ne, iiɖe Yosef ɔbi Yesu ɔɖe ɣɛɛ?
Boɣe ɔ̃ ɔse gu ɔ̃ ɔnyi, ne ɔso lɛ ise ɔto ɔɣɛ sɔ kato ɔse?” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Minyua so ɔwararã.
Kuwɛ̃ iibawo wũ kɔrɛ ɔba si iiɖe Tete gɔ lopia me katɔ̃me loboregu wũ ɔpia me, fiɛ loatara wũ lobɔrɛgu i makpise ame ku iyi tsɔra.
Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze ɔtsɛrɛ masɛ sɔ, ‘Ɣaa to ɔ̃ate ma ɔɖuɖu ara.’ Ne ɔso ɔbiara gɔ nsɛ ɔkã atsue fiɛ ɔsɛ ɔsuã ara ɔbɔrɛgu i Tete kɔrɛ ne, ɔsɛ ɔba wũ kɔrɛ.
Nnɛgbe iite sɔ kuwɛ̃ ɔɔnya Tete ɔnya.
Ngɔ lobɔrɛ i Ɣaa kɔrɛ pɛ nɖe ngɔ loɔnya Tete ɔnya.
Gbaã loto loɣere mi sɔ ngɔ lofɔ ɔɖe ne, ɔba ngbã mɛ loisɛ miro.
Mme nɖe aɖera wa nsɛ atã ngbã.
Mi mawa ɔɖe aɖera wa marɔ mana i fafuĩ ame, ɣɛɛ makpi.
Ɣɛɛ aɖera wa nsɛ abɔrɛ i kato ne, aɖe aɖera wa i ɔbiara gɔ loɖe wã iibakpi.
Mme nɖe aɖera wa mba ngbã fiɛ abɔrɛ i kato ne.
Ɔbiara gɔ loaɖe aɖera wagbe ne, ɔto ɔ̃asɛ ngbã sɔ ɔ̃ibakpi.
Aɖera wa loatã wũ nɖe wũ sosina dzɛ loasu lotã sɔ kayiiso maturi aana ngbã.” Ne ma Yudase ɔtsɛgu so kakpadzɛ̃ i sikpã ame mato makarɛ sɔ, “Nda i ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe aasu ɔ̃ siturina ɔtã bo boɖe?” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Gbaã loto loɣere mi sɔ, si miiwe Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi sina, minɛ ɔ̃ ima ne, ngbã kumiwɛ̃ iibawe i mi ame.
Ngɔ lowe wũ siturina, fiɛ ɔnɛ wũ ima ba ngbã mɛ nna katui fiɛ loatara wũ lobɔrɛgu i makpise ame ku iyi tsɔra.
Alasɔ wũ siturina nɖe aɖera mɔmɔ fiɛ wũ ima nɖe ira sɛɛ nɛ maanɛ.
Ngɔ lowe wũ siturina fiɛ ɔnɛ wũ ima ne, ɔpia i wũ ame fiɛ mme wũ lopia i ɔ̃ ame.
Kumɛgɔ i Tete gɔ mba ngbã ɔpia me katɔ̃me fiɛ iki i ɔ̃ ame ne loba ngbã ne, ngbɔ ame i ngɔ lowe wũ siturina aawe ngbã ne.
Nwagbe nɖe aɖera wa lose i kato aba ne, aise lɛ nwa i mi mawa ɔɖe ɣɛɛ makpi.
Ɔbiara gɔ loaɖe aɖera wa loto loɣɛ ala ngbe iibakpi ɔnya.” Yesu ɔɣɛ ara wagbe gɔ ɔto ɔte ara i ma Yudase kasarɛkɔ̃ i Kapernaum.
Atɔ̃me Wa Nsɛ Atã Ngbã Mɛ Loisɛ Miro.
Gɔ marasuãdze gbodzoo ɔnɔ ara ite nɛgbe ne, maɣɛ sɔ, “Ara wa ɔto ɔte ngbe ba ɔle gbaã!
Nna loafɔ wã?” Atoa sɔ kuwɛ̃ iiɣere Yesu kuira ne, ɔɣe nnɛ siwũti mato, ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mi wũ nnɛgbe ɔta iya mi iso?
Ne iyɔ nda iabara mi si minya Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi ɔya ɔkɛlɛ kato ngbegɔ ɔwe koko.
Ɣaa Siwarã nsɛ sitã ngbã, ɔturi ɔle na i kuira ame.
Atɔ̃me wa loɣere mi ne, siwarã gu ngbã aɖe.
Ɣɛɛ mi mawɛ̃ iifɔ me miɖe.” Yesu ɔɣere ma ngbɔ ala ta karɔ̃kasɛkɔ̃ ne, ɔɣe mma loifɔ wũ maɖe gu ngɔ loaɖi wũ ɔtã.
Ne ka ɔɣere ma ana sɔ, “Nnɛgbe ɔso loɣere mi sɔ kuwɛ̃ iibawo wũ kɔrɛ ɔba si iiɖe Tete loɖi wũ ɔri ne.” Ita i ɔwi gɔgbe ame ne, Yesu marasuãdze gbodzoo ɔkpese wũ i kama sɔ maisibasiai wũ.
Ne Yesu ɔfiniki ɔkarɛ marasuãdze iweo-inyɔ ma wũ sɔ, “Mi wũ miakpese me i kama?” Simon Petro ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Bosate, nna kɔrɛ boakɛlɛ?
Aba atɔ̃me wa nsɛ atã ngbã.
Fiɛ ana ne, bofɔ boɖe, fiɛ boɣe sɔ fɔ nɖe Ɔsekelea gɔ lobɔrɛ i Ɣaa kɔrɛ.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Iiɖe mi maturi iweo-inyɔ loɖi lotã so?
Ɣɛɛ mi ndɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɖe Ɔbosam!” Yesu ɔɣɛ nnɛgbe i Yuda gɔ nɖe Simon Iskariot ɔbi iso.
Alasɔ atoa sɔ ɔɖe maturi iweo-inyɔ ndɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ne, ɔ̃ nto ɔ̃aɖi wũ ɔtã ne.
Yesu Gu Ɔ̃ Manyiibi Iso Itɔ̃me.
Nnɛgbe kama ne, Yesu ɔwe ɔki i Galilea, ɔ̃ibie sɔ ɔ̃akpese ɔkiki i Yudea karɔ̃ iso ala ma Yudase makpakpa to mabie sɔ maɖoe wũ.
Ɔwi gɔ ame masɛ maɖe Kukpakɛ Ame Isɛ Iyi ɔɔbore ibo.
Ne ɔso Yesu manyiibi ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Bɔrɛ i ngbe si akɛlɛ Yudea sɔ fɔ marasuãdze aanya ara wa ato abara.
Alasɔ ɔbiara gɔ nto ɔbie sɔ ɔfɔ iyere iisɛ ɔbara ara ɔwɛrɛ.
Gɔ ato abara ara wagbe ne, tã kayiiso ɔɖuɖu si matsue-ɔ!” Maɣɛ ngbɔ ala nane ɔ̃ manyiibi iifɔ wũ maɖe.
Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Wũ ɔwi iiɣo, mi ne, ɔwi biara lɛ ɔtã mi.
Kayiiso maturi iibawo mi ɔtsiri, ɣɛɛ matsiri me, alasɔ nsɛ loɖi ma ara nyanyarĩa loɣere ma.
Mikɛlɛ iyi kaɖekɔ̃ ne mme loito loba alasɔ wũ ɔwi sɛɛ iiɣo.” Gɔ ɔɣere ma ngbɔ ne, ka ɔwe i Galilea.
Yesu Ɔsɛ Kukpakɛ Ame Iyi Kaɖekɔ̃.
Gɔ ɔ̃ manyiibi ɔɔkɛlɛ iyi kaɖekɔ̃ kama ne, Yesu ɔ̃ wũ ɔba ɔ̃akɛlɛ i iwɛrɛ ame, ɣɛɛ ɔ̃ikɛlɛ kpawee.
Ma Yudase makpakpa ɔtsɛ wũ inyɔnyɔ, ne mato makarɛ sɔ, “Lɛ i ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔmɔ pia?” Maturi gbodzoo ɔɣɛ siwɔwɔi i Yesu iso.
Mawɛ̃ sɔ ɔturi sɛɛ ɔɖe, mawɛ̃ ana sɔ, “Ooɣo!
Ɔto ɔkã maturi ɔyura!” Ɣɛɛ kuwɛ̃ iiɣɛ kuira i ɔ̃ iso kpawee alasɔ mato manigã ma Yudase makpakpa.
Yesu Ɔte Ara I Iyi Kaɖekɔ̃.
Iyi nɛ mato maɖe ndɛ̃ndɛ̃ ne, Yesu ɔba ɔ̃abo Ɣaa Isɔrɛyo ame ɔtsɛ ara ite.
Ibara ma Yudase makpakpa ɣii matsɛ ikarɛ sɔ, “Nda ibara fiɛ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ɣe ara ngbɔ gɔ ɔ̃ifɔ ikpadzɛ̃ kuiwɛ̃?” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ara wa loto lote ne, iiɖe mme mɔmɔ are aɖe, ɣɛɛ Ɣaa gɔ lopia me katɔ̃me are aɖe.
Ɔbiara gɔ nto ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃abara Ɣaa kuɖɔɛ to ɔ̃atsue si ara wa loto lote ne, wũ ɔle iso iɖe, ɣee Ɣaa ɔle ame abɔrɛ.
Ɔturi gɔ nsɛ ɔɖe ika i ɔ̃ ɔle ame sɛ ɔbie iyere ɔtã so, ɣɛɛ ngɔ nto ɔbie iyere ɔtã ngɔ lopia wũ katɔ̃me sɛ ɔɣɛ ɔnukuare fiɛ sila kusiwɛ̃ na i ɔ̃ ame.
Iiɖe Mose lotã mi mmara?
Ɣɛɛ mi kuwɛ̃ iito miɖe mmara iso.
Be ɔso mito mibie sɔ miaɖoe me?” Mmamɔ ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Siwarã lalaa pia i fɔ ame!
Nna nto ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃aɖoe-ɔ?” Ne Yesu ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Iwawãra iwɛ̃ saã nɛ lobara ɔbara mi ɣii.
Mose ɔtã mi mmara sɔ mitu sirɛrɛ̃, ɣɛɛ iiɖe Mose ɔwi i sirɛrɛ̃ itu ɔsɛ karɔ̃, ka masɛ mabara ne ta mi mawa ɔwi, ne ɔso misɛ mitu mi mabi sirɛrɛ̃ ku Iwarãyi ne.
Si maawo ɔturi sirɛrɛ̃ ɔtu ku Iwarãyi, ɣɛɛ maitu Mose mmara ne, be ɔso fiɛ mito minagu me sikpã sɔ losa ɔturi ku Iwarãyi?
Midaanyɔ maturi i katɔ̃ miɣɛgu ma atɔ̃me, ɣɛɛ miɣɛ atɔ̃me i ɔri iso.” Maturi Ɔkarɛ Sɔ Bɛrɛ Yesu Nɖe Kristo?
Mawɛ̃ i Yerusalem ɔtsɛ ikarɛ sɔ, “Iiɖe ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe i makpakpa to mabie sɔ maɖoe ne?
Ɣɛɛ minyɔ wũ!
Ɔ̃ nɣɛ i ngbe ɔto ɔɖe ika i ɔgbami, ɣɛɛ maito mawo wũ kuira ɔɣere!
Ɛɛbɛrɛ ɔfɔ maɔfɔ wũ gbaã sɔ ɔ̃ nɖe Kristo?
Si Kristo ɔba ne, kuwɛ̃ iibatsue ngbegɔ ɔbɔrɛ, ɣɛɛ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ne, boɣe ngbegɔ ɔbɔrɛ.” Gɔ Yesu to ɔte ara i Isɔrɛyo ame ne, ɔla kulu teteree ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Mibua miɣe me gu ngbegɔ lobɔrɛ?
Loiba i mme mɔmɔ ɔle ame.
Ngɔ lopia me katɔ̃me ne, nukuarese ɔɖe, fiɛ miiɣe wũ.
Ɣɛɛ mme loɣe wũ alasɔ ɔ̃ kɔrɛ lobɔrɛ fiɛ ɔ̃ lopia me katɔ̃me.” Nnɛgbe ɔso ne, mabie sɔ si mamɔɛ̃ wũ, ɣɛɛ kuwɛ̃ iiwo kɔrɔ̃ ɔɖi ɔsia wũ iso alasɔ ɔ̃ ɔkpiwi iiɣo.
Ɣɛɛ maturi gbodzoo i ma ndɛ̃ ɔfɔ wũ maɖe mato makarɛ sɔ, “Si Kristo ɔba ne, ɔ̃abara awawãra wa loɖo nwa i ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ɔɔbara?” Mapia Isɔrɛyo Madzuɛ̃se Sɔ Mamɔɛ̃ Yesu.
Ma Farisise ɔnɔ maturi gbodzoo to maɣɛ siwɔwɔi dzɛgbe i Yesu iso, ne ɔso ma gu masɔrɛdze makpakpa ɔpia madzuɛ̃se sɔ mamɔɛ̃ wũ mabɔ.
Ne Yesu ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Loto loawe i mi kɔrɛ ɔwi kɛkɛĩ, ne kama ne, loakpese lokɛlɛ ngɔ lopia me katɔ̃me kɔrɛ.
Mito miabie me, ɣɛɛ miito mianya me, alasɔ miito miaɣo ngbegɔ loawe ɔba.” Ne ma Yudase makpakpa ɔkarɛ so sɔ, “Lɛ ɔto ɔba ɔ̃akɛlɛ fiɛ boabie wũ boibanya wũ?
Ɔbie ɔto sɔ ɔ̃akɛlɛ ma Yudase ma mpia i ma Helase simagɛ̃ ame ɔsɛ ɔ̃ate ma Helase ara?
Itɔ̃me nɛ ɔɣɛ ngbe karɔ̃ ɣɛɛ?
Ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Mito mianyɔnyɔ me, ɣɛɛ miibanya me.’ Ɔɣɛ ana sɔ, ‘Ngbegɔ losɛ ne, miibawo ɔba.’ ” Iyi tsɔra nɛ lobua inya iɖo i iyi iɖe ame ne, Yesu ɔta ɔya ɔla kulu teteree sɔ, “Ɔbiara gɔ i ɔme to ɔkore si ɔba wũ kɔrɛ ɔba ɔ̃anɛ ndu.
Ɔbiara gɔ lofɔ me ɔɖe fiɛ ɔnɛ ndu mɛgbe ne, lɛ kumɛgɔ i Ɔko Sekelea ɔɣɛ ne, ‘Ndu mɛ loisɛ misɔ̃ fiɛ misɛ mitã ɔturi ngbã aabore ɔkore mibɔrɛ i ɔ̃ ɔtu ame.’ ” Yesu ɔɣɛ nnɛgbe i Siwarã dzɛ mma lofɔ wũ maɖe aafɔ iso.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, gɔ Yesu iita ɔbɔrɛ i makpise ame ɔkɛlɛ ikpawaĩ ame ɔso ne, Ɣaa iisu Siwarã Bielea ɔtã marasuãdze.
Iɣɛɣɛso Ɔbo I Ma Yudase Ndɛ̃.
Maturi gbodzoo mamɔ mawɛ̃ ma lonɔ nnɛ i Yesu ɔɣɛ ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Gbaã ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ne, Ɣaa Kanyaɖidze ɔɖe.” Mamama ana sɔ, “Ɔ̃ nɖe Kristo.” Ɣɛɛ mamama ana sɔ, “Kristo iibabɔrɛ i Galilea.
Ɔko Sekelea ɔɣɛ sɔ Kristo ne, David ɔwa tɛtɛ ɔ̃aɖe fiɛ ɔ̃abɔrɛ i Betlehem ngbegɔ i David ɔse.” Ne ɔso iɣɛɣɛso ɔbo i ma ɔɖuɖu ndɛ̃ ala Yesu ɔso.
Mawɛ̃ ɔbie sɔ si mamɔɛ̃ wũ, ɣɛɛ kuwɛ̃ iiwo kɔrɔ̃ ɔɖi ɔsia wũ iso.
Ma Yudase Makpakpa Iifɔ Yesu Maɖe.
Gɔ madzuɛ̃se ɔkpese makɛlɛ ne, masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu ma Farisise ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Be ɔso fiɛ miimɔɛ̃ wũ mibɔ?” Madzuɛ̃se ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Boinɔ bonɔ kuwɛ̃ ɔɖe ika lɛ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe!” Ne ma Farisise ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Mi wũ ne, ɔ̃ɔpia mi iti ndu?
Miɔnya minya ɔkpakpa ɔwɛ̃, ɣee ɔ Farisise ɔwɛ̃ ɔfɔ wũ ɔɖe?
Maturi gbodzoo magbe iiɣe Mose mmara, ne ɔso Ɣaa sigbarĩ siai ma!” Nikodemo gɔ nɖe ma ndɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ fiɛ ɔ̃ɔsɛ Yesu kɔrɛ ɔnya ɔɣere matsɔra sɔ, “Bo mmara iitã bo ɔri sɔ boatã ɔturi ipɔ ku ɔwi gɔ ame boiɣɛgu wũ atɔ̃me bonɔ ɔ̃ kanya ame itɔ̃me.” Ɣɛɛ matã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Fɔ wũ Galilea abɔrɛ?
Fafarɛ Ɔko Sekelea ame kukaakɔ ne ato aatsue sɔ Ɣaa Kanyaɖidze kuwɛ̃ iibabɔrɛ i Galilea ɔnya.” (Ne ɔso ɔbiara ɔrui ɔkɛlɛ ɔ̃ iyo.)
Mamɔɛ̃ Ɔrɔ̃go Ɔwɛ̃ Gɔ Nto Ɔɖe Asɔrɔ̃ Yesu ɔ̃ wũ ɔrui ɔkɛlɛ Nnɔĩ Adziri Kube iso.
Kaɖesɛ̃a kaya tutuutu ne, ɔkpese ɔba Ɣaa Isɔrɛyo.
Maturi ɔɖuɖu ɔba ɔ̃ kɔrɛ fiɛ ɔsɛ i karɔ̃ ɔtsɛ ma ara ite.
Maratedze gu ma Farisise ɔkɔ ɔrɔ̃go ɔwɛ̃ gɔ mamɔɛ̃ gɔ ɔto ɔɖe asɔrɔ̃ mabɔ maaɣedza i ɔgba ame.
Maɣere Yesu sɔ, “Ratedze, mamɔɛ̃ ɔrɔ̃go gɔgbe kɔrɔ̃ kɔrɔ̃ gɔ ɔto ɔɖe asɔrɔ̃.
I mmara mɛ i Mose ɔtã bo kanya ne, ikote sɔ boapɛ wũ ata boɖoe, ɣɛɛ ne, be ato aɣɛ i ne iso?” Makarɛ Yesu itɔ̃me nɛgbe si mala wũ manyɔ si maana itɔ̃me nɛ iso maaya fiɛ maatã wũ ipɔ.
Ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔkadza ɔto ɔtsɛrɛ ara i karɔ̃ ala ɔ̃ irɔĩ.
Gɔ maɣɛ matogu Yesu itɔ̃me ikarɛ ne, ɔtara iti kato ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mi ndɛ̃ ngɔ loibara ikpi ɔnya si ɔɖe katɔ̃ ɔpɛ ɔrɔ̃go gɔgbe ita.” Yesu ɔledza ikadza ɔto ɔtsɛrɛ ara i karɔ̃.
Gɔ manɔ itɔ̃me nɛgbe ne, marui ɔwɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ita i makpakpa iso iba iakuti Yesu gu ɔrɔ̃go ɔnɔwɛ̃.
Gɔ Yesu ɔtara so fiɛ ɔnya sɔ ma ɔɖuɖu ɔɔrui ne, ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ɔrɔ̃go, i ɖe ma?
Ma kuwɛ̃ iitã-ɔ ipɔ?” Ne Ɔrɔ̃go ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Ooɣo, Bosate.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Iyɔ mme wũ loitã-ɔ ipɔ.
Kɛlɛ, ɣɛɛ daasibara ikpi ana.” Yesu Nɖe Kayiiso Ikpawaĩ.
Nnɛmɔ kama ne, Yesu ɔɖegu mmamɔ ika ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mme nɖe kayiiso ikpawaĩ, ne ɔso ɔbiara gɔ losiai me iibasɛ i idududu ame ɔnya ɣɛɛ ɔ̃ana ngbã ame ikpawaĩ.” Ma Farisise ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ato aɖe aɖansiɛ i fɔ mɔmɔ iso, ne ɔso fɔ aɖansiɛ iiɖe ɔnukuare.” Ne Yesu ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Si loɖe so aɖansiɛ kɔra ne, wũ aɖansiɛ ɖe ɔnukuare alasɔ loɣe ngbegɔ lose loba gu ngbegɔ losɛ.
Mi ne, miiɣe ngbegɔ lose gu ngbegɔ losɛ.
Mi ne, maturi ara inyɔ kanya misɛ miɣɛ mi atɔ̃me, ɣɛɛ mme ne, loisɛ loɣɛgu kuwɛ̃ atɔ̃me.
Fiɛ si loɣɛ itɔ̃me ana ne, wũ atɔ̃me iɣɛ to iaya, alasɔ iiɖe wũ ɔnɔwɛ̃ mme nsɛ loɣɛ, ɣɛɛ bo gu ngɔ lopia me katɔ̃me.
Matsɛrɛ mapia i mi mmara ɔko ame sɔ si maturi inyɔ ɔɖe aɖansiɛ i ira iso ne, iyɔ ma itɔ̃me ɖe ɔnukuare.
Mme ne, nsɛ loɖe so aɖansiɛ fiɛ Tete gɔ lopia me katɔ̃me ana sɛ ɔɖe me aɖansiɛ.” Ne mato makarɛ Yesu sɔ, “Lɛ i fɔ Ɔse pia?” Ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Miiɣe me, fiɛ miiɣe Tete ana.
Si ɔɣe miɣe me ne, tee miatsue wũ Ɔse ana.” Yesu ɔte ara wagbe i Isɔrɛyo ngbegɔ masɛ mato ara masɛ.
Kuwɛ̃ iiwo wũ ɔmɔɛ̃ alasɔ ɔ̃ ɔkpiwi iiɣo.
Yesu ɔledza ma iɣere sɔ, “Loto loarui i mi kɔrɛ, miabie me, ɣɛɛ miakpi i mi akpi ame.
Ngbegɔ losɛ ne, miibawo mmɔ ɔba.” Ne ma Yudase to makarɛ so sɔ, “Ɔɖoe ɔto ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃aɖoe so ɔso fiɛ ɔto ɔɣɛ sɔ ‘Ngbegɔ losɛ ne miibawo ɔba’?” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mi ne, kayiiso ngbe mibɔrɛ, ɣɛɛ mme ne, kato lobɔrɛ.
Mi ne, kayiiso maturi miɖe, ɣɛɛ mme ne, loibɔrɛ i kayi gagbe iso.
Ne ɔso loto loɣere mi sɔ mito miakpi i mi akpi ame ne.
Si miifɔ miɖe sɔ mme nɖe ngɔ loɖe ne, miakpi miwe i mi akpi ame.” Makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Fɔ nɖe nna?” Ne ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Loɔɣere mi ta karɔ̃kasɛkɔ̃ fiɛ ngbɔ ame loto loɣere mi ne.
Loba atɔ̃me gbodzoo i mi iso wa loasu lotã mi ala ipɔ, ɣɛɛ ngɔ lopia me katɔ̃me ne, nukuarese ɔɖe.
Fiɛ nnɛ lonɔ lobɔrɛgu i ɔ̃ kɔrɛ imomo loto lopɛ lotã kayiiso.” Maitsue sɔ Ɣaa iso i Yesu to ɔɖe ika.
Ne ɔso Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ɔwi gɔ miakɔlɛ Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi kato ne, ɔwi gɔmɔ ame miatsue sɔ Mme nɖe ngɔ Loɖe ne.
Ana ne, miatsue sɔ loisɛ lobara kuira i wũ ɔle ame, ɣɛɛ nnɛ i Tete ɔɣere me losɛ loɣɛ.
Ngɔ lopia me katɔ̃me piagu me fiɛ ɔ̃isɛ ɔnyua me ɔsɛ, alasɔ nsɛ lobara ɔ̃ kuɖɔɛ ɔwi biara ame.” Maturi gbodzoo ma lonɔ ara wa i Yesu ɔɣɛ ngbe, ɔfɔ wũ maɖe.
Yesu Ɔɖi Mma Nɖe Abraham Mawa Ɔte.
Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma Yudase ma lofɔ wũ maɖe sɔ, “Si mibara i ara wa lote mi iso ne, iyɔ wũ marasuãdze mɔmɔ miɖe.
Miatsue ɔnukuare, fiɛ ɔnukuare aatã mi isɛguso.” Maɣere wũ sɔ, “Abraham mawa boɖe, fiɛ boiɖe kuwɛ̃ masande.
Ne ɔso be ɔso fiɛ ato aɣɛ sɔ boana isɛguso?” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Gbaã loto loɣere mi sɔ ɔbiara gɔ nsɛ ɔbara ikpi ne, ikpi ɔsande ɔɖe.
Ɔsande iisɛ ɔwe i iyo ɔwi biara ame, ɣɛɛ iyo ɔbi sɛ ɔwe i iyo ɔwi biara.
Ne ɔso si Ɣaa Ɔbi ɔtã mi isɛguso ne, miasɛgu so gbaã.
Loɣe sɔ Abraham mawa miɖe, ɣɛɛ mito mibie sɔ si miɖoe me alasɔ wũ atɔ̃me iimɔɛ̃ mi ɔtu.
Nnɛ lonya i Tete kɔrɛ loto loɣere mi, fiɛ mi wũ nnɛ minɔ i mi ɔse kɔrɛ mito mibara.” Matã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Abraham mawa boɖe.” Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Si Abraham mawa miɖe ne, tee miabara ara lɛ Abraham awe.
Ɣɛɛ kiniɔ ne, mito mibie sɔ miaɖoe me, mme gɔ nto loɣere mi ɔnukuare gɔ lonɔ lobɔrɛgu i Ɣaa kɔrɛ.
Abraham iisɛ ngbã ngbɔ.
Mi ne, ara wa i mi ɔse mɔmɔ ɔbara mito mibara.” Ma Yudase ɔtã Yesu mmuai sɔ, “Iiɖe ɔmagɛ̃ ame mabi boɖe.
Ɔse ɔwɛ̃ saã gɔ boba nɖe Ɣaa!” Yesu Ɔɖi Mma Nɖe Tsirise Mabi Ɔte.
Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Si biele ne Ɣaa nɖe mi Ɔse ne, tee miaɖɔɛ me alasɔ Ɣaa kɔrɛ lobɔrɛ loba i ngbe.
Loiba i wũ mɔmɔ ɔle ame, ɣɛɛ ɔ̃ lopia me katɔ̃me.
Be ɔso fiɛ miito minɔ nnɛ loto lote mi karɔ̃?
Gɔ miito mibie sɔ minɔ wũ itɔ̃me ɔso.
Ɔbosam mabi miɖe, fiɛ mito mibie sɔ miabara ara wa nsɛ akpɛ̃ mi ɔse ɔkã.
Ta karɔ̃kasɛkɔ̃ ne, turiɖoese ɔɖe fiɛ ɔ̃isɛ ɔɖɔɛ ɔnukuare alasɔ ɔnukuare na i ɔ̃ ame.
Si ɔto ɔla sila ne, ɔtu iisɛ ɔkpa wũ alasɔ ne nɖe ɔ̃ ngbã ne.
Ladze ɔɖe fiɛ ɔ̃ nɖe maladze ɔɖuɖu ɔse.
Ɣɛɛ mme ne, ɔnukuare loto loɣere mi, fiɛ ne ɔso miifɔ me miɖe ne.
Mi nna loawo me ɔɣere sɔ loɖe ipɔ ala lobara ikpi?
Si loto loɣere mi ɔnukuare ne, be ɔso miito mifɔ me miɖe?
Ngɔ lobɔrɛ i Ɣaa kɔrɛ sɛ ɔkã Ɣaa itɔ̃me atsue.
Mi ɣɛɛ ne, iiɖe Ɣaa kɔrɛ mibɔrɛ, ne ɔso miito mikã atsue ne.” Yesu Ɔɖi So Ɔte Ma Yudase.
Ne ma Yudase ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Si boɣere-ɔ sɔ ɔ Samariase aɖe ne siwarã lalaa pia i fɔ ame ne, bola sila?” Yesu ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Siwarã lalaa na i wũ ame.
Loto lokɔlɛ Tete iyere kato, ɣɛɛ mito mibɔ me karɔ̃.
Loito lole so, ɣɛɛ ɔwɛ̃ pia gɔ nsɛ ɔle me.
Ɔ̃ nɖe atɔ̃meɣɛdze bɔlɔlɔa ne.
Gbaã loto loɣere mi sɔ ngɔ nsɛ ɔbara i wũ ara ite iso iibakpi ɔnya.” Ne ma Yudase ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Kini bosia ita sɔ gbaã ne, siwarã lalaa pia i fɔ ame ne!
Abraham ɔkpi, fiɛ kanyamaɖidze ana ɔkpi.
Ɣɛɛ ato aɣere bo sɔ ngɔ lobara i fɔ ara ite iso iibakpi ɔnya.
Boifɔ nnɛ ato aɣɛ boɖe alasɔ bo ɔwa Abraham ɔkpi, fiɛ kanyamaɖidze ana ɔkpi.
Mme ɔturi igbã ato abu so sɔ aɖe?” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Si ɔle loto so ne, iyɔ ile nɛmɔ iiɖe kuira.
Ɣɛɛ ngɔ nsɛ ɔle me nɖe wũ Ɔse, ngɔ ame mito mikpere sɔ mi Ɣaa.
Miiɣe wũ, ɣɛɛ mme loɣe wũ.
Si loɣɛ sɔ loiɣe wũ ne, loakpese ladze lɛ mi.
Ɣɛɛ mme loɣe wũ fiɛ losɛ lokã wũ atsue.
So ɔɣɔ mi ɔwa Abraham gɔ ɔtsue sɔ loto loaba.
Ɔnya ne, fiɛ so ɔɣɔ wũ.” Ma Yudase ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Gɔ aifɔ akɔ siru ne ɔɣɛ ato sɔ anya Abraham?” Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Gbaã loto loɣere mi sɔ si maaɣe Abraham ne, ka lopia kayi.” Gɔ ɔɣɛ ngbɔ ne, mamala ata sɔ si mapɛ wũ maɖoe ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔwɛrɛ ɔbɔrɛ i ma ndɛ̃ i Isɔrɛyo ame mmɔ.
Yesu Ɔsa Nɔbiɛdze Ɔwɛ̃.
Gɔ Yesu sɛ ɔto ɔfe ne, ɔnya ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ maɣe nɔbiɛdze.
Ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ratedze, nna lobara ikpi ɔso fiɛ maɣe wũ nɔbiɛdze?
Ɔ̃ mɔmɔ ɛɛbɛrɛ ɔ̃ maɣese lobara ikpi?” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Iiɖe ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ɣee ɔ̃ maɣese lobara ikpi, ɣɛɛ maɣe wũ ngbɔ sɔ si Ɣaa aaɖi ɔ̃ ɔle ɔte iki i ɔ̃ iso.
Ayi kumɛgɔ bopia i ikpɛnɛ ame ne, ikote sɔ boabara ngɔ lopia me katɔ̃me karabara.
Kasɛ̃ to kaba gɔ kuwɛ̃ iisibabara karabara.
Ayi kumɛgɔ lopia i kayiiso ne, mme nɖe kayiiso ɔkaniɛ.” Gɔ Yesu ɔɣɛ ngbɔ ne, ɔtua sinyatu ɔfere i karɔ̃ ɔsu ɔbara ibata ɔsu ɔnukutu i ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔmɔ anɔmi iso.
Ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Kɛlɛ aapie ndu i Siloa ibu ame.” Siloa karɔ̃ nɖe sɔ ɔpia wũ katɔ̃me.
Ne ɔso ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ɔrui ɔsɛ ɔ̃apie ndu i ibu ame ɔtsɛ ara inya, fiɛ ɔkpese ɔba.
Gɔ ɔ̃ kagbamiku maturi gu mma nsɛ manya ɔwanyi ara ɔnya wũ ne, makarɛ sɔ, “Iiɖe ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe nsɛ ɔsɛ ɔwanyi ara?” Mawɛ̃ sɔ ɔ̃ ɔɖe, mamama ana sɔ, “Ooɣo, ɔre kere ɔre wũ.” Ne ɔ̃ mɔmɔ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mme loɖe.” Makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Nda ibara fiɛ fɔ anɔmi ɔbusi?” Ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ marɔ sɔ Yesu ɔɖe lobara ibata ɔnukutu me anɔmi fiɛ ɔɣere me sɔ lokɛlɛ loapie ndu i Siloa ibu ame.
Ne gɔ lobara ne, lotsɛ ara inya.” Makarɛ wũ sɔ, “I lɛ ɔpia?” Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Loiɣe.” Ma Farisise Ɔfafarɛ Nɔbiɛdze Isosarɛ Ame.
Makɔ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ loɖe nɔbiɛdze ngbe makɛlɛgu ma Farisise kɔrɛ.
Iyi nɛ i Yesu ɔbara ibata ɔsu ɔsa ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ne, Iwarãyi iɖe.
Ma Farisise ɔledza wũ ikarɛ kumɛgɔ iɖe ɔbara fiɛ ɔ̃ anɔmi ɔbusi.
Ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ɔbara ibata ɔsia me i anɔmi iso fiɛ losɛ loafore katɔ̃ kere ne lotsɛ inya ne.” Ma Farisise mawɛ̃ ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ lobara ira nɛgbe ne, iiɖe Ɣaa kɔrɛ iɖe ɔbɔrɛ ala ɔ̃isɛ ɔwarɛ Iwarãyi mmara.” Ɣɛɛ mamama ana sɔ, “Nda i ngɔ nɖe kpibaradze aawo awawãra wagbe igbã ɔbara?” Ne ɔso iɣɛɣɛso ɔbo i ma ndɛ̃.
Ma Farisise ɔledza ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ikarɛ sɔ, “Gɔ ɔ̃ losa-ɔ ne, be abu sɔ ɔɖe?” Ne ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Ɣaa Kanyaɖidze ɔɖe.” Ma Yudase makpakpa iifɔ maɖe sɔ ɔ̃ anɔmi ɔbiɛ fiɛ kiniɔ ne, ka ɔto ɔnya ara, ne ɔso mapia masɛ maakpere ɔ̃ maɣese mabɔ.
Ne makarɛ ma sɔ, “Mi ɔbi ɔɖe ngbe?
Mi sɔ nɔbiɛdze ɔɖe miɣe wũ, nda ibara fiɛ ka ɔto ɔnya ara?” Maɣese ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Boɣe sɔ bo ɔbi ɔɖe fiɛ ɔ̃ anɔmi ɔbiɛ fiɛ boɣe wũ.
Ɣɛɛ kumɛgɔ ibara fiɛ ka ɔto ɔnya ara ne, boiɣe, fiɛ boiɣe ngɔ losa wũ ana.
Mikarɛ wũ ne ɔ̃ɔkpa anɔ gɔ ɔ̃awo so kanya ɔɖi!” Ɔ̃ maɣese ɔtã mmuai ngbɔ alasɔ mato manigã ma Yudase makpakpa ma loɔsɛ iti ame maɣɛ masɛ sɔ ɔrere gɔ loaɣɛ sɔ ɔfɔ Yesu ɔɖe sɔ ɔ̃ nɖe Kristo ne, maasa wũ maɖi i ma kasarɛkɔ̃.
Ne ɔso i ɔ̃ maɣese ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Mikarɛ wũ ne ɔ̃isiɖe ɔbiɛtɛ ne!” Maledza ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ikpere ibɔ ɔkpɛ nyɔare maɣere wũ sɔ, “Kã ndamu tã Ɣaa sɔ aaɣere bo ɔnukuare.
Bo boɣe sɔ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ losa-ɔ ne, kpibaradze ɔɖe.” Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ lona isosarɛ ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Kpibaradze ɔɖe o-o, kpibaradze ɔ̃iɖe o-o ne, loiɣe.
Ira ka iwɛ̃ loɣe, ne nɖe sɔ, ɔwiɔ ne, anɔmi ɔbiɛ me, ɣɛɛ kiniɔ ne, ka loto lonya ara.” Ne makpakpa mamɔ ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Be iɖe ɔbara-ɔ?
Nda iɖe ɔbara fiɛ ɔsa-ɔ atsɛ inya?” Ne ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔmɔ to ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Loɔɣere mi koko, ɣɛɛ misɛ̃ sɔ miito minɔ.
Be ɔso si loledza mi iɣere?
Ɛɛbɛrɛ mi wũ ɔbie mito sɔ miakpese ɔ̃ marasuãdze?” Ne matia wũ maɣere sɔ, “Fɔ nɖe ɔ̃ rasuãdze.
Bo ɣɛɛ ne, Mose marasuãdze boɖe.
Boɣe sɔ Ɣaa ɔɖegu Mose ika, ɣɛɛ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ne, boiɣe nane ngbegɔ ɔbɔrɛ!” Ne ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe to ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Iba ɣaa sɔ miiɣe ngbegɔ ɔbɔrɛ, ɣɛɛ ɔ̃ lobusi me anɔmi ne!
Boɣe sɔ Ɣaa iisɛ ɔkã makpibaradze atsue, ɣɛɛ mma nsɛ mawarɛ wũ fiɛ masɛ mabara ɔ̃ kuɖɔɛ ne, ɔsɛ ɔkã ma atsue.
Ita i kayiiso karɔ̃kasɛkɔ̃ ne, boinɔ bonɔ sɔ kuwɛ̃ ɔbusi ɔturi gɔ maɣe nɔbiɛdze anɔmi.
Ne ɔso si iiɖe Ɣaa kɔrɛ ɔbɔrɛ ne, ɔ̃ibawo ira nɛgbe igbã ɔbara.” Ne makpakpa mamɔ ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Fɔ gɔ maɣe i ikpi ame, makararã-ɔ i ikpi ame ne, fɔ loaba aate bo ara?” Ne masa wũ maɖi i ma ikuri ame ne.
Mma Nɖe Siwarã Ame Manɔbiɛdze.
Yesu ɔnɔ sɔ maɔsa nɔbiɛdze maɖi i ma ikuri ame, ne ɔso gɔ ɔnya wũ ne, ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Afɔ Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi aɖe?” Ne ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Tete, te me ɔnyiiɔ si loafɔ wũ loɖe.” Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ɔɔnya wũ koko, ɔ̃ nto ɔɖegu-ɔ ika ne.” Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Bosate, lofɔ loɖe!” Ne ɔpɛ agɛgɛ̃ i Yesu katɔ̃ ɔsɔrɛ wũ ne.
Yesu ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Loba kayiiso sɔ si loɣɛgu kã atɔ̃me sɔ mma loito manya ara si manya, fiɛ mma nto manya si madaasinya.” Gɔ ma Farisise mawɛ̃ ma mpia i mmɔ ɔnɔ nnɛ i Yesu ɔɣɛ ne, makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Be ato aɣɛ?
Bo wũ manɔbiɛdze boɖe?” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Si manɔbiɛdze miɖe ne, tee miiɖe makpibaradze, ɣɛɛ gɔ mi sɔ mito minya ara ne, ne ɔso miɖe ipɔ ne.”
Yesu Ɔpɛ Igbã I Masɛrɛkɔdze Iso.
Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Gbaã loto loɣere mi sɔ ngɔ loiki i kayogodɔ̃ ɔbo i isɛrɛyo ame, ɣɛɛ ɔya ɔkpã ɔbo i kame ne, yukukpe gu raninadze ɔɖe.
Ngɔ nsɛ ɔki i kayogodɔ̃ ɔbo i ɔkpã ame ne, ɔ̃ nɖe masɛrɛkɔdze ne.
Kayogodɔ̃ dzuɛ̃se sɛ ɔsese wũ kukui, masɛrɛ sɛ manɔ ɔ̃ silɔ si ɔto ɔkpere ɔ̃ masɛrɛ ayere fiɛ ɔ̃akɔ ma ɔbɔrɛgu.
Fiɛ si ɔ̃ɔkɔ ɔ̃ masɛrɛ ɔɖi ne, ɔsɛ ɔɖe ma katɔ̃ fiɛ ka maasiai wũ, alasɔ maɣe ɔ̃ silɔ.
Maibasiai ɔturi mama, ɣɛɛ maatere maɣɛ wũ alasɔ maiɣe ɔ̃ silɔ.” Yesu ɔpɛ ma igbã nɛgbe, ɣɛɛ mainɔ nnɛ ɔɣere ma karɔ̃.
Yesu Nɖe Masɛrɛkɔdze Sɛɛ.
Ne ɔso Yesu ɔledza ma iɣere sɔ, “Gbaã loto loɣere mi sɔ mme nɖe kayogodɔ̃ lotã masɛrɛ.
Mma ɔɖuɖu loɖe me katɔ̃ maba ne, mayukukpe gu maraninadze maɖe ne ɔso masɛrɛ iikã ma atsue.
Mme nɖe kayogodɔ̃ fiɛ ɔbiara gɔ loki i wũ ame ɔbo i kame ne, ɔ̃ana iɖi.
Ɔ̃abo ɔbɔrɛ fiɛ ɔ̃ana aɖera kaɖekɔ̃.
Yukukpe ne, kayu gu ituriɖoe gu ara inina ɔso fiɛ ɔsɛ ɔba, ɣɛɛ mme ne, loba sɔ si maturi aana ngbã mɛ loyi.
“Mme nɖe masɛrɛkɔdze sɛɛ gɔ loabie sɔ ɔ̃akpi ala masɛrɛ iti.
Ɣɛɛ ngɔ masu sɔ ɔnyɔ masɛrɛ iso fiɛ iiɖe ɔ̃ mɔmɔ mare maɖe ne, si ɔnya ɔgidi to ɔba ne, ɔsɛ ɔrui ɔtere ɔnyua mabɔi.
Ɔgidi aabo i masɛrɛ ndɛ̃ ɔmɔɛ̃ ma, ɔsamarã ma.
Rabaradze gɔgbe aarui ɔtere alasɔ kuso ɔ̃afɔ, ne ɔso ɔ̃isu kuira i masɛrɛ iso.
“Mme nɖe masɛrɛkɔdze sɛɛ ne.
Loɣe wũ mare, fiɛ ma wũ maɣe me lɛ kumɛgɔ ame i Tete ɣe me fiɛ mme wũ loɣe wũ.
Losu wũ ngbã lotã i masɛrɛ iti.
Loba masɛrɛ mama ma loibɔrɛ i ɔkpã gɔgbe ame fiɛ ipia sɔ loakɔ ma lobɔ.
Maanɔ wũ silɔ fiɛ ma ɔɖuɖu aakpese ikuri iwɛ̃ ku kɔdze ɔwɛ̃.
“Tete sɛ ɔɖɔɛ me alasɔ losu wũ ngbã lotã fiɛ loakpese lofɔ me ana.
Kuwɛ̃ iibawo wũ ngbã ɔfɔ i wũ kɔrɛ, ɣɛɛ mme mɔmɔ kuɖɔɛ ame losu me lotã.
Loba ɔle sɔ loasu lotã fiɛ loba ɔle ana sɔ loakpese lofɔ me.
Nnɛgbe i Tete ɔpia me sɔ lobara ne.” Yesu atɔ̃me wagbe ɔledza iɣɛɣɛso ibɔ i ma Yudase ndɛ̃.
Gbodzoo i ma ndɛ̃ ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Siwarã lalaa pia i ɔ̃ ame.
Ɔto ɔlala, ne ɔso midaakã wũ atsue.” Ɣɛɛ mamama ana ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Ngɔ ame i siwarã lalaa pia iibawo ika ɔɖe kumɛgɔgbe!
Siwarã lalaa iibawo nɔbiɛdze anɔmi ɔbusi.” Ma Yudase Iifɔ Yesu Maɖe.
Ɔyu ɔwi ne, ma Yudase ɔɖe Ɣaa Isɔrɛyo Isekelera iyi i Yerusalem.
Gɔ Yesu sɛ ɔki i Salomo kakpataku ame i Isɔrɛyo ame ne, ma Yudase ɔba maaki malɔ wũ makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ku mme ɔwi aaɣere bo ɔnukuare?
Si fɔ nɖe Kristo ne, ɣere bo ɖi.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Loɔɣere mi koko, ɣɛɛ miito mifɔ me miɖe.
Ara wa loto lobara i wũ Ɔse iyere ame nto aɖe ika i wũ iso.
Ɣɛɛ miito mifɔ me miɖe, alasɔ iiɖe wũ masɛrɛ miɖe.
Wũ masɛrɛ sɛ makã me atsue, loɣe ma, fiɛ masɛ masiai me.
Nsɛ lotã ma ngbã mɛ loibaro fiɛ maibawɔ.
Kuwɛ̃ iibawo ma ɔpɛ ɔfɔ i wũ nrɔɔ̃ ame.
Tete gɔ losu ma ɔtã me ne, ɔmɔ ɔɖo ɔturi biara, ne ɔso kuwɛ̃ iibawo ma ɔpɛ ɔfɔ i ɔ̃ nrɔɔ̃ ame.
Bo gu Tete ne, mawɛ̃ boɖe.” Ne ma Yudase ɔledza ata imala sɔ si mapɛ wũ ne.
Yesu ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Loɔbara ara sɛɛ gbodzoo wa i Tete ɔpia me sɔ lobara i mi ndɛ̃.
Wã ndɛ̃ imele ɔso mito miba miapɛ me ata?” Matã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Boito bobie sɔ boapɛ-ɔ ata ala ara sɛɛ wa abara ɔso, ɣɛɛ imusuora nɛ aɣɛ ɔso!
Ɔturi awune kere aɖe, ɣɛɛ asu so ato akateragu Ɣaa!” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Matsɛrɛ mapia i Ɔko Sekelea ame sɔ Ɣaa ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Mi se lɛ Ɣaa.’ Si Ɣaa ɔkpere mma ɔso i ɔ̃ itɔ̃me ɔba sɔ mase lɛ Ɣaa, fiɛ nnɛ matsɛrɛ masɛ i Ɔko Sekelea ame ne, maibawo ne ɔfinikira ne, ɔɣere mito me sɔ mme gɔ i Ɣaa ɔɖi ɔsese kayiiso ne, loɣɛ imusuora sɔ loɣɛ sɔ Ɣaa Ɔbi loɖe?
Si loito lobara Tete karabara ne, iyɔ midaafɔ me miɖe.
Ɣɛɛ si loto lobara Tete karabara ne, si miifɔ me miɖe kɔra ne, mifɔ wũ karabara miɖe.
Ne loatã mitsue, fiɛ mianɔ karɔ̃ sɔ Tete pia i wũ ame fiɛ mme wũ lopia i Tete ame ne.” Ngbe ana ne, mabie sɔ si mamɔɛ̃ Yesu, ɣɛɛ ɔbɔrɛ ma ndɛ̃ ɔwi.
Ɔkpese ɔsɛ ɔ̃awara Yordan ɔwore ɔkɛlɛ ngbegɔ i Yohanes ɔpie maturi Ɣaa ndu ku ɔwi gɔ lofe, ne ka ɔwe i mmɔ ne.
Maturi gbodzoo ɔba ɔ̃ kɔrɛ maba maaɣɛ sɔ, “Yohanes iibara awawãra, ɣɛɛ ara wa ɔɖuɖu ɔɣɛ i ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe iso ne, gbaã iɖe.” Ne ɔso maturi gbodzoo ɔfɔ Yesu maɖe i mmɔ.
Lazaro Kukpi.
Ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ sɔ Lazaro fiɛ ɔbɔrɛ i Betania ɔmagɛ̃ ame ɔmɔɛ̃ ɔnyɛ.
Ɔmagɛ̃ gɔgbe nɖe Maria gu ɔ̃ ɔnyiibi Marta mɛrɛ̃ aɖe ne.
Maria gɔgbe ɔɖe loba ɔ̃afedza nnɔĩ kɔrɔ̃kɔrɔ̃a ɔfere i Bosate Yesu ngba fiɛ ɔsu ɔ̃ iti siwɛrɛ̃ ɔnukutu ne.
Ɔ̃ ɔnyiibi nɖe Lazaro gɔ nto ɔmɔɛ̃ ɔnyɛ i ngbe ne.
Lazaro manyiiko ɔpia Yesu ɔturi sɔ, “Bosate, fɔ ɔlaa gɔ abua asɛ aɖɔɛ to ɔnyɛ.” Gɔ Yesu ɔnɔ kanya gagbe ne, ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Ɔnyɛ gɔgbe iiɖe ɔkpinyɛ, ɣɛɛ ɔɖe ira nɛ loakɔlɛ Ɣaa iyere kato, fiɛ iaki i ne iso ana ne, maakɔlɛ Ɣaa Ɔbi ɔ̃ wũ kato.” Yesu ɔbua ɔsɛ ɔɖɔɛ Lazaro gu ɔ̃ manyiiko kukaakɔ.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ ɔnɔ Lazaro ɔnyɛ ne, ɔwe i ngbegɔ ɔpia akpɛnɛ anyɔ ɔbua.
Ne ɔɣere ɔ̃ marasuãdze sɔ, “Mitã bokpese bokɛlɛ Yudea.” Ne ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ratedze, iifɔ ɔwi gɔ ma Yudase ɔbie sɔ si mapɛ-ɔ ata, ne ato abie sɔ boakpese bokɛlɛ mmɔ ana?” Yesu ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Iɖɔwũ iweo-inyɔ iɖe mpia i ikpɛnɛ ame.
Ne ɔso ɔbiara gɔ nsɛ i ikpɛnɛ ikpawaĩ ame ne, ɔ̃isɛ ɔtura, alasɔ ɔsɛ ɔnya kayiiso gagbe ikpawaĩ.
Ɣɛɛ si ɔsɛ i kasɛ̃ ame ne, ɔsɛ ɔtura, alasɔ ɔna ikpawaĩ.” Gɔ Yesu ɔɣere ma ngbɔ ne, ɔɣɛ ana sɔ, “Bo ɔlaa Lazaro ɔɔrɛ sirɛ, ɣɛɛ losɛ loatara wũ.” Ne marasuãdze ɔɣere Bosate sɔ, “Si sirɛ ɔɔsu wũ ne, iyɔ ɔto ɔ̃asarɛ.” Ɔɣɛ i Yesu to sɔ Lazaro ɔɔkpi, ɣɛɛ marasuãdze ɔbu sɔ sirɛ gbaã ɔto ɔɣɛ ala. Ne ɔso ɔɣere ma ɔɖi sɔ, “Lazaro ɔɔkpi.
Ɣɛɛ mi ɔso ne, iba me isoɣɔ sɔ lona i ɔ̃ kɔrɛ si miafɔ miɖe.
Mitã bokɛlɛ ɔ̃ kɔrɛ.” Ne Toma gɔ marɔ sɔ Inyɔɔbi ɔɣere marasuãdze sɔ, “Mitã bosiai Ratedze si bosɛ boakpigu wũ!” Yesu Ɔpia Lazaro Manyiibi Kɔrɔ̃ I Kayiri.
Gɔ Yesu ɔsɛ ɔ̃abo mmɔ ne, ɔnya sɔ iɔfɔ akpɛnɛ ana gɔ mabiara Lazaro.
Ita i Yerusalem iba Betania ne, iaɖe agu anyɔ kere, ne ɔso ma Yudase gbodzoo ɔba sɔ si maba maatã Maria gu Marta ndzo i ma ɔnyiete kukpi iso.
Gɔ Marta ɔnɔ sɔ Yesu ka ɔba ne, ɔta ɔkɛlɛ sɔ ɔ̃asarɛgu wũ, ɣɛɛ Maria ɔwe i iyo ame.
Mmɔ i Marta to ɔɣere Yesu sɔ, “Bosate, si ɔpia apia ne, tee bo ɔnyiete iikpi!
Ɣɛɛ kiniɔ kɔra ne, loɣe sɔ Ɣaa to ɔ̃abara ira biara nɛ akarɛ wũ.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Fɔ ɔnyiete to ɔ̃ata ɔwe ngbã.” Ne Marta to ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Loɣe sɔ ɔto ɔ̃ata ɔwe ngbã ku Iyi Tsɔra nɛ i makpise aata iso.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Mme nɖe makpise ita gu ngbã ne.
Ngɔ lofɔ me ɔɖe to ɔ̃asɛ ngbã atoa sɔ ɔkpi, fiɛ ɔbiara gɔ nsi ngbã fiɛ ɔfɔ me ɔɖe ne, ɔ̃ibakpi.
Afɔ nnɛgbe aɖe?” Ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Aĩ, Bosate.
Lofɔ loɖe sɔ fɔ nɖe Kristo, Ɣaa Ɔbi gɔ maɣɛ masɛ sɔ ɔ̃aba kayiiso.” Yesu Ɔbiɛ Kaku.
Gɔ Marta ɔɣɛ ngbɔ ne, ɔkpese ɔkɛlɛ ɔsɛ ɔ̃akpere ɔ̃ ɔnyiibi Maria ɔɣedza i kuruɛ ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ratedze ɔba ɔto ɔkarɛ-ɔ iti.” Gɔ Maria ɔnɔ ngbɔ ne, ɔta ɔluwɛ̃ sɔ ɔ̃asarɛgu wũ.
Ɔwi gɔgbe ame ɔɖuɖu ne, Yesu iibo ɔmagɛ̃ ame, ɔɣɛ i ngbegɔ i Marta ɔba ɔ̃asarɛgu wũ.
Ma Yudase ma mpia i iyo mato matã Maria katetere ɔta masiai wũ gɔ manya sɔ ɔpɛ siwa ɔbɔrɛ i iyo.
Mabu sɔ siainyɔ ne, ikpibiɔ katɔ̃ ka ɔsɛ ɔ̃abiɛ kaku.
Ɔwi gɔ Maria ɔbo ngbegɔ i Yesu ɣɛ fiɛ ɔnya wũ ne, ɔpɛ agɛgɛ̃ i ɔ̃ katɔ̃ ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Si ɔpia apia i ngbe ne, tee wũ ɔnyiete iikpi.” Gɔ Yesu ɔnya kumɛgɔ i Maria to ɔbiɛ gu kumɛgɔ i ma Yudase ma loba maaya wũ ana to mabiɛ ne, imararã Yesu fiɛ ikpɛ̃ wũ nnya.
Ne ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Lɛ mibiara wũ?” Matã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Bosate, ba nyɔ.” Mmɔ ne, Yesu ɔbiɛ.
Ne ma Yudase to maɣɛ sɔ, “Minyɔ kumɛgɔ ɔɖɔɛ wũ!” Ɣɛɛ mawɛ̃ ana ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Gɔ ɔwo nɔbiɛdze anɔmi ɔbusi ne, ɔ̃ibawo ɔtã sɔ Lazaro iibakpi?” Yesu Ɔtara Lazaro Ɔbɔrɛgu I Makpise Ame.
Yesu ɔtɔrɛ̃ i ɔ̃ ame, ɔsɛ ɔkɛlɛ ikpibiɔ nɛ mpia i ɔkpolo ame fiɛ mali ita masɛ̃ kanya kɔrɛ.
Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mili ita miɖi i ɔkpolo kanya.” Ne Lazaro ɔnyiiko gɔ nɖe Marta ɔɣere Yesu sɔ, “Ɔfiã ka ɔpia ala iɔfɔ ayi ana gɔ mabiara wũ!” Yesu ɔɣere Marta sɔ, “Loiɣere-ɔ sɔ si afɔ me aɖe ne, ato aanya Ɣaa ɔle?” Gɔ mali ita maɖi ne, Yesu ɔnyɔ kato ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Tete, nto lopɛ-ɔ siba, sɔ asɛ akã me atsue.
Loɣe sɔ asɛ akã me atsue ɔwi biara, ɣɛɛ mma nɣɛ i ngbe ɔso loto loɣɛ si maafɔ maɖe sɔ fɔ lopia me katɔ̃me.” Gɔ ɔɣɛ nnɛgbe ɔro ne, ɔla kulu teteree sɔ, “Lazaro, ta bɔrɛ ba!” Ɔluwɛ̃ ɔturi gɔ lokpi ɔta ɔbɔrɛ.
Ɔkati gɔ mamini wũ nrɔɔ̃ gu ngba mini wũ iso, fiɛ ngɔ ana nyi wũ i katɔ̃ fiɛ ɔta ɔbɔrɛ ɔba.
Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mikurisi wũ ara iso si ɔkɛlɛ.” Ma Yudase Ɔsɛ Iti Ame Sɔ Maaɖoe Yesu.
Maturi gbodzoo ma loba maaya Maria ɔnya ara wa i Yesu ɔbara, ne ɔso mafɔ wũ maɖe.
Ɣɛɛ mawɛ̃ ɔrui makɛlɛ ma Farisise kɔrɛ masɛ maaɣere ma nnɛ i Yesu ɔbara.
Ne ɔso ma Farisise gu masɔrɛdze makpakpa ɔsarɛgu matɔ̃meɣɛdze makarɛ sɔ, “Be boabara?
Minyɔ awawãra gbodzoo wa i ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe to ɔbara!
Si botã ɔkɛlɛgu i katɔ̃ kumɛgɔgbe ne, maturi ɔɖuɖu to maafɔ wũ maɖe, iyɔ ma Romase abã to maaba maabiɛ bo Isɔrɛyo gu bo karɔ̃!” Ma ndɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ nɖe Kayafa fiɛ ɔ̃ nɖe sɔrɛdzekpakpa pelepele ku ikɔ nɛmɔ ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Mibo ndu miɣede!
Miiɣe sɔ ilɛ sɔ miatã ɔturi ɔwɛ̃ ɔkpi i kaɖe iti iɖo sɔ kaɖe ɔɖuɖu aawɔ?” Gbaã ne, iiɖe ɔ̃ mɔmɔ adzuni aɖe ɔɣɛ ngbe, ɣɛɛ lɛ sɔrɛdzekpakpa pelepele ku ikɔ nɛmɔ ne, itɔ̃me iɖe ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ sɔ Yesu to ɔba ɔ̃akpi i ma Yudase iti.
Fiɛ iiɖe ma Yudase ɔnɔwɛ̃ kere iti, ɣɛɛ si ɔ̃asa Ɣaa mabi ma ɔɖuɖu loki makã kayiiso kanya.
Ita i iyi nɛmɔ iso ne, ma Yudase makpakpa ɔsɛ iti ame kumɛgɔ maabara fiɛ maaɖoe Yesu.
Ne ɔso Yesu iisisɛ ɔsɛ kpawee i Yudea karɔ̃ iso, ɣɛɛ ɔrui ɔkɛlɛ fafuĩ ame i ɔmagɛ̃ gɔ marɔ sɔ Efrayim ame ku ɔ̃ marasuãdze masɛ maawe i mmɔ.
Ma Yudase Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo Iyi ɔɔbore ibo, ne ɔso maturi gbodzoo ɔbɔrɛ i abuiti ame maba Yerusalem si maba maasekelera so matã iyi iɖe.
Gɔ masakanya i Ɣaa Isɔrɛyo ame ne, mala maɔnyɔnyɔ Yesu, ne ɔso mato makarɛ so sɔ, “Nda minya?
Ɔ̃ito ɔ̃aba iyi kaɖekɔ̃ lo?” Ɣɛɛ masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu ma Farisise ɔpia maturi sɔ si ɔrere ɣe ngbegɔ Yesu pia ne, ɔte ma si maakɛlɛ masɛ maamɔɛ̃ wũ.
Maria Ɔsɔla Yesu Nnɔĩ I Betania.
Gɔ iɔkuti ayi akuɔ fiɛ maaɖe Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo Iyi ne, Yesu ɔkɛlɛ Betania i Lazaro gɔ ɔtara ɔbɔrɛgu i makpise ame aɖe.
Mawa kutsuɛ aɖera i mmɔ matã wũ.
Marta loɖe ngɔ losia ma aɖera i ɔpɔrɔ̃ iso fiɛ Lazaro ɔ̃ wũ ɔwe i mma losɛ i ɔpɔrɔ̃ iti ndɛ̃.
Maria ɔfedza nnɔĩ kɔrɔ̃kɔrɔ̃ miwɛ̃ mɛ lofɔ kuɣa gbaã ibui ɔfere Yesu i ngba fiɛ ka ɔsu ɔ̃ iti siwɛrɛ̃ ɔnukutu me.
Nnɔĩ ɔfiã ɔfɔ iyo ame ɔɖuɖu.
Ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔwɛ̃ gɔ nɖe Yuda Iskariot gɔ loaɖi Yesu ɔtã ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Be ɔso fiɛ maibarɔdɛ̃ nnɔĩ mɛgbe sikãfudza abi alafa atɛ masu sikã matã mawɛrɛba?” Ɔɣɛ nnɛgbe iiɖe sɔ mawɛrɛba ara nsɛ aɖo wũ kayiri, ɣɛɛ yukukpe ɔɖe ɔso.
Ɔ̃ nto sikã kakotoi, ne ɔso ɔsɛ ɔyu nnɛ mpia i kame.
Ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Minyua wũ, mitã wũ ɔledza me ɔtã wũ ibiarayi.
Mawɛrɛba to maawe i mi kɔrɛ ɔwi biara, ɣɛɛ mme ne, loito loawe i mi kɔrɛ ɔwi biara.” Ma Yudase Ɔsɛ Iti Ame Nyanyarĩa I Lazaro Iso.
Ma Yudase gbodzoo ɔnɔ sɔ Yesu pia i Betania, ne ɔso masiai wũ kama maba mmɔ.
Iiɖe Yesu ɔnɔwɛ̃ ɔso fiɛ maba, ɣɛɛ si maba maanya Lazaro gɔ ɔtara ɔbɔrɛgu i makpise ame ana.
Ne ɔso masɔrɛdze makpakpa ɔsɛ iti ame sɔ maaɖoe Lazaro ɔ̃ wũ, alasɔ ɔ̃ ɔso i ma Yudase gbodzoo to makpese ma i kama mafɔ Yesu maɖe.
Yesu Ɔkɛlɛ Yerusalem Lɛ Igara Awe.
Gɔ kaɖe ɔsɛ̃ ne, maturi gbodzoo ma loba Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo Iyi kaɖekɔ̃ ɔnɔ sɔ Yesu to ɔba Yerusalem.
Ne ɔso masu sikɛ mato fiɛ mabɔrɛ sɔ maasarɛgu wũ.
Mato mafa kayiɖu sɔ, “Hosiana!
Maale ngɔ nto ɔba i Bosate iyere ame!
Maale Israel Igara!” Yesu ɔna ɔfirimu ɔsi i iso lɛ kumɛgɔ i Ɔko Sekelea ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Zion Ɔmagɛ̃, daanigã!
Ɔɔnya fɔ Igara nto ɔba, ɔsi i ɔfirimu ibi iso!” Yesu marasuãdze iinɔ ira nɛgbe karɔ̃ ku ɔwi gɔmɔ ame, ɣɛɛ ɔwi gɔ ɔ̃ɔta ɔbɔrɛ i makpise ame ɔkɛlɛ ikpawaĩ ame ne, manyigi sɔ Ɔko Sekelea ɔɣɛ ngbɔ, fiɛ mabara ngbɔ matã wũ ana.
Mma lowe i Yesu kɔrɛ ku ɔwi gɔ ɔkpere Lazaro ɔbɔrɛgu i ikpibiɔ ame fiɛ ɔtara wũ ɔbɔrɛgu i makpise ame ɔsɛ maaɣɛ nnɛ loba.
Nnɛgbe ɔso i maturi gbodzoo mamɔ ɔsarɛgu wũ ne, alasɔ manɔ iwawãra nɛ ɔbara i ngbe.
Ne ma Farisise to maɣere so sɔ, “Minya sɔ boito bona kayakpa ɖuɖuuɖu?
Kayiiso maturi ɔɖuɖu ka masiai wũ!” Ma Helase Mawɛ̃ Ɔbie Yesu.
Ma Helase mawɛ̃ pia i mma loba masɔrɛ Ɣaa i iyi kaɖekɔ̃ i Yerusalem ame.
Maba maaɣere Filipo gɔ lobɔrɛ i Betsaida i Galilea sɔ, “Tete, boto bobie sɔ boanya Yesu.” Filipo ɔsɛ ɔ̃aɣere Andrea fiɛ ma inyɔɔ ka masɛ maaɣere Yesu.
Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ɔwi ɔɔɣo gɔ maapia Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi kuwarɛ siare.
Gbaã loto loɣere mi sɔ si ititabi iibo i karɔ̃ ame iburi ne, ne ɔnɔwɛ̃ saã kere iɖe mpia, ɣɛɛ si iburi ne, isɛ ipia abi gbodzoo.
Ngɔ nsɛ ɔɖɔɛ ɔ̃ ngbã ne, ɔto ɔ̃ayura me, ɣɛɛ ngɔ lotsiri ɔ̃ ngbã i kayi gagbe ame ne, ɔkɔla me ɔtã ngbã mɛ loibaro minya.
Ɔbiara gɔ nto ɔbie sɔ ɔ̃asumu me ne, ɔsiai me si wũ maɖabo aawegu me i ngbegɔ lopia.
Tete to ɔ̃awarɛ ɔbiara gɔ nsɛ ɔsumu me.
Yesu Ɔɣɛ Ɔ̃ Kukpi Iso Itɔ̃me.
“Kiniɔ ne, loto lomararã so i wũ ɔtu ame, fiɛ loiɣe nnɛ loaɣɛ.
Ɔɣɛ si loɣɛ sɔ, ‘Tete, ɖi me bɔrɛgu i inyɛwe ɔwi gɔgbe ame’?
Ooɣo, ala ɔwi gɔgbe ɔso fiɛ loba kayi ne.
Tete, kɔlɛ fɔ iyere kato!” Ne silɔ ɔɖe ika sibɔrɛgu i kato sɔ, “Loɔkɔlɛ wũ iyere kato koko, fiɛ loto loaledza ibara ana.” Maturi gbodzoo ma nɣɛ i ɔ̃ kɔrɛ ɔnɔ silɔ, ne ma mawɛ̃ to maɣɛ sɔ kado loɖu.
Mawɛ̃ ana sɔ, “Ɣaa kpabo loɖegu wũ ika.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Iiɖe wũ ɔso fiɛ silɔ ɔɖe ika, ɣɛɛ mi ɔso.
“Ɔwi ɔɔɣo gɔ maaɣɛgu kayiiso maturi atɔ̃me, fiɛ maaturi ngɔ nto ɔɖe kayiiso iso iyara.
Fiɛ si maɔkɔlɛ me kato i kayiiso ne, loaboregu maturi ɔɖuɖu lopia so.” Yesu ɔɣɛ nnɛgbe ɔte kukpi gɔ igbã ɔ̃akpi.
Ne maturi gbodzoo mamɔ to maɣere wũ sɔ, “I bo Ɔko Sekelea ame ne, matsɛrɛ mapia sɔ Kristo iibakpi ɔnya, ne ɔso be ɔso fiɛ ato aɣɛ sɔ maakɔlɛ Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi kato?
Nna nɖe Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi gɔgbe?” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ɔkaniɛ to ɔ̃awe i mi kɔrɛ ɔwi kɛkɛĩ, ne ɔso misɛ i ɔkaniɛ ame si idududu iibafu mi iso.
Alasɔ ngɔ nsɛ ɔsɛ i idududu ame iisɛ ɔtsue ngbegɔ ɔsɛ.
Ne ɔso mifɔ ɔkaniɛ miɖe gɔ ɔpia i mi kɔrɛ si miaɖe ikpawaĩ ame maturi.” Gɔ Yesu ɔɣere ma ara wagbe ɔro ne, ɔrui ɔsɛ ɔ̃akɔla so.
Ma Yudase Ɔte Sɔ Maifɔ Yesu Maɖe.
Atoa sɔ Yesu ɔbara awawãra wagbe ɔɖuɖu i ma ndɛ̃ ne, maifɔ wũ maɖe.
Ɣɛɛ iba ngbɔ sɔ nnɛ i Ɣaa Kanyaɖidze Yesaya ɔtsɛrɛ ɔsɛ aaba i ne ame sɔ, “Bosate, nna lofɔ bo itɔ̃me nɛ boɣɛ ɔɖe?
Fiɛ mabe ndɛ̃ iɖe ɔɖi ɔ̃ ɔle ɔte?” Ne ɔso maiwo ɔfɔ ɔɖe alasɔ Yesaya ɔtsɛrɛ ana sɔ, “Ɣaa ɔbiɛ ma anɔmi fiɛ ɔtã maba atsue ɔle.
Sɔ ma anɔmi iibanya, fiɛ ma adzuni ana iibanɔ ara karɔ̃, ‘Fiɛ maafiniki maba wũ kɔrɛ fiɛ loasa ma.’ Ngbɔ i Ɣaa ɔɣɛ ne.” Yesaya ɔɣɛ ngbɔ alasɔ ɔnya Yesu ikpawaĩ fiɛ ɔɖe ika i ɔ̃ iso.
Atoa sɔ ise kumɛgɔgbe ne, ma Yudase makpakpa gbodzoo ɔfɔ Yesu maɖe, ɣɛɛ gɔ mato manigã ma Farisise ɔso ne, maisɛ maɖe ika i ne iso kpawee sɔ maaba maasa ma maɖi i kasarɛkɔ̃.
Alasɔ masɛ maɖɔɛ maturi ile maɖo Ɣaa ile.
Yesu Atɔ̃me Lotã Maturi Ipɔ.
Yesu ɔla kulu teteree ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Ngɔ lofɔ me ɔɖe ne, iiɖe wũ ɔnɔwɛ̃ iɖe ɔfɔ, ɣɛɛ bo gu ngɔ lopia me katɔ̃me iɖe ɔfɔ.
Ɔbiara gɔ lonya me ana ne, ɔ̃ɔnya ngɔ lopia me katɔ̃me.
Loba kayi ame lɛ ikpawaĩ awe, sɔ ɔbiara gɔ lofɔ me ɔɖe iisibawe i idududu ame.
“Si ɔrere ɔnɔ wũ itɔ̃me fiɛ ɔ̃ibara i ne iso ne, loibaɣɛgu wũ atɔ̃me.
Loiba loɣɛgu kayiiso atɔ̃me, ɣɛɛ loba lotã kã iɖi.
Ngɔ losɛ̃ me fiɛ ɔ̃ifɔ wũ itɔ̃me ne, ɔba ngɔ loaɣɛgu wũ atɔ̃me.
Wũ ara wa lote loaɣɛgu wũ atɔ̃me ku iyi tsɔra.
Alasɔ loiɖe ika i mme mɔmɔ ɔle ame, ɣɛɛ Tete gɔ lopia me katɔ̃me lotã me ɔle sɔ loɖe ika loɣɛ nnɛ loaɣɛ.
Loɣe sɔ ɔ̃ itɔ̃me sɛ itã ngbã mɛ nna katui.
Ne ɔso nnɛ losɛ loɣɛ ne, ne nɖe nnɛ i Tete ɔɣere me sɔ loɣɛ ne.”
Yesu Ɔfore Ɔ̃ Marasuãdze Ngba.
Iyi nɛ i kaɖe aasɛ̃ fiɛ maaɖe Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo Iyi ne, Yesu ka ɔɣe sɔ ɔ̃ ɔwi ɔɔɣo gɔ ɔ̃abɔrɛ i kayi gagbe iso ɔkɛlɛ ɔ̃ Ɔse kɔrɛ.
Ɔɖɔɛ mma nɖe ɔ̃ mare i kayiiso fiɛ ɔɖɔɛ ma ɔsɛ ɔ̃ɔbo ta kawirikɔ̃.
Kutsuɛ gɔmɔ gɔ Yesu gu ɔ̃ marasuãdze si mato maɖe ara ne, Ɔbosam ɔɔsu adzuni lalaa ɔpia i Yuda gɔ nɖe Simon Iskariot ɔbi ame koko sɔ ɔɖi Yesu ɔtã.
Yesu ɣe sɔ ɔ̃ Ɔse ɔsu ɔle ɔɖuɖu ɔtã wũ, ɔɣe sɔ Ɣaa kɔrɛ ɔbɔrɛ fiɛ Ɔ̃ kɔrɛ ɔto ɔkpese ɔkɛlɛ.
Ne ɔso ɔta i ɔpɔrɔ̃ katɔ̃, ɔɖi ɔ̃ awu tagbaraa wa ɔpia ɔsɛ, fiɛ ka ɔsu ɔsa ɔkpasa.
Ne ɔka ndu ɔfere i kapoi ame, ne ɔtsɛ ma ngba ifore, isu ɔsa gɔ ɔkpasa iɖiɖi ma ndu i ngba.
Gɔ Yesu ɔbo Simon Petro kɔrɛ ne, Petro ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Bosate, ɔbie ato sɔ aba aafore me ngba?” Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Kiniɔ ne, ainɔ nnɛ loto lobara karɔ̃, ɣɛɛ ɔwi kama ne, ato aanɔ karɔ̃.” Petro ɔɖi kanya sɔ, “Ooɣo!
Aibafore me ngba anya.” Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Si aitã lofore-ɔ ngba ne, tsue sɔ ana kaɖekɔ̃ i wũ ame.” Ne Simon Petro ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Bosate, si ngbɔ ne, iyɔ daafore me ngba kere, ɣɛɛ fore me nrɔɔ̃ gu iti ana!” Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ngɔ loɔpie ndu ɔɔsekele koko, ne ɔso ɔ̃isinya itupie iɖo ngba ifore.
Mi ɔɖuɖu ɔɔsekele, iɖo ɔwɛ̃.” Yesu ɔɣɛ ngbɔ alasɔ ka ɔɣe ngɔ loaɖi wũ ɔtã.
Ne ɔso ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Mi ɔɖuɖu ɔɔsekele iɖo ɔwɛ̃” ne.
Gɔ Yesu ɔɔfore ma ngba ɔro ne, ɔkpesegu ɔ̃ awu ɔpia, fiɛ ka ɔsɛ ɔ̃asɛ i ɔ̃ kasɛkɔ̃ i ɔpɔrɔ̃ iti.
Ne ɔkarɛ ɔ̃ masiaidze sɔ, “Minɔ nnɛ lobara ngbe karɔ̃?
Misɛ mikpere me sɔ Ratedze gu Bosate, ilɛ ngbɔ, alasɔ ngbɔ loɖe ne.
Mme gɔ mme nɖe mi Sate gu Ratedze ne, lofore mi ngba.
Ne ɔso mi wũ mifore mi malaa ngba.
