Loɔsɛ ikparĩ lotã mi, ne ɔso mi wũ mibara nnɛ lobara lotã mi mitã so.
Gbaã loto loɣere mi sɔ ɔɖabo iisɛ ɔɖo ɔ̃ ɔkɔse, fiɛ katɔ̃mesɛdze iisɛ ɔɖo ngɔ lopia wũ katɔ̃me.
Kiniɔ gɔ ka miɣe ɔnukuare gɔgbe ne, so aaɣɔ mi si misu ara wagbe mipia i kurabarara ame.
“Iiɖe mi ɔɖuɖu ɔso loto loɣɛ nnɛgbe, loɣe mma loɖi.
Ɣɛɛ si itɔ̃me nɛ matsɛrɛ mapia i Ɔko Sekelea ame aaba i ne ame sɔ, ‘Bo gu ngɔ nto bopia kɔrɔ̃ i irɔi ame boɖe ara lota ɔya me iso.’ “Loto loɣere mi nnɛgbe tɔtɔ fiɛ iaba, sɔ si iba ne, miatsue sɔ, ‘Mme nɖe ngɔ Loɖe.’ Gbaã loto loɣere mi sɔ ɔbiara gɔ lofɔ ngɔ mme lopia katɔ̃me ne, mme iɖe ɔfɔ.
Fiɛ ɔbiara gɔ lofɔ me ne, ngɔ lopia me katɔ̃me iɖe ɔfɔ.” Yesu Ɔɣɛ Ɔsɛ Sɔ Mato Maaɖi Wũ Matã.
Gɔ Yesu ɔɣɛ ara wagbe ɔro ne, ɔmararã so ta ɔ̃ ɔtu ame.
Ne ɔɣere ma ɔɖi sɔ, “Gbaã loto loɣere mi sɔ mi ndɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ to ɔ̃aɖi me ɔtã.” Marasuãdze ɔkpɔkpɔtɔ pelepele mato manyɔ so i katɔ̃ sɔ ma nna ɔto.
Rasuãdze gɔ i Yesu sɛ ɔɖɔɛ ɔɖo si ɔmatã wũ.
Ne Simon Petro ɔma wũ anɔmi sɔ, “Karɛ wũ sɔ nna ɔto ɔɣɛ ala.” Ne rasuãdze gɔmɔ ɔbore ɔbo Yesu ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Bosate, nna ɔɖe?” Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ngɔ loakpɛti aɖera loti kutu losu lotã ne, ɔ̃ ɔɖe ne.” Ne ɔso Yesu ɔkpɛti aɖera, ɔti kutu fiɛ ka ɔsu ɔtã Yuda, Simon Iskariot ɔbi.
Ɔluwɛ̃ gɔ Yuda ɔfɔ aɖera ne, Satana ɔbo i ɔ̃ ame.
Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Pɛ siwa si abara nnɛ ato abie sɔ abara.” Mma nsi i ɔpɔrɔ̃ katɔ̃ kuwɛ̃ iinɔ nnɛ i Yesu ɔɣere Yuda karɔ̃.
Gɔ Yuda kɔrɛ i sikã kakotoi se ɔso ne, marasuãdze mawɛ̃ ɔbu sɔ ɔɣere i Yesu to wũ sɔ ɔsɛ ɔ̃aɣa ara ɔtã iyi iɖe, ɣee ɔbie irere ɔtã mawɛrɛba.
Gɔ Yuda ɔfɔ aɖera ne, ɔbɔrɛ i iyo ɔluwɛ̃.
Kasɛ̃ ka iɖe.
Yesu Ɔtã Ɔ̃ Marasuãdze Mmara Ɣɛtɛ.
Gɔ Yuda ɔbɔrɛ i iyo kama ne, Yesu ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Kiniɔ ne, maɔɖi Ɔturi Awune Ɔbi ikpawaĩ mate, fiɛ iki i ɔ̃ iso ne, Ɣaa ikpawaĩ ana ɔɔte sekelee.
Si makɔlɛ Ɣaa iyere kato iki Ɔbi iso ne, iyɔ Ɣaa to ɔ̃akɔlɛ Ɔbi iyere iki i ɔ̃ mɔmɔ iso ɔluwɛ̃.
“Wũ mabi, loisibawe i mi kɔrɛ ɔwi ɔdzoro.
Mito miabie me, ɣɛɛ lɛ kumɛgɔ loɣere ma Yudase makpakpa ne, ‘Ngbegɔ losɛ ne, miito miawo mmɔ ɔba.’ “Kiniɔ ne, mmara ɣɛtɛ loto lotã mi sɔ miɖɔɛ so.
Lɛ kumɛgɔ loɖɔɛ mi ne, mi wũ miɖɔɛ so ngbɔ.
Si mito miɖɔɛ so ne, ɔbiara to ɔ̃atsue sɔ wũ marasuãdze miɖe.” Yesu Ɔɣɛ Ɔsɛ Sɔ Petro To Ɔ̃asɛ̃ Wũ.
Ne Simon Petro ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Bosate, i lɛ asɛ?” Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ngbegɔ losɛ ne, aito aawo ɔba kiniɔ, ɣɛɛ ɔwi kama ne, ato aaba mmɔ.” Petro ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Be ɔso loibawo-ɔ ɔsiai kiniɔ?
Si inya kɔra ne, loakpi i fɔ iti!” Ne Yesu ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Afɔ aɖe sɔ aakpi i wũ iti?
Gbaã loto loɣere-ɔ sɔ, si kɔkɔ ɖeakatɔ̃ aaɖi kanya ne, ɔɔsɛ̃ me ikpɛ itɛ sɔ aiɣe me.”
Yesu Ɔpia Ɔ̃ Marasuãdze Katetere.
Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Midaati mikpakpa, mifɔ Ɣaa miɖe si mifɔ me wũ miɖe.
Kuwekɔ̃ gbodzoo pia i Tete iyo ame, ne ɔso losɛ loaledza kɔ̃ losɛ mi.
Si iise ngbɔ ne, loibaɣere mi.
Si loɔsɛ loaledza kabokɔ̃ losɛ mi ne, loakpese loba loakɔ mi sɔ ngbegɔ lopia ne, mi wũ miawe i mmɔ.
Miɣe ɔri gɔ iso miaki fiɛ miaba ngbegɔ losɛ.” Yesu Nɖe Ɔri Bielea Gɔ Iso Maaki Fiɛ Maanya Ɣaa.
Ne Toma ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Bosate, gɔ boiɣe ngbegɔ asɛ ne, nda boabara fiɛ boatsue ɔri?” Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Mme nɖe ɔri, ɔnukuare gu ngbã.
Kuwɛ̃ iibawo Tete kɔrɛ ɔkɛlɛ si ɔ̃iki i wũ iso.
Si ɔɣe miɣe me ne, tee miɣe Tete ɔ̃ wũ.
Ɣɛɛ ita i kiniɔ ne, miɔtsue wũ fiɛ miɔnya wũ ana.” Mmɔ i Filipo to ɔɣere Yesu sɔ, “Bosate, te bo Tete, si imi bo.” Yesu ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Filipo, kokooko gɔ lopia i mi kɔrɛ ne, aiɣe me, ɣɛɛ?
Ɔbiara gɔ loɔnya me ne, ɔ̃ɔnya Tete.
Be ɔso fiɛ ato aɣɛ sɔ, ‘Te bo Tete’?
Ɛɛbɛrɛ aifɔ aɖe sɔ Tete pia i wũ ame fiɛ mme wũ lopia i Tete ame?
Atɔ̃me wa losɛ loɣere mi ne, iiɖe wũ kɔrɛ abɔrɛ.
Tete mɔmɔ gɔ mpia i wũ ame nto ɔbara ɔ̃ karabara.
Mifɔ me miɖe sɔ lopia i Tete ame fiɛ Tete ɔ̃ wũ ɔpia i wũ ame.
Si miibawo ne ɔfɔ ɔɖe ne, mifɔ miɖe ala wũ kurabarara ɔso.
Gbaã loto loɣere mi sɔ ɔbiara gɔ lofɔ me ɔɖe ne, ara wa loto lobara ne, ɔto ɔ̃abara wã, fiɛ ɔto ɔ̃abara nwa loɖo ngbɔ ana ala losɛ Tete kɔrɛ.
Fiɛ loabara ira biara nɛ miakarɛ i wũ iyere ame sɔ Tete iyere aakɔlɛ kato iki i Ɔbi iso.
Ira biara nɛ miakarɛ me i wũ iyere ame ne, loabara ne.” Yesu Ɔɣɛ Siwarã Bielea Isese Ɔsɛ.
Ne Yesu ɔɣɛ ana sɔ, “Si mito miɖɔɛ me ne, mito miabara i wũ mmara iso.
Nto loakarɛ Tete fiɛ ɔ̃asese mi Buaidze mama gɔ loibarui i mi kɔrɛ ɔnya.
Ɔ̃ nɖe Siwarã dzɛ nsɛ siɖi ɔnukuare i Ɣaa iso site ne.
Kayiiso maturi iibawo wũ ɔfɔ alasɔ maibawo wũ ɔnya fiɛ maatsue wũ.
Ɣɛɛ mi ne, miɣe wũ alasɔ ɔpiagu mi, fiɛ ɔpia i mi ame.
“Loibanyua mi losɛ lɛ makpise mabi.
Loto loakpese loba mi kɔrɛ.
Ikuti kɛkɛĩ gɔ kayiiso iisibanya me, ɣɛɛ mi mito mianya me.
Gɔ losi ngbã ɔso ne, mi wũ mito miasɛ ngbã.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ne, mito miatsue sɔ lopia i Tete ame, mi wũ mipia i wũ ame, fiɛ mme wũ lopia i mi ame.
“Ngɔ lomɔɛ̃ wũ mmara ɔto fiɛ ɔto ɔɖe me i iso ne, ɔ̃ nɖe ngɔ nto ɔɖɔɛ me ne.
Ngɔ nto ɔɖɔɛ me ne, Tete to ɔ̃aɖɔɛ wũ, fiɛ mme wũ loto loaɖɔɛ wũ fiɛ loaɖi so lote wũ.” Ne Yuda gɔ loiɖe Iskariot ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Bosate, nda ibara fiɛ bo kere aaɖi so ate fiɛ iiɖegu kayiiso maturi?” Yesu ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Si ɔrere to ɔɖɔɛ me ne, ɔɖe wũ mmara iso.
Iyɔ Tete to ɔ̃aɖɔɛ wũ, fiɛ mme gu Tete aaɖi kasɛkɔ̃ i ɔ̃ kɔrɛ.
Ngɔ loito ɔɖɔɛ me ne, ɔ̃isɛ ɔmɔɛ̃ wũ itɔ̃me ɔla.
Atɔ̃me wa loɣɛ minɔ ne, iiɖe mme mɔmɔ are aɖe, ɣɛɛ Tete gɔ lopia me katɔ̃me are aɖe.
“Loɣere mi atɔ̃me wagbe gɔ lokpese lopia i mi kɔrɛ.
Ɣɛɛ Buaidze gɔ nɖe Siwarã Bielea dzɛ i Tete aasese i wũ iyere ame ne, ɔ̃ nto ɔ̃ate mi ira biara fiɛ ɔ̃anyigira mi ara wa ɔɖuɖu loɣere mi ne.
“Isobuɛ si iwegu mi.
Wũ isobuɛ loto lotã mi.
Iiɖe kumɛgɔ i kayiiso sɛ katã isobuɛ loto lotã mi.
Midaamararã so, midaanigã ana.
Minɔ loɣere mi sɔ, ‘Si lorui i mi kɔrɛ ne, loto loakpese loba.’ Si mito miɖɔɛ me ne, miana isoɣɔ sɔ loto lokɛlɛ Tete kɔrɛ, alasɔ ɔmɔ ɔɖo me.
Kiniɔ ne loɔɣere mi nnɛgbe loɖegu katɔ̃ sɔ si iba ne, miafɔ miɖe.
Loisibakɛlɛgu i katɔ̃ loɖe ika gbodzoo, alasɔ ngɔ nto ɔɖe kayi gagbe iso ka ɔba, ɣɛɛ ɔna ɔle i wũ iso.
Ɣɛɛ ikote sɔ kayiiso aatsue sɔ nsɛ loɖɔɛ Tete, fiɛ nsɛ lobara i ɔ̃ itɔ̃me iso.
“A o-o, mita si borui i ngbe.
Yesu Nɖe Kuɖedziri Gbaã.
“Mme nɖe kuɖedziri gbaã, fiɛ Tete nɖe adziribi kpɛ̃dze.
Wũ idzirikpa biara nɛ loisɛ iɣɔ̃ abi ne, ɔsɛ ɔtu ne ɔɖi, fiɛ ibiara nɛ nsɛ iɣɔ̃ abi ne, ɔsɛ ɔyuɛ ne ɔledza sɔ iawo abi gbodzoo ɔɣɔ̃.
Mi iso ɔɔsekele koko ala ara wa loɔte mi ɔso.
Miwe i wũ ame si mme wũ lowe i mi ame.
Kumɛgɔ ame i idzirikpa iibawo abi ɔɣɔ̃ si iito i kudziri iso ne, ngbɔ ame mi wũ miibawo abi ɔɣɔ̃ si miiwe i wũ ame ne.
“Mme nɖe kuɖedziri fiɛ mi nɖe akpa.
Ngɔ mpia i wũ ame fiɛ mme wũ lopia i ɔ̃ ame ne, ɔto ɔ̃aɣɔ̃ abi gbodzoo, alasɔ si lona i mi ame ne, miibawo kuira ɔbara.
Ɔbiara gɔ loisɛ ɔwe i wũ ame ne, ɔse lɛ idzirikpa nɛ matu maɖi i kudziri iso fiɛ maafuĩdza masɛ ikore.
Akpa wamɔ igbã ne, masɛ masa wã kanya mapia wã ɔtɔ atsue.
Si miwe i wũ ame fiɛ wũ itɔ̃me ana ɔwe i mi ame ne, iyɔ mito miakarɛ ira biara nɛ miɖɔɛ fiɛ miana ne ana.
Si miɣɔ̃ abi gbodzoo ne, isɛ ikɔlɛ Tete iyere kato fiɛ isɛ isia ita sɔ wũ marasuãdze miɖe.
Nsɛ loɖɔɛ mi lɛ kumɛgɔ i Tete sɛ ɔɖɔɛ me, miwe i wũ kuɖɔɛ ame.
Si mibara i wũ mmara iso ne, miakɛlɛgu i katɔ̃ miwe i wũ kuɖɔɛ ame lɛ kumɛgɔ lokã Tete atsue fiɛ lopia i ɔ̃ kuɖɔɛ ame.
“Loɔɣere mi ara wagbe sɔ wũ isoɣɔ aawe i mi ame fiɛ mi isoɣɔ aayi pɔpɔɔpɔ.
Wũ mmara nɖe sɔ, miɖɔɛ so lɛ kumɛgɔ loto loɖɔɛ mi.
Kuɖɔɛ gɔ loɖo gɔ i ɔturi aawe ɔtã ɔ̃ malaa nɖe sɔ ɔ̃asu ɔ̃ ngbã ɔtã i ma iti.
Wũ malaa miɖe si mibara i nnɛ loɣere mi iso.
Loisito lokpere mi sɔ maɖabo, alasɔ ɔɖabo iisɛ ɔtsue nnɛ i ma ɔkɔse sɛ ɔbara.
Ɣɛɛ ne, ka loto lokpere mi sɔ wũ malaa, alasɔ loɔɣere mi ira biara nɛ lonɔ lobɔrɛgu i Tete kɔrɛ.
Iiɖe mi loɖi me, ɣɛɛ mme loɖi mi, fiɛ losɛra mi sɔ si miasɛ miaɣɔ̃ abi gbodzoo fiɛ mi abi aase ɔwi biara.
Iyɔ Tete aatã mi ira biara nɛ mikarɛ i wũ iyere ame.
Mmara mɛ loto lotã mi nɖe sɔ, miɖɔɛ so.” Kayiiso Maturi Sɛ Matsiri Yesu Masiaidze.
Ne Yesu ɔɣɛ ana sɔ, “Si kayiiso maturi ɔtsiri mi ne, mitsue sɔ maɔɖe katɔ̃ matsiri me koko.
Si kayiiso maturi miɖe ne, tee maaɖɔɛ mi lɛ ma malaa.
Ɣɛɛ kayiiso ame lokpere mi loɖi fiɛ miisiɖe kayiiso maturi, ne ɔso fiɛ matsiri mi ne.
Minyigi sɔ loɣere mi sɔ, ‘Ɔɖabo iisɛ ɔɖo ɔ̃ ɔkɔse.’ Si mati me kama ne, mi wũ mato maati mi kama.
Si makã wũ ara ite atsue ne, mi wũ mato maakã mi ara ite atsue.
Ɣɛɛ mato maabara mi ara wagbe ɔɖuɖu alasɔ miɖe wũ mare fiɛ maiɣe ngɔ lopia me katɔ̃me.
Si lodaaba loaɖe ma ika ne, tee maibaɖe ipɔ i ikpi iti.
Ɣɛɛ kiniɔ ne, masiina kafara itu kuiwɛ̃ i ma akpi iti.
Ɔbiara gɔ lotsiri me ɔtsiri Tete ana.
Si iiɖe ɔbara lobara karabara ga igbã i kuwɛ̃ iibara i ma ndɛ̃ ɔnya ne, tee maibaɖe ipɔ i ikpi iti.
Ɣɛɛ kiniɔ ne, manya ara wa lobara fiɛ matsiri bo gu Tete inyɔ.
Iba ngbɔ sɔ nnɛ matsɛrɛ mapia i ma mmara ɔko ame aaba i ne ame sɔ, ‘Matsiri me siefe.’ “Loto loasese mi Buaidze gɔ loabɔrɛ i Tete kɔrɛ.
Ɔ̃ nɖe Siwarã dzɛ nsɛ siɖi ɔnukuare i Ɣaa iso site.
Si ɔ̃ɔse i Tete kɔrɛ ɔba ne, ɔto ɔ̃aɖe aɖansiɛ i wũ iso ɔtã mi.
Mi wũ maɖansiɛ miɖe me alasɔ miɔwegu me ita i karɔ̃kasɛkɔ̃.
“Loɔɣere mi ara wagbe ɔɖuɖu si nrɔɔ̃ iibafɛ̃ mi i mi kafɔkaɖe ame.
Mato maasa mi maɖi i ma kusarɛkɔ̃, fiɛ ɔwi to ɔ̃aba gɔ si ɔrere ɔɖoe mi ne, ɔ̃abu sɔ Ɣaa karabara kaɖe ɔto ɔbara.
Maturi to maabara mi ara wagbe alasɔ maiɣe me, ɣee Tete.
Ɣɛɛ loto loɣere mi ara wagbe sɔ si ɔwi ɔɣo fiɛ mato mabara wã ne, mianyigi sɔ loɔɣere mi.
“Loiɣere mi ara wagbe ta karɔ̃kasɛkɔ̃ alasɔ lopia i mi kɔrɛ.
Kiniɔ ne, ka losɛ ngɔ lopia me katɔ̃me kɔrɛ, ɣɛɛ mi kuwɛ̃ iito mikarɛ me sɔ lɛ losɛ.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ loɣere mi ara wagbe ɔso ne, ka mito mimararã so.
Atoa sɔ ise ngbɔ ne, gbaã loto loɣere mi sɔ ilɛ itã mi sɔ loakɛlɛ, alasɔ si loikɛlɛ ne, Buaidze iibawo mi kɔrɛ ɔba.
Ɣɛɛ si lokɛlɛ ne, loasu wũ losese mi.
Si ɔba ne, ɔto ɔ̃aɖi ɔte kayiiso maturi sɔ mayu ɔri i ikpi gu sibɔlɔlɔ gu atɔ̃me iɣɛgu iso.
Mayu ɔri i ikpi iso alasɔ maifɔ me maɖe.
Mayu ɔri i sibɔlɔlɔ iso alasɔ loto lokɛlɛ Tete kɔrɛ fiɛ miisibanya me minya.
Mayu ɔri i atɔ̃me iɣɛgu iso alasɔ Ɣaa ɔɔɣɛgu ngɔ nto ɔɖe kayi gagbe iso atɔ̃me ɔtã wũ ipɔ.
“Loba atɔ̃me gbodzoo loaɣere mi, ɣɛɛ kiniɔ ne, ato aaɖo mi iti.
Ɔwi gɔ i Siwarã dzɛ nsɛ siɖi ɔnukuare i Ɣaa iso site ɔɔba ne, sito siate mi ɔnukuare ɔɖuɖu i Ɣaa iso.
Ɔ̃ibaɖe ika i ɔ̃ mɔmɔ ɔle ame, ɣɛɛ ara wa ɔnɔ ɔ̃aɣɛ, fiɛ ɔto ɔ̃aɣere mi ara wa nto aaba i katɔ̃.
Ɔ̃ gɔmɔ loatã makɔlɛ wũ iyere kato ne, alasɔ ɔto ɔ̃aɖi ara wa ɔfɔ i wũ kɔrɛ ɔte mi.
Ara wa ɔɖuɖu nɖe Tete are ne, wũ are aɖe, ne ɔso loɣere mi sɔ nnɛ i Siwarã ɔnɔ sibɔrɛgu i wũ kɔrɛ siaɣere mi ne.” Marasuãdze Isomararã To Iakpese Ma Isoɣɔ.
Ne Yesu ɔsɔgu i katɔ̃ ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Ikuti kɛkɛĩ ne, miisibanya me, ɣɛɛ ɔwi kurukutu kama ne, mito mianya me ana.” Ne ɔ̃ marasuãdze ɔkarɛ so sɔ, “Mme itɔ̃me igbã iɖe ɔto ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Ikuti kɛkɛĩ ne, miisibanya me, ɣɛɛ ɔwi kurukutu kama ne, mito mianya me ana,’ fiɛ ɔto ɔɣɛ ana sɔ, ‘Alasɔ losɛ Tete kɔrɛ’?
Nnɛ ɔɣɛ sɔ ikuti kɛkɛĩ ne boisibanya wũ karɔ̃, ɣɛɛ?
Boinɔ itɔ̃me nɛ ɔɣɛ ngbe karɔ̃.” Yesu ɣe sɔ ɔ̃ marasuãdze to mabie sɔ makarɛ wũ itɔ̃me, ne ɔso ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Itɔ̃me nɛ loɣɛ sɔ ikuti kɛkɛĩ ne miibanya me, ɣɛɛ ɔwi kɛkɛĩ kama ne mito mianya me mito mikakarɛ so ɛɛbɛrɛ?
Gbaã loto loɣere mi sɔ mito miabiɛ misɛ kaku, ɣɛɛ kayiiso maturi to maana isoɣɔ.
Mito miamararã so, ɣɛɛ mi isomararã to iakpese isoɣɔ.
Si ɔrɔ̃go ɔɣewi ɔɣo ne, ɔsɛ ɔwe i isoma ame, alasɔ ɔɣe sɔ ibo ɔnawi ɔɔɣo, ɣɛɛ si ɔ̃ɔɣe ɔbi ne, ka ɔsɛ ɔɣara ɔ̃ inyɛwe, alasɔ ɔba isoɣɔ sɔ ɔ̃ɔɣe ɔbi ɔbɔ kayiiso.
Ngbɔ mito mimararã so kiniɔ ne, ɣɛɛ loto loaledza mi inya, fiɛ so aaɣɔ mi gbaã sɔ kuwɛ̃ iibawo mi isoɣɔ ɔmɔɛ̃ ɔfɔ.
“Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, miisibakarɛ me kuira.
Fiɛ gbaã loto loɣere mi sɔ si mikarɛ Tete ira biara ne, ɔto ɔ̃atã mi i wũ iyere ame.
Ipɛ i kiniɔ ne, miikarɛ kuira i wũ iyere ame.
Mikarɛ ara fiɛ miafɔ, sɔ mi isoɣɔ aayi.
Yesu Ɔɔɖe Kayiiso Iso.
“Losu agbã loɣere mi ara wagbe, ɣɛɛ ɔwi to ɔba gɔ loisibaɖe mi aka i agbã ame.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ne, loaɣere mi ara loɖi i Tete iso.
Iyi nɛmɔ ne, mito miakarɛ ara i wũ iyere ame.
Loito loɣɛ sɔ mme loakarɛ Tete ara i mi kanya, alasɔ Tete mɔmɔ to ɔɖɔɛ mi.
Ɔto ɔɖɔɛ mi alasɔ mito miɖɔɛ me fiɛ mifɔ miɖe sɔ Ɣaa kɔrɛ lobɔrɛ.
Gbaã, Tete kɔrɛ lobɔrɛ loba kayiiso, fiɛ loɔbɔrɛ i kayiiso loto lokpese lokɛlɛ ɔ̃ kɔrɛ.” Marasuãdze ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ɛɣɛɛ̃, kini ato aɖe bo ika aɖi fiɛ iiɖe agbã ame ne.
Kini botsue sɔ aɣe ira biara ne iinya sɔ kuwɛ̃ aakarɛ-ɔ kuira ne.
Iki i nnɛgbe iso ne, boɔfɔ boɖe sɔ Ɣaa kɔrɛ abɔrɛ.” Yesu ɔtã ma mmuai sɔ, “Miɔfɔ miɖe kini?
Ɔwi to ɔba fiɛ ɔ̃ɔɣo, gɔ mi ɔɖuɖu to miasame miɣɛ me mikɛlɛ mi ayo ikuti wũ ɔnɔwɛ̃.
Ɣɛɛ loiɖe wũ ɔnɔwɛ̃ alasɔ Tete piagu me.
Loɔɣere mi ara wagbe si so aaɣɔ mi i mi mawɛ̃ ibaragu me ame.
Kayiiso to kaatã miwe inyɛ, ɣɛɛ mina ɔtu alasɔ loɔɖe kayiiso iso!”
Yesu Ɔkparama Kayi.
Gɔ Yesu ɔɣɛ ara wagbe ɔro ne, ɔkɔlɛ anɔ ɔnyɔ kato, ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Tete, ɔwi ɔɔɣo.
Kɔlɛ fɔ Ɔbi iyere kato si fɔ Ɔbi ana aakɔlɛ fɔ ire kato.
Alasɔ atã wũ ɔle i maturi ɔɖuɖu iso sɔ ɔ̃atã mma ɔɖuɖu asu atã wũ ngbã mɛ nna katui.
Ngbã mɛ nna katui karɔ̃ nɖe sɔ maatsue sɔ fɔ ɔnɔwɛ̃ nɖe Ɣaa gbaã fiɛ maatsue Yesu Kristo gɔ apia katɔ̃me ana.
Loɔkɔlɛ fɔ iyere kato i karɔ̃ iso, alasɔ loɔro karabara ga apia me sɔ lobara.
Kiniɔ ne Tete, kɔlɛ wũ iyere kato i fɔ anɔ isɛ iabo ngbegɔ losia ku ɔwi gɔ lowe i fɔ kɔrɛ ta kayi karɔ̃kasɛkɔ̃.
Yesu Ɔkparama Kayi Ɔtã Ɔ̃ Marasuãdze.
“Loɔɖi-ɔ lote mma atã me abɔrɛgu i kayi ame.
Fɔ mare maɖe, fiɛ fɔ losu ma atã me.
Makã fɔ itɔ̃me atsue, fiɛ kiniɔ ne, ka maɣe sɔ ira biara nɛ atã me ne, fɔ kɔrɛ ibɔrɛ.
Loɣere ma katɔ̃me ga apia me, fiɛ mafɔ kã.
Maɣe sɔ gbaã ne, fɔ kɔrɛ lobɔrɛ fiɛ mafɔ maɖe sɔ fɔ lopia me katɔ̃me.
Loito lokparama kayi lotã kayiiso, ɣɛɛ mma atã me iti loto lokparama kayi, alasɔ fɔ mare maɖe.
“Mma ɔɖuɖu nɖe wũ mare ne, fɔ mare maɖe.
Fiɛ mma ɔɖuɖu nɖe fɔ mare ne, wũ mare maɖe.
Ma iso asɛ akɔlɛ wũ iyere kato akigu.
Kiniɔ ne, ka loba fɔ kɔrɛ, losiina i kayiiso, ɣɛɛ ma mapia i kayiiso.
Tete Sekelea, dzuɛ̃ ma i ɔle gɔ mpia i fɔ iyere nɛ atã me ame sɔ maaɖe mawɛ̃ lɛ kumɛgɔ i bo gu-ɔ ɖe mawɛ̃.
Ɔwi gɔ lopia i ma kɔrɛ ne, lodzuɛ̃ ma ala ɔle gɔ mpia i iyere nɛ atã me ame.
Lodzuɛ̃ ma sɔ ma kuwɛ̃ iiyu iɖo ngɔ ikote sɔ ɔ̃ayu, sɔ nnɛ matsɛrɛ masɛ i Ɔko Sekelea ame aaba i ne ame.
“Ɣɛɛ kiniɔ ne, ka loba fɔ kɔrɛ.
Loɣɛ atɔ̃me wagbe i kayiiso sɔ wũ isoɣɔ aayi ma situ ame pɔpɔɔpɔ lɛ kumɛgɔ mme wũ loba isoɣɔ kiniɔ.
Loɣere ma fɔ itɔ̃me fiɛ kayiiso ɔtsiri ma alasɔ maiɖe kayiiso mare lɛ kumɛgɔ mme wũ loiɖe kayiiso ɔre.
“Loito lokarɛ sɔ mɔɛ̃ ma ɖi i kayiiso, ɣɛɛ nnɛ loto lokarɛ nɖe sɔ dzuɛ̃ ma ɖi bɔrɛgu i Tsirise nrɔɔ̃ ame.
Kumɛgɔ ame loiɖe kayiiso ɔre ne, ngbɔ ame ma wũ maiɖe kayiiso mare ne.
Bara ma sekelee iki i ɔnukuare ame, fɔ itɔ̃me nɖe ɔnukuare.
Lopia ma kayiiso maturi kɔrɛ lɛ kumɛgɔ fɔ wũ apia me kayiiso.
Ma ɔso ne, lobara so sekelee lotã-ɔ sɔ ma wũ ne, maabara so sekelee gbaã matã-ɔ.
Yesu Ɔkparama Kayi I Mafɔɖedze Ɔɖuɖu Iti.
“Iiɖe ma ɔnɔwɛ̃ saã iti loto lokparama kayi, ɣɛɛ mma ana ɔɖuɖu loafɔ me maɖe iki i ma itɔ̃me iso iti.
Tete!
Tã sɔ ma ɔɖuɖu aaɖe mawɛ̃.
Mawe i bo ame lɛ kumɛgɔ apia i wũ ame fiɛ mme wũ lopia i fɔ ame.
Maɖe mawɛ̃ si kayiiso maturi aafɔ maɖe sɔ fɔ lopia me katɔ̃me.
“Lopia ma kuwarɛ lɛ kumɛgɔ apia me kuwarɛ sɔ si maaɖe mawɛ̃ lɛ kumɛgɔ i bo gu-ɔ ɖe mawɛ̃.
Lopia i ma ame, fiɛ fɔ wũ apia i wũ ame sɔ maaɖe mawɛ̃ pelepele sɔ kayiiso aatsue sɔ fɔ lopia me katɔ̃me fiɛ asɛ aɖɔɛ fɔ mabi lɛ kumɛgɔ asɛ aɖɔɛ me.
“Tete!
Fɔ losu ma atã me fiɛ loto lobie sɔ mawe i ngbegɔ lopia fiɛ maanya wũ ikpawaĩ nɛ atã me.
Alasɔ ato aɖɔɛ me fiɛ abara kayiiso.
“Tete Bɔlɔlɔa!
Kayiiso maturi iiɣe-ɔ, ɣɛɛ mme loɣe-ɔ, fiɛ mmagbe ɣe sɔ fɔ lopia me katɔ̃me.
Loɖi-ɔ lote ma fiɛ loto loakɛlɛgu i katɔ̃ lobara ngbɔ sɔ kuɖɔɛ gɔ aba atã me aawe i ma ame fiɛ mme wũ loawe i ma ame.”
Mamɔɛ̃ Yesu.
Gɔ Yesu ɔkparama kayi ɔro ne, ɔruigu ɔ̃ marasuãdze mawara Kidron Kaworenya makɛlɛ nnɔĩ adziri kakpɛkɔ̃ kawɛ̃ ame.
Yuda gɔ loɖi Yesu ɔtã ana ɣe mmɔ, alasɔ ɔwi gbodzoo ame ne, Yesu sɛ ɔkɔ ɔ̃ marasuãdze masɛ maasarɛ i mmɔ.
Ne ɔso Yuda ɔkɔ makpakpɛ̃dze ikuri iwɛ̃ gu kasɔrɛkɔ̃ madzuɛ̃se ma i masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu ma Farisise ɔsese kakpɛkɔ̃ gamɔ ame.
Mato akpira, kaka sitɔ gu sikaniɛ.
Yesu ɣe ira biara nɛ loabɔrɛ wũ iso, ne ɔso ɔbɔrɛ ɔya i katɔ̃ ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Nna mito mibie?” Matã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Yesu Nasaretse boto bobie.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mme nɖe wũ.” Yuda gɔ loɖi wũ ɔtã ana ɣɛ i ma kɔrɛ mmɔ.
Gɔ Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mme nɖe wũ” ne, masɛ simasima mabɔrɛ marɔ̃.
Ɔledza ma ikarɛ sɔ, “Nna mito mibie?” Maledza wũ mmuai itã sɔ, “Yesu Nasaretse.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Loɔɣere mi koko sɔ mme nɖe wũ ne, ne ɔso si mme mito mibie ne, miɖi mmagbe ɔri si makɛlɛ.” Ɔɣɛ nnɛgbe si itɔ̃me nɛ ɔ̃ɔɣere ma ɔɖegu katɔ̃ aaba i ne ame sɔ, “Tete, mma asu atã me ne, loiyura ma kuwɛ̃.” Ne Simon Petro gɔ nto ipɛmi ɔɖi ne i ɔyuɛ ame ɔwe sɔrɛdzekpakpa pelepele ɔɖabo kuɖearɔ̃ kutsue ɔtara.
Ɔɖabo gɔmɔ marɔ sɔ Malkos ne.
Ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔɣere Petro sɔ, “Kpesera fɔ ipɛmi pia i ne kawekɔ̃.
Iikote sɔ loanɛ inyɛwe ikɔi nɛ i Tete ɔtã me?” Makɔ Yesu Makɛlɛgu Hana Katɔ̃.
Ne kama ne, Roma makpakpɛ̃dze gu ma ɔkpakpa gu ma Yudase madzuɛ̃se ɔmɔɛ̃ Yesu, manyi wũ.
Makɔ wũ makɛlɛgu Hana kɔrɛ.
Hana gɔgbe nɖe mase ɔtã Kayafa gɔ nɖe sɔrɛdzekpakpa pelepele ku ikɔ nɛmɔ ne.
Kayafa gɔgbe ame ɔɖe lotã ma Yudase adzuni sɔ ilɛ iɖo sɔ ɔturi ɔwɛ̃ aakpi i kaɖe ɔɖuɖu iti ne.
Petro Ɔsɛ̃ Sɔ Ɔ̃iɣe Yesu.
Simon Petro gu rasuãdze ɔwɛ̃ ɔsiai Yesu i kama.
Gɔ makɛlɛ sɔrɛdzekpakpa pelepele iyo ne, rasuãdze gɔmɔ ɔ̃ ɔbo i iyo ame, alasɔ ma gu Sɔrɛdzekpakpa ɣe so kukaakɔ.
Ɣɛɛ Petro ɣɛ i inyamɔ.
Rasuãdze gɔmɔ ɔkpese ɔkɛlɛ kayogodɔ̃ ɔsɛ ɔ̃aɖegu ɔbirɔ̃gomi gɔ nto ɔdzuɛ̃ mmɔ ika fiɛ ɔtã wũ ɔri ɔkɔ Petro ɔbogu i iyo.
Ɔbirɔ̃gomi gɔ nɣɛ i kayogodɔ̃ mmɔ ɔkarɛ Petro sɔ, “Fɔ wũ iiɖe ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe rasuãdze ɔwɛ̃ aɖe, ɣɛɛ?” Ne Petro sɔ, “Ooɣo lo, loiɖe ma ɔwɛ̃!” Ɔyu pia, ne ɔso maɖabo gu madzuɛ̃se ɔpia ɔtɔ maɣɛ maki malɔ mato mawa.
Ne ɔso Petro ɣɛ i ma kɔrɛ ɔto ɔwa ɔtɔ.
Sɔrɛdzekpakpa Pelepele Ɔkarɛ Yesu Atɔ̃me.
Sɔrɛdzekpakpa pelepele ɔkarɛ Yesu atɔ̃me ɔsegu i ɔ̃ marasuãdze gu ɔ̃ ara wa ɔto ɔte iso.
Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ɔwi biara lopia loto lote maturi ara i ɔgbami, fiɛ wũ ara ite ɔɖuɖu ana ne, lote wã i kasarɛkɔ̃ gu Isɔrɛyo ame ngbegɔ i ma Yudase ɔɖuɖu ɔsakanya, ne ɔso loite kuira i iwɛrɛ ame.
Be ɔso mme ato akarɛ atɔ̃me?
Karɛ mma lonɔ wũ ara wa lote ma.
Maɣe nnɛ loɣɛ.” Gɔ Yesu ɔɣɛ ngbɔ ne, dzuɛ̃se ɔwɛ̃ gɔ nɣɛ i mmɔ ɔpɛ wũ ɔrɔ̃ta i kutsueti ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Sɔrɛdzekpakpa pelepele ato aɖegu ika ngbɔ?” Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Si loɣɛ nnɛ loilɛ ne, ɣere ɔbiara i ngbe nnɛ loɣɛ fiɛ iilɛ, ɣɛɛ si loiɣɛ kuira nyanyarĩa ne, be ɔso ato apɛ me ɔrɔ̃ta?” Ne ɔso Hana ɔkpesegu Yesu gɔ manyi nrɔɔ̃ ɔsese Kayafa gɔ nɖe sɔrɛdzekpakpa pelepele kɔrɛ.
Gɔ Simon Petro ɣɛ ɔtogu ɔtɔ iwa ne, mma nɣɛ i mmɔ ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Fɔ wũ ne, iiɖe ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe rasuãdze ɔwɛ̃ aɖe, ɣɛɛ?” Ɣɛɛ Petro ɔsɛ̃, ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Loiɖe ma ɔwɛ̃!” Sɔrɛdzekpakpa pelepele maɖabo ɔwɛ̃ gɔ i Petro ɔtu kutsue ɔnyii ana ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Nnisɔ lonya-ɔ fɔ wũ i kakpɛkɔ̃ ame ku ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe?” Ngbe ana ne, Petro ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Ooɣo!” Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, kɔkɔ ɔbo.
Makɔ Yesu Makɛlɛgu Pilato Kɔrɛ.
Kaya tutuutu ne, makɔ Yesu mabɔrɛgu i Kayafa iyo makɛlɛgu abã ɔkpakpa iyo.
Gɔ ma Yudase makpakpa ɔɔsekelera so sɔ maawo Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo Iyi aɖera ɔɖe ɔso ne, maibo i iyo ame.
Ne ɔso Pilato ɔbɔrɛ ɔkɛlɛ ma kɔrɛ i inyamɔ ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Mme ikpi i ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ɔbara?” Matã mmuai sɔ, “Si ɔ̃ibara ikpi kuiwɛ̃ ne, boibakɔ wũ bobɔ-ɔ.” Ne Pilato to ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Iyɔ mi mɔmɔ mikɔ wũ mikɛlɛgu miaɣɛgu wũ atɔ̃me i mi mmara kanya.” Matã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Maitã bo ɔri sɔ boatã ɔturi kukpi ipɔ.” Nnɛgbe ɔba ngbɔ sɔ nnɛ i Yesu mɔmɔ ɔɣɛ ɔsu ɔte kukpi gɔ igbã ɔ̃akpi ɔba i ne ame.
Pilato ɔkpese ɔbo i atɔ̃mekaɣɛkɔ̃ ɔkarɛ Yesu sɔ, “Fɔ nɖe ma Yudase igara?” Ne Yesu ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Fɔ mɔmɔ kɔrɛ i itɔ̃me nɛgbe ɔbɔrɛ ɛɛbɛrɛ manyiiɔ loɖe-ɔ wũ iso ika?” Pilato ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Ɔ Yudase loɖe?
Fɔ mɔmɔ maturi gu masɔrɛdze makpakpa lokɔ-ɔ mabɔ me.
Be iɖe abara?” Ne Yesu ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Wũ sigarakaɖekɔ̃ iibɔrɛ i kayi gagbe iso, si ngbe sibɔrɛ ne, tee wũ makpabo aakpɛ̃ mafɔ me mabɔrɛgu i ma Yudase nrɔɔ̃ ame, ɣɛɛ ne, wũ sigarakaɖekɔ̃ iibɔrɛ i ngbe!” Pilato ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ne iyɔ igara aɖe?” Ne Yesu ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Fɔ nto aɣɛ sɔ igara loɖe.
Ira ka iwɛ̃ nɛgbe ɔso fiɛ maɣe me mapia i kayi gagbe ame ne, sɔ loaɣɛ ɔnukuare.
Ɔbiara gɔ nɖe ɔnukuare ɔre sɛ ɔkã me atsue.” Ne Pilato ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Be nɖe ɔnukuare?” Ne Pilato ɔbɔrɛ ɔkɛlɛ ma Yudase kɔrɛ i inyamɔ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Loinya ikpi kuiwɛ̃ nɛ iso loaya fiɛ loatã wũ kukpi ipɔ lo.
Ɣɛɛ i mi kubarara kanya ne, nsɛ loɖi yorɛdze ɔwɛ̃ lotã mi ku Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo Iyi ɔɖewi biara.
Ne ɔso lonyua ma Yudase Igara lotã mi?” Mala kulu matã mmuai sɔ, “Ooɣo, boibie wũ!
Bobie Baraba!” Baraba gɔgbe ne, ɔturi gɔ lota ɔya abã iso ɔɖe.
Matã Yesu Kukpi Ipɔ.
Ne ɔso Pilato ɔtã makpakpɛ̃dze ɔkɔ Yesu maruigu masɛ maapɛ wũ nyanyarĩ ku ala iporoibi.
Masu miyu mabara ala sigaraikoto masu matɔ̃medza wũ fiɛ ka masu ɔgo rɛtɛa ɔkati mafu wũ lɛ igara.
Mabore mabo wũ mafa kayiɖu sɔ, “Ɣii-ɣiiɖuu!
Ma Yudase Igara o-o!” Maɣɛ ngbɔ ne mapɛ wũ sirɔ̃ta.
Pilato ɔledza ibɔrɛ ikɛlɛ isɛ iaɣere ma Yudase sɔ, “Minyɔ, loto lokɔ wũ lobɔ mi si minya sɔ loinyagu wũ ku ikpi nɛ ɔso loatã wũ kukpi ipɔ.” Ne ɔso Yesu ɔbɔrɛ ɔba ɔtɔ̃me miyu ikoto fiɛ ka ɔpia ɔgo awu rɛtɛa tagbaraa.
Ne Pilato ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Minyɔ wũ!
Ɔturi i ngbe ne!” Gɔ masɔrɛdze makpakpa gu Isɔrɛyo madzuɛ̃se ɔnya wũ ne, mala kulu sɔ, “Pɛ wũ matãra i kudziri iso!
Pɛ wũ matãra i kudziri iso!” Ne Pilato ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mikɔ wũ mikɛlɛgu miapɛ wũ mimatãra i kudziri iso, ɣɛɛ mme ne, loinya ikpi kuiwɛ̃ nɛ ɔso loatã wũ kukpi ipɔ.” Ne maturi to mala kulu maɣɛ sɔ, “Boba mmara mɛ loɣɛ sɔ ikote sɔ ɔ̃akpi, alasɔ ɔto ɔkpere so sɔ Ɣaa Ɔbi ɔɖe.” Gɔ Pilato ɔnɔ nnɛgbe ne, ifɔ̃ ɔmɔɛ̃ wũ ibua.
Ne ɔkpese ɔkɛlɛ iyo ame fiɛ ɔkarɛ Yesu sɔ, “I lɛ abɔrɛ?” Ɣɛɛ Yesu iitã wũ mmuai.
Pilato ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Be, aito apia me kanya?
Tsue sɔ loba ɔle gɔ loawo-ɔ ɔnyua ɣee lotã mapɛ-ɔ mamatãra i kudziri iso!” Mmɔ i Yesu ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Ɔle gɔ kɔra aba i wũ iso ne, Ɣaa pɛ lotã-ɔ ɔso.
Ne ɔso ngɔ loɖi me ɔtã-ɔ ɔbara ikpi siare ɔɖo-ɔ.” Nnɛgbe ɔso ne, Pilato ɔbie sɔ si ɔnyua wũ, ɣɛɛ ma Yudase ɔla kulu teteree sɔ, “Si anyua ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ne, iyɔ aiɖe Roma Igarakpakpa ɔlaa.
Ɔbiara gɔ losɛra so sigara ne, ɔta ɔya i Igarakpakpa iso!” Gɔ Pilato ɔnɔ atɔ̃me wagbe ne, ɔkɔ Yesu ɔkɛlɛgu inyamɔ.
Ɔsɛ ɔ̃asɛ i iyara nɛ iso masɛ masɛ maɣɛ atɔ̃me fiɛ masɛ marɔ ne sɔ Itabɛbɛa iso.
I ma Yudase siɖe ame ne, masɛ marɔ mmɔ sɔ Gabata.
Iyi nɛmɔ nɖe Iledzaso itã Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo Iyi iɖe ne.
Ne Pilato ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Nya mi Igara ngbe!” Ne mala kulu teteree sɔ, “Kɔ wũ ruigu!
Kɔ wũ ruigu!
Pɛ wũ matãra i kudziri iso!” Ne Pilato ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Lopɛ mi Igara lomatãra i kudziri iso?” Ne masɔrɛdze makpakpa ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Bona igara kuwɛ̃ iɖo Roma Igarakpakpa Kaisaro!” Gɔ maɣɛ ngbɔ ne, Pilato ɔtara Yesu ɔpia ma i nrɔɔ̃ ame sɔ masɛ maapɛ wũ mamatãra i kudziri iso.
Mapɛ Yesu Mamatãra Kudziri Iso.
Ne ɔso makpakpɛ̃dze ɔkɔ Yesu maruigu.
Gɔ matã wũ ɔsore ɔdziri ne, makɔ wũ makɛlɛgu ngbegɔ marɔ Itikui Kabemi.
Fiɛ si Hebrise ame ne, masɛ marɔ mmɔ sɔ Golgata.
Mapɛ wũ mamatãra i kudziri iso i ngbe.
Mapɛ maturi inyɔ mawɛ̃ ana mamatãra i ma adziri iso mabua wũ iso.
Ɔwɛ̃ i kuɖearɔ̃ iso, ɔwɛ̃ ana i kubena iso fiɛ Yesu ka ɔpia ma i ndɛ̃.
Pilato ɔtã matsɛrɛ mamatãra i Yesu sitikpe sɔ, “Yesu Nasaretse, Ma Yudase Igara.” Ma Yudase gbodzoo ɔka ira nɛ matsɛrɛ masia i kudziri iso alasɔ ngbegɔ mapɛ Yesu mamatãra i kudziri iso ɔbore imatã Yerusalem.
Ana ne, matsɛrɛ i si Hebrise gu si Romase gu si Helase ame.
Masɔrɛdzekpakpa iitɔrã, maɣere Pilato sɔ, “Daatsɛrɛ sɔ ‘Ma Yudase Igara,’ ɣɛɛ tsɛrɛ sɔ, ‘Ngɔgbe nto ɔɣɛ sɔ ɔ̃ nɖe ma Yudase Igara ne.’ ” Ɣɛɛ Pilato ɔsɛ̃, ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Nnɛ loɔtsɛrɛ ne, loɔtsɛrɛ koko.” Gɔ makpakpɛ̃dze ɔpɛ Yesu mamatãra i kudziri iso maro ne, maɣɛ ɔ̃ arapia aka ana, kpakpɛ̃dze biara ɔfɔ ika iwɛ̃.
Awu awɛ̃ ɔkuti wa iiɖe ɔkã makã ɣɛɛ ɔwe mawe wã ita i kato isɛ iabɔrɛ i kala.
Makpakpɛ̃dze ɔɣere so sɔ, “Midaatã bokɛ wã, ɣɛɛ mitã bobara kareremi si bonyɔ sɔ nna aaɣo.” Iba ngbɔ sɔ nnɛ matsɛrɛ mapia i Ɔko Sekelea ame aaba i ne ame sɔ, “Masu wũ arapia maɣɛ so.
Fiɛ mabara kareremi i wũ awu iso.” Ne ɔso ngbɔ tutuutu i makpakpɛ̃dze ɔbara ne.
Kudziri gɔ iso mapɛ Yesu mamatãra kɔrɛ ne, marɔ̃go mawɛ̃ ɣɛ.
Ma nɖe Yesu ɔnyi gu ɔ̃ ɔnyiibi gu Klopa ɔre Maria gu Maria Magdalase.
Gɔ Yesu ɔnya ɔ̃ ɔnyi gu ɔ̃ rasuãdze gɔ ɔ̃isɛ ɔpia kuɣɛ ɣɛ mabore mamatã wũ ne, ɔɣere ɔ̃ ɔnyi sɔ, “Mmã, nya fɔ ɔbi!” Ne ɔɣere rasuãdze gɔmɔ ana sɔ, “Fɔ wũ, nya fɔ ɔnyi.” Ne ɔso ita i iyi nɛmɔ ne, rasuãdze gɔgbe ɔkɔ Yesu ɔnyi ɔkɛlɛgu ɔ̃ iyo ɔnyɔ wũ iso.
Yesu Ɔkpi.
Yesu ɣe sɔ ira biara ɔɔba kawirikɔ̃, ɣɛɛ si nnɛ matsɛrɛ masɛ aaba i ne ame ne, ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Ɔme to ɔkore me.” Ituɖura iwɛ̃ se i mmɔ iyi ku ndã bea.
Ne ɔso masu ɖɔti pukupukua mapia i me ame maɖu i ɔdziri iso masɔ̃ Yesu i kanya.
Gɔ ɔfɔ ndã bea mɛmɔ ɔro ne, ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Iɔro kini!” Gɔ ɔɣɛ ngbɔ ne, ɔbɔ iti karɔ̃ kere ne ɔsora ne.
Makpakpɛ̃dze Ɔtsue Yesu Ira I Iwãgɛsɛ.
Iledzaso itã Iwarãyi iyi iso iɖe i ara wagbe ɔba, fiɛ kaɖesɛ̃a ɖe Iwarãyi sekelea itã ma Yudase, ne ɔso maibie sɔ makpise si mamatã i adziri iso ku Iwarãyi.
Ne ɔso masɛ maaɣere Pilato sɔ ɔtã ɔri si masɛ maafɛfɛ̃ ma ngba si mabɛse ma i adziri iso.
Ne ɔso makpakpɛ̃dze ɔba maturi inyɔ ma mapɛ mamatãra i adziri iso ku Yesu kɔrɛ.
Mafɛ̃ ɔɖeakatɔ̃ gu ɔnyɔare ngba.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ mabo Yesu iso ne, manya sɔ ɔ̃ɔkpi koko ne ɔso maisifɛ̃ ɔ̃ ngba.
Ɣɛɛ kpakpɛ̃dze ɔwɛ̃ ɔsu ɔ̃ ifele ɔtsue Yesu iwãgɛsɛ fiɛ ndu gu ima ɔbɔrɛ.
Ngɔ lonya sɔ ara wagbe ɔba ɔɖe loɖe wã aɖansiɛ sɔ si fɔ wũ aafɔ aɖe.
Ara wa ɔɣɛ ne, gbaã iɖe fiɛ ɔɣe sɔ ɔnukuare iɖe ɔɣɛ.
Iba ngbɔ sɔ nnɛ matsɛrɛ masɛ i Ɔko Sekelea ame aaba i ne ame sɔ, “Maibafɛ̃ ɔ̃ ikui kuiwɛ̃.” Matsɛrɛ masɛ i kakɔi mama ana sɔ, “Mato maanyɔ ngɔ matsue ira.” Mabiara Yesu.
Nnɛgbe kama ne, Yosef gɔ lose i Arimatea ɔba ɔ̃akarɛ Pilato sɔ ɔsu Yesu kpise ɔtã wũ.
Ɔɖe Yesu rasuãdze ɣɛɛ i iwɛrɛ ame alasɔ ɔto ɔnigã ma Yudase makpakpa ɔso ne.
Pilato ɔɖi wũ ɔri, ne ɔso ɔsu kpise ɔruigu.
Nikodemo gɔ loba Yesu kɔrɛ ku kasɛ̃ ɔnya ana ɔba.
Ɔsu awa wa masu korobo gu awa kɔrɔ̃kɔrɔ̃a mabara ala fiɛ masɛ masu maledza ala makpise fiɛ wã ɔrɔrã aaɖe lɛ ito iwɛ̃ ɔbɔ.
Marɛrɛ̃ inyɔ magbe ɔsu awa mapia i ɔkati ame mamini kpise, kumɛgɔ i ma Yudase sɛ mabara fiɛ masɛ mabiara ɔturi.
I ngbegɔ mapɛ Yesu mamatãra i kudziri iso ne, kakpɛkɔ̃ kawɛ̃ pia i mmɔ.
Ikpibiɔ ɣɛtɛ nɛ ame maibiara ɔturi manya ana se i kã ame.
Gɔ kaɖesɛ̃a to iaɖe Iwarãyi fiɛ ikpibiɔ nɛmɔ ɔɔbore imatã mmɔ ɔso ne, masu Yesu mabiara i mmɔ.
Yesu Ɔta Ɔbɔrɛ I Makpise Ame.
Kɔsiɖa kaya tutuutu gɔ kayi iikpa karo ne, Maria Magdalase ɔkɛlɛ ikpibiɔ kɔrɛ fiɛ ɔnya sɔ maɔli ita nɛ mali matɛ̃ ikpibiɔ kanya maɖi.
Ɔtere ɔkɛlɛ Simon Petro gu rasuãdze gɔ i Yesu iisɛ ɔpia kuɣɛ kɔrɛ ɔsɛ ɔ̃aɣere ma sɔ, “Maɔmɔɛ̃ Bosate maɖi i ikpibiɔ ame fiɛ boiɣe ngbegɔ masu wũ masɛ!” Petro gu rasuãdze gɔmɔ ɔta sɔ makɛlɛ ikpibiɔ kɔrɛ.
Ma inyɔɔ ɔtere ise, ɣɛɛ rasuãdze gɔmɔ ɔtere ɔɖe Petro katɔ̃ ɔbo ikpibiɔ kɔrɛ.
Ɔbɔ iti karɔ̃ ɔnya sikati fudza dzɛmɔ, ɣɛɛ ɔ̃ibo i ikpibiɔ ame.
Gɔ Simon Petro ɔtere ɔba ɔ̃abo ne, ɔfe ɔbo i iwo ame, ɔnya sikati fudza dzɛmɔ gɔ sise.
Ɔnya ɔkati gɔ masu manyi Yesu iti ana.
Ɔ̃isakanyagu ɔkati gɔ masu mamini Yesu kɔrɛ, ɣɛɛ makarĩ masɛ i kuruɛ.
Mmɔ i rasuãdze nyɔare gɔ loɖe katɔ̃ ɔ̃ wũ ɔbo i ikpibiɔ ame.
Ɔnya ara wagbe fiɛ ka ɔfɔ ɔɖe.
Ɣɛɛ ta kiniɔ ne, mainɔ karɔ̃ nnɛ i Ɔko Sekelea ɔɣɛ sɔ Yesu aata ɔbɔrɛ i makpise ame.
Yesu Ɔɖi So Ɔte Maria Magdalase.
Ne marasuãdze ɔkpese makɛlɛ iyo ne.
Ɣɛɛ Maria Magdalase ɔba ɔɣɛ i ikpibiɔ kɔrɛ ɔto ɔbiɛ.
Gɔ ɔtogu kaku ibiɛ ne, ɔbɔ iti karɔ̃ ɔnyɔ ikpibiɔ ame ne, ɔnya Ɣaa makpabo inyɔ ma mpia ara fudza gɔ masi i ngbegɔ marara Yesu.
Ɔwɛ̃ si i sitikpe fiɛ ɔwɛ̃ ana si i ngbalɔ.
Ne makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ɔrɔ̃go, be ɔso ato abiɛ?” Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Manyiiɔ ɔsu wũ ɔkɔse maruigu fiɛ loiɣe ngbegɔ masu wũ masɛ.” Gɔ ɔpɛ ɔfiniki ne, ɔnya Yesu ɣɛ wũ i kɔrɛ, ɣɛɛ ɔ̃iɣe sɔ Yesu ɔɖe.
Ne Yesu ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ɔrɔ̃go, be ɔso ato abiɛ?
Nna ato abie?” Ɣɛɛ Maria ɔbu sɔ ngɔ nto ɔnyɔ mmɔ iso ɔɖe, ne ɔso ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Bokɔse, loto-ɔ i kukpa, si fɔ losu wũ asɛ i kakɔi karere ne, te me ngbegɔ asɛ wũ si losɛ loasu wũ.” Mmɔ i Yesu ɔkpere wũ sɔ, “Maria!” Gɔ Maria ɔfiniki ɔnyɔ wũ ne, ɔla kulu i si Hebrise ame sɔ, “Rabuni!” gɔ ne karɔ̃ nɖe sɔ Ratedze.
Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Daasimɔɛ̃ me, alasɔ loikɛlɛ Tete kɔrɛ i kato.
Ɣɛɛ ne, kɛlɛ wũ manyiibi kɔrɛ si asɛ aaɣere ma sɔ, loto lokpese lokɛlɛ wũ Ɣaa gɔ nɖe ma Ɣaa gu wũ Ɔse gɔ nɖe ma Ɔse kɔrɛ.” Ne ɔso Maria Magdalase ɔsɛ ɔ̃aɣere marasuãdze sɔ ɔnya Bosate fiɛ ka ɔɣere ma ara wa i Yesu ɔɣere wũ.
Yesu Ɔɖi So Ɔte Ɔ̃ Marasuãdze.
Kɔsiɖa gɔmɔ kutsuɛ ne, marasuãdze ɔsakanya.
Masɛ̃ iyo mapia so ala mato manigã ma Yudase makpakpa.
Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, Yesu ɔba ɔ̃aya i ma ndɛ̃ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Isobuɛ itã mi.” Gɔ ɔɣere ma ngbɔ ɔro ne, ɔsu ɔ̃ nrɔɔ̃ gu iwãgɛsɛ ɔte ma.
So ɔɣɔ marasuãdze gbaã alasɔ manya Bosate.
Ne Yesu ɔledza ma iɣere sɔ, “Isobuɛ itã mi, kumɛgɔ ame i Tete ɔpia me katɔ̃me ne, ngbɔ ame loto lopia mi ne.” Ne ɔwarã ɔfere ma iso ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mifɔ Siwarã Bielea.
Si misu maturi akpi mitsɛ ma ne, Ɣaa to ɔ̃asu ɔtsɛ ma, ɣɛɛ si miisu mitsɛ ma ne, Ɣaa iibasu ɔtsɛ ma.” Yesu Ɔɖi So Ɔte Toma.
Ɔwi gɔ i Yesu ɔba ma kɔrɛ ne, marasuãdze iweo-inyɔ ndɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ nɖe Toma fiɛ masɛ marɔ sɔ Inyɔɔbi na i ma ndɛ̃.
Ne ɔso marasuãdze tsɔra ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Bonya Bosate!” Ne Toma ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ lonya aɣɛipã wa i ɔ̃ nrɔɔ̃, losu wũ kɔrɔ̃ lopia i apã wamɔ ame gu ɔ̃ iwãgɛsɛ ame ne, loibafɔ loɖe lonya.” Ɖapɛ ɔwɛ̃ kama ne, marasuãdze pia i iyo fiɛ Toma ana ɔwe i ma ndɛ̃.
Masɛ̃ akui mapia so ɣɛɛ Yesu ɔba ɔ̃aya i ma ndɛ̃.
Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Isobuɛ itã mi.” Ne ɔɣere Toma sɔ, “Ba su fɔ irɔĩ pia i ngbe.
Nyɔ wũ nrɔɔ̃ si asu fɔ kɔrɔ̃ apia i wũ iwãgɛsɛ ame.
Nyua ɔwararã si afɔ aɖe!” Ne Toma ɔɖi kanya sɔ, “Wũ Sate gu wũ Ɣaa!” Ne Yesu ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ɔɔfɔ aɖe alasɔ ɔɔnya me?
So aaɣɔ mma loisɛ manya fiɛ masɛ mafɔ me maɖe!” Nnɛ Ɔso Matsɛrɛ Ɔko Gɔgbe.
Yesu ɔbara awawãra gbodzoo i ɔ̃ marasuãdze kɔrɛ wa maitsɛrɛ mapia i ɔko gɔgbe ame.
Ɣɛɛ matsɛrɛ nwagbe masɛ sɔ si aafɔ aɖe sɔ Yesu nɖe Kristo gu Ɣaa Ɔbi, fiɛ iki i ɔ̃ ifɔ iɖe ame ne, aana ngbã.
Marasuãdze Ɔnya Yesu I Ɔpo Katɔ̃.
Nwagbe kama ne, Yesu ɔledza so iɖi ite ɔ̃ marasuãdze i Tiberia Ɔpo kanya.
Kumɛgɔ ɔɖi so ɔte ma i ngbe ne.
Iyi iwɛ̃ ne, Yesu marasuãdze mawɛ̃ ɔsikanya.
Ma nɖe Simon Petro gu Toma gɔ masɛ marɔ sɔ Inyɔɔbi gu Nataniel gɔ lobɔrɛ i Kana i Galilea karɔ̃ iso gu Zebedeo mabi gu marasuãdze inyɔ mama.
Ne Simon Petro ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Losɛ akpɛ kaɖikɔ̃.” Ne matsɔra ana ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Bo wũ boaba bokɛlɛ.” Ne ɔso ma ɔɖuɖu ɔbo i ɔkolo ame makɛlɛ, ɣɛɛ kasɛ̃ ɔɖuɖu ne, maiɖi ikpɛ kuiwɛ̃.
Kaya gɔ kuɣɛ̃ ɔsɔ̃ kuto kuba ne, Yesu ɔba ɔ̃ɔya i ɔpo kanya, ɣɛɛ marasuãdze iiɣe sɔ ɔ̃ ɔɖe.
Ne ɔkpere ma ɔkarɛ sɔ, “Maporoporoi, miɔɖi akpɛ awɛ̃?” Matã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Ooɣo!” Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mipia mi asabu i mi ɔkolo kuɖearɔ̃ iso ne mito miaɖi akpɛ.” Gɔ mapia asabu ne, maiwo ɔkpadzɛ̃ ala akpɛ gbodzoo wa mamɔɛ̃ ɔso.
Rasuãdze gɔ i Yesu iisɛ ɔpia kuɣɛ ɔɣere Petro sɔ, “Bosate ɔɖe lo!” Gɔ Petro ɔnɔ sɔ Bosate ɔɖe ne, ɔsu ɔ̃ kato awu ɔkpasa alasɔ ɔɖi wã ɔsɛ.
Ɔkɔlɛ ɔbo i ndu ame ɔɣa ndu ɔkɛlɛ ɔkpokpo.
Marasuãdze tsɔra ɔsɛ ɔkolo ame maba mato makpadzɛ̃ asabu wa loyi ku akpɛ.
Ma gu ɔkpokpo ndɛ̃ aaɖe lɛ nrɔɔ̃ siru kere.
Gɔ maso i ɔkpokpo ne, manya sɔ mapia ɔtɔ i mmɔ ikpɛ sia iso, abolo ana se i mmɔ.
Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Miɖi akpɛ wa mimɔɛ̃ awɛ̃ mibɔ.” Ne Simon Petro ɔya ɔbo i ɔkolo ame ɔkpadzɛ̃ asabu wa loyigu akpɛ siare ɔbɔ ɔkpokpo ne.
Akpɛ ɔɖuɖu ɖe kulafa gu siru-atɛ, ɣɛɛ atoa sɔ asi ngbɔ ne, asabu iikɛkɛ.
Ne kama ne, Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Miba miaɖe ara.” Ɣɛɛ ma kuwɛ̃ iiwe ɔtu ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Fɔ nɖe nna?” alasɔ maɣe sɔ Bosate ɔɖe.
Ne Yesu ɔbore ɔbo ɔsu abolo ɔtã ma, ne kama ne, ɔsu ikpɛ ana ɔtã ma.
Nnɛgbe nɖe ɔkpɛ tɛare gɔ i Yesu ɔɖi so ɔte ɔ̃ marasuãdze gɔ ɔta ɔbɔrɛ i makpise ame ne.
Gɔ maɖe ara maro ne, Yesu ɔkarɛ Simon Petro sɔ, “Simon, Yohanes ɔbi, ato aɖɔɛ me aɖo matsɔra magbe?” Ne Petro ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Aĩ, Bosate, fɔ mɔmɔ aɣe sɔ loto loɖɔɛ-ɔ.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Nyɔ wũ asɛrɛbi iso.” Ɔkpɛ nyɔare ne, Yesu ɔledza wũ ikarɛ sɔ, “Simon, Yona ɔbi, ato aɖɔɛ me?” Ne Petro ɔledza iɣɛ sɔ, “Aĩ, Bosate, fɔ mɔmɔ aɣe sɔ loto loɖɔɛ-ɔ.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Nyɔ wũ masɛrɛ iso.” Ɔkpɛ tɛare ne, Yesu ɔledza Petro ikarɛ sɔ, “Simon, Yona ɔbi, ato aɖɔɛ me?” Iɖaa Petro, alasɔ Yesu ɔledza wũ ikarɛ ɔkpɛ tɛare sɔ ato aɖɔɛ me, ne ɔso ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Bosate!
Fɔ mɔmɔ aɣe ira biara, fiɛ aɣe sɔ loto loɖɔɛ-ɔ.” Ne Yesu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Nyɔ wũ masɛrɛ iso.
Gbaã loto loɣere-ɔ sɔ ɔwi gɔ aɖe ɔporoporoi ne, asɛ aledza so abɔrɛ asɛ ngbegɔ aɖɔɛ, ɣɛɛ si ɔɔbe ne, ato atara fɔ nrɔɔ̃ kato, ɔturi mama ɔnyi-ɔ ɔkati, ɔkɔ-ɔ ɔkɛlɛgu ngbegɔ aito abie sɔ aasɛ.” Yesu ɔɣɛ nnɛgbe si ɔsu ɔte kukpi gɔ igbã i Petro aakpi ɔsu ɔkɔlɛ Ɣaa iyere kato.
Gɔ ɔɣɛ ngbɔ ɔro ne, ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Siai me.” Ne gɔ Petro ɔfiniki ne, ɔnya rasuãdze gɔ i Yesu iisɛ ɔpia kuɣɛ sɔ ɔɣɛ i mmɔ.
Rasuãdze gɔgbe ɔɖe lopiɛtɛ i Yesu iso ku ɔwi gɔ mato maɖe kutsuɛ aɖera ɔkarɛ Yesu sɔ, “Bosate, nna loaɖi-ɔ ɔtã ne.” Ne ɔso gɔ Petro ɔnya wũ ne, ɔkarɛ Yesu sɔ, “Bosate, ne ngɔgbe ɔ̃ ne, nda iase wũ?” Ne Yesu ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Si mme sɔ ɔsɛ gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ loakpese loba ne, be isu-ɔ i mmɔ?
Fɔ ne, siai me.” Nnɛgbe ɔso ne, iki ikã i marasuãdze ndɛ̃ sɔ rasuãdze gɔmɔ iibakpi.
Ɣɛɛ Yesu iiɣɛ sɔ ɔ̃ibakpi, ɔɣɛ ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Si mme sɔ ɔsɛ gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ loakpese loba ne, be isu-ɔ i mmɔ?” Rasuãdze gɔgbe ɔɖe loɣɛ ara wagbe fiɛ ɔtsɛrɛ wã ɔsɛ fiɛ boɣe sɔ nnɛ ɔɣɛ ne, gbaã iɖe ne.
Yesu ɔbara ara gbodzoo gɔ si sɔ matsɛrɛ wã ɔɖuɖu masɛ iwɛ̃ iwɛ̃ ne, lofɔ loɖe sɔ kayiiso ɔɖuɖu iibana siko dzɛmɔ karɔ̃kasɛkɔ̃.
Wũ ɔnyii Tiofilo, i wũ ɔko ɖeakatɔ̃ ame ne, lotsɛrɛ loɣere-ɔ ara wa ɔɖuɖu i Yesu ɔbara gu nwa ɔte, ita i ɔwi gɔ ɔsɛ ɔ̃ karabara karɔ̃ isɛ iabo ɔwi gɔ i Ɣaa ɔsu wũ ɔkɛlɛgu kato.
Si ɔ̃akɛlɛ kato ne, Yesu ɔki i Siwarã Bielea ɔle iso ɔte katɔ̃memasɛdze ma ɔɖi ɔtã so ara.
I ɔ̃ kukpi kama ne, ɔɖi so ɔte ma i siri agbãagbã iso i ayi sina ame sɔ gbaã ne, ɔpia ngbã.
Ɔɖe mma lonya wũ ika i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ iso.
Ɔwi ɔwɛ̃ gɔ masakanya ne, ɔsɛ̃ ɔtã ma sɔ, “Midaarui i Yerusalem.
Ɣɛɛ miwe misia Siwarã Bielea dzɛ loɣere mi sɔ wũ Ɔse ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ sɔ ɔ̃atã mi.
Yohanes ne, ndu miɖe ɔsu ɔbara Ɣaa itupie kubarara ɔtã maturi.
Ɣɛɛ ayi kɛkɛĩ ame ne, Ɣaa to ɔ̃asu Siwarã Bielea ɔpie mi.” Ɣaa Ɔsu Yesu Ɔkɛlɛgu Kato.
Gɔ katɔ̃memasɛdze gu Yesu ɔledza isarɛ ne, makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Bosate, kiniɔkiniɔ ato abie sɔ aaledza Israel sigarakaɖekɔ̃ itara?” Ne Yesu ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Iinya sɔ miatsue ɔwi ɣee ayi wa i Tete ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ i ɔ̃ ɔle ame sɔ nnɛmɔ aaba.
Ɣɛɛ ne, mito miafɔ ɔle ɔwi gɔ i Siwarã Bielea ɔɔba mi iso, miaɣɛ wũ itɔ̃me ita i Yerusalem gu Yudea ɔɖuɖu gu Samaria isɛ iabo kayiiso katsɔrakɔ̃.” Gɔ ɔɣere ma ara wagbe ɔro ne, Ɣaa ɔsu wũ ɔkɛlɛgu kato gɔ maɣɛ mato manyɔ wũ gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ ɔbo i idɔdɔ ame fiɛ ɔyu ma i anɔ.
Gɔ maɣɛ mato manyɔ ɔ̃ kuɖokpo ikɛlɛ ne, ɔluwɛ̃ marɛrɛ̃ inyɔ mawɛ̃ ma mpia ara fudza ɔɖi so mate ma, ne maɣere ma sɔ, “Galilea marɛrɛ̃, be ɔso fiɛ miɣɛ minyɔ kato ngbɔ?
Yesu gɔ i Ɣaa ɔfɔ ɔbɔrɛgu i mi kɔrɛ fiɛ ɔkɛlɛ kato ne, ɔto ɔ̃aledza ikpese iba lɛ kumɛgɔ minya wũ ɔse fiɛ ɔkɛlɛ kato.” Matia Ɔfɔ Yuda Kasɛkɔ̃.
Ne kama ne, katɔ̃memasɛdze ɔso mabɔrɛ i kube gɔ marɔ sɔ Nnɔĩ adziri Kube iso makɛlɛ Yerusalem.
Ita i mmɔ ibo ɔmagɛ̃ ame aaɖe lɛ igu iwɛ̃ kere.
Gɔ masɛ maabo ɔmagɛ̃ ame ne, maya makɛlɛ ma kawekɔ̃ i iyo nɛ matsue masia iso ame.
Mma lowe i mmɔ nɖe Petro gu Yohanes gu Yakobo gu Andrea gu Filipo gu Toma gu Bartolomeo gu Mateo gu Yakobo gɔ nɖe Alfeo ɔbi gu Simon gɔ nto ɔkpɛ̃ ɔtã isɛguso gu Yuda gɔ nɖe Yakobo ɔbi.
Mmagbe ɔɖuɖu gu marɔ̃go mawɛ̃ gu Yesu ɔnyi Maria gu Yesu makpeama ɔwe adzuni awɛ̃ mala maɔsarɛ maɔkparama kayi ɔwi biara.
Ayi wamɔ ame ne, mma lofɔ maɖe ɔba maasarɛ, maaɖe lɛ maturi kulafa gu sinyɔ.
Ne Petro ɔta ɔya ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Wũ manyii, ara wa matsɛrɛ i Ɔko Sekelea ame ne, ikote sɔ iaba i ne ame lɛ kumɛgɔ i Siwarã Bielea ɔki i Igara David iso ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ kokooko i Yuda gɔ loɖi Yesu ɔtã mamɔɛ̃ iso.
Yuda ɔ̃ wũ ɔɖe bo ikuri ame ɔwɛ̃ gɔ i Bosate ɔɖi sɔ tee ɔ̃abara katɔ̃memasɛdze karabara.” Masu ɔ̃ ikpi sikã dzɛ ɔfɔ maɣa karɔ̃ ga iso ɔsɛ ɔ̃akpi.
Gɔ ɔkpase ne, ɔfã ɔbiɛ, ne ɔ̃ ayirira ɔɖuɖu ɔbɔrɛ afere i karɔ̃ ne.
Ɔ̃ kukpi itɔ̃me ɔki ikã i Yerusalem maturi ɔɖuɖu ɔnɔ ne.
Ngbegɔ ɔkpi masɛ makpere sɔ Hakeldamak i ma siɖe ame gɔ karɔ̃ nɖe sɔ Ima Karɔ̃.
Ne Petro ɔkɛlɛgu i katɔ̃ sɔ, “Matsɛrɛ i David Kuka Ɔko ame sɔ, ‘Ɔ̃ iyo si ikpese iyoku, kuwɛ̃ si ɔdaasɛ i mmɔ.’ Matsɛrɛ ana sɔ, ‘Mitã sɔ ɔturi mama si ɔya i ɔ̃ kanya.’ Ne ɔso ne, ikote sɔ ɔmama aabo i bo ndɛ̃ lɛ aɖansiɛ ɔtã Bosate Yesu ita ibɔrɛ i makpise ame.
Iaɖe ngɔ lowe i bo ikuri ame ku ɔwi gɔ ɔɖuɖu i bo gu Yesu sɛ boki, ita i ɔwi gɔ i Yohanes ɔpɛ Ɣaa itupie kubarara imomo isɛ iabo ɔwi gɔ i Ɣaa ɔsu Yesu ɔkɛlɛgu kato.” Ne ɔso maɖi maturi inyɔ ma nɖe Matia gu Yosef gɔ masɛ makpere sɔ Barsaba, ana ne, masɛ makpere wũ sɔ Yusto.
Ne kama makparama kayi maɣɛ sɔ, “Bosate, fɔ nɣe maturi ɔɖuɖu adzuni ame.
Ne ɔso te bo ngɔ aɖi i maturi inyɔ magbe ndɛ̃ sɔ ɔ̃aya i katɔ̃memasɛdze ndɛ̃ ngbegɔ i Yuda ɔnyua fiɛ ɔkɛlɛ ngbegɔ lokote wũ.” Gɔ makidza atalebi sɔ si masu manyɔ sɔ ma nna i Ɣaa ɔɖi ne, Matia ɔkpɛ loya, ne ɔso masu wũ mabua i katɔ̃memasɛdze iweo-ɔwɛ̃ mamɔ iso.
Siwarã Bielea Ɔba Ku Pentekoste Iyi.
Gɔ iyi nɛ masɛ makpere sɔ Pentekoste Iyi ɔɣo ne, mafɔɖedze ɔɖuɖu ɔsakanya i kakɔi kawɛ̃.
Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, manɔ kulu lɛ ɔwiri nto ɔkpɛ̃ teteree kubɔrɛ i kato.
Kulu gɔgbe ɔba kuayi iyo nɛ ame mapia ɔɖuɖu.
Ira iwɛ̃ nɛ nse lɛ ɔtɔ sinyagɛmi ɔɣɛɣɛ so iba iasia i ma ati iso.
Siwarã Bielea ɔbo i ma ɔɖuɖu ame matsɛ ikaɖe mato male Ɣaa i siɖe agbãagbã ame lɛ kumɛgɔ i Siwarã ɔtã ma ɔle.
Ɔwi gɔgbe ame tutuutu ne, ma Yudase ma nsɛ manigã Ɣaa fiɛ mase i kayiiso abuiti ɔɖuɖu ame ɔba mapia i Yerusalem.
Gɔ manɔ kulu gɔgbe ne, maturi gbodzoo ɔtere makɛlɛ mmɔ.
Gɔ manya sɔ Yesu masiaidze nɣɛ mato maɣɛ abuiti ɔɖuɖu wa ame mabɔrɛ siɖe ne, ibara ma ɣii.
Ne ɔso ifɔ̃ ɔtidza ma, makpɔkpɔtɔ, ne matsɛ ikarɛ so sɔ, “Mmagbe ɔɖuɖu ne, iiɖe Galilea maturi maɖe?
Nda ibara fiɛ boto bonɔ maɖe ika i bo abuiti siɖe ame?
Ma Partise gu ma Mediase gu ma Elamse gu mawɛ̃ ma lobɔrɛ i Mesopotamia gu Yudea gu Kapadokia gu Ponto gu Asia gu Frigia gu Pamfilia gu Egipte gu Libia kasɛ ga lomatã Kirene gu mafɔ ma lobɔrɛ i Roma fiɛ maɖe ma Yudase gu mma lokpese ma Yudase ikuri ame maturi, gu ma Kretase gu ma Arabiase.
Bo ɔɖuɖu to bonɔ mato mafa Ɣaa kaɣiɖu i bo siɖe ame.” Gɔ ibara ma ɣaa fiɛ makpɔkpɔtɔ ne, makarɛ so sɔ, “Mme itɔ̃me igbã iɖe ngbe?” Ne mawɛ̃ to maɣɛ sɔ, “Ndã miɖe nto mimɔɛ̃ ma.
Iiɖe kuira iɖe.” Petro Ɔɖe Ma Yudase Ika.
Mmɔ i Petro gu maturi iweo-ɔwɛ̃ ɔta maya fiɛ Petro ɔkɔlɛ ɔ̃ silɔ sɔ, “Mi ma Yudase gu mi ma nsi i Yerusalem ɔɖuɖu, lobie sɔ loaɖi ara wagbe karɔ̃ lote mi.
Mikã me atsue kukaakɔ si minɔ.
Marɛrɛ̃ magbe iito marɛ̃ ndã lɛ kumɛgɔ mibu.
Mi mɔmɔ minya sɔ kaya iɖɔwũ kaiwɛ̃ ame kere bopia.
Ɣɛɛ ne, nnɛ mito minya ngbe nɖe nnɛ i Ɣaa Kanyaɖidze Yoel ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ kokooko.
Ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Ɣaa ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Ayi tsɔra ame ne, nto loafedza wũ Siwarã lofere i maturi ɔɖuɖu iso.
Mi mabibirɛrɛ̃ gu mabi birɔ̃gomi to maaɣɛ wũ itɔ̃me, mi maporoporoi to maanya kaɖikate, mi makpakpa ana to maasɛ̃ arɛ.
Gbaã ne, i ayi wamɔ ame ne, wũ Siwarã to siaba wũ maɖabo rɔ̃go gu marɛrɛ̃ iso, fiɛ maaɣɛ wũ itɔ̃me.
Loatã sɔ awawãra wa loabara ɣii aabɔrɛ i kuɖokpo gu karɔ̃ iso ɔɖuɖu.
Mito mianya ima gu ɔtɔ gu kuɣɔ gɔ lota lipii.
Kuɣɛ̃ to kuabara kpinaa.
Ɔgbaworeti to ɔ̃arɛtɛ lɛ ima, fiɛ kuɖokpo Ɔlesate iyi siare nɛmɔ aaba.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, ɔbiara gɔ loakpere Ɣaa sɔ ɔnyɔ wũ nnya aana ngbã.” ’ ” Ne Petro ɔɣɛ ana sɔ, “Bo aɖe Israel kaɖe, mito minɔ?
Yesu Nasaretse nɖe ngɔ i Ɣaa kɔrɔ̃ sia iso fiɛ ɔsɔla wũ nnɔĩ.
Ɣaa ɔsia nnɛgbe ita gɔ ɔki i ɔ̃ iso ɔɖi ɔle gu awawãra gu akparĩ ɔte i mi ndɛ̃ lɛ kumɛgɔ i mi mɔmɔ miɣe.
Ɣɛɛ i Ɣaa ɔri iɖi ame gu ɔ̃ itsue iɖegu katɔ̃ ame ne, ɔnyua wũ ɔtã mi.
Mi gu matilese ɔɖi wũ miɖoe ku ɔwi gɔ mipɛ wũ mimatãra i kudziri iso.
Ɣɛɛ Ɣaa ɔtara wũ ɔbɔrɛgu i makpise ame.
Ɔbɔrɛ i kukpi nrɔɔ̃ ame, alasɔ kukpi iiwo wũ ɔmɔɛ̃ ɔpia i kugbagɔrɔĩ ame.
Igara David ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ i ɔ̃ iso sɔ, ‘Lonya sɔ Bosate ɣɛ me i kɔrɛ ɔwi biara.
Gɔ ɔɣɛ me i kuɖearɔ̃ iso ɔso ne, loibanigã.
Nnɛgbe ɔso ne, wũ ɔtu ɔyi ku isoɣɔ, loasu silɔ lole wũ ɔwi ɖaa.
Loawe i ɔriinyɔ ame atoa sɔ wũ sosina to siakpi.
Alasɔ aibanyua wũ ɔkala atã ikpibiɔ.
Ana ne, aibatã fɔ Ɔbi Sekelea sina ɔburi.
Ate me fɔ ngbã ɔri.
Fɔ kɔrɛ iwe isoɣɔ pia i wũ ame gbaã.’ “Ne ɔso ne, wũ manyii, nto loɣere mi kukaakɔ sɔ bo ɔwa David ɔkpi.
Mabiara wũ.
Ɔ̃ ikpibiɔ ana se i bo ndɛ̃ ipɛ i nɔme.
Ɣɛɛ ne, Ɣaa kanyaɖidze ɔɖe.
Ɣaa ɔkarã irɔĩ iso sɔ ɔ̃abara David ɔwa tɛtɛ ɔɖe sigara i David sigaraiyara iso.
Gɔ David ɔnya nnɛ nse i katɔ̃ ɔso ne, ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ sɔ Kristo to ɔ̃ata ɔbɔrɛ i makpise ame.
Ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Ɔ̃ibanyua wũ ɔtã kukpi fiɛ ɔ̃ibanyua ɔ̃ sina ɔburi i ikpibiɔ ame.’ Yesu gɔgbe i Ɣaa ɔtara ɔbɔrɛgu i makpise ame ɔso i bo ɔɖuɖu ɖe itɔ̃me nɛgbe maɖansiɛ ne.
Kiniɔ ne, ɔ̃ Ɔse Ɣaa ɔtã wũ kasɛkɔ̃ kɔlɛa i ɔ̃ kuɖearɔ̃ iso, ɔsu Siwarã Bielea ɔtã wũ lɛ kumɛgɔ ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ fiɛ mito minya, minɔ ana ngbe.
Iiɖe David lota ɔbɔrɛ i makpise ame ɔkɛlɛ kato.
Ɣɛɛ ne, ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ sɔ, ‘Bosate Ɣaa ɔɣere wũ Sate sɔ, “Sɛ i wũ kuɖearɔ̃ iso, gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ loasu fɔ matsirise lopia i fɔ ngba kayirinɔ.” ’ Ne ɔso nto lobie sɔ loɣere mi Israel kaɖe ɔɖuɖu sɔ, Ɣaa ɔɖe lobara Yesu gɔ mipɛ mimatãra i kudziri iso sɔ ɔ̃ɔkpese Bosate gu Kristo.” Gɔ manɔ Petro atɔ̃me ne, itsue ma situ.
Ne ɔso makarɛ wũ gu katɔ̃memasɛdze tsɔra sɔ, “Bo manyii, be si bobara?” Ne Petro ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ikote sɔ mi ɔbiara kɛkɛ aanyua ikpi ɔbara ɔfiniki ɔba Bosate kɔrɛ, ɔfɔ Ɣaa itupie kubarara i Yesu Kristo iyere ame sɔ Ɣaa asu ɔ̃ akpi ɔtsɛ wũ iyɔ miɔfɔ Siwarã Bielea lɛ kumɛgɔ ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ.
Nnɛ ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ ne, ise itã mi gu mi mabi gu mma lobɔrɛ i kadzorokɔ̃.
Mma ɔɖuɖu i Bosate Ɣaa aakpere ɔbɔ ɔ̃ kɔrɛ.” Petro ɔɣere ma ara gbodzoo, ɔpɛ ma nrɔɔ̃, ɔtã ma kuka sɔ, “Miɖi so mibɔrɛgu i kutsue ikpadzɛ̃ nɛ nto iaba i ɔɣekparɛ nyanyarĩa gɔgbe iso.” Nɛgbe ɔso ne, maturi gbodzoo i ma ndɛ̃ ɔfɔ Petro itɔ̃me maɖe, ne mapie ma ndu i Yesu iyere ame gɔ maaɖe lɛ maturi kukpi kutɛ.
Masu so mabua i mma lofɔ Ɣaa maɖe iso ku iyi nɛmɔ.
Mana ɔwi matã katɔ̃memasɛdze.
Ne ɔso mate ma ara, makparama kayi, maɖe ara masakanya fiɛ masɛ i kanya kawɛ̃ ibara ame ana.
Mafɔɖedze Ɔbara Sinyii Gbaã.
Kumɛgɔ i katɔ̃memasɛdze ɔbara awawãra gu akparĩ ɔtã maturi ɔsu kuwarɛ matã Ɣaa.
Mafɔɖedze ɔɖuɖu ɔla maɔsarɛ ɔwi biara, ana ne, ibiara nɛ i ɔwɛ̃ ba ne, ma ɔɖuɖu ire iɖe.
Si marɔdɛ̃ ma ira irere ne, masɛ masu sikã maɣɛ so kumɛgɔ inya ɔbiara kanya.
Mala maɔsɛ Ɣaa iyo iyi biara kɛkɛ, ana ne, mala maɔsarɛ i akuri akuri ame i ma ayo maɔɖe ara i isoɣɔ gu ɔtu sekelea ame.
Mala maɔpɛ Ɣaa siba maɔle wũ ana, ne ɔso maturi ɔɖuɖu sɛ mawarɛ ma.
Iyi biara Bosate ɔla ɔ̃ɔsu mma lona iɖi ɔ̃ɔbua i ma iso.
Ɣaa Ɔsa Ɔturi Gɔ Lofɛfɛ̃ Ɔsi I Karɔ̃.
Iyi iwɛ̃ ne, Petro gu Yohanes ɔkɛlɛ Isɔrɛyo ku kakɔme iɖɔwũ itɛ ame, ɔwi gɔ i ma Yudase sɛ makparama kayi.
Gɔ mabo kayogodɔ̃ ga masɛ marɔ Kulɛ Kayogodɔ̃ ne, manya ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ nɖe bafã ita i ɔwi gɔ maɣe wũ.
Ɔ̃ masate sɛ masu wũ masɛ i mmɔ iyi biara sɔ si ɔla ɔ̃ɔwanyi ara i mma nsɛ maki i mmɔ makɛlɛ Isɔrɛyo ame kɔrɛ.
Gɔ ɔnya Petro gu Yohanes to mafe mabo iyo ne, ɔkarɛ ma sɔ matã wũ sikã.
Matui maya manyɔ wũ totoroo, ne Petro ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Nyɔ bo!” Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔmɔ ɔkɔlɛ anɔ ɔto ɔnyɔ ma ku adzuni sɔ mato maba maatã wũ ira iwɛ̃.
Ne Petro ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Mme lona sikã kusiwɛ̃ loatã-ɔ!
Ɣɛɛ ne, loatã-ɔ nnɛ loba!
Loɣere-ɔ i Yesu Kristo Nasaretse iyere ame sɔ ta ya si asɛ!” Petro ɔmɔɛ̃ wũ kuɖearɔ̃ sɔ ɔta ɔya.
Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, ɔle ɔbo i ɔ̃ ngba gu akpakpokpo ame!
Ne ɔkɔlɛ ɔɣo ɔtsɛ isɛ ɔsiai ma ɔbo Isɔrɛyo ame ɔsɛ ɔkiki ɔkɔlɛ ɔɣo ɔle Ɣaa ne.
Gɔ maturi ɔɖuɖu ɔnya wũ ɔsɛ ɔto ɔle Ɣaa, fiɛ matsue sɔ ɔ̃ nsɛ ɔɖɔɛ ɔsɛ i Isɔrɛyo Kulɛ Kayogodɔ̃ ɔwanyi ara ne, makpɔkpɔtɔ, ibara ma ɣaa i kumɛgɔ ɔsarɛ iti.
Petro Ɔɖe Ika I Yesu Ɔle Iso I Isɔrɛyo.
Maturi ɔɖuɖu ɔtere maba ngbegɔ marɔ sɔ Salomo Kakpakɛ i Isɔrɛyo ame.
Maba maanya ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ losarɛ ɔɖo ɔmatã Petro gu Yohanes iso kpa gɔ ɔ̃ isarɛ ɔbara ma ɣii.
Gɔ Petro ɔnya maturi ne, ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Israel kaɖe, be ɔso fiɛ nnɛgbe to ibara mi ɣaa?
Be ɔso fiɛ mito minyɔ bo lɛ sɔ bo isekele kaɖu ɣee bo ɔle ame iɖe bobara ngɔgbe ɔsarɛ!
Ɣaa gɔ nɖe Abraham gu Isak gu Yakob gu bo mawa Ɣaa ne, ɔ̃ loɔkɔlɛ ɔ̃ Ɔbi Yesu kato ne.
Misɛ̃ wũ i Pilato katɔ̃ sɔ miiɣe wũ gɔ Pilato ɔbie sɔ si ɔnyua wũ.
Misɛ̃ ɔturi Sekelea gu Ɔbɔlɔlɔa, ɣɛɛ minɔ karɔ̃ sɔ ɔnyua turiɖoese i ɔ̃ kanya ɔtã mi.
Miɖoe ngɔ nsɛ ɔtã maturi ngbã.
Ɣɛɛ ne, Ɣaa ɔledza wũ itara ibɔrɛgu i makpise ame.
Bo mɔmɔ bonya wũ ku bo anɔ.
Iki i Yesu iyere ame fiɛ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ miɣe fiɛ mito minya ngbe ɔna isosarɛ.
Gɔ ɔfɔ Yesu ɔɖe ɔso ne, Bosate ɔtã wũ isosarɛ nɛ loyi fiɛ mi ɔɖuɖu to minya.
“Manyii, loɣe sɔ idaatsue lotã mi gu mi makpakpa ɔbara nnɛgbe.
Ɣɛɛ ne, Ɣaa ɔki i kanyamaɖidze ɔɖuɖu iso ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ sɔ Kristo to ɔ̃aki i ibo nɛmɔ igbã ame.
Ne ɔso fiɛ ɔtã ma atɔ̃me ɔba i ne ame ne.
Ne ɔso mifiniki misiai Ɣaa si ɔsu mi akpi ɔtsɛ mi si isobuɛ aaba ibɔrɛ i Ɔ̃ kɔrɛ, iyɔ ɔ̃ɔsese mi Kristo gɔ i ɔ̃ mɔmɔ ɔɖi ɔsɛ mi.
Ipia sɔ Yesu aawe i kato gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ ɔwi gɔ i ɔ̃ Ɔse aasu ira biara ɔsɛ i ne kasekɔ̃ lɛ kumɛgɔ ɔɣɛ koko ɔkigu i ɔ̃ kanyamaɖidze sekelea iso.
Lɛ kumɛgɔ i Mose ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Bosate gɔ nɖe mi Ɣaa to ɔ̃asese mi kanyaɖidze mama ɔbɔrɛgu i mi ndɛ̃ lɛ me.
Ne ɔso mikã wũ atsue i ibiara nɛ ɔ̃aɣere mi ame.
Ɔbiara gɔ loibakã ɔ̃ itɔ̃me atsue ne, Ɣaa aaɖi wũ ɔbɔrɛgu i ɔ̃ maturi ndɛ̃ pelepele.’ “Gbagbaã ne, Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze ɔɖuɖu ita i Samuel iso ne, maɣɛ masɛ koko i ara wa nto aaba ku ayi wagbe ame.
Mi nɖe Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze mabi, fiɛ Ɣaa mɔmɔ lonyi kanya ku mi mawa ɔkigu i ɔ̃ kanyamaɖidze iso.
Ɔɣere Abraham sɔ iaki ɔ̃ ɔwa tɛtɛ iso ɔ̃atã kayiiso ɔɖuɖu iwarã gu isobuɛ.
Ne ɔso gɔ Ɣaa ɔɖi ɔ̃ ɔɖabo Kristo ne, ɔɖe katɔ̃ ɔpia wũ mi kɔrɛ sɔ ɔtã mi kusɛkusɛ si mi ɔbiara aafiniki ɔbɔrɛ i mi akpi ame.”
Mamɔɛ̃ Petro Gu Yohanes.
Ɔwi gɔ i Petro gu Yohanes ɣɛ mato maɖe maturi ika ne, masɔrɛdze gu isɔrɛyo madzuɛ̃se ɔkpakpa gu ma Zadukise mawɛ̃ ɔba maabo mmɔ.
Gɔ manɔ sɔ Petro gu Yohanes ɣɛ mato mate ara sɔ mma loɔkpi to maaledza ita lɛ kumɛgɔ i Yesu ɔta ɔbɔrɛ i makpise ame ne, sikpã ɔkpɛ̃ ma gbaã.
Ne ɔso mamɔɛ̃ ma.
Gɔ kaɖe ɔɔro ɔso ne, masu ma mapia i iyo gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ kaɖesɛ̃a.
Ɣɛɛ maturi gbodzoo ma lonɔ atɔ̃me wagbe ɔfɔ Itɔ̃me Bielea maɖe.
Mafɔɖedze kusime ɔba iaɖe lɛ marɛrɛ̃ kukpi kuru ɔɖui.
Gɔ kaɖe ɔsɛ̃ ne, ma Yudase matɔ̃ɖedze gu kaɖe makpakpa gu mmara matedze ɔsarɛ i Yerusalem.
Masarɛgu sɔrɛdzekpakpa pelepele Hana gu Kayafa gu Yohanes gu Aleksandro gu sɔrɛdzekpakpa pelepele manyii mawɛ̃.
Ne ka maɖi Petro gu Yohanes mabɔ i ma katɔ̃ makarɛ ma sɔ, “Nna iyere gu ɔle ame iɖe mibara ara wagbe?” Mmɔ i Petro gɔ loyi ku Siwarã Bielea ɔle ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Bo matɔ̃ɖedze gu makpakpa, si mikarɛ sɔ bokparara kayiribielea ga bobara bafã gɔgbe gu kumɛgɔ bosa wũ ne, mitã loɣere mi gu Israel kaɖe ɔɖuɖu ira iwɛ̃.
Iki i Yesu Kristo gɔ lobɔrɛ i Nasaret iyere ame, ngɔ mipɛ mimatãra i kudziri iso, fiɛ Ɣaa ɔledza wũ itara ibɔrɛgu i makpise ame iyere ame i ngɔgbe ɔna isosarɛ.
Yesu gɔgbe iso i Ɔko Sekelea ɔɖe ika sɔ, ‘Ita nɛ i mi mayotsuedze ɔsɛ̃ ne, ne lokpese ita nɛ lofɔ kuɣa iɖo ata ɔɖuɖu ne.’ Ɔ̃ ɔnɔwɛ̃ saã nɖe Ɖidze, alasɔ ɔ̃ nɖe ngɔ i Ɣaa ɔtã iyere gu ɔle sɔ maturi ɔɖuɖu i kayiiso aaki i ɔ̃ iso mana ngbã.” Gɔ manya kumɛgɔ i Petro gu Yohanes ɔɖe ika gu ɔtu fiɛ maɣe ana sɔ mma loiɣe ɔko gu mma nna ɖibia kuwɛ̃ i kaɖe ame maɖe ne, ibara ma ɣii.
Manya maɖi ite sɔ masiai Yesu.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ mato manya ngɔ masa ɣɛ i ma katɔ̃ mmɔ ne, maiwo kuira ɔɣɛ.
Gɔ makɔ ma maɖi i kayaso ame mmɔ ne, makpakpa kerekere ɔsɛ iti ame.
Mawɛ̃ ɔkarɛ sɔ, “Be iɖe boabara mmagbe?
Boibawo ɔsɛ̃ sɔ iiɖe ma lobara iwawãra nɛgbe!
Ɔbiara i Yerusalem ɣe, fiɛ maɔnɔ itɔ̃me nɛgbe.
Ɣɛɛ ne, mitã bosɛ̃ botã ma sɔ madaasiɖe ika i ngɔ marɔ Yesu iyere ame ana, si itɔ̃me nɛgbe iisibasamarã.” Gɔ maledza ma ikpere ibɔ i ma kasarɛkɔ̃ ne, masɛ̃ matã ma sɔ ita i kiniɔ ne, madaasiɣɛ ɣee mate kuira i Yesu iyere ame.
Ne Petro gu Yohanes ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Mi mɔmɔ minyɔ ne kukaakɔ.
Be loabo Ɣaa anɔ iɖo?
Si bokã mi atsue ɣee si bobara Ɣaa kuɖɔɛ?
Nwa bonya gu nwa bonɔ ne, boibawo kanya ɔma i wã iso.” Gɔ makpakpa mamɔ ɔkɛkɛ anɔ mapia ma ne, manyua ma.
Kumɛgɔ i maturi ɔɖuɖu to male Ɣaa ala ɔ̃ kurabarara ɔso ne, mainya kuira nɛ iso maakpadzɛ̃ ma kutsue.
Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ lona isosarɛ ɔɔfɔ lɛ akɔ sina gu kama.
Gɔ manyua Petro gu Yohanes ne, makɛlɛ ma maturi kɔrɛ masɛ maaɣere ma nnɛ i makpakpa ɔɣere ma.
Mafɔɖedze ɔɖuɖu ɔsakanya, ne makɔlɛ silɔ kato makparama kayi sɔ, “O Bosate, fɔ gɔ lobara kato gu karɔ̃ gu ɔpo gu ara ɔɖuɖu wa mpia i wã ame.
Fɔ loki i fɔ Siwarã Bielea ame aɖe ika akigu i bo ɔwa David gɔ nɖe fɔ ɔɖabo iso sɔ, ‘Be ɔso i kayiiso maturi to mata matui, fiɛ nɖebi ana to mabu adzuni siefe?
Kayiiso magara ɔbara kanya kawɛ̃ fiɛ ma matɔ̃ɖedze ɔsa so kanya mata sɔ maakpɛ̃gu Ɣaa gu ɔ̃ Kristo.’ Gbagbaã iɖe sɔ Herodes gu Pontio Pilato gu Israel kaɖe gu mma loiɖe Israel maturi ɔsa so kanya i ɔmagɛ̃ gɔgbe ame mata maya i fɔ Ɔɖabo Sekelea Yesu gɔ asɔla nnɔĩ iso.
Ɣɛɛ i fɔ ɔle gu iwola ame ne, atã ma ɔri sɔ mabara ara wa fɔ aɣɛ asɛ sɔ maabara.
Kiniɔ ne, O Bosate, nyɔ anɔ wa mato makɛkɛ mapia bo!
Tã bo ma nɖe fɔ maɖabo kagbegbe, sɔ boawo fɔ itɔ̃me ɔɣɛ.
Pɛgu maturi si asa ma abara awawãra gbodzoo i fɔ Ɔɖabo Sekelea Yesu iyere ame.” Gɔ makparama kayi maro ne, iyo nɛ ame mapia ɔti, ne Siwarã Bielea ɔba siayi i ma ame ɔɖuɖu matsɛ Ɣaa Itɔ̃me Bielea iɣɛ ku kagbegbe ne.
Mafɔɖedze Ɔbuai So.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, mma ɔɖuɖu lofɔ maɖe ɖe mawɛ̃ i ɔbara gu adzuni ame, ma kuwɛ̃ iisɛ ɔbu ɔ̃ ɔnɔwɛ̃ saã ɔkpɛ.
Ɣɛɛ ne, ira biara nɛ i ɔwɛ̃ ba ɖe ma ɔɖuɖu ire.
Ne ɔso katɔ̃memasɛdze ɔɣɛ Bosate Yesu ita ibɔrɛ i makpise ame iso itɔ̃me gu ɔle siare fiɛ Ɣaa nnyainyɔ siare ɔwegu ma ɔɖuɖu.
Kuwɛ̃ iiɖe wɛrɛba i ma ndɛ̃ alasɔ mma mba ayo ɣee nrɔ̃ ne, masu ma ara marɔdɛ̃.
Ne masu sikã dzɛ mana mapia i katɔ̃memasɛdze nrɔɔ̃ ame maɣɛ ɔbiara kumɛgɔ i ɔ̃ anyaa ɔsi kanya ne.
Ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɔwe mmɔ gɔ marɔ sɔ Yosef ɔbɔrɛ i Levi ɔɣekparɛ ame fiɛ ɔbɔrɛ i Kipro karɔ̃ iso.
Katɔ̃memasɛdze ɔtã wũ iyere sɔ Barnaba gɔ karɔ̃ nɖe Kateteretãse.
Ɔ̃ wũ ɔsu ɔ̃ karɔ̃ ɔrɔdɛ̃ ɔsu sikã ɔbɔ katɔ̃memasɛdze.
Anania Gu Safira Ɔla Sila.
Ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ana ɔwe gɔ marɔ sɔ Anania fiɛ ɔ̃ ɔre nɖe Safira.
Ma wũ makpɛti ma karɔ̃ marɔdɛ̃.
I ɔrɔ̃go itsue ame ne, ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔsu sikã siwɛ̃ ɔkɔla fiɛ ɔsu sikutia ɔba ɔ̃apia i katɔ̃memasɛdze nrɔɔ̃ ame.
Ne Petro ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Anania, be ɔso fiɛ atã Satana ɔɖe-ɔ iso fiɛ ato ala sila atã Siwarã Bielea?
Mikuti karɔ̃ ga mikpɛti mirɔdɛ̃ sikã siwɛ̃ misɛ so.
Mi mba karɔ̃ ga misu mirɔdɛ̃, fiɛ kuso gɔ matã mi ana ne, mi mba.
Be ɔso fiɛ atã sɔ mibara ira nyanyarĩa nɛgbe igbã?
Iiɖe maturi awune iɖe mila sila mitã, ɣɛɛ Ɣaa.” Gɔ Anania ɔnɔ atɔ̃me wagbe ne, ɔluwɛ̃ ɔrɔ̃ ɔfere i karɔ̃ ɔkpi!
Ifɔ̃ siare ɔmɔɛ̃ mma ɔɖuɖu lonɔ nnɛ loba.
Ne maporoporoi ma mpia i ma ndɛ̃ i mmɔ ɔsu ɔkati mamini wũ, maputa wũ masɛ maabiara ne.
Lɛ iɖɔwũ itɛ kama ne, ɔ̃ ɔre ɔba ɔ̃ɔbo mmɔ gɔ ɔ̃iɣe nnɛ loba.
Ne Petro ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ɣere me, karɔ̃ ga i mi gu fɔ ɔrã ɔrɔdɛ̃ ne, sikã dzɛ matã mi ɔɖuɖu i ngbe ne?” Ne ɔrɔ̃go ɔfɔ kanya sɔ, “Aĩ, sikã ɔɖuɖu mmɔ ne.” Petro ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Be ɔso fiɛ mi gu fɔ ɔrã ɔbara kanya kawɛ̃ sɔ miala Siwarã Bielea minyɔ?
Nyɔ, maporoporoi ma loputa fɔ ɔrã masɛ maabiara ɔɔba maɣɛ sɔ maaputa-ɔ fɔ wũ makɛlɛgu.” Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, ɔ̃ wũ ɔrɔ̃ ɔfere i karɔ̃ i Petro ngbatɔ̃ ɔkpi kɛrɛrɛ.
Gɔ maporoporoi ɔba maanya sɔ ɔ̃ɔkpi ɔrɛ ne, maputa wũ makɛlɛgu masɛ maabiara i ɔ̃ ɔrã kɔrɛ.
Ne ɔso ifɔ̃ siare ɔmɔɛ̃ mafɔɖedze gu mma ɔɖuɖu lonɔ ara wa loba.
Katɔ̃memasɛdze Ɔbara Awawãra Agbãagbã.
Katɔ̃memasɛdze ɔbara awawãra gu akparĩ gbodzoo i maturi ndɛ̃.
Mafɔɖedze ɔɖuɖu sɛ masarɛ i isɔrɛyo ngbegɔ marɔ sɔ Salomo kakpakɛ ame.
Maturi mama ma loifiniki sɛ manigã ma ibore ibo, ɣɛɛ mala maɔwarɛ ma.
Ɣɛɛ maturi gbodzoo, marɛrɛ̃ gu marɔ̃go, ɔfiniki mafɔ Bosate maɖe maba maabo i mafɔɖedze ikuri ame.
Maturi ɔsu manyɛse maba maarara i sikala iso i siriruɛ ngbegɔ mafɔ maɖe sɔ si Petro to ɔfe ne, bidɛ ɔ̃ kusɔ aasia i manyɛse iso.
Masu manyɛse gbodzoo gu mma ɔɖuɖu i siwarã lalaa to siɖaa mabɔrɛgu i simagɛ̃ dzɛ loki silɔ Yerusalem mabɔ ma kɔrɛ fiɛ masa ma ɔɖuɖu.
Ma Yudase Makpakpa Ɔkpɛ̃gu Katɔ̃memasɛdze Sirerɛ.
Sɔrɛdzekpakpa pelepele gu ma ikuri nɛ marɔ sɔ ma Zadukise ɔtsɛ sirerɛ ikpɛ̃gu katɔ̃memasɛdze teteree.
Ne ɔso mamɔɛ̃ katɔ̃memasɛdze masɛ maapia i iyo ame.
Ɣɛɛ kasɛ̃ ne, Ɣaa kpabo ɔba ɔ̃asese ma kayogodɔ̃ ɔɖi ma.
Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mikɛlɛ Isɔrɛyo si misɛ miaɣere maturi ngbã ɣɛtɛ mɛgbe iso ara ɔɖuɖu!” Gɔ kaɖe ɔsɛ̃ ne, makɛlɛ isɔrɛyo ame masɛ maatsɛ ara ite lɛ kumɛgɔ i Ɣaa kpabo ɔɣere ma.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, sɔrɛdzekpakpa pelepele gu ɔ̃ makpakpa laa gu ma Yudase matɔ̃ɖedze ɔsarɛ, ne mapia iyo madzuɛ̃se sɔ masɛ maaɖi katɔ̃memasɛdze i iyo mabɔ.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ makɛlɛ ne, maisɛ maanya ma!
Ne ɔso makpese maba maaɣere ma sɔ, “Gɔ bosɛ ne, bonya sɔ kukui ɔsɛ̃ kpakpara, madzuɛ̃se ana ɣɛ i kanya.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ bosese ne, mma bomɔɛ̃ bopia mmɔ kuwɛ̃ na i iyo ame!” Gɔ isɔrɛyo madzuɛ̃se ɔkpakpa gu sɔrɛdzekpakpa ɔnɔ itɔ̃me nɛgbe ne, awururu ɔkpɛ̃ ma gbaã, alasɔ maitsue nnɛ iɖe loba.
Ne ɔwɛ̃ ɔba ɔ̃aɣere ma sɔ, “Mma mimɔɛ̃ mipia iyo ne, maɣɛ i isɔrɛyo mato mate maturi ara.” Mmɔ i isɔrɛyo madzuɛ̃se ɔkpakpa gu ɔ̃ maturi ɔta makɛlɛ sɔ maamɔɛ̃ ma mabɔ.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ mato manigã sɔ mma losakanya i mmɔ aapɛ ma ata ɔso ne, maimɔɛ̃ ma sikitii.
Gɔ masɛ maakɔ katɔ̃memasɛdze mabɔ ne, maɖi ma maɣedza i ma Yudase matɔ̃ɖedze katɔ̃ sɔ masɔrɛdze ɔkpakpa pelepele si ɔkarɛ ma itɔ̃me.
Ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, “Boiɣere mi sɔ midaasiɣɛ kuira i Yesu gɔgbe iso?
Ɣɛɛ miɔkararã itɔ̃me nɛgbe i Yerusalem ɔɖuɖu.
Mibie ana sɔ miatã bo ipɔ i Yesu kukpi iti!” Mmɔ i Petro gu katɔ̃memasɛdze mama ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Ikote sɔ boakã Ɣaa atsue boɖo maturi awune.
Yesu gɔ mitã mapɛ mamatãra i kudziri iso fiɛ ɔkpi ne, bo mawa Ɣaa ɔtara wũ ɔbɔrɛgu i makpise ame ɔpia ngbã.
Ɣaa ɔtara wũ ɔsia i kakpakpakɔi i ɔ̃ kuɖearɔ̃ iso.
Ɔsu wũ ɔbara Ɔkpakpa gu Ɖidze sɔ Israel kaɖe ana ɔri mafiniki i ma situ ame mana akpi isu itsɛ.
Bo gu Siwarã Bielea dzɛ i Ɣaa ɔsu ɔtã mma nsɛ makã wũ atsue ne, bo nɖe ara wagbe maɖansiɛ ne.” Gɔ manɔ atɔ̃me wagbe ne, sikpã ɔmɔɛ̃ ma gbaã.
Ne ɔso masia ita sɔ maaɖoe katɔ̃memasɛdze magbe.
Ɣɛɛ ma ndɛ̃ ɔ Farisise ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Gamaliel fiɛ ɔɖe Mose mmara tedze ɔsɛ̃ ɔtã ma.
Maturi ɔɖuɖu sɛ mawarɛ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe kukaakɔ.
Ɔta ɔya i atɔ̃mekaɣɛkɔ̃ ɔɣɛ sɔ matã maɖi katɔ̃memasɛdze si ma kerekere si masɛ iti ame.
Mmɔ ɔto ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Israel maturi, minyɔ kukaakɔ nnɛ mito mibie sɔ miabaragu mmagbe!
Ɔwi gɔ lofe ame ne, ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ sɔ Teuda ɔbara so lɛ ngɔ lobua ɔnya.
Maturi alafa ana ɔta masiai wũ.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ maɖoe wũ ne, ɔ̃ masiaidze ɔsame, ne ɔ̃ ikuri nɛmɔ ɔbiɛ ne.
Ne kama ɔwi gɔ maka maturi ne, Yuda gɔ lobɔrɛ i Galilea ɔsa maturi mawɛ̃ kanya mata maya i abã iso.
Gɔ maɖoe wũ ne, ɔ̃ masiaidze ɔsame.
Ne ɔso nnɛ nto loɣere mi nɖe sɔ, minyua mmagbe.
Si ara wa mato mate gu nwa mato mabara ne ma mɔmɔ are aɖe ne, ɔwi kurukutu ame ne wã ɔɖuɖu to atui.
Ɣɛɛ si Ɣaa kurabarara kuɖe ne, miibawo ma ɔtindza.
Si iiɖe ngbɔ ne, iyi to iba gɔ mianya sɔ Ɣaa mɔmɔ mito mikpɛ̃gu!” Ɔ̃ kuka ɔtã mafinikira ma adzuni.
Ne ɔso makpere katɔ̃memasɛdze mabɔ ma ndɛ̃, ne mapɛ ma maɣere ma sɔ madaasiɖe ika kuiwɛ̃ i Yesu itɔ̃me iso fiɛ manyua ma ne.
Gɔ mato makɛlɛ ne, isoɣɔ lala ɔbo i ma ame, alasɔ manya sɔ Ɣaa ɔka ma ɔpia i mma lokote sɔ maana kunuarɛ i Yesu iti.
Ne kama ne, iyi biara mala maɔte Itɔ̃me Bielea sɔ Yesu nɖe Kristo i ma Yudase isɔrɛyo gu maturi ayo.
Maɖi Mabuaidze Ikɔdzɛ.
Ɔwi gɔ i marasuãdze ɔtsɛ isi ibua ne, kakpadzɛ̃ ɔba i ma Yudase ma nsɛ maɣɛ Griki siɖe gu mma nsɛ maɣɛ si Hebrise ndɛ̃ sɔ si maɣɛ ikpɛnɛ araɖea ne, aito aɣo makuɛdze ma nto maɣɛ Griki siɖe.
Ne ɔso katɔ̃memasɛdze iweo-inyɔ ɔkpere marasuãdze tsɔra ɔɖuɖu maɣere ma sɔ, “Ikote sɔ boasu bo ɔwi botã Ɣaa itɔ̃me iɣɛ ne iiɖe araɖea kutsuɛ.
Ne ɔso kiniɔ ne, manyii, minyɔ mi ndɛ̃ si miɖi marɛrɛ̃ ikɔdzɛ ma anɔ lokpa fiɛ Siwarã Bielea ana pia i ma ame.
Mmamɔ boasu boɣedza i karabara gamɔ kanya, si bosu bo ɔwi botã kayi ikparama gu Itɔ̃me Bielea iɣɛ.” Itɔ̃me nɛgbe ɔkote ma ɔɖuɖu, ne ɔso maɖi Stefano gɔ nɖe ɔturi gɔ mba kafɔkaɖe, fiɛ Siwarã Bielea ana pia i ɔ̃ ame.
Maɖi Filipo, Prokoro, Nikanor, Timon, Parmena gu ɔfɔ gɔ lokpese ɔ Yudase gɔ marɔ Nikolao fiɛ ɔbɔrɛ i Antiokia sɔ mabuai Stefano.
Maturi ikɔdzɛ magbe maɖi mate katɔ̃memasɛdze ne.
Makparama kayi masu ma nrɔɔ̃ masia ma iso itã karabara.
Maturi gbodzoo ɔfɔ Itɔ̃me Bielea gɔ itã sɔ mma lofɔ maɖe ɔba maasi i Yerusalem.
Ma Yudase masɔrɛdze gbodzoo ana ɔfiniki masiai kafɔkaɖe gagbe.
Ma Yudase Makpakpa Ɔmɔɛ̃ Stefano.
Stefano gɔ loyi ku abualɛra gu ɔle ɔbara awawãra gbodzoo i maturi ndɛ̃.
Ma Yudase masande ikuri nɛ i ma makɔse ɔnyua fiɛ mabɔrɛ i Kirene gu Aleksandria gu mma lobɔrɛ i Kilikia gu Asia ɔtsɛ atɔ̃me ikpadzɛ̃gu Stefano.
Ɣɛɛ kuwɛ̃ i ma ndɛ̃ iiwo ɔya i Stefano kanya, alasɔ Siwarã ɔtã wũ iwola nɛ ɔɖe ala ika.
Ne ɔso mabara kanya kawɛ̃ ku mawɛ̃ sɔ maaɖaɛ kanya masia wũ iso sɔ, “Bonɔ sɔ Stefano ɔɣɛ ara wa lota aya i Mose gu Ɣaa iso.” Kanya iɖaɛ nɛgbe ɔtã sikpã ɔmɔɛ̃ mmara matedze gu ma Yudase makpakpa gu maturi ɔɖuɖu.
Ne ɔso mamɔɛ̃ wũ makɛlɛgu ma atɔ̃mekaɣɛkɔ̃.
Mma makɔ mabɔ sɔ maɖaɛ wũ kanya ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Stefano ne, ɔsɛ ɔɖe ika ɔta ɔya i Isɔrɛyo Sekelea gu Mose mmara iso ɔwi biara.
Bonɔ ɔɣɛ ana sɔ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ lobɔrɛ i Nasaret fiɛ marɔ wũ Yesu ne, ɔto ɔ̃abiɛ Isɔrɛyo nɛgbe fiɛ ɔ̃afinikira Mose mmara mɛ ɔtã bo.” Mma ɔɖuɖu nsi i atɔ̃mekaɣɛkɔ̃ mmɔ ɔkarã anɔ i Stefano iso, ne manya sɔ ɔ̃ katɔ̃ to ka fiɛ lɛ Ɣaa kpabo kare.
Stefano Ɔɖi Ɣaa Itɔ̃me Bielea Kanya.
Sɔrɛdzekpakpa pelepele ɔkarɛ Stefano sɔ, “Ara wa mato maɣɛ ne gbaã iɖe?” Ne Stefano ɔtã mmuai sɔ, “Tete mɛrɛ̃ gu wũ manyii, mikã me atsue.
Ɣaa, Isekelesate ɔɖi so ɔte bo ɔwa Abraham i Mesopotamia karɔ̃ iso fiɛ ɔta i mmɔ ɔkɛlɛ karɔ̃ ga marɔ Haran iso.
Ɣaa ɔɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Rui i fɔ maturi kɔrɛ gu fɔ karɔ̃ iso si akɛlɛ karɔ̃ ga loate-ɔ iso!’ Ne ɔso ɔbɔrɛ i ɔ̃ karɔ̃ iso, ɔkɛlɛ ɔ̃asɛ i Haran gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ ɔ̃ ɔse ɔkpi.
Ne Ɣaa ɔkɔ wũ ɔbɔ ngbegɔ misi ngbe nɔme ne.
Ɣaa iitã Abraham kaɖekɔ̃ kukawɛ̃, nane karɔ̃ kɛkɛĩ ngbe.
Ɣɛɛ ne, ɔɣere wũ ɔɖegu katɔ̃ sɔ karɔ̃ gagbe to kaakpese ɔ̃ gu ɔ̃ mabi kare i ɔwi gɔ nto ɔba ame atoa sɔ ɔ̃iɣe ɔbi kuwɛ̃ iba iabo ɔwi gɔmɔ ame.
Ɣaa ɔɣere wũ kumɛgɔ i ɔ̃ mawa ɔɖuɖu to maakpese masande i kafɔrɔ̃ iso, mmamɔ to maabara ma ɔtile gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ akɔ alafa ana aafe.
Ɔɣere wũ ana sɔ, ‘Loto loakpadzɛ̃ karɔ̃ ga iso maaɖe masande maturi kutsue.
Ne kama ne, mato maabɔrɛ i mmɔ maba maafɛ̃ ara matã me i karɔ̃ ga iso bosi ngbe.’ Ne Ɣaa to ɔsu sirɛrɛ̃ itu ndamu ɔtã Abraham sɔ ɔwi gɔ nto ɔba ame ne, ne loaɖe ikparĩ i ɔ̃ Ɣaa gu Abraham ɔɣekparɛ ndɛ̃ ne.
Gɔ Abraham ɔɣe Isak ne, ɔtu wũ sirɛrɛ̃ ku ɔ̃ iyi farafanava.
Isak ana ɔɣe Yakob fiɛ Yakob ana ɔɣe nlɛ miweo-minyɔ fiɛ ma ɔɖuɖu ana ɔtu sirɛrɛ̃.
“Yakob mabi ɔbɛbɛ anɔ i ma ɔnyiibi Yosef iso.
Ne ɔso mamɔɛ̃ wũ marɔdɛ̃ matã maturi ma losu wũ makɛlɛgu Egipte karɔ̃ iso.
Ɣɛɛ ne, Ɣaa ɔwegu wũ, fiɛ ɔɖi wũ ɔbɔrɛgu i ɔ̃ inyɛwe ɔɖuɖu ame.
Ɣaa ɔtã wũ abualɛra gu inɔgba wodoroa, ne ɔso Egipte igara ɔsu wũ ɔbara ɔ̃ karɔ̃ ɔɖuɖu gu ɔ̃ iyo nyɔisose.
“Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, kukã siare kuwɛ̃ ɔba i Egipte gu Kanan karɔ̃ ɔɖuɖu iso gɔ ibɔ inyɛwe i bo mawa iso ala mana araɖea.
Gɔ Yakob ɔnɔ sɔ araɖea pia i Egipte ne, ɔpia ɔ̃ mabi sɔ masɛ maaɣa araɖea mabɔ ɔkpɛ ɖeakatɔ̃.
Ne gɔ Yakob mabi ɔkpese makɛlɛ mmɔ ɔkpɛ nyɔa sɔ maaɣa araɖea ne, Yosef ɔɖi so ɔte ma, ne ka ɔɖi ma ɔte Igara Farao ne.
Ne kama ne, Yosef ɔpia ma sɔ masɛ maakɔ ɔ̃ ɔse Yakob gu ɔ̃ manyii ɔɖuɖu mabɔ Egipte gɔ ma ɔɖuɖu aaɖe lɛ maturi sikɔdzɛ-iru.
Ne ɔso Yakob ɔrui ɔkɛlɛ ɔsɛ ɔ̃ɔwe i Egipte mmɔ gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ ɔ̃ gu bo mawa ɔkpi.
Masore ma makpesegu masɛ maabiara i ɔmagɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Sikem.
Mabiara ma i kabiarakɔ̃ ga i Abraham ɔɣa i Hemor mabi kɔrɛ ala sikãfudza.
“Ɔwi gɔ i Ɣaa ɔwi gɔ ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ sɔ ɔ̃abara nnɛ ɔɣere Abraham ɔbore ɔbo ne, bo mawa ɔɔsi gbodzoo i Egipte.
Iba ana sɔ igara ɣɛtɛ gɔ loiɣe Yosef ɔtsɛ iɖe iso i Egipte.
Farao gɔgbe ɔbara bo mawa ɔtile sɔ si ɔwɔra ma.
Ɔtã sɔ masu ma mabi ɣɛtɛ mapɛyu si makpi.
“Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame maɣe Mose ne.
Gɔ ɔ̃ ara ɔbo Ɣaa anɔ ɔso ne, ɔ̃ maɣese ɔsu wũ makɔla i ma iyo manyɔ wũ iso awa atɛ i kuɖokpo.
Gɔ manya sɔ maisibawo wũ ɔkɔla ne, maɖi wũ masɛ i ɔgbami.
Ne Farao ɔbi birɔ̃gomi ɔsɛ ɔ̃ɔnya wũ ɔsu ɔba ɔ̃abara ɔ̃ kayiri ame ɔbi ne.
Ɔla wũ fiɛ mate wũ Egipte maturi kubarara gu ma iwola ɔɖuɖu, ɔwe ɔle i ikaɖe gu kurabara ame.
“Gɔ Mose ɔfɔ akɔ sina ne, iba wũ iti ame sɔ ɔ̃akɛlɛ ɔ̃aya ɔ̃ manyii ma Israelse.
Gɔ ɔsɛ ɔ̃ɔbo ne, ɔnya ɔ Egiptese sɔ ɔto ɔbara ɔ Israelse amumuɣɔ.
Mose ɔkɛlɛ sɔ ɔ̃afɔ ɔ Israelse, ne ɔɖoe ɔ Egiptese gɔmɔ ne.
Mose ɔfɔ ɔɖe sɔ ɔ̃ manyii aanya wũ lɛ ngɔ i Ɣaa ɔpia sɔ ɔba ɔ̃aɖi ma, ɣɛɛ mainya wũ ngbɔ.
Gɔ kaɖe ɔsɛ̃ fiɛ Mose ɔledza ma kɔrɛ isɛ ne, ɔnya gɔ ma Israelse inyɔ to makpɛ̃.
Gɔ ɔkɛlɛ sɔ ɔ̃akpura ma ne, ɔkarɛ ma sɔ, ‘Wũ maturi, manyiibi miɖe, ne ɔso minyua ɔkpɛ̃.’ “Ɣɛɛ ngɔ nto ɔbara ɔ̃ ɔnyii ɔtile ɔli Mose ɔkarɛ ana sɔ ‘Nna lobara-ɔ bo isoɖedze gu atɔ̃meɣɛdze?
Ɛɛbɛrɛ abie sɔ aaɖoe me lɛ kumɛgɔ aɖoe ɔ Egiptese gɔmɔ kɔmakaɖe?’ Gɔ Mose ɔnɔ itɔ̃me nɛgbe ne, ifɔ̃ ɔmɔɛ̃ wũ, ne ɔtere ɔsɛ ɔ̃awɛrɛ i Midian karɔ̃ iso lɛ ɔfɔ ne.
Mmɔ ɔɣe ɔ̃ mabi birɛrɛĩ inyɔ ne.
“Akɔ sina kama ne, Ɣaa kpabo ɔɖi so ɔte wũ i ɔtɔ gɔ nto ɔtsue i kadzirimi kawɛ̃ iso i fafuĩ ame i Sinai kube kɔrɛ.
Gɔ Mose ɔnya ira nɛgbe ne, ibara wũ ɣii, ne ɔso ɔbore ɔbo sɔ si ɔnyɔ kukaakɔ ɣɛɛ, Ɣaa ɔkpere wũ ɔɣere sɔ, ‘Mme nɖe fɔ mawa Abraham gu Isak gu Yakob mɛrɛ̃ Ɣaa ne.’ Iti pɛ̃ gu ifɔ ɔmɔɛ̃ Mose, ne ɔso ɔ̃ibie sɔ ɔ̃anyɔ mmɔ isɛ.
“Ne Bosate to ɔɣere wũ sɔ, ‘Ɖi fɔ ndokota!
Alasɔ karɔ̃ ga iso aɣɛ ne, karɔ̃ sekelea kaɖe.
Gbaã ne, lonya inyɛwe nɛ ame i wũ maturi pia i Egipte karɔ̃ iso.
Nto lonɔ kumɛgɔ mato mabiɛ makpere me.
Ne ɔso loba sɔ si loba loaɖi ma.
Ba, nto lopia-ɔ Egipte.’ “Mose gɔ masɛ̃ fiɛ makarɛ wũ sɔ, ‘Nna loɖi-ɔ bo isoɖedze gu atɔ̃meɣɛdze?’ ne, ɔ̃ ame i Ɣaa ɔpia sɔ ɔsɛ ɔ̃aɖi ma si ɔkpese Ɖidze gu isoɖedze iki i Ɣaa kpabo gɔ ɔnya i kadzirimi ga nto katsue kɔrɛ ne.
Ɔɖi ma ɔbɔrɛgu i Egipte fiɛ ɔbara awawãra gbodzoo i Egipte mmɔ gu Ɔpo Rɛtɛa katɔ̃ ku ɔwi gɔ mawe makiki i fafuĩ ame akɔ-sina buu.
“Mose mɔmɔ ɔɖe loɣere ma Israelse sɔ, ‘Mi Ɣaa to ɔ̃asese mi kanyaɖidze mama lɛ me ɔbɔrɛgu i mi ndɛ̃.’ Mose nɖe ngɔ losa bo mawa kanya ku ɔwi gɔ ma Israelse pia i fafuĩ ame.
Ɔ̃ ame nɖe ngɔ i Ɣaa kpabo ɔɖegu ika i Sinai kube iso ne.
Ɔ̃ ɔɖe lowegu bo mawa fiɛ ɔfɔ Ɣaa itɔ̃me nɛ nsɛ itã ngbã ɔtã bo ne.
“Ɣɛɛ bo mawa ɔta maya Mose iso, masɛ̃ wũ, fiɛ i ma situ ame ne, mabie sɔ si makpese makɛlɛ Egipte karɔ̃ iso.
Ne maɣere Mose ɔnyiibi Aron sɔ, ‘Bara aɣɔ wa loakɔ bo tã bo, alasɔ boiɣe nnɛ lobara Mose gɔ lokɔ bo ɔbɔrɛgu i Egipte.’ Ne ɔso mabara kuɣɔ gɔ nse lɛ inantsuĩbi, mafɛ̃ ara matã kɔ̃, fiɛ matsɛ iyi iɖe ku isoɣɔ i ara wa mabara ngbe ɔso.
Nnɛgbe ɔso i Ɣaa ɔkpese ma i kama fiɛ matsɛ kuɣɛ̃ gu ɔgbaworeti gu awami isɔrɛ ne.
Nnɛgbe i Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze ɔtsɛrɛ i Ɔko Sekelea ame maɣɛ sɔ, ‘Israel kaɖe, iiɖe me misu mabɔi mifɛ̃ ara mitã i akɔ sina wa miwe i fafuĩ ame!
Bowũ ne, misu Molok kuɣɔ iyo gu Romfa iwãmi wa nɖe aɣɔ wa mipɔ sɔ miasɔrɛ.
Ne ɔso nto loatã sɔ maamɔɛ̃ mi sisande makɛlɛgu ta Babilonia kama.’ “Sikati ikpayo nɛ ame i Ɣaa sɛ ɔɖi so ɔte ɔwe i ɔwa mɛrɛ̃ kɔrɛ ku ɔwi gɔ mawe i fafuĩ ame.
Mabara ikpayo nɛgbe lɛ kumɛgɔ i Ɣaa ɔɖi ɔte Mose sɔ abara ne tutuutu.
Akɔ gbodzoo kama ne, Yosua ɔkɔ bo mase ma losore sikati ikpayo nɛgbe masɛ maakpɛ̃gu mma i Ɣaa ɔsa ɔbɔrɛgu i nrɔ̃ mɛgbe iso.
Ikpayo ɔwe i karɔ̃ gagbe iso gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ ibo Igara David ɔwi ame.
Ɣaa ɔwegu David gbaã, ne ɔso David ɔkarɛ Ɣaa sɔ ɔtã wũ ɔri si ɔtsue iyo ɔtã Yakob Ɣaa.
Ɣɛɛ ne, Igara Salomo ɔɖe lotsue iyo nɛmɔ.
Ɣaa kato gu karɔ̃ baradze ɣɛɛ ne, ɔ̃isɛ ɔsɛ i ayo wa i maturi awune ɔtsue ame.
Ɣaa ɔki i ɔ̃ kanyamaɖidze iso ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Kuɖokpo nɖe wũ sigaraiyara, fiɛ karɔ̃ nɖe wũ kukpa kasiakɔ̃.
Ne ɔso mme iyo igbã miawo ɔtsue ɔtã me, ɛɛbɛrɛ lona kasɛkɔ̃?
Iiɖe mme lobara ira biara?’ ” Ne Stefano ɔɣere ma ana sɔ, “Mi matsuelese!
Mitɛ̃ra atsue i Ɣaa itɔ̃me iso lɛ kumɛgɔ i mi mase ɔbara.
Ɔwi biara mita miɣɛ i Siwarã Bielea iso.
Ɣaa kanyaɖidze ɔmele i mi mawa iibie sɔ maaɖoe?
Maɖoe Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze ma loɣɛ masɛ sɔ Ɔsekelea to ɔ̃aba.
Ɔsekelea gɔmɔ ana ne, miɖi wũ mitã maɖoe.
Mi lofɔ Ɣaa mmara mibɔrɛgu i Ɣaa makpabo nrɔɔ̃ ame, ɣɛɛ misɛ̃ me iso ibara.” Mapɛ Stefano Ata.
Gɔ manɔ atɔ̃me wa i Stefano ɔɣɛ i ma iso ne, ma situ ɔta siya gbaã, itã makɛrɛ̃ anyɛ i sikpã ame.
Ɣɛɛ Stefano gɔ ame i Siwarã Bielea ɔyi ɔkɔlɛ ɔ̃ anɔmi ɔnyɔ kato, ne ɔnya Ɣaa ifiɛ gu Yesu gɔ ɔɣɛ i ɔ̃ kuɖearɔ̃ iso.
Ne ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Minyɔ!
Lonya sɔ kuɖokpo ɔbusi, Maturi Awune Ɔbi ɣɛ i Ɣaa kuɖearɔ̃ iso!” Matsɛ sikpabo teteree, matɛ̃ arɔĩ i atsueyoi, matere mamɔɛ̃ wũ.
Ne gɔ mabore wũ maɖi i ɔmagɛ̃ ame ne, matsɛ wũ ata ipɛ, mma lola sila masia wũ iso ɔɖi ma awu siare masɛ i ɔporoporoi ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Saulo ngbatɔ̃.
Ɔwi gɔ mato mapɛ wũ ata ne, Stefano ɔkparama kayi ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Bosate Yesu, fɔ wũ siwarã!” Ne ɔpɛ agɛgɛ̃ ɔla kulu teteree sɔ, “Tete, daasu ikpi nɛgbe atã ma kuso!” Gɔ ɔɣɛ ngbɔ ɔro ne, ɔkpi.
Ɔwi gɔ mato maɖoe Stefano ne, Saulo lola ɔ̃ɔpia ma ɔle.
Saulo Ɔkpɛ̃gu Mafɔɖedze.
Ita i iyi nɛmɔ ne, matsɛ mafɔɖedze ma i Yerusalem ikpɛ̃gu teteree.
Ma ɔɖuɖu ɔtere makɛlɛ Yudea gu Samaria.
Ɣɛɛ katɔ̃memasɛdze ɔwe i Yerusalem.
Mafɔɖedze mawɛ̃ ɔba maasu Stefano masɛ maabiara ku kaku gu imararãso siare.
Saulo ɔsu ɔsia so iso teteree sɔ ɔ̃awɔra mafɔɖedze ikuri.
Ɔsɛ ɔbo i ayo ɔmɔɛ̃ marɛrɛ̃ gu marɔ̃go ɔkɛlɛgu ɔ̃apia i iyo.
Filipo Ɔɣɛ Itɔ̃me Bielea I Samaria.
Mma losame ɔɣɛ Itɔ̃me Bielea i kakɔi biara ga makɛlɛ.
Filipo ɔkɛlɛ Samaria ɔmagɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ame ɔsɛ ɔ̃aɣɛ Kristo iso itɔ̃me i mmɔ.
Maturi gbodzoo ɔkã wũ atsue ala awawãra gbodzoo wa ɔbara fiɛ manya ɔso.
Ɔsa siwarã lalaa ɔɖi i maturi gbodzoo ame.
Sila kulu fiɛ sibɔrɛ i ma ame.
Ɔsa mma lokpi kasɛkasɛ gu mma lofɛfɛ̃ masi i karɔ̃ ana.
Nnɛgbe ɔso ne, isoɣɔ ɔba i Samaria ɔmagɛ̃ ame gbaã!
Ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ pia i Samaria gɔ marɔ Simon.
Ɔɖe wase fiɛ ɔwi gbodzoo ame ngbe ne, ɔ̃ awa ibara sɛ ibara maturi ɣaa.
Ɔbua ɔsɛ ɔkɔlɛ so kato sɔ ɔturi nyaa ɔɖe.
Samaria marɛrɛ̃ gu marɔ̃go gu mabiɛtɛ ɔɖuɖu sɛ mawarɛ wũ ala ɔ̃ kurabarara ɔso.
Ne ɔso maɖe ika i ɔ̃ iso sɔ, “Ɔ̃ nɖe kuɖokpo ikpa!” Kumɛgɔ i ɔ̃ awa ibara ɔfɔ ma ati ame ɔso ne, masɛ makã wũ atsue.
Ɣɛɛ kiniɔ ne, mafɔ Filipo Itɔ̃me Bielea nɛ ɔɣɛ i Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ gu Yesu Kristo iyere maɖe.
Marɛrɛ̃ gu marɔ̃go gbodzoo ɔfɔ Ɣaa itupie kubarara.
Simon ana ɔfɔ ɔɖe, ne ɔso gɔ ɔfɔ Ɣaa itupie kubarara ne, ɔla ɔ̃ɔsiai Filipo ɔsɛ kakɔi biara.
Awawãra wa i Filipo to ɔbara ana ɔbara wũ ɣaa.
Gɔ katɔ̃memasɛdze ma mpia i Yerusalem ɔnɔ sɔ ma Samariase ɔfɔ Ɣaa itɔ̃me ne, mapia Petro gu Yohanes ma kɔrɛ.
Gɔ maba maabo ne, makparama kayi ku mafɔɖedze ɣɛtɛ magbe sɔ mafɔ Siwarã Bielea.
Alasɔ iba iabo ɔwi gɔmɔ ne, maifɔ Siwarã Bielea.
Ɣaa itupie kere maɔfɔ i Bosate Yesu iyere ame.
Petro gu Yohanes ɔsu nrɔɔ̃ masia ma iso, ne mafɔ Siwarã Bielea ne.
Gɔ Simon ɔnya sɔ katɔ̃memasɛdze ne nrɔɔ̃ kere masia ma iso fiɛ mafɔ Siwarã Bielea ne, ɔsu sikã si ɔtã katɔ̃memasɛdze ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mitã sɔ mme wũ loana ɔle gɔgbe sɔ ɔbiara gɔ iso loasia nrɔɔ̃ ne, ɔ̃afɔ Siwarã Bielea.” Ne Petro ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Mi gu fɔ sikã ɔɖuɖu si miwɔ!
Daabu sɔ aawo Ɣaa karatã ɔɣa ku sikã!
Aito aawo karabara gagbe ame ɔwe, alasɔ fɔ ɔtu ame iikpa i Ɣaa anɔ.
Finiki i adzuni nyanyarĩa wagbe ame si akparama kayi, siainyɔ Bosate to ɔ̃asu fɔ ikpi ɔtsɛ-ɔ ala fɔ adzuni iilɛ!
Ala ne, lonya sɔ aba kanɔbɛbɛ, fiɛ ikpi ibara ana ɔyi i fɔ ame.” Ne Simon ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Pɛ Bosate nrɔɔ̃ i wũ iti sɔ ara nyanyarĩa wa aɣɛ ngbe kuiwɛ̃ iibabɔrɛ me iso!” Gɔ Petro gu Yohanes ɔɣɛ Itɔ̃me Bielea i mmɔ maro ne, makpese makɛlɛ Yerusalem gɔ makiki i Samaria simagɛ̃ gbodzoo ame maɣɛ Itɔ̃me Bielea.
Filipo Ɔɖegu Etiopia Ɔkpakpa Ika.
Ɣɛɛ Ɣaa kpabo ɔɣere Filipo sɔ, “Kɛlɛ ɔri gɔ lobɔrɛ i Yerusalem fiɛ ɔki i fafuĩ ame ɔso ɔkpa Gasa iso!” Bielea ɔta ɔkɛlɛ ɔri gɔmɔ iso.
Gɔ ɔsɛ ɔto ɔkɛlɛ ne, ɔsɛ ɔ̃ɔtu ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ nɖe sikã nyɔisose ɔkpakpa i Etiopia igararɔ̃go gɔ marɔ sɔ Kandake sigarakaɖekɔ̃.
Ɔkpakpa gɔgbe ɔbɔrɛ i Yerusalem ɔsɛ ɔkparama kayi.
Gɔ ɔ̃ɔsɛ ɔkpese ɔto ɔkɛlɛ iyo ne, ɔsi i keke gɔ i ipɔngɔ to ikpadzɛ̃ ame ɔto ɔka Ɔko Sekelea gɔ i Ɣaa Kanyaɖidze Yesaya ɔtsɛrɛ.
Ne Siwarã Bielea ɔɣere Filipo sɔ, “Sɛ kɛlɛ si abore abo keke!” Filipo ɔtara ngbã ɔbore ɔmatã wũ, kere ɔnɔ gɔ ɔkpakpa to ɔka Yesaya ɔko.
Ne ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ato anɔ nnɛ ato aka ngbe karɔ̃?” Ne ɔkpakpa gɔgbe ɔtã wũ mmuai sɔ, “Nda loabara loanɔ karɔ̃ gɔ kuwɛ̃ na ɔ̃aɖi karɔ̃ ɔtã me?” Ne ɔtã Filipo iti sɔ ɔya ɔba i keke ame ɔba ɔ̃asɛ i ɔ̃ kɔrɛ ne.
Atɔ̃me wa ɔto ɔka i Ɔko Sekelea ame nɖe sɔ, “Masɛgu wũ lɛ sɛrɛrerɔ̃ gɔ masɛ maaɖoe.
Ɔsiai ma lɛ sɛrɛrerɔ̃ gɔ maakparɛ̃ siwɛrɛ̃ fiɛ ɔ̃ito ɔbiɛ.
Ɔ̃ibusi ɔ̃ kanya ana.
Mapia wũ kunuarɛ, ɣɛɛ ɔ̃ina ngɔ loafɔ wũ kanya.
Ɔna ɔɣekparɛ, Alasɔ maɖoe wũ maɖi i kayi gagbe ame?” Ne ɔkpakpa gɔmɔ to ɔkarɛ Filipo sɔ, “Yesaya ne, ɔ̃ mɔmɔ iso iɖe ɔɖe ika, ɛɛbɛrɛ ɔturi mama iso iɖe?” Filipo ɔsɛ karɔ̃ ɔsu Ɔko Sekelea gɔgbe itɔ̃me ɔɖiɖi Itɔ̃me Bielea karɔ̃ ɔte wũ ise i Yesu iso.
-Gɔ masɛ mato makɛlɛ ne, masɛ maanya itubu gɔ iɣɛ i kakɔi kawɛ̃ i ɔri kuruɛ.
Ne ɔkpakpa gɔmɔ to ɔkarɛ sɔ, “Nyɔ ndu.
Be ɔso loibawo Ɣaa itupie kubarara ɔfɔ?” Ɔtã matindza keke maɣedza, ne ma inyɔɔ ɔso mabo i ndu ame fiɛ Filipo ɔpie wũ ndu ne.
Gɔ mabɔrɛ i ndu ame ne, Bosate Siwarã ɔsu Filipo siruigu, ne ɔso ɔkpakpa gɔgbe iisinya wũ ana.
Ɔ̃ wũ ne, ɔkɛlɛ kaa ku isoɣɔ.
Nnɛgbe kama ne, Filipo ka ɔnya sɔ ɔɣɛ i Azoto ɔmagɛ̃ ame.
Ka ɔɣɛ Ɣaa itɔ̃me i mmɔ gu simagɛ̃ dzɛ mpia i ɔri iso ɔɖuɖu isɛ iabo ta Kaisarea ɔmagɛ̃ ame ana.
Saulo Ɔsu So Ɔtã Yesu.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ɔɖuɖu ne, Saulo to ɔnyɔnyɔ Bosate masiaidze gu anɔmi rɛtɛa sɔ ɔ̃aɖoe.
Ɔkɛlɛ ma Yudase sɔrɛdzekpakpa pelepele kɔrɛ.
Ɔsɛ ɔ̃akarɛ wũ sɔ ɔtã wũ siko dzɛ ɔ̃asu ɔkɛlɛgu ma Yudase kusarɛkɔ̃ i Damasko fiɛ ɔ̃ana ɔle ɔmɔɛ̃ marɛrɛ̃ gu marɔ̃go ma ɔɖuɖu nsiai kafɔkaɖe ɣɛtɛ ɔkɛlɛgu Yerusalem.
Ɔwi gɔ ɔ̃ɔbore ɔbo Damasko ne, ɔluwɛ̃ ikpawaĩ ɔfiɛ ibɔrɛ i kato ifere wũ.
Ɔbɔrɛ ɔfere i karɔ̃, ne ɔnɔ silɔ siwɛ̃ ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Saulo, Saulo, be ɔso fiɛ ato akpɛ̃gu me ngbɔ?” Ne Saulo ɔkarɛ sɔ, “Bosate, fɔ nna aɖe?” Silɔ dzɛmɔ ɣere wũ sɔ, “Mme nɖe Yesu gɔ ato akpɛ̃gu teteree ne.
Kiniɔ ne, kpɛ̃ ta si akɛlɛ ɔmagɛ̃ ame ne mato maaɣere-ɔ nnɛ ikote sɔ aabara.” Marɛrɛ̃ ma nsɛgu Saulo ɔkpɛ̃ so kpara.
Manɔ ikaɖe, ɣɛɛ mainya kuwɛ̃.
Gɔ Saulo ɔta ɔya fiɛ ɔbusi anɔmi ne, ɔ̃isito ɔnya.
Ne ɔso mamɔɛ̃ wũ kɔrɔ̃ makɔ wũ mabogu i Damasko ɔmagɛ̃ ame.
Ɔwe i mmɔ akpɛnɛ atɛ gɔ ɔ̃inya, ɔ̃iɖe ara fiɛ ɔ̃inɛ ndu ana.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, fɔɖedze ɔwɛ̃ pia i Damasko gɔ marɔ Anania.
Bosate ɔɖi so ɔte wũ ɔkpere wũ sɔ, “Anania!” Ne ɔtɔrã wũ sɔ, “Bosate, ɔɔnya me!” Ne Bosate ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ta si aki ɔri gɔ masɛ marɔ sɔ Tɔrɔrɔ iso si akɛlɛ Yuda iyo si akarɛ ɔ Tarsose gɔ marɔ Saulo iti.
Ɔpia i mmɔ ɔto ɔkparama kayi.
Alasɔ loɔɖi lote wũ sɔ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Anania to ɔ̃aba ɔ̃asia wũ nrɔɔ̃ iso fiɛ ɔ̃atsɛ inya.” Mmɔ i Anania ɔɖi kanya sɔ, “Bosate, loɔnɔ i kakɔi biara ɔtile gɔ i ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe to ɔbara mafɔɖedze i Yerusalem!
Fiɛ lonɔ ana sɔ ɔfɔ ɔle ɔbɔrɛgu i masɔrɛdze makpakpa kɔrɛ sɔ ɔ̃aba ɔ̃amɔɛ̃ mafɔɖedze ɔɖuɖu ma mpia i Damasko!” Ɣɛɛ Bosate ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ta si akɛlɛ aabara nnɛ loto loɣere-ɔ.
Alasɔ loɖi Saulo lɛ ngɔ loasu wũ Itɔ̃me Bielea ɔkɛlɛgu mma loiɖe ma Israelse gu magara katɔ̃ gu Israel kaɖe ɔɖuɖu.
Nto loate wũ kumɛgɔ ɔ̃awe inyɛ i wũ iti.” Ne ɔso Anania ɔta ɔkɛlɛ, gɔ ɔbo iyo fiɛ ɔnya Saulo ne, ɔsu kɔrɔ̃ ɔsia wũ iso, ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Wũ ɔnyii Saulo, Bosate Yesu gɔ loɖi so ɔte-ɔ i ɔri iso ne, ɔ̃ lopia me fɔ kɔrɛ sɔ si atsɛ inya si Siwarã Bielea aaba siayi fɔ ame ne.” Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, ibara Saulo lɛ akolo lokpa i ɔ̃ anɔmi iso, ne ɔtsɛ ara inya ne.
Ɔta ɔtã mabara wũ Ɣaa itupie kubarara.
Gɔ ɔɖe aɖera ne, ka ɔna ɔle.
Saulo Ɔɣɛ Itɔ̃me Bielea I Damasko.
Saulo ɔwe i mafɔɖedze ma mpia i Damasko kɔrɛ ayi kɛkɛĩ.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, ɔkɛlɛ ma Yudase kusarɛkɔ̃ ɔtsɛ ma Yesu iso itɔ̃me iɣere sɔ Ɣaa Ɔbi ɔɖe.
Ibara mma ɔɖuɖu lonɔ ɔ̃ itɔ̃me ɣii.
Ne makarɛ so sɔ, “Iiɖe ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ɔɖe mpia ɔto ɔɖoe Yesu masiaidze i Yerusalem ayi wa lofe ɣɛɛ?
Bonɔ ana sɔ mafɔɖedze ɔba ɔmɔɛ̃ i ngbe ɔkɛlɛgu masɔrɛdze makpakpa.” Ɣɛɛ Saulo itɔ̃me iɣɛ ɔwe ɔle ibua fiɛ ɔ̃ ara karɔ̃ iɖi ite sɔ Yesu nɖe Kristo ɔtã sɔ ma Yudase ma mpia i Damasko mmɔ kuwɛ̃ iiwo kuira ɔɣɛ.
Ayi gbodzoo kama ne, ma Yudase ɔsɛ iti ame sɔ maaɖoe wũ.
Ɣɛɛ mayu maɣere Saulo sɔ ngbɔ i mawɛ̃ to mabie sɔ maaɖoe wũ ne.
Matsirise magbe ɔdzuɛ̃ kayogodɔ̃ kasɛ̃ gu anɔwã sɔ si maana wũ maɖoe.
Ɣɛɛ mafɔɖedze ɔsu wũ mapia i kasɛsɛi ga iso mapia ɔwɛ̃ ame fiɛ makigu i iyoi nɛ mpia i ibere ame masora wũ ku kasɛ̃!
Saulo Ɔsɛ Ɔ̃abo Yerusalem Gɔ ɔsɛ ɔ̃abo Yerusalem ne, ɔbie sɔ si ɔbo i mafɔɖedze ma mpia i mmɔ ndɛ̃.
Ɣɛɛ ma ɔɖuɖu to manigã wũ.
Mabu sɔ ɔsɔsɔla ɔto ma sɔ ɔ̃ɔfiniki.
Ne Barnaba ɔkɔ wũ ɔkɛlɛgu katɔ̃memasɛdze kɔrɛ fiɛ ɔɣere ma kumɛgɔ i Saulo ɔsarɛgu Bosate gɔ ɔto ɔkɛlɛ Damasko ne.
Ɔɣere ma nnɛ i Bosate ɔɣere wũ gu Itɔ̃me Bielea nɛ ɔɣɛ ku katetere i Yesu iyere ame i Damasko.
Ne ɔso Saulo ka ɔwe i ma ndɛ̃ faa ɔwi ɔɖuɖu fiɛ ɔɣɛ Bosate itɔ̃me ku kagbegbe i Yerusalem.
Gɔ ma Yudase mawɛ̃ ma nsɛ maɣɛ Griki siɖe gu Saulo ɔtsɛ ikaɖe gu kakpadzɛ̃ ne, mabie sɔ si maɖoe wũ.
Gɔ mafɔɖedze ɔnɔ sɔ mawɛ̃ to mabie sɔ maɖoe wũ ne, makɔ wũ makɛlɛgu Kaisarea fiɛ ka masese wũ kaa ga nɖe Tarso.
Ne ɔso mafɔɖedze ma mpia i Yudea gu Galilea gu Samaria karɔ̃ iso ɔna iwarã gɔ kunigã iisiwe.
Mana ɔtu gu ɔle gɔ lobɔrɛ i Siwarã Bielea ame gɔ itã masi fiɛ masu kuwarɛ matã Bosate.
Petro Ɔkɛlɛ Lida Gu Yopa.
Gɔ Petro pia ɔkiki ɔnyɔ mafɔɖedze i ma simagɛ̃ ame ne, ɔba ɔ̃ɔbo mafɔɖedze ma mpia i ɔmagɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Lida kɔrɛ.
Ɔnya ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Ainea gɔ lofɛfɛ̃ ɔrɛ i ɔkala iso akɔ farafana.
Ne gɔ Petro ɔnya wũ ne, ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ainea, nyɔ!
Yesu Kristo ɔɔsa-ɔ!
Ta ya, si akarĩ fɔ ɔkala.” Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, ɔta ɔya ku isosarɛ.
Gɔ manya sɔ Ainea ɔɔta ɔsɛ ne, Lida gu Saron maturi ɔɖuɖu ɔsu so matã Bosate.
I Yopa ne, ɔrɔ̃go ɔwɛ̃ pia marɔ sɔ Tabita.
I Griki siɖe ame ne, marɔ wũ Dorkas gɔ karɔ̃ nɖe Kuɔ.
Ɔɖe fɔɖedze gɔ mba kayiribielea fiɛ ɔsɛ ɔtã mawɛrɛba ara ɔwi biara.
Ɔba ɔ̃amɔɛ̃ ɔnyɛ kere, ne ɔkpi ne.
Gɔ mapie wũ ndu maledza wũ ne, masɛ wũ i iyo nɛ matsue masia i kato ame.
Gɔ manɔ sɔ Petro ɔba ɔpia i Lida fiɛ iidzorogu Yopa ne, mapia maturi inyɔ sɔ masɛ maapɛ wũ nrɔɔ̃ si ɔsiai ma kukpakukpa ɔba.
Ɔ̃ wũ ɔta ɔsiai ma, ne gɔ ɔba ɔ̃ɔbo ne, makɔ wũ makɛlɛgu iyo nɛ masɛ kpise.
Makpisemare ɔki malɔ Petro mato mabiɛ mate wũ arapia wa i Dorkas ɔkã ɔtã ma ku ɔwi gɔ ɔsi ngbã.
Petro ɔɣere ma ɔɖuɖu sɔ mabɔrɛ i iyo ame, ne ɔpɛ agɛgɛ̃ ɔkparama kayi ne.
Ɔpɛ ɔfiniki ɔnyɔ kpise i katɔ̃ ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Tabita, ta!” Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, ɔbusi anɔmi.
Gɔ ɔnya Petro ne, ɔta ɔsɛ.
Petro ɔmɔɛ̃ wũ i kɔrɔ̃ ɔtara ɔɣedza fiɛ ka ɔkpere mafɔɖedze ɔɖuɖu gu makpisemare sɔ maba, ne ɔtara Dorkas gbanadze ɔpia ma i nrɔɔ̃ ame ne.
Itɔ̃me nɛgbe ɔki ikã Yopa ɔɖuɖu, ne ɔso maturi gbodzoo ɔfɔ Bosate maɖe.
Ne kama ne, Petro ka ɔwe i Yopa ɔmagɛ̃ ame ayi gbodzoo i Simon ɔwɛ̃ gɔ nsɛ ɔbara mabɔi siko karabara kɔrɛ.
Kornelio Ɔpia Petro Ɔturi.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ne, ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɔsɛ i Kaisarea ɔmagɛ̃ ame gɔ marɔ Kornelio.
Ɔkpakpa ɔɖe i ma Romase makpakpɛ̃dze ma marɔ sɔ ma Italiase makpakpɛ̃dze ame.
Ɔɖe ɔturi sɛɛ fiɛ ɔ̃ gu ɔ̃ iyo maturi ɔɖuɖu sɛ manigã Ɣaa.
Ɔsɛ ɔtã mawɛrɛba ara fiɛ ɔsɛ ɔɖɔɛ kayi ikparama ɔwi biara.
Iyi iwɛ̃ ito ikɛlɛ iɖɔwũ itɛ ku kakɔme ne, ɔnya iɖi ite.
Iɖi ite nɛgbe ame ne, ɔnya sɔ Ɣaa kpabo ɔwɛ̃ ɔba ɔ̃ kɔrɛ ɔkpere wũ sɔ, “Kornelio!” Gɔ Kornelio ɔnya wũ ne, ifɔ̃ ɔmɔɛ̃ wũ gbaã.
Ne ɔkarɛ wũ sɔ, “Bosate, be ato abie?” Ne Ɣaa kpabo ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Fɔ kayiribielea ibara gu fɔ kayi ikparama ɔɔbo Ɣaa kɔrɛ.
Pia maturi si makɛlɛ Yopa masɛ maakpere ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Simon Petro mabɔ.
Ɔpia i Simon gɔ nsi i ɔpo katɔ̃ fiɛ ɔsɛ ɔbara mabɔi siko karabara kɔrɛ.” Gɔ Ɣaa kpabo gɔgbe ɔrui ne, Kornelio ɔkpere ɔ̃ iyo maturi inyɔ gu ɔ̃ kpakpɛ̃dze ɔwɛ̃ gɔ nto ɔdzuɛ̃ wũ fiɛ ɔɖe ɔturi sɛɛ.
Ɔɣere ma nnɛ loba, fiɛ ka ɔpia ma sɔ makɛlɛ Yopa.
Kaɖesɛ̃a gɔ masɛ i ɔri mato makɛlɛ fiɛ maɔbore mabo Yopa ne, Petro ɔya ɔkɛlɛ ɔ̃ isã sɔ ɔ̃ɔkparama kayi ku kakɔme iɖɔwũ iweo-inyɔ ame.
Kukã ɔba kuakpɛ̃ wũ teteree, ɣɛɛ ɔwi gɔmɔ ne, kini matsɛ aɖera iwa ne.
Ibara wũ kere lɛ sirɛ ame ɔto ɔbo.
Mmɔ iɖe ɔnya sɔ kuɖokpo ɔbusi, ɔnya ira iwɛ̃ lɛ ɔkati siare gɔ mamɔɛ̃ akpakpai ana mato masora mabɔ karɔ̃.
Ɔkati gɔgbe ame ne, mabɔi agbãagbã, mma nsɛ mabore i karɔ̃ gu mma nsɛ i ngba iso gu kurodzai ana pia.
Ɔnɔ silɔ siwɛ̃ ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Petro, ta si aɖoe si aɖe.” Ne Petro ɔɣɛ sɔ, “Ooɣo!
Iibaba ngbɔ!
Bosate, loiɖe mabɔi ma i bo ma Yudase iisɛ bopɛgu lonya!” Silɔ ɔledza wũ iɣere sɔ, “Ira nɛ i Ɣaa ɔɔsekelera ne, daarɔ ne sɔ iikpa!” Ɔnya iɖi ite nɛgbe ikpɛ itɛ buu.
Ɔkpɛ tɛa ne, masu ɔkati gɔgbe makɛlɛgu kato.
Ira nɛ i Petro ɔnya ɔbara wũ ɣii, ne ɔkarɛ so sɔ, “Be i iɖi ite nɛgbe to ite?” Ɔwi gɔmɔ ana ne, mma i Kornelio ɔpia ɔɔba maabo ɔmagɛ̃ ame.
Ne gɔ manya iyo nɛ mato mabie ne, maba maaya i kayogodɔ̃.
Ne makarɛ si mmɔ i Simon Petro si ne.
Gɔ Petro si ɔto ɔbu iti ame i ɔ̃ iɖi ite iso gu kumɛgɔ ɔ̃abara ɔ̃anɔ karɔ̃ ne, Siwarã Bielea ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Maturi itɛ ɔba mato mabie-ɔ.
Ta si asɛ aanya ma.
Daanigã sɔ aasiai ma akɛlɛ ala me lopia ma.” Ne Petro ɔta ɔkɛlɛ ma kɔrɛ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mme nɖe ngɔ mito mibie.
Wũ kɔrɛ pɔkɔsɔɔ?” Ne maɣere wũ sɔ, “Bo wũ boisɛ ku ikpi, Kornelio gɔ nɖe ma Romase makpakpɛ̃dze ɔkpakpa lopia bo fɔ kɔrɛ.
Ɔturi sɛɛ ɔɖe gɔ nsɛ ɔwarɛ Ɣaa.
Ma Yudase ɔɖuɖu sɛ maɖɔɛ ɔ̃ itɔ̃me gbaã.
Ɣaa kpabo ɔwɛ̃ loɣere wũ sɔ ɔpia si makpere-ɔ si ɔnɔ fɔ kanya ame kutsuɛ.” Ne ɔso Petro ɔtã ma mabo i kawekɔ̃, ɔfɔ ma lɛ ɔ̃ mafɔ awe.
Gɔ kaɖe ɔsɛ̃ ne, ɔ̃ gu mafɔɖedze mawɛ̃ ma lobɔrɛ i Yopa ɔsiai ma makɛlɛ.
Si maasɛ maabo Kaisarea gu kaɖesɛ̃a ne, Kornelio ɔɔsa ɔ̃ iyo maturi kanya gu ɔ̃ malaa masi masia Petro iba.
Gɔ Petro ɔbo kayogodɔ̃ ne, Kornelio ɔpɛ agɛgɛ̃ i Petro katɔ̃, ɔbɔ iti karɔ̃ ɔtã wũ.
Ne Petro ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ta ya!
Mme wũ ɔturi loɖe.” Gɔ mato maɖe ika ne, Kornelio ɔkɔ wũ ɔbogu i iyo fiɛ ɔnya sɔ maturi gbodzoo ɔsakanya.
Ne Petro ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Mi mɔmɔ miɣe sɔ bo ma Yudase mmara iitã me ɔri sɔ loawo ngɔ loiɖe bo aɖe ɔturi iyo ɔbo, ɣee losu so lomatãra i ɔ̃ iso.
Ɣɛɛ Ɣaa ɔɖi ɔte me sɔ lodaanyɔ ɔturi kuwɛ̃ lɛ ɔturi gɔ loikpa.
Ne ɔso fiɛ gɔ maba maakpere me ne, lota loba ne.
Be ɔso fiɛ ato abie me?” Ne Kornelio ka ɔpia kanya ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ka iaɖe lɛ ayi ana ngbe gɔ loto lokparama kayi ku kakɔme.
Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ ɔbɔrɛ me i katɔ̃ gɔ ɔpia ara wa nto afiɛ atsue anɔmi!
Ɔ̃ loɣere me sɔ, ‘Kornelio, fɔ kayiribielea ibara gu fɔ kayi ikparama ɔɖuɖu ɔɔbo Ɣaa kɔrɛ!
Pia maturi si makɛlɛ Yopa si masɛ maakpere Simon Petro gɔ mpia i Simon gɔ nsɛ ɔbara mabɔi siko karabara i ɔpo kanya kɔrɛ.’ Ɔluwɛ̃ ne lopia sɔ maba maakpere-ɔ, fiɛ fɔ wũ abara kukaakɔ sɔ aba ne.
Ne ɔso bosi bosia-ɔ i Ɣaa anɔ ame sɔ ka ba ɣere bo nnɛ i Bosate ɔtã-ɔ sɔ ɣere bo ne.” Petro Ɔɖiɖi Itɔ̃me Bielea Karɔ̃ Ɔte Ma.
Ne Petro ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Loɔnya sekelee sɔ Bosate iisɛ ɔnyɔ maturi i katɔ̃.
Ɣɛɛ i karɔ̃ biara iso ne, ngɔ lonya ɔbɔ so karɔ̃ ɔtã Ɣaa fiɛ ɔsɛ ɔbara ɔ̃ kuɖɔɛ ne, Ɣaa sɛ ɔfɔ wũ.
Lofɔ loɖe sɔ minɔ itɔ̃me nɛ i Ɣaa ɔɣere Israel mabi sɔ, Itɔ̃me Bielea iki Yesu Kristo gɔ nɖe maturi ɔɖuɖu Sate ame boaki boana isobuɛ.
Fiɛ miɣe ara nyaa wa loba i Yudea karɔ̃ iso ɔɖuɖu wa losɛ karɔ̃ i Galilea karɔ̃ iso ita i ɔwi gɔ i Yohanes ɔpɛ imomo i Ɣaa itupie kubarara iso.
Minɔ ana kumɛgɔ i Ɣaa ɔsu Siwarã Bielea ɔsia Yesu gɔ lobɔrɛ i Nasaret ikparĩ fiɛ ɔsu ɔle ana ɔtã wũ.
Ɔwe ɔki ɔbara ara sɛɛ fiɛ ɔsa mma ɔɖuɖu i Ɔbosam to ɔkpɛ̃gu, alasɔ Ɣaa sɛgu wũ.
Ara wa ɔba ɔ̃abara i Israel karɔ̃ iso gu Yerusalem ne, bonya wã ala anɔ.
Mmɔ i maɖoe wũ iki ipɛ wũ imatãra i kudziri iso ne.
Ɣɛɛ ne, Ɣaa ɔledza wũ itara ibɔrɛgu i kukpi ame ku iyi tɛare iso, fiɛ ɔtã sɔ maturi ɔnya wũ.
Iiɖe maturi ɔɖuɖu lonya wũ.
Ɣɛɛ bo ma i Ɣaa ɔɖi ne, bo lonya wũ ne.
Boɖe fiɛ bonɛgu wũ ana i ɔ̃ ita kama.
Bo iɖe i Yesu ɔpia sɔ bosɛ boaɣɛ Itɔ̃me Bielea nɛgbe i kakɔi biara, si boɣere ma sɔ, Ɣaa ɔsu Yesu ɔbara makpise gu manyɔdze atɔ̃meɣɛdze.
Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze ɔɖuɖu ɔtsɛrɛ i ɔ̃ iso sɔ ɔturi biara gɔ loafɔ wũ ɔɖe ne, Ɣaa to ɔ̃asu ɔ̃ akpi ɔtsɛ wũ i Yesu iyere ame.” Siwarã Bielea Ɔbo I Mma Loiɖe Ma Yudase Ana Ame.
Ɔwi gɔ i Petro ɣɛ ɔto ɔɣɛ atɔ̃me wagbe ne, Siwarã Bielea ɔso sifere mma nsi mato makã wũ atsue ɔɖuɖu iso!
Ma Yudase fɔɖedze ma losiai Petro masɛ mmɔ ne, nnɛgbe ɔbara ma ɣaa, alasɔ Siwarã Bielea ɔba i mma loiɖe ma Yudase iso.
Manɔ mma loiɖe ma Yudase to maɣɛ siɖe agbãagbã male Ɣaa.
Ne Petro ɔkarɛ sɔ, “Gɔ maɔfɔ Siwarã Bielea lɛ kumɛgɔ bo wũ bofɔ ne, boibawo ma ɔri ɔtɛ̃ sɔ madaafɔ Ɣaa itupie.” Ne ɔso ɔtã sɔ mapie ma ndu i Yesu Kristo iyere ame.
Ne kama ne, mapɛ Petro nrɔɔ̃ sɔ ɔwegu ma ayi kɛkɛĩ.
Petro Ɔɖi Ara Karɔ̃ Ɔte Yerusalem Mafɔɖedze.
Katɔ̃memasɛdze gu mafɔɖedze ma i Yudea ɔnɔ sɔ mma loiɖe ma Yudase ana ɔɔfɔ Ɣaa itɔ̃me.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ Petro ɔkpese ɔkɛlɛ Yerusalem ne, ma Yudase fɔɖedze mawɛ̃ ɔtsɛgu wũ atɔ̃me ikpadzɛ̃gu, mabie sɔ mma loiɖe ma Yudase fiɛ mafiniki si matu sirɛrɛ̃.
Maɣere wũ sɔ, “Asɛ aabara mawɛ̃ ku mafɔ ma loitu sirɛrɛ̃ fiɛ apia kɔrɔ̃ aɖegu ma aɖera i irɔi ame!” Ne Petro ɔɖiɖi ara wagbe ɔɖuɖu karɔ̃ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Gɔ lopia i Yopa nto lokparama kayi ne, lɛ sirɛ nto lorɛ ne, lonya kaɖikate.
Lonya kato ɔbusi fiɛ ira nɛ nse lɛ ɔkati siare gɔ mamɔɛ̃ akpakpai ana i kato ɔso ɔba i karɔ̃ i wũ kɔrɛ.
Gɔ lonyɔ ɔ̃ ame ne, lonya ayo ame mabɔi gu mabɔi lalaa, ma nsɛ masɛ i ngba iso, mma nsɛ mabore i karɔ̃ gu kurodzai.
Lonɔ silɔ ɔɣere me sɔ, ‘Petro!
Ta si aɖoe mawɛ̃ si aɖe.’ “Ne loɖi kanya sɔ, ‘Bosate, ooɣo!
Iibaba ngbɔ!
Loiɖe mabɔi ma i bo ma Yudase iisɛ bopɛgu lonya.’ “Ɣɛɛ silɔ dzɛgbe ɔledza iɣɛ sɔ, ‘Ira nɛ i Ɣaa ɔɔsekelera ne, daaɣɛ sɔ iikpa.’ Ibara ngbɔ ikpɛ itɛ buu.
Ne kama ne, makpesegu ɔkati siare gɔgbe gu mabɔi i kame makɛlɛgu kato.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame tutuutu ne, maturi itɛ ma mapia mabɔrɛgu i Kaisarea sɔ maba maakpere me mabɔ ɔɔba maɣɛ i iyo nɛ ame lopia kayogodɔ̃.
