Siwarã Bielea ɔɣere me sɔ lota losiai ma ne lodaanigã.
Ne ɔso mafɔɖedze ikuɔ mawɛ̃ magbe ɔta masiai me fiɛ bokɛlɛ ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔ lopia me ɔturi iyo.
Ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ɔɣere bo sɔ, ‘Ɣaa kpabo ɔwɛ̃ ɔɖi so ɔte wũ i ɔ̃ iyo ɔɣere wũ sɔ ɔpia maturi Yopa si masɛ maakpere ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ sɔ Simon Petro.
Ɔ̃ loaɣere-ɔ nnɛ i mi gu fɔ iyo maturi ɔɖuɖu aabara fiɛ miana iɖi ne.’ “Ne kama ne, lotsɛ ma Itɔ̃me Bielea iɣere.
Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, Siwarã Bielea ɔba siayi ma ame lɛ kumɛgɔ siba bo iso ku karɔ̃kasɛkɔ̃!
Mmɔ lonyigi nnɛ i Bosate ɔɣere bo sɔ, ‘Gbagbaã ne, Yohanes ɔsu ndu ɔpie maturi.
Ɣɛɛ ne, Ɣaa to ɔ̃asu Siwarã Bielea ɔpie mi.’ Gɔ Ɣaa lotã mma loiɖe ma Yudase karatã ga ame ɔsu ɔtã bo ku ɔwi gɔ bofɔ Bosate Yesu Kristo boɖe ne, mme nɖe nna fiɛ loatɛ̃ Ɣaa ɔri?” Gɔ manɔ atɔ̃me wagbe ne, manyua ma kakpadzɛ̃, ne matsɛ Ɣaa ile iɣɛ sɔ, “Gbaã ne, Ɣaa ɔɔtã mma loiɖe ma Yudase ɔri sɔ maaba ɔ̃ kɔrɛ fiɛ maana ngbã.” Antiokia Mafɔɖedze Ɔsi Mabua.
Ɔwi gɔ i ara wagbe to aba ne, mafɔɖedze ma lotere inyɛwe nɛ loba ma iso iki i Stefano iɖoe ame ɔsɛ maabo Foinike gu Kipro gu Antiokia ame.
Makiki mato maɣɛ Itɔ̃me Bielea.
Ɣɛɛ ne, ma Yudase kere mato maɣere.
Ɣɛɛ mafɔɖedze mawɛ̃ ma lobɔrɛ i Kipro gu Kirene ɔkɛlɛ Antiokia sɔ maaɣere mma loiɖe ma Yudase Bosate Yesu iso itɔ̃me.
Kumɛgɔ i Bosate ɔle piagu ma ɔso ne, maturi gbodzoo ɔfiniki mafɔ Bosate maɖe.
Gɔ mafɔɖedze ma i Yerusalem ɔnɔ ara wa nto aba i mmɔ ne, mapia Barnaba sɔ ɔkɛlɛ Antiokia.
Gɔ ɔbo mmɔ fiɛ ɔnya kumɛgɔ i Ɣaa nnyainyɔ piagu ma ne, so ɔɣɔ wũ gbaã, ne ɔpia ma ɔtɔ ɔbua sɔ mawe i Bosate ame teteree ku ma situ ɔɖuɖu ne.
Barnaba ɖe ɔturi sɛɛ gɔ mba kafɔkaɖe, fiɛ Siwarã Bielea ɔyi ɔ̃ ame.
Iki i ɔ̃ ibuai ame ne, mafɔɖedze ɔba maasi gbodzoo.
Barnaba ɔkɛlɛ Tarso sɔ ɔ̃abie Saulo.
Gɔ ɔnya wũ ne, ɔkɔ wũ ɔbɔ Antiokia, fiɛ ma inyɔɔ ɔwe i mmɔ ikɔ iwɛ̃ buu.
Mawe i mmɔ mate maturi gbodzoo ara.
Antiokia mmɔ iɖe maɖe katɔ̃ makpere mafɔɖedze sɔ Kristo mare ne.
Ayi wamɔ ame ne, Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze mawɛ̃ ɔbɔrɛ i Yerusalem maba Antiokia.
Ma ɔwɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Agabo ɔta ɔya i Siwarã Bielea ɔle ame ɔɣɛ sɔ kukã siare to kuabo kayiiso ɔɖuɖu.
Nnɛgbe ɔba ngbɔ ku ɔwi gɔ i Klaudio to ɔɖe sigara.
Ne ɔso mafɔɖedze ma i Antiokia ɔsia ita sɔ maato ara i ɔbiara ɔle kanya masese manyii ma mpia i Yudea.
Gɔ masa ara wagbe kanya ne, masu matã Barnaba gu Saulo sɔ masu makɛlɛgu mafɔɖedze makpakpa i Yerusalem.
Herodes Ɔkpɛ̃gu Katɔ̃memasɛdze.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, Igara Herodes ɔtsɛ mafɔɖedze mawɛ̃ kama iti si ɔbara ma ɔtile.
Ɔtã maɖoe Yakobo gɔ nɖe Yohanes ɔnyiibi ala ipɛmi.
Gɔ ɔnya sɔ nnɛ ɔbara ɔwe ma Yudase ɔmɛrɛ̃ ne, ɔtã mamɔɛ̃ Petro ana ku ɔwi gɔ nɖe Boɖoboɖo Gɔ Loita Iyi ɔɖewi.
Masu wũ mapia i iyo nɛ i madzuɛ̃se ina akuri ana wa nsɛ manyuarã so to madzuɛ̃ ame.
Herodes adzuni loɖe sɔ ɔ̃aɖi wũ ɔtã ɔ̃ maturi maɣɛgu atɔ̃me i itiri ku iyi nɛ masɛ marɔ sɔ Kukpi Ɔtakuwara Bo Iyi iɖe kama.
Gɔ Petro rɛ i iyo ne, mafɔɖedze ɔkparama kayi i ɔ̃ iti teteree.
Ɣaa Ɔɖi Petro I Kugbagɔrɔĩ Ame.
Iyi nɛ kaɖesɛ̃a i Herodes aaɖi Petro ɔtã maɣɛgu atɔ̃me kasɛ̃ ame ne, Petro rɛ i madzuɛ̃se inyɔ ndɛ̃ ɔto ɔrɛ sirɛ.
Mapia wũ i kugbagɔrɔĩ kunyɔ ame i madzuɛ̃se inyɔ ndɛ̃, fiɛ madzuɛ̃se mawɛ̃ ana ɣɛ i kayogodɔ̃.
Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, Ɣaa kpabo ɔwɛ̃ ɔba ɔ̃ɔya i Petro kɔrɛ.
Ikpawaĩ ɔfiɛ ibo i iyo ame, ne ɔpɛ Petro iwãgɛsɛ ɔtara sɔ, “Ta ya mala!” Kugbagɔrɔĩ gɔ mpia wũ i nrɔɔ̃ kere lokpase kuse i karɔ̃.
Kpabo gɔgbe ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Nyi so kafiami si apia fɔ ndokota!” Petro ɔbara ngbɔ.
Ne kpabo ɔledza wũ iɣere sɔ, “Su fɔ awu tagbaraa pia si asiai me!” Ne Petro ɔbɔrɛ ɔsiai wũ ne.
Ɔwi gɔgbe ame ɔɖuɖu ne, ito ibara wũ lɛ kurɛ ɔto ɔsɛ̃, ɔ̃itsue sɔ gbaã iɖe Maki mabɔrɛ i kayogodɔ̃ ɖeakatɔ̃ gu kanyɔare ame gu kɔ̃ madzuɛ̃se ndɛ̃.
Gɔ masɛ maabo ibɔra kukui gɔ nɖe kayogɔdɔ̃ siare ga losese kabo i ɔmagɛ̃ ame ne, kã mɔmɔ ɔsese so.
Maki mabɔrɛ i mmɔ ana.
Gɔ mata masia i ɔri ɔwɛ̃ iso masɛ kɛkɛĩ ne, Ɣaa kpabo gɔmɔ ɔyu i Petro anɔ.
Gɔ Petro ɔba ɔ̃atsue nnɛ loba ne, ɔɣere so sɔ, “Gbagbaã ne, Bosate lopia ɔ̃ kpabo sɔ ɔba ɔ̃ɔɖi me ɔbɔrɛgu i Herodes nrɔɔ̃ ame gu ara wa i ma Yudase ɔbu sɔ maabara me ame!” Gɔ Petro ɔbu nnɛ loba ne, ɔrui ɔkɛlɛ Maria gɔ nɖe Yohanes gɔ marɔ ana sɔ Marko ɔnyi iyo.
Mmɔ i mafɔɖedze gbodzoo ɔsakanya mato makparama kayi ne.
Gɔ ɔkpukpura ɔkpã kayogodɔ̃ ga nsɔ̃ ɔri ne, ɔɖabo birɔ̃gomi gɔ marɔ Roda ɔba sɔ ɔba ɔ̃asese.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ ɔnɔ Petro silɔ ɔɖi ite ne, isoɣɔ lala ɔmɔɛ̃ wũ ɔso ɔ̃isese iyo.
Ɔtere ɔkɛlɛ ɔ̃ maturi kɔrɛ ɔsɛ ɔ̃aɣere ma sɔ Petro ɔɔba ɔɣɛ i kayogodɔ̃.
Ɣɛɛ maifɔ maɖe.
Makarɛ wũ sɔ, “Ɔlala ato?” Ɣɛɛ gɔ ɔtogu isɛ̃ ipia ma sɔ gbaã iɖe ne, maɣere so sɔ, “Siainyɔ ɔ̃ Ɣaa kpabo ɔɖe loɔba ɔɣɛ i mmɔ.” Ɔwi gɔgbe ɔɖuɖu ame ne, Petro ɣɛ i mmɔ ɔtogu kukui ikpukpura.
Gɔ masɛ maasese kukui fiɛ manya wũ ne, ibara ma ɣii!
Gɔ ɔlora ma ala kɔrɔ̃ ne, ɔɣere ma ara wa loba gu kumɛgɔ i Bosate ɔba ɔ̃aɖi wũ ɔbɔrɛgu i iyo.
Ɔɣere ma sɔ maɣere Yakobo gu matsɔra nnɛ loba.
Ne kama ne, ɔrui i mmɔ ɔkɛlɛ kakɔi mama.
Gɔ kaɖe ɔsɛ̃ ne, ikpɔkpɔtɔ siare ɔbo i madzuɛ̃se ndɛ̃ alasɔ maiɣe nnɛ lobɔrɛ Petro iso.
Gɔ Herodes ɔnyɔnyɔ Petro kukaakɔ fiɛ ɔ̃inya wũ ne, ɔtã mamɔɛ̃ madzuɛ̃se mamɔ mabɔ wũ.
Gɔ ɔɣɛgu ma atɔ̃me ne, ɔtã sɔ maɖoe ma.
Ne kama ne, Herodes ɔrui i Yudea ɔkɛlɛ Kaisarea sɔ ɔ̃asɛ i mmɔ kɛkɛĩ.
Igara Herodes Ɔkpi.
Ɔwi gɔmɔ ame ne, kulu ɔwe i Herodes gu Tiro gu ma Sidonse ndɛ̃.
Mapia makpabo mabɔrɛgu i Tiro gu Sidon sɔ masɛ maanya wũ.
Gɔ masɛ ne, makarɛ ibuai mabɔrɛgu i Blasto gɔ nɖe Herodes ɔɖabo kɔrɛ sɔ ɔtã Herodes iti ɔtã ma si mafere kanya ndu i ma simagɛ̃ gu Herodes ndɛ̃ alasɔ Herodes karɔ̃ iso i ma aɖera sɛ abɔrɛ.
Iyi nɛ i Igara Herodes ɔsɛ ma sɔ maba ne, ɔpia ɔ̃ agagã gu ɔ̃ sigara ara fiɛ ɔsɛ i ɔ̃ sigaraiyara iso ɔtsɛ ika iɖe.
Gɔ ɔɖe ika ɔro ne, maturi ɔla kulu maɣɛ sɔ, “Ɣaa silɔ siɖe ngbe ne iiɖe ɔturi sire siɖe!” Ɔluwɛ̃ ne, Ɣaa kpabo ɔtã Herodes ɔbo ɔnyɛ, alasɔ ɔ̃isu ile ɔtã Ɣaa.
Makorogbarɛ ɔwe wũ fiɛ ɔkpi.
Bosate Itɔ̃me Bielea ɔɣa gbaã, itã sɔ mafɔɖedze ana ɔsi mabua.
Gɔ Barnaba gu Saulo ɔro ma karabara ga mapia ma ɔbara ne, marui i Yerusalem fiɛ makɔ Yohanes gɔ marɔ ana sɔ Marko maruigu.
Mapia Barnaba Gu Saulo Katɔ̃me.
I Antiokia ne, Bosate kanyamaɖidze gu maratedze ɔwe i mafɔɖedze ikuri ame.
Ma nɖe Barnaba gu Simon gɔ marɔ Ɔturi Kpinakpina gu Lukio gɔ lobɔrɛ i Kirene gu Manaen gɔ nɖe Igara Herodes sibiɛtɛ ame ɔlaa gu Saulo.
Gɔ mapia mato manyi kanya male Ɣaa ne, Siwarã Bielea ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Miɖi Barnaba gu Saulo misɛ mitã karabara ga ɔso lokpere ma.” Gɔ manyi kanya, makparama kayi i ma iti ne, masia ma nrɔɔ̃ iso, ne maɖi ma ɔri ne.
Barnaba Gu Saulo Ɔkɛlɛ Kipro.
Gɔ Siwarã Bielea ɔɖi Barnaba gu Saulo ɔri ne, makɛlɛ ɔmagɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Seleukia.
Mmɔ iɖe masɛ maasu ɔkolo mawara makɛlɛ karɔ̃ ga i ndu ɔki milɔ marɔ sɔ Kipro iso ne.
Gɔ masɛ maabo ɔmagɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Salami ame ne, makɛlɛ ma Yudase kusarɛkɔ̃ masɛ maaɣɛ Bosate itɔ̃me.
Marko Yohanes ana siai ma lɛ ma buaidze.
Nnɛgbe kama ne, mafe makɛlɛ ɔmagɛ̃ gɔ marɔ Pafo.
Mmɔ iɖe masarɛgu ɔ Yudase gɔ marɔ Bar-Yesu.
Ɔsɛ ɔpɛ sibɔ fiɛ ɔɖe mila kanyaɖidze.
Wase gɔgbe gu abã ɔkpakpa gɔ marɔ Sergio Paulo ne, malaa maɖe.
Ɔkpakpa nɔgbadze gɔgbe ɔpia sɔ makpere Barnaba gu Saulo mabɔ si ɔnya ma, alasɔ ɔto ɔbie sɔ ɔnɔ Ɣaa itɔ̃me.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ masɛ ne, wase gɔ masɛ marɔ ana sɔ Elima i Griki siɖe ame ne, ɔkpadzɛ̃gu ma atɔ̃me.
Ɔbie sɔ si ɔfinikira ɔkpakpa adzuni i itɔ̃me nɛ i Saulo gu Barnaba ɔba maɣɛ iso.
Ɣɛɛ Saulo gɔ masɛ marɔ Paulo ana fiɛ Siwarã Bielea ɔyi i ɔ̃ ame ɔnyɔ Elima totoroo ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Fɔ Satana ɔbi, ayigu mila gu kasɔla fiɛ atsiri ira sɛɛ, mme ɔwi aanyua ita iya i Ɣaa ɔnukuare iso?
Bosate to ɔ̃akpadzɛ̃-ɔ kutsue ɔtã sɔ fɔ anɔmi aabiɛ, aisibanya kuɣɛ̃ gbɔgbɔɔgbɔ iafɔ ɔwi!” Ɔluwɛ̃ ɔ̃ anɔ ko lobara wũ guduu ɔ̃isito ɔnya ɔtsɛ nrɔɔ̃ ilala ibie maturi sɔ mamɔɛ̃ wũ kɔrɔ̃.
Gɔ abã ɔkpakpa ɔnya nnɛ loba ne, Bosate Itɔ̃me Bielea ite ɔbara wũ ɣaa, ne ɔso ɔfɔ ɔɖe.
Barnaba Gu Saulo Ɔkɛlɛ Atiokia I Pisidia.
Paulo gu mma nsiai wũ ɔbo i ɔkolo ame marui i Pafo makɛlɛ Perge ɔmagɛ̃ gɔ mpia i Pamfilia.
Mmɔ i Marko Yohanes ɔkpese ma i kama ɔkɛlɛ Yerusalem ne.
Gɔ mabɔrɛ i Perge ne, makɛlɛ Antiokia ɔmagɛ̃ i Pisidia kumɛ iso.
Iwarãyi iso ne, makɛlɛ ma Yudase kasarɛkɔ̃ masɛ maasɛ i karɔ̃.
Ɔwi gɔ maɔka ara mabɔrɛgu i Mose mmara ɔko gu Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze ara itsɛrɛ ame maro ne, kasarɛkɔ̃ matɔ̃ɖedze ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Manyii, si mi ɔrere ba itɔ̃me nɛ loapia bo ɔle ne, ɔba ɔ̃aɣɛ.” Ne Paulo ɔta ɔkɔlɛ kɔrɔ̃ ɔɣere ma sɔ, “Ma Israelse gu mi mma loiɖe ma Israelse ɔɖuɖu, mi mma nsɛ mawarɛ Ɣaa ne, mikã atsue si minɔ!
Ɣaa gɔ i ma Israelse sɛ manigã ɔɖi bo mawa fiɛ ɔkɔlɛ ma kato ɔbara ma kaɖe siare ɔwi gɔ maɖe mafɔ i Egipte.
Ɔ̃ mɔmɔ loɖi ma ɔbɔrɛgu i sisande ame i Egipte karɔ̃ iso ku ɔ̃ ɔle.
Ɔnyɔ ma iso i fafuĩ ame gɔ mawe makiki i akɔ sina ame.
Gɔ ɔwɔra abuiti akɔdzɛ maturi ma i Kanan ne, ɔsu ma nrɔ̃ ɔtã ma Israelse lɛ ma kaɖekɔ̃ awe.
Ara wagbe ɔɖuɖu ɔba lɛ akɔ alafa ana gu siru ame.
“Ne kama ne, Ɣaa ɔtã ma atɔ̃memaɣɛdze ma loɖe ma iso isɛ iabo kanyaɖidze Samuel ɔwi.
Ne matã wũ iti sɔ ɔsɛra igara ɔtã ma.
Ɣaa ɔtã ma Kis ɔbi Saulo gɔ lobɔrɛ i Benyamin ɔɣekparɛ ame, fiɛ ɔɖe sigara akɔ sina.
Ɣɛɛ Ɣaa ɔtara wũ i iyara iso fiɛ ɔsu David ɔsɛra i ɔ̃ kanya.
David gɔgbe nɖe ngɔ iso i Ɣaa ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Yese Ɔbi David nɖe ɔturi gɔ ara lomɔɛ̃ me ɔtu, alasɔ ɔto ɔ̃abara wũ kuɖɔɛ.’ “David gɔgbe ɔɣekparɛ ame ne, Ɣaa ɔɖi Ɖidze gɔ nɖe Yesu gɔ ɔtã ma Israelse lɛ kumɛgɔ ɔkã ndamu ɔtã bo ne.
Si Yesu aaba ne, Ndupiedze Yohanes ɔba ɔ̃aɣere ɔturi biara i Israel sɔ ɔfiniki ɔbɔrɛ i ɔ̃ akpi ame si ɔsu ɔ̃ anɔ ɔsia i Ɣaa iso si ɔtã mapie wũ ndu.
Ɔwi gɔ i Yohanes karabara ɔɔbo kawirikɔ̃ ne, ɔkarɛ sɔ, ‘Mibu sɔ mme nɖe Mesia?
Ooɣo!
Ɔsiai me i kama ɔto ɔba, fiɛ loikote sɔ loasɛ i ɔ̃ ngbatɔ̃ ɖuɖuuɖu.’ “Manyii, mi ma nɖe Abraham mabi gu mi ma loiɖe ma Yudase ɣɛɛ misɛ miwarɛ Ɣaa ne, mikã atsue si minɔ!
Iɖi nnɛgbe ne, bo ɔɖuɖu ire iɖe!
Mma mpia i Yerusalem gu ma makpakpa iitsue sɔ Yesu nɖe Ɖidze gɔ boto bonyɔ ɔri.
Mainɔ Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze ara wa maɣɛ masɛ fiɛ masɛ maka ku iwarãyi biara iso karɔ̃.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ matã wũ kukpi ipɔ ne, matã sɔ kanyamaɖidze atɔ̃me ɔba i ne ame.
Mainyagu wũ ikpi kuiwɛ̃ nɛ ɔso maatã wũ kukpi ipɔ, ɣɛɛ maɣere Pilato sɔ ɔɖoe wũ.
Gɔ maɔbara ara wa ɔɖuɖu i Ɔko Sekelea ɔɣɛ ɔsɛ i ɔ̃ kukpi iso maro ne, mabɛse wũ i kudziri iso masɛ maabiara i ikpibiɔ ame.
Ɣɛɛ Ɣaa ɔtara wũ ɔɖi i makpise ndɛ̃ ɔpia ngbã.
Ne kama ne, ma gu mma lobɔrɛ i Galilea makɛlɛ Yerusalem ɔnya wũ ɔwi gbodzoo.
Mmamɔ nɖe ɔ̃ maɖansiɛ matã ma Israelse ne.
“Ɣaa ndamu mɛ ɔkã ɔtã bo mawa ne, me Itɔ̃me Bielea bosu bobɔ mi si miatsue sɔ Ɣaa ɔbara i ɔ̃ ndamu iso ɔtã bo.
Ne ɔso i Ɣaa ɔtara Yesu ɔbɔrɛgu i makpise ame ɔtã bo lɛ kumɛgɔ i David ɔtsɛrɛ i ɔ̃ kuka nyɔare ame sɔ Ɣaa ɔɣɛ i Yesu iso sɔ, ‘Wũ Ɔbi aɖe.
fiɛ nɔme lokpese fɔ ɔse.’ Gɔ Ɣaa ɔtara Yesu ɔbɔrɛgu i makpise ame sɔ ɔ̃ibaburi ɔnya lɛ kumɛgɔ i Ɣaa ɔɣɛ i ɔ̃ iso sɔ, ‘Loatã-ɔ wũ kusɛkusɛ sekelea ndamu mɛ lokã lotã David.’ Fiɛ ana ne, ɔɣɛ i David kuka mama ame sɔ, ‘Aibatã sɔ fɔ Ɔturi Sekelea aaburi ɔwe i ikpibiɔ ame.’ “Iiɖe David itɔ̃me nɛgbe to, alasɔ gɔ ɔ̃ɔsɛ ngbã ɔbara Ɣaa mɔmɔ kuɖɔɛ ne, ɔkpi mabiara wũ, fiɛ ɔ̃ sosina ana ɔburi.
Ɣɛɛ Yesu gɔ i Ɣaa ɔtara ɔbɔrɛgu i makpise ame ne, ɔ̃ sosina iiburi.
“Manyii, mikã atsue!
Iki i Yesu gɔgbe iyere ame ne, Ɣaa to ɔ̃asu mi akpi ɔtsɛ mi.
Ɔbiara gɔ lofɔ Yesu ɔɖe ne, Ɣaa to ɔ̃atã wũ ibɛ.
Ira nɛ i Mose mmara iiwo ɔbara Ne ɔso minyɔ kukaakɔ!
Midaatã sɔ Ɣaa kanyamaɖidze atɔ̃me wa maɣɛ masɛ aaba mi iso.
Alasɔ Ɣaa ɔɣɛ sɔ, ‘Mi mma loisɛ miwarɛ wũ itɔ̃me ne, minyɔ kukaakɔ ito iabara mi ɣaa fiɛ miawɔ!
Alasɔ loto loabara ira iwɛ̃ i mi ɔwi ame gɔ si minɔ ɣee maɣere mi ne, miibafɔ miɖe.’ ” Ɔwi gɔ Paulo gu Barnaba to marui i kasarɛkɔ̃ ne, maturi ɔɣere ma sɔ maledza ikpese iba iaɖe ma ika i ara wagbe iso ku iwarãyi nɛ loaba iso.
Gɔ masame ne, ma Yudase gbodzoo gu mma lofiniki makpese ma Yudase fiɛ masɛ manigã Ɣaa i kasarɛkɔ̃ mmɔ ɔsiai Paulo gu Barnaba.
Maka ma kumɛgɔ maaya teteree i Ɣaa nnyainyɔ nɛ ɔsu ɔtã ma ngbe ame.
Iwarãyi nɛ ka losiai nnɛmɔ ne, ikuti kɛkɛĩ tee kaɖe gamɔ maturi ɔɖuɖu ɔsɛ kasarɛkɔ̃ sɔ maanɔ Bosate itɔ̃me.
Gɔ ma Yudase makpakpa ɔnya maturi kposu ma loba kasarɛkɔ̃ ne, ma anɔmi ɔrɛtɛ ne matsɛ kakpadzɛ̃ ku Paulo mato maɣɛ atsuɛ pɛ̃ i nnɛ ɔto ɔɣɛ iso.
Ne Paulo gu Barnaba ɔɣere ma ku kagbegbe sɔ, “Mi ma Yudase ikote sɔ boaɣere Itɔ̃me Bielea nɛgbe tɔtɔ.
Ɣɛɛ ngbɔ minɔ ne fiɛ misɛ̃ sɔ miito mifɔ ngbã mɛ nna katui itɔ̃me nɛgbe ne, bosu ne botã mma loiɖe ma Yudase.
Nnɛgbe nɖe katɔ̃me ga i Ɣaa ɔpia bo sɔ, ‘Loasu-ɔ lobara ɔkaniɛ lotã mma loiɖe ma Yudase si aasu iɖi nɛgbe abɔ kayiiso ɔɖuɖu.’ ” Gɔ mma loiɖe ma Yudase ɔnɔ nnɛ maɣɛ ne, so ɔɣɔ ma male Bosate Itɔ̃me.
Mma ɔɖuɖu i Bosate ɔɖi ɔtã ngbã ɔfiniki makpese mafɔɖedze.
Bosate itɔ̃me ɔki ikã karɔ̃ gamɔ iso ɔɖuɖu.
Ma Yudase ɔnina ɔmagɛ̃ makpakpa gu marɔ̃go mawɛ̃ ma mba kawarɛtɔ̃ fiɛ masɛ manigã Ɣaa adzuni, ne ɔso kulu ɔba i ma gu Paulo mɛrɛ̃ ndɛ̃, masa ma maɖi ta ma ibuiti ame.
Paulo gu Barnaba ɔkpakpa ma ngba sise mafere i ɔmagɛ̃ ame si ite sɔ ɔmagɛ̃ gɔmɔ maturi ɔsɛ̃ ma.
Ne kama marui makɛlɛ Ikonion.
Ɣɛɛ mafɔɖedze ma i Antiokia ne, so ɔɣɔ ma fiɛ Siwarã Bielea ɔyi ma ame gbaã!
Paulo Gu Barnaba Ɔbo Ikonion.
Gɔ mabo Ikonion ana ne, Paulo gu Barnaba ɔkɛlɛ ma Yudase kasarɛkɔ̃.
Ne gɔ maɣere ma Yudase gu mma loiɖe ma Yudase Itɔ̃me Bielea ne, ma gbodzoo ɔfɔ maɖe.
Ma Yudase ma loifɔ Bosate itɔ̃me maɖe ɔsu kakpadzɛ̃ mapia i mma loiɖe ma Yudase gu Paulo gu Barnaba ndɛ̃.
Ɣɛɛ katɔ̃memasɛdze ɔwe i ɔmagɛ̃ gɔgbe ame ɔwi kɛkɛĩ.
Mawe kafɔkaɖe i Bosate ame fiɛ maɣɛ Itɔ̃me Bielea gu ɔle.
Ɣaa ana ɔki i awawãra gbodzoo wa mabara ame ɔsia ita sɔ nnyainyɔ itɔ̃me nɛ mato maɣɛ ne, gbaã iɖe.
Itã sɔ ɔmagɛ̃ ame maturi ɔɣɛ so aka anyɔ.
Mawɛ̃ ɔsiai ma Yudase, fiɛ mawɛ̃ ana ɔsiai katɔ̃memasɛdze.
Gɔ mma loiɖe ma Yudase gu ma Yudase gu ma makpakpa ɔta sɔ maabara katɔ̃memasɛdze ɔtile fiɛ maapɛ ma ata ne, katɔ̃memasɛdze ɔnɔ, ne matere makɛlɛ Likaonia simagɛ̃ dzɛ nɖe Listra gu Derbe gu simagɛ̃ dzɛ mpia i ndɛ̃ mmɔ ame ne.
Masɛ maaɣɛ Itɔ̃me Bielea i mmɔ.
Paulo Gu Barnaba Ɔkɛlɛ Listra Gu Derbe.
I Listra ne, manya ɔrɛrɛ̃ ɔwɛ̃ gɔ nɖe bafã fiɛ ɔ̃ita ɔsɛ ɔnya gɔ maɣe wũ.
Ɔsi i mmɔ ɔto ɔkã Itɔ̃me Bielea nɛ i Paulo to ɔɣɛ atsue.
Gɔ Paulo ɔnyɔ wũ totoroo sɔ ɔba kafɔkaɖe i Yesu ame fiɛ ɔfɔ ɔɖe sɔ ɔ̃awo isosarɛ ɔna ne, ɔla kulu ɔɣere wũ sɔ, “Ta ya i fɔ ngba iso!” Ne ɔrɛrɛ̃ gɔgbe ɔkɔlɛ ɔɣo ɔtsɛ isɛ ikiki ne.
Gɔ mma nɣɛ mato manɔ itɔ̃me ɔnya nnɛ i Paulo ɔbara ne, mala kulu teteree i Likaonia siɖe ame sɔ, “Aɣɔ loso aba i bo ndɛ̃ lɛ maturi!” Ne ɔso matã Barnaba iyere sɔ Seus fiɛ makpere Paulo ɔ̃ wũ sɔ Herme, alasɔ ɔ̃ loɖe ika.
Ne Seus ɔbia gɔ kuɣɔ iyo lobore imatã ɔmagɛ̃ ibere ɔsu manantsuĩ rɛrɛ̃ gu aɣatati aɣɔ̃la ɔbɔ sɔ ɔ̃ gu ɔ̃ maturi aasu masɔrɛ katɔ̃memasɛdze i ɔmagɛ̃ kayogodɔ̃.
Gɔ Paulo gu Barnaba ɔnɔ nnɛ mato mabie sɔ mabara ne, makɛkɛ ma awu wa mapia.
Matere mabo i maturi ndɛ̃ mato kulu sɔ, “Tete mɛrɛ̃, be iɖe mito mibara?
Bo wũ maturi awune kere boɖe lɛ mi.
Boba mi kɔrɛ ngbe gu Itɔ̃me Bielea.
Minyua ara wa nna karɔ̃ ngbe ɔbara si mifiniki misu ile mitã Bosate gɔ mba ngbã.
Ɔ̃ lobara kato gu karɔ̃ gu ɔpo gu ara wa ɔɖuɖu mpia i ɔ̃ ame!
Kokooko ne, ɔɖi kayi atsue sɔ maturi si mabara nnɛ maɖɔɛ.
Ɣɛɛ ne, ɔtogu ɔ̃ ara sɛɛ iɖi ite wa nto ate sɔ ɔpia gbaã.
Ɔsɛ ɔtã kado ɔpɛ i ɔwi iso ɔtã siraɖui gu araɖea gu isoɣɔ ana.” Atoa sɔ katɔ̃memasɛdze ɔɣɛ nwagbe ɔɖuɖu ne, ibua iɖa fiɛ mawo ma ɔtindza sɔ madaasɔrɛ ma.
Gɔ ma Yudase mawɛ̃ ma lobɔrɛ i Antiokia gu Ikonion ɔba maafinikira mmagbe adzuni ne, matã sɔ mapɛ Paulo ata mabore wũ maɖi i ɔmagɛ̃ ame gɔ mabu sɔ ɔ̃ɔkpi.
Ɣɛɛ gɔ mafɔɖedze ma mpia i mmɔ ɔki malɔ wũ ne, ɔledza ita ikpese ikɛlɛ ɔmagɛ̃ ame.
Gɔ kaɖe ɔsɛ̃ ne, ɔ̃ gu Barnaba ɔrui makɛlɛ Derbe.
Paulo Gu Barnaba Ɔkpese Makɛlɛ Antiokia Gɔ I Siria.
Gɔ masɛ maaɣɛ Itɔ̃me Bielea i Derbe ne, mana mafɔɖedze gbodzoo.
Ne ka makpese makɛlɛ Listra gu Ikonion gu Antiokia i Pisidia ne.
Masɛ maapia mafɔɖedze ma mpia i mmɔ ɔle sɔ maya teteree i ma kafɔkaɖe ame.
Maɣere ma ana sɔ, “Ikote sɔ boawe anyɛ gbodzoo fiɛ boana Ɣaa sigarakaɖekɔ̃ ame bobo.” Gɔ Paulo gu Barnaba ɔɖi matɔ̃ɖedze matã mafɔɖedze akuri ɔɖuɖu ne, manyi kanya makparama kayi, ne masu ma mapia i Bosate gɔ mafɔ maɖe nrɔɔ̃ ame ne.
Gɔ mabɔrɛ i Pisidia simagɛ̃ ame ne, makpese makɛlɛ Pamfilia karɔ̃ iso.
Maɣɛ Itɔ̃me Bielea i Perge fiɛ mafe makɛlɛ Atalia.
Gɔ mabɔrɛ i Atalia ne, maki i ndu iso makɛlɛ Antiokia ngbegɔ i matɔ̃ɖedze ɔsu ma mapia i Bosate nrɔɔ̃ ame ku ɔwi gɔ lofe ame sɔ ɔnyɔ ma nnya si ɔtã ma maro karabara ga mato maro ngbe.
Gɔ masɛ maabo Antiokia ne, makpere mafɔɖedze ma mpia i mmɔ masakanya fiɛ maɣere ma nnɛ manya i ma irisɛ ame.
Maɣere ma nwa i Ɣaa ɔbara ɔkigu i ma iso gu kumɛgɔ ɔ̃ɔbusi kafɔkaɖe ɔri ɔtã mma loiɖe ma Yudase.
Ne ka mawe i Antiokia gu mafɔɖedze igu ame ne.
